MAR 1:1 Ɗesǝ a shee pwoo ɗeret nkaa Jesu Kristi Nguɓam, Làa Naan.
MAR 1:2 Kaaɗe gyet mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal mǝ Aizaya ngusatpwoo Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Naan wur sat nǝ, an nlep ngulep fen shindǝm a kyeen fwaa, <<mbǝkǝ wur ɗak ar fwaa ɗi.
MAR 1:3 Mee gwar kǝ pǝreppee shi ɗoo ɗeɗes a naaryil, <Wur ɗak ar nDaa Wur aar ar nwur ndir-ndir!> >>
MAR 1:4 Joon ngucìn baptisma, a wur jì put a naaryil. Wur satpwoo Naan ngurum mo, mbǝkǝ mmo tuwap ɗi, kǝ nwur cìn baptisma ɗi mmo, mbe fwo kǝ shikbish mo-mo.
MAR 1:5 Nenyil nJudiya mo, kǝ nenyil nJerusalem mo ɗes, mo pwat dǝm pee Joon ɗi, ɗe mo woo shikbish fur mo, ɓe wur cìn baptisma mmo nɗǝǝn gyeen nJodan.
MAR 1:6 Joon lep a nlǝr ɗe mo ɗak shi shweep raakumi, wur kǝ ɗyiin zaal ɗe mo ɗak shi shim shin ciir mɓwoon fin. Wur kǝ se a ciɓel, kǝ nloor nshìi ɗe mo a yil.
MAR 1:7 Wur sat ngurum mo nǝnee, <<Mee gwar pǝ jì mɓwoon fen, ɗe, wur ɗes met nghan, kǝ baa ɗeret fen nǝ mak, kǝ nghan ɗoom mbǝkǝ nghan fwen teng kwoopshi wur ɗi kas.
MAR 1:8 Wen kǝn cìn baptisma nwun a shi am, ɗangɓǝ gwar nǝ wur njì ɓe wur ncìn baptisma nwun a shi Riin Ɗeɓang.>>
MAR 1:9 nƊǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ Jesu yool nyil nNazaret mǝ Galili, kǝ wur dǝm pǝ Joon ɗi gyeen nJodan, ɓe Joon cìn baptisma nwur nɗǝǝn gyeen nJodan nǝ.
MAR 1:10 Kaaɗe Jesu nkaa put nɗǝǝn am nǝ, ɓe abet, wur naa ɗengnaan a wuwang. Ɓe Riin sham kaa mbul sǝ, nǝ sham lang nkaa wur.
MAR 1:11 Kǝzak, mee ɗoo put nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Gha a Làa fen ɗe nwal gha, kǝ kat retnyit kǝ gha hakyeng.>>
MAR 1:12 Abet-abet, ɓǝ Riin Naan dǝm kǝ Jesu a naaryil.
MAR 1:13 Jesu cìn teer laarfeer a yil nǝ, a peeɗi ngujwaan kam wur ɗi. Wur yem ashak kǝ luwaa yil mo. Nenlep Naan mo jì ɓam wur
MAR 1:14 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ yaa Joon le nɗǝǝn lushoot, ɓǝ Jesu dǝm wul nGalili, wur nkaa satpwoo ɗeret mǝ Naan.
MAR 1:15 Wur sat ngurum mo nǝnee, <<Pee nǝ kǝ wul, kǝ mulki kǝ Naan nǝ kus zak. Wu tuwap, wu shinzeen mpwoo ɗeret nǝ.>>
MAR 1:16 Kaaɗe Jesu a ar ɗel mpwoo am kuur mǝ Galili, ɓǝ wur naa Simon Pita kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fin Andru, mon nkaa bwet shang mɓut am, mbe yak pupwap mo.
MAR 1:17 Ɓe Jesu wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu jì nɗang nghan, ɓe nghan nle kǝ wu ɗee a nensatpwo kǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ wu dul gurum mo shin jì pee nghan ɗi kaaɗi wuu yak pupwap sǝ.>>
MAR 1:18 Abet, ɓe mo yool yit shang fur mo, ɓe mo dǝm nɗang wur.
MAR 1:19 Kaaɗe wur gyes dǝm ɗe a kyeen lee, ɓe wur naa Jemis làa Zeɓeɗi, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fin Joon, mo nɗǝǝn tii zak. Mon nkaa ɗak shang fur mo.
MAR 1:20 Abet, ɓe wur pet mo. Ɓe mo yool yit puun fur Zeɓeɗi nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, ashak kǝ nen ɗe moo cìn ɗak mmo. Ɓe mo dǝm nɗang Jesu.
MAR 1:21 Mo dǝm nɗǝǝn Kaparnahum, ɓe Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn mee lu Naan parpuus Nookɗi. Ɓe wur yaa kámpwoo Naan ngurum mo.
MAR 1:22 Kám wur nǝ aapwoo mmo zam, mbǝɗe wu kám a kaa gwar ɗe wu kǝ iiko sǝ, baa a kaa nenkám Wàar Mosis mo sǝ kas.
MAR 1:23 Mee gwar wu kǝ riin ɗebish, nɗǝǝn lu Naan nǝ, ɓe gwar nǝ ɓwet or.
MAR 1:24 Wur sat nee, <<Jesu ngwe Nazaret, a me kaat mun kǝ gha ye? A jì mpesi a mbe twe mun aa? Wen man nǝ, gha a gwar ɗeɓang mǝ Naan.>>
MAR 1:25 Jesu gwak riin ɗebish nǝnee, <<A ɗok tǝtǝk! A put aku nɗǝǝn gwar nǝ!>>
MAR 1:26 Kaaɗe riin ɗebish nǝ yoon gwar nǝ ɓal-ɓal, ɓe nǝ le or shiɓal, ɓe nǝ put nɗǝǝn gwar nǝ.
MAR 1:27 Ne aapwoo gurum nǝ mo jir, har mo ɗoom tal pushak nǝ, <<A me nɗesǝ ye? A mee kám ɗepoo nɗesi! Wu satpwoo shi iiko, ɓe har riin ɗebish mo cìn mbii ɗe wu sat.>>
MAR 1:28 Abet ɓe pwoo nkaa Jesu nǝ put dǝm nɗǝǝn yil ɗe mo neer Galili ciirkaat jir.
MAR 1:29 Kaaɗe mo pwat nɗǝǝn lu Naan nǝ, ɓe mo dǝm ntul Simon Pita kǝ Andru, ashak kǝ Jemis kǝ Joon.
MAR 1:30 Ɓe mo kat nǝǝnkaam Pita waa saam kǝ cilem. Abet ɓe mo sat nJesu.
MAR 1:31 Ɓe wur jì yaa sar waa, wu ɗyeep waa tong a tǝng, ɓe cilem nǝ kyes nwar, ɓe war cìn ɗak mbiise mmo.
MAR 1:32 Nkansǝǝn, kaaɗi puus nǝ ɗoom taa nlu, ɓe gurum mo jì kǝ nen ciinkoom mo ɗes, ɗe mo kǝ riin ɗebish mo pee Jesu ɗi.
MAR 1:33 Nen yilkaam nǝ mo jir, mo jì kuur mpolu nǝ.
MAR 1:34 Jesu bar nenciinkoom mo ɗes, kǝ shwal mo shini-shini, wu pwat kǝ riin ɗebish mo ɗes zak. Baa wu yit kǝ riin ɗebish nǝ mo leshap ɗe kas, mbǝɗe mo kǝ man wur.
MAR 1:35 Ɗaar nǝ, ɓe Jesu yool put mpar-mpar, ɓe wur dǝm a peeɗi baa mee gurum ɗi kas, mbe wur ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan).
MAR 1:36 Pita kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur, mo pwat dǝm mbe yap wur.
MAR 1:37 Kaaɗe mo kat wur, ɓe mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Gurum mo jir mo nkaa yap gha.>>
MAR 1:38 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu yit kǝ mu dǝm njep yil ɗe mo akyeen sǝ, mbǝkǝ nghan dǝm nsatpwo Naan ɗi nyil mǝnǝ mo zak. Mbǝɗe wen jì a mbe satpwoo Naan nǝ.>>
MAR 1:39 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nGalili jir, wu satpwoo Naan ngurum mo nɗǝǝn lu Naan mo, kǝ wur pwat kǝ riin ɗebish mo zak.
MAR 1:40 Mee nguloom jì kurum nfurum ntoom Jesu, ɓe wu ɗang pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<Katɗang a rǝɓet, ɓe gha mak bar nghan kǝ wen ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang.>>
MAR 1:41 Jesu naajeel gwar nǝ, ɓe wu zan sar fin, wu tung gwar nǝ, ɗang wur sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<wen nlap ii, aa bar.
MAR 1:42 Abet, ɓe loom nǝ kyes, ɓe gwar nǝ zum.
MAR 1:43 Jesu satpwoo ngwar nǝ shiɓal. Ɓe wur ɓwet gwar nǝ abet-abet.
MAR 1:44 Ɓe wur sat ngwar nǝnee, <<A tap, taji a sat mee mbii mmee gurum kas. Ɗangɓe a dǝm a kam sak fwaa mpris, mbǝkǝ wur naa gha ɗi, kǝ a shin zuum ɗi zak, kaaɗi gyet Mosis sat nǝ, nen ɗe mo ke ten zum, ɓe mo shin mbiizuum, mbǝkǝ gurum mo man nnǝ moo ke ɗee a ɗebǝbar.>>
MAR 1:45 Ɗangɓe gwar nǝ wur put, ɓe wur yaa satpwoo nǝ gurum mo ɗes, ɓe pwoo nǝ kaatpee jir, har nǝ le kǝ baa Jesu mak baa ɗel nɗǝǝn yil nǝ agaak kas. Ɗangɓe wur tong a peeɗi baa mee gurum mo ɗe kas. Jir kǝsǝ, ɓe gurum mo pwat shipee-shipee, mo dǝm pee wur ɗi.
MAR 2:1 mƁwoon jep teer mo ɓe Jesu wur ɗel nɗǝǝn Kaparnahum, ɓe gurum mo kǝlǝng nǝ, wur waaji ntul.
MAR 2:2 Gurum mo ɗes mo gam lu nǝ, har mpolu, ɗe baa mee pee ɗenshii ɗi kas. Jesu nkaa satpwoo Naan mmo.
MAR 2:3 Ɓe mee des mo feer, mo jì kǝ mee gwar ɗe foshik wur fii, pee Jesu ɗi.
MAR 2:4 Mbǝ ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, ɓe baa mo mak dǝm kǝ gwar nǝ kus pee Jesu ɗe kas. Ɗangɓǝ mo kàa tap wang ɗeng lu nǝ nciit kǝ pee ɗi Jesu wur nɗǝǝn nǝ. Kaaɗe mo wang ɗeng lu nǝ, ɓe mo lep gwar nǝ sham nkaa mbiisaam, ɗe gwar nii saam nkaa nǝ.
MAR 2:5 Kaaɗe Jesu naa shinzeen mo nǝ, ɓe wu sat ngwe foshik ɗe fii nǝ nǝnee, <<Làa fen, mo kǝ fwo shikbish fwaa mo ngha.>>
MAR 2:6 Ɗangɓe pak nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, ɗe moo tong ɗe, mo nkaa pan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo nǝnee,
MAR 2:7 <<A me le ɗang gwar ɗesǝ wur sat pwoo mǝnǝ ye? Wur leshin kaa Naan sǝ! Baa mee gurum mak fwo shikbish kas, see Naan bǝshin ɓejee ɗak.>>
MAR 2:8 Abet, ɓe Jesu man mbii ɗe moo pan nǝ nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<A mi le ɗang wuu pan mbii ɗesǝ mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo ye?
MAR 2:9 A ɗeɗang fiyeel met ye? Ɗe wen nsat nguciinkoom nǝnee, <mo kǝ fwo shikbish fwaa mo ngha,> aa koo ɗe wen nsat nwur nǝnee, <A yool a mang mbiisaam fwaa a mwaan> yi?
MAR 2:10 Ɗangɓǝ mbǝkǝ wu man ɗe nǝ, Làa Gurum, wur kǝ iiko nkaa yil nǝ, mbe fwo shikbish mo. Ɓe Jesu sat ngwar ɗe foshik wur fii nǝ, nǝnee,
MAR 2:11 <<Wen sat gha, a yool, a mang mbiisaam fwaa a dǝm ntul>>
MAR 2:12 Abet, ɓe gwar nǝ wur yool, wur mang mbiisaam fin, ɓe wur put dǝm ntul a yit mo jir. Ɓe nǝ aapwoo mo jir, ɓe mo kwoop Naan, mo sat nǝ, <<Baa muu cam naa mee mbii aapwoo kaa ɗesǝ sǝ kas.>>
MAR 2:13 Jesu put dǝm mpwoo am kuur zak, ɓe gurum mo ɗes, mo jì kuur pee wur ɗe. Ɓe wu yaa kámpwoo Naan mmo.
MAR 2:14 Ɓe kaaɗi wur a ar ɗel dǝm, ɓe wur naa Livai làa Alfiyas, wur tong a peelap shool wap. Jesu sat nwur nǝnee, <<A jì nɗang an.>> Ɓe Livai wur yool taa nɗang Jesu.
MAR 2:15 Kaaɗe Jesu dǝm tong a peese mbiise nlu Livai, ɓe nenlapwap mo ɗes, kǝ nenshikbish mo, nen ɗe baa moo kyeer Wàar Mosis kas, kǝ pak gurum mo ɗes, mo jì tong ashak kǝ Jesu kǝ jeplep wur mo, a peese mbiise nǝ.
MAR 2:16 Ɓe nenkám Wàar nMosis mo, ɗe mo a nen Farisi mo, mo naa Jesu wur nkaa sese ashak kǝ nenshikbish mo, kǝ nenlapwap mo. Ɓe mo sat jeplep mo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang Jesu wur sese ashak kǝ nenlapwap mo, kǝ nenshikbish mo yi?>>
MAR 2:17 Kaaɗe Jesu kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe wur lap mmo nǝnee, <<Baa nen ɗe mon nkoom, mon nyap nguyen kas, amma a nen ɗe mo a gok. Baa wen jì a mbe pet nen ɗe ndere mo kas, amma wen jì a mbe pet nenshikbish mo.>>
MAR 2:18 Nenlep nJoon mo, kǝ nen Farisi mo, mon nkaa wet kǝ neen. Pak gurum mo jì pee Jesu ɗi, mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe nenlep nJoon mo, kǝ mǝ nen Farisi mo, moo wet kǝ neen, ɗangɓǝ baa jeplep fwaa, moo wet kǝ neen kas yi?>>
MAR 2:19 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wu yee nǝ, nǝn mmak cìn kǝ mǝzep ɗe mo a pee serǝɓet mǝ ɗyik, mon ntong kǝ neen, ɓe mish kǝ matpoo nǝ wur ɗe ashak kǝ mo me? Katɗang mish matpoo nǝ wur kuɗi ashak kǝ mo, ɓe baa mon mmak wet kǝ neen kas.
MAR 2:20 Ɗangɓǝ puus nǝ mon njì, ɗe mon mmang mish nǝ nkaa mo. Ɗangɓe, mon ntong kǝ neen nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo.
MAR 2:21 Baa mee gurum mak luwas nlǝr ɗesǝǝr shi fuwaat ɗepoo kas, katɗang wu cìn kǝsǝ, ɓe fuwaat ɗepoo, ɗe wu luwas nlǝr ɗesǝǝr nǝ ɗishik, nǝn nkur, ɓe nǝn nwaa tee nlǝr ɗesǝǝr nǝ, ɓe tee mǝnǝn nɗes met nɗinshee.
MAR 2:22 Kǝzak, baa mee gurum mak ɗoo am anab ɗepoo nɗǝǝn tuulshim ɗesǝǝr mo kas. Katɗang wur cìn kǝsǝ, ɓe am anab ɗepoo nǝn mpyan tuulshim ɗesǝǝr nǝ mo, kǝ am anab nǝn mɓeer, kǝ tuulshim nǝ mon ntee zak. Amma moo ɗoo am anab ɗepoo a nɗǝǝn tuulshim ɗepoo mo.>>
MAR 2:23 Mee parpuus Nookɗi, ɓe Jesu yaa ar ɗel mɓut mmaar ɗǝɓen. Kaaɗe mo a ar ɗel nǝ, ɓe nenɗǝm nɗang Jesu mo ɗoom cǝlang pak ɗǝɓen nǝ.
MAR 2:24 Nen Farisi mo sat nJesu nǝnee, <<A naa jeplep fwaa mo nkaa cìn mbii ɗe baa nǝ ret kǝ mo cìn mǝnǝ parpuus Nookɗi kas.>>
MAR 2:25 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Ashee, baa wuu cam tang mbii ɗe mo ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nkaa mbii ɗe gyet Devit, kǝ nenyil ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur mo cìn, kaaɗi gyet neenláa wur kǝ nenyil ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur kas se?
MAR 2:26 Gyet wur ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝǝɗes, ɓe wur mang gǝǝl aas ɗe mo kǝ ten shin nǝn nNaan, wur se, kǝ wur shin pak nenyil ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur. Gǝǝl aas ɗe baa a mee gurum buu mak se nǝ kas, see a pris mo ɗak. Gyet wur ɗel Lu Naan ɗǝǝɗes nǝ a mɓít ɗe Abiyata wur a pris ɗǝǝɗes met jir.>>
MAR 2:27 Jesu sat mmo nǝ, <<Mo le parpuus Nookɗi nǝ a mbe gurum, baa mo le a gurum mbe parpuus Nookɗi nǝ kas.
MAR 2:28 Ɗesǝ nǝ kám nǝ, Làa Gurum, wur a Daa mǝ puus Nookɗi nǝ zak.>>
MAR 3:1 Jesu waa baa ɗel nɗǝǝn mee lu Naan. Ɓe mee gwar ɗi nlu nǝ, ɗe sar wur fii.
MAR 3:2 Pak gurum mo leyit fur mo nkaa Jesu, mbǝkǝ mo naa ɗe. Kyet wur mbar gwar nǝ mpuus Nookɗi wa? Mbǝkǝ mo kat mbii cìn mwaanaa ɗi.
MAR 3:3 Jesu sat gwar ɗe sar wur nǝ fii nǝnee, <<A yool a jì a ɗar sǝ agaak.>>
MAR 3:4 Ɓe wur tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Kyet Wàar Mosis nǝ sat nǝ, mu cìn a mbii ɗeret mpuus Nookɗi, aa koo mu cìn a mbii ɗebish ye? Mu ɓam seen gurum aa, koo mu tutu seen nǝ ye?>> Amma mo ɗok tǝtǝk.
MAR 3:5 Jesu naa mo shi tuup, mbǝɗe nǝ shwal nwur mɓut mɓe ɓalkáa kǝ mo nǝ, ɓǝ wur sat ngwar nǝnee, <<A zan sar fwaa.>> Ɓe gwar nǝ zan sar nǝ, ɓe sar wur nǝ zuum.
MAR 3:6 Nen Farisi mo pwat, ɓǝ abet, mo dǝm ɓwolpwoo ashak kǝ nen nHerot mo, mbǝkǝ mo yap ar ɗe mon ntu Jesu ɗe.
MAR 3:7 Jesu yool dǝm mpwoo am kuur, ashak kǝ nenɗǝm nɗang wur mo, ɓe nen Galili mo, kǝ nen Judiya mo ɗes, mo dǝm nɗang wur,
MAR 3:8 kǝ nen ɗe mo nkwang nJerusalem, kǝ nkwang Idumiya, kǝ canɗel nkwang Jodan, kǝ nkwang yil nTaya kǝ Sidon zak. Gurum mo ɗes mo jì pee Jesu ɗi. Mɓeɗi mo kǝlǝng mbii ɗewur cìn mo jir.
MAR 3:9 Jesu sat njeplep fir mo, kǝ mo tang mee tii le nwur kus, mbǝkǝ taji ɗuu gurum nǝ mo jyar jì ɗwat wur ɗe kas.
MAR 3:10 Mɓeɗi wur kǝ bar gurum mo ɗes, ɓe nenciinkoom mo ɗe nkaa jì, mbǝkǝ mo tung wur ɗe.
MAR 3:11 Kǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ riin ɗebish mo, katɗang mo naa wur, ɓe mmo taa ntoom nwur, ɓe mo bwet or nǝnee, <<Gha a Làa Naan.>>
MAR 3:12 Ɗangɓe Jesu sat nriin ɗebish nǝ mo shiɓal hakyeng, nǝ, Taji mo woo wuɗi kas.
MAR 3:13 Jesu kaa aɗeng jwak, ɓe wur pǝrep nen ɗewur rǝɓet mo, ɓe mo jì pee wur ɗi.
MAR 3:14 Wur bǝlǝp gurum mo kaapaat baavǝl, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗe a jeplep nwur mo, kǝ mo tong ɗi ashak kǝ wur, kǝ wur lep mo ɗe mɓe satpwoo Naan.
MAR 3:15 Wur shin mbal mo mbe ceen riin ɗebish mo zak.
MAR 3:16 Sǝm nen ɗewur bǝlǝp mo kaapaat baavǝl nǝ, mo a Simon, ɗe Jesu le sǝm nwur a Pita.
MAR 3:17 Kǝ Jemis làa Zeɓeɗi, kǝ Joon ɗyemnǝǝn Jemis, wur le sǝm mo a Bowanarjis, ɗe shii mǝnǝ nǝ, (moo cìn mbii a koo nluu ɗe nii petpee sǝ.)
MAR 3:18 Kǝ Andru, kǝ Filip, kǝ Bartolomi, kǝ Matiyu, kǝ Tomas, kǝ Jemis làa Alfiyas, kǝ Taddawus, kǝ Simon, ɗe moo pet wur a Zeelot.
MAR 3:19 Kǝ Judas Iskariyot, gwar ɗewur ji seet kǝ Jesu sǝ.
MAR 3:20 Jesu waa baa ntul zak. Ɓe gurum mo ɗes mo waa baaji kuur pee wur ɗi zak, har nǝ le kǝ baa Jesu kǝ jeplep wur mo mak se mbiise kas.
MAR 3:21 Kaaɗe nen wur mo kǝlǝng nǝ, baa wur mak katpee mbe se mbiise kas, kǝ mo kǝlǝng gurum moo sat nǝ, Jesu kǝ tar, ɓe mo dǝm mbe yaa wur.
MAR 3:22 Pak nenkám Wàar Mosis ɗe mo pwat nJerusalem ji, mo sat zak nǝnee, <<Jesu kǝ Beelzebul, ɗe nǝ a mishkoom mǝ riin ɗebish mo, kǝ wur kǝ ceen riin ɗebish mo a shiɓal mǝ mishkom kǝ riin ɗebish mo.>>
MAR 3:23 Jesu pǝrep mo jì kus, ɓe wur sat Sǝmpwoo mo nǝnee, <<Cinarang ɗangɓe ngujwaan nwaa ceen ngujwaan put yi?
MAR 3:24 Katɗang ɓe mee yil ɗǝdes ɓàk set vǝl, mɓe cìn lek kǝ set, ɓe yil ɗǝdes mǝnǝn nleng.
MAR 3:25 Katɗang ɓe mee nentul mo ɓàk sut vǝl, mbe cìn lek kǝ shak, ɓe tul mǝnǝn nleng.
MAR 3:26 mBe mǝnǝ, kaɗang ɓe ngujwaan wur ɓàk mulki wur ɗe vǝl, mbe cìn lek kǝ foshik wur, ɓe baa mulki wur nǝn nɗar kas, ɓe a kyes wur nǝ mmǝnǝ.
MAR 3:27 Baa mee gurum mak ɗel ntul nguɓal, mbǝkǝ wur hǝr long wur ɗǝ kas, see koo wur shee ɓwot nguɓal nǝ akuɗang, ɓe wur mmak hǝr long wur nǝ.
MAR 3:28 <<Azeen, kǝn sat nwun nǝ, shikbish ɗe gurum moo cìn, kǝ pwoo ɗebish ɗe moo sat, ɓe Naan wur nfwo shikbish mǝnǝn ngurum mo.
MAR 3:29 Ɗangɓǝ katɗang mee gwar cìn shikbish, nkaa Riin Naan, ɓe baa Naan nfwo gwar mǝnǝ kas, mɓe vit. Mɓeɗi wu cìn a shikbish ɗe baa Naan cam fwo nǝ nwur kas har ngaa-ngaa.>>
MAR 3:30 Jesu satpwoo ɗesǝ a mbǝɗe pak gurum moo sat nǝnee, <<Wur kǝ riin ɗebish.>>
MAR 3:31 Nǝǝn Jesu kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn wur mo jì ɗar atǝleng, ɓe mo lep mee gurum ɗel pet wur.
MAR 3:32 Gurum mo ɗes mo tong neer Jesu cǝǝrkaat, mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Nǝǝn fwaa, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fwaa moo rǝɓet naa gha atǝleng.>>
MAR 3:33 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<A wii a nǝǝn fen, kǝ a wii mo a ɗyemnǝǝn fen yi?>>
MAR 3:34 Ɓe wur lyap nen ɗe moo tong neer wur cǝǝrkaat, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu naa, a nǝǝn fen, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fen mon nɗesi!
MAR 3:35 Ngwar ɗewur cìn ɗyen kǝ Naan, ɓe a gwar mǝnǝ a ɗyemnǝǝn fen ɗemish, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fen ɗe mat, kǝ nǝǝn fen zak.>>
MAR 4:1 Jesu waa baa yaa kám-kam ɗe ngurum mo mpwoo am kuur nǝ. Ɓe gurum mo ɗes mo jì kuur pee wur ɗi. Mbe ɗuu kǝ gurum nǝ mo, ɓe Jesu ɗel tong nɗǝǝn tii nkaa am nǝ, ɓe ɗuu kǝ gurum nǝ mo jì ɗar pǝkom am kuur nǝ.
MAR 4:2 Jesu kám mbii mo ngurum mo ɗes shi sǝmpwoo mo. Nɗǝǝn kám wur nǝ mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee,
MAR 4:3 <<wu lekom! Gyet mee ngumaar wur put dǝm mɓe ɓwet cirem mɓut mmaar.
MAR 4:4 Ɓe kaaɗi wur nkaa ɓwet cirem nǝ, ɓe pak cirem nǝ mo taa nkaa ar, ɓe nyer mo sham cak cirem nǝ se.
MAR 4:5 Pak cirem nǝ mo taa nkaa kwoop, a peeɗi baa nǝ kǝ yil ɗes kas. Abet, ɓe cirem nǝ mo ciir kàa.
MAR 4:6 Kaaɗe puuskàa ɓe mo caan har mo fii, mbǝɗe baa mo kat yil ɗes mbe sham seen kas.
MAR 4:7 Pak cirem nǝ mo taa mɓut nhǝr mo, ɓe mo kàa wurang nɗǝǝn hǝr nǝ mo, ɓe hǝr nǝ mo tǝreng káa mmo, ɓe baa mo le mee aa kas.
MAR 4:8 Pak cirem nǝ mo taa nkaa yil ɗeret, ɓe mo kàa wurang rǝret, kǝ mo le àa ɗes. Memee le àa mo laarkun, kǝ memee le mo laarpeemee, kǝ memee le mo kambil.>>
MAR 4:9 Jesu sat nǝnee, <<Ngwar ɗewur kǝ koom mǝ kǝlǝngpee, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur kǝlǝng.>>
MAR 4:10 Kaaɗe Jesu ɗee mbǝshin, ɓe pak nen ɗe mo kǝlǝng sǝmpwoo nǝ, mo jì ashak kǝ jeplep wur ɗe ɗekaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo. Mo jì tal pǝ wur, mbǝkǝ wur sat shii Sǝmpwoo nǝ ɗi mmo.
MAR 4:11 Jesu sat mmo nǝ, <<Naan shin man nwun, mbǝkǝ wur manshii kǝ mbii ɗe mo a sǝsok mǝ mulki Naan, amma pee nen ɗe atǝlǝng mo, ɓe moo kǝlǝng mbii ɗesǝ mo jir a shi sǝmpwoo.
MAR 4:12 Mbǝkǝ koo <ɗe mo naa, ɓe mon nnaa shi yit ɗak, amma baa mon nnaashii nǝ kas. Pee nen ɗe mo kǝlǝng, ɓe mon nkǝlǝng a shi kom ɗak, amma baa mon mmanshii nǝ kas, mbǝkǝ taji mo ciir, kǝ Naan fwo shikbish fur mo ɗi.>>
MAR 4:13 Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Baa wuu manshii sǝmpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ kas aa? Cinarang ɗang wun mmanshii kǝ koor sǝmpwoo nǝ mo yi?
MAR 4:14 Shii kǝ sǝmpwoo nǝ nɗesi, ngumaar nǝ wur a kaa ngusatpwoo Naan sǝ.
MAR 4:15 Pak gurum mo a kaa cirem ɗe mo taa a ar sǝ, ɗe katɗang mo kǝlǝng pwoo Naan nǝ, ɓe abet, ngujwaan wur jì ghǝr pwoo ɗe mo kǝlǝng nǝ nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo.
MAR 4:16 Pak gurum mo a kaa cirem ɗe mo ɓwet a kwoop sǝ, ɗe katɗang mo kǝlǝng pwoo kǝ Naan ni, ɓe mo lap shi retnyit kǝlak-kǝlak.
MAR 4:17 Amma baa nǝ sham seen jurum-jurum, nɗǝǝn mo kas, kǝ baa mon nteer vǝl kas. Katɗang mee luk yool koo gurum mo shin jeel mmo, mbe pwoo Naan nǝ, ɓe abet, mo baa shiɓwoon kǝlak-kǝlak.
MAR 4:18 Pak gurum mo a kaa cirem ɗe mo taa mɓut nghǝr mo sǝ, ɗe katɗang mo kǝlǝng pwoo Naan nǝ,
MAR 4:19 ɓe, mbe pan kǝ mbii mo, kǝ choor long mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo, kǝ numpee mǝ long mo, kǝ fwoot mǝ pak mbii mo, mo vwan pwoo nǝ, ɓe baa mo làa-làa kas.
MAR 4:20 Pak gurum mo a kaa cirem ɗe mo ɓwet mo nkaa yil ɗeret sǝ, ɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo Naan nǝ. Ɓe mo lap nǝ, ɓe pwoo Naan nǝ cìn ɗak ɗes nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo, kaa cirem ɗe nǝ làa-làa mo ɗes sǝ. Pak mo làa-làa laarkun, pak mo laarpeemee kǝ pak mo kambil.>>
MAR 4:21 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Kyet mee gurum nle wus nfitila, ɗang wur waa mang ɗaa ɗeɗes paa nǝ ɗi wa? Koo wur waa le nǝ nder peesaam wa? Amma wur nle nǝ aɗeng pee, a pee le fitila.
MAR 4:22 Baa mee mbii ɗe, ɗe nǝ a sǝsok ɗe nǝn nook put agaak kas, kǝ baa mee mbii ɗe, ɗe nǝ a pǝpaa, ɗe mon nook put kǝ nǝ agaak kas.
MAR 4:23 Ngwar ɗewur kǝ kom mǝ kǝlǝngpee, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur kǝleng.>>
MAR 4:24 Wur sat mmo zak nǝnee, <<Wu cìn pan nkaa mbii ɗe wuu kǝlǝng mo. Shi ɗaa ɗe wuu kám mbii ɗe ngurum mo, ɓe mon nkám mbii mo wun a shi shik zak, ɓe nǝn ngam met mumo nǝ zak.
MAR 4:25 Koo ɗang weyi ɗewur kǝ mbii, ɓe mon ncin ɗyikǝ nwur. Ɗangɓe gwar ɗe baa wur kǝ mee mbii kas, ɓe mon nsǝǝt nwaa yaa wur kǝ rep mbii ɗewur kǝ nǝ.>>
MAR 4:26 Jesu sat zak nǝnee, <<Mulki Naan nǝ a kaa mee gwar ɗe wu ɓwet cirem ɗǝɓen mɓut mmaar sǝ.
MAR 4:27 Ɓe wur saam mpar, kǝ wur yool mbít, ɓe ɗǝɓen nii kàa nii wurang. Ɓe baa wur man kaaɗi nii wurang sǝ kas.
MAR 4:28 Yil nǝ shikáa wur, nii kǝ le mbii kǝkop mo kaa làa-làa. Nshee, ɓe nǝ wurang kàa pyan kom, ɓe nǝ putkáa, kǝ nǝ le àa.
MAR 4:29 Kaaɗe ɗǝɓen nǝ nung, ɓe wur mang cuk dǝm ɗiip ɗǝɓen nǝ abet, mbǝɗe pee mak ɗiip nǝ.>>
MAR 4:30 Jesu sat nǝnee, <<Mun nkám mulki Naan nǝ a kaa me sǝ yi? Kǝ mun nkám nǝ a shi sǝmpwoo ɗeɗangyii?
MAR 4:31 Nǝ a kaa àas kǝ mee tǝng, ɗe moo pet nǝ a mustad sǝ, ɗe nǝ kat met àas kǝ cirem mo jir, ɗang ɓe katɗang mo kop nǝ nyil,
MAR 4:32 ɓe nǝ yool wurang, ɓe nǝ ɗee a tǝng ɗeɗes zam. Nii put song ɗenan-nan mo, ɓe nyer mo jì le tish fur mo mɓut riin ni.>>
MAR 4:33 Jesu satpwoo ngurum mo, nkaa mulki kǝ Naan shi sǝmpwoo mo shini-shini, kaaɗi mo mak manshii nǝ sǝ.
MAR 4:34 Baa Jesu satpwoo ngurum nǝ mo kas, see a shi sǝmpwoo mo. Ɗang be katɗang wur ɗee mbǝshin ashak kǝ jeplep nwur mo, ɓe wur tap yakshii sǝmpwoo nǝ mmo jir.
MAR 4:35 Parpuus mǝnǝ, nkansǝǝn, ɓe Jesu sat njeplep fin mo nǝnee, <<Wu yool mmun, kǝ mu canɗel mu dǝm nkor ɗesí.>>
MAR 4:36 Mo yool yit ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, ɓe mo dǝm ashak kǝ Jesu nɗǝǝn tii ɗewur tong nɗǝǝn nǝ. Pak tii nǝ mo yool dǝm nɗang wur zak.
MAR 4:37 Mee kut ɗeɗes nǝ yool nkaa am nǝ, ɓe am ɗel nɗǝǝn tii nǝ. Ɓe tii nǝ ɗoom gam kǝ am.
MAR 4:38 Ɗangbe Jesu nsaam mɓwoon nɗǝǝn tii nǝ. Ɓe jeplep wur mo dǝm mii wur. Mo sat nǝ, <<Ngukám, a naa mun murep mbǝsǝ kas aa?>>
MAR 4:39 Jesu wur mii, ɓe wur gwak kut nǝ, ɓǝ wur sat am kuur nǝ nǝnee, <<A ɗok tǝtǝk. A saam coot.>> Ɓe kut nǝ ɗar, pee ɗokshik tǝtǝk.
MAR 4:40 Jesu sat njeplep wur mo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang kǝǝrmuut yaa wun ye? Har yaksǝ, ɓe baa wun shinzeen kas aa?>>
MAR 4:41 Nǝ aapwoo mmo ɗes zam, ɓe mo sat nshak nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur a weye? Ɗe har kut kǝ am kuur, mo cìn nɗyen wur!>>
MAR 5:1 Jesu kǝ jeplep wur mo can am kuur ɗe Galilee ɗel, ɓe mo jì wul nkor ɗǝǝr mu yil nGarasin.
MAR 5:2 Kaaɗe Jesu put nɗǝǝn tii nǝ abet ɓe wur kaat kǝ mee gwar ɗewur kǝ riin ɗebish, wur kǝ tong a nɗǝǝn gwoot kǝcir mo.
MAR 5:3 A peetong kǝ ngwar nǝ mmǝnǝ. Baa mee gurum katɓal ɗe mmak yaa wur ɓwoot kas. Koo ɗe mo ɓwoot wur a shi tǝsek, ɓǝ wur kǝ saa tǝsek nǝ.
MAR 5:4 Di moo naa njwal shii fir mo mɓut nfut, kǝ mo ɓwoot sar wur mo shi tǝsek, ɗang ɓe wur roop nfut nǝ, kǝ wur kǝram tǝsek nǝ fwo. Baa mee gurum mak cìn mee mbii nwur kas.
MAR 5:5 Par kǝ puus, ɓe wur tong a nɗǝǝn kǝcir, kǝ nɗǝǝn jwak mo, kǝ wur le or, kǝ wur kóon foshik wur nkaa jwak nǝ mo.
MAR 5:6 Kaaɗe wur naa Jesu kǝ jì jong-jong, ɓe wur yool su dǝm, wur dǝm kurum nfurum ntoom wur.
MAR 5:7 Ɓe wur bwet ɗoo shiɓal nǝnee, <<A me kaat mun kǝ gha ye? Jesu Làa Naan Ɗehai! Wen ɗang pǝ gha mbe sǝm Naan, taji a lejeel nghan kas.>>
MAR 5:8 Gwar nǝ sat kǝsǝ, a mbǝɗe Jesu kǝ sat nriin ɗebish nǝ nǝnee, <<A put aku mɓut ngwar nǝ, gha riin ɗebish.>>
MAR 5:9 Jesu tal pǝ gwar nǝ nǝnee, <<Sǝm fwaa a weyi?>> Gwar nǝ lap nǝnee, <<Sǝm fen nǝ a Lijiyon, ɗe shii kǝ mǝnǝ nǝ, mun ɗi ɗes.>>
MAR 5:10 Riin ɗebish nǝ mo ɗang pǝ Jesu hakyeng, mbǝkǝ taji wur ceen mo pwat nɗǝǝn yil mǝnǝ kas.
MAR 5:11 Kus kǝ peemǝnǝ, ɓe kuur kǝ danus mo ɗi ɗes, mo nkaa se shit shituur jwak.
MAR 5:12 Riin ɗebish nǝ mo ɗang pǝ Jesu, kǝ wur cínpee mmo, kǝ mo dǝm ɗel ɗe nɗǝǝn danus nǝ mo.
MAR 5:13 Jesu cínpee mmo, ɓe riin ɗebish nǝ mo pwat nɗǝǝn gwar nǝ, ɓe mo dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn danus nǝ mo. Ɗuu kǝ danus nǝ mo wul ngal vǝl, mo yool shwe sham a shituur jwak, ɓe mo sham ɓeer nɗǝǝn am canɗar nǝ, har mo murap jir.
MAR 5:14 Nentap danus nǝ mo shwe dǝm sat ngurum mo nɗǝǝn yilkaam, kǝ jepyil mo jir. Gurum mo pwat jì mɓe naa mbii ɗe nǝ kǝ cìn.
MAR 5:15 Mo jì pee Jesu ɗe, ɓe mo naa gwar ɗe di wur kǝ riin ɗebish mo wur kǝ tong, kǝ nlǝr a lǝlep, kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ɗyen fin rǝret, ɓe kǝǝrmuut yaa mo.
MAR 5:16 Nen ɗe mo cìn mbii ɗesǝ nǝ a yit fur, ɓe mo yakshii nǝ ngurum mo, kaaɗi Jesu bar gwar ɗe di wur kǝ riin ɗebish mo sǝ, kǝ kaaɗi danus nǝ mo murap sǝ.
MAR 5:17 Ɗangɓe nenyil nǝ mo ɗang pǝ Jesu, kǝ wur yool put nɗǝǝn yil fur.
MAR 5:18 Kaaɗe Jesu pǝ ɗel nɗǝǝn tii, ɓe gwar ɗe, wur kǝ riin ɗebish sǝ, wur ɗang pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<A yit an dǝm ɗi nɗang gha.>>
MAR 5:19 Amma baa Jesu rǝɓet kas. Wur sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<A waa baa ntul, pee ɗyemnǝǝn fwaa mo ɗi, mbǝkǝ a satpwoo ɗe mmo nkaa mbii ɗeɗes ɗe Naan kǝ cìn gha, kǝ ɗewur kǝ naajeel fwaa.>>
MAR 5:20 Gwar nǝ wur baa waa, ɓe wur taa satpwoo nǝ nenyil ɗe nkwang nyil nDikapolis mo, nkaa mbii ɗeɗes ɗe Jesu kǝ cìn nwur. Mbii ɗe gwar nǝ sat nǝ aapwoo ngurum mo.
MAR 5:21 Jesu waa baa canɗel nkwang nkor ɗese, nɗǝǝn am, ɓe gurum mo ɗes mo jì kuur pee wur ɗi, mpwo am kuur nǝ.
MAR 5:22 Mee gwar ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Jairus, wur a memee nɗǝǝn nennan-nan mǝ mee lu Naan, wur jì kurum ntoom Jesu.
MAR 5:23 Wur ɗang pǝ Jesu hakyeng, wur sat nǝnee, <<Reep fen ɗelee war pǝ yap muut. A jì a lesar fwaa nkaa war, mbǝkǝ war kat seen ɗi.>>
MAR 5:24 Jesu yool dǝm ashak kǝ Jairus, ɓe gurum mo ɗes mo dǝm nɗang wur, ɓe mo neer wur cǝǝrkaat kus-kus.
MAR 5:25 Mee mat war ɗe zak, ɗe waa kǝ ɓeer toom mbe ɓit mo kaapaat baavǝl.
MAR 5:26 War kǝ kyes long fin mo jir pǝ nenyen mo, jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa memee mak bar war kas. Ɗangɓe shwal war nii war sǝǝt cicíi nnǝ.
MAR 5:27 Kaaɗe war kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mbii ɗe Jesu wur cìn mo, ɓe war dǝm ɗel mɓut ɗuu gurum nǝ mo. Ɓe war tap dǝm mɓwoon Jesu, ɓe war tung pǝkom nlǝr wur.
MAR 5:28 Mɓeɗi war kǝ ten pan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup war nǝnee, <<Katɗang ɓe an tung koo a pǝkom nlǝr wur ɗe ɓejee ɗak, ɓe an mbar.>>
MAR 5:29 Aasǝ ɓe, war tung pǝkom nlǝr wur nǝ, ɓe abet, toom war nǝ ɗar. War man nɗǝǝn fwoshik war nǝ, nee shwal war nǝ kǝ kyes jee.
MAR 5:30 Abet Jesu man nǝ, iiko kǝ put nɗǝǝn foshik wur nǝ, ɓe wur ciir tal pǝ gurum nǝ mo, nǝnee, <<A wii tung nlǝr fen yi?>>
MAR 5:31 Jeplep wur mo lap nwur nǝnee, <<A naa ɗuu gurum nǝ mo neer gha ciirkaat, ɓe a sat nǝnee, <A wii tung gha yi> aa?>>
MAR 5:32 Jesu ciir mbǝkǝ wur naa gwar ɗe tung pǝkom nlǝr wur nǝ ɗi.
MAR 5:33 Mat nǝ war man koom ɗe war kǝ kat nǝ, ɓe war jì shi kǝǝrmuut kǝ ɗaar, war kurum nyil ntoom Jesu, ɓe war sat zeen nwur jir mbii ɗe nǝ kǝ cìn.
MAR 5:34 Jesu sat nwar nǝnee, <<Reep fen, shinzeen fii nǝ le kǝ yi ɗee a ɗebǝbar. Shwal fii nǝ kyes. Yi dǝm, yi wul riyang.>>
MAR 5:35 Kaaɗe Jesu kuɗi nkaa sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe mee des mo tong ntul Jairus mo jì, ɓe mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Reep fwaa war kǝ muut, Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe taji a lejeel Ngukám wur kas.>>
MAR 5:36 Amma Jesu lekom kaa baa wur kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe mo sat nǝ kas sǝ. Ɓe wur sat nJairus nǝnee, <<Taji pǝtuup fwaa wat kas, amma a shinzeen ɓejee.>>
MAR 5:37 Baa Jesu yit kǝ mee gurum dǝm nɗang wur kas, see a Pita, kǝ Jemis kǝ Joon ɗyemnǝǝn Jemis ɓejee ɗak.
MAR 5:38 Kaaɗe mo jì wul ntul Jairus nǝ, ɓe Jesu naa gurum mo nkaa fwo ruruu, mo nkaa wal, mo nkaa maap zak.
MAR 5:39 Wur ɗel nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang, wuu fwo ruruu kǝ wun mmaap yi? Baa laareep nǝ war kǝ muut kas, amma war a nsaam ɓejee.>>
MAR 5:40 Amma gurum nǝ mo jir, mo shwar wur shi shwar mǝ ɓakpee. Kaaɗe wur le kǝ gurum nǝ mo pwat atǝleng jir. Ɓe wur le kǝ puun kǝ nǝǝn reep nǝ, kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur, mo ɗel nɗǝǝn lu ɗe laareep nǝ war kǝ saam ɗi.
MAR 5:41 Ɓe wur yaa sar laareep nǝ, ɓe wur sat nwar nǝnee, <<Talifa kumi> ɗe shii mǝnǝ a nǝ, <<Apa, wen sat yi, yi yool.>>
MAR 5:42 Abet ɓe reep nǝ war yool ɗar, war yaa mwaan. Ɓitlàa war nǝ a kaapaat baavǝl. Nǝ aapwoo ngurum mo ɗes hakyeng.
MAR 5:43 Jesu satpwoo mmo shiɓal nǝnee, <<Taji wu satpwoo mmee gurum nkaa nǝ kas.>> Wur sat zak nǝnee, <<wu shin mbiise nwar se.>>
MAR 6:1 Jesu yool yit peemǝnǝ, ɓe wur waaji nɗǝǝn yil wur. Jeplep wur ɗe mo jì nɗang wur.
MAR 6:2 Kaaɗe parpuus Nookɗi nǝ wul, ɓe wur yaa kám-kam ngurum mo, nɗǝǝn lu Naan. Gurum mo ɗes mo kǝlǝng wur, nǝ aapwoo mmo, ɓe mo sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur kat mbii ɗesǝ mo jir a nneyi? Mo shin a seen ɗeɗang ngwar ɗesǝ ye? Ɗe nǝ le kǝ wur cìn mbii aapwoo ɗenan-nan sǝ mo yi?
MAR 6:3 Baa a ngu pwas shyeep sǝ nɗesǝ kas aa? Ɗyem kǝ Meeri, ɗe ɗyemnǝǝn wur mo a Jemis, kǝ Josep, kǝ Judas, kǝ Simon kas aa? Ɗe ɗyemnǝǝn wur ɗe mat sǝ mo, ashak kǝ mu zak, kas aa?>> Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe mo langtuup kǝ wur.
MAR 6:4 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Baa gurum moo cii shin ɗeɗes ngusatpwoo Naan kas, see a pǝ nenyil wur mo, kǝ ɗang wur mo, kǝ nentul wur mo, a moo cii shin ɗeɗes nwur ɓejee ɗak.>>
MAR 6:5 Baa wur cìn mee mbii aapwoo ɗenan-nan mo mpeemǝnǝ kas, amma wur lesar nkaa pak nenciinkoom mo lee ɗak, ɓǝ wur bar mo.
MAR 6:6 Nǝ aapwoo nJesu zam, mbǝɗe baa gurum nǝ mo shinzeen kas.
MAR 6:7 Jesu mwaan neer jepyil nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ wur kámpwoo Naan ɗe ngurum mo. Wur pǝrep jeplep wur ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo, ɓe wur lep mo she seet vǝl-vǝl. Wur shin iiko mmo nkaa riin ɗebish mo.
MAR 6:8 Wur sat mmo shiɓal nǝnee, <<Taji wu mang mee mbii mbǝ mwaan nǝ kas, koo gill aas, koo kuluk, koo shool nɗǝǝn daam fuu mo kas.
MAR 6:9 Amma wu mak mang kammwaan, kǝ wu jwal kwoopshi nshii fuu mo ɓejee ɗak. Kǝ taji wu lep nlǝr mo vǝl kas.
MAR 6:10 Koo tul ɗeɗangyii, ɗe wu ɗel ɗe, ɓe wu tong ntul mǝnǝ, har parɗe wun nyool wu yit pee nǝ.
MAR 6:11 Koo pee ɗeɗangyi ɗe baa mo lap wun kas, kǝ baa mo kǝlǝng pwoo fuu kas zak, ɓe katɗang wun a ar put mbe nǝ, ɓe wu ɓwap ǝrong ɗe nǝn nkaa shii fuu mo, mbǝkǝ nǝ ɗee ɗe a langtǝng nkaa nenyil nǝ mo, nǝ mo cii lap wun.>>
MAR 6:12 Ɗangɓe mo pwat dǝm yaa satpwoo Naan ngurum mo, mbǝkǝ gurum mo tuwap ɗi.
MAR 6:13 Mo ceen riin ɗebish mo ɗes, kǝ mo pwes nenciinkoom mo ɗes shi mwoor paat, kǝ mo bar mo.
MAR 6:14 Mishkoom Herot kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa Jesu, mbǝɗe sǝm Jesu nǝ ɗee a ɗemǝman ngurum mo jir, mbe mbii aapwoo ɗewur cìn mo, ɓe nǝ le kǝ pak gurum moo sat nǝnee, <<A Joon ngucìn baptisma wur kǝ yool a peemúut. A nǝ le ɗangɓe wur kǝ iiko mbe cìn mbii aapwoo ɗesǝ mo.>>
MAR 6:15 Amma pak gurum mo sat nǝnee, <<A Ilaija jì kámshin agaak.>> Kǝ pak mo sat nǝnee, <<Wur a ngusatpwoo Naan, koo memee nɗǝǝn nensatpwo Naan ɗe gyet yam mo sǝ.>>
MAR 6:16 Kaaɗe Herot wur kǝlǝng mǝnǝ, ɓe wur sat nǝnee, <<A Joon ɗe Di wen kǝn le kǝ mo can káa wur sí. A wur kǝ baa yool a peemúut.>>
MAR 6:17 Di Herot shikáa wur, wur kǝ lep gurum mo dǝm yaa Joon ɓwoot le nlushoot, mbe Herodiyas mat ɗyemnǝǝn nwur Filip, ɗe Herot wur kǝ lap war mmat.
MAR 6:18 Mɓeɗi Di Joon wur naa nsat nHerot nǝ, <<Baa nǝ ret kǝ a lapmat kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fwaa kas.>>
MAR 6:19 A mpeemǝnǝ ɓe Herodiyas war fes naa Joon kǝ yit ɗǝ bish, ɓe war rǝɓet tu Joon, ɗang baa war kat ar nǝ kas.
MAR 6:20 Herot wur kǝǝr Joon, mbǝɗe wur man nǝ, Joon wur a nguzeen, kǝ gwar ɗe ndere. Nǝ le kǝ nHerot tap kǝ Joon rǝret nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ. Herot wur kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe Joon kǝ sat mo shi retnyit, amma pwoo nǝ moo daampee nwur zam.
MAR 6:21 Aɓwoon jep mǝnǝ, ɓe Herodiyas waa katpee mɓe tu Joon, a parpuus ɗe mishkoom nHerot wur cet mbii serǝɓet, mɓe pan parpuus ɗe gyet mo làa wur ɗe. Ɓe wur pǝrep mishkoom ɗe mon nder wur, kǝ nenyil ɗenan-nan nkaa shiitoon nwur mo, kǝ nenyil ɗenan-nan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Galili, mbǝkǝ mo jì ɗe mɓe serǝɓet nǝ.
MAR 6:22 Ɓe reep kǝ Herodiyas war ɗel met kook, ɓe nǝ ret nHerot nyit zam, kǝ nenyil ɗe moo tong a pee sese ashak kǝ wur zak. Mishkoom Herot wur sat nreep nǝ war nǝnee, <<Koo mbii ɗeɗangyii, ɗe yii rǝɓet, ɓe yi ɗang, ɓe wen ncin nyi.>>
MAR 6:23 Wur waa baa tuweerpwoo nwar shiɓal zak nǝ, <<Koo a meye ɗe yi ɗang pǝ an jir, ɓe an ncin nyi. Koo ɗang nǝ a koor mulki fen, ɓe nghan nshin nyi.>>
MAR 6:24 Reep nǝ war dǝm tal pǝ nǝǝn waa nǝnee, <<Wen nɗang a meye?>> Nǝǝn nǝ war sat nǝnee, <<Yi dǝm yi sat wur shin káa Joon nguchìn baptisma nyi.>>
MAR 6:25 Reep nǝ war baa pǝ mishkoom ɗe kǝlak-kǝlak, ɓe war sat nwur nǝnee, <<A shin kaa nJoon nguchìn baptisma an nɗǝǝn kong sǝ.>>
MAR 6:26 Mbii ɗe war ɗang ɗesǝ nǝ wàt pǝtuup mishkoom zam, amma mbǝɗe wur kǝ ten tuweerpwoo nreep nǝ war shi ɓǝlemcuk, ntoom mǝzep wur nǝ mo, ɓe nǝ ɗee nwur a tǝng, kǝ wur shin káa nJoon nwar.
MAR 6:27 Abet-abet mishkoom Herot wur lep mee shiitoon mɓut nen tappee wur mo ke wur dǝm can káa nJoon jì kǝ ɗi. Shiitong nǝ wur dǝm can káa Joon nɗǝǝn lushoot.
MAR 6:28 Ɓe wur jì kǝ káa nǝ nɗǝǝn kong. Ɓe wur shin nwar. Ɓe war dǝm shin nnǝǝn fer.
MAR 6:29 Kaaɗe jeplep Joon mo kǝlǝng nǝ mo kǝ tu Joon, ɓe mo jì mang kúm wur dǝm wum nɗǝǝn kǝcir.
MAR 6:30 Jeplep Jesu mo waaji pǝ wur ɗe, ɓe mo sat nwur mbii ɗe mo dǝm cìn mo, kǝ mbii ɗe mo kǝ kám ngurum mo zak.
MAR 6:31 Mɓeɗi gurum mo ɗes moo jì, kǝ pak moo waa baa zak, ɓe nǝ le kǝ baa Jesu kǝ jeplep fir mo katpee ɗe mon nse mbiise ɗe kas. Ɓe Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu jì mmun, mu dǝm mbǝsun a peeɗi baa gurum mo ɗe kas kǝ wun wu nook ɗi.>>
MAR 6:32 Ɓe mo dǝm mbusut nɗǝǝn mee tii am, mpeeɗe baa gurum mo ɗi kas.
MAR 6:33 Amma gurum nǝ mo naa moo dǝm, kǝ mo man nǝ, a mo. Ɓe gurum nǝ mo yool nɗeen yilkaam mo jir, mo yaa ar a ɗǝǝr nshii, ɓe mo dǝm taa tǝleng nJesu kǝ jeplep wur mo.
MAR 6:34 Kaaɗe Jesu put nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, ɓe wu naa gurum mo kuur ɗes. Ɓe wur naa mo jeel wur nyit, ɗang mo ɗee a kaa tǝm ɗe baa mo kǝ ngunaa kas sǝ. Wur ɗoom kám mbii mo mmo ɗes.
MAR 6:35 Kus yak puus nru, ɓe jeplep nwur mo jì sat nwur nǝnee, <<A naa puus nǝ kus kǝ ru, ɗang pee ɗesǝ nǝ a naaryil ɗe baa tul gurum mo ɗi kas.
MAR 6:36 A sat ngurum nǝ mo dǝm, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm ɗe nɗǝǝn tul nenmaar mo, kǝ jepyil ɗe mo neer pee ɗesǝ cǝǝrkaat, mo seet mbiise ɗe shikáa fur.>>
MAR 6:37 Ɗangɓe Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wu shin mbiise mmo se.>> Mo lap nwur nǝnee, <<Mun ndem mu seet gǝǝl aas mǝ shool zinariya kambil vǝl, kǝ mu shin mmo se aa?>>
MAR 6:38 Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wun kǝ gǝǝl aas mo a kong ye? Wu dǝm wu naa ɗe.>> Kaaɗe mo dǝm naa, ɓe mo sat nǝnee, <<Mun kǝ gǝǝl aas mo paat, kǝ pupwap mo vǝl.>>
MAR 6:39 Ɓe Jesu sat njeplep wur mo ɓàk gurum nǝ mo tong nyil, shikuur-shikuur nkaa ɗem ɗe mǝlep nǝ.
MAR 6:40 Aasǝ ɓe gurum nǝ mo tong nyil shikuur-shikuur, pak mo kambil-kambil, ɗang pak mo laarpaat-laarpaat.
MAR 6:41 Jesu mang gǝǝl aas ɗepaat nǝ mo, kǝ pupwap ɗe vǝl nǝ mo, ɓe wur ɗyeep yit fer aɗeng, ɓe wur cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan. Ɓe wur yilang gǝǝl aas nǝ shin jeplep wur mo, kǝ mo swap ɗe ngurum nǝ mo se, kǝzak, wur ɓàk pupwap ɗe vǝl nǝ mmo aasǝ zak.
MAR 6:42 Gurum nǝ mo jir, mo se ǝɓǝl.
MAR 6:43 Har nen mwaan nɗang wur nǝ mo kok kor gǝǝl aas kǝ pupwap ɗe mo ɗee ɗe, ɓe nǝ gam kǝcik mo kaapaat baavǝl.
MAR 6:44 Ɗaa ɗe mo se mbiise nǝ, mo wul ngal paat.
MAR 6:45 Abet, ɓe Jesu le kǝ nen mwaan nɗang wur mo ɗel nɗǝǝn tii, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm ɗi nwur atǝleng, mbe canɗel nkor Betseda, kǝ wur ɓwet ɗuu kǝ gurum nǝ mo ɗe akuɗang.
MAR 6:46 Aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ ɓwet mo, ɓe wu kaa aɗeng jwak mɓe cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan).
MAR 6:47 Kaaɗe tii nǝ kǝ wul a naar am kuur nǝ, ɓe pee kǝ shool. Jesu wur ɗee ɗi a ɗǝǝr mɓǝshin.
MAR 6:48 Wur naa mo nkaa shwaajeel, mpee tung tii nǝ, mbǝɗe mee kut ɗeɗes nii baa kǝ mo shiɓwoon. Ɓe wur mwaan nkaa am kuur nǝ ke wur dǝm pee mo ɗi, naar kǝ karfe kun har dǝm karfe mpeemee. Kaaɗe wur dǝm wul pee mo ɗi, ɓe wur cìn kaa wur nɗǝɗel mo sǝ.
MAR 6:49 Ɓe, kaaɗi mo naa wur mwaan nkaa am nǝ, ɓe mo pan nǝ a mee nshon, ɓe mo ɓwet or.
MAR 6:50 Mɓeɗi mo jir mo naa wur, ɓe kǝǝrmuut fes yaa mo ɗes. Abet, ɓe Jesu leshap kǝ mo, wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu ɓwet pǝtuup fuu mo, a an. Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa wun kas.>>
MAR 6:51 Ɓe wur kàa ɗel nɗǝǝn tii nǝ ashak kǝ mo, ɗangɓe kut nǝ ɗar coot. Ɓe nǝ aapwoo mmo zam.
MAR 6:52 Mɓeɗi baa mo manshii kǝ pwoo nkaa mbii aapwoo ɗe Jesu cìn nkaa gǝǝl aas, ɗang wur shin ngurum mo ngal paat mo se sǝ kas. Mɓeɗi baa pǝtuup fur mo mak manshii nǝ rǝret kas.
MAR 6:53 Kaaɗe mo can am nǝ ɗel, ɓe mo jì wul kwang nyil nGenesaret, ɓe mo ɗyiin tii nǝ pǝkom ɗǝǝr.
MAR 6:54 Kaaɗe mo pwat nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, ɓe abet-abet Ɓe gurum mo man nǝ, a Jesu.
MAR 6:55 Mo yool shwe dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir, ɓe mo ghǝr nenciinkoom mo nkaa mbiisaam fur mo, mo dǝm kǝ mo mpee ɗe mo kǝlǝng nnǝ Jesu ɗi.
MAR 6:56 Peeɗi Jesu ɗel ɗe jir, koo nɗǝǝn jepyil mo, koo nɗǝǝn yilkaam mo, koo a peemaar mo, ɓe gurum mo ghǝr nenciinkoom fur mo, mo le mo mpwoo lutuk, kǝ mo ɗang pǝ Jesu, katɗang wur rǝɓet, ɓe wur yit kǝ mo tung koo a pǝkom nlǝr wur ɗe ɓejee ɗak. Nen ɗe mo tung nlǝr wur nǝ jir, ɓe mo bar.
MAR 7:1 Nen Farisi mo, kǝ pak nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, ɗe mo tong nJerusalem, mo jì kuur pee Jesu ɗi.
MAR 7:2 Ɓe mo naa pak jeplep Jesu moo se mbiise shi sar ɗe baa nǝ ɓang kas, shii kǝ mǝnǝ nǝ, baa mo vwang sar fur mo kaaɗi nen Farisi mo sat nnǝ, mo cìn sǝ kas.
MAR 7:3 Baa nen Farisi mo kǝ nen Yahudi mo jir, moo see mbiise kas, see mo shee vwang sar fur mo rǝret akuɗang. Moo tap aa mbii ɗe gyet mǝyii fur moo loot kǝ cìn nǝ.
MAR 7:4 Katɗang mo tong nlutuk jì, ɓe baa mon nse mee mbii kas, see mo shee vwang sut rǝret akuɗang. Pak mbii mo ɗǝɗes, ɗe moo cìn, ɗe mo kám a pǝ nen mǝyii fur mo, kaa vwang laaɗaa mo, kǝ tuul mo, kǝ ɗaa bòng mo sǝ.
MAR 7:5 Nen Farisi mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar nMosis mo tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe baa jeplep fwaa moo tap kǝ kám kǝ nen mǝyii funu mo kas ye? Har moo se mbiise shi sar ɗe baa mo ɓang kas.>>
MAR 7:6 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wun nen mwaan ndang Naan shi pǝtuup vǝl-vǝl mo. Gyet Aizaya wur satpwoo nkaa wun azeen nǝnee, <Nen ɗesǝ moo shin ɗeɗes nghan a shi mǝshpwoo fur mo. Amma pǝtuup fur mo jong kǝ an.
MAR 7:7 Moo seyil nghan a buu. Kám ɗe moo kám nǝ a Wàar mǝ gurum mo.
MAR 7:8 Wuu yit Wàar Naan, kǝ wu ɗyel a Wàar ɗe gurum moo loot kǝ cìn nǝ.>>
MAR 7:9 Wur sat mmo zak nǝnee, <<Wun kǝ mee ar seen mbe cii Wàar Naan mo, mbǝkǝ wu ɗyel kám fuu mo ɗe.
MAR 7:10 Mosis sat nǝnee, <A shin ɗeɗes mpuun fwaa kǝ nǝǝn fwaa,> Kǝzak nǝnee, <gwar ɗewur satpwoo ɗebish nkaa puun koo nǝǝn wur, ɓe mon ntu wur ating.>
MAR 7:11 Amma wuu kám ngurum mo nǝ, <Katɗang gurum wu kǝ mee mbii ɗe nǝ ret kǝ wu ɓam puun wur ɗe, koo nǝǝn wur shi shik, ɗangɓe wu sat nǝ, nǝ a Korban, (ɗe shii mǝnǝ nnǝ, nǝ a mǝ Naan).
MAR 7:12 Ɓe baa wu kuɗi wuu yit nwur cìn mee mbii mɓe ɓam puun wur ɗe kǝ nǝǝn wur ɗe kas.
MAR 7:13 A mɓe kám fuu ɗesǝ mo, ɓe wuu lepwoo Naan ɗee a mbii ɗebuu, kǝ mbii mo ɗes ɗe wuu cìn mo aasǝ zak.>>
MAR 7:14 Jesu waa baa pet ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu lekom, kǝ wur kǝlǝng mbii ɗe an nsat ɗi, kǝ wur manshii nǝ ɗe zak.
MAR 7:15 Baa mee mbii ɗe gurum kǝ se mpwoo, nǝn nle kǝ gurum ɗee a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan kas, amma a mbii ɗe moo kàa pwat mpwoo gurum, a mǝnǝ moo ke le gurum ɗee a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan.>>
MAR 7:16 Katɗang gwar ɗe kǝ kom mɓe kǝlǝngpee, ɓe wu kǝleng.
MAR 7:17 Kaaɗe Jesu yool yit ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, ɓe wur dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn lu. Ɓe jeplep wur mo tal shii sǝmpwoo mǝnǝ pǝ wur.
MAR 7:18 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Baa wun wu manshii nǝ kas zak aa? Wu man nǝ, koo a mbii ɗeɗangyi ɗe gurum se, ɓe baa nǝn mmak le gurum ɗee a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan kas.
MAR 7:19 Mɓeɗi mbii ɗe gurum se, ɓe baa nii ɗel sham a nɗǝǝn pǝtuup wur kas, amma nii ɗel sham a nɗǝǝn ɓut nwur, ɓe wu ndem kǝn nǝ nɗyes.>> Jesu satpwoo ɗese, a mbǝkǝ wur kám ɗe nǝ, baa mee mbiise mak le gurum ɗee a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan kas.
MAR 7:20 Jesu sat zak nǝnee, <<A mbii ɗe moo kàa pwat nɗǝǝn pǝtuup gurum, a moo le gurum a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan.
MAR 7:21 Mɓeɗi a nɗǝǝn pǝtuup ngurum, ɓe pan ɗebish moo pwat a ɗi. Mbii mo kaa tang mat mo, kǝ wat, kǝ tukáa, kǝ ngaa.
MAR 7:22 Kǝ tǝlǝk, kǝ yaa bǝ pǝtuup, kǝ gwampee, kǝ ciin yaasut, kǝ zuur, kǝ wat sǝm, kǝ ɗyeep kaa, kǝ dak mwen.
MAR 7:23 A mbii ɗebish ɗesi mo jir, ɗe moo pwat nɗǝǝn pǝtuup gurum, a mǝnǝ moo ke le gurum ɗee a mbii ɗebish (nyaknkap) nyit Naan.>>
MAR 7:24 Jesu yool a peemǝnǝ zak, ɓe wur dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nTaya kǝ Sidon. Wur dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn mee lu, ɗe baa wur rǝɓet kǝ mee gurum manpee ɗewur ɗe kas, amma jir kǝsǝ, ɓe gurum mo dǝm yap wur kat.
MAR 7:25 Kaaɗe mee mat, ɗe riin ɗebish nɗǝǝn reep war ɗelee, war kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa Jesu, ɓe abet, war jì taa ntoom wur.
MAR 7:26 Baa mat nǝ war a mat Yahudi kas, war a mat Heleni. Mo làa war a nFonisha, ɗe nǝn nyil nSiriya. War ɗang pǝ Jesu, mbǝkǝ wur ceen riin ɗebish nǝ put mɓut nreep war nǝ.
MAR 7:27 Jesu lap nwar nǝnee, <<Yi yit kǝ mu shin mbiise njeplu mo ǝɓǝl ɗi aku, mbǝɗe baa nǝ ret kǝ mu mang mbiise mǝ jep mo, kǝ mu fwo nǝn as mo kas.>>
MAR 7:28 Amma waa sat nǝ, <<Ii, nǝ aasǝ Daa, amma as nǝ moo se rep pak mbiise ɗe nii ɗong nyil, nder peetong mǝ sese jeplu nǝ mo.>>
MAR 7:29 Jesu sat nwar nǝnee, <<Mbǝ pwoo ɗe yi sat sǝ, ɓe yi dǝm ntul wur-wur, riin ɗebish nǝ kǝ put mɓut nreep fii nǝ.>>
MAR 7:30 Kaaɗe mat nǝ war baa ntul far, ɓe war kat reep war nsaam nkaa mbiisaam. Riin ɗebish nǝ kǝ put nɗǝǝn reep nǝ jee.
MAR 7:31 Jesu yool yit yil nTaya, ɓe wur taa mer nSidon, ɓe wur jì wul am kuur mǝ Galili, nkwang nyil nDikapolis.
MAR 7:32 Mee des mo jì kǝ mee tǝding, ɗe baa wur mak leshap kas pee Jesu ɗe. Mo ɗang pǝ wur, kǝ wur lesar wur ɗi nkaa tǝding nǝ.
MAR 7:33 Mɓut ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, ɓe Jesu yaa tǝding nǝ nsar, dǝm kǝ wur mee kwang coot mbǝshin. Jesu jwal nǝkongsar fin mo nɗǝǝn kom gwar nǝ, kǝ wur ɓwet lii, ɓe wu tung liis gwar nǝ zak.
MAR 7:34 Jesu naapee kaa aɗeng, ɗangɓe wur nook puut, ɓe wur sat ntǝding nǝ shi lǝpwoo mu nenyil Arameek mo nǝnee, <<Iffata>> ɗe shii kǝ mǝnǝ nǝ, <<Wang!>>
MAR 7:35 Ɓe abet, ɓe gwar nǝ kǝlǝngpee, kǝ liis nwur nǝ fween, ɓe wur leshap rǝret.
MAR 7:36 Jesu satpwoo ngurum nǝ mo shiɓal nǝ, taji mo satpwoo nkaa nǝ mmee gurum kas, amma a koppee ɗe mon nɗok tǝtǝk, ɓe mo waa dǝm satpwoo ngurum mo nkaa nǝ ɗes.
MAR 7:37 Nǝ aapwoo ngurum nǝ mo hakyeng, ɗangɓe mo sat nǝnee, <<Wur cìn mbii mo jir a ndǝre-ndǝre. Wur le kǝ komjoor mo kǝlǝngpee, kǝ tǝding mo leshap zak.>>
MAR 8:1 Nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɓe ɗuu gurum nǝ mo waa baa kuur pǝ Jesu ɗi ɗes. Ɓe baa mo kǝ mbiise kas. Jesu pǝrep nen jeplep wur mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee,
MAR 8:2 <<Wen naajeel ɗuu gurum sǝ mo, mbǝɗe mo kǝ cìn teer kun ashak kǝ an nɗesi, ɗang baa mo kuɗi kǝ mbiise kas.
MAR 8:3 Katɗang wen ɓwet mo shindǝm ntul fur mo kǝ neen, ɓe mon ntaa muutleet a ar, mbǝɗe pak mo pwat a mpee ɗejong.>>
MAR 8:4 Jeplep Jesu mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Mun mmak kat mbiise a nneye, a naaryil ɗese, ɗe ɗuu gurum sǝ mon nse kǝ nǝ mak ǝɓǝl mo ɗe ye?>>
MAR 8:5 Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wun kǝ gǝǝl aas mo a kong ye?>> Mo lap nǝnee, <<Mun kǝ gǝǝl aas nǝ mo a pwovǝl.>>
MAR 8:6 Jesu sat nɗuu gurum nǝ mo tong nyil. Ɓe wur mang gǝǝl aas ɗe pwovǝl nǝ mo, wur cin ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan. Ɓe wur yilang gǝǝl aas nǝ mo, wur shin jeplep wur mo, mbǝkǝ mo shwap ɗe ngurum nǝ mo, ɓe jeplep wur nǝ mo shwap ngurum nǝ mo se.
MAR 8:7 Mo kǝ rep pak pupwap mo ɗikǝ lee. Jesu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan nkaa pupwap nǝ mo, ɓe wur shin jeplep wur mo, mbǝkǝ mo shin ɗe ngurum nǝ mo se zak.
MAR 8:8 Ɗuu gurum nǝ mo se, har mo ǝɓǝl jir. Ɗangɓe jeplep Jesu mo kok koor mbiise ɗe nǝ ɗee ɗe, ɓe nǝ gam kǝcik mo pwovǝl.
MAR 8:9 Ɗuu gurum ɗe mo se mbiise nǝ mo wul ngal feer. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe Jesu ɓwet gurum nǝ mo shin waa.
MAR 8:10 Ɓe abet, Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn tii ashak kǝ jeplep wur mo, ɓe mo ɗel dǝm nyil nDalmanuta.
MAR 8:11 Pak nen Farisi mo jì pee Jesu ɗe, ɓe mo ɗoom ɓeetshik kǝ Jesu, mbǝkǝ mo kam wur ɗe. Ɓe mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<A cìn mee mbii aapwoo ɗe nǝ tong aɗeng sham ɗe.>>
MAR 8:12 Ɓe Jesu nook puut kǝ tuup. Wur sat mmo nǝ, <<A me le ɗang gurum ɗe nyiicinsǝ moo rǝɓet naa mee mbii aapwoo ɗe nǝ tong aɗeng sham ye? Azeen, kǝn sat nwun nǝ, baa mon nkám mee mbii aapwoo nen ɗe nyiicinsǝ mo kas.>>
MAR 8:13 Jesu yool yit mo, ɓe wur baa ɗel nɗǝǝn tii am, mbǝkǝ wur can am ɗel dǝm nkor ɗesí.
MAR 8:14 Jeplep Jesu mo munsut mmang gǝǝl aas pan, ɗang ɓe mo kǝ memee mǝndong ɓejee nɗǝǝn tii nǝ.
MAR 8:15 Jesu sat mmo shiɓal nǝnee, <<Wu tap kǝ kám (yist) mǝ nen Farisi mo kǝ mǝ Herot.>>
MAR 8:16 Jeplep wur nǝ mo ɗoom ɓeet ashak, nǝnee, <<Wur sat pwoo mǝnǝ a mbǝɗe baa mun kǝ gǝǝl aas kas.>>
MAR 8:17 Jesu man mbii ɗe moo ɓeet nǝ, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang wuu ɓeet nnǝ, baa wun kǝ gǝǝl aas kas yi? Tan, har yaksǝ ɓe baa wu naashii nǝ kǝ wu man kas aa? Pǝtuup fuu nǝ mo ɗee a ɗeɓal ɗe mo cíi manshii kǝ nǝ me?
MAR 8:18 Wun kǝ yit, mɓe naapee, ɓe baa wu naapee shi shik kas aa? Wun kǝ kom mɓe kǝlǝngpee, ɓe baa wun kǝlǝngpee shi shik kas aa? Wuu munshik ee?
MAR 8:19 Gǝǝl aas ɗepaat sǝ mo, ɗe di an yilang nshin ngurum mo ngal paat mo se sǝ. Ɓe di wu kok koor gǝǝl aas ɗe nǝ ɗee ɗe, ɓe di nǝ gam kǝcik mo a kong ye?>> Mo lap nǝ, <<di nǝ gam kǝcik mo kaapaat baavǝl.>>
MAR 8:20 <<Koo ɗang wuu munshik gǝǝl aas ɗe pwovǝl sǝ mo, ɗe di an yilang nshin ngurum mo ngal feer mo se sǝ ye? Ɓe di wur kok koor gǝǝl aas ɗe nǝ ɗee ɗe, ɓe di nǝ gam kǝcik mo a kong yi?>> Mo lap nǝ, <<di nǝ gam kǝcik mo pwovǝl.>>
MAR 8:21 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<To, ɓe yaksǝ, baa wu manshii nǝ kas aa?>>
MAR 8:22 Mo jì wul mBetseda. Ɓe mee des mo jì kǝ mee nguvum pee Jesu ɗe. Mo ɗang pǝ wur, kǝ wur tung nguvum nǝ ɗi.
MAR 8:23 Ɓe Jesu yaa nguvum nǝ nsar, ɓe wur put kǝ nguvum nǝ aɓwoon laayil nǝ. Kaaɗe Jesu tus lii nkaa yit kǝ nguvum nǝ, ɓe wur lesar wur mo nkaa nguvum nǝ. Ɓe wur tal pǝ nguvum nǝ nǝnee, <<Aa naa mee mbii ye?>>
MAR 8:24 Ɓe nguvum nǝ wur ɗyeep yit, ɓe wur lap nǝnee, <<Ii, wen naa gurum mo, ɗang ɓe nghan naa mo, a kaa tǝng ɗe moo mwaan sǝ.>>
MAR 8:25 Jesu baa lesar fin mo nkaa nyit gwar nǝ, ɓe yit gwar nǝ wang, ɓǝ wur naapee, har wur naa mbii mo rǝret jir.
MAR 8:26 Jesu ɓwet gwar nǝ shindǝm ntul fir, ɗang wur sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<Taji a baa ɗel nɗǝǝn laayil nǝ kas.>>
MAR 8:27 Jesu kǝ jeplep wur mo yool put, ɓe mo dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn jepyil ɗe mo nkwang nSizariya mǝ Filipi. Kaaɗe mo a ar, ɓe Jesu tal pǝ jeplep wur mo nǝnee, <<Gurum moo sat nǝ an a weyi?>>
MAR 8:28 Jeplep nwur mo lap nǝnee, <<Pak gurum nǝ moo sat nǝnee, <gha a Joon ngucìn baptisma,> ɗang pak moo sat zak nǝnee, <gha a Ilaija.> Pak moo sat nǝnee, <gha a memee mɓut nensatpwoo Naan mo.>>
MAR 8:29 Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Amma wun, wuu sat nǝ, nghan a weyi?>> Pita lap nwur nǝ, <<Gha a Kristi.>>
MAR 8:30 Jesu satpwoo mmo shiɓal nǝ, taji mo sat mee pwoo nkaa wuɗi a Kristi Nguɓam ɗe Naan lep kas.
MAR 8:31 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe Jesu ɗoom kám jeplep wur nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Nǝ a tǝng Làa Gurum, wur nshwaajeel mo ɗes shini-shini, kǝzak, nennan-nan mo, kǝ pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, mon chii wur, ɗangɓe mon ntu wur. Ɓe parpuus ɗekun, ɓe wur mbaa yool a peemúut.>>
MAR 8:32 Jesu satpwoo ɗesǝ mmo agaak, ɓe Pita pet Jesu dǝm kǝ wur mmee kwang coot, ɓe wur jǝǝr wur.
MAR 8:33 Amma Jesu ciir naa jeplep wur nǝ mo, ɓe wur sat mPita nǝnee, <<A baku pee an ɗe, gha Shetan! Mɓeɗi baa gha aa pan a mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Naan kas. Amma pan fwaa nǝ a mǝ gurum mo ɓejee.>>
MAR 8:34 Jesu pǝrep ɗuu gurum nǝ mo ashak kǝ jeplep wur nǝ mo, ɓe wu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Katɗang mee gurum rǝɓet jì nɗang an, ɓe naa tǝng wur cii shin kǝ wur ɗakshin ɗe mɓe shwaajeel, nǝn nɗee a kaa wur mang a shiyeepmúut fin, kǝ wur jì ɗe nɗang an sǝ.
MAR 8:35 Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur rǝɓet ɓam seen fir, ɓe nǝn nloom wur, amma koo gwar ɗeɗang ye, ɗewur shin seen fin mbe sǝm fen, kǝ mɓe pwoo ɗeret nǝ zak, ɓe gwar mǝnǝn nkat seen.
MAR 8:36 Gurum nkat a lǝɓet ɗeɗang ye, katɗang wur kat mbii ɗe mǝ yil nǝ mo jir, amma katɗang seen wur loom a wu, ɓe kwoop mbii mǝnǝ mo a meyii?
MAR 8:37 A me a mbii ɗe gurum wu nshin a koppee kǝ seen wur yi?
MAR 8:38 Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗe naashwoop yaa wur mɓe nghan, kǝ kám fen mo nyiicinsǝ, ɗe nǝ a mǝ nenɓutbish mo, kǝ nen ɗe baa mo man Naan kas. Ɓe Làa Gurum, wur ncìn naashwoop kǝ gwar nǝ zak, parpuus ɗe wu njì nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes mǝ puun wur ɗe ashak kǝ nenlep Naan ɗeɓang mo.>>
MAR 9:1 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen nzeen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, pak mo ɗe nɗǝǝn nen ɗe moo ɗirang mpeesǝ, baa mon mmurep kas, naa tǝng mo naa mulki Naan nǝ jì shi mbal akuɗang.>>
MAR 9:2 nƁwoon teer mo peemee, ɓe Jesu mang Pita, kǝ Jemis, kǝ Joon. Wur kàa kǝ mo a mee ɗeng jwak ɗewurang, mon mbusut. Ɓe fwoshik Jesu nǝ cǝǝr nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes wur a yit fur.
MAR 9:3 Nlǝr wur mo cǝǝr ɗee a ɗepiyaa pet-pet, ɗangɓe nǝ mang yit mmo. Baa mee gurum nɗǝǝn yil sǝ mak vwang nlǝr piyaa kaa mǝnǝ sǝ kas.
MAR 9:4 Ɗangɓe jeplep Jesu mo naa Mosis, kǝ Ilaija mon nkaa leshap kǝ Jesu.
MAR 9:5 Ɓe Pita sat nJesu nǝnee, <<Ngukám, nǝ ret kaaɗi mun ɗe mpeesǝ sǝ. A yit kǝ mo ɗyik bìt mo kun, memee gha, memee Mosis, kǝ me ɗi Ilaija.>>
MAR 9:6 Baa Pita man mbii ɗe nwur nsat kas, mbǝɗe kǝǝrmuut nii fes yaa mo.
MAR 9:7 Ɗangɓe nluu jì paa mo, kǝ mo kǝlǝng mee ɗoo nǝ put nɗǝǝn nluu nǝ, ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Ɗesǝ a Làa fen, ɗe wen nwal nwur zam. Wu kǝlǝng wur.>>
MAR 9:8 Abet, kaaɗi mo ciir naapee, ɓe baa mo naa mee gurum kuɗi ashak kǝ mo kas, ɓe a Jesu nbǝshin ɓejee.
MAR 9:9 Kaaɗe mo a ar sham aɗeng jwak nǝ, ɓe Jesu sat mmo shiɓal nǝ, taji mo sat mmee gurum mbii ɗe mo naa kas, naa tǝng Làa Gurum wur yool a peemúut akuɗang.
MAR 9:10 Baa mo sat mbii ɗe mo kǝ naa nǝ mmee gurum kas, amma mo tal peshak nǝnee, <<A me a shii kǝ yool a peemúut nǝ yi?>>
MAR 9:11 Mo tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang nenkám Wàar Mosis mo sat nǝnee, <<Ting Ilaija wur shee jì akuɗang yi?>>
MAR 9:12 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Ilaija wur nshee jì, mbǝkǝ wur ɗak mbii mo ɗe reret jir. Ɓe a me le ɗangɓe mo kǝ ten ran nǝ, Làa Gurum wur nshwaajeel mo ɗes shini-shinǝ mon mɓák wur, kǝ le wur a ɗebuu yi?
MAR 9:13 Amma wen sat nwun nǝ, Ilaija wur kǝ ten jì, kǝ mo kǝ cìn mbii ɗe mo rǝɓet kǝ wur jir, kaaɗi mo kǝ ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nkaa wur sǝ.>>
MAR 9:14 Kaaɗe mo sham wul pee kor jeplep wur nǝ mo ɗe, ɓe mo naa ɗuu gurum mo ɗes pee mo ɗe, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, mo nkaa ɓeetshik kǝ nen mwaan nɗang Jesu nǝ mo.
MAR 9:15 Kaaɗe ɗuu gurum nǝ mo naa Jesu, ɓe nǝ aapwoo mo jir. Abet, ɓe mo shwe dǝm pee wur ɗe, ɓe mo tok kǝ wur.
MAR 9:16 Jesu tal pǝ jeplep wur nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wuu cin a ɓeetshik me kǝ mo yi?>>
MAR 9:17 Ɓe mee gwar mɓut ɗuu gurum nǝ mo wur lap nǝnee, <<Ngukám, wen jì kǝ làa fen pee gha ɗe, mbǝɗe wur kǝ riin ɗebish, ɗe nǝ kǝ cíi leshap nwur.
MAR 9:18 Tong ɓe nii jì yool yaa wur karmat, ɓe nii mang wur shweer nyil, ɗang tǝfil kǝ jì put nwur mpwoo, ɗang wur kǝ sǝm oos, ɗangɓe nii le kǝ fwoshik wur nǝ fii. Wen ɗang pǝ jeplep fwaa mo, mbǝkǝ mo ceen riin ɗebish nǝ put ɗe, amma baa mo mak kas.>>
MAR 9:19 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun nen ɗe nyicinsǝ baa wur shinzeen kas! Wen ntong ashak kǝ wun mɓe vit aa? Wu jì kǝ làa nǝ pee an ɗi.>>
MAR 9:20 Mo jì kǝ làa nǝ pee Jesu ɗi. Kaaɗe riin ɗebish nǝ naa Jesu, ɓe abet nǝ yoon làa nǝ, nǝ mang wur shweer nyil, ɓe làa nǝ wur bǝring nyil, tǝfil jì put nwur mpwoo.
MAR 9:21 Jesu tal pǝ puun làa nǝ nǝnee, <<Mbii ɗesǝ nǝ yaa cìn ɗyem fwaa nǝ a pǝrangyi?>> Puun nǝ wur lap nǝnee, <<Pǝgyet wur kuɗi a làa ɗelee.
MAR 9:22 Nii naa mang wur vwet nɗǝǝn wus, kǝ nɗǝǝn am zak, mbǝkǝ nǝ tu wur ɗi. Amma katɗang gha mak cìn mee mbii, ɓe a naajeel fen, kambok a ɓam mun.>>
MAR 9:23 Jesu sat nwur nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang waa sat nǝnee, <Katɗang wen mak yi?> Ngwar ɗewur shinzeen, ɓe mbii mo jir, mon mmak cìn mɓe wur.>>
MAR 9:24 Abet-abet, ɓe puun làa nǝ wur ɗyeep ɗoo fir nǝnee, <<Wen shinzeen. A ɓam an kǝ ciin shinzeen fen nǝ!>>
MAR 9:25 Kaaɗe Jesu naa ɗes gurum nǝ mo jar jì kus-kus, ɓe wur gwak riin ɗebish nǝ, wur sat nnǝ nǝnee, <<Gha, riin ɗebish ɗe waa cíi leshap kǝ kǝlǝngpee ngurum. Wen sat ngha, a put mɓut nlàa nǝ. Taji a baa ɗel nɗǝǝn làa nǝ zak kas.>>
MAR 9:26 Aɓwoon ɗe riin ɗebish nǝ le or, ɓe nǝ yoon làa nǝ shiɓal, ɓe nǝ mang làa nǝ vwet nyil, ɓe nǝ put. Làa nǝ wur gan nyil kaa wur kǝ mumuut sǝ, ɗangɓe nǝǝn gurum nǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Làa nǝ kǝ muut.>>
MAR 9:27 Amma Jesu yaa sar làa nǝ, wu ɗyeep wur, ɓe làa nǝ yool ɗar atǝng.
MAR 9:28 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn lu, ɓe jeplep wur mo tal pǝ wur coot nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe baa mun mu mak put kǝ riin ɗebish nǝ kas yi?>>
MAR 9:29 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Baa mbii kaa ɗesǝ nǝn mmak put kas, see a shi leshap kǝ Naan. >>
MAR 9:30 Jesu kǝ jeplep wur nǝ mo yool yit peemǝnǝ, ɓe mo yaa ar ɗel nyil nGalili, ɓe baa wur rǝɓet kǝ gurum mo man peeɗi wur ɗe kas.
MAR 9:31 Mɓeɗi wur nkaa kam jeplep wur mo nǝnee, <<Mon nshin Làa Gurum nɗǝǝn sar gurum mo, ɓe mon ntu wur, ɗangɓe a puus ɗekun ɓe wur nyool a peemúut.>>
MAR 9:32 Amma baa jeplep Jesu nǝ mo manshii pwoo mǝnǝ kas, ɗang mo kǝǝr tal nǝ pǝ wur zak.
MAR 9:33 Kaaɗe mo jì wul nyil nKaparnahum, ɓe Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn lu, ɓe wur tal pǝ jeplep wur nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Ɗe wuu ɓeetshik, a nkaa me, a ar sǝ yi?>>
MAR 9:34 Amma mo ɗok tǝtǝk, mbǝɗe mo kǝ ɓeetshik kǝ shak a ar nǝ, a wii a ɗeɗes met jir nɗǝǝn ɗun yi?
MAR 9:35 Jesu tong nyil, ɓe wur pǝrep jeplep wur ɗe kaapaat baavǝl nǝ mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝ, <<Katɗang mee gurum rǝɓet ɗen a ɗenshee, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu ɗee a ɗe aɓwoon, kǝ a wur nɗen a nguɗak niyee mo jir zak.>>
MAR 9:36 Wur pet mee làa ɗelee, ɓe wur le làa nǝ ɗar nnaar fur, ɓe wur mang làa nǝ nsar fin, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee,
MAR 9:37 <<Koo gwar ɗeɗangyii, ɗewur lap mee làa ɗelee kaa ɗesǝ sǝ, nɗǝǝn sǝm fen, ɓe gwar nǝ lap a nghan mmǝnǝ. Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur lap an zak, ɓe baa wur lap a nghan mbǝsen ɓejee kas, amma wur lap a gwar ɗewur lep an shiin ji mmǝnǝ zak.>>
MAR 9:38 Joon sat nwur nǝnee, <<Ngukám ɗe mu naa mee gwar wu nkaa ceen riin ɗebish mo pwat nɗǝǝn gurum mo shi sǝm fwaa, ɓe mǝ cíi nwur, mbǝɗe baa wur a memee nɗǝǝn mun kas.>>
MAR 9:39 Amma Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Taji wu cíi nwur kas. Mɓeɗi baa mee gurum mak cìn mee mbii aapwoo shi sǝm fen, ɗangɓe wur waa ciir satpwoo ɗebish nkaa an kas.
MAR 9:40 Mɓeɗi gwar ɗe baa wur a shaarlek fun kas, ɓe gwar nǝ a munu mmǝnǝ.
MAR 9:41 Azeen nzeen kǝ sat nwun nǝ, koo gwar ɗeɗangyii, ɗewur shin am nwun shwaa, mbǝɗe wun a mu Kristi mo, ɓe gwar mǝnǝn nlap kwat nǝ hakyeng.>>
MAR 9:42 <<Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur le kǝ memee mǝndong nɗǝǝn jep sǝ mo, ɗe mo shinzeen an, mo cìn shikbish, ɓe nǝ nret met kǝ mo ɗyiin mee fin ɗyees ɗak ɗetoon ntook gwar mǝnǝ, kǝ mo vwet wur ɗe nɗǝǝn am kuur.
MAR 9:43 Katɗang sar fwaa nǝ le kǝ a cìn shikbish, ɓe a can nǝ a vwet. Mɓeɗi ngyal ɗesi ɓe a ɗel nɗǝǝn peeseen kǝ sar mǝndong, nǝ ret met aku ɗe mon nvwet gha nɗǝǝn aawus ɗe dǝm ngaa-ngaa, ɓe gha kǝ sar mo vǝl.
MAR 9:44 A peeɗi nyet ɗe moo se gurum mo, baa mon cham murap kas, kǝ baa wus nǝn cham pit ɗe kas zak.
MAR 9:45 Kǝ katɗang ɓe shii fwaa nǝ le kǝ a cìn shikbish, ɓe a can nǝ a vwet. Mɓeɗi ngyal a ɗel nɗǝǝn peeseen shi shii mǝndong, nǝ ret met, aku ɗe mon nvwet gha nɗǝǝn aawus ɗe dǝm ngaa-ngaa ɓe gha kǝ shii mo vǝl.
MAR 9:46 A peeɗi nyet ɗe moo se gurum mo, baa mon cham murap kas, kǝ baa wus nǝn cham pit ɗe kas zak.
MAR 9:47 Kǝ katɗang ɓe yit fwaa nǝ le kǝ a cìn shikbish, ɓe a pun nǝ a vwet. Mɓeɗi ngyal ɗeesi ɓe a ɗel nɗǝǝn mulki mǝ Naan kǝ yit mǝndong, nǝ ret met aku ɗe mon nvwet gha nɗǝǝn aawus ɗe dǝm ngaa-ngaa, ɓe gha kǝ yit mo vǝl.
MAR 9:48 A peeɗi nyet ɗe moo se gurum mo, baa mon cham murap kas, kǝ baa wus nǝn cham pit ɗi kas zak.
MAR 9:49 <<Mon ncìn ɗak shi wus, mbǝkǝ mo le gurum mo pan shee ret ɗe jir, kaaɗi moo le kǝǝn nkaa mbii, mbǝkǝ taji nǝ wam kas sǝ.
MAR 9:50 Kǝǝn nǝ a mbii ɗeret, ɗang ɓe katɗang baa kǝǝn nǝ kuɗi kǝ shang kas, ɓe mon nɗak nǝ a shi me, mbǝkǝ nǝ waa shang ɗe yi? Wun jeplep fen mo, wu tongryang kǝ shak, kaa kǝǝn ɗe baa nii ɓàkshak kǝ shang nǝ kas sǝ.>>
MAR 10:1 Jesu yool yit peemǝnǝ, ɓe wur dǝm nkwang yil nJudiya, wur canɗel nkor Jodan. Ɗuu gurum mo ɗes mo waaji kuur pee wur ɗi, ɗangɓe wur kámpwoo Naan mmo, kaaɗi wur loot kǝ nǝ sǝ.
MAR 10:2 Pak nen Farisi mo jì pee wur ɗi, mbǝkǝ mo kam wur ɗi, ɓe mo tal nǝnee, <<Kyet Wàar Mosis nǝ sat nǝ, gurum mak ceen mat wur mbe koo a mbii ɗebish ɗeɗangyi ɗe war cìn waa?>>
MAR 10:3 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Gyet Mosis ran nnǝ, wur ncìn a meyii?>>
MAR 10:4 Mo lap nǝnee, <<Mosis ran nnǝ, gurum mak ceen mat wur, katɗang wur kǝ ten ran haal mǝ tuɗyik shin nwar.>>
MAR 10:5 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<A mbǝɗe wun a nen cíishik mo, a nǝ le ɗang gyet Mosis ran Wàar ɗesǝ mo nwun.
MAR 10:6 Gyet a Naan wur le mish kǝ mat pugyet ɗe nshee kǝ yil nǝ.
MAR 10:7 <Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe gurum wur nyit puun kǝ nǝǝn wur mo, mbǝkǝ wur ɓalkaa wur ɗe ashak kǝ mat wur.
MAR 10:8 Ɗangɓe mo weet, mon nɗee a nan ɗemǝndong. Aɓwoon ɗese, ɓe baa mo kuɗi a gurum mo vǝl kas, amma moo ɗee a nan ɗemǝndong.>
MAR 10:9 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe nen ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten ɓàl mo ashak, ɓe taji mee gurum ɓàk mo kas.>>
MAR 10:10 Kaaɗe mo ɗel nlu, ɓe jeplep wur mo waa baa tal shii pwoo mǝnǝ ɗe pǝ wur.
MAR 10:11 Ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi wur ceen mat wur, mbǝkǝ wur lap mee mat ɗecì ɗi, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ cìn a ngaa nkaa mat wur ɗe mmǝnǝ.
MAR 10:12 Kǝ katɗang ɓe, mee mat war yit mish war, mbǝkǝ war dǝm ɗyik ɗe mmee gwar ɗecì, ɓe war cìn a ngaa mmǝnǝ.>>
MAR 10:13 Pak gurum mo jì kǝ jep ɗe ɗyeen-ɗyeen mo pee Jesu ɗi, mbǝkǝ wu le ɗeret ɗe nkaa mo shi sar wur, ɓe jeplep wur mo gwak gurum nǝ mo.
MAR 10:14 Amma kaaɗi Jesu naa mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ làa nwur mɓut, ɓe wur sat jeplep mu mo nǝnee, <<Wur yit kǝ jep ɗe ɗyeen-ɗyeen mo jì pee an ɗe, taji wur daam mo kas. Mɓeɗi mulki Naan nǝ a mɓe nen ɗe mo kǝ mǝse kaa mǝ jep ɗe ɗyeen-ɗyeen mo sǝ.
MAR 10:15 Azeen-nzeen sat nwun nǝ, koo weye ɗe baa wur le Naan a ɗeɗes nɗǝǝn pǝtuup wur shi mǝse ɗe nǝ kaa mǝ jep ɗeɗyeen mo sǝ kas, ɓe baa wur mmak ɗel nɗǝǝn mulki Naan kas, koo dǝɓen.>>
MAR 10:16 Ɗangɓe Jesu ghǝr jep nǝ mo nkaa baal wur, ɓe wur le sar nkaa mo, ɗang wur le ɗeret nkaa mo.
MAR 10:17 Kaaɗe Jesu yool put mɓe dǝm, ɓe mee gwar su jì kurum nfurum ntoom wur. Gwar nǝ tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Ngukám ɗeret, an ncìn a ɗak ɗeret ɗeɗang, mbǝkǝ wen kat seen ɗe dǝm ngaa-ngaa ɗe yi?>>
MAR 10:18 Jesu lap nwur nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang a pet an a Ngukám ɗeret yi? Baa mee gurum ɗe a ɗeret kas, see a Naan mbǝshin ɓejee ɗak.
MAR 10:19 Gha man mbii ɗe Wàar Mosis nǝ mo sat jir nǝnee, <Taji a tukáa kas. Taji a cìn ngaa kas. Taji a cìn wat kas. Taji a cìn langtǝng mǝ ɗung nkaa gǝnang fwaa kas. Kǝ taji a seen a gurum mo kas. A shin ɗeɗes mpuun fwaa, kǝ nǝǝn fwaa.> >>
MAR 10:20 Gwar nǝ wur lap nǝnee, <<Ngukám, nghan kǝn ten tap Wàar ɗesǝ mo jir pegyet din kuɗi a làa zǝlang.>>
MAR 10:21 Jesu naa gwar nǝ shi wal, ɓe wur sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<A mbii mǝndong ɗee ɗe nghan ɓejee. A dǝm, a sǝrep long fwaa mo jir, kǝ a ɓàk shool nǝ ɗe nenjeel mo, ɗangɓe waa nkat long nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe a jì nɗang nghan.>>
MAR 10:22 Kaaɗe gwar nǝ wur kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ wàt pǝtuup nwur, ɗangɓe wur waa baa shi pǝtuup ɗewuwat, mbǝɗe wur kǝ long mo ɗes zam.
MAR 10:23 Jesu lyap jeplep wur mo cǝǝrkaat, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Nin nluk, kǝ nenlong mon nɗel nɗǝǝn mulki Naan.>>
MAR 10:24 Kaaɗe jeplep wur mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ aapwoo mmo zam. Jesu baa sat mmo zak nǝnee, <<Jep fen mo, nǝ luk, kǝ gurum wur ɗel nɗǝǝn mulki Naan.
MAR 10:25 Ngyal ɗesǝ ɓe raakumi nkǝlak ɗel nɗǝǝn fung ngilili, met aku ɗe ngulong wur ndel nɗǝǝn mulki Naan.>>
MAR 10:26 Kaaɗe jeplep wur mo waa baa kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ sǝǝt aapwoo mo zam. Ɓe mo sat kǝ shak nǝnee, <<Katɗang mbii nǝ aasǝ, ɓe a wii mmak kat ɓam yi?>>
MAR 10:27 Amma Jesu lyap mo, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Baa gurum mak cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo kas, amma Naan wur mak cìn mbii mo jir.>>
MAR 10:28 Ɗangɓe Pita sat nǝnee, <<A naa, mun kǝ yit mbii mo jir, mbǝkǝ mu dǝm ɗi nɗang gha.>>
MAR 10:29 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen kǝn sat nwun, koo a gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur yit tul, koo ɗyemnǝǝn ɗemish mo, koo ɗyemnǝǝn ɗe mat mo, koo nǝǝn, koo jep mo, koo mmaar, mɓe sǝm fen, kǝ mɓe pwoo ɗeret,
MAR 10:30 ɓe wur nkat tul mo, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn ɗemish mo, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn ɗe mat mo, kǝ nǝǝn mo, kǝ jep mo, kǝ mmaar mo, har mo wul kambil nyiicinsǝ, ashak kǝ shwaajeel, kǝ wur nkat seen ɗe dǝm ngaa-ngaa nɗǝǝn seen ɗe nǝn pǝ jì zak.
MAR 10:31 Pak gurum ɗenshee mo ɗes, mon nyool ɗee a nen ɗe aɓwoon mo. Nen ɗe aɓwoon mon nyool ɗee a nen ɗenshee mo zak.>>
MAR 10:32 Kaaɗe mo a ar kàa nJerusalem, ɓe Jesu táa kyeen mmo ɓe nǝ aapwoo mo, kǝ nǝ lekǝǝrmuut nen ɗe moo dǝm nɗang wur nǝ mo. Ɓe Jesu pǝrep jeplep wur ɗe kaapaat baavǝl nǝ mo, dǝm mmee kwang mbǝsut, ɓe wur sat mmo mbii ɗe mon nkàa cìn nwur nJerusalem.
MAR 10:33 Nǝnee, <<Wu naa, mun a ar kàa nJerusalem nɗesi, katɗang mu wul, ɓe mon nseet Làa Gurum nɗǝǝn sar pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nen kám Wàar kǝ Mosis mo, ɗang mon ncanɗyeel muut nwur. Mon nshin wur nsar nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas.
MAR 10:34 Kǝ mon nshwar wur, mon ntwas lii nkaa wur. Mon nfwo nɓwat nwur, mon ntu wur zak, ɗangɓe parpuus ɗekun, ɓe wur nyool a peemúut.>>
MAR 10:35 Ɗangɓe Jemis kǝ Joon, jep Zeɓeɗi mo, mo jì pee Jesu ɗi, ɓe mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Ngukám, muu rǝɓet kǝ koo a meye ɗi mu ɗang pǝ gha ɓe a cin mmun.>>
MAR 10:36 Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wuu rǝɓet kǝ wen cin a me nwun ye?>>
MAR 10:37 Mo lap nwur nǝnee, <<Katɗang a rǝɓet, ɓe parɗe ghan ntong nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes fwaa, ɓe a le kǝ mun mu tong ashak kǝ gha, memee nsarse fwaa, kǝ memee nsarkul fwaa zak.>>
MAR 10:38 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Baa wur man mbii ɗe wuu ɗang nǝ kas. Wun mmak shwaajeel ɗe nghan nshwaa nǝ aa? Wun mmak lap baptisma ɗe mon ncìn nghan nǝ aa?
MAR 10:39 Mo lap nǝnee, <<Ii mun mmak.>> Ɗangɓe Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen wun mmak nshwaajeel ɗe wen nshwaa nǝ, kǝ baptisma ɗe mon ncìn nghan nǝ.
MAR 10:40 Amma mbe shin pee nwun tong nsarse fen, kǝ nsarkul fen, baa an kǝ ɓal ɗe an ncin mǝnǝ nwun kas. Amma nǝ a mɓee nen ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten ɗak nǝ le mbe mo.>>
MAR 10:41 Kaaɗe jeplep wur ɗe kaapaat sǝ mo kǝlǝng ɗang mǝnǝ, ɓe mo langtuup kǝ Jemis kǝ Joon.
MAR 10:42 Jesu pǝrep mo jì ashak jir, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu man nǝ, a mishkom nen ɗe baa mo a nenyil Yahudi mo kas, moo lesut fur mo a ɗeɗes nkaa nen fur mo, kǝ nennan fur mo, moo kám iiko fur mo zam, nkaa gurum nǝ mo.
MAR 10:43 Amma baa nǝn nɗen nnaar fuu aasǝ kas. Koo gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur yool ɗee a ɗeɗes nnaar fuu, ɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ wur sham kǝ káa wur, mbe cìn ɗak nwun.
MAR 10:44 Kǝ koo gwar ye ɗewur rǝɓet ɗee a ɗenshee nɗǝǝn wun, ɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ wur ɗee a kǝrem fuu jir.
MAR 10:45 Baa Làa Gurum wur jì a mbǝkǝ gurum mo cìn ɗak ɗe nwur kas, amma a mbǝkǝ wur cìn ɗak ɗe ngurum mo, kǝ wur shin seen fir ɗi mbe ang gurum mo ɗes zak.>>
MAR 10:46 Mo jì wul nJeriko, ɓe kaaɗi Jesu a ar put nɗǝǝn Jeriko nǝ, ashak kǝ jeplep wur mo, kǝ ɗuu kǝ gurum mo ɗes. Ɓe mee nguvum ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Bartimawus làa Timawus, wur kǝ tong a pwoo ar mbe ɗang-ɗang.
MAR 10:47 Kaaɗe nguvum nǝ wur kǝlǝng nǝ, a Jesu ngu Nazaret, ɓe wur yaa ɗyeep ɗoo shiɓal nǝnee, <<Jesu, Làa Devit, a naajeel fen!>>
MAR 10:48 Gurum mo ɗes mo gwak wur, ɓǝ mo sat nwur ɗok kǝtǝk. Dang ɓe wur waa sǝǝt ɗyeep ɗoo ɓalɓal nǝnee, <<Làa Devit, a naajeel fen.>>
MAR 10:49 Jesu ɗar, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu pet wur shin ji.>> Ɗangɓe mo pet nguvum nǝ, mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa gha kas. A yool, Jesu kǝ pet gha.>>
MAR 10:50 Nguvum nǝ wur vwet mbiisǝp wur, ɓe wur sham yool wuret, dǝm pee Jesu ɗe.
MAR 10:51 Jesu tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Aa rǝɓet kǝ nghan cìn a me nghan ye?>> Nguvum nǝ wur lap nǝnee, <<Ngukám, a le kǝ yit fen mo naapee.>>
MAR 10:52 Jesu sat nwur nǝnee, <<To yit fwaa mo naapee ɗak, mbǝɗe waa shinzeen nnǝ an mbar gha.>> Abet-abet, ɓe yit wur nǝ mo naapee. Ɓe wur dǝm nɗang Jesu, kǝ wur shin ɗeɗes nNaan.
MAR 11:1 Kaaɗe mo jì wul kus kǝ Jerusalem, ɓe mo jì wul mBetfaji, kǝ Betani mǝ Jwakpaat. Ɓe Jesu lep jeplep fir mo vǝl.
MAR 11:2 Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wur dǝm nɗǝǝn laayil ɗe nǝ a kyeen fuu sǝ. Katɗang wu wul, ɓe abet, wun nkat mee làa jaaki ɗe a ɗiɗiin, ɗe baa mee gurum kǝ cam lang nkaa nǝ kas. Ɓe wur shang wur jì kǝ nǝ mpesi.
MAR 11:3 Katɗang mee gurum tal pǝ wun nǝnee, <A me le ɗang wuu shang jaaki nǝ yi?> Ɓe wur sat nǝ, a Daa wur kǝ rǝɓet nǝ. Aɓwoon ɓe wu mbaa lep nǝ shi jì abet.> >>
MAR 11:4 Mo dǝm kat làa jaaki nǝ a ɗiɗiin mpolu kus kǝ pwoo ar. Kaaɗe mo yaa shang nǝ,
MAR 11:5 ɓe nen ɗe moo ɗar ɗe a pee nǝ, mo sat nǝnee, <<A me le ɗang wuu shang làa jaaki nǝ yi?>>
MAR 11:6 Ɓe jeplep nǝ mo lap nciit kǝ mbii ɗe Jesu sat mmo. Ɗangɓe nenjaaki nǝ mo yit mmo dǝm ɗe kǝ nǝ.
MAR 11:7 Kaaɗe jeplep nǝ mo jì kǝ làa jaaki nǝn Jesu, ɓe mo le nlǝr fur mo nkaa jaaki nǝ, ɓe Jesu lang nkaa nǝ.
MAR 11:8 Gurum mo ɗes mo paa ar nǝ shi nlǝr fur mo, ɓǝ pak mo saa kom kǝkar mɓut mmaar mo, mo paa ar nǝ shi-shik zak.
MAR 11:9 Nen ɗe mo akyeen, kǝ ɗe mon mɓwoon Jesu, mo ɗyeep ɗoo fur mo sat nǝnee, <<Hosana! Daa le ɗeret nkaa gwar ɗewur jì nɗǝǝn sǝm Daa!
MAR 11:10 Naan le ɗeret nkaa mulki ɗe mu puun fun Devit nǝ, nii jì wul. Hosana Naan nɗǝǝn mulki fin.>>
MAR 11:11 Kaaɗe Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn Jerusalem, ɓe wur ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ. Ɓe wur naa mbii mo ɗe nɗǝǝn Lu Naan nǝ jir. Kaaɗe kansǝǝn kǝ ten cìn, ɓe wur put dǝm nBetani ashak kǝ jeplep wur ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo.
MAR 11:12 Daɗaar nǝ, ɓe kaaɗi mo kǝ yool yit Betani nǝ, ɓe neenláa nJesu.
MAR 11:13 Kaaɗe wur naa mee tǝngkyeen kǝ ɗee jong, ɗe nǝ lǝhǝt kǝ kom zam, ɓe wur dǝm mbe naa tǝngkyeen nǝ, kyet nii mee làa mo wa, ɗangɓǝ wur kat nii lǝhǝt aa kompee ɓejee ɗak, mbǝɗe baa a tar làa mǝ keen nǝ kas.
MAR 11:14 Jesu sat ntǝngkyeen nǝ nǝnee, <<Taji mee gurum kuɗi kǝ se làa kyeen mɓut wii zak kas.>> Jeplep wur mo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗewur sat ntǝngkyeen nǝ.
MAR 11:15 Kaaɗe mo jì wul nJerusalem. Ɓe Jesu ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, wur yaa ceen nenwer mo, kǝ nenseet mbii mo nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ. Wur bǝrep teebul mǝ nen pǝring shool mo, kǝ mbii tong mǝ nensǝrep mbul mo.
MAR 11:16 Baa wur yit kǝ mee gurum mang mee mbii ji ɗel seet kǝnǝ afur nɗǝǝn lu Naan nǝ kas zak.
MAR 11:17 Wur kám ngurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Nǝ a rǝran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <Mon mpet lu fen a lu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mbe gurum ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir,> amma wun kǝ ciir kǝ ni, kǝ nǝ ɗee a gwoot mu nwat mo.>>
MAR 11:18 Kaaɗe pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe mo tang ar ɗe mon ntu Jesu ɗe. Amma mo kǝǝr wur, mbǝɗe kám wur nǝ aapwoo nɗuu gurum nǝ mo jir.
MAR 11:19 Kaaɗe kansǝǝn cìn, ɓe Jesu kǝ jeplep fir mo, mo pwat yit yilkaam nǝ.
MAR 11:20 Daɗar mɓít, ɓe kaaɗi mo a ar ɗel, ɓe mo taa naa tǝngkyeen nǝ kǝ fii sham put jir.
MAR 11:21 Kaaɗe Pita panpwoo ɗe doon Jesu sat ntǝngkyeen nǝ, ɓe wur sat nJesu nǝnee, <<Ngukám, a naa tǝngkyeen ɗe doon a le ɗoor sí, nǝ kǝ fii jee.>>
MAR 11:22 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu shinzeen nNaan.
MAR 11:23 Ɓe azeen-nzeen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, koo a gwar ɗeɗangyi ɗewur sat njwak ɗesǝ nǝnee, <A yool a sham a taa nɗǝǝn am kuur sǝ.> Katɗang baa gwar nǝ sat pwoo mǝnǝ a shi pǝtuup vǝl kas, amma gwar nǝ shinzeen nǝ, mbii ɗewur sat nǝn ncìn, ɓe nǝn ncìn.
MAR 11:24 A mpeemǝnǝ, ɓe wen sat nwun nǝ, koo mbii ɗeɗangyi ɗe wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe nǝ, ɗang wur shinzeen nǝ, wuu ten wur lap mbii ɗewur ɗang nǝ, ɓe Naan wur nshin nwun.
MAR 11:25 Kǝ koo a pǝrangye ɗe wu yaa chìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), ɓe wur fwo shikbish ɗe gurum mo cìn nwun, mbǝkǝ Naan puun fuu ɗe aɗeng wur fwo shikbish fuu mo ɗe nwun zak.
MAR 11:26 Mɓeɗi katɗang baa wur fwo shikbish ɗe gurum mo cìn nwun kas, ɓe baa Naan puun fuu ɗe aɗeng wur nfwo shikbish fuu mo wun kas zak.
MAR 11:27 Mo waaji nJerusalem, ɓe kaaɗi Jesu nkaa mwaan nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɓe pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, kǝ nennan-nan mo, mo jì pee wur ɗi.
MAR 11:28 Ɓe mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Waa aa cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo a shi iiko ɗeɗangyii? A wii shin iiko ɗesǝ nwaa yi?>>
MAR 11:29 Jesu lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wen kǝn rǝɓet tal mee mbii pǝ wun ɗe zak. Katɗang wu lap nghan, ɓe an nsat nwun iiko ɗe nghan kǝn cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo shi shik zak.
MAR 11:30 Kyet gyet a Naan lep Joon mbǝkǝ wu jì cìn baptisma ɗe ngurum mo aa? Aa koo gyet a gurum mo lep wu yi? Wu lap nghan.>>
MAR 11:31 Mo ɓeet ɓwet nshak nǝnee, <<Katɗang mu sat nǝ, Gyet a Naan lep wur shin ji, ɓe wur nsat nǝnee, <A me le ɗang baa gyet wu shinzeen nwur kas ye?>
MAR 11:32 Ɗangɓe katɗang mu sat nǝ, gyet a gurum lep Joon jì, ɓe gurum nǝ mon nlangtuup.>> Moo kǝǝr gurum mo, mbǝɗe gurum nǝ mo jir moo le Joon a ngusatpwoo Naan.
MAR 11:33 Ɗangɓe mo lap nJesu nǝnee, <<Baa mu man kas.>> Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe baa wen nsat nwun gwar ɗe shin iiko nghan, mɓe cìn mbii aapwoo nǝ mo kas zak.>>
MAR 12:1 Jesu ɗoom sat pwoo ngurum mo shi sǝmpwoo mo nǝnee, <<Gyet mee ngulu wur kop anab mo mbong wur, ɓe wur neer nǝ shi kok, wur ɓwan mee tuun mɓe ɗwat làa tǝng anab nǝ, kǝzak, wur ɗyik mee ɗengpee mɓe naa anab nǝ. Ɗangɓe wur yit mar nǝ nsar mee kǝ nennaa mar mo, mbǝkǝ mo naa bong nǝ ɗe nwur. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe wur yool dǝm mmee yil.
MAR 12:2 Kaaɗe tar nung làa anab nǝ wul, ɓe wur lep mee kǝrem nwur dǝm pee nennaa maar anab nǝ mo ɗe, mbǝkǝ kǝrem lap pak làa anab nǝ dǝm kǝ nǝ ɗe nwur.
MAR 12:3 Ɗangɓe nennaa maar anab nǝ mo yaa kǝrem ni, mo nǝram wur, ɓe mo ceen wur baa shi sar ɗe nfii.
MAR 12:4 Ngulu nǝ wur waa baa lep mee kǝrem shiin dǝm pee mo ɗe zak. Ɓe mo nas wur nkáa, kǝ mo shínjeel nkǝrem mǝnǝ zak.
MAR 12:5 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe ngulu nǝ wu waa baa lep mee kǝrem dǝm pee nennaa mar nǝ mo zak, ɓe mo yaa kǝrem mǝnǝ tu, kǝ moo naa ncìn mpak kǝrem nǝ mo aasǝ zak, har mo nǝram pak mo, kǝ mo twe pak mo.
MAR 12:6 Ngulu nǝ wur ɗee ɗe kǝ memee mǝndong, ɗe mǝnǝ a làa wur ɗewur nwal nlàa nǝ zam. Ɓe wur lep làa nǝ dǝm pee nennaa bong nǝ mo ɗe, aɓwoon kǝ kǝrem nǝ mo jir. Ngulu nǝ wur pan nǝnee, <Nentap maar nǝ mon naa ɗeɗes kǝ làa fin.>
MAR 12:7 Ɗangɓe nennaa maar nǝ mo sat nshak nǝnee, <wu naa a làa ɗe mǝnǝn nyool ghǝr kop puun nǝ nɗesi, wu jì mmun, kǝ mǝ tu wur, mbǝkǝ kop nǝ ɗee ɗe a munu.>
MAR 12:8 Ɗangɓe mo yaa làa nǝ tu, ɓe mo vwet kúm nǝ shin ciir mɓwoon kok maar nǝ.
MAR 12:9 Wur pan nǝ, ngumaar nǝ wur ncìn a me kǝ nennaa maar ɗesǝ nǝ mo ye? Wun njì twe nennaa mar ɗesǝ nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ wur le mee nennaa mar ɗecì mo ɗi.
MAR 12:10 Baa wuu cam tang pwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ kas me? Ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<nGhǝk ɗe nen ɗyiklu mo cii nǝ, <<Ɓe a nǝ ɗee a ɗeɗes nɗǝǝn kwang lu nǝ.
MAR 12:11 Ɗesǝ nǝ a ɗak ɗe Daa wur kǝ ten cìn; <<Nǝ a mbii aapwoo pee mun ɗi!> >>
MAR 12:12 Nennan mǝ nen Yahudi mo yappee mɓe yaa Jesu, mbǝɗe mo man nǝ, wur sat sǝmpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ a nkaa mo, ɗangɓǝ baa mo mak yaa wur kas, mbǝɗe mo kǝǝr ɗuu gurum nǝ mo. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe mo yool yit wur ɗe, ɓe mo dǝm ntul.
MAR 12:13 Ɗangɓe nen Farisi mo kǝ nen nHerot mo lep pak nen fur mo shindǝm pee Jesu ɗe, mbǝkǝ mo kat mee mbii ɗe mon nyaa wur ɗi nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗewur sat mo.
MAR 12:14 Kaaɗe mo jì, ɓe mo sat nJesu nǝnee, <<Ngukám, mu man nǝ, gha a nguzeen, baa waa kǝ kak mee gurum kas, ɗang baa waa kǝ shangyit mmee gurum kas zak, ɗangɓǝ gha aa kám ar Naan ngurum mo azeen-nzeen. Kyet nǝn ndere kǝ mu kwatwap Siza, mishkoom ɗeɗes mu nen Rom mo aa, koo mu nook kwat nǝ yi?>>
MAR 12:15 Ɗangɓe mbǝɗe Jesu man pan ɗebish mǝ pǝtuup fur mo, ɓe wur lap mmo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe wuu kam nghan yi? Wu jì kǝ mee shool zinariya nǝ nghan naa.>>
MAR 12:16 Ɓe mo jì kǝ memee nwur. Ɓe Jesu tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<A mǝ riin mukáa, kǝ sǝm mu we, a rǝran nkaa shool nǝ yi?>> Mo lap nǝnee, <<A mǝ Siza mishkoom nRom.>>
MAR 12:17 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu shin nSiza mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Siza, kǝ wu shin Naan mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Naan zak.>> Nǝ aapwoo mmo zam mɓe mbii ɗewur sat nǝ.
MAR 12:18 Pak nen Saddusi mo, nen ɗe moo sat nǝ, baa mee yool a peemúut ɗe kas, mo jì pee Jesu ɗe, ɓe mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee,
MAR 12:19 <<Ngukám, Mosis kǝ ran mmun nǝ, katɗang mee gurum muut seet yit mat wur ɗi, ɗe baa war làa-làa nwur kas, ɓe nnǝ mee ɗyemnǝǝn wur lap matkaa nǝ, mbǝkǝ wur làa-làa mo ɗe nɗyemnǝǝn fin ɗe wu kǝ ten muut nǝ.
MAR 12:20 Gyet mee ɗyemnǝǝnshak mo ɗe pwovǝl. Gwar ɗenshee nǝ wur lapmat, ɓe wur muut nɗin nlàa mee làa.
MAR 12:21 Ɓe ɗyemnǝǝn fin ɗevǝl nǝ wur lap matkaa nǝ, ɓe baa wur làa mee làa kas, ɗang wur jì muut. Gwar ɗekun nǝ wur waa lap matkaa nǝ war zak.
MAR 12:22 Ɗang mo pwovǝl, mo lapmat nǝ war, ɓǝ mo jì murǝp jir, ɓe baa memee yit mee làa ɗee ɗe kas. Kyes nǝ, ɓe mat nǝ war yool muut aɓwoon kǝ mo nǝ jir zak.
MAR 12:23 To, katɗang parpuus yool a peemúut, ɓe war kǝ nɗee a mat we nɗǝǝn mo pwovǝl sǝ ye? Mɓeɗi mo jir, mo kǝ lap war mmat.>>
MAR 12:24 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun wuu ɗel ɗikǝ, mbǝɗe baa wu man mbii ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan kas, kǝ baa wu man ɗeɗes Naan kas zak.
MAR 12:25 Mɓeɗi parpuus ɗe nen nǝ mon nyool a peemúut, ɓe mon nɗee a kaa nenlep Naan ɗe aɗeng mo sǝ. Baa mee lapmat, koo dǝmɗyik ɗe kas.
MAR 12:26 Pwoo nkaa yool a peemúut mǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ ten murǝp mo, ɓe baa wuu kam tang pwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nǝ nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Mosis kas aa? Mbii ɗe Naan sat nwur nɗǝǝn làa lǝǝt ɗe nǝ lapwus sí nǝ, <Wen a Naan kǝ Abraham, kǝ Naan Aizik, kǝ Naan kǝ Jekop.>
MAR 12:27 Baa wur a Naan mu nenmuut mo kas, amma a mǝ nen ɗe mmeen mo. (Ɗesǝ nǝ kám nǝ koo ɗe mo kǝ ten murap ɓe mo ɗe kǝ seen pee Naan.) Wun wu ɗel ɗikǝ bish-bish hakyeng!>>
MAR 12:28 Mee gwar mɓut nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, wur jì kǝlǝng mo nkaa ɓeetshik nǝ, ɓe wur kǝlǝng Jesu tap lappwoo nǝ nen Saddusi mo rǝret. Ɓe wur tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<A Wàar ɗeɗang a ɗeɗes met jir nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ mo yi?>>
MAR 12:29 Jesu lap nwur nǝnee, <<A Wàar ɗeɗes met nǝ nɗesi, <Wun nen Isreil mo, wur kǝleng. Daa Naan fun, a wur a Daa mǝndong ɓejee.
MAR 12:30 A wal nDaa Naan fwaa shi pǝtuup fwaa jir, shi seen fwaa jir, kǝ shi pan fwaa jir, kǝ shiɓal fwaa jir.>
MAR 12:31 Ɗe vǝl nǝ a kaa mǝnǝ sǝ zak nǝnee, <A wal ngǝnang fwaa kaa sak fwaa sǝ.> Baa mee Wàar ɗe waa ɗes met ɗe vǝl sǝ mo kas.>>
MAR 12:32 Ngukám Wàar Mosis nǝ wur sat nJesu nǝnee, <<Azeen Ngukám, a sat a rǝret. Daa Naan wur a mǝndong ɓejee ɗak, baa memee ɗe kas, see a wur mbǝshin.
MAR 12:33 Kǝ nǝ a tǝng kǝ gurum nwal nwur shi pǝtuup fin jir, kǝ shi pan fin jir, kǝ shiɓal fin jir, kǝ gurum nwal ngǝnǝǝn fin kaa shin fin sǝ zak. Wàar ɗe vǝl sǝ mo ret met nlong ɗe gurum moo shin mbe wus mbiizuum, kǝ koor mbiizuum ɗe gurum moo shin mon nNaan jir.>>
MAR 12:34 Kaaɗe Jesu kǝlǝng gwar nǝ tap lappwoo nǝ rǝret, ɓe wur sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<Baa waa jong kǝ mulki Naan kas.>> Aɓwoon ɗesǝ ɓe baa mee gurum mak katɓal mputuup mɓe tal mee pwoo ɗe pǝ Jesu zak kas.
MAR 12:35 Kaaɗe Jesu nkaa kam-kam ngurum mo nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɓe wur tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe nenkám Wàar Mosis moo sat nǝ, <Kristi wur a làa Devit ye?>
MAR 12:36 Mɓeɗi Riin Naan nǝ le kǝ Devit shikáa fin wu sat nǝnee, <Daa wu sat nDaa fen nǝ, A tong nsarse fen. Har parɗi wen le shaarlek fwaa mo tong nder shii fwaa.>
MAR 12:37 Devit pet Kristi a Daa fin, ɓe cirang ɗang Kristi wu waa ciir ɗee a Làa Devit zak ye?>> Ɗuu gurum nǝ mo kǝlǝng wur shi retnyit.
MAR 12:38 nƊǝǝn kám Jesu, ɓe wur sat ngurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wu tap kǝ kam nenkám Wàar Mosis mo. Mo a nen ɗe moo jwal nlǝr ɗeshwal-shwal mo, kǝ moo mwaan mbǝkǝ gurum mo naa mo ɗi. Moo rǝɓet kǝ gurum mo tok kǝ mo nɗǝǝn lutuk.
MAR 12:39 Kǝ moo rǝɓet peetong mǝ nennan-nan mo nɗǝǝn lu Naan mo, kǝ moo rǝɓet peetong ɗeret met jir mo a pee serǝɓet mo.
MAR 12:40 A moo yak matkaa mo kǝ lee fur mo, kǝ moo ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) ɗeshwal-shwal mo shi nyang zak, mbǝkǝ gurum mo kwoop mo ɗi. Mɓee mbii ɗebish ɗe moo cìn ɗesǝ mo, ɓe Naan wur ncin kwat ɗeshwal mo ɗes hakyeng.>>
MAR 12:41 Kaaɗe Jesu tong a kyeen, kus kǝ pee ɓwet shool mbiizuum mǝ Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓe wur naa kaaɗi gurum moo ɓwet shool mbiizuum fur mo ɗe nɗǝǝn nǝ. Pak nenlong mo ɗes mo ɓwet shool ɗes nɗǝǝn nǝ.
MAR 12:42 Ɓe mee matkaa ɗe war a matjeel waa jì ɓwet rep anini mo vǝl ɗe nɗǝǝn nǝ zak.
MAR 12:43 Jesu pǝrep jeplep wur nǝ mo jì ashak, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen kǝn sat nwun, mbii ɗe matkaa ɗejeel ɗesǝ waa ɓwet nɗǝǝn kwati mǝ ɓwet mbiizuum nǝ, nǝ met mǝ koor gurum nǝ mo jir.
MAR 12:44 Mɓeɗi nen ɗesǝ mo jir, mo ɓwet mbiizuum nǝ a mɓut nɗes mǝ long ɗe mo kǝni, ɗangɓǝ war nɗǝǝn jeel war, ɓe war sǝhǝt ɓwet a kyes kǝ mbii ɗe war kǝ nǝ.>>
MAR 13:1 Kaaɗe Jesu a ar put nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓe memee mɓut jeplep nwur mo sat nǝnee, <<Koi, Ngukám, a naa lu ɗeret ɗe mo tap ɗyik mo shi nghǝk ɗenan-nan sǝ mo.>>
MAR 13:2 Jesu lap nǝnee, <<Aa naa a lu ɗe mo ɗyik mo nan-nan shi nghǝk sǝ mo aa? Baa mon nyit mee nghǝk tong nkaa nghǝk mpee ɗesǝ kas, amma mon nshirip mo jir.>>
MAR 13:3 Kaaɗe Jesu tong nkaa Jwakpaat ɗe nii naa shak kǝ Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɓe Pita, kǝ Jemis, kǝ Joon, kǝ Andru, mo jì tal pǝ wur a sǝsok, mo sat nwur nǝnee,
MAR 13:4 <<A sat mmun, mbii ɗesǝ mon yool cìn a pǝrangyi? Kǝ mun nnaa a mbii aapwoo ɗeɗang, katɗang mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗoom gam yi?>>
MAR 13:5 Jesu ɗoom sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu tap, taji mee gurum ngwam wun kas.
MAR 13:6 Mɓeɗi gurum mo ɗes mon njì nɗǝǝn sǝm fen, kǝ mo sat nǝ, wuɗun a wen, ɗangɓe mon ngwam gurum mo ɗes.
MAR 13:7 Katɗang ɓe wu kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa lek mo, kǝ pwoo kyetwa nkaa lek mo, ɓe taji kǝǝrmuut yaa wun kas, mbǝɗe nǝ atǝng mbii ɗesǝ mon nyool cìn akuɗang, ɓe parkyes yil nii kuɗi kǝ jì.
MAR 13:8 Pak yil mon nyool lek nkaa pak yil mo, kǝ mee mulki mon nyool lek nkaa mee mulki ɗecì mo. Yil nǝn ntungpee ɗes-ɗes shipee-shipee, neen nǝn ntaa, nɗǝǝn yil nǝ mo. Ɗangɓe mbii ɗesǝ mo jir a shee kǝ jeel, kaaɗi aak kǝ shee se mat sǝ.
MAR 13:9 <<Ɗangɓe wu tap kǝ káa fuu, mbǝɗe gurum mon nyool sǝrep wun nsar kǝ nentokɗyeel mo, kǝ mon nnǝram wun nɗǝǝn lu Naan mo. Mon ndǝm kǝ wun ntoom gofna, kǝ mishkoom mo, mbe sǝm fen. Ɗesǝ nǝn nle kǝ wun katpee satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗe ntoom mo.
MAR 13:10 Ɗangɓe akuɗang kyes kǝ yil nii jì, ɓe tǝng see mo shee satpwoo Naan ɗeret sǝ ngurum mo jir nɗǝǝn yil nǝ akuɗang.
MAR 13:11 Katɗang ɓe mo yak wun, kǝ mo dǝm kǝ wun nluɗyeel ɓe taji wu an suk mbe mbii ɗe wun nsat kas. Mɓeɗi a Riin Naan wur nkám wun mbii ɗe wun nsat mo. Mɓeɗi baa a wun nkaa satpwoo nǝ kas, amma a Riin Naan wur nkaa satpwoo nǝ.
MAR 13:12 Ɗyemnǝǝnshak mon nsǝrep shak har mpee muut, ɓǝ puun wur nseet làa fin zak. Jep mon nyool lek kǝ puun fur mo, kǝ nǝǝn wu mo, ɓe mon nle kǝ mo twe mo.
MAR 13:13 Gurum mon ncii wun jir, mɓe sǝm fen. Ɗangɓe gwar ɗe wu gung har peekyes nǝ, ɓe a wur nkat ɓam.>>
MAR 13:14 <<Ɗangɓe katɗang wu naa mbii ɗebish, ɗe nii watpee ɗee buu, nii ɗar a peeɗi baa nǝ ret kǝ nǝ ɗar ɗe kas. (Ngwar ɗewur tang pwoo ɗesǝ ni, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu manshii nǝ). Ɓe nenyil ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Judiya, mo swe dǝm mɓut jwak mo.
MAR 13:15 Ngwar ɗewur nkaa ɗeng lu, ɓe taji wu sham ɗel nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, mɓe mang lée fin mo kas.
MAR 13:16 Kǝ gwar ɗewur a peemaar a yil, ɓe taji wu waa baa ntul mbǝ mang mbiisǝp fin kas.
MAR 13:17 Amma jeel nǝn nsǝǝt naat nkaa mat aak mo, kǝ mat ɗe mon nkaa shin wur njep mo nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo.
MAR 13:18 Wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nNaan, mbǝkǝ taji mbii ɗesǝ mo cìn a ntarkut kas.
MAR 13:19 Mɓeɗi jeel ɗeɗes nǝn njì taa nkaa gurum mo nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɗe baa mo kǝ cam naa nǝ kas, pǝgyet Naan shee leyil nǝ ɗe, har cicinsi, kǝ baa gurum mon mbaa naajeel mǝnǝ ɗe zak kas har ngaa-ngaa.
MAR 13:20 Katɗang ɗe baa Daa Naan wur baa kǝ pak teer nǝ mo kas, ɓe baa ɗe mee gurum mmak kat bar kas, amma a mɓe sǝm kǝ nen ɗebǝbǝlǝp nǝ mo, ɓe Naan wur baa kǝ pak teer nǝ mo.
MAR 13:21 <<Katɗang mee gurum sat nwun nǝnee, <Wu naa, Kristi wu mpesi.> Koo ɗang nnǝ, <wu naa, wur akyeen sí!> Ɓe taji wu shinzeen mpwoo mǝnǝ kas.
MAR 13:22 Mɓeɗi nen ɗe mon ncìn ɗung, nnǝ wuɗun a Kristi, kǝ nen ɗe mo lesut a kaa nensatpwoo Naan mo sǝ, ɗangɓǝ mo a nenɗung mo, mon njì put ɗes. Mon ncìn mbii aapwoo mo ɗes, kǝ mbii lukshik mo zak. Mbeekǝ katɗang nǝ mak cìn, ɓe mo ngwam nen ɗe Naan wu kǝ ten bǝlǝp mo.
MAR 13:23 Amma wu tap kǝ káa fuu mo. Wen kǝn satpwoo ɗesǝ mo nwun nshee akuɗang pee nii wul.>>
MAR 13:24 <<Aɓwoon kǝ jeel mǝnǝ mo, ɓe puus nǝn ncǝǝr ɗee a peenkoo, kǝ baa tar nǝn mɓangpee kas, nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo.
MAR 13:25 Kǝ zar ɗe aɗeng mon mɓeer sham nyil, kǝ iiko ɗe mo aɗeng mon ntungpee zak.
MAR 13:26 Ɗangɓe gurum mon naa Làa Gurum, wur sham put nɗǝǝn nluu ɗe aɗeng, shi iiko kǝ Ɗehai, kǝ ɓal ɗǝɗes.
MAR 13:27 Ɓe wur nlep nenlep Naan mo, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm kok nen ɗewur kǝ ten bǝlǝp mo kuur ashak, nɗǝǝn kwang ɗe feer mǝ yil nǝ. Yaa mpeeɗar kǝ yil nǝ jir, ɓe dǝm wul mpeeɗar kǝ ɗeng nǝ.>>
MAR 13:28 <<Wu yit kǝ tǝngkyeen nǝ ɗee a mbiikám pee wun ɗi. Katɗang song tǝngkyeen nǝ mo ɗoom put kǝ kompee ɗepoo, ɓe wu man nǝ, tarlok nǝ kus mmǝnǝ.
MAR 13:29 Aasǝ zak, katɗang wu naa mbii ɗesǝ mo cìn jir, ɓe wu man nǝ, wen kǝn jì wul kus-kus mmǝnǝ.
MAR 13:30 Azeen nzeen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, Baa gurum ɗe yaksǝ mon mmurep jir kas, nǝ atǝng mbii ɗesǝ mo gam jir akuɗang.
MAR 13:31 Ɗeng kǝ yil mon nɗel dǝm weet, ɗangɓǝ baa pwoo fen mmak cam ɗel dǝm kas.>>
MAR 13:32 <<Baa mee gurum mak man puus mǝnǝ, kǝ pee nǝ kas, koo a nenlep Naan ɗe aɗeng mo, kǝ koo a Làa nǝ shikáa fin, ɓe baa wur man kas, amma see a puun ɓejee ɗak.
MAR 13:33 Wu tap kǝ káa fuu mo, kǝ wu tong shi gongpee, mbǝɗe baa wu man parɗi pee nǝn nwul ɗe kas.
MAR 13:34 Katɗang pee nǝ wul, ɓe nǝn nɗee a kaa mee gurum ɗe wu yool mɓe dǝm mwaan jong-jong sǝ. Akuɗang wur yool yit tul nǝ, ɓe wu le nǝ nsar kǝ kǝrem fin mo, wu shwap ɗak nkǝrem fin nǝ mo jir, shimǝndong-shimǝndong. Wur sat ngutap kǝ shiyeepkǝpang mǝ tul nǝ nǝnee, <A tong shi gongpee rǝret.>
MAR 13:35 Mbǝmǝnǝ, wu tong shi gongpee, mbǝɗe baa wu man parpuus ɗe ngulu nǝ wu mbaajì wul ɗe kas. Meeɓe wu mbaajì nkansǝǝn, koo a nnaar mpar, koo a nciit kǝ pǝɓit, koo a mɓít.
MAR 13:36 Mbǝkǝ taji wur mbaajì nwun ndi mman, ɗangɓe wur kat wu ɗee nsaam kas.
MAR 13:37 Mbii ɗe wen sat nwun, ɓe an kǝn sat a ngurum mo jir mmǝnǝ nǝ, wu tong shi gongpee.>>
MAR 14:1 Ɗee teer mo ɗe vǝl, kǝ mo cìn retnyit mǝ Canɗel ɗi, kǝ mu retnyit mǝ gǝǝl aas ɗe baa nǝ kǝ yist kas. Ɓe pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, mo tang ar ɗe mon nyaa Jesu ɗe shi seen, mbǝkǝ mo tu wur ɗi.
MAR 14:2 Ɗangɓe mo waa sat nǝnee, <<Baa mun nyaa wur a nɗǝǝn teer mǝ retnyit sǝ kas, mbǝkǝ taji gurum nǝ mo yool lek nkaa mun.>>
MAR 14:3 Kaaɗe Jesu nyil mBetani, nɗǝǝn lu kǝ Siman nguloom, ɓe wur nkaa se mbiise. Ɓe mee mat war jì kǝ tuut mwoor ɗe nǝ kǝ toos shangshang ɗe moo pet nǝ a nard, ɗe nǝ kǝrim zam. Ɓe war tep took kǝ tuut nǝ, mbǝkǝ war ɗoo mwoor nǝn nJesu nkáa.
MAR 14:4 Amma nǝ láa mpak gurum ɗe mo ɗe mɓut, har mo satpwoo kǝ shak nǝnee, <<A me le ɗangɓe moo tǝkook kǝ mwoor ɗesǝ aasǝ yi?
MAR 14:5 Ɗe nǝ ret kǝ mo seet kǝ mwoor ɗesǝ nǝ nkaa shool zinariya ɗe nǝ met kambil kun, mbǝkǝ mo shin shool nǝ ɗe nenjeel mo.>> Pak gurum nǝ mo gwak mat nǝ war, shi tuup.
MAR 14:6 Amma Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu yit war ɗi. A me le ɗang wuu daampee nwar yi? War cìn a ɗak ɗeret nghan hakyeng.
MAR 14:7 Wun ɗi ashak kǝ nenjeel mo shidaar-shidaar, mpeemǝnǝ ɓe koo a par ɗeɗangyi ɗe wuu rǝɓet, ɓe wun mmak cìn ɗeret mmo. Amma baa wun nkat nghan ashak kǝ wun shidaar-shidaar kas.
MAR 14:8 War kǝ cìn mbii ɗe waa mak cìn nǝ. Mwoor ɗe waa kǝ ɗoo nkaa fwoshik fen sǝ, war cìn mǝnǝ a mɓe ɗak san fen mɓe wum.
MAR 14:9 Azeen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, koo a pee ɗeɗangyi nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ jir, ɗe mon nsatpwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ ni, ɓe mbii ɗe mat ɗesǝ war cìn nghan, ɓe mon nkǝǝ sat nǝ mɓe pan war.>>
MAR 14:10 Judas Iskariyot, ɗewur a memee nɗǝǝn jeplep Jesu ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo, Wur dǝm pee pris ɗenan-nan mo ɗi, mbǝkǝ wur seet kǝ Jesu ɗe nɗǝǝn sar mo.
MAR 14:11 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ ret mon nyit zam, har mo tuweerpwoo nǝ, mon nshin shool nwur. Yaa mparmǝni, ɓe Judas Iskariyot naa nyap ar ɗewur nseet kǝ Jesu ɗi mo.
MAR 14:12 Parpuus ɗenshee ɗe mǝ gǝǝl aas ɗe baa nǝ kǝ yist kas, ɗe nǝ a puus ɗe moo fet tǝm mo, mbǝ mbiise mǝ retnyit mǝ Canɗel nǝ. Ɓe jeplep kǝ Jesu mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Aa rǝɓet kǝ mu dǝm mu ɗak peese mbiise mǝ Canɗel nǝ nghan a nneyi?>>
MAR 14:13 Jesu lep memee mo vǝl nɗǝǝn jeplep fin mo, wu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu ɗel nɗǝǝn yilkaam ni, ɓe wun nkat kǝ mee gurum ɗewur kǝ tuul am nkáa, ɓe wu dǝm nɗang wur,
