MAR 14:14 har nɗǝǝn lu ɗewur ndǝm ɗel ɗe. Ɓe wu tal pǝ ngulu nǝ nǝnee, <Ngukám wur sat nnǝ, lumǝzep ɗe wen nse mbiise Tong Ashak mu Canɗel ashak kǝ jeplep fen mo, nǝ a nneyi?>
MAR 14:15 Ngulu nǝ wur nkám mee luɗeng ɗeɗes nwun, ɗe mo kǝ ɗakle. Ɓe wu ɗak mbiise nǝ mmun, nlu mǝni.>>
MAR 14:16 Jeplep ɗe vǝl nǝ mo yool dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn yilkaamnǝ, ɓe mo kat nǝ a kaaɗi Jesu wu sat mmo sǝ, ɓe mo ɗak mbiise Tong Ashak mǝ Canɗel nǝ nlu ni.
MAR 14:17 Kaaɗe kansǝǝn cìn, ɓe Jesu jì ashak kǝ jeplep ɗe kaapaat baavǝl nǝ mo.
MAR 14:18 Mon nkaa se mbiise nǝ, ɓe Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen-nzeen, kǝn sat nwun, memee nɗǝǝn wun wu nseet kǝ an. A gwar ɗe mun nkaa sese ashak kǝ wur yaksǝ.>>
MAR 14:19 Pwoo ɗe Jesu sat, nǝ wàt pǝtuup mmo zam, ɓe mo ɗoom tal pǝ wur shimǝndong-shimǝndong nǝnee, <<Daa a an aa?>>
MAR 14:20 Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<A memee nɗǝǝn wun ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo. A gwar ɗewur sham kǝ gǝǝl aas nsar mbǝ lep mpuk nɗaa kǝ an.
MAR 14:21 Mɓeɗi Làa Gurum, wur mmuut a kaaɗi mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nkaa wur sǝ. Amma jeel nǝn ntaa nkaa gwar ɗewur seet kǝ Làa Gurum. Ngyal ɗesi ɓe, Di mon nnook làa gwar mǝni, ɓe ɗi nǝ ret met nwur.>>
MAR 14:22 Kaaɗe mo nkaa sese nǝ, ɓe Jesu mang gǝǝl aas, ɓe wur cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan nkaa nǝ, ɓe wur yilang nǝ, ɓe wur shin njeplep fin mo. Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu lap, ɗesǝ nǝ a fwoshik fen.>>
MAR 14:23 Wur mang mee laaɗaa zak, ɓe wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan nkaa nǝ, ɓe wur shin mmo. Ɓe mo jir mo shwaa nɗǝǝn nǝ.
MAR 14:24 Ɓe wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Ɗesǝ nǝ a toom fen ɗe nǝ ɗee a gam mǝ tuweerpwoo ɗepoo shi toom mǝ Naan, ɗe nǝ yaa ɗak mɓe toom fen ɗe mon mɓeer nǝ mɓe gurum mo ɗes.
MAR 14:25 Azeen-nzeen, kǝn sat nwun nǝ, baa an mbaa shwaa am anab ɗi kas, see parɗi an nshwaa am anab ɗepoo nǝ nɗǝǝn mulki Naan.>>
MAR 14:26 Kaaɗe mo cìn kook, ɓe mo pwat dǝm a Jwakpaat.
MAR 14:27 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun jir wun nshwe wu yit nghan ɗi, mbǝɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <Wen ntu ngukiyeer tǝm nǝ mo, ɓe tǝm nǝ mon ntiit shini-shini.>
MAR 14:28 Amma aɓwoon ɗe Naan wur baa yool kǝ an a peemúut, ɓe an ndǝm nwun akyeen nyil nGalili.>>
MAR 14:29 Pita sat nJesu nǝnee, <<Koo ɗe mo jir, mo shwe yit gha ɗe, ɓe baa wen cam yit waa kas.>>
MAR 14:30 Jesu sat mPita nǝnee, <<Azeen-nzeen kǝn sat gha nǝ, mpar cicinsi, akuɗang deel taaɗoo yit vǝl, ɓe waa nciipwoo yit kun nǝ, baa waa man an kas.>>
MAR 14:31 Amma Pita lappwoo nJesu shiɓal hakyeng nǝnee, <<Koo ɗangɗe nǝ atǝng kǝ wen muut ashak kǝ gha, ɓe baa wen cam cíipwoo kas.>> Ɓe koor jeplep Jesu nǝ mo sat aasǝ zak.
MAR 14:32 Mo jì wul mee peeɗi moo pet nǝ a Getsamani, ɓe Jesu sat njeplep fin mo nǝnee, <<Wu tong mpeesǝ, aku nghan cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) ɗi.>>
MAR 14:33 Ɓe Jesu dǝm ashak kǝ Pita, kǝ Jemis, kǝ Joon. Pǝtuup fin nǝ wat, nǝ daampee nwur zam hakyeng.
MAR 14:34 Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Pǝtuup fen nǝ wat zam, har kaa nǝn ntǝtu nghan sǝ. Wu tong mpeesǝ, kǝ wur gongpee ɗe.>>
MAR 14:35 Wur gyes dǝm ɗe akyeen lee, ɓe wur dǝm kurum nyil, wur cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nǝnee, <<Puun fen, katɗang ɗe nǝ mak cìn, ɓe taji wen shwaajeel ɗesǝ nǝ kas.>>
MAR 14:36 Kǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Daa, puun fen, waa mak cìn mbii mo jir, ɓe a baa kǝ kap mǝ jeel ɗesǝ aku pee nghan ɗe. Baa a kaaɗi wen kǝn rǝɓet sǝ kas, amma see a kaaɗi waa aa rǝɓet sǝ.>>
MAR 14:37 Wur waa dǝm pee jeplep fin ɗekun nǝ mo ɗe, ɓe wur kat mo nkaa saam. Ɓe wur sat mPita nǝnee, <<Simon waa a nkaa saam wo? Tan, baa a mak gongpee mɓe awa mǝndong kas aa?
MAR 14:38 Wu tong shi gongpee, kǝ wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), mbǝkǝ taji wu ɗel mɓut jwaan kas. Riin nǝ rǝɓet ɗak, amma nan nǝ cii, mbǝɗe baa nǝ ɓal kas.>>
MAR 14:39 Jesu waa dǝm ɗe, a pee ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nǝ, ɓe wur waa baa cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) a kaaɗi wur cìn nshee sǝ zak.
MAR 14:40 Wur waa baaji kat jeplep ɗekun nǝ mo ɗe nsaam zak, mbǝɗe yit fur mo toon kǝ nsaam. Baa mo man mbii ɗe mon nlap nwur kas.
MAR 14:41 Kaaɗe wur waa waaji pee jeplep nǝ mo ɗe yit ɗekun, ɓe wur sat mmo nǝ, <<Har yaksǝ, ɓe wun ɗe nkaa saam kǝ nookɗi aa? Nǝ mak kǝsǝ, pee nǝ kǝ wul. Mo kǝ seet kǝ Làa Gurum nsar nenshikbish mo.
MAR 14:42 Wu yool mmun seet. Wu naa gwar ɗewur seet kǝ an wur kǝ jì wul.>>
MAR 14:43 Kaaɗe Jesu kuɗi nkaa leshap mǝni, ɓe Judas Iskariyot, ɗewur a memee nɗǝǝn jeplep Jesu ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo, wur jì wul ashak kǝ ɗuu gurum mo ɗes nɗang wur. Gurum nǝ mo kǝ kwai mo, kǝ kam mo. A pris ɗenan-nan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, kǝ nennan-nan mo, a mo lep gurum nǝ mo.
MAR 14:44 Gwar ɗewur seet kǝ Jesu nǝ, wur kǝ ten cìn mee ɓe naa man (alaama) mmo nǝnee, <<Ngwar ɗe wen tok kǝ wur, ɗang wen tung wur shi mǝshpwoo, ɓe a gwar nǝ mmǝnǝ. Ɓe wu yaa wur rǝret, wu dǝm kǝ wur.>>
MAR 14:45 Kaaɗe Judas jì, ɓe wur dǝm pee Jesu ɗe abet, kǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Ngukám.>> Ɓe wur tok kǝ Jesu, ɗangɓe wur tung Jesu shi mǝshpwoo zak.
MAR 14:46 Ɗangɓe mo jì yaa Jesu.
MAR 14:47 Amma memee nɗǝǝn nen ɗe moo ɗar ɗe mpee nǝ, wur shang kwai fin, ɓe wur can kom kǝ kǝrem mǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ vwet nyil.
MAR 14:48 Jesu sat nɗuu kǝ gurum nǝ mo nǝ, <<Wun, wu pwat wur jì kǝ kwai mo, kǝ duul mo, mbǝkǝ wu yaa wen ɗe, kaa wen a mee kus wat sǝ aa?
MAR 14:49 Shidaar-shidaar ɓe an ɗe ashak kǝ wun, kǝ an kǝn kám nwun nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɓe baa wu yaa an kas. Amma mbii ɗesǝ mo cìn aasǝ jir, a mbǝkǝ pwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ran mo nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan mo gam ɗe.>>
MAR 14:50 Jeplep wur mo jir, mo yool shwe yit wur ɗe.
MAR 14:51 Mee ɗyem zǝlang wur ɗi, ɗewur sup a mee fuwaat nkaa shin ɓejee, wur dǝm nɗang Jesu, kaaɗi mo yaa wur,
MAR 14:52 ɓe wur su dǝm ngum, wur yit fuwaat nǝ mmo.
MAR 14:53 Mo dǝm kǝ Jesu ntul kǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ, a peeɗi pris ɗenan-nan mo, kǝ nennan-nan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis moo kuur ɗe ashak.
MAR 14:54 Pita tap dǝm nɗang Jesu aɓwoon jong-jong, har ntul kǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ, ɓe wur ɗel tong ashak kǝ nentappee mo, kǝ wur kǝ kǝlǝng wong wus ɗe.
MAR 14:55 Pris ɗenan-nan nǝ mo, kǝ kuur nennan-nan nǝ mo jir, mo tang mbii ɗe mon cìn langtǝng mǝ ɗung mo nkaa wur, mbǝkǝ mo katpee tu Jesu ɗe, amma baa mo kat kas.
MAR 14:56 Koo ɗi gurum mo ɗes mo jì kǝ langtǝng mǝ ɗung mo nkaa Jesu, ɓe baa mbii ɗe mo sat nkaa Jesu nǝ mo yakshak kas.
MAR 14:57 Pak gurum mo yool ɗar atǝng, kǝ mo sat mbii ɗe mǝ ɗung nkaa Jesu nǝnee,
MAR 14:58 <<Mu kǝlǝng wur sat nǝnee, <wuɗin nshirip Lu Naan ɗeɗes sǝ, ɗe gurum mo ɗyik nǝ shi sar, ɗangɓe wuɗin mbaa ɗyik memee ɗe nɗǝǝn teer mo kun zak, ɗe baa a shi sar kas.> >>
MAR 14:59 Jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa mbii ɗe mo sat nǝ mo yakshak kas.
MAR 14:60 Ɗangɓe pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ wur yool ɗar atǝng nnaar fur. Ɓe wur tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<Baa waa kǝ mee mbii ɗe waa nlap nkaa pwoo ɗesǝ mo kas aa? A sat a me nkaa mbii ɗe des ɗesǝ mo sat nkaa gha yi?>>
MAR 14:61 Amma Jesu ɗok kǝtǝk, baa wur lap mee pwoo kas. Ɓe pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ wur waa baa tal ɗe pǝ Jesu zak nǝnee, <<A gha a Kristi Làa Naan Ɗehai aa?>>
MAR 14:62 Jesu lap nǝnee, <<A nghan a wu, wun nnaa Làa Gurum, wur tong nsarse Naan ɗeɓal met jir, ɓǝ wun nnaa wur jì nɗǝǝn nluu ɗe aɗeng mo zak.>>
MAR 14:63 Kaaɗe pris ɗeɗes met jir, wur kǝlǝng pwoo mǝni, ɓe wur yilang nlǝr fin mo, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Muu tang a langtǝng ɗeɗang ɗikǝ zak yi?
MAR 14:64 Yaksǝ, wu kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe Jesu wur sat, ɗewur leshin a kaa Naan sǝ. Wur naa arang nkaa pwoo mǝnǝ yi?>> Ɓe mo jir, mo canɗyeel muut nJesu.
MAR 14:65 Pak mo yaa twes lii nkaa wur, mo paa yit wur mo, ɗang mo nǝrem wur, ɓǝ mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<A woo gwar ɗe cut gha nǝ mmun.>> Ɓe nentappee mo nǝrem wur hakyeng.
MAR 14:66 Kaaɗe Pita ɗar a fur nder luɗyeel nǝ, ɓe mee reep ɗe war a kǝrem pris ɗeɗes nǝ war jì.
MAR 14:67 Ɓe kaaɗi war naa Pita ke tong a wus, ɓe war tǝǝr yit nzing nkaa Pita, ɓǝ war sat nǝnee, <<Gha ashak kǝ Jesu ngwe Nazaret zak!>>
MAR 14:68 Ɗangɓe Pita cíipwoo nǝnee, <<Baa wen man mbii ɗe yii sat nǝ kas, baa wen man pwoo mǝnǝ kas.>> Ɓe wur yaa ar ɗel put nshiyeeppǝbong.
MAR 14:69 Ɓe reep ɗe war a kǝrem mu pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ war baa naa wur ɗe, ɓe war sat nen ɗe moo ɗar mpwoo shiyeeppǝbong nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗǝsi wur a memee mɓut nen Jesu nǝ mo.>>
MAR 14:70 Amma Pita baa cíipwoo ɗe zak. Lang ɗi lee, ɓe nen ɗe moo ɗar ɗi pee nǝ, mo sat mPita nǝnee, <<Azeen-nzeen, gha a mee mɓut nen Jesu nǝ mo, mbǝɗe gha a ngu Galili.>>
MAR 14:71 Amma Pita cíipwoo, wur ɗalwus, wur sat nǝnee, <<Naan shin kar nghan katɗang wen man gwar ɗe wuu satpwoo nkaa wur nǝ.>>
MAR 14:72 Abet-abet, ɓe deel tokshik ɗe vǝl. Ɓe Pita yeepwoo ɗe Jesu sat nwur sí nǝnee, <<Akuɗang deel tokshik yit vǝl, ɓe ghan cíipwoo fen yit kun nnǝ, baa a man wen kas.>> Kaaɗe Pita yeepwo mǝni, ɓe nǝ tep kwak nwur, ɓǝ wur yaa gwar maap.
MAR 15:1 Kaaɗe ɓit mang, ɓe pris ɗenan-nan mo, ashak kǝ nennan-nan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, kǝ nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo jir, mo kuur ashak, ɓe mo lepwoo, ɓe mo ɓwot sar kǝ Jesu, mo dǝm shin wur mPailet.
MAR 15:2 Pailet tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<A gha a mishkom nen Yahudi mo aa? Jesu lap nǝnee, <<aa ten a sat.>>
MAR 15:3 Pris ɗenan-nan nǝ mo jì kǝ langtǝng mǝ ɗung mo ɗes nkaa Jesu.
MAR 15:4 Pailet, wur waa baa tal pǝ Jesu nǝnee, <<Baa gha kǝ mee pwoo ɗe ghan nlap kas aa? A naa pwoo mo ɗes ɗe mo jì kǝ mo nkaa gha>>
MAR 15:5 Amma baa Jesu lap mee pwoo nwur koo mǝndong kas, har nǝ fes aapwoo mPailet zam.
MAR 15:6 Gyet ɓe koo a parpuus mǝ retnyit mǝ Canɗel ɗeɗangyii, ɓe Pailet wur kǝ loot ɓwet mee gurum ɗe ɓuɓwoot mǝndong mmo, ɗe gurum nǝ moo rǝɓet.
MAR 15:7 Mee gwar ɗe moo pet sǝm nwur a Barabbas, wur ɗe a ɓuɓwoot nlushoot ashak kǝ nenbwetɓeer mo, ɗe mo kǝ tukáa nɗǝǝn ɓwetɓeer fur nǝ.
MAR 15:8 Ɗuu gurum nǝ mo jì kus, ɓe mo yaa ɗang nǝ pǝ Pailet, kǝ wur ɓwet mee gurum ɗe mmo, kaaɗi wur loot kǝ cìn nǝ sǝ.
MAR 15:9 Pailet tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wuu rǝɓet kǝ nghan ɓwet a mishkoom mǝ nen Yahudi mo nwun aa?>>
MAR 15:10 Pailet man nǝ, pris ɗenan nǝ mo jì kǝ Jesu ntoom fin a mbǝ zuur.
MAR 15:11 Ɗangɓe pris ɗenan mo kar ɗuu gurum nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mo ɗang pǝ Pailet kǝ wu ɓwet Barabbas ɗe mmo.
MAR 15:12 Pailet waa baa sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wuu rǝɓet kǝ nghan cìn a me kǝ gwar ɗe wuu pet wu a mishkoom nen Yahudi mo yi?>>
MAR 15:13 Ɗangɓe mo waa sǝǝt le or shiɓal nǝnee, <<A le kǝ mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeep.>>
MAR 15:14 Pailet sat mmo nǝnee, <<A mɓe meye? Wur cin a mbii ɗebish ɗeɗang yi?>> Be mo waa sǝǝt le or shi ɗoo ɗeɗes hakyeng, <<A le kǝ mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeep! A le kǝ mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeep!>>
MAR 15:15 Mɓeɗi Pailet rǝɓet kǝ nǝ ret ɗe nɗuu kǝ gurum nǝ mon nyit, ɓe wu ɓwet Barabbas mmo. Amma aɓwoon ɗewur fwo nbwat Jesu, ɓe wur shin Jesu mmo, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm pwas wur ɗe nkaa shiyeep.
MAR 15:16 Ɗangɓe shiitoon mo ɗel kǝ Jesu nɗǝǝn lu mǝ gofna nǝ, ɗe moo pet nǝ a Praitoriyum, ɓe mo pǝrep shiitoon ɗe mpee mǝnǝ mo jir, mo jì kuur ashak pee Jesu ɗi.
MAR 15:17 Mo lep mee nlǝr ɗe nǝ naat pan a tup nJesu, kǝ mo ráa mee mbiikáa ghǝr, mo lep nwur nkáa.
MAR 15:18 Ɗangɓe mo tok kǝ nwur nǝnee, <<Muu tok kǝ gha da mishkoom nen Yahudi mo.>>
MAR 15:19 Ɓe mo cut wur nkáa shi raas, ɓǝ mo tus lii nkaa wur. Ɓe mo kurum nfurum, kǝ mo seyil nwur.
MAR 15:20 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ shwar, kǝ ɓák wur, ɓe mo shang nlǝr ɗenaat pan a tup nǝ nkaa wur, ɗangɓe mo lep nlǝr nwur mo nwur. Ɓe mo put dǝm kǝ wur atǝleng, mbǝkǝ mo pwas wur ɗe.
MAR 15:21 Kaaɗe mo a ar dǝm nǝ, ɓe mo taa kaat kǝ mee gwar, ɗe moo pet sim nwur a Simon, wu a ngu Sairin, puun Alekzanda kǝ Rufus, wur tong mmee laayil jì ɗe, ɓe shiitoon nǝ mo le wur mang shiyeepmúut Jesu nǝ ating.
MAR 15:22 Mo jì wul kǝ Jesu mmee peeɗi moo pet nǝ a Golgofa (shii kǝ Golgofa nǝ a ɗyeskáa.)
MAR 15:23 Mo shin am anab ɗe mo kǝ riyeep nǝ kǝ mee yen ɗe moo pet naa myrrh nwur, amma wur cii shwaa nǝ.
MAR 15:24 Kaaɗe mo pwas Jesu nkaa shiyeep, ɓe mo koospaa mɓe ɓàk nlǝr wur. Ɓe Mo ɓàk nlǝr nwur mo nnaar mu. Ɓe mo bǝlǝp mbǝkǝ mo naa be ɗe koo a gwar ɗeɗangyi nwur nkat ɗi.
MAR 15:25 Mo pwas Jesu nkaa shiyeepyoom nǝ a kaa karfe pwoofeer ɗe mǝ bit sǝ.
MAR 15:26 Mo ran pwoo nkaa mbii ɗe nǝ le ɗang mo tu Jesu, mo lang nkaa shiyeepyoom nǝ nɗeel nkáa nJesu, ɗǝ nǝ sat nǝnee, << A MISHKOOM MƏ NEN YAHUDI MO NƊESƏ.
MAR 15:27 Mo pwas mee kus wat mo vǝl ashak kǝ Jesu zak. Mo pwas memee nkwang sarse nwur, ɓǝ memee nkwang sarkul nwur zak.
MAR 15:28 Mo cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo jir a mbǝkǝ pwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝ gam ɗe nǝnee, <<Mon tang wur mɓut nenɗebish mo.
MAR 15:29 Nen ɗe mo ɗel ar peeɗi mo pwas Jesu ɗe, mo zǝkkáa fur mo, kǝ mo nwangpwoo nwur nǝnee, <<Kaigwa! Waa ɗe di a sat nǝ, waa nshirip Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɗangɓe nghan mbaa ɗyik nǝ ɗe nɗǝǝn teer mo kun zak.
MAR 15:30 A ɓam sak kǝse! A sham nkaa shiyeep nǝ shiko.>>
MAR 15:31 Pris ɗenan-nan mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, mo shwar, ɓǝ mo toklong nJesu zak, mo sat nǝnee, <<Waa ɓam nen ɗeci mo, ɗangɓǝ baa waa mak ɓam sak kas.
MAR 15:32 Katɗang gha a Kristi azeen-nzeen, mishkoom nen Isreil mo. Ɓe a sham nyil nkaa shiyeepmúut nǝ yaksǝ, mbǝkǝ mu naa, kǝ mun shinzeen ɗe.>> Wat ɗe mo pwas mo ashak kǝ Jesu, mo satpwoo ɗebuu nwur zak.
MAR 15:33 Kaaɗe karfe kaapaat baavǝl mǝ puus a naar ting-tǝng nǝ wul, ɓe pee nǝ rii nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir, ɗel dǝm wul karfe kun mǝ puus.
MAR 15:34 Kaaɗe karfe kun nǝ cìn, ɓe Jesu wu petpee shi ɗoo ɗǝɗes, nǝnee, <<Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?>> Manshii nǝ a nǝnee, <<Naan fen, Naan fen. A mbeeme ɗang a yit an yi?>>
MAR 15:35 Kaaɗe pak gurum mo mɓut nen ɗe moo ɗar ɗe mpee nǝ, mo kǝlǝng petpee mǝni, ɓe mo sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur kǝ pet a Ilaija>>
MAR 15:36 Ɓe memee nɗǝǝn mo, wur su dǝm mang tuvuk lep nɗǝǝn am anab ɗeɗwang, wur lep nkaa rep mee kam. Wur lep kàa nJesu mbǝkǝ wur ɗyas ɗe. Pak gurum nǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Wu ɗar aku mun naa mbii ɗe nǝn ncìn ɗi ɗe, kyet Ilaija wun njì ɓam wur wo?>>
MAR 15:37 Jesu waa baa bwet or shi ɗoo ɗǝɗes, ɓe wur shang nookmuut.
MAR 15:38 Ɓe fuwaat ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes ɗe nii paapee Ɗeɓang met jir, nǝ tee sham a naar ɓe nǝ ɓàk vǝl.
MAR 15:39 Kaaɗe gwar ɗǝǝɗes nkaa shiitoon mo kambil mǝndong ɗewur ɗar kus kǝ shiyeepmúut nǝ, wur naa kaaɗi Jesu shang nookmuut, ɓe wu sat nǝ, <<Azeen-nzeen, gwar ɗesǝ wur a Làa Naan.>>
MAR 15:40 Pak mat moo ɗar ɗe pan jong, mon nkaa naa mbii ɗe nii cìn jir. nƊǝǝn mat nǝ mo, ɓe Meeri Makdalin waa ɗe, kǝ Salome kǝ Meeri nǝǝn Jemis ɗelee kǝ Josep.
MAR 15:41 A mo a mat ɗe di mo dǝm nɗang Jesu, kǝ moo cìn ɗak nwur kaaɗi di wur kuɗi nɗǝǝn yil nGalili, kǝ pak mat mo ɗes ɗe mo yool nGalili jì ashak kǝ wur nJerusalem.
MAR 15:42 Nciit kǝ mǝni, ɓe kansǝǝn cìn, a parpuus ɗe gurum moo ɗak sut ɗe, mbǝɗe ɗaar nǝ a puus nookɗi.
MAR 15:43 Ɓe Josep ngu Arimafiya, mee gwar ɗǝɗes, ɗewur nɗǝǝn nenɓeetpwoo mo, wur shikáa fin wur nkaa gong jì kǝ mulki Naan. Wur yaa pǝtuup, ɓe wur dǝm ɗang kúm Jesu pǝ Pailet, mbǝkǝ wur dǝm wum ɗe.
MAR 15:44 Nǝ aapwoo mPailet zam, mbǝɗe wur kǝlǝng nǝ, Jesu kǝ ten muut. Ɗangɓe Pailet pet shiitoon ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓe wur tal pǝ shiitoon nǝnee, <<Kyet Jesu kǝ ten muut a yam wo?>>
MAR 15:45 Kaaɗe Pailet kǝlǝng mbii ɗe shiitoon nǝ sat, ɓe Pailet sat mmo kǝ mo dǝm shin kúm Jesu nǝn nJosep.
MAR 15:46 Ɗangɓe Josep seet kǝ mee fuwaat ɗepiyaa. Ɓe wur sham kǝ kúm Jesu nǝ, wur ɓwot kúm nǝ shi fuwaat nǝ. Ɓe wur dǝm le kúm Jesu nǝ nɗǝǝn kǝcir ɗe mo am nǝ nɗǝǝn jwak. Ɓe wur tup mee nghǝk ɗǝɗes, wur paa pwoo kǝcir nǝ ɗi.
MAR 15:47 Meeri Makdalin, kǝ Meeri nǝǝn kǝ Josep, mo naapee ɗe mo le kum Jesu nǝ ɗi.
MAR 16:1 Aɓwoon kǝ parpuus Nookɗi mǝ nen Yahudi mo, ɓe Meeri Makdalin kǝ Salome, kǝ Meeri nǝǝn kǝ Jemis, mo seet mwoor tus shangshang, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm pwes ɗe nkaa kúm Jesu.
MAR 16:2 Parpuus ɗenshee mɓut nteer pwovǝl sǝ mo, mɓít nciit kǝ ɗe puus mɓe kaa ɓe mat nǝ mo pwat dǝm a peeɗi kǝcir nǝ ɗi.
MAR 16:3 Mon nkaa sat nǝ shak a ar nǝnee, <<A wii mbet nghǝk ɗeɗes nǝ mmun mpwoo kǝcir nǝ ye?>>
MAR 16:4 Ɓe kaaɗi mo ɗyeep yit, ɓe mo naa mo kǝ bèt nghǝk ɗeɗes nǝ baa kǝnǝ. Nghǝk nǝ a ɗeɗes hakyeng.
MAR 16:5 Kaaɗe mo ɗel nɗǝǝn kǝcir nǝ, ɓe mo naa mee zǝlang wur tong nkwang sarse, wur kǝ nlǝr ɗepiyaa, ɓe nǝ lekǝǝrmuut mmo zam.
MAR 16:6 Zǝlang nǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa wun kas, mbǝɗe wen man nǝ, wun pǝ yap a Jesu ngu Nazaret. Gwar ɗe mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeep sí, wur kǝ yool a peemúut nǝ. Baa wur mpesi kas. Wu jì wu naapee ɗe mo le wur ɗe nɗesi!
MAR 16:7 Ɓe wu dǝm, wu sat jeplep wur mo, kǝ Pita nǝ, wur kǝ yool a peemúut, yaksǝ wur a ar dǝm nGalili a tǝleng nwun. Wun ndem wu naa wur a mpee mǝni, kaaɗi dǝ wur kǝ ten sat nwun sǝ.>>
MAR 16:8 Ɗangɓe mat nǝ mo yool pwat yit kǝcir nǝ, ɓe mo shwe dǝm kǝ kǝǝrmuut, ɗang nǝ aapwoo mo zak. Baa mo taa sat mee mbii mmee gurum kas, mbǝɗe kǝǝrmuut nǝ fes yaa mo zam.
MAR 16:9 Kaaɗe Jesu yool mɓít parpuus ɗenshee, ɗe nǝ a puus Láadi ɓe wur shee kámshin fin a mMeeri Makdalin, a war a mat ɗe di Jesu kǝ ceen riin ɗebish mo pwoovǝl pwat nɗǝǝn war sí.
MAR 16:10 War dǝm sat nen ɗe di mo ashak kǝ Jesu. Mon nkaa wal kǝ maap.
MAR 16:11 Amma kaaɗi mo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe war sat nǝ, Jesu wur kǝ yool a peemúut, ɗangɓe wen kǝ naa wur, ɓe baa mo shinzeen kas.
MAR 16:12 Aɓwoon mǝni, ɓe Jesu kámshin mmee jeplep wur mo vǝl, kaaɗi mo a ar dǝm mmee laayil.
MAR 16:13 Mo ciir dǝm sat nkoor jeplep nǝ mo nǝ, wuɗun kǝ naa Jesu, amma baa koor nǝ mo shinzeen kas.
MAR 16:14 Aɓwoon ɗese, ɓe Jesu jì kámshin njeplep ɗe kaapaat baamǝndong sǝ mo, ɓe moo tong a peese mbiise. Wur gwak mo mɓe ciin shinzeen fur, kǝ mbǝɗe pǝtuup fur mo a ɗeɓal, mbǝɗe baa mo shinzeen nen ɗe mo naa wur aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ yool a peemúut kas.
MAR 16:15 Jesu sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wur dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir, wur satpwoo ɗeret ɗe ngurum mo jir.
MAR 16:16 Gwar ɗewur shinzeen, kǝ mo cìn baptisma wur zak, ɓe wur nkat ɓam, amma gwar ɗewur cii shinzeen, ɓe mon ncanɗyeel muut nwur.
MAR 16:17 Mon nnaa mbii aapwoo ɗesǝ mo pǝ nen ɗe mo shinzeen nghan. Mon nshin iiko mmo mɓe ceen riin ɗebish mo nɗǝǝn sǝm fen. Mon nkatpwoo shi liispwoo mo shini-shini.
MAR 16:18 Katɗang mo yak nwòo mo, koo mo shwaa yen tupee ɓe baa nǝn ncìn mee mbii mmo kas koo dǝɓen. Mon nle sar fur mo nkaa nenciinkoom mo ɓe mon mbar.>>
MAR 16:19 Aɓwoon ɗe Daa Jesu kǝ leshap kǝ mo, ɓe mo mang wur kaa aɗeng Naan. Ɓe wur kàa tong nsarse Naan.
MAR 16:20 Jeplep nǝ mo pwat dǝm satpwoo Naan shipe-shipe. Daa wur cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mo, wur kám agaak nǝ, pwoo ɗe moo sat nǝ azeen shi mbii aapwoo ɗe mo cìn mo.
ACT 1:1 Dǝm pǝ gha Tiyofilus. Nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal fen ɗenshee, ɓǝ wen ran pwoo nkaa mbii ɗe Jesu wur cìn mo, kǝ mbii ɗewur kám mo.
ACT 1:2 Dǝm wul parpuus ɗe Naan mang wur kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng. Aku ɗang Naan mang wur kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng, ɓǝ wur leshap nnen ɗewur kǝ bǝlǝp mo, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗe a jeplep fin mo, shi iiko mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang.
ACT 1:3 Mbǝ teer mo laarfeer aɓwoon ɗe Jesu kǝ yool a peemúut, ɓǝ wur woo shin mmo yit ɗes, nɗǝǝn ar mo shini-shini, ɗe nǝ kám agaak nǝ, wur ɗi mmeen azeen-zeen. Mo naa Jesu, kǝ wur leshap mmo nkaa mulki mǝ Naan.
ACT 1:4 Par mǝ puus sǝ, ɓǝ kaaɗe wur ɗi ashak kǝ jeplep fin mo, ɓǝ wur leshap mmo ɓalɓal nǝnee, <<Taji wu yool wu yit Jerusalem kas. Ɗangɓe wu tong, wu naa gam zuum ɗe puun fen wur kǝ ten cweer nwun, ɗe wuu kǝlǝng nǝ mpwoo fen.
ACT 1:5 Dǝ Joon wur cìn baptisma ngurum mo a shi am, ɗang ɗee meeteer mo ɗi a lee ɗak, ɓǝ mon ncìn baptisma nwun a shi Riin Ɗeɓang.>> Mo Mang Jesu Kàa Kǝ Wur Aɗeng
ACT 1:6 Kaaɗe jeplep Jesu mo kuur ashak, ɓǝ mo tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<Daa, gha mbǝ cin shin mulki nǝ nnen Isreil mo a nɗǝǝn meeteer ɗesǝ mo ee?>>
ACT 1:7 Jesu lap mo nǝnee, <<Baa ɗesǝ nǝ a muu, mbǝkǝ nwun man puus nǝ, kǝ ɓit ɗe Daa kǝ ten le mo nɗǝǝn iiko fin kas.
ACT 1:8 Ɗangɓǝ Naan wur nshin ɓal nwun, katɗang Riin Ɗeɓang sham nkaa wun. Ɓǝ wun mbǝ ɗee a langtǝng fen mhffig o nɗǝǝn Jerusalem, kǝ nɗǝǝn Judiya jir, kǝ Samariya, dǝm wul nɗǝǝn yil mo jir zak.>>
ACT 1:9 Kaaɗe wur sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo mang wur kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng a yit mo. Yaksǝ nluu jì paa wur, baa mo kutɗi naa wur kas.
ACT 1:10 Kaaɗe mo ɗi nkaa ban yit mo mo kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng, ɓǝ mee gurum mo vǝl, mo jì ɗar pǝ mo ɗi, kǝ nlǝr piyaa petpet
ACT 1:11 Nen nǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Wun nnen Galili mo, a mii le ɗang wuu ɗar, wuu ban yit kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng ii? Jesu ɗe wu naa mo kǝ mang wur kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng pǝ wun ɗi sǝ, ɓǝ wur mbǝ baa sham a kǝsǝ zak.>>
ACT 1:12 Ɓǝ jeplep mǝ Jesu mo yool yit Zuul Paat ɗe nǝ kus kǝ Jerusalem, ɗejong nǝ kǝ Jerusalem a meel mǝndong ɓejee ɗak.
ACT 1:13 Kaaɗe mo jì wul nɗǝǝn pee kaam nǝ, ɓǝ mo dǝm kàa nɗǝǝn luɗeng, a pee ɗe moo tong ɗi. A mon nɗesǝ, Pita, kǝ Joon, kǝ Jemis, kǝ Andru, Filip kǝ Tomas, Bartolomi, kǝ Matiyu, kǝ Jemis ɗyem Alfiyas, kǝ Simon Zelot, memee mɓut mee nnen ɗe gyet mo ɓalkaa mo mbǝ tang mulki mǝ yil mo, kǝ Judas làa Jemis.
ACT 1:14 Nen ɗesǝ mo ɓalkaa mo mo ashak mbǝ ɗangnaan shidaar-shidaar, shi pǝtuup mǝndong ashak kǝ pak shurep mo, kǝ Meri nǝǝn Jesu, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fin mo zak.
ACT 1:15 Nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ nen shinzeen nǝ mo kuur ashak, (ɗe ɗuu mo nǝ wul kambil mǝndong kǝ laarvǝl), ɓǝ Pita yool ɗar atǝng nnaar mo mbǝ leshap, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee,
ACT 1:16 <<Ɗyemnaa mo, nǝ a tǝng kǝ mo gampwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal mǝ Naan. Pwoo ɗe gyet Riin Ɗeɓang le kǝ Devit leshap nkaa Judas ngwe ɗewur ɗee a ngukám ar nnen ɗe dǝ mo yaa Jesu.
ACT 1:17 Dǝ wur a memee mɓut mmun, kǝ dǝ wur cìn pak ɗak fun ɗesǝ nǝ zak.>>
ACT 1:18 (Shi shool ɗe Judas lap mbǝ kwat ɗak fin ɗebish, ɓǝ wur dǝm seet mee maar ɗishik. A pee ɗewur sham taa wur muut, wur piin ɓut fin, dǝm kat pinbut wur mo pwat ɓeer.
ACT 1:19 Mbii ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗemǝman ngurum ɗe moo tong nɗǝǝn yil nJerusalem jir, moo pet maar ɗesǝ nǝ shi liispwoo mo a Akeldama. Ɗe shii mǝnǝ a maar toom).
ACT 1:20 <<Mbǝɗǝ mo Jeplep Jesu mo ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Zabura nǝnee, <<Wu ar kǝ nlu wur nǝ ɗee a kǝrem. Taji mee gurum tong nɗǝǝn nǝ kas,> Kǝ mo ran zak nǝnee, <Wu yit kǝ mee gurum ɗee ɗi a koppee wur nǝ.>
ACT 1:21 <<Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ ret kǝ mmun bǝlǝp mee gurum mɓut nnen ɗe peegyet mo ɗi ashak kǝ mun, kaaɗe dǝ Daa Jesu wur kǝ mwaan dǝm kǝ mun shipee-shipee sǝ.
ACT 1:22 Yool mɓít ɗe Joon kǝ cìn baptisma ngurum mo, dǝm wul parpuus ɗe Naan mang Jesu kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng, pǝ mun ɗi. Nǝ ɗee a tǝng kǝ memee mɓut nnen ɗe mun mbǝlǝp sǝ mo, wur ɗee a ngusatpwoo nkaa yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut nǝ ashak kǝ mun.>>
ACT 1:23 Aasǝ ɓǝ mo le gurum mo vǝl ɗe sǝm mo mo a Josep ɗe moo pet wur a Barsabas koo Jastus, kǝ Matiyas zak.
ACT 1:24 Yaksǝ mo ɗangnaan nǝnee, <<Daa, gha ɗe a man pǝtuup gurum mo jir. A kám ngwe ɗe waa a bǝlǝp mmun, nɗǝǝn des ɗevǝl sǝ mo.
ACT 1:25 Mbǝkǝ ngwe nǝ cìn ɗak ɗi a koppee mǝ Judas kaa memee nɗǝǝn jeplep kǝ Jesu mo sǝ. Dǝ Judas yool yit ɗak nǝ ɗi, mbǝkǝ nwur dǝm ɗi a pee ɗyem fin.>>
ACT 1:26 Kaaɗe mo ɓwet bǝlǝp nǝ, ɓǝ nǝ taa nkaa, Matiyas. Yool mmǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo tang Matiyas ashak kǝ jeplep ɗe kaapaat baamǝndong nǝ mo.
ACT 2:1 Kaaɗe parpuus Pentikos nǝ wul, ɓǝ nen shinzeen nǝ moo kuur ashak a pee mǝndong jir.
ACT 2:2 Yaksǝ, nnen mman, ɓǝ mee ɗoo ɗe fiipee ka kut ɗeɓal-ɓal sǝ, nǝ tong aɗeng sham gam lu ɗe moo tong ɗi jir.
ACT 2:3 Yaksǝ mo naa mee mbii kàa mbǝlem wus sǝ, nǝ sham lang nkaa mo jir
ACT 2:4 Mo gam mo jir shi Riin Ɗeɓang, yaksǝ mo ɗoom leshap mo shi liispwoo mo shini-shini, kaaɗe Riin Ɗeɓang kám mmo sǝ.
ACT 2:5 Nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ pak nen Yahudi mo nɗǝǝn Jerusalem ɗe moo kǝǝr Naan mo ɗi, kǝ ɗe mo pwat nɗǝǝn yil mo shini-shinǝ jir, mo jì nJerusalem.
ACT 2:6 Kaaɗe gurum mo kǝlǝng ɗoo nǝ, ɓǝ ɗuu mǝ gurum nǝ mo kuur a peeshak. Nǝ aapwoo ngurum nǝ mo, mbǝɗe koo a ngwe ɗeɗangyi, ɓǝ wur kǝlǝng nen shinzeen nǝ mo nkaa leshap shi liispwoo mǝ yil fin.
ACT 2:7 Nǝ lekǝǝrmuut, ɗang nǝ aapwoo mo, ɓǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Nen ɗe moo leshap sǝ mo jir, a nen Galili mo.
ACT 2:8 Cirang ɗang koo a ngwe ɗǝɗang nɗǝǝn mun, pǝ kǝlǝng mo nkaa leshap shi liispwoo mǝ yil fin ii?
ACT 2:9 Mun mu tong a nyil mPartiya, kǝ Mediya, kǝ Elam, kǝ nen ɗe mo tong nɗǝǝn Mesopotamiya, kǝ Judiya, kǝ Kapadosiya, kǝ Pontus, kǝ Eshiya,
ACT 2:10 Kǝ Firijiya, kǝ Pamfiliya, kǝ Ijip, kǝ ngaar Libiya, kus kǝ Sairin, kǝ pak fun mo a mǝzep ɗe mo tong nyil nRom jì ɗi.
ACT 2:11 (Mo a nen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen ɗe mo jì ɗeɗel nɗǝǝn nen Yahudi mo). Kǝ nen Kritan mo, kǝ nen Arab mo. Muu kǝlǝng mo nkaa leshap nkaa mbii aapwoo ɗǝnan-nan ɗe Naan wur cìn mo shi liispwoo mǝ yil fun mo.>>
ACT 2:12 Nǝ aapwoo mmo, ɗang nǝ suur mo jir, ɗang mo baa tal pǝ shak nǝnee, <<A mii a shii mbii ɗesǝ yii?>>
ACT 2:13 Ɗangɓǝ pak gurum mo nwang pwoo mmo, ɗang mo sat nǝnee, <<Nen ɗesǝ mo raa a am anab.>> Pita leshap nƊuu Gurum Mo Parpuus Pentikos
ACT 2:14 Ɓǝ Pita yool ɗar atǝng ashak kǝ jeplep ɗe kaapaat baamǝndong sǝ mo, ɓǝ wur ɗiyeep ɗoo fin ɓalɓal, ɓǝ wur sat nɗuu gurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wun nen Yahudi mo, kǝ wun nen ɗe wuu tong nJerusalem jir. Wu lekom kǝ nwen sat shii mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗi nwun.
ACT 2:15 Baa nen ɗesǝ mo raa a am anab kǝ nǝ yir kaa mo kaaɗe wuu pan sǝ kas, mbǝɗe pee nǝ kutɗi a pwoofeer mǝ bít nɗesǝ ɓejee ɗak.
ACT 2:16 Ɗangɓǝ, ɗesǝ nǝ a mbii ɗe gyet ngusat pwoo Naan Jowel kǝ ten sat sǝ nǝnee,
ACT 2:17 <Naan wur sat nǝnee, Nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝ kyes nǝ mo. Ɓǝ an mbǝ nɗoo Riin fen nkaa gurum mo jir. Jep fuu ɗemish mo, kǝ ɗe mat mo, mon nsatpwoo Naan ngurum mo, kǝ mbii ɗe mo mbǝ jì akyeen. Zǝlang fuu mon nnaa mbii ɗesǝsok mo, ɗe Naan wur rǝɓet kám nǝ mmo, kǝ dǝkaam fuu mon nsuun suun mo.
ACT 2:18 Kǝzak, nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ an mbǝ ɗoo Riin fen nkaa kǝrem fen ɗemish mo, kǝ ɗe mat mo. Ɓǝ mon nsatpwoo fen, kǝ mbii ɗe mo mbǝ jì akyeen zak.
ACT 2:19 An mbǝ cìn mbii lukshik mo aɗeng, ɗang an mbǝ cìn mbii aapwoo mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ, ɗe toom kǝ wus, kǝ ɗiyeel, mon ɗen kàa gǝrong-gǝrong,
ACT 2:20 akuɗang puus ɗeɗes, kǝ iiko mǝ Daa nǝn njì, ɓǝ Puus nǝn nciir ɗee a peenkwoo, kǝ tar nǝn nciir ɗee a toom zak.
ACT 2:21 Parmǝnǝ, ɓǝ koo a ngwe ɗeɗangyii, ɗewur pet sǝm mǝ Daa ɓǝ a wur nkat ɓam.>
ACT 2:22 <<Wun nen Isreil mo! Wu lekom kǝ wu kǝlǝng pwoo ɗesǝ mo ɗe. Jesu ngu Nazaret, ngwe ɗe Naan kat retnyit kǝ wur, kǝ ɗe Naan cìn mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo mo kǝ Sǝmpwoo mo nsar wur a yit fuu. Wun shikáa fuu wu man nǝ, mbii ɗesǝ mo cìn a kǝsǝ.
ACT 2:23 A Jesu ɗesǝ ɗe mo seet wur nsar fuu. Mbǝɗǝ a Naan kǝ ten le, kǝ wur man nǝ, nǝn ncìn a kǝsǝ. A wun wu tu wur, mbǝɗe a wun wu le, kǝ nnenshikbish mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeep.
ACT 2:24 Ɗangɓe Naan yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut, kǝ wur fween Jesu nɗǝǝn jeel mǝ muut, mbǝɗe baa muut nǝ mmak yaa wur le ntuun nǝ kas.
ACT 2:25 Mbǝɗǝ gyet Devit kǝ ten leshap nkaa Jesu nǝnee, wen naa Daa ashak kǝ an shidaar-shidaar. Mbǝɗǝ wur kus kǝ an, ɓǝ baa mee mbii mmak daampee nghan kas.
ACT 2:26 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ pǝtuup fen nǝ gam kǝ retnyit, ɗang lis fen met kook retnyit. Dǝm wul a ɗe fwooshik fen tong nɗǝǝn canciin zak.
ACT 2:27 Mbǝɗǝ baa gha mmak yit seen fen nɗǝǝn kǝcir kas, kǝ baa gha mmak yit Ngwe Ɗeɓang fwaa nwur naa wam nɗǝǝn kǝcir kas.
ACT 2:28 Waa a ten a kám ar ɗe mo a mǝ seen nghan. Kǝ gha mbǝ ngam pǝtuup fen shi retnyit ntoom fwaa zak.>
ACT 2:29 <<Ɗyemnaa mo, wu lekom, kǝ nghan leshap ɗi nwun rǝrret nkaa puunkaam fun Devit, ɗe gyet wur muut, ɓǝ mo wum wur, kǝcir wur nǝ ɗi mpee ɗesǝ har cicinsǝ.
ACT 2:30 Gyet wur a ngusat pwoo mǝ Naan, ɗang wur man mbii ɗe Naan kǝ ten cweer nǝnee, wur nyool le memee nɗǝǝn ɗang wur mo, kǝ nwur ɗee ɗi a mishkoom koo Devit sǝ.
ACT 2:31 Gyet Devit kǝ ten naa mbii ɗe Naan nyool cìn akyeen, a kǝsǝ ɓǝ, wur leshap nkaa yool mǝ Kristi a peemúut nǝnee. Baa Naan nyit wur a peemúut kas, kǝ baa fwooshik wur nǝn nwam nɗǝǝn kǝcir kas.
ACT 2:32 A Jesu ɗesǝ ɗe Naan kǝ yool kǝ wur a peemúut, ɗang mun sǝ jir, mun a langtǝng nǝ Jesu kǝ yool a peemúut.
ACT 2:33 Mo kǝ le Jesu a ɗeɗes, yaksǝ wur kǝ tong nsarse mǝ Naan, wur kǝ lap Riin Ɗeɓang pǝ Naan kaaɗe gyet wur kǝ cweer sǝ. Mbii ɗe wuu naa, kǝ ɗe wuu kǝlǝng sǝ, a zuum mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang ɗewur kǝ ɗoo shin sham nkaa mun.
ACT 2:34 Baa gyet Devit kǝ kaa aɗeng kas, ɗang wur shikáa fin sat nǝnee <Daa wur kǝ sat nDaa fen nǝnee, A tong nsarse fen.
ACT 2:35 Dǝm wul a ɗe an nle shaarlek fwaa mo ɗee a mbii leshii ngha.>
ACT 2:36 <<Mbǝ mǝnǝ, wu yit kǝ nnen Isreil mo jir, mo man azeen-zeen nǝnee, An pǝ leshap a nkaa Jesu ɗe wu pwas wur sǝ. Ɗangɓe Naan kǝ le wur ɗee a Daa, kǝ Kristi zak.>>
ACT 2:37 Kaaɗe gurum nǝ mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ sul pǝtuup mmo hakyeng, yaksǝ mo sat mPita kǝ koor jeplep nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, mun mbǝ ncìn a mii?>>
ACT 2:38 Ɓǝ Pita lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wu tuwap, mbǝkǝ mmo cìn baptisma ɗi nwun jir ngwe ɗeɗangyii nɗǝǝn wun, nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Jesu Kristi, mbǝkǝ nNaan fwo shikbish fuu mo ɗi nwun. Ɓǝ wun mbǝ lap zuum mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang.
ACT 2:39 Pwoo ɗe mo cweer nǝ, a mbǝ wun, kǝ jep fuu mo, kǝ mbǝ nen ɗejong mo jir, kǝ koo a ngwe ɗeɗangyii ɗe Daa fun Naan wur mpet zak.>>
ACT 2:40 Shi pwoo mo ɗes, ɓǝ wur leshap mmo ɓalɓal, ɗang wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu shang káa fuu mo mɓut kar ɗe nǝ mbǝ jì nkaa nen ɗebish ɗe nyicinsǝ mo.>>
ACT 2:41 Nen ɗe mo shinzeen mpwoo ɗewur le nǝ, ɓǝ mo cìn baptisma mmo, parpuus mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo kat gurum mo ɗyikye koo ngal kun sǝ.
ACT 2:42 Moo tong ashak shidaar-shidaar mbǝ kǝlǝng kám mǝ jeplep Jesu mo, kǝ shaar ashak, kǝ moo sese ashak, kǝ ɗangnaan ashak zak. Tong Nǝ Dǝm Dan Jesu Mo
ACT 2:43 Jeplep mǝ Jesu nǝ mo, cìn mbii aapwoo mo kǝ mbii lukshik mo ɗes, nǝ le kǝ gurum mo kǝǝr Naan zam.
ACT 2:44 Nen ɗe mo shinzeen nJesu jir, ɓǝ mo ɓalkaa mo mo ashak, kǝ mo le mbii mo mo ashak jir, a pee mǝndong.
ACT 2:45 Mo sǝrep mbii mo mo, kǝ long fur mo jir, mbǝkǝ mo shwap ɗi ashak, koo a wii, ɓǝ baa wur kat mee mbii jee nwur kas.
ACT 2:46 Koo puus ɗeɗangyii ɓǝ moo dǝm kuur ashak, nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝzak mo kǝ se mbiise fur mo ashak nɗǝǝn lu fur mo shi retnyit hakyeng, kǝ shi pǝtuup ɗemǝndong.
ACT 2:47 Moo kwoop Naan, ɗang gurum moo kǝlǝng retnyit kǝ mo. Koo a puus ɗeɗangyii, ɓǝ Daa wur jì kǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ kat ɓam ɗyikye mmo.
ACT 3:1 Par sǝ ɓǝ Pita kǝ Joon mo kàa nLu Naan ɗeɗes mbǝ ɗangnaan koo kun ɗe mǝ puus sǝ.
ACT 3:2 Yaksǝ mo kat mee gwar ɗe mo làa wur a kurumkut mpwoo lu nǝ, ɗe moo pet a Ɗeret. Koo puus ɗeɗangyii ɓǝ moo mang wur jì le mpwoo lu nǝ, mbǝkǝ nwur ɗang shool ɗi pǝ nen ɗe moo ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ.
ACT 3:3 Kaaɗe wur naa Pita kǝ Joon mo mbǝ ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan nǝ, ɓǝ wur ɗang shool pǝ mo.
ACT 3:4 Pita kǝ Joon mo ban yit nkaa wur. Ɓǝ Pita sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<A naa mun.>>
ACT 3:5 Yaksǝ wur lepyit nkaa mo, mbǝɗe wur pan nǝ, mon nshin mee mbii nɗin.
ACT 3:6 Pita sat ngwar nǝ nǝnee, <<Baa an kǝ mee shool azurfa, koo zinariya kas. Mbii ɗe an kǝ nǝ, ɓǝ an nshin ngha. Nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Jesu Kristi ngu Nazaret, a yool a mwaan.>>
ACT 3:7 Pita yaa sarse mǝ gwar nǝ, kǝn nwur wur ɗiyeep gwar nǝ ɗi. Yaksǝ abet-abet, ɓǝ kwakshii wur mo, kǝ ɓaas wur mo katɓal.
ACT 3:8 Ɓǝ gwar nǝ yool mǝreppee shi shii fin mo, ɗang wur ɗoom mwaan, dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ ashak kǝ mo zak. Wur nkaa mwaan, ɗang wur nkaa mǝreppee, kǝzak wur nkaa kwoop Naan.
ACT 3:9 Kaaɗe gurum mo naa wur nkaa mwaan, ɗang wur nkaa kwoop Naan,
ACT 3:10 ɓǝ mo man nǝ, a gwar ɗe di moo mang wur jì le mpwoo lu Naan ɗe moo pet a Ɗeret mbǝkǝ nwur ɗang shool ɗi pǝ gurum mo. Nǝ aapwoo ngurum nǝ mo zam, kǝzak nǝ lekǝǝrmuut mo mbǝ mbii ɗe mo cin ngwar nǝ.
ACT 3:11 Kaaɗe gwar nǝ wur ɗyiin nɗang Pita kǝ Joon, ɓǝ nǝ aapwoo ngurum nǝ mo zam, yaksǝ mo su dǝm pǝ mo ɗi nɗǝǝn kuut ɗe moo pet a mǝ Solomon.
ACT 3:12 Kaaɗe Pita naa a kǝsǝ, ɓǝ wur sat ngurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wun nen Isreil mo! A mii le ɗang bar gwar ɗesǝ nǝ aapwoo nwun yii? A mii le ɗang wuu ban yit nkaa mun, koo a shi mee ɗeɗes fun, koo a shi mee ɗeret fun, ɗang mu le ngwar ɗesǝ mwaan yii?
ACT 3:13 A Naan mǝ Abraham kǝ mǝ Aizik kǝ mǝ Jekop, kǝ mǝ puun fun mo, a wur le nguɗak fin Jesu a ɗeɗes. Dǝ a wun wu seet Jesu, ɗang wu cii wur ntoom Pailet, kaaɗe Pailet sat nǝ, ɗyin mbǝ ɓwet Jesu.
ACT 3:14 Dǝ wu cii ngwe Ɗeɓang, ɗewur a ngwe ɗe ndǝre, mbǝkǝ nwun ɗang mmo ɓwet a ngutukáa ɗi nwun.
ACT 3:15 Wu tu ngwe ɗewur a tuus mǝ seen, ɗe a wur shin seen ngurum mo. Ɗangɓe Naan yool kǝ wur a peemúut, ɗang mun a langtǝng mǝnǝ.
ACT 3:16 A shi shinzeen nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Jesu, a nǝ le ɗang gwar ɗesǝ, kat bar. Gwar ɗe wu naa, kǝ ɗe wu man sǝ. A nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Jesu, kǝ shinzeen ɗe nǝ put pǝ wur ɗi, a nǝ le ngwar ɗesǝ wur ɗee a ngu nkoom kǝdǝng-dǝng, a yit fuu jir.
ACT 3:17 <<Yaksǝ ɗyemnaa mo, wen man nǝ, mbii ɗe dǝ wun kǝ nennan fuu mo, wu cìn nJesu, ɓǝ dǝ wu cìn a mbǝ ciin man.
ACT 3:18 Ɗangɓe Naan yit kǝ mo cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo jir, a mbǝkǝ mmo gampwoo ɗe gyet Naan kǝ ten sat mpwoo nensatpwoo fin mo nǝ, Kristi fin mbǝ shwaajeel.
ACT 3:19 Wu tuwap, mbǝkǝ nwun ciir pǝ Naan ɗi, mbǝkǝ nNaan fwoo shikbish fuu mo ɗi nwun. Katɗang wu tuwap azeen-zeen, ɓǝ Naan mbǝ naa ngam wun shi mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Riin fin, mbǝkǝ taji nǝ waam wun kas.
ACT 3:20 Kǝ wur mbǝ lep Jesu Kristi, ɗewur kǝ ten bǝlǝp wur mbǝ wun.
ACT 3:21 Wur mbǝ tong nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, dǝm wul parɗe Naan ciir kǝ mbii mo ɗee a ɗepwoo jir akuɗang. Kaaɗe gyet Naan kǝ ten cweer mpwoo nensatpwoo fin ɗeɓang mo pǝgyet ɗi yam-yam sǝ.
ACT 3:22 Gyet Mosis sat nǝnee, <Daa Naan fuu mbǝ yool kǝ mee ngusatpwoo fin nwun, mɓut nnen fuu mo, kaa wen sǝ.> Nǝ a tǝng nwun lekom, kǝ nwun kǝlǝng mbii ɗewur mbǝ sat mo ɗi nwun jir.
ACT 3:23 Koo a ngwe ɗeɗangyii ɗe baa wur mbǝ lekom kǝ nwur kǝlǝng ngusatpwoo Naan mǝnǝ ɗi kas, ɓǝ mon nshang wur baa kǝ nǝ mɓut nen Naan mo.
ACT 3:24 Nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo jir, yool mɓít Samuwel, kǝ nensatpwoo Naan ɗe mo jì mɓwoon wur zak, mo jir mo kǝ ten leshap nkaa teer ɗesǝ mo.
ACT 3:25 Pwoo ɗe gyet Naan wur cweer mpwoo nensatpwoo fin mo nǝ a mbǝ wun, kǝ nwun sekop mǝ mbii ɗe gyet Naan wur kǝ ten cweer mpuun fuu mo shi toom, kǝ ɗe gyet wur sat Abraham nǝnee, <A nɗǝǝn ɗang fwaa, ɓǝ gurum ɗe nɗǝǝn yil nǝ mo jir, mon nkat ɗeret.>
ACT 3:26 Kaaɗe Naan wur bǝlǝp nguɗak fin, ɓǝ Naan wur shee lep wur shin jì a pǝ wun ɗi, mbǝkǝ nwur le ɗeret ɗi nkaa wun, kǝ mbǝkǝ nǝ ciir ɗi kǝ koo a wii nɗǝǝn wun, kǝ nwur yit cìn mbii ɗebish mo ɗi.>>
ACT 4:1 Kaaɗe Pita kǝ Joon, mo ɗi nkaa leshap ngurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ pak pris mo, kǝ ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ nentap Lu Naan ɗeɗes, kǝ pak nen Sadusi mo, mo jì pǝ mo ɗi.
ACT 4:2 Nǝ láa mmo mɓut, mbǝɗe jeplep ɗevǝl nǝ mo, nkaa kám ngurum mo nǝ, Jesu kǝ yool a peemúut. Ɗe nǝ kám nǝ, katɗang gurum mo murep, ɓǝ mon nyool a peemúut mmǝnǝ.
ACT 4:3 Mo yaa Pita kǝ Joon, ɓǝ mo dǝm shoot mo teer nlushoot, mbǝɗe kansǝǝn kǝ cìn.
ACT 4:4 Jir aasǝ gurum mo ɗes mo shinzeen mpwoo nǝ, ɗe daas mo kus kǝ wul ngal paat.
ACT 4:5 Dǝɗaar nǝ, ɓǝ nen taatǝleng mǝ nen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo mo, kǝ nenkám Wàar Mosis mo, mo kuur ashak, nJerusalem.
ACT 4:6 Kǝ Anas ɗewur a pris ɗeɗes met jir, wur ɗi ashak kǝ mo, kǝ Kayafas, kǝ Joon kǝ Alekzanda, kǝ nen ɗe mo a ɗang mǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ zak.
ACT 4:7 Kaaɗe mo lep kǝ mmo dǝm jì kǝ Pita kǝ Joon, ɓǝ mo le mmo ɗar ntoom mo. Yaksǝ mo ɗoom tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<A shi ɗeɗes mǝ wii, koo a nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ wii, ɓǝ wuu cìn mbii ɗesǝ yii?>>
ACT 4:8 Mbǝɗǝ Pita wur gam kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, ɓǝ wur lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wun nen taatǝleng mǝ gurum mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo.
ACT 4:9 Katɗang wu tokɗyeel mun cicinsǝ a mbǝ ɗeret ɗe mo cìn ngwar ɗe dǝ wur a kurumkut sǝ, kǝ nkaa ar ɗe gwar nǝ wur ɗee a ɗebǝbar sǝ,
ACT 4:10 ɓǝ wu yit kǝ mbii ɗesǝ ɗee a mǝ man pǝ wun ɗi, kǝ nen Isreil mo jir nee, a shi sǝm mǝ Jesu Kristi ngu Nazaret, ɗe wu pwas wur nkaa shiyeep ɗewur muut, ɗangnaan yool kǝ wur a peemúut. A mbǝ Jesu, ɗang gwar ɗesǝ wur ɗar ntoom fuu a ɗebǝbar.
ACT 4:11 A Jesu a ngwe ɗe mo kǝ ten ran pwoo nkaa wur nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Naan nǝnee, <Ngǝk ɗe wun nen ɗyiklu mo wu cii, ɓǝ a nǝ ɗee a ngǝk ɗekǝkoop met jir nɗǝǝn kwang mǝ lu nǝ.>
ACT 4:12 Baa gurum mon nwaa mak kat mee ɓam pǝ mee ngwe ɗi kas. Mbǝɗǝ nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ jir, ɓǝ baa Naan kǝ shin ɗeɗes mmee ngwe, mbǝkǝ nwur ɓam gurum mo ɗi kas, tǝng a nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu Kristi ɓejee ɗak>>
ACT 4:13 Kaaɗe mo naa Pita kǝ Joon, mo leshap ɓalɓal, baa kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas, ɓǝ nǝ aapwoo mmo, mbǝɗe baa Pita kǝ Joon mo a mee mbii kas, kǝzak baa mo kǝ kam tang ran dǝm jong kas zak nǝ tang mo pǝtuup nǝ ɗe mo ashak kǝ Jesu.
ACT 4:14 Baa nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo mak cìn mee mbii kas, mbǝɗe mo naa gwar ɗe mo kǝ bar wur nǝ, wur ɗar ɗi ashak kǝ Pita kǝ Joon.
ACT 4:15 Aasǝ, ɓǝ mo le kǝ mmo pwat kǝ Pita kǝ Joon, mbǝkǝ mmo ɓeet ɗi ashak mbii ɗe mon ncìn kǝ mo.
ACT 4:16 Mo sat nǝnee, <<Mmun ncìn a mii kǝ nen ɗesǝ mo yii? Azeen-zeen gurum ɗe moo tong nɗǝǝn nJerusalem jir, mo kǝ man nǝ, Naan kǝ cìn mee mbii lukshik ɗeɗes nsar kǝ Pita kǝ Joon, ɗang baa mun mmak cíipwoo nǝ kas.
ACT 4:17 Mbǝkǝ taji gurum mo ɗes mo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ kas, ɓǝ wu yit kǝ mmun cíi mmo nǝ, taji mo baa leshap ɗi mmee gurum nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu kas.>>
ACT 4:18 Kaaɗe mo waa pet Pita kǝ Joon mo ɗel, ɓǝ mo sat mmo ɓalɓal nǝnee, <<Taji wu baa wu sat meepwoo, koo wu kám mee mbii nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu kas.>>
ACT 4:19 Ɗangɓe Pita kǝ Joon mo lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wun shikáa fuu wu ɓeet, kyet nǝn nret nNaan nyit kǝ mmun cìn a mbii ɗe wun wu sat aa? Koo a mbii ɗe Naan sat yii?
ACT 4:20 Baa mun mbǝ nook leshap nkaa mbii ɗe mu naa, kǝ mbii ɗe mu kǝlǝng kas.>>
ACT 4:21 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ gwak mo ɓalɓal kǝ lekǝǝrmuut mmo, ɓǝ mo ɓwet mo, baa nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo mak cin mee kar ɗebish mPita kǝ Joon kas, mbǝɗe gurum nǝ mo jir, mon nkaa kwoop Naan mbǝ mbii ɗe mo naa nǝ cìn.
ACT 4:22 Gwar ɗe mo bar wur shi ar ɗe mǝ aapwoo nǝ, ɓit wur mo met nlaarfeer.
ACT 4:23 Kaaɗe mo ɓwet Pita kǝ Joon, ɓǝ mo dǝm pǝ nniyee fur mo ɗi. Mo sat nniyee fur nǝ mo, mbii ɗe pris ɗenan-nan mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo sat mmo jir.
ACT 4:24 Kaaɗe nen shinzeen nǝ mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo ɗangnaan shi pǝtuup mǝndong, nǝnee, <<Daa Ɗehai, ɗe waa a le ɗeng kǝ yil, kǝ am kuur mo, kǝ mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn mo jir.
ACT 4:25 Gyet a shi Riin Ɗeɓang, ɓǝ waa a leshap mpwoo mǝ kǝrem fwaa ɗewur a puunkaam fun Devit nǝnee <A mii le ɗang gurum ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, mo yool ntuup yii? A mii le ɗang gurum nǝ mo kǝ pan ɗebish nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo, mbǝ cìn mbii ɗebuu mo yii?
ACT 4:26 Deskoom ɗe mǝ yil nǝ mo, mo kǝ ɗak sut fur mo mbǝ lek, kǝ nenpanyil mo kǝ ɓalkaa fur mo ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo yaa lek ɗi kǝ Daa Naan kǝ Kristi fin zak.>
ACT 4:27 Mbǝɗǝ azeen-zeen nɗǝǝn pee nkaam ɗesǝ, ɓǝ Herot kǝ Pontus Pailet, ashak kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ nen Isreil mo, mo kǝ kuur ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗee a shaarlek mǝ nguɗak fwaa Jesu Ɗeɓang, ɗe waa a bǝlǝp wur, ɗe a gha le nwur ɗee a Kristi.
ACT 4:28 Mo kuur ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo cìn koo a mbii ɗeɗangyii ɗe a gha aa ten a le shi iiko fwaa kǝ reɓet fwaa nǝ, mbii nǝ mon ncìn a kǝsǝ.
ACT 4:29 Yaksǝ Daa Naan a naa kǝǝrmuut ɗe moo le mmun. A shínɓal mmun kǝrem fwaa mo, mbǝkǝ mmun satpwoo fwaa ɗi ɓalɓal, baa ashak kǝ kǝǝrmuut kas.
ACT 4:30 A le kǝn iiko fwaa nǝ bar gurum mo, kǝ a le kǝ mbii lukshik mo kǝ mbii aapwoo mo cìn nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ nguɗak fwaa Jesu Ɗeɓang.>>
ACT 4:31 Kaaɗe mo kyes ɗangnaan mǝnǝ, ɓǝ pee ɗe moo kuur ɗi ashak, nǝ sǝǝn. Mo gam kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang jir, yaksǝ mo yaa satpwoo mǝ Naan ɓalɓal agaak, baa ashak kǝ kǝǝrmuut kas.
ACT 4:32 Nen ɗe mo shinzeen nJesu jir, ɓǝ pan mo mo, kǝ mǝse mo mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong jir zak. Baa mee gurum nɗǝǝn mo mak sat nǝ, long fin nǝ a mǝnǝ mbǝshin kas, ɗang mo le mbii fur mo jir, ashak.
ACT 4:33 Jeplep nǝ mo ɗee a langtǝng shi iiko, nkaa yool mǝ Daa Jesu a peemúut. Daa Naan le ɗeret nkaa mo jir hakyeng.
ACT 4:34 Baa mee ngwe ɗee, a ngujeel nɗǝǝn mo koo mǝndong kas, mbǝɗe nen ɗe mo kǝ maar mo, kǝ lu mo, ɓǝ mo sǝrep mo jir,
ACT 4:35 ɓǝ mo jì shin shool mǝ mbii ɗe mo kǝ sǝrep nǝ mon njeplep mǝ Jesu nǝ mo. Ɓǝ jeplep nǝ mo shwap shool nǝ nnen shinzeen nǝ mo nciit-nciit, mbǝkǝ koo ngwe ɗeɗangyii, ɓǝ wur kat mbii ɗewur kǝ reɓet.
ACT 4:36 Kaaɗe mo nkaa cìn mǝnǝ kǝsǝ, ɓǝ Josep ngu Livai, ɗewur put a nyil nSaiprus, kǝ ɗe jeplep nǝ mo le sǝm nwur a Barnabas, (ɗe shii mǝ sǝm mǝnǝ a nǝ, Ngwe ɗewur kǝ caapee).
ACT 4:37 Wur mang mee maar fin seet, ɓǝ wur jì shin shool nǝ jir njeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 5:1 Mee gwar ɗi, ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Ananiyas, kǝ mat fin Saffira, mo mang mee maar fur mo seet.
ACT 5:2 Ɗangɓe wur kǝ mat fin mo ɓalpwoo mo ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo sok pak shool nǝ ɗi, ɗang Ananiyas jì shin koor shool nǝ njeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 5:3 Ɗangɓe Pita sat nǝnee, <<Ananiyas, a mii le ɗang a yit kǝ nngujwaan gam pǝtuup fwaa, kǝn nghan cìn ɗung ɗi nRiin Ɗeɓangyii? Mbǝɗǝ aa sok pak shool maar nǝ.
ACT 5:4 Akuɗang aa mang maar nǝ a seet, ɓǝ baa dǝ nǝ a mwaa kas aa? Kǝzak aɓwoon ɗe dǝ a mang maar nǝ a seet, ɓǝ baa shool nǝ a mwaa kas ee? A mii le ɗang a kat pan mǝ cìn mbii ɗesǝ nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fwaa yii? Baa a cìn ɗung ɗesǝ nǝ a ngurum mo kas, a cìn ɗung nǝ a nNaan.>>
ACT 5:5 Kaaɗe Ananiyas kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur taa nyil, wur muut. Nen ɗe mo kǝlǝng muut nǝ jir, ɓǝ kǝǝrmuut ɗeɗes yaa mo hakyeng.
ACT 5:6 Zǝlang mo jì ɗel nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, ɓǝ mo ɓwoot kúm wur nǝ shi zaal, ɓǝ mo mang kúm nǝ put kǝ nǝ a tool, ɗang dǝm wum wur.
ACT 5:7 Aɓwoon ɗe mo tong koo awa kun sǝ, ɓǝ mat wur Saffira jì ɗel nlu nǝ. Baa war man mbii ɗe nǝ kǝ tung kas.
ACT 5:8 Pita tal pǝ war nǝnee, <<Yi sat nghan, kyet a jee mǝ shool ɗe wu seet kǝ maar nǝ nɗesǝ aa?>> War lap nǝnee, <<Ii, a jee shool nǝ mmǝnǝ.>>
ACT 5:9 Pita sat nwar nǝnee, <<A mii le ɗang wu ɓalpwoo ashak kǝ mish fii, mbǝkǝ nwun wu kam Riin mǝ Daa Naan ɗi ee? Yi kǝlǝng shii mǝ nen ɗe mo waa nwum mish fii mo kǝ jì wul mpwoo lu sǝ. Mo mbǝ mang kúm fii nǝ put kǝ nǝ a kǝsǝ zak.>>
ACT 5:10 Abet-abet ɓǝ war sham taa nyil nshii Pita, yaksǝ war muut. Kaaɗe zǝlang nǝ mo jì ɗel nlu nǝ, ɓǝ mo kat war kǝ muut, ɓǝ mo mang kúm nǝ put kǝ nǝ a tool, ɓǝ mo dǝm wum war pǝshak kǝ mish fer.
ACT 5:11 Kǝǝrmuut ɗeɗes yaa nen shinzeen nǝ mo jir, kǝ nen ɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mbii mǝnǝ mo.
ACT 5:12 Jeplep nǝ mo cìn mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo mo ɗes, nnaar gurum nǝ mo. Nenshínzeen nǝ moo kuur ashak jir nɗǝǝn kuut mǝ Solomon shi pǝtuup ɗemǝndong.
ACT 5:13 Ɗangɓe nɗǝǝn koor gurum ɗe baa mo shinzeen kas, ɓǝ baa mee ngwe mak gung, ɗewur mɓàlkáa fin ashak kǝ mo kas. Jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ gurum mo kǝ kwoop mo hakyeng.
ACT 5:14 Gurum mo ɗes, daas mo kǝ shurep mo, mo shinzeen nDaa, ɓǝ mo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak kǝ nen shinzeen nǝ mo, ɗe nen shinzeen nǝ mo ɗes hakyeng.
ACT 5:15 Mbǝ mbii aapwoo ɗe jeplep nǝ mo cìn, ɓǝ gurum mo kok nengok mo jì le pǝkom ar nkaa gwaansaam mo, kǝ kurkwaa mo, mbǝkǝ katɗang Pita jì ɗel, ɓǝ mǝ riin wur nǝ ntáa tung pak nengok nǝ mo ɗi.
ACT 5:16 Nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil ɗe mo neer Jerusalem ciirkaat mo jì kuur. Mo jì kǝ nen ɗe baa mo kǝlǝng koom kas, kǝ nen ɗe riin ɗebish mo kǝ lejeel mmo, ɓǝ jeplep nǝ mo bar mo jir.
ACT 5:17 Pris ɗeɗes met jir kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur jir, ɗe mo a soon mǝ nen Sadusi mo, mo gam kǝ zuur mbǝ jeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 5:18 Mo yak jeplep nǝ mo, mo dǝm le mo nɗǝǝn lushoot.
ACT 5:19 Ɗangɓe mpar, ɓǝ mee ngulep mǝ Daa jì wang pwoo lushoot nǝ mmo, ɓǝ wur pwat kǝ mo, ɗang wur sat mmo nǝnee,
ACT 5:20 <<Wu dǝm, wu ɗar nɗǝǝn Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝn nwun satpwoo mǝ seen ɗesǝ nǝ ɗi ngurum mo jir.>>
ACT 5:21 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ ɗaar mɓít-mɓít, mo dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓǝ mo yaa kámpwoo Naan ngurum mo. Ɓǝ pris ɗeɗes met nǝ jì kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur, ɓǝ mo pǝrep nenɓeetpwoo mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan ɗe mǝ nen Yahudi mo, mo kuur ashak jir. Yaksǝ mo lep jepkam mo shindǝm nlushoot nǝ, mbǝkǝ mmo jì ɗi kǝ jeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 5:22 Ɗangɓe kaaɗe jepkam nǝ mo dǝm, ɓǝ baa mo dǝm kat jeplep nǝ mo ɗi nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ kas. Yaksǝ jepkam nǝ mo baaji sat mmo nǝnee,
ACT 5:23 <<Mu kat lushoot nǝ a shishoot rǝrret, kǝ nentappee nǝ mo kǝ ɗar mpwoo lu nǝ mo, ɗang kaaɗe mu wang lu nǝ, ɓǝ baa mu kat jeplep nǝ mo ɗi kas.>>
ACT 5:24 Kaaɗe ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa nentap Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝ pris ɗǝnan-nan mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ daampee mmo zam, mbǝ jeplep nǝ mo, mbǝɗe baa mo man mbii ɗe nǝ kǝ kat jeplep nǝ mo kas.
ACT 5:25 Mee gurum jì sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu naa, nen ɗe wu le mo nɗǝǝn lushoot sǝ, mon nkaa kam-kam ngurum mo nɗǝǝn Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ.>>
ACT 5:26 Yaksǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa nentap Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ dǝm, ashak kǝ pak nentap lu mǝ Naan nǝ mo, mo dǝm jì kǝ jeplep nǝ mo. Ɗang baa mo dǝm jì kǝ mo a shi mee ɓal kas, mbǝɗe mo kǝǝr gurum nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ taji gurum nǝ mo car mo shi ndǝng kas.
ACT 5:27 Kaaɗe mo jì kǝ jeplep nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo le mmo ɗar ntoom mǝ nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo. Yaksǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ tal pǝ Pita kǝ Joon nǝnee,
ACT 5:28 <<Muu tǝǝrsar nwun ɓalɓal nǝ, taji baa wu kám mee mbii ngurum mo nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu kas. Ɗangɓe mbii ɗe wuu cìn ɗesǝ nǝ, wuu ɗaar a mbǝkǝ nwun sat ɗi ngurum mo nǝ, a mun mu tu gwar ɗesǝ nǝ, kǝzak wu gam Jerusalem shi kám fuu ɗesǝ nǝ zak.>>
ACT 5:29 Ɗangɓe Pita kǝ jeplep nǝ mo, mo lap mmo nǝnee, <<Nǝ a tǝng kǝ mun cìn a mbii ɗe Naan sat, met mbii ɗe gurum mo sat.
ACT 5:30 Jesu ɗe wu tu wur, ɗe wu pwas wur nkaa shiyeepyoom, ɓǝ Naan mǝ puun fun mo, kǝ yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut.
ACT 5:31 Naan kǝ yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut, ɓǝ yaksǝ Jesu kǝ tong nsarse mǝ Naan, a wur a Laakop kǝ Nguɓam zak. A wur wang ar tuwap nnen Isreil mo, mbǝkǝ nNaan fwo shikbish mo mo ɗi zak.
ACT 5:32 Mun a langtǝng mǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo, kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang ɗe Naan shin nnen ɗe mo cìn ɗyen wur, mo kǝ cìn langtǝng nǝ a kǝsǝ zak.>>
ACT 5:33 Kaaɗe kuur mǝ nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ láa mmo mɓut hakyeng, dǝm wul a ɗe moo reɓet twe jeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 5:34 Ɗang mee ngu Farisi ɗe kǝ kám Wàar mǝ Mosis, ɗi sǝm wur a Gamaliyel, gurum mo jir mo kǝ shin ɗeɗes nwur. Wur yool ɗar atǝng nɗǝǝn lu ɓeetpwoo nǝ, ɓǝ wur le kǝ mmo pwat kǝ jeplep nǝ mo a tool ɓe reppee lee.
ACT 5:35 Ɓǝ wur sat nnen ɓeetpwoo nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, nen Isreil mo. Wu tap kǝ mbii ɗe wuu reɓet cìn nǝn ndes ɗesǝ mo.
ACT 5:36 Gyet yam-yam, ɓǝ mee gwar ɗe, ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Tudas, wur kǝ cam yool a kǝsǝ. Gyet wur lekáa fin a koo mee ngwe ɗeɗes sǝ, ɗe gurum mo koo kambil feer sǝ mo dǝm nɗang wur. Ɗang aɓwoon ɗe mo tu wur, ɓǝ nen ɗe mo dǝm nɗang wur nǝ jir, mo rangkáa, baa mo ɗee a mee mbii kas.
ACT 5:37 Aɓwoon Tudas, ɓǝ Judas, mee ngu Galili yool zak, nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗe moo tang ɗuu gurum mo ɗi, yaksǝ wur dul pak gurum mo dǝm nɗang shin, ɗang aɓwoon ɗe mo tu wur zak, ɓǝ nen ɗe mo dǝm nɗang wur jir, mo rangkáa.
ACT 5:38 Mbǝmǝnǝ an pǝ sat nwun, taji wu cìn mee mbii ndes ɗesǝ mo kas. Wu yit mo mbǝsut. Mbǝɗǝ katɗang pwoo ɗe moo kám ngurum mo, kǝ ɗak ɗe mo kǝ cìn nǝ a mǝ mǝse mǝ gurum, ɓǝ nǝn nyool ɗee a ɗebuu.
ACT 5:39 Ɗang katɗang mbii ɗe moo cìn nǝ a mǝ Naan, ɓǝ baa mu mmak se koorong nkaa mo kas. Wu tap taji nwun ɗee koo wun a nlek kǝ Naan sǝ kas.>>
ACT 5:40 Nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo kǝlǝngkar Gamaliyel nǝ. Mo pǝrep jeplep nǝ mo cin jì ɗel zak, ɓǝ mo sǝrem mo, kǝzak mo tǝǝrsar mmo ɓalɓal nǝnee, <<Taji baa wu sat mee pwoo ɗi nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu zak kas.>> Aɓwoon pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo ɓwet mo.
ACT 5:41 Jeplep nǝ mo pwat ntoom mǝ nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo shi retnyit, mbǝɗe mo mak shwaajeel mbǝ sǝm mǝ Jesu.
ACT 5:42 Yool parmǝnǝ, ɓǝ baa mo nook kám kǝ leshap mǝ Naan ngurum mo, nɗǝǝn Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ kǝ nɗǝǝn lu mǝ gurum mo, koo puus ɗeɗangyii kas, nǝ Jesu a Kristi.
ACT 6:1 Kaaɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗoom yaa ɓul, nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ mee ɓǝlep yool nnaar mǝ nnen ɗe mo man pwoo mǝ nen Grik mo kǝ nen Yahudi ɗe mo kǝ tong nJerusalem, mbǝɗe nen ɗe mo man pwoo Grik nǝ mo sat nǝ, baa mo kǝ shìn mbiise Matkáa fur mo mɓut mbiise ɗe moo shwap shidaar-shidaar kas.
ACT 6:2 Aasǝ ɓǝ, jeplep ɗe kaapaat baavǝl nǝ mo pǝrep kuur mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo jir, kǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Baa nǝ ret kǝ mmun nook satpwoo mǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ mu ɗee ɗi ɓàk mbiise kas.
ACT 6:3 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɗyemnaa mo, wu bǝlǝp mee gurum mo pwoovǝl nnaar fuu, ɗe mo kǝ mǝse ɗeret, kǝ ɗe mo gam kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, kǝ ɗe mo manshii mǝ mbii zak. Mbǝkǝ mun le mo tap ɗi kǝ ɗak shwap mbiise nǝ.
ACT 6:4 Ɗang mun, mbǝ sekyeen kǝ ɗangnaan shidaar-shidaar kǝ satpwoo mǝ Naan.>>
ACT 6:5 Pwoo ɗe jeplep nǝ mo sat nǝ, ret nkuur mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo jir. Aasǝ ɓǝ mo bǝlǝp Stivin, ɗewur gam kǝ shinzeen, kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, kǝ Filip, kǝ Prokorus, kǝ Nikanor, kǝ Timoti, kǝ Parmenas, kǝ Nikolas ngu Antiyok, ɗe gyet wur kǝ piring mbǝ seyil nNaan mǝ nen Yahudi mo.
ACT 6:6 Mo jì kǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ bǝlǝp mo ntoom jeplep nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo ɗangnaan kǝzak mo lesar fur mo nkaa mo.
ACT 6:7 Pwoo Naan nǝ sekyeen, dǝm wul a ɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nJerusalem mo ɓul ɗes hakyeng, kǝ pris mo ɗes mo shinzeen nJesu Kristi.
ACT 6:8 Stivin, ɗewur gam kǝ ɗeret kǝ ɓal mǝ Naan, wur cìn mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo ɗenan mo nnaar gurum mo.
ACT 6:9 Ɗangɓe pak gurum mo ɗi, ɗe mo a mmee lu Naan ɗe mo kǝ pet a lu Naan mǝ nen Frimen mo. Nen ɗesǝ mo a nnen Yahudi ɗe mo pwat nyil nSairin, kǝ Alekzandriya, kǝ ngaar yil nSilisiya, kǝ mǝ yil Eshiya mo zak, mo yool kǝ pwoo mo, kǝ ɓeetshik nkaa Stivin.
ACT 6:10 Ɗang baa mo mak katɓal ɗe mon nɗar kǝn mo cin ɓeetshik ɗi kǝ Stivin kas, mbǝɗe wur leshap a shi ɗyen ɗe Riin mǝ Naan shin nwur.
ACT 6:11 Mo kar pak gurum mo a sǝsok, mbǝkǝ mmo sat ɗi nǝnee, <<Mu kǝlǝng Stivin satpwoo ɗebish nkaa Mosis, ɗang wur baa satpwoo ɗebuu nkaa Naan zak.>>
ACT 6:12 Pwoo ɗe mo sat nǝ láa ngurum nǝ mo mɓut, ɓǝ pak nen ɗǝnan-nan mo, kǝ pak nenkám Wàar Mosis mo. Mo yool kǝ tuup, mo dǝm yaa Stivin, ɓǝ mo jì kǝ wur ntoom mǝ kuur mǝ nenɓeetpwoo mo.
ACT 6:13 Kǝzak mo jì kǝ langtǝng mǝ ɗung mo, ɗe mo sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur leshap ɗebish nkaa Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝ nkaa Wàar Mosis shidaar-shidaar zak.
ACT 6:14 Mu kǝlǝng wur sat nǝ, Jesu ngu Nazaret mbǝ shirip Lu mǝ Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝn nwur cǝǝr kǝ mbii ɗe muu loot kǝ cìn mo, ɗe gyet Mosis shin mo mmun.>>
ACT 6:15 Nen ɗe moo tong ɗi a pee ɓeetpwoo nǝ jir, mo ban yit fur mo nkaa Stivin, ɓǝ mo naa yit wur nǝ ɗee a koo yit ngulep mǝ Naan sǝ.
ACT 7:1 Pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ wur tal pǝ Stivin nǝnee, <<Mbii ɗe moo sat nkaa gha sǝ, mo azeen aa?>>
ACT 7:2 Yaksǝ Stivin lap nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, kǝ puun mo, wu lekom, kǝn nwun kǝlǝng mbii ɗe an mbǝ sat nǝ ɗi. Gyet Naan Ɗehai wur woo shin fin mpuun fun Abraham, ɓǝ wur kutɗi nyil mMesopotamiya, akuɗang wur dǝm tong nɗǝǝn yil nHaran.
ACT 7:3 Naan sat nwur nǝnee, <A yool a yit yil fwaa, kǝ ɗang fwaa mo zak, kǝn nghan dǝm ɗi mmee yil ɗe an mbǝ kám nǝ ngha.>
ACT 7:4 Abraham yool yit yil nen Kaldiya mo, kǝn wur dǝm tong ɗi nɗǝǝn yil nHaran. Aɓwoon ɗe puun Abraham muut nyil nHaran, ɓǝ Naan jì kǝ Abraham nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, ɗe wuu tong nɗǝǝn nǝ yaksǝ.
ACT 7:5 Ɗangɓǝ baa Naan shin rep pak yil nǝ Abraham, mbǝkǝ nǝ ɗee ɗi a mǝ káa wur, koo kaa mang shii mǝndong sǝ kas. Jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ Naan cweerpwoo Abraham nǝ, wur mbǝ shin yil nǝ Abraham, kǝ nǝ ɗee a mbii sekop wur, dǝm wul kǝ ɗang wur ɗe mon njì mɓwoon wur zak. Koo ɗe gyet mɓít mǝnǝ, ɓǝ baa Abraham kǝ mee làa kas aku.
ACT 7:6 Gyet Naan sat zak nǝnee, <Dang Abraham mon mbǝ ɗee a mǝzep mo nɗǝǝn mee yil ɗecì. Nenyil mǝnǝ mon nle kǝ mmo cìn ɗak laatong zak, kǝ mon nle mmo ɗee a kǝrem mo, mbǝ ɓit kambil feer.>
ACT 7:7 Naan wur baa sat ɗyikye zak nǝnee, <An mbǝ tokɗyeel nnen ɗe mo le mo ɗee a kǝrem, ɗang aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ an mbǝ pwat kǝ mo aku mɓut yil mǝnǝ, mbǝkǝ mmo jì seyil ɗi nghan nɗǝǝn pee ɗesǝ.>
ACT 7:8 Naan sat Abraham can-can, kǝ nǝ ɗee a Sǝmpwoo (alaama) mǝ pwoo ɗe Naan kǝ ten cweer nAbraham shi toom. Mbǝ mǝnǝ kaaɗe Abraham làa Aizik, ɓǝ wur can ɗyem fin nǝ nkaa puus nɗepwookun. Aizik can làa wur Jekop a kǝsǝ zak, kǝ Jekop can jep fin mo, ɗe mo a puun fun ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo a kǝsǝ zak.
ACT 7:9 <<Puun fun ɗesǝ mo, mo cìn zuur kǝ Josep, yaksǝ mo seet kǝ wur sham nyil Ijip koo kǝrem sǝ. Ɗangɓe Naan ɗi ashak kǝ wur.
ACT 7:10 Naan ɓam Josef mɓut jeel ɗe mo taa nkaa wur jir. Naan shin ɗeret nJosep, kǝ manshii mǝ cìn mbii ntoom Feero, mishkoom Ijip, ɗe nǝ le nwur ɗen Josep a ɗeɗes nkaa yil Ijip, kǝ nkaa lu fin zak.
ACT 7:11 Mee neen ɗeɗes taa nyil Ijip jir, kǝ yil nKeenan ɗe nǝ jì kǝ jeel ɗeɗes hakyeng, ɗe le baa puun fun mo kat mbiise kas.
ACT 7:12 kaaɗe Jekop kǝlǝng nǝ, mbiise ɗi nyil Ijip, ɓǝ wur shee lep puun fun mo sham nyil Ijip nǝ.
ACT 7:13 A nɗǝǝn sham mo nɗevǝl nyil Ijip nǝ, ɗang Josef woo shin nɗyemnǝǝn fin mo. A mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ Feero man ɗang mǝ Josep mo jir.
ACT 7:14 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ Josep lep kǝ mmo kàa pet puun fin Jekop kǝ nen wur mo jir. Nen ɗe mo pet mo shin sham nyil Ijip nǝ jir, mo wul laarpwoovǝl baapaat.
ACT 7:15 Nǝ le ɗang Jekop sham nyil Ijip, ɓǝ wur sham muut a nyil mǝnǝ, kǝzak puun fun mo jì murep a nyil Ijip zak.
ACT 7:16 Yaksǝ mo kok kúm mo mo kàa kǝ mo nyil nShekem, mbǝkǝ mo wum mo ɗi nɗǝǝn kǝcir ɗe gyet Abraham kǝ seet shi azurfa mo, nsar jep Hamor mo.
ACT 7:17 kaaɗe pee nǝ wul kus, mbǝkǝ nNaan gam mbii ɗe gyet wur kǝ ten cweer Abraham, ɓǝ nen fun mo kǝ ɓul ɗes nɗǝǝn yil Ijip nǝ hakyeng.
ACT 7:18 Nen Ijip mo lep mee mishkoom ɗepwoo nyil Ijip, ɗe baa wur man mee pwoo nkaa Josep kas.
ACT 7:19 Mishkoom ɗesǝ wur gwam puun fun mo, ɗang wur shin jeel mpuun fun mo, wur le kǝ mpuun fun mo fwo jep fur mo mbǝkǝ mmo murep ɗi.
ACT 7:20 A nɗǝǝn ɓit mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo làa Mosis. Gyet Mosis a mee làa ɗeret naa zam. Puun wur mo kyeer wur nɗǝǝn lu mbǝ tar kun.
ACT 7:21 Ɗang kaaɗe mo put dǝm le wur a tǝleng, ɓǝ reep Feero mang Mosis ɗyel, kǝ nwar kyeer wur koo làa fer sǝ.
ACT 7:22 Mo kám man mǝ nen Ijip mo mMosis jir, yaksǝ wur yool ɗee a mee ngwe ɗeɗes nɗǝǝn mbii ɗewur sat mo, kǝ mbii ɗewur cìn mo zak.
ACT 7:23 <<Kaaɗe Mosis wul ɓit mo laarfeer, ɓǝ wur pan mputuup fin mbǝ dǝm naa ɗyemnǝǝn fin nen Isreil mo.
ACT 7:24 Yaksǝ wur táa naa mee ngu Ijip nkaa shinjeel mmee ngu Isreil. Ɓǝ Mosis dǝm ɓam ngu Isreil nǝ, kǝ nwur lap ɗi ngwar nǝ. Yaksǝ Mosis tu ngu Ijip nǝ.
ACT 7:25 Mosis pan nǝ, nen fin mo mmanshii mǝnǝ nǝ, Naan mbǝ ɓam mo a shi sar fin. Ɗang baa mo manshii nǝ kas.
ACT 7:26 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ Mosis kat mee nen Isreil mo vǝl, pǝ lek nshak. Yaksǝ wur reɓet ɓen mo, kǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <Daa mo, wun a ɗyemnǝǝnshak, a mii le ɗang wuu lek nshak yii?>
ACT 7:27 Ɗangɓǝ gwar ɗewur nkaa shinjeel ngǝnǝǝn nǝ, bet Mosis shin baa aku, kǝ nwur sat mMosis nǝnee, <A wii le gha a mishkoom kǝ ngutokɗyeel nkaa mun ii?
ACT 7:28 Aa reɓet tu wen a kaaɗe doon a tu ngu Ijip sǝ mee?>
ACT 7:29 Kaaɗe Mosis kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur su ar yil Ijip, kǝ nwur dǝm tong ɗi nyil mMidiyan, koo mǝzep sǝ. A nɗǝǝn yil mMidiyan nǝ, ɓǝ Mosis làa jep ɗemish mo vǝl.
ACT 7:30 <<Aɓwoon ɓit mo laarfeer, ɓǝ mee ngulep mǝ Naan jì woo shin mMosis, shi mbǝlem wus nkaa mee laalǝǝt a yil kus kǝ zuul Sinai.
ACT 7:31 Kaaɗe Mosis naa wus nǝ, ɓǝ nǝ aapwoo nwur, ɓǝ wur gyes dǝm ɗi kus rep laalǝǝt nǝ, mbǝkǝ nwur naa ɗi rǝrret, ɓǝ wur kǝlǝng ɗoo mǝ Daa, nǝnee,
ACT 7:32 <A an a Naan mǝ puun fwaa mo, Naan mǝ Abraham, kǝ mǝ Aizik, kǝ mǝ Jekop.> Yaksǝ Mosis ɗaar, mbǝɗe kǝǝrmuut fes yaa wur zam, baa wur katɓal ɗewur mbǝ mak naa wus nǝ kas.
ACT 7:33 Daa Naan sat mMosis nǝnee, <A shwat kwoopshi ɗe mon nshii fwaa, mbǝɗe pee ɗe aa ɗar ɗi yaksǝ, nǝ a pee ɗeɓang.
ACT 7:34 Azeen-zeen, an kǝn naajeel nen fen ɗe mon nyil Ijip, kǝn kǝlǝng gwan mo mo. Mbǝmǝnǝ kǝn sham, mbǝkǝ nghan ɓam mo ɗi zak. Mbǝ mǝnǝ, a jì kǝ nghan lep gha shindǝm nyil Ijip.>
ACT 7:35 <<Gyet nen Isreil mo cii Mosis, ɓǝ gyet mo sat nǝnee, <A wii le gha a mishkoom kǝ ngutokɗyeel nkaa mun yii?> A Mosis a ngwe ɗe gyet Naan lep wur, mbǝkǝ nwur ɗee a Taakyeen kǝ Nguɓam mǝ nen Isreil mo shi ɓam mǝ ngulep mǝ Naan ɗe gyet wur woo shin mMosis nɗǝǝn rep laalǝǝt a yil sǝ.
ACT 7:36 A Mosis put kǝ nen Isreil mo nɗǝǝn yil Ijip, kǝzak gyet wur cìn mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo mo nɗǝǝn yil Ijip nǝ, kǝ nɗǝǝn Am kuur Ɗenaat, kǝ a naaryil, mbǝ ɓit mo laarfeer zak.
ACT 7:37 <<Gyet a Mosis sat nnen Isreil mo nǝnee, <Naan mbǝ yool lep mee ngusat pwoo Naan nwun, koo an sǝ, mɓut nnen fuu mo.>
ACT 7:38 Gyet Mosis ɗi ashak kǝ kuur nen Isreil mo a naaryil, ashak kǝ puun fun mo, kǝ ngulep mǝ Naan ɗe gyet wur leshap kǝ Mosis nkaa nzuul Sinai. A mbǝɗe gyet Mosis kǝ kǝlǝngkar mǝ seen pǝ Naan ɗi shin mmun.
ACT 7:39 <<Ɗangɓe gyet puun fun mo cii cìn mbii ɗe Mosis sat, kǝzak mo toklong shi Mosis, kǝ mo le mputuup fur mo mbǝ waa baa dǝm Ijip.
ACT 7:40 Mo sat Eeron nǝnee, <A kǝlem pak naan mo mmun, ɗe mon ntaa mmun akyeen. Mbǝɗǝ baa mu man mbii ɗe nǝ kat Mosis ɗe gyet wur put kǝ mun nɗǝǝn nyil Ijip kas.>
ACT 7:41 A nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ mo kǝlem mee laanǝng kǝ nǝ ɗee mmo, koo mee naan sǝ. Mo jì kǝ mbiizuum mo laanǝng nǝ, yaksǝ mo serǝɓet mǝ retnyit mbǝ naan ɗe mo kǝlem shi sar fur mo.
ACT 7:42 Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ Naan cǝǝr kǝɓwoon mmo, kǝzak wur le kǝ mmo seyil ɗi nzar mo, kǝ mbii ɗe aɗeng mo. Kaaɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ nensatpwoo kǝ Naan mo nǝnee, <Wun nen Isreil mo, nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗelaarfeer sǝ mo a naaryil, ɓǝ baa gyet wu saa long mo, kǝ wus mbiizuum mo, a mbǝ an kas.
ACT 7:43 Ɗang gyet wuu mang a Tent mǝ kùm Molek, wu mwaan kǝ nǝ, kǝ zar mǝ kùm fuu Refan. Wu kǝlem mbii ɗesǝ mo, mbǝkǝ nwun seyil ɗi mmo. Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ an mbǝ le kǝ mmo dǝm kǝ wun jong-jong, ɗe dǝm ɗel yil ɗe aɓwoon mBabilon.>
ACT 7:44 <<Gyet puun fun mo kǝ Tent mǝ langtǝng nǝ, Naan ɗi ashak kǝ mo a naaryil. Mo ɗak Tent mǝnǝ a nciit-nciit kǝ ɗe Naan shin mMosis naa. Mosis sat mmo tap ɗak a kǝsǝ zak.
ACT 7:45 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ puunkaam fun mo lap Tent mǝnǝ pǝ puun fur mo kǝ mmo mang Bìt mǝ Daa nǝ pan kaaɗe mo ɗel ashak kǝ Joshuwa nɗǝǝn yil ɗe Naan shin mmo. Naan ceen nenyil mǝnǝ mo, ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, a yit puun fun mo. Tent mǝnǝ war ɗi jì wul mɓít mǝ Devit.
ACT 7:46 Devit kat ɗeret ntoom Naan, wur ɗang, mbǝkǝ nwur ɗyik mee peetong ɗi nNaan mǝ Jekop.
ACT 7:47 Ɗangɓe a Solomon yool ɗyiklu Naan nǝ.
ACT 7:48 Jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ baa Daa Naan Ɗehai kǝ tong a nɗǝǝn lu ɗe gurum mo ɗyik kas. Pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ nciit kǝ pwoo ɗe gyet ngusatpwoo Naan ten sat nǝnee,
ACT 7:49 <Naan sat nǝ, ɗengnaan nǝ a peetong fen, kǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ a pee leshii fen zak. Wun nɗyik a mee lu ɗǝɗang nghan yii? Peeɗe an nnookɗi a nii?
ACT 7:50 Baa a sar fen le mbii ɗesǝ mo jir kas aa?>
ACT 7:51 <<Wun nencinshik mo, ɗe pǝtuup fuu mo ɗee a koo mǝ nenkum mo sǝ. Wuu ɗee a komjoor mo mbǝ cíikǝlǝngpwoo mǝ Naan, kǝzak wu cii Riin Ɗeɓang shidaar-shidaar, kaaɗe gyet puun fuu mo kǝ cìn sǝ. Mbǝmǝnǝ wun a koo puun fuu mo gyet sǝ zak.
ACT 7:52 Gyet puun fuu mo shínjeel nnenkop pwoo Naan mo jir. Gyet mo twe nen ɗe moo leshap nkaa jì Ngwe ɗe ndǝre sǝ, ɗe yaksǝ ɓǝ a wun seet wur, ɗang a wun, wu tu wur zak.
ACT 7:53 A wun a nen ɗe wu lap Wàar mǝ Naan ɗewur shin nwun nsar nenlep mǝ Naan mo, ɗang baa wu cìn mbii ɗe Wàar nǝ mo sat kas.>>
ACT 7:54 Kaaɗe nenɓeetpwoo nǝ mo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe Stivin sat mmo, ɓǝ nǝ láa mmo mɓut ɗes hakyeng, yaksǝ mo ǝrep sar fur mo mbǝ tuup.
ACT 7:55 Mbǝɗǝ Stivin gam kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, ɓǝ wur naapee kaa aɗeng, ɓǝ wur naa Ɗehai mǝ Naan, kǝ Daa Jesu kǝ ɗar nsarse kǝ Naan zak.
ACT 7:56 Ɓǝ Stivin sat nǝnee, <<Wu naa mo wang ɗengnaan, kǝzak Làa kǝ Gurum kǝ ɗar nsarse mǝ Naan.>>
ACT 7:57 Ɗangɓe gurum nǝ mo lep or shi ɗoo ɗeɗes, kǝ mmo duur kom fur mo shi sar fur mo, ɓǝ mo yool su jì taa nkaa Stivin.
ACT 7:58 Mo dul wur put mɓwoon pee nkaam nǝ, ɓǝ mo car wur shi gyǝk ɓǝ wur muut. Nen ɗe mo car Stivin nǝ mo, shwat nlǝr fur mo, mo le pǝ mee zǝlang ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Sool.
ACT 7:59 Kaaɗe mon nkaa car Stivin, ɓǝ wur nkaa ɗangnaan nǝnee, <<Daa Jesu, a lap seen fen.>>
ACT 7:60 Yaksǝ wur kurum mfurum, ɓǝ wur petpee shi ɗoo ɗeɗes nǝnee, <<Daa Naan, a fwoo shikbish ɗesǝ nǝ mmo.>> Kaaɗe wur sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur muut.
ACT 8:1 Nǝ fes ret nSool nyit zam, mbǝɗe mo tu Stivin. Parpuus mǝnǝ, ɓǝ jeel ɗeɗes nǝ táa nkaa kuur mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe moo tong nJerusalem. Mbǝ jeel nǝ, ɓǝ mo rangkáa jir, dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya, kǝ Samariya, tǝng ɗee a jeplep nǝ mo ɗe nJerusalem ɓejee ɗak.
ACT 8:2 Pak nen ɗe mo kǝǝr Naan, mo wum Stivin, kǝzak mo yém mmaap mbǝ muut wur nǝ.
ACT 8:3 Ɗangɓe Sool shínjeel nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo ɗes hakyeng. Wur dǝm ɗel shitul-shitul, kǝn nwur yak daas mo, kǝ shurep mo, dǝm shoot mo nɗǝǝn lushoot.
ACT 8:4 Nen ɗe mo rangkáa nǝ mo. Mo dǝm kop pwoo Naan ngurum mo koo a pee ɗeɗangyii ɗe mo dǝm ɗi.
ACT 8:5 Filip dǝm mmee pee kaam ɗe nen nSamariya, wur nkaa leshap ngurum mo nkaa Kristi mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 8:6 Kaaɗe kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo kǝlǝng, ɗang mo naa mbii lukshik ɗe Filip pǝ cìn mo zak, ɓǝ mo lekom, kǝzak mo lepan fur mo nkaa mbii ɗewur sat nǝ.
ACT 8:7 Riin ɗebish mo lep or ɗeɗes, kǝzak mo pwat mɓut ngurum mo ɗes. Mo bar gurum mo ɗes ɗe shik mo mo fii, kǝ kǝɓel mo.
ACT 8:8 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ gurum mo kat retnyit ɗes nɗǝǝn pee nkaam mǝnǝ.
ACT 8:9 Mee gwar ɗewur ɗi nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ, ɗe sǝm wur a Simon, ɗe mbǝ ɓit mo ɗes, ɓǝ wur kǝcin mulak, kǝzak wur kǝcin mbii aapwoo mo a yit mǝ nen Samariya mo. Wur cutzung nǝ, ɗyin a mee ngwe ɗeɗes.
ACT 8:10 Gurum mo jir mo kǝ lepyit nkaa wur, yool nɗeɗyeen mo, dǝm wul nɗenannan mo, ɗang moo sat nǝ, gwar ɗesǝ wur aa ɓal mǝ Naan ɗe moo pet a iiko Ɗeɗes Met
ACT 8:11 Moo lepyit nkaa wur, a mbǝɗe ɓit mo ɗes, ɓǝ wur cìn mbii aapwoo mo a yit mo mo shi mulak nǝ.
ACT 8:12 Ɗang kaaɗe mo shinzeen mpwoo ɗeret ɗe Filip sat mmo, nkaa mulki mǝ Naan, kǝ nkaa Jesu Kristi zak, ɓǝ mo cìn baptisma ndaas mo, kǝ shurep mo ɗe mo shinzeen.
ACT 8:13 Simon shikáa fin shinzeen zak, ɓǝ mo cìn baptisma nwur. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm nɗang Filip, ɗang nǝ aapwoo nwur mbǝ mbii lukshik mo, kǝ ɗak ɗǝnan-nan ɗewur naa Filip kǝcin mo.
ACT 8:14 Kaaɗe jeplep ɗe moo tong nJerusalem mo kǝlǝng nǝ, nen Samariya mo kǝ lappwoo Naan, ɓǝ mo lep Pita kǝ Joon dǝm pǝ mo ɗi.
ACT 8:15 Kaaɗe Pita kǝ Joon mo dǝm wul, ɓǝ mo ɗangnaan nkaa nen ɗe mo shinzeen nǝ. Mbǝkǝ nNaan shin Riin Ɗeɓang ɗe mmo.
ACT 8:16 Mbǝɗǝ baa Riin Ɗeɓang kǝ sham nkaa memee nɗǝǝn mo kas. Mo kǝ cìn a baptisma mmo nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Daa Jesu ɓejee ɗak.
ACT 8:17 Pita kǝ Joon, mo lesar fur mo nkaa mo, ɓǝ Naan shin Riin Ɗeɓang ngurum nǝ mo.
ACT 8:18 Kaaɗe Simon naa nǝ, moo shin Riin Ɗeɓang nǝ nnen shinzeen nǝ mo, a mbǝɗe jeplep nǝ mo lesar fur mo nkaa mo, ɓǝ wur shin shool mPita kǝ Joon, ɗang wur sat mmo nǝnee,
ACT 8:19 <<Wu shin ɓal mǝnǝ nghan zak, mbǝkǝ koo wii ɗe wen lesar fen nkaa wur, ɓǝ wur nkat Riin Ɗeɓang nǝ zak.>>
ACT 8:20 Ɗangɓǝ Pita sat nSimon nǝnee, <<Waa kǝ shool fwaa nǝ, wun nɗel nwus. Mbǝɗǝ aa pan nǝ, a mmak seet mbiizuum mǝ Naan a shi shool.
ACT 8:21 Baa mee mbii ɓàl gha kǝ mun mɓut ɗak fun ɗesǝ nǝ kas mbǝɗe baa pǝtuup fwa nǝ nɗere a kǝkyeen nNaan kas.
ACT 8:22 A tuwap mbǝ pan fwaa ɗebish nǝ, kǝzak a ɗang Daa Naan, mbǝkǝ nNaan fwoo shikbish mǝ pan kǝ pǝtuup fwaa ɗebish nǝ ɗi ngha.
ACT 8:23 Mbǝɗǝ wen naa, aa gam kǝ zuur ɗebish, ɗang aa ɗee a ɗe ɓuɓwoot nɗǝǝn shikbish.>>
ACT 8:24 Simon sat mPita kǝ Joon nǝnee, <<Kuzuk, wu ɗang pǝ Daa Naan, mbǝkǝ taji memee nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe wu sat sǝ mo kat an kas.>>
ACT 8:25 Aɓwoon ɗe Pita kǝ Joon mo kǝ satpwoo nkaa Jesu, ɗang mo leshap Naan zak, ɓǝ kaaɗe mo a ar kàa nJerusalem, ɓǝ mo taa kop pwoo ɗeret nǝ nɗǝǝn jepyil mo ɗes, ɗe mo nSamariya.
ACT 8:26 Mee ngulep mǝ Naan sat mFilip nǝnee, <<A yool a sham nkor ngyeen a ar ɗe nǝ yool nJerusalem dǝm wul nGaza, ɗe nǝ a naaryil.>>
ACT 8:27 Wur yool seet, ɓǝ wur taakáat kǝ mee ngu Itiyopiya ɗewur a meermuut. Wur a mee ngwe ɗeɗes ɗewur tap kǝ long mǝ mishkoom ɗe mat, Kandes mǝ yil Itiyopiya. Gwar ɗesǝ wur waa a nJerusalem mbǝ seyil nNaan.
ACT 8:28 Kaaɗe wur a ar baa waa, ɓǝ wur kǝ tong nɗǝǝn mbiilang, wur nkaa tang ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan Aizaya.
ACT 8:29 Ɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang sat mFilip nǝnee, <<A dǝm kus kǝ mbiilang ɗesǝ.>>
ACT 8:30 Filip su dǝm kus kǝ mbiilang nǝ, ɓǝ wur kǝlǝng gwar nǝ nkaa tang ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan Aizaya. Yaksǝ Filip tal pǝ gwar nǝ nǝnee, <<A manshii mǝ mbii ɗe gha nkaa tang nǝ aa?>>
ACT 8:31 Gwar nǝ lap nǝnee, <<Cirang ɗang an mbǝ mmanshii mǝnǝ ɗi ii? Kat baa a mee gurum kámshii mǝnǝ nghan kas ii?>> Gwar nǝ sat mFilip kàa tong ashak kǝ wur.
ACT 8:32 A pwoo ɗewur nkaa tang nǝ nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal nǝ nɗesǝ, ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Wur a koo tǝm ɗe mo kǝ dǝm kǝnǝ, mpee saa sǝ. Koo tǝm ɗe ɗok tǝtǝk ntoom mǝ ngusaa shweep nǝ sǝ, Wur ɗok tǝtǝk a kǝsǝ zak.
ACT 8:33 Mbǝɗǝ wur sham kǝ káa fin, ɓǝ baa mo tokɗyeel nwur nkaa zeen kas. A wii mmak yool leshap nkaa ɗang wur mo ii? Mbǝɗǝ mo kǝ mang seen wur nɗǝǝn yil nǝ.>>
ACT 8:34 Ɓǝ ngu Itiyopiya nǝ wur tal pǝ Filip nǝnee, <<A sat nghan. Gyet ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan ɗesǝ wur leshap nǝ a nkaa wii? Wur leshap nǝ a nkaa shin aa? Koo a mee ngwe ɗecì yii?>>
ACT 8:35 Yaksǝ Filip ɗoom leshap ɗeret nkaa Jesu, shi pwoo ɗe gwar nǝ kǝ tang nǝ.
ACT 8:36 Kaaɗe mon mwaan a ar nǝ, ɓǝ mo jì wul mpee ɗe am ɗi, ɓǝ ngu Itiyopiya nǝ wur sat mFilip nǝnee, <<A naa am sǝsǝ! A mii ncíi kǝ nghan cìn baptisma nghan ii?>>
ACT 8:37 Filip lap nǝnee, <<Katɗang a shinzeen nJesu shi pǝtuup mǝndong azeen-zeen, ɓǝ mon ncìn baptisma ngha. Ngu Itiyopiya nǝ wur sat nǝ, Nshinzeen nǝ Jesu Kristi wur a Làa mǝ Naan azeen-zeen.>>
ACT 8:38 Yaksǝ gwar nǝ wur le mbiilang nǝ ɗar. Ɓǝ Filip kǝ gwar ɗe nǝ, mo sham nɗǝǝn am nǝ dukvǝl, ɓǝ Filip cìn baptisma ngwar nǝ.
ACT 8:39 Kaaɗe mo kàa pwat mɓut am nǝ, ɓǝ Riin mǝ Daa, mang Filip dǝm kǝ wur mmee mpee. Baa ngu Itiyopiya nǝ wur kutɗi kǝ naa Filip zak kas. Yaksǝ wur sekyeen kǝ mwaan fin, kǝzak wur gam kǝ retnyit.
ACT 8:40 Gurum mo naa Filip nɗǝǝn yil Azotus. Wur dǝm shipee-shipee nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ mo jir, mbǝ kop pwoo ɗeret nǝ, dǝm wul nSizariya.
ACT 9:1 Sool sekyeen kǝ shinjeel nnenseet nɗang Jesu mo, wur tang ar mbǝ twe mo. Aasǝ ɓǝ, wur dǝm pǝ pris ɗeɗes met jir nǝ.
ACT 9:2 Yaksǝ Sool ɗang pǝ pris ɗeɗes nǝ, mbǝkǝ nwur shin lep a rǝran mmo ɗewur ndǝm kǝ mmo nLu mǝ Naan mo, ɗe mo nDamaskus, mbǝkǝ katɗang wur kat nen ɗe moo dǝm nɗang ar Jesu, koo daas mo kǝ shurep mo, ɓǝ wur yak mo jì kǝ mo nJerusalem.
ACT 9:3 Kaaɗe wur jì wul kus kǝ Damaskus, ɓǝ nnen mman, ɓǝ mee peeɓang tong aɗeng sham ɓangpee ɗewur ɗe.
ACT 9:4 Yaksǝ wur taa nyil, kǝzak wur kǝlǝng mee ɗoo kǝ sat nǝnee, <<Sool, Sool! A mii le ɗang aa shinjeel nghan yii?>>
ACT 9:5 Yaksǝ Sool tal nǝnee, <<A gha a wii Daa?>> Ɗoo nǝ lap nǝnee, <<A an Jesu, ɗe gha nkaa shinjeel nghan.
ACT 9:6 A yool a ɗel nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ, ɓǝ mon nsat nghan mbii ɗe nǝ a tǝng gha ncìn.>>
ACT 9:7 Nen ɗe mon mwaan nǝ ashak kǝ wur mo ɗar tǝtǝk, baa mo le mee shap kas, mo kǝlǝng ɗoo nǝ, ɗang baa mo naa nguleshap nǝ kas.
ACT 9:8 Sool yool ɗar atǝng, ɓǝ wur wang yit fin, ɗang, baa wur mak naapee kas. Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ mo yaa sar nwur, mo ɗel kǝ wur nDamaskus.
ACT 9:9 Mbǝ teer mo kun, ɓǝ baa wur mak naapee kas, kǝzak baa wur se mee mbiise, koo shwaa mee mbii kas zak.
ACT 9:10 Mee nguseet nɗang Jesu ɗi nDamaskus, ɗe moo pet wur a Ananiyas. Daa sat Ananiyas nɗǝǝn suun nǝnee, <<Ananiyas!>> Yaksǝ wur lap nǝnee, <<An sǝsǝ Daa.>>
ACT 9:11 Daa sat nwur nǝnee, <<A yool a dǝm a ar ɗesǝ, ɗe moo pet a Sham ndǝr-ndǝr, ɓǝ a tal mee gwar ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Sool, wur a ngu Tarsus. Wur ntul Judas. Yaksǝ ɓǝ wur nkaa ɗangnaan.
ACT 9:12 Nɗǝǝn suun wur, ɓǝ wur naa mee gwar ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Ananiyas, wur jì ɗel, ɗang wur lesar fin nkaa wur, mbǝkǝ nyit fin mo baa naapee ɗi zak.>>
ACT 9:13 Ɗangɓe Ananiyas lap nǝnee, <<Daa, gurum mo ɗes mo kǝ leshap nghan, nkaa niyang ɗe gwar ɗesǝ wur kǝcin nnen fwaa ɗe mon nJerusalem.
ACT 9:14 Kǝzak wur jì mpee ɗesǝ nDamaskus, shipee ɗe pris ɗenan mo shin nwur, mbǝkǝ nwur yak nen ɗe mo shinzeen nɗǝǝn sǝm fwaa jir.>>
ACT 9:15 Ɗangɓe Daa lap wur nǝnee, <<A yool a dǝm, mbǝɗe an kǝn bǝlǝp wur, mbǝkǝ nwur cìn ɗak ɗi nghan. Wur mbǝ le kǝn nnen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ mishkoom mo, kǝ nnen Yahudi mo man sǝm fen zak.
ACT 9:16 An mbǝ kám nwur jeel ɗe nwur mbǝ shwaa mo mbǝ sǝm fen.>>
ACT 9:17 Ananiyas yool dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn lu Judas nǝ. Wur lesar fin mo nkaa Sool, ɗang wur sat nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa Sool, Daa Jesu ɗewur woo shin fin ngha, kaaɗe gha a ar jì mpee ɗesǝ, a wur lep an, mbǝkǝ nghan baa a naapee ɗi zak. Kǝ mmo gam gha shi Riin Ɗeɓang zak.>>
ACT 9:18 Abet-abet ɓerep mee mbii mo koo feel mǝ pupwap sǝ, mo pwat nyit Sool, mo sham ɗong nyil, ɓǝ yit wur mo cin naapee. Yaksǝ wur yool ɗar atǝng, ɓǝ mo cìn baptisma nwur.
ACT 9:19 Aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ se mbiise, ɓǝ wur baa katɓal zak. Sool tong ashak kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nDamaskus, mbǝ meeteer mo ruk.
ACT 9:20 Abet-abet ɓǝ wur dǝm nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan mo ɓǝ wur ɗoom sat nǝ, Jesu a Làa Naan.
ACT 9:21 Nen ɗe mo kǝlǝng wur jir, ɓǝ nǝ aapwoo mmo, ɗang mo tal nǝnee, <<Baa a gwar ɗewur twe nen ɗe mo shinzeen nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu, nɗǝǝn Jerusalem sǝ nɗesǝ kas ee? Wur jì mpee ɗesǝ a mbǝkǝ nwur yak mo dǝm kǝ mo a ɓuɓwoot pǝ pris ɗǝnan-nan mo ɗi zak kas aa?>>
ACT 9:22 Ɗangɓe Sool katɓal, kǝn nwur leshap ɗi ɓal-ɓal, ɗe nǝ kám agaak nǝ, Jesu wur a Kristi azeen-zeen. Pwoo ɗewur sat nǝ mo, nǝ daampee nnen Yahudi ɗe moo tong nDamaskus.
ACT 9:23 Aɓwoon meeteer mo ɗes, ɓǝ nen Yahudi mo ɓeetpwoo kǝ sut, mbǝkǝ mmo tu Sool ɗi.
ACT 9:24 Ɗang pwoo ɗe mo ɓwoot nǝ taa nkom Sool. Mo tap pwoo lu ɗe mon mpee nkaam nǝ mpar kǝ puus, mbǝkǝ mmo tu Sool ɗe.
ACT 9:25 Ɗangɓe nen shinzeen ɗe mo dǝm ɗang Sool nǝ mo, mo mang wur nɗǝǝn kǝci mpar, ɓǝ mo ɓwet wur sham mɓwoon pee nkaam nǝ nɗǝǝn mee fung.
ACT 9:26 Kaaɗe Sool wul nJerusalem, ɓǝ wur tang ar ɗewur mbǝ ɓàlkáa wur ɗi ashak kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo. Ɗangɓe mo jir, mo kǝǝr wur, mbǝɗe baa mo shinzeen nǝ, wur kǝ ɗee a nguseet nɗang Jesu kas.
ACT 9:27 Yaksǝ a Barnabas jì kǝ wur pǝ jeplep nǝ mo ɗi, kǝn nwur leshap ngurum nǝ mo, kaaɗe Sool kǝ naa Daa Jesu a ar, nǝ, Daa Jesu kǝ leshap kǝ Sool. Barnabas leshap mmo nkaa sat pwoo kǝ Naan nɗǝǝn Jesu agaak, ɗe Sool kǝ cìn nɗǝǝn Damaskus, baa ashak kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas, koo dǝɓen.
ACT 9:28 Aasǝ ɓǝ wur tong ashak kǝ mo. Kǝzak wur mwaan dǝm shipee-shipee nɗǝǝn Jerusalem, kǝzak wur satpwoo kǝ Naan ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Daa Jesu.
ACT 9:29 Wur naa nleshap nǝ, kǝ ɓeetshik kǝ nen Yahudi ɗe moo kǝlǝng pwoo kǝ nen Helene mo, ɗe nǝ le kǝ mmo tang ar ɗe mon ntu wur ɗi.
ACT 9:30 Jir aasǝ kaaɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu mo kǝlǝng mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo dǝm kǝ Sool nSizariya, kǝ mo lep wur shindǝm nTarsus.
ACT 9:31 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nJudiya, kǝ Galili, kǝ Samariya, mo tongriyang nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo. Shi ɓam mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo katɓal, ɗang mo ɓul zak. Moo mwaan nɗǝǝn kǝǝr mǝ Naan, ɗang moo shin ɗeɗes nNaan zak.
ACT 9:32 Pita mwaan shipee-shipee jir, ɓǝ wur jì wul pǝ nen Naan mo, ɗe mo kǝ tong nLidda.
ACT 9:33 Yaksǝ wur kat mee gwar ɗi mpee nkaam mǝnǝ, ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Aniyas, ɗewur kǝ mee shwal ɗe nǝ fii shik wur, ɗe baa wur mak yool a peesaam kas, mbǝ ɓit mo pwookun.
ACT 9:34 Pita sat nwur nǝnee, <<Aniyas, Jesu Kristi wur bar gha. A yool a ciɓet mbiisaam fwaa.>> Abet-abet, ɓǝ wur yool.
ACT 9:35 Kaaɗe jir nen ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn Lidda kǝ Sharon mo naa wur bar, ɓǝ mo cǝǝr kǝ pǝtuup fur mo, ɗe nǝ le mmo shinzeen nDaa.
ACT 9:36 Mee mat seet nɗang Jesu war ɗi nɗǝǝn yil nJoppa, ɗe sǝm war a Tabita, sǝm war nǝ shi liispwoo mǝ nen Heleni mo a Dokas, ɗe shii kǝnǝ a <<Tap.>> Mat ɗesǝ war kǝ cìn ɗak ɗeret mo, ɗang war kǝ ɓam nenjeel mo zak.
ACT 9:37 Nɗǝǝn meeteer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ mee shwal yaa war, ɗe nǝ le nwar muut. Kaaɗe mo vwang kúm war, ɓǝ mo le nɗǝǝn mee luɗeng.
ACT 9:38 Lidda kus kǝ Joppa, ɓǝ kaaɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu mo kǝlǝng nǝ Pita ɗi nJoppa, ɓǝ mo lep gurum mo vǝl shindǝm pǝ wur ɗe, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗang ɗi pǝ wur, kǝ nwur jì pǝ mo ɗi kǝkǝlak, taji wur taa ɗee bir kas.
ACT 9:39 Pita yool dǝm ashak kǝ mo, kaaɗe mo jì wul, ɓǝ mo kàa kǝ wur nɗǝǝn luɗeng nǝ. A pee ɗe matkaa mo jì ɗirang pǝ wur ɗi. Mo nkaa wal, ɗang mo kám nlǝr mo, kǝ leelep mo, ɗe dǝ Tabita kǝ raa mmatkáa nǝ mo, ɓǝ war kutɗi seen.
ACT 9:40 Ɗangɓe Pita le mmo pwat a tool jir, ɓǝ wur kurum mfurum, kǝ nwur ɗangnaan ɗi. Yaksǝ wur cǝǝr pǝ kúm nǝ ɗe, wur sat nǝnee, <<Tabita yi yool.>> Yaksǝ war wang yit fer. Kaaɗe war naa Pita, ɓǝ war yool tong atǝng.
ACT 9:41 Ɓǝ wur yaa sar nwar, ɗang wur ɗiyeep war ɗar atǝng. Ɓǝ wur pǝrep nen mǝ Naan nǝ mo, kǝ matkaa nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur shin Tabita mo kǝ seen.
ACT 9:42 Mbii ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗemǝman nɗǝǝn yil nJoppa jir, ɓǝ gurum mo ɗes mo shinzeen nDaa.
ACT 9:43 Pita tong ashak kǝ mee nguɗak shim, ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Simon, mbǝ teer mo ɗes ɗe nJoppa nǝ.
ACT 10:1 Mee gwar ɗi nɗǝǝn Sizariya, ɗe sǝm wur a Konilus, wur a mee ngwe ɗeɗes, ɗewur kǝ tap kǝ shiitoon mo kambil mǝndong, ɗe mǝ yil Itali.
ACT 10:2 Wur a mee ngwe ɗewur le pǝtuup fin nkaa Naan, kǝzak wur kǝǝr Naan ashak kǝ nenlu fin mo jir. Wur shin zuum ngurum mo ɗes, kǝ wur kǝ naa ndang Naan shidaar-shidaar.
ACT 10:3 Parmeeci sǝ, koo kun ɗe mǝ puus sǝ, ɓǝ nɗǝǝn suun, ɓǝ wur naa ngulep kǝ Naan agaak, ɗang ngulep nǝ sat nwur nǝnee, <<Konilus,>>
ACT 10:4 Ɓǝ Konilus naa ngulep nǝ shi yit kǝǝrmuut, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<A mii yii Daa?>> Ngulep mǝ Naan sat nKonilus nǝnee, <<Naan kǝ lap ɗang fwaa mo, kǝ mbiizuum ɗe aa shin nenjeel mo, ɓǝ mo kǝkàa wul pǝ Naan ɗi aɗeng, ɗang mo ɗee a mbii ɗe Naan pan gha zak.
ACT 10:5 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓǝ a lep mee gurum mo dǝm nJoppa, mbǝkǝ mmo dǝm pet mee gwar ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Simon Pita, jì ntul fwaa.
ACT 10:6 Wur tong a nlu Simon nguɗak shim, ɗe lu wur nǝ kus kǝ pwoo Am kuur sǝ.>>
ACT 10:7 Kaaɗe ngulep mǝ Naan leshap kǝ Konilus, ɓǝ Konilus pet kǝrem fin mo vǝl kǝ mee shiitoon, ɗewur a ngwe ɗe ndǝre mɓut nen ɗe mo kǝ cìn ɗak ntul fin shidaar-shidaar.
ACT 10:8 Aɓwoon ɗewur sat mmo mbii ɗe nǝ cìn jir, ɓǝ wur lep mo dǝm nJoppa.
ACT 10:9 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mo yaa ar, ɓǝ mo jì wul kus kǝ pee nkaam nǝ. Pita kǝkàa nluɗeng mbǝ ɗangnaan, koo puus a naar sǝ.
ACT 10:10 Neenláa nwur, ɗang wur reɓet mee mbii ɗewur nse. Kaaɗe mo kutɗi nkaa cet mbiise nǝ, ɓǝ Pita cin mee suun.
ACT 10:11 Ɗee wur naa ɗengnaan nǝ wang, ɗang mee mbii tong aɗeng sham koo haal ɗeɗes sǝ. Mo yaa sham kǝnǝ nyil shi kwang nǝ mo feer.
ACT 10:12 Nɗǝǝn nǝ, ɓǝ koo a luwaa ɗeɗangyii, ɗe mo kǝ mwaan shi shii feer mo, kǝ ɗe mo kǝ fee shi ɓut mo, kǝ nyer ɗe mo kǝ yool ncáap mo ɗiɓut jir.
ACT 10:13 Ɓǝ Pita kǝlǝng mee ɗoo kǝ sat nǝnee, <<Pita a yool, a can a se.>>
ACT 10:14 Ɗangɓe Pita lap nǝnee, <<Hai Daa! Baa wen kǝn cam se mee luwaa ɗebuu, koo ɗe baa nǝ ret kǝ ngu Yahudi se kas.>>
ACT 10:15 Pita waa cin kǝlǝng ɗoo nǝ ɗe zak, ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Mbii ɗe Naan kǝ le a ɗeɓang, ɓǝ taji waa a le a ɗebuu kas.>>
ACT 10:16 Mo cìn a kǝsǝ dǝm wul ar kun, ɓǝ mo waa baakàa kǝ haal nǝ aɗeng.
ACT 10:17 Kaaɗe Pita nkaa panshii mǝ suun nǝ, ɓǝ nen ɗe Konilus lep mo sǝ, mo kǝ ten yap lu mǝ Simon nǝ mo kat, ɓǝ mo jì ɗar mpwoo lu nǝ.
ACT 10:18 Mo petpee, ɓǝ mo tal nǝnee, <<Kyet gwar ɗe mo kǝ pet wur a Simon Pita sǝ, kǝ tong a nlu ɗesǝ ee?>>
ACT 10:19 Kaaɗe Pita kutɗi nkaa panshii mǝ suun ɗesǝ nǝ, ɓǝ Riin mǝ Naan sat nwur nǝnee, <<A naa mee gurum mo kun, mo pǝ yap gha.
ACT 10:20 A yool, a sham, kǝ nghan seet ashak kǝ mo, baa a shi mee kyetwo kas, mbǝɗe a an lep mo.>>
ACT 10:21 Ɓǝ Pita sham pǝ nen nǝ mo ɗi, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<An sǝ, a an a ngwe ɗe wun pǝ yap nǝ. Wu jì a mbǝ miyi?>>
ACT 10:22 Mo lap nǝnee, <<A mee ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon mo, ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Konilus ɗewur a mee ngwe ɗe ndǝre, ngukǝǝr Naan. Ɗe nen Yahudi mo jir mo kǝ kwoop wur. A mee ngulep mǝ Naan ɗeɓang jì sat nwur nǝ, wur lep mo pet gha, kǝ nghan dǝm ɗi ntul fin, mbǝkǝ nwur kǝlǝng mbii ɗe gha mbǝ sat nǝ ɗi nwur.>>
ACT 10:23 Pita ɗel kǝ des ɗekun nǝ mo nlu, mbǝkǝ mmo teer ɗi. Daar nǝ, ɓǝ Pita yool seet ashak kǝ mo. Pak nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nJoppa mo seet ashak kǝ wur.
ACT 10:24 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mo dǝm wul nSizariya. Konilus nkaa ɗarnaa mo. Wur kǝ ten pǝrep ɗang fin mo, kǝ shaar fin mo, mo kuur ashak ɗes.
ACT 10:25 Kaaɗe Pita a ar ɗel nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, ɓǝ Konilus kaat wur, ɓǝ wur taa mPita ntoom, mbǝ seeyil nwur.
ACT 10:26 Ɗangɓe Pita ɗiyeep Konilus, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<A yool atǝng, wen shikáa fen, an a gurum koo waa sǝ zak.>>
ACT 10:27 Pita nkaa leshap kǝ Konilus, ɓǝ kaaɗe wur ɗel, nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, ɓǝ wur kat gurum mo kǝ kuur ashak ɗes.
ACT 10:28 Pita sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun shikáa fuu wu man nǝ, baa nǝ ndǝre kǝ ngu Yahudi ɓalkaa fin ashak kǝ mee soon ɗecì mo, koo wur jì pǝ mo ɗi kas. Ɗangɓe Naan kǝ kám nghan, kǝ taji wen mpet mee gurum a ɗebuu, koo ɗebish kas.
ACT 10:29 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, kaaɗe wu lep mo pet an sǝ, ɓǝ wen jì pǝ wun ɗi, baa wen cii kas. Mbǝmǝnǝ wen reɓet kǝlǝng mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝ nwun pet an nǝ.>>
ACT 10:30 Konilus sat nǝnee, <<Nǝ kus aa teer mo feer cicinsǝ, nciit kǝ pee kǝsǝ, ɓǝ nkaa ndang Naan nkun mǝ puus nɗǝǝn lu fen. Ɓǝ nnaa mee gwar sǝ, ɗe nlǝr wur mo piyaa pet-pet, wur jì ɗar a kyeen fen.
ACT 10:31 Yaksǝ wur sat nǝnee, Konilus! Naan kǝ lap ɗang fwaa, kǝ mbiizuum ɗe aa shin nenjeel mo sǝ, mo ɗee a mbii ɗe Naan wur pan gha zak.
ACT 10:32 Mbǝ mǝnǝ a lep-lep dǝm nJoppa, kǝ mo dǝm pet mee gwar ɗe sǝm wur a Simon Pita, wur kǝ tong a ntul mǝ Simon nguɗak shim, ɗe lu wur nǝ kus kǝ pwoo am kuur sǝ.
ACT 10:33 Abet-abet ɓǝ wen nlep-lep shindǝm pǝ gha ɗi. Nǝ ret zam kaaɗe a jì mpee ɗesǝ. Mun sǝ jir ntoom mǝ Naan yaksǝ, mbǝkǝ mmun kǝlǝng mbii ɗe Daa wur sat ngha, mbǝkǝ nghan sat ɗi mmun.>>
ACT 10:34 Pita leshap mmo nǝnee, <<Azeen-zeen wen naa nǝ, baa Naan kǝ ɓakyit mmee gurum kas.
ACT 10:35 Ɗangɓǝ Naan wur kǝ lap gurum mo jir, ɗe mo kǝ kǝǝr wur, kǝzak moo cìn mbii ɗeret mo zak.
ACT 10:36 A pwoo ɗe Naan wur lep nnen Isreil mo nɗesǝ. Moo leshap ɗeret, ɗe nǝ a mǝ tongriyang mmo nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi, ɗewur a Daa mǝ mbii mo jir,
ACT 10:37 Wun shikáa fuu, wu man mbii aapwoo ɗe mo kǝ cìn nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya jir. Gyet mo shee cìn nǝ a nGalili, aɓwoon ɗe gyet Joon ngucìn baptisma wur leshap mmo nkaa nǝ.
ACT 10:38 Ɗesǝ nǝ a pwoo nkaa Jesu Ngu Nazaret, ɗe gyet Naan ɗoo Riin Ɗeɓang kǝ iiko nkaa wur. Wur dǝm koo a pee ɗeɗangyii, ɓǝ wur cìn ɗak ɗeret, ɗewur bar nen ɗe mon ndǝr ɓal mǝ nngujwaan jir, mbǝɗe Naan ashak kǝ wur.
ACT 10:39 Mun a langtǝng mǝ mbii ɗewur cìn mo jir nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya, kǝ nɗǝǝn Jerusalem zak. A wur a ɗe gyet mo tu wur, kaaɗe gyet mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeepyoom sǝ, ɗee wur muut.
ACT 10:40 Jir aasǝ Naan yool kǝ wur a peemúut parpuus ɗekun, kǝzak Naan le kǝ nwur woo shin fin mmun agaak.
ACT 10:41 Baa a gurum mo jir mo naa wur kas, ɗang wur woo shin a mmun, ɗe Naan kǝ ten bǝlǝp mun, kǝ mmun ɗee ɗi a langtǝng fin. Gyet muu se mbiise kǝ shwaa am ashak kǝ wur, aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ yool a peemúut zak.
ACT 10:42 Wur sat mmun ɓalɓal nǝ, mu satpwoo mǝ Naan ngurum mo jir zak, kǝ mmun tong a langtǝng ɗi nǝ, a Jesu wur a gwar ɗe Naan shin ɗeɗes nwur, mbǝkǝ nwur ɗee ɗi a ngutokɗyeel nnen ɗe mmeen mo, kǝ nnen ɗe mo kǝ murep mo zak.
ACT 10:43 A wur a ngwe ɗe gyet nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo jir, mo kǝ ten tong a langtǝng wur nǝ, a mbǝ sǝm wur, ɗang koo a ngwe ɗeɗangyii ɗewur shinzeen, ɓǝ wur nkat fwo mǝ shikbish wur mo.>>
ACT 10:44 Kaaɗe Pita kutɗi nkaa leshap ɗesǝ mmo, ɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang sham nkaa nen ɗe mo pǝ kǝlǝng pwoo nǝ jir.
ACT 10:45 Nen Yahudi ɗe mo a nen shinzeen ɗe mo jì ashak kǝ Pita sǝ, nǝ aapwoo mmo, Mbǝɗǝ mo naa Naan shin Riin Ɗeɓang shi zuum nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas zak.
ACT 10:46 Mo kǝlǝng mo kǝ leshap shi pak liispwoo mo, ɗang mon nkaa shin ɗeɗes nNaan. Ɓǝ Pita sat nǝnee,
ACT 10:47 <<Kyet mee gurum mmak cíi nkaa am ɗe mon ncìn baptisma ɗi nnen ɗesǝ mo aa? Mbǝɗǝ mo kǝ lap Riin Ɗeɓang nǝ a kaaɗe gyet mmun mu lap sǝ.>>
ACT 10:48 Yaksǝ Pita le kǝ mo cìn baptisma mmo nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu Kristi. Mo ɗang pǝ Pita, mbǝkǝ nwur pan yém ɗi ashak kǝ mo mbǝ rep meeteer mo ruk akuɗang.
ACT 11:1 Jeplep mo kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nJudiya, mo kǝlǝng nǝ, pak gurum ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, mo kǝ lappwoo Naan zak.
ACT 11:2 Kaaɗe Pita kàa wul nJerusalem, ɓǝ nen shinzeen ɗe mo kǝ can mo, mo yool kǝ pwoo nkaa wur.
ACT 11:3 Mo sat nǝnee, <<Waa dǝm a ɗel nlu mǝ nen ɗe nsuluk mo har a se mbiise ashak kǝ mo.>>
ACT 11:4 Aasǝ ɓǝ Pita yaa yakshii mǝ mbii ɗe nǝ cìn jir, wur sat mmo nǝnee,
ACT 11:5 <<Dǝ an nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nJoppa, ɓǝ kaaɗe an nkaa ɗangnaan ɓǝ wen suun. Ɓǝ nɗǝǝn suun nǝ, nnaa mee haal ɗeɗes ɗe nǝ tong aɗeng sham ɗe, nǝ kǝ kwang mo feer, nǝ sham wul pǝ an ɗi.
ACT 11:6 Wen ban yit nkaa nǝ, ɓǝ nnaa longlu mo, kǝ luwaayil mo, kǝ mbii ɗe mo kǝ fee shi ɓut mo, kǝ nyer ɗe mo kǝ yool ncáap, mo ɗi nɗǝǝn nǝ.
ACT 11:7 Ɓǝ nkǝlǝng mee ɗoo, ɗe nǝ sat nghan nǝnee, <Pita, a yool a saa mo, a se.>
ACT 11:8 Ɗangɓe wen nsat nǝnee, <Hai Daa! Baa wen kǝn cam se mee luwaa ɗebuu, koo ɗe baa nǝ ret kǝ ngu Yahudi se kas.>
ACT 11:9 Yaksǝ ɗoo nǝ cin sat ɗi nghan aɗeng nǝnee, <Mbii ɗe Naan le a ɗeɓang, ɓǝ taji a le nǝ a ɗebish kas.>
ACT 11:10 Mo cìn a kǝsǝ, dǝm wul ar kun, ɓǝ mo waa baa dul haal nǝ kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng.
ACT 11:11 Abet, nciit kǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ gurum mo kun, ɗe mo kǝ lep mo nSizariya mbǝ jì pet an, mo kǝ ɗar mpwoo lu ɗe an ɗi.
ACT 11:12 Riin mǝ Naan sat nghan nǝ, a seet ashak kǝ mo, baa ashak kǝ mee kyetwo kas. Pak nenseet nɗang Jesu mo peemee, mo seet ashak kǝ an zak, ɓǝ mu dǝm mu ɗel nlu kǝ gwar nǝ.
ACT 11:13 Yaksǝ gwar nǝ wur sat mmun nǝ, ɗi naa mee ngulep mǝ Naan kǝ ɗar nɗǝǝn lu fin, ɗang ngulep nǝ sat nɗyin nǝnee, <A lep shindǝm nJoppa, kǝ mo pet mee gwar ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Simon Pita jì ntul fwaa.>
ACT 11:14 Wur mbǝ nsatpwoo nghan ɗe nǝn nle kǝ nwun kat ɓam, waa kǝ nenlu fwaa mo jir.
ACT 11:15 <<Kaaɗe nɗoom leshap, ɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang sham nkaa mo, nciit kǝ ɗe dǝ wur sham nkaa mun nshee sǝ.
ACT 11:16 Ɓǝ nǝ le nghan panpwoo mǝ Daa, ɗe gyet wur sat nǝnee, <Joon kǝ cìn baptisma ngurum mo a shi am, ɗangnaan wur mbǝ ncìn baptisma nwun a shi Riin Ɗeɓang.>
ACT 11:17 Katɗang ɓǝ mbiizuum ɗesǝ, ɗe Naan wur shin mmo, nǝ a ɗemǝndong kǝ ɗewur shin mmun, mbǝɗe mu shinzeen nDaa Jesu Kristi, ɓǝ wen a wii, ɗe an mmak cíi nNaan yii?>>
ACT 11:18 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo ɗok tǝtǝk, yaksǝ mo kwoop Naan ɗeɗes. Mo sat nǝ, <<Daa Naan kǝ shínpee nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, mbǝkǝ mo tuwap, kǝ mo kat seen ɗi zak.>>
ACT 11:19 Nen ɗe dǝ mo rangkáa mbǝ jeel ɗe nǝ kǝ yool, ɗe nǝ le gyet mo tu Stivin, ɓǝ pak mo dǝm wul nyil mFonisha, kǝ Saiprus, kǝ pee nkaam nAntiyok. Baa mo satpwoo Naan nǝ, mmee nen ɗecì mo kas, tǝng a nnen Yahudi mo ɓejee ɗak.
