ACT 11:20 Ɗangɓe pak nen shinzeen nǝ mo, ɗe mo a nen Saiprus mo, kǝ Sairin mo, mo dǝm wul Antiyok, ɓǝ mo kop pwoo Naan nǝ nnen Helene mo zak, kǝzak mo leshap ɗeret ngurum mo nkaa Daa Jesu.
ACT 11:21 Iiko mǝ Daa nǝ ɗi ashak kǝ mo, ɓǝ gurum mo ɗes mo shinzeen, ɓǝ mo ciir kǝ pǝtuup fur mo pǝ Daa Naan ɗi.
ACT 11:22 Pwoo nkaa mo nǝ wul nkom mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn Jerusalem, ɓǝ mo lep Barnabas, kǝ nwur dǝm ɗe Antiyok nǝ.
ACT 11:23 Kaaɗe wur seet wul, ɓǝ wur naa ɗeret ɗe Naan le nkaa mo, ɓǝ wur kat retnyit, ɗang wur leshap mmo jir, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen nNaan azeen-zeen shi pǝtuup fur mo jir.
ACT 11:24 Barnabas a mee ngwe ɗe ndǝre, kǝzak wur gam kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, kǝ shinzeen zak. Gurum mo ɗes mo shinzeen nDaa zak.
ACT 11:25 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ Barnabas dǝm nTarsus, mbǝ yap Sool.
ACT 11:26 Kaaɗe wur kat Sool, ɓǝ wur jì kǝ wur nAntiyok. Mbǝ ɓit mǝndong, ɓǝ Barnabas kǝ Sool moo kaat ashak kǝ nen shinzeen nǝ mo, yaksǝ mo kám-kam ngurum mo. Mo shee pet nenseet nɗang Jesu mo a Kristiyan a nɗǝǝn pee nkaam Antiyok.
ACT 11:27 Nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ pak nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo pwat nJerusalem, ɓǝ mo jì Antiyok.
ACT 11:28 Memee nɗǝǝn mo, ɗe sǝm wur a Agabus, wur yool ɗar atǝng, ɓǝ wur sat agaak shi iiko ɓal mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang nǝnee, <<Mee neen ɗeɗes nǝ mbǝ taa nkaa yil nǝ jir.>> Mo cìn mǝnǝ a nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗe Klodiyus a mishkoom.
ACT 11:29 Nenseet nɗang Jesu mo le pǝtuup fur mo, kǝ koo weyi, ɓǝ wur shin mbii ɗewur mak, mbǝkǝ mmo lep ɓam dǝm ɗi nnen shinzeen ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya.
ACT 11:30 Kaaɗe mo cak zuum fur nǝ mo le ashak, ɓǝ mo lep shindǝm nnen ɗǝnan-nan mǝ nen shinzeen ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya nsar Barnabas kǝ Sool.
ACT 12:1 Nɗǝǝn teer mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ mishkoom Herot ɗoom shinjeel ɓaanɓaan nkaa pak nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo.
ACT 12:2 Wur tu Jemis, ɗyemnǝǝn mǝ Joon shi kwai.
ACT 12:3 Kaaɗe mishkoom Herot naa muut mǝ Jemis nǝ ret nnen Yahudi mon nyit, ɓǝ wur waa cin shin yaa Pita zak. Ɗesǝ nǝ ɗen a nciit kǝ ɗe mo kǝ se mbiise retnyit mǝ gilaas ɗe baa nǝ kǝ yist kas
ACT 12:4 Kaaɗe Herot yaa Pita, ɓǝ wur le wur nɗǝǝn lushoot, nsar shiitoon mo kaapaat baapeemee, mbǝkǝ mmo tap wur ɗe rǝrret. Herot kǝ lepan nǝ, ɗyin mbǝ put kǝ Pita ntoom gurum mo aɓwoon mǝ retnyit nǝ mɓekǝ tok ɗiyeel.
ACT 12:5 Kaaɗe Pita ɗi a ɓuɓwoot nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mon nkaa ɗangnaan hakyeng, mbǝ wur.
ACT 12:6 Ɗangɓǝ mpar, ɗe daar ɓǝ Herot wur lepan mbǝ put kǝ Pita, mbǝkǝ nwur shinjeel ɗi nwur. Ɓǝ Pita nsaam nnaar shiitoon mo vǝl. Mo ɓwoot wur shi shoolbǝring mo vǝl. Nentappee mo ɗe mpwoo lushoot nǝ, mon nkaa tappee rǝrret.
ACT 12:7 Yaksǝ ngulep mǝ Daa jì ɗar pǝ Pita ɗi, ɓǝ peeɓang nǝ ɓangpee nɗǝǝn lu nǝ. Ngulep mǝ Daa cut Pita nkwoop, wur mii Pita, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<A yool nkyen>> Yaksǝ shoolbǝring ɗe mo nsar wur mo ɗong nyil.
ACT 12:8 Ngulep nǝ sat nwur nǝnee, <<A lep lee fwaa, kǝzak a jwal kwoopshi fwaa mo.>> Ɓǝ Pita wur cìn mbii ɗe ngulep nǝ sat. Ngulep nǝ sat nwur zak nǝnee, <<A sǝp mbiisǝp fwaa. A jì nɗang an.>>
ACT 12:9 Pita put dǝm nɗang ngulep nǝ. Baa wur man nǝ, mbii ɗe ngulep nǝ cìn nǝ azeen kas. Mbǝɗǝ wur pan nǝ ɗyin a nsuun.
ACT 12:10 Kaaɗe mo ɗel nentappee ɗenshee mo, kǝ ɗevǝl mo, ɓǝ mo jì wul mpwoo lu ɗe mo ɗak a shi shool, ɗe nii naa nkwoop pee nkaam, ɓǝ pwoo lu mǝnǝ wang shikáa fer. Ɓǝ mo pwat, mo yaa ar ɗemǝndong. Ɓǝ nnen mman, ɓǝ ngulep nǝ wur yit Pita mbǝshin.
ACT 12:11 Kaaɗe Pita kǝ winshin mɓut mbii ɗe nǝ cìn, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Yaksǝ, wen mman azeen-zeen nǝ, a Daa lep ngulep fin, mbǝkǝ nwur jì ɓam an ɗi nsar Herot, kǝ mbii ɗe nen Yahudi mon nkaa lepyit nǝ, nǝn ncìn.>>
ACT 12:12 Kaaɗe wur winshin mɓut nǝ a kǝsǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm nlu Meeri nǝǝn Joon, ɗe moo pet wur a Maak zak. A pee ɗe gurum mo kǝ kuur ɗi ɗes, kǝ mo nkaa ɗangnaan ɗi.
ACT 12:13 Kaaɗe Pita ɓwap pwoo lu, ɓǝ mee laareep ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm war a Roda, war jì mbǝ wang pwoo lu nǝ.
ACT 12:14 Kaaɗe war kǝlǝng ɗoo nǝ a mǝ Pita, ɓǝ baa war wang pwoo lu nǝ kas mbǝ retnyit. Ɗangɓe war waa cin shin, kǝ nwar sat nnen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn lu nǝ, Pita kǝ ɗar a tool mpwoo lu nǝ.
ACT 12:15 Mo sat nwar nǝnee, <<Yii tǝttar aa?>> Ɗangɓe war sat nǝ, tǝng a Pita azeen-zeen. Yaksǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<A ngulep wur.>>
ACT 12:16 Ɗangɓe Pita naa a mɓwap pwoo lu nǝ ɗak, ɓǝ kaaɗe mo wang pwoo lu nǝ, ɓǝ mo naa a Pita azeen-zeen, ɓǝ nǝ aapwoo mmo zam.
ACT 12:17 Ɗangɓe Pita ɗǝk sar mmo, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗok tǝtǝk. Ɓǝ wur yakshii nǝ mmo, kaaɗe Daa put kǝ ɗyin nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ. Wur sat mmo zak nǝnee, <<Wu satpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ nJemis, kǝ koor nen shinzeen nǝ mo zak.>> Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ Pita yool dǝm mmee pee ɗecì.
ACT 12:18 Kaaɗe ɓitmang, ɓǝ mee ɓǝlep ɗeɗes yool nnaar shiitoon ɗe mo kǝ tap Pita nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ, mbǝɗe baa mo man mbii ɗe nǝ cìn Pita kas.
ACT 12:19 Herot kǝ le kǝ mmo dǝm yappee ɗe Pita dǝm ɗi, ɓǝ baa mo dǝm kat wur kas. Herot tal pǝ shiitoon nǝ mo rǝrret, ɓǝ wur le kǝ mmo twe mo ɗi. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ Herot yool yit yil nJudiya, kǝ nwur dǝm ɗi nyil nSizariya, ɓǝ wur dǝm cìn mee rep teer mo ɗe mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 12:20 Herot langtuup kǝ nen Taya mo, kǝ nen Saidon mo hakyeng. Aasǝ ɓǝ mo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo dǝm naa wur ɗi. Mo shee yap ar ɗe mon ndǝm naa Herot a pǝ Blastus ɗi, ɗewur a ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa lu mishkoom nǝ. Yaksǝ mo dǝm pǝ Herot ɗi, ɓǝ mo ɗang pǝ wur, kǝ mmo kat tongriyang ɗi pǝ mishkoom, mbǝɗe yil mo nii kat mbiise a nɗǝǝn yil mishkoom nǝ.
ACT 12:21 Kaaɗe puus ɗe mo kǝ le nǝ wul, ɓǝ Herot tap jwal lee fin ɗe mǝ mishkoom, wur tap tong nkaa mbii tong mǝ ɗeɗes fin, ɓǝ wur leshap nnen nǝ mo.
ACT 12:22 Nen nǝ mo le or, ɗang mo sat nǝnee, <<Ɗesǝ nǝ a ɗoo mǝ mee naan baa a mǝ gurum kas.>>
ACT 12:23 Nnen mman, ɓǝ mee ngulep mǝ Daa Naan cut Herot, mbǝɗe baa wur shin ɗeɗes nNaan kas. Ɓǝ yaksǝ nyet mo se Herot ɓǝ wur muut.
ACT 12:24 Gurum mo ɗes mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝ Naan, ɓǝ mo shinzeen, ɓǝ pwoo mǝ Naan nǝ dǝm shipee-shipee zak.
ACT 12:25 Kaaɗe Barnabas kǝ Sool mo kyes ɗak fur, ɓǝ mo baaji nJerusalem ashak kǝ Joon ɗe mo kǝ pet wur a Maak.
ACT 13:1 Nɗǝǝn kuur kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon Antiyok, ɓǝ pak nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo, kǝ nenkam-kám mo ɗi. Barnabas, kǝ Simiyon ɗe mo kǝ pet wur a ɗetǝp, kǝ Lusiyus ngu Sairin, kǝ Manayen ɗewur wurang ashak kǝ mishkoom Herot, kǝ Sool.
ACT 13:2 Kaaɗe mon nkaa seyil nDaa ɗang mon nkaa yaa pwoo kǝ neen zak, ɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang sat nǝnee, <<Wu bǝlǝp Barnabas kǝ Sool wu le nghan, mbǝ ɗak ɗe an kǝn mpet mo mbǝ cìn nǝ.>>
ACT 13:3 Ɓǝ mo yaa pwoo kǝ neen, ɗang mo ɗangnaan zak, ɓǝ mo lesar nkaa mo, ɓǝ mo ɓwet Barnabas kǝ Sool mo shinseet.
ACT 13:4 Riin Ɗeɓang lep Barnabas kǝ Sool mo shindǝm nSelusiya, ɓǝ mo dǝm ɗel tii mpeemǝnǝ, kǝ mo dǝm ɗe nSaiprus.
ACT 13:5 Kaaɗe mo wul nSalamis, ɓǝ mo satpwoo mǝ Naan ngurum mo nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo. Joon ɗe sǝm wur a Maak sǝ, wur ɗe ashak kǝ mo mbǝ ɓam.
ACT 13:6 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn yil ɗe Am kuur neer nǝ cǝǝrkaat jir ɓǝ, mo dǝm wul mPafos, ɓǝ mo kat mee ngu Yahudi ɗe mo kǝ petsǝm wur a Barjesu wur a ngucìn yen ɗebish, kǝzak wur leshin a koo ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan sǝ, ɗang baa wur a ngusatpwoo Naan kas.
ACT 13:7 Wur ɗi ashak kǝ nguɗak mǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ, gofna Sarjiyus Polo, wur a mee ngumanshii mbii zam. Gofna nǝ wur pet Barnabas kǝ Sool, mbǝɗe wur reɓet kǝlǝng pwoo mǝ Naan pǝ mo ɗi.
ACT 13:8 Ɗangɓe Elimas nguyen ɗebish sǝ, (A sǝm wur nǝ mmǝnǝ shi liispwoo mǝ Heleni) wur cíi mmo, mbǝɗe wur rǝɓet kǝ taji gofna nǝ wur shinzeen mpwoo mǝ Naan kas.
ACT 13:9 Ɗangɓe Sool ɗe moo pet wur a Pool, wur gam kǝ Riin mǝ Naan, ɓǝ wur ban yit fǝn nzǝng nkaa ngucìn yen ɗebish nǝ,
ACT 13:10 ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Waa làa mǝ ngunjwaan! Gha a shaarlek mǝ mbii ɗe ndǝre mo jir. Kǝzak pǝtuup fwaa nǝ gam kǝ gwampee, kǝ cìn nyang. Aa ɗaar shidaar-shidaar, mbǝkǝ nghan cǝǝr kǝ zeen mǝ Daa, mbǝkǝ nǝ ɗee ɗi a ɗung.
ACT 13:11 A naa yaksǝ, Daa Naan wur mbǝ le kǝ gha ɗee a vum. Baa gha mmak naa puus kas, mbǝ reppee lee.>> Abet-abet, ɓǝ vuun, kǝ peenkwoo mo jì paa Elimas, ɓǝ wur ɗoom yappee, mbǝ yap ngwe ɗe mbǝ yaakam nwur.
ACT 13:12 Kaaɗe gofna nǝ wur naa mbii aapwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur shinzeen, mbǝɗe nǝ fes aapwoo nwur nkaa kám ɗewur kǝlǝng nkaa Daa Naan.
ACT 13:13 Pool kǝ nnen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur, mo yool mPafos, ɓǝ mo ɗel nɗǝǝn tii, kǝ mo dǝm ɗi mPaga ɗe nǝ nyil mPamfiliya, ɓǝ Joon Maak yit mo mpeemǝnǝ, kǝ nwur baa dǝm ɗi nJerusalem.
ACT 13:14 Mo yool mPaga, ɓǝ mo ɗel dǝm Antiyok ɗe nǝ mPisidiya. Parpuus Nookɗi, ɓǝ mo ɗel nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan, ɓǝ mo tong ɗi.
ACT 13:15 Aɓwoon ɗe mee gurum kǝ tang nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Wàar mǝ Mosis mo, kǝ nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo, ɓǝ nen ɗǝnan-nan nkaa lu mǝ Naan nǝ, mo lep sat mmo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, katɗang wun kǝ mee pwoo ɗe wun mbǝ sat ngurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ wu sat.>>
ACT 13:16 Pool yool ɗar atǝng, ɓǝ wur ɗiyeep sar wur, mbǝkǝ ngurum nǝ mo ɗok ɗe tǝtǝk, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Wun nnen Isreil mo, kǝ wun nen ɗe baa wun a nnen Isreil mo kas, ɗe wuu kǝǝr Naan, wu lekom fuu mo.
ACT 13:17 Naan mǝ nnen Isreil mo, bǝlǝp puun fun mo ɗang wur le mo a ɗeɗes, ɓǝ mo a mǝzep nɗǝǝn yil Ijip. Wur put kǝ mo nɗǝǝn yil Ijip shiɓal fin ɗeɗes zak.
ACT 13:18 Mbǝ ɓit mo laarfeer, ɓǝ wur mang gung kǝ mo a naaryil.
ACT 13:19 Wur le kǝ mmo twe mee soon mo pwoovǝl nɗǝǝn yil nKeenan, ɓǝ wur shin yil mǝnǝ nnen fin Isreil mo, ɓǝ nǝ ɗee mo a mbii kok kop. Mo tong nɗǝǝn yil mǝnǝ mbǝ ɓit mo kambil feer kǝ laarpaat.
ACT 13:20 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur shin nentokɗyeel mo mmo, dǝm jì wul mɓít mǝ ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan Samuwel.
ACT 13:21 Kaaɗe mo ɗang pǝ Naan kǝ nwur shin mishkoom mmo, ɓǝ Naan shin Sool làa mǝ Kish mmo, ɗewur a ɗang mǝ Benjamin. Sool se mishkoom nǝ mbǝ ɓit mo laarfeer.
ACT 13:22 Aɓwoon ɗe Naan shang Sool mɓut nɗak mishkoom nǝ. Ɓǝ wur bǝlǝp Devit kǝ nwur ɗee a mishkoom mo. Naan shin langtǝng nkaa Devit nǝnee, <An kǝn nkat Devit làa mǝ Jese, a ngwe ɗe wen nreɓet hakyeng. Wur mbǝ cin mbii ɗe nsat mo nwur jir.>
ACT 13:23 A nɗǝǝn ɗang mǝ gwar ɗe ɗesǝ, ɓǝ Naan jì kǝ Jesu Nguɓam mbǝ nnen Isreil mo, kaaɗe gyet Naan kǝ ten tuweer mmo sǝ.
ACT 13:24 Akuɗang Jesu jì, ɓǝ Joon kǝ ten satpwoo Naan nnen Isreil mo jir nǝnee, <Mo tuwap, mbǝkǝ mmo cin baptisma ɗi mmo zak.>
ACT 13:25 Kaaɗe Joon kus kǝ kyes ɗak fin, ɓǝ wur tal pǝ gurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <Wun, pǝpan nǝ, an a wii? Baa a an a ngwe ɗe wun mbǝ ɗarnaa jì wur kas. Ɗangɓe wu lekom, mee gurum mbǝ jì aɓwoon fen, ɗe koo a teng kwoopshi ɗe nshii wur mo, ɓǝ baa ɗeret fen nǝ mak kǝ nghan fwen teng kwoopshi wur nǝ mo kas.>
ACT 13:26 <<Ɗyemnaa mo! Jep mǝ ɗang Abraham mo, kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, ɗe mo kǝ kǝǝr Naan nɗǝǝn wun. A mbǝ wun jir, ɓǝ Naan kǝ lep pwoo ɓam ɗesǝ nǝ jì.
ACT 13:27 Nen ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn Jerusalem kǝ nennan fur mo, baa mo man nǝ, Jesu a Nguɓam kas, kǝzak baa mo manshii mǝ pwoo nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo, ɗe mo kǝ tang koo a parpuus Nookɗi ɗeɗangyii kas zak. Gyet mo gampwoo ɗe gyet nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo kǝ ten sat kaaɗe gyet mo tokɗyeel muut nJesu sǝ.
ACT 13:28 Koo ɗe baa gyet mo kat wur cìn mee shikbish ɗe nǝ mak muut nwur kas, ɓǝ mo ɗang pǝ Pailet kǝ mmo tu wur ɗi.
ACT 13:29 Kaaɗe mbii ɗe mo kǝ ten nran nkaa wur mo gam jir, ɓǝ mo sham kǝ kúm wur nkaa shiyeepyoom nǝ, ɓǝ mo dǝm le kúm wur nɗǝǝn gwoot kǝcir.
ACT 13:30 Ɗangɓe Naan yool kǝ wur a peemúut.
ACT 13:31 Mbǝ meeteer mo ɗes, ɓǝ wur woo shin fin nnen ɗe gyet mo kǝ mwaan ashak kǝ wur, yool nGalili jì nJerusalem. Yaksǝ ɓǝ mo ɗee a langtǝng wur pǝ gurum mo ɗi.
ACT 13:32 Mmun, muu satpwoo ɗeret nwun, a pwoo ɗe gyet Naan kǝ ten cweer mpuun fun mo.
ACT 13:33 Naan kǝgam pǝ mun jep mo mo nɗesǝ, kaaɗe wur yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut. Ɗesǝ nǝ nciit kǝ mbii ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn Zabura ɗevǝl sǝ nǝnee, <Gha a Làa fen, cicinsǝ an kǝn ɗee a puun fwaa.>
ACT 13:34 A pwoo ɗe Naan sat nkaa yool wur a peemúut nɗesǝ nǝnee, <Baa wur mbǝ baa cam muut ɗe zak kas> Kǝzak Naan sat zak nǝnee, <An mbǝ le ɗeret ɗe nǝ azeen-zeen nkaa wun, ɗe gyet kǝn ten ncweer nDevit.>
ACT 13:35 Kǝzak, wur sat nɗǝǝn mee Zabura nǝnee, <Baa gha mmak yit kǝ ngwe fwaa ɗeɓang wam nɗǝǝn kǝcir kas.>
ACT 13:36 <<Gyet Devit kǝ cìn ɗak nciit kǝ ɗyen mǝ Naan mɓít fin mo, ɓǝ wur muut, ɓǝ mo wum wur ashak kǝ puun fin mo, ɓǝ wur wam.
ACT 13:37 Ɗang Jesu ɗe Naan kǝ yool kǝ wur a peemúut, baa wur wam nɗǝǝn kǝcir kas.
ACT 13:38 Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo! Wu man nǝ, a mbǝ ɗeret mǝ gwar ɗesǝ nǝ, ɓǝ mun nkaa leshap nwun nkaa fwo mǝ shikbish fuu mo.
ACT 13:39 A mbǝ Jesu zak, ɗang koo ngwe ɗeɗangyii ɗewur shinzeen, ɓǝ wur mbǝ kat ɓam nɗǝǝn shikbish mo jir. Ɗangɓe baa Wàar Mosis nǝ mo mak ɓam wun mɓut shikbish fuu mo kas.
ACT 13:40 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, wu tap kǝ káa fuu mo, kǝ taji mbii ɗe gyet nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo sat nǝ sham taa nkaa wun kas. Gyet mo sat nǝnee,
ACT 13:41 <Wu lekom, wun nenɓákpee mo, nǝn aapwoo nwun, ɗang wu mmurep. Mbǝɗǝ an mbǝ cìn mee ɗak nɗǝǝn teer fuu mo, ɗak ɗe baa wun mbǝ shínzeen nnǝ kas, koo dǝɓen. Koo ɗe mee gurum leshap nwun nkaa nǝnee, ɓǝ baa wun mbǝ shínzeen kas.> >>
ACT 13:42 Kaaɗe Pool kǝ Barabbas mo a ar put nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan nǝ, ɓǝ gurum nǝ mo ɗang pǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mmo cin leshap ɗi nkaa mbii ɗe mo kǝ sat mo, parpuus Nookɗi ɗe mbǝ jì zak.
ACT 13:43 Ɓǝ aɓwoon ɗe gurum mo rangkáa a peekuur nǝ, ɓǝ nnen Yahudi mo ɗes, kǝ nnen ɗe mo kǝ ciir ɗee a nnen Yahudi mo. Nen ɗe moo lepyit nkaa Naan, mo seet nɗang Pool kǝ Barnabas. Yaksǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas mo leshap mmo, shínɓal mmo mputuup, mbǝkǝ mmo mwaan ɗi nɗǝǝn ɗeret mǝ Naan.
ACT 13:44 Kaaɗe parpuus Nookɗi nǝ jì wul, ɓǝ nen pee nkaam nǝ mo ɗes hakyeng mo baaji kuur, mbǝ kǝlǝng pwoo mǝ Naan nǝ, ɗee rep pak mo nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ a lee ɗak.
ACT 13:45 Ɗangɓe kaaɗe nnen Yahudi mo naa gurum mo kuur ɗes, ɓǝ pǝtuup mo mo gam kǝ zuur zam, nǝ le mmo sat nǝ, mbii ɗe Pool sat nǝ mo a ɗung, ɗang mo leshap ɗebuu nkaa wur zak.
ACT 13:46 Yaksǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas mo waa sǝǝt leshap nǝ ɓalɓal agaak baa kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas. Mo sat nǝnee, <<Nǝ a tǝng kǝ mo shee satpwoo mǝ Naan nǝ a nwun, ɗang wu ciipwoo Naan nǝ, kǝzak wu lesuk a koo baa wun kǝkoop nǝ mbǝ kat seen ɗe dǝm nghaa-nghaa kas. Ɓǝ yaksǝ, mun mbǝ yit wun, mbǝkǝ mmun dǝm mu satpwoo mǝ Naan nǝ ɗe nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas.
ACT 13:47 Mbǝɗǝ Daa kǝ sat mmun nǝnee, <An kǝn le gha, mbǝkǝ nghan ɗee a peeɓang mbǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas. Mbǝkǝ nɗǝǝn gha, ɓǝ gurum ɗe nɗǝǝn yil nǝ mo jir, mo mbǝ kat ɓam ɗi.> >>
ACT 13:48 Kaaɗe nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo kǝlǝng retnyit zam, kǝzak mo lepwoo mǝ Naan a ɗeɗes. Nen ɗe mo kǝ ten bǝlǝp mo le, mbǝkǝ mmo kat seen ɗe dǝm nghaa-nghaa ɗi.
ACT 13:49 Pwoo kǝ Daa Naan nǝ dǝm shipee-shipee nɗǝǝn yil mǝnǝ jir.
ACT 13:50 Ɗangɓe nnen Yahudi mo kar pak shurep ɗe mo kǝǝr Naan, shurep ɗǝnan-nan mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo, kǝ mmo shinjeel ɗe nkaa Pool kǝ Barnabas. Ɗangɓe mo ceen Pool kǝ Barnabas put aku nɗǝǝn yil mo.
ACT 13:51 Ɓǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas mo ɓwap ǝrong ɗe nǝn nkaa shii mo mo, mbǝkǝ nǝ ɗee ɗi a langtǝng nkaa nen pee nkaam nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo dǝm Ikoniyum.
ACT 13:52 Nenseet nɗang Jesu mo gam kǝ retnyit zam, ɗang mo gam kǝ Riin mǝ Naan zak.
ACT 14:1 nƊǝǝn Ikoniyum, ɓǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas mo ɗel nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo. Ɓǝ mo sat pwoo mǝ Naan, ɗe gurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, mo shinzeen.
ACT 14:2 Ɗangɓe nnen Yahudi ɗe mo cii shinzeen mpwoo nǝ, mo kar, kǝzak mo lepshii nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, mbǝkǝ mmo yool ɗi kǝ pwoo ɗebuu nkaa nenseet nɗang Jesu mo.
ACT 14:3 Pool kǝ Barnabas mo tong mpee nkaam mǝnǝ, mbǝ teer mo ɗes hakyeng, kǝ mmo leshap ngurum mo nkaa Daa ɓalɓal agaak, baa ashak kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas. Mo ɗee a langtǝng mǝ pwoo wur ɗeret nǝ, mbǝɗe Daa kǝ le kǝn Pool kǝ Barnabas mo cìn mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo mo.
ACT 14:4 Nen pee nkaam nǝ mo ɓàksut vǝl, pak mo dǝm nɗang pwoo mǝ nnen Yahudi mo, ɗang pak mo dǝm nɗang pwoo mǝ jeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 14:5 Nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ nnen Yahudi mo, mo ɓalpwoo mo mo ashak kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mmo shinjeel ɗi njeplep nǝ mo, kǝ mmo car mo ɗi shi ghǝk zak.
ACT 14:6 Yaksǝ kaaɗe jeplep nǝ mo kǝlǝng mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo pwat shwe dǝm mpee nkaam nListira kǝ Debi, ɗe mo ngaar yil nLukoniya, kǝ pak jepyil ɗe mo neer pee nkaam mǝnǝ mo.
ACT 14:7 Mo leshap ɗeret ngurum mo mpeemǝnǝ mo zak.
ACT 14:8 Nɗǝǝn Listira nǝ, ɓǝ mee gwar wur ɗi, ɗe shii wur mo kut, mbǝɗe pǝgyet mo làa wur a kurumkut ɓe baa wur kǝ cam mwaan shi shii fin kas.
ACT 14:9 Wur lekom mbǝkǝ nwur kǝlǝng Pool ɗe nkaa leshap. Pool ban yit nzǝng nkaa gwar nǝ, ɓǝ kaaɗe wur naa gwar nǝ kǝ shinzeen ɗe nǝ mak kǝn mo bar gwar nǝ,
ACT 14:10 yaksǝ Pool sat shi ɗoo ɗeɗes nǝnee, <<A yool a ɗar shi shii fwaa!>> Ɓǝ gwar nǝ wur sham yool metpee, ɗang wur mwaan zak.
ACT 14:11 Kaaɗe kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo naa mbii ɗe Pool cìn ɓǝ mo ɗiyeep ɗoo fur mo shi liispwoo mǝ nnen Lukoniya mo, mo sat nǝnee, <<A naan mo sham pǝ mun ɗe, nɗǝǝn nan koo mun gurum sǝ.>>
ACT 14:12 Mo pet Barnabas a Ziiyos, ɗang mo pet Pool a Hamis, mbǝɗe a Pool wur a ngusatpwoo nǝ.
ACT 14:13 Yaksǝ mishkoom kùm ɗe mǝ Ziiyos, ɗe lu kùm wur nǝ kus kǝ pee nkaam nǝ, wur jì kǝ kus nǝng mo, kǝ pelɗem mo, ngaar pǝbong nǝ, mbǝɗe wur kǝ kuur gurum nǝ mo, mo kǝ reɓet wus mbiizuum njeplep nǝ mo.
ACT 14:14 Ɗangɓe, kaaɗe, Barnabas kǝ Pool mo kǝlǝng mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo yilang nlǝr fur mo. Mo shwe dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn kuur gurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo le or, ɓǝ mo sat nǝnee,
ACT 14:15 <<Hee des oo! A mii le ɗang wun pǝ reɓet cìn mbii mǝnǝ ii? Mun a gurum mo koo wun sǝ. Mu jì mpee ɗesǝ a mbǝkǝ mmo satpwoo ɗeret ɗe nwun, mbǝkǝ nwun yit mbii ɗebuu sǝ mo ɗi, ɗe baa mo kǝ mee koop nǝ kas. Mbǝkǝ nwun jì pǝ Naan ɗewur kǝ seen. A wur le ɗeng, kǝ yil, kǝ Am kuur mo, kǝ mbii ɗe nɗǝǝn mo jir zak.
ACT 14:16 Dǝ yam-yam ɓǝ, a Naan shínpee ngurum mo jir, kǝ mo mwaan nɗǝǝn ar ɗe mo kǝ reɓet.
ACT 14:17 Jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ baa wur kǝ cam nook cìn langtǝng mbǝ shin fin kas, mbǝɗe wur cìn mbii ɗeret mo. A wur shin fwan sham nwun aɗeng, kǝ mbii kǝkop fuu mo ntarpas, ɗang a wur shin mbiise nwun ɗes zak, kǝzak a wur gam pǝtuup fuu mo shi retnyit zak.>>
ACT 14:18 Jeplep nǝ mo leshap ɗesǝ mmo, jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ a prurut, ɗang mo cíi nkuur kǝ gurum nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ taji gurum nǝ mo wus mbiizuum mbǝ seyil mmo kas.
ACT 14:19 Ɗangɓe pak nnen Yahudi mo pwat Antiyok, ɗe nǝ mPisidiya, kǝ Ikoniyum, mo jì mangɗyeen ngurum nǝ mo, ɗe mo kar kuur gurum nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mmo yool ɗi kǝ lek nkaa jeplep nǝ mo. Yaksǝ mo car Pool shi ghǝk, ɓǝ mo fee wur put kǝ nǝ aɓwoon pee nkaam nǝ. Mo pan nǝ, Pool kǝ muut.
ACT 14:20 Ɗang kaaɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu mo jì neer Pool, ɓǝ wur yool, wur ɗel nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ. Daar nǝ, ɓǝ wur kǝ Barnabas mo pwat dǝm nDebi.
ACT 14:21 Pool kǝ Barnabas, mo dǝm leshap ɗeret nǝ nnen pee nkaam nDaabi mo, ɓǝ gurum mo ɗes mo shinzeen nDaa Jesu. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo baaji nListira, kǝ Ikoniyum, kǝ Antiyok zak.
ACT 14:22 Mo shínɓal mputuup nenseet nɗang Jesu mo. Mo leshap mmo, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗar ɗe ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen mo, kǝ mo kám mo zak nǝnee, <<Mun shwaajeel ɗes, akuɗang ɓǝ mun mbǝ mmak ɗel nɗǝǝn pee ɗehai mǝ Naan.>>
ACT 14:23 Pool kǝ Barnabas mo bǝlǝp nen ɗenan-nan mo, mbǝ koo a kuur mǝ nenseet ndang Naan ɗǝɗang mo ii, ashak kǝ ɗang, kǝ yaa pwoo kǝ neen zak, ɓǝ mo le nnen ɗe mo bǝlǝp nǝ mo nsar mǝ Daa, ɗe mo shinzeen nwur.
ACT 14:24 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ taaɗel ngaar mPisidiya, ɓǝ mo jì wul mPamfiliya.
ACT 14:25 Kaaɗe mo kǝ satpwoo nǝ nɗǝǝn Paga, ɓǝ mo yool sham dǝm Ataliya.
ACT 14:26 Mo yool mpee mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo ɗel tii, kǝn mmo baaji ɗin Antiyok, pee nkaam ɗe dǝ mo shee ɗangnaan ɗi nkaa mo, mbǝkǝ nɗeret mǝ Naan nǝ kyeer mo ɗi nɗǝǝn ɗak, ɗe yaksǝ ɓǝ mo kǝ cìn kyes.
ACT 14:27 Kaaɗe mo baaji wul, ɓǝ mo pet kuur nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo ashak jir, ɓǝ mo leshap ngurum nǝ mo nkaa mbii ɗe Naan le kǝ mmo cìn, kǝ kaaɗe wur wang ar mǝ shinzeen nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas zak.
ACT 14:28 Mo tong nɗǝǝn pee nkaam mǝnǝ ɗes, ashak kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo.
ACT 15:1 Pak gurum mo tong nJudiya mo jì nAntiyok, ɓǝ mo jì kám nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Katɗang baa mo can wun, kaaɗe Wàar mǝ Mosis sat sǝ kas, ɓǝ baa wun mbǝ mak kat ɓam kas.>>
ACT 15:2 Pool kǝ Barnabas mo cìn ɓeetshik ɗes kǝ mo, nkaa kám mǝnǝ. Aasǝ ɓǝ, mo bǝlǝp Pool kǝ Barnabas kǝ pak gurum mo nɗǝǝn nen shinzeen nǝ mo, kǝ mmo dǝm nJerusalem pǝ jeplep mo ɗi, kǝ nennan mǝ Eklesiya mo, mbǝkǝ mmo dǝm ɓeetpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ ɗi.
ACT 15:3 Eklesiya mo ɓwet mo, ɓǝ mo taa mer nyil mFonisha kǝ Samariya. Mo satpwoo tuwap mǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, kǝzak kaaɗe mo le pǝtuup mo mo pǝ Naan ɗi. Pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ jì kǝ retnyit nnenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo hakyeng.
ACT 15:4 Kaaɗe mo wul nJerusalem, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo kǝ jeplep mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo, mo kaat mo. Yaksǝ mo yakshii mǝ mbii ɗe Naan wur cìn ashak kǝ mo jir.
ACT 15:5 Yaksǝ pak nen shinzeen ɗe mo a mǝ ar mǝ nen Farisi mo, mo yool kǝ pwoo nǝnee, <<Nǝ ret kǝ tǝng mo can nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, kǝzak nǝ a tǝng mo tap Wàar mǝ Mosis rǝrret zak.>>
ACT 15:6 Jeplep mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ Eklesiya nǝ, mo kuur ashak, mbǝkǝ mmo naashii mǝ pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ ɗi.
ACT 15:7 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ ɓeetpwoo nǝ ɗes ndǝr-ndǝr hakyeng, ɓǝ Pita yool ɗar atǝng, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo! Wu man nǝ, Naan shee bǝlǝp an mɓut nwun, mbǝkǝ nghan sat pwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗi nnen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ mmo shinzeen ɗi.
ACT 15:8 Naan ɗewur man pǝtuup mǝ gurum mo jir, wur kám agaak nǝ, ɗyin ɗi lap mo, kaaɗe wur shin Riin Ɗeɓang mmo, nciit kǝ ɗe dǝ wur kǝ shin mmun sǝ zak.
ACT 15:9 Baa Naan ɓàkyit mmun kǝ mo kas. Wur vwang shikbish ɗe nɗǝǝn pǝtuup mo mo, a mbǝɗe mo shinzeen.
ACT 15:10 Mbǝ mǝnǝ yaksǝ, ɓǝ a mii le ɗang wun pǝ kam Naan ii? Wun nkaa le lée ɗe toon nkaa took mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo, ɗe koo a puun fun mo, kǝ mun, ɓǝ baa mu mak mang lée nǝ mo kas.
ACT 15:11 Hai! Mu shinzeen nǝ, a mbǝ ɗeret mǝ Daa fun Jesu, ɗang mu kat ɓam, kaaɗe mo kat ɓam nǝ sǝ zak.>>
ACT 15:12 Kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo ɗok tǝtǝk, kǝ mmo lekom mbǝ kǝlǝng pwoo mǝ Barnabas, kǝ Pool, kaaɗe mo nkaa leshap mmo nkaa mbii lukshik mo, kǝ mbii aapwoo mo, ɗe Naan le kǝ mPool kǝ Barnabas mo cìn, nɗǝǝn nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas.
ACT 15:13 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kyes leshap nǝ, ɓǝ Jemis sat nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, wu lekom kǝ nwun kǝlǝng an ɗi.
ACT 15:14 Pita kǝ leshap nwun nkaa wal ɗe Naan shee kám nǝ nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas. Wur shwat pak mo nɗǝǝn mo, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗee ɗi a nen fin mo.
ACT 15:15 Ɗesǝ nǝ a nciit kǝ pwoo mǝ nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo, ɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Naan nǝnee,
ACT 15:16 <Aɓwoon ɗesǝ ɓǝ an mbǝ baajì. Mbǝkǝ nghan mbaa ɗi kǝ lu mǝ Devit ɗe nǝ shirip sǝ ɗi. An mbǝ baa ɗiyeep kǝrem lu ɗe mo kǝ shirip nǝ zak.
ACT 15:17 Mbǝkǝ nkoor gurum mo jir, ɓǝ mo jì tang Daa ɗi, kǝ jir nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, ɗe an kǝn pǝrep mo, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗi a nen fen mo.
ACT 15:18 A Daa kǝ sat a kǝsǝ! Wur kǝ ten le kǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗee a ɗemǝman pegyet ɗi yam-yam.>
ACT 15:19 <<Mbǝ mǝnǝ, nnaa mǝnǝ, ɓǝ taji wu le nǝ luk nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, ɗe mo ciir kǝ pǝtuup fur mo pǝ Naan ɗi.
ACT 15:20 Ɗangɓe mu ran lep a rǝran mmo, mbǝkǝ mmun sat ɗi mmo nǝnee. Taji mo se mee mbiise ɗe mo kǝ ten shin nkùm kas. Kǝzak taji mo cìn ngaa kas. Taji mo se luwaa mǝ long ɗe mo miyoor took nǝ kas. Kǝzak taji mo se toom kas zak.
ACT 15:21 Mbǝɗǝ mo kǝ tang Wàar mǝ Mosis nǝ peedǝ ɗi yam-yam, koo a parpuus Nookɗi ɗeɗangyii nɗǝǝn lu mǝ Naan nǝ mo jir, kǝ nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ mo jir zak.>>
ACT 15:22 Jeplep nǝ mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo, kǝ nen shinzeen nǝ mo jir, mo naa nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ mmo bǝlǝp pak gurum mo nnaar fur, mbǝkǝ mmo lep mo shindǝm Antiyok ashak kǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas. Ɓǝ mo bǝlǝp Judas ɗe moo pet wur a Barsabas, kǝ Silas zak, ɗe mo a ɗǝnan-nan mɓut nnen shinzeen nǝ mo.
ACT 15:23 Yaksǝ mo lep mo shindǝm ashak kǝ lep a rǝran ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Jeplep mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ Eklesiya mo, mun ɗyemnǝǝn fuu mo, muu lep tokshik fun ɗeɗes dǝm pǝ wun ɗyemnǝǝn fun, nenseet nɗang Jesu mo, ɗe baa wun a nnen Yahudi mo kas. Ɗe wuu tong nɗǝǝn yil Antiyok, kǝ Siriya, kǝ Silisiya.
ACT 15:24 Mu kǝlǝng nǝ, pak gurum mo nɗǝǝn nen ɗe mo pwat pǝ mun ɗi, mo kǝ dǝm daampee nwun shi pwoo mo, kǝ mmo ringshii nwun. Ɓǝ baa a mun mu lep mo kas.
ACT 15:25 Kaaɗe mu kuur ashak, ɓǝ pwoo fun mo seet ndangshak, ɓǝ mu naa nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ mmun bǝlǝp pak gurum mo, mbǝkǝ mmun lep mo dǝm pǝ wun ɗi. Mo dǝm ashak kǝ shaar fun mo Barnabas kǝ Pool.
ACT 15:26 Mo kǝ shin seen fur mo mbǝ cìn ɗak mǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi.
ACT 15:27 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, mu lep Judas kǝ Silas dǝm pǝ wun ɗi. Mo shikáa fur, mon nyakshii mǝ mbii ɗe mǝ nran nɗǝǝn lep a rǝran nǝ nwun shi pwoo.
ACT 15:28 Mbǝɗǝ Riin Ɗeɓang kǝ naa nǝ ret, ɗang mmun mu naa nǝ ret a kǝsǝ zak, mbǝkǝ taji mo le mee lée toon nkaa wun, waa met mbii ɗesǝ mo kas.
ACT 15:29 Taji wu se mbiise ɗe mo kǝ ten shin nkùm kas, kǝzak taji wu se luwaa ashak kǝ toom kas. Taji wu se luwaa mǝ long ɗe mo miyoor took nǝ kas, ɗang taji wu cìn ngaa kas. Katɗang baa wuu cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo kas, ɓǝ nǝ ret zam. Ɗang mukaat. Wu tongriyang.>>
ACT 15:30 Mo lep nenlep nǝ mo shinseet, ɓǝ mo dǝm Antiyok, a mpee ɗe kuur mǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗi ashak, ɓǝ mo shin lep ɗe a rǝran nǝ mmo.
ACT 15:31 Kaaɗe mo tang lep a rǝran nǝ ngurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo kǝlǝng retnyit zam, mbǝɗe pwoo nǝ fes gangkwak mmo zam.
ACT 15:32 Mbǝɗǝ Judas kǝ Silas, mo a nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo zak, ɓǝ mo shínɓal ngurum nǝ mo mputuup zak.
ACT 15:33 Aɓwoon ɗe mo cìn rep teer mo nɗǝǝn Antiyok ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo ɓwet mo ryang, mbǝkǝ mmo baa ɗi pǝ nen ɗe dǝ mo lep mo.
ACT 15:34 Ɗangɓǝ Silas naa nǝ nǝ ret kǝ nɗyin ɗi tong ɗi mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 15:35 Ɓǝ Pool kǝ Barnabas mo tong nɗǝǝn Antiyok mbǝ rep teer mo. Mo nkaa kám, kǝzak mo nkaa satpwoo mǝ Daa, ashak kǝ pak gurum mo ɗes.
ACT 15:36 Aɓwoon meeteer mo ruk, ɓǝ Pool sat mBarnabas nǝnee, <<Nǝ ret kǝ mmun cin mu dǝm, mbǝkǝ mmun tok kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo nɗǝǝn koo a pee nkaam ɗeɗangyii ɓe kǝ mun nakoom mu ɗi.>>
ACT 15:37 Barnabas reɓet kǝ mmo seet ashak kǝ Joon ɗe moo pet wur a Maak.
ACT 15:38 Ɗangɓǝ Pool naa baa nǝ ret kǝ nwur seet ashak kǝ mo a peeɗak nǝ kas. Mbǝɗǝ dǝ wur kǝ su yit mo ɗe nyil mPamfiliya kǝzak baa wur sekyeen ashak kǝ mo nɗǝǝn ɗak nǝ kas.
ACT 15:39 Ɓǝ ɓeetshik yool mmo nnaar, ɗe nǝ le mmo ɓàkshak. Barnabas mang Maak ashak kǝ wur, ɓǝ mo ɗel nɗǝǝn tii kǝ mmo dǝm ɗi nSaiprus.
ACT 15:40 Ɗangɓǝ Pool bǝlǝp Silas. Ɓǝ aɓwoon ɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), ɓǝ mo le mo nsar ɗeret mǝ Daa Naan, ɓǝ mo pwat seet.
ACT 15:41 Pool ɗel dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nSiriya kǝ Silisiya, wur nkaa gangkwak nnenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mo mpeemǝnǝ jir.
ACT 16:1 Pool jì wul nDebi kǝ Listira. Yaksǝ wur kat mee nguseet nɗang Jesu nɗǝǝn Listira nǝ, ɗe sǝm wur a Timoti. Wur a làa mee mat Yahudi ɗe war shinzeen nDaa Jesu, ɗang puun wur a ngu Heleni.
ACT 16:2 Nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nListira kǝ Ikoniyum, moo kwoop mǝse kǝ Timoti nǝ.
ACT 16:3 Pool reɓet kǝ nTimoti seet nɗang wur, a kǝsǝ ɓǝ Pool can Timoti, mbǝ nnen Yahudi ɗe mo nɗǝǝn peemǝnǝ mo. Mbǝɗǝ mo jir, mo man nǝ, puun Timoti a ngu Heleni.
ACT 16:4 Kaaɗe mo a ar mwaan, ɓǝ mo dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn pee nkaam mo, kǝ mo leshap kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon mpeemǝnǝ mo, nkaa Wàar ɗe jeplep mo, kǝ nennan mǝ Eklesiya ɗe nJerusalem mo kǝ sat, mbǝkǝ nnenseet nɗang Jesu mo tap ɗi kǝ Wàar nǝ mo.
ACT 16:5 Aasǝ ɓǝ, nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen fur, ɗang mo ɓul shidaar shidaar zak
ACT 16:6 Pool kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ wur, mo ɗel dǝm nɗǝǝn yil nFirjiya kǝ yil nGalati zak, mbǝɗe baa Riin Ɗeɓang yit kǝ mmo satpwoo Naan nɗǝǝn yil Eshiya kas.
ACT 16:7 Kaaɗe mo wul a pee ɓàkyil mǝ nen Misiya mo, ɓǝ moo reɓet ɗel dǝm nyil mBisiniya, ɗang Riin Jesu tǝǝrsar mmo.
ACT 16:8 Aasǝ ɓǝ, mo ɗel dǝm nɗǝǝn yil mMisiya, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗel sham ɗi nyil nTrowas.
ACT 16:9 Mparmǝnǝ, ɓǝ Pool teer suun nǝ, ɗi naa mee ngu Masidoniya kǝ ɗar, ɗang wur nkaa ɗang pǝ ɗyin nǝnee, <<A can a ɗel nyil mMasidoniya kǝ nghan ɓam mun ɗi!>>
ACT 16:10 Kaaɗe Pool suun suun ɗesǝ, ɓǝ abet-abet mu ɗak sun mbǝ dǝm Masidoniya nǝ, mbǝɗe mu man azeen-zeen nǝ, a Naan pet mun, mbǝkǝ mmun dǝm mu satpwoo fin ɗi mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 16:11 Mu yool nɗǝǝn tii nTrowas, ɓǝ mu ɗel mu seet wur-wur mbǝ dǝm nSamotras. Daar nǝ ɓǝ mu jì mu wul Niyapolis.
ACT 16:12 Mu yool a mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu mwan shi ji nFilipi, ɗe nǝ a pee nkaam ɗeɗes ngaar mMasidoniya. Nǝ a mee yil ɗe nǝn ndǝr nen Rom mo. Yaksǝ mu cìn meeteer mo ruk nɗǝǝn pee nkaam mǝnǝ.
ACT 16:13 Parpuus Nookɗi, ɓǝ mu put mpee nkaam nǝ, kǝn mmun dǝm ɗi mpwoo dung, a pee ɗe mu pan nǝ, mun nkat mee pee ɗangnaan ɗi. Mu tong ɗi mpwoo dung nǝ, mu leshap kǝ shurep ɗe mo jì kuur ɗi.
ACT 16:14 Mee mat war ɗi mɓut nnen ɗe mo kǝlǝng mun, sǝm war a Lidiya ɗe war a mat Tayatira, ɗe war kǝ seet kǝ leelep ɗe rǝrret mo, kǝzak war a mat ɗe war kǝ seyil nNaan zak. Daa Naan wang pǝtuup war, nǝ le nwar lappwoo ɗe Pool kǝ sat mo.
ACT 16:15 Aɓwoon ɗe mo cìn baptisma nwar kǝ nenlu war mo jir, ɓǝ war ɗang pǝ mun nǝnee, <<Katɗang wu le, nǝ an a mat ɗe wen shinzeen nDaa azeen-zeen, ɓǝ wu jì ntul fen.>> Nǝ le nwar ɗyiin shi mun, mbǝ dǝm ntul fer nǝ.
ACT 16:16 Par sǝ kaaɗe mun mbǝ dǝm mbǝ ndang Naan ɓǝ mukaat kǝ mee reep ɗe war mat joon, ɗe nii le kǝn nwar naa mbii ɗe mo mbǝ jì a kyeen. War kǝ naa njì kǝ shool ɗes mpuun fer mo, mbǝɗe war kǝ naa mbii ɗe mo mbǝ cìn a kyeen ngurum mo.
ACT 16:17 War naa jì nɗang Pool kǝ mun, ɗang war le or nǝnee, <<Nen ɗesǝ mo a kǝrem mǝ Naan Ɗehai, kǝzak mon nkaa sat a ar ɗe mǝ ɓam nwun!>>
ACT 16:18 War naa ncìn a kǝsǝ, mbǝ meeteer mo ɗes, dǝm wul a ɗe nǝ láa mPool mɓut ɗes hakyeng, ɓǝ wur ciir sat nriin ɗebish nǝ nǝnee, <<An pǝ sat nghan nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu Kristi, a put aku mɓut nwar.>> Abet-abet ɓǝ riin ɗebish nǝ put nɗǝǝn war.
ACT 16:19 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe puun war mo naa ar kat shool mo nǝ duu, ɓǝ mo yaa Pool kǝ Silas, mo dul mo dǝm kǝ nǝ ntoom nen tokɗyeel mo mpeepring.
ACT 16:20 Kaaɗe mo jì kǝ mo ntoom nentokɗyeel nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Nen ɗesǝ mo a nnen Yahudi. Moo ring gurum mo nɗǝǝn pee nkaam fun.
ACT 16:21 Mo nkaa kám mbii mo mmun, ɗe baa muu loot cìn mo kas. Mbǝ mǝnǝ, baa mu lap mbii ɗe mon nkaa kám nǝ kas, mbǝɗe mun a nnen Rom mo.>>
ACT 16:22 Yaksǝ ɗuu gurum nǝ mo jir mo yool táa nkaa Pool kǝ Silas. Nen tokɗyeel nǝ mo le kǝ mmo yilang nlǝr mPool kǝ Silas. Ɓǝ mo le kǝ mmo nǝrem mo shi kam.
ACT 16:23 Kaaɗe mo nǝrem mo ɗes, ɓǝ mo dǝm shoot mo nɗǝǝn lushoot. Mo sat ngutap nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ, kǝn nwur tap mo ɗe rǝret.
ACT 16:24 Kaaɗe gwar nǝ kǝlǝng pwoo nǝ ɓal a kǝsǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm shoot Pool kǝ Silas nɗǝǝn lushoot ɗe nǝ ndǝǝn-ndǝǝn, ɓǝ wur jwal shii mo mo mɓut nfut.
ACT 16:25 Nnaar par, ɓǝ Pool kǝ Silas mo nkaa ɗangnaan kǝ kook mǝ kwoop Naan. Nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ mo lekom kǝ moo kǝlǝng Pool kǝ Silas ɗe.
ACT 16:26 Ɓǝ nnen mman, yil nǝ sǝǝn ɗes hakyeng, yaksǝ kuk lushoot nǝ mo yoon. Abet ɓǝ pwoo lushoot nǝ mo wang, ɓǝ shoolbǝring ɗe mo ɓwoot nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ jir mo fwen.
ACT 16:27 Kaaɗe ngutap nen ɗe mo, a shishoot nǝ mo mii nsaam, ɓǝ wur naa pwoo lushoot nǝ mo a wuwang jir, ɓǝ wur shang kwai fin, mbǝkǝ nwur tu shik ɗe, mbǝɗe wur pan nǝ nnen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ jir mo, mo kǝ pwat shwe seet jee.
ACT 16:28 Ɗangɓǝ Pool ɗiyeep ɗoo ɓalɓal nǝnee, <<Taji a le mee láa nsak kas, mbǝɗe mun ɗi jir.>>
ACT 16:29 Yaksǝ ngutap nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ wur pet mo jì kǝ wus, ɓǝ wur yool kǝkǝlak, ɗel taa ntoom Pool kǝ Silas, wur nkaa ɗaar mbǝ kǝǝrmuut.
ACT 16:30 Ɓǝ wur put kǝ mo a tool, kǝn nwur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Daa mo, an cin a miyi, kǝ nghan kat ɓam ɗi yi?>>
ACT 16:31 Mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<A shinzeen nDaa Jesu. Ɓǝ gha mbǝ nkat ɓam, waa kǝ nenlu fwaa mo jir.>>
ACT 16:32 Mo satpwoo Naan nwur ashak kǝ nenlu fin mo jir.
ACT 16:33 Ɓǝ mparmǝnǝ, wur vwang láa mo mo. Yaksǝ abet-abet mo cìn baptisma nwur, ashak kǝ nenlu fin mo jir.
ACT 16:34 Wur jì kǝ mo ntul fin, kǝn nwur shin mbiise mmo. Pǝtuup wur nǝ gam kǝ retnyit ɗes hakyeng, mbǝɗe wur ashak kǝ nenlu fin mo jir, mo shinzeen nDaa Naan.
ACT 16:35 Ɓǝ kaaɗe ɓitmang, ɓǝ nenɗyeel nǝ mo lep jepkam mo, mbǝkǝ mmo sat ɗi ngutap nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ mo nǝnee, <<A ɓwet des ɗevǝl sǝ mo.>>
ACT 16:36 Yaksǝ ngutap nen ɗe mo a shishoot nǝ sat mPool nǝnee, <<Nenɗyeel mo lep-lep nǝ, mun ɓwet gha kǝ Silas, mbǝkǝ nwun seet mbuu ɗi. Mbǝ mǝnǝ wu put yaksǝ, kǝn nwun seet ɗi ryang.>>
ACT 16:37 Ɗang Pool sat njepkám nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Doo mo kǝ nǝrem mun agaak, ɓǝ baa mo kǝ tokɗyeel mmun, mbǝkǝ mmo man ɗi nǝ kyet muu cin mee mbii ɗebish ɗi kas. Mun ɗe mun a nnen Rom mo. Kǝzak doon mo dǝm shoot mun nlushoot zak. Ɗangɓǝ yaksǝ, ɓǝ moo reɓet ceen mun a sǝsok aa? Dǝm wu sat mo jì pwat kǝ mun shikáa fur.>>
ACT 16:38 Aasǝ ɓǝ, jepkam nǝ mo baa, ɓǝ mo satpwoo ɗe Pool sat nnentokɗyeel nǝ mo. Kaaɗe nentokɗyeel nǝ mo kǝlǝng nǝ, Pool kǝ Silas mo a nnen Rom mo, ɓǝ kǝǝrmuut yaa mo.
ACT 16:39 Ɓǝ nentokɗyeel nǝ mo jì ɗang pǝ Pool kǝ Silas, mbǝkǝ mmo fwoo ɗi mmo. Yaksǝ mo tap put kǝ mo nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ, ɗangɓǝ mo sat mPool kǝ Silas kǝ mmo yit pee nkaam nǝ.
ACT 16:40 Aɓwoon ɗe Pool kǝ Silas mo kǝ pwat nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ, ɓǝ mo dǝm ntul Lidiya. A pee ɗe mo kat nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗe, ɓǝ mo leshap mǝ caa pǝtuup ngurum nǝ mo, ɗang mo yool yit pee nkaam mǝnǝ ɗi.
ACT 17:1 Pool kǝ Silas mo yaa ar dǝm put Amfipolis kǝ Apoloniya, ɓǝ mo jì wul nTasoloni, a pee ɗe lu Naan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo ɗi.
ACT 17:2 Ɓǝ Pool ɗel nLu Naan, kaaɗe wur loot kǝ cìn nǝ sǝ. Mbǝ puus Nookɗi mo yitkun, ɓǝ Pool nkaa ɓeetpwoo kǝ gurum nǝ mo nɗǝǝn pwoo Naan.
ACT 17:3 Wur nkaa kámshii mǝ pwoo Naan nǝ mmo, ɗe mo naa nǝ ɗee agaak nǝ, nǝ a tǝng kǝn Kristi shwaajeel, ɗang wur nyool a peemúut zak. Wur sat zak nǝnee, <<Jesu ɗe an kǝn satpwoo nwun nkaa wur sǝ, a wur a Kristi.>>
ACT 17:4 Pak nnen Yahudi nǝ mo shinzeen mpwoo ɗe Pool sat ɓǝ, nǝ le mmo seet nɗang Pool kǝ Silas. Aasǝ zak, ɓǝ nnen Heleni mo ɗes ɗe mo kǝ kǝǝr Naan, mo shinzeen ashak kǝ pak shurep ɗǝnan-nan mo.
ACT 17:5 Ɗangɓe nnen Yahudi mo gam kǝ zuur, mbǝɗe gurum mo ɗes mo dǝm nɗang kám mǝ Pool kǝ Silas, ɓǝ mo dǝm pǝrep pak nen ɗebish mo, kǝ jepkut ɗe mo kǝ tong mpwoo lutuk mo, mo kuur mo ashak. Yaksǝ mo yool kǝ or kǝ pwoo ɗebuu koo mo tǝttar sǝ nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ. Ɓǝ mo shwe dǝm ntul Jesen, mo nkaa yap Pool kǝ Silas, mbǝkǝ mmo put ɗi kǝ mo pǝ ɗuu mǝ gurum nǝ mo.
ACT 17:6 Ɗang kaaɗe baa mo kat mo kas, ɓǝ mo fee Jesen, kǝ pak nenseet nɗang Jesu mo pwat, ɓǝ mo jì kǝ mo ntoom nen ɗǝnan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo. Mo nkaa le or nǝnee, <<Nen ɗesǝ mo, ɗe mo kǝ ciir kǝ yil nǝ shikáa atuum, mo jì mpee ɗesǝ zak.
ACT 17:7 Nǝ le Jesen lap mo le ntul fin! Moo tep a Wàar mǝ Siza, mbǝɗe mon nkaa sat nǝ, mee mishkoom ɗi, ɗe mo kǝ pet wur a Jesu.>>
ACT 17:8 Kaaɗe gurum nǝ mo kǝ nen ɗǝnan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ daampee mmo, ɓǝ tuup tu mo zam.
ACT 17:9 Yaksǝ nen ɗǝnan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo le Jesen kǝ pak nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo kwat shool ɓwet, akuɗang mo ɓwet mo.
ACT 17:10 Kaaɗe par cìn, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo sat mPool kǝ Silas, kǝn mmo dǝm nyil mBeriya. Kaaɗe mo dǝm wul mBeriya, ɓǝ mo ɗel nɗǝǝn lu Naan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo.
ACT 17:11 Nen Yahudi ɗe mon mBeriya, mo kǝ ɗyen met nnen Yahudi ɗe mon nTasoloni, mbǝɗe mo kǝlǝngkar nǝ shi pǝtuup mǝndong rǝret, ɗang mo nkaa bǝlǝp pwoo Naan, shidaar shidaar mbǝkǝ mmo naa ɗi nǝ, kyet pwoo ɗe Pool sat mo azeen aa?
ACT 17:12 Nen Yahudi mo ɗes mo shinzeen, kǝ pak nnen Heleni mo ɗes mo shinzeen, daas mo kǝ pak shurep ɗǝnan-nan mo zak.
ACT 17:13 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe nnen Yahudi ɗe mon nTasoloni, mo kǝlǝng nǝ, Pool nkaa sat pwoo Naan nɗǝǝn yil mBeriya. Yaksǝ mo dǝm kar ɗuu mǝ gurum ɗe mon nyil mBeriya nǝ, mbǝkǝ mmo yool kǝ lek nkaa Pool kǝ Silas zak.
ACT 17:14 Abet, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo lep Pool dǝm mpwoo Am kuur ɗang Silas kǝ Timoti mo pan yém ɗi nyil mBeriya nǝ.
ACT 17:15 Nen ɗe mo dǝm ɓwet Pool, mo seet ndangshak kǝ wur ɓǝ mo dǝm wul Atens. Ɓǝ mo baa nyil mBeriya ashak kǝ lep mǝ Pool pǝ Silas kǝ Timoti nǝ, mo dǝm kat ɗyin kǝkǝlak.
ACT 17:16 Kaaɗe Pool nkaa ɗarnaa jì Timoti mpee nkaam Atens nǝ, ɓǝ nǝ daampee nwur zam, mbǝɗe wur naa pee nkaam nǝ gam kǝ kùm mo koo a pee ɗǝɗangyi.
ACT 17:17 Yaksǝ Pool bǝlǝp shii pwoo Naan nǝ ashak kǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nnen Heleni ɗe mo kǝ seyil nNaan, nɗǝǝn lu Naan mǝ nnen Yahudi nǝ mo, kǝ wur satpwoo Naan nɗes gurum ɗe mo kǝ jì nɗǝǝn lutuk zak.
ACT 17:18 Yaksǝ pak nnen Ipikuriyan mo, kǝ nnen Stoyik mo, des ɗesǝ mo a nenman mo. Mo kaat kǝ Pool, ɓǝ mo ɗoom ɓeetshik kǝ wur. Yaksǝ pak mo sat nǝnee, <<Ngulupwoo buu koo mwen sǝ, kǝ reɓet sat a miyi?>> Ɗang pak mo sat nǝnee, <<Muu kǝlǝng koo wur leshap a nkaa mee Naan ɗecì mo sǝ.>> Mo leshap ɗesǝ, a mbǝɗe Pool nkaa satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Jesu, kǝ yool a peemúut zak.
ACT 17:19 Mo yaa Pool, ɓǝ mo kàa kǝ wur a peekuur ɗe mo kǝ pet a Ariyopagus, ɓǝ mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Muu reɓet manshii mǝ kám ɗepwoo ɗe gha nkaa leshap nkaa nǝ sǝ.
ACT 17:20 Mbǝɗǝ pak mbii ɗe waa a sat nǝ mo a ɗepwoo pǝ mun ɗi, kǝzak muu reɓet manshii mo nǝ.>>
ACT 17:21 (Nen pee nkaam Atens mo jir, kǝ mǝzep ɗe mo jì tong ɗi, mo kǝ fes reɓet kǝlǝng, kǝ leshap nkaa mbii ɗepwoo mo, ɓǝ mo le nǝ ɗee a koo ɗak sǝ.)
ACT 17:22 Pool yool ɗar a peekuur ɗe moo pet a Ariyopagus nǝ, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun nnen Atens mo! An pǝ naa wun a nen ɗe wuu seyil nnaan mo ɗes hakyeng.
ACT 17:23 Mbǝɗǝ kaaɗe an pǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn pee nkaam fuu nǝ, ɓǝ an pǝ naa mbii ɗe wuu seyil mmo shini-shinǝ. Nǝ le nghan kat mee peewus mbiizuum, ɗe mo ran-ran nkaa nǝ nǝnee, <Mbǝ Naan ɗe baa mu man wur kas.> Naan ɗe baa wu man wur kas, ɗe wuu seyil nwur sǝ, an pǝ kǝn leshap nwun a nkaa wur.
ACT 17:24 <<Naan ɗewur leyil ɗesǝ, kǝ mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir. Wur a Daa mǝ ɗeng kǝ yil ɗesǝ, kǝ baa wur kǝ tong a nɗǝǝn lu ɗe gurum mo ɗyik shi sar mbǝ seyil nwur kas.
ACT 17:25 Baa wur kǝ yap mee ɓam pǝ gurum kas koo dǝɓen, mbǝɗe a wur shikáa fin, kǝ shin seen kǝ nook ngurum mo, kǝ mbii mo jir zak.
ACT 17:26 A nɗǝǝn gurum mǝndong, ɓǝ Naan le peeput mǝ gurum ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ mo shini-shinǝ jir. Wur le kǝ mmo tong nkaa yil nǝ jir. Wur kǝ tap le ɓit nǝ mo, kǝ peekaat mǝ yil fur nǝ mo shini-shinǝ zak.
ACT 17:27 Naan cìn kǝsǝ, a mbǝkǝ ngurum mo yap wur ɗi, meeɓe, mon nyap wur kat, mbǝɗe baa wur jong kǝ mun gurum kas.
ACT 17:28 A mbǝ ɗeɓal mǝ Naan, ɓǝ muu kat seen, kǝ muu mwaan, ɗang mun ɗe zak. Kaaɗe pak nenkook fuu mo kǝ sat sǝ nǝnee, <Mun zak, a jep wur mo.>
ACT 17:29 Kaaɗe mun a jep mǝ Naan mo sǝ, ɓǝ baa nǝ ret kǝ mmun pan nǝ, mǝse mǝ Naan nǝ a koo mbii ɗe gurum mo kǝ ɗak a shi zinariya, koo azurfa, koo ngǝk, koo mee mbii ɗe gurum mo am shi seen fur kas.
ACT 17:30 Gyet yam-yam ɓǝ baa Naan leɗyeen nkaa mwen mǝ gurum nǝ mo kas, ɗang yaksǝ, ɓǝ wur kǝ sat ngurum mo tuwap jir, koo a nɗǝǝn yil ɗǝɗang yi.
ACT 17:31 Mbǝɗǝ Naan lepuus ɗewur mbǝ tokɗyeel ngurum ɗe nɗǝǝn nyil nǝ jir, shi gwar ɗewur kǝ ten bǝlǝp. Naan wur kǝ woo langtǝng mǝnǝ ngurum mo agaak jir, mbǝɗe wur kǝ yool kǝ gwar mǝnǝ a peemúut.>>
ACT 17:32 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng Pool leshap nkaa yool a peemúut, ɓǝ pak mo shwar wur shi shwar mǝ ɓákpee, ɗang pak mo nǝnee. Muu reɓet kǝn nghan cin a leshap ɗi nkaa mbii ɗesǝ zak.
ACT 17:33 Aasǝ ɓǝ Pool yool yit peekuur nǝ ɗi.
ACT 17:34 Pak gurum nǝ mo seet nɗang wur, ɓǝ mo shinzeen. Mɓut nnen ɗe mo shinzeen nǝ, a Diyonisiyus ɗewur a memee mɓut nennan mǝ peekuur ɗe mo kǝ pet nǝ a Ariyopagus, kǝ mee mat ɗe moo petsǝm war a Damaris, kǝ pak gurum mo.
ACT 18:1 Aɓwoon ɗesǝ, ɓǝ Pool yool yit Atens, ɓǝ wur dǝm nKoronti.
ACT 18:2 Ɓe wur kat mee ngu Yahudi, ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Akila, ɗe mo làa wur a mPontus. Wur kǝ mat fin Priskila mo yool a Itali mo jì nKoronti nǝ. Mbǝɗe mishkoom Klodiyus sat nǝ, nen Yahudi mo jir, mo yool aku nRom. Pool dǝm pǝ mo ɗi.
ACT 18:3 Ɓe wur tong pǝ mo ɗi, mbǝɗe wur a nguɗak Tent koo mo sǝ, ɗang mo cìn ɗak fur ashak zak.
ACT 18:4 Koo a parpuus Nookɗi ɗeɗangyii, ɓǝ Pool kǝ naa mɓeetshik kǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen Heleni mo mbǝkǝ mo shinzeen ɗi.
ACT 18:5 Kaaɗe Silas kǝ Timoti mo tong mMasidoniya jì wul, ɓǝ Pool fes lekáa fin kyap, mbǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ, ɗang wur ɗee a langtǝng nen Yahudi mo nǝ, Jesu a Kristi.
ACT 18:6 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe nen Yahudi mo ciipwoo nǝ, kǝzak mo leshap ɗebuu nwur, ɓǝ wur ciir kǝɓwoon mmo, ɓǝ wur sat mmo kǝ tuup nǝnee, <<Katɗang wu murep nɗǝǝn shikbish fuu mo, ɓǝ a wun wu lesuk. Baa mee sar fen ɗiɓut kas. Yool nyaksǝ, ɓǝ an mbǝ dǝm a pǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas.>>
ACT 18:7 Wur yool yit lu Naan mǝ nen Yahudi nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur dǝm ɗel ntul mee gwar ɗe mo kǝ petsǝm wur a Titus Jastus. Wur a mee nguseyil nNaan, ɗe lu wur nǝ kus kǝ lu Naan nǝ.
ACT 18:8 Krispus ngwe ɗeɗes nlu Naan nǝ, shinzeen nDaa ashak kǝ nenlu wur mo jir. Kǝzak gurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn nen Koronti mo, ɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo Pool nǝ, ɓǝ mo shinzeen, yaksǝ mo cìn baptisma mmo zak.
ACT 18:9 Parmeeci sǝ mpar, ɓǝ Daa leshap kǝ Pool nɗǝǝn suun nǝnee, <<Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa gha kas, a satpwoo nǝ, kǝzak taji a nook sat nǝ kas.
ACT 18:10 Mbǝɗǝ an ɗi ashak kǝ gha. Baa mee gurum mmak cìn mee mbii nghan kas. Mbǝɗǝ an ɗi kǝ gurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn pee nkaam ɗesǝ nǝ.>>
ACT 18:11 Aasǝ ɓǝ, Pool tong nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nKoronti, mbǝ ɓit mǝndong kǝ koor, wur nkaa kámpwoo Naan ngurum mo.
ACT 18:12 Ɗangɓǝ nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗe moo le Galiyo a gofna mǝ yil Akaya, ɓǝ nnen Yahudi mo ɓalkaa ashak, ɓǝ mo yaa Pool dǝm kǝ wur pǝ nentokɗyeel mo ɗi.
ACT 18:13 Mo sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur nkaa pǝring kǝ pan mǝ gurum mo, mbǝkǝ mmo seyil ɗi nNaan nɗǝǝn ar ɗe baa nǝ nciit kǝ Wàar nǝ kas.>>
ACT 18:14 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe Pool ɗoom leshap, ɓǝ Galiyo ɗewur a gofna, sat nnen Yahudi nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Wun nnen Yahudi mo! Katɗang ɓǝ ɗe gwar ɗe ɗesǝ wur cìn a mee mbii ɗebish, kǝ koo ɗewur wat a mee mbii, ɓǝ yoo an mmak lekom kǝn nghan nkǝlǝng wun ɗi.
ACT 18:15 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe nǝ a ɓeetshik nkaa pak pwoo mo, kǝ sǝmpwoo, kǝ Wàar fuu mo, ɓǝ wu dǝm wu ɓeet mǝnǝ mbuu shikáa fuu. Baa an mbǝ reɓet ɗee a ngutokɗyeel mǝ mbii koo mǝnǝ mo sǝ kas.>>
ACT 18:16 Yaksǝ wur ceen mo shin pwat aku nɗǝǝn luɗyeel nǝ.
ACT 18:17 Mo jir mo yaa Sostenis, ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa lu Naan nǝ, ɓǝ mo nǝrem wur mpwoo luɗyeel nǝ, ɗang baa Galiyo lekáa ɗyikye kas.
ACT 18:18 Pool waa cin tong ɗi nKoronti nǝ ɗes ashak kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo. Ɓǝ wur yool yit mo, ɓǝ wur ɗel nɗǝǝn tii mbǝ dǝm nyil nSiriya, ashak kǝ Priskila kǝ mish war Akila. Akuɗang Pool yool seet, ɓǝ wur sak káa fin nSenkiriya, mbǝkǝ nwur gampwoo ɗewur kǝ ten cweer nǝn nNaan nkaa shin fin.
ACT 18:19 Mo jì wul nɗǝǝn yil Afisus ɓǝ Pool yit Priskila kǝ Akila mpee mǝnǝ. Yaksǝ wur dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn lu Naan, kǝ wur yakshii mǝ pwoo mo ashak kǝ nnen Yahudi mo.
ACT 18:20 Kaaɗe mo ɗang pǝ wur kǝ nwur pan yém ɗe pǝ mo, ɓǝ wur cíi.
ACT 18:21 Ɗangɓe kaaɗe wur yool yit mo, ɓǝ wur cweerpwoo mmo nǝnee, <<Katɗang Naan reɓet, ɓǝ an mbǝ baajì pǝ wun ɗi.>> Aasǝ ɓǝ, wur ɗel nɗǝǝn tii dǝm nAfisus.
ACT 18:22 Kaaɗe wur dǝm wul nSizariya, ɓǝ wur kàa nJerusalem, kǝ nwur tok ɗi kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm Antiyok.
ACT 18:23 Aɓwoon ɗewur pan cìn rep teer mo ɗe, ɓǝ wur yool dǝm shipee-shipee, ngaar yil nGalati, kǝ Firijiya, wur nkaa gangkwak mputuup nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo jir.
ACT 18:24 Mee ngu Yahudi ɗe moo petsǝm wur a Apolos, ɗe mo làa wur a nAlekzandriya, ɓe wur ji Afisus. Wur a mee nguman, ɗang wur man ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Naan ɗes hakyeng.
ACT 18:25 Mo kǝ kám ar ɗe nǝ a mǝ Daa nwur, ɗang wur ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn nǝ. Wur leshap, ɗang wur kám ngurum mo nkaa Daa Jesu ndǝre-ndǝre, ɗang jir kǝsǝ, ɓe wur man a baptisma mǝ Joon ɓejee ɗak.
ACT 18:26 Wur ɗoom kop pwoo Naan agaak, baa ashak kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas, nɗǝǝn lu Naan nǝ. Kaaɗe Priskila kǝ Akila mo kǝlǝng wur, ɓǝ mo pet wur dǝm kǝ nǝ ntul fur, kǝn mmo sǝǝt kám ar mǝ Naan ɗi nwur ndǝre-ndǝre.
ACT 18:27 Apolos yool mbǝ dǝm Akaya, ɓe nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon Afisus mo ɓam wur, shi ran lep a rǝran shin nwur pán nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon nyil Akaya, mbǝkǝ mmo kaat wur ɗi, katɗang wur dǝm wul. Kaaɗe wur dǝm wul, ɓǝ wur ɓam nnen ɗe mo kǝ shinzeen mbǝ ɗeret mǝ Daa zam.
ACT 18:28 Wur gan nnen Yahudi mo ntoom kǝ gurum mo, mbǝ ɓeetshik, kǝzak wur kám ngurum mo agaak, wur nkaa leshap mmo nkaa mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pwoo Naan nǝnee, <<Jesu wur a Kristi azeen-zeen.>>
ACT 19:1 Kaaɗe Apolos ɗi nɗǝǝn Koronti, ɓǝ Pool nkaa mwaan nɗǝǝn yil mo, ɓǝ wur jì wul Afisus. Yaksǝ wur jì kat pak nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗi mpee nkaam mǝnǝ.
ACT 19:2 Ɓǝ wur tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Kaaɗe dǝ wu shinzeen, ɓǝ wuu lap Riin Ɗeɓang ee?>> Mo lap nwur nǝnee, <<Hai, baa muu cam kǝlǝng mee pwoo nkaa Riin Ɗeɓang kas.>>
ACT 19:3 Wur tal pǝ mo nǝnee, <<Ɓǝ dǝ mo cìn a baptisma ɗǝɗang nwun yii?>> Mo lap nǝnee, <<A baptisma mǝ Joon.>>
ACT 19:4 Pool sat mmo nǝnee, <<Baptisma mǝ Joon nǝ a mbǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ tuwap. Gyet Joon sat nnen Yahudi mo shinzeen a ngwe ɗewur mbǝ jì mɓwoon fin. A Jesu mmǝnǝ.>>
ACT 19:5 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗesǝ, ɓǝ mo cìn baptisma mmo nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa Jesu.
ACT 19:6 Pool lesar fin nkaa mo, ɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang sham nkaa mo, ɓǝ mo leshap shi liispwoo ɗecì mo, ɗang mo satpwoo Naan ngurum mo.
ACT 19:7 Nen ɗe mo lap baptisma nǝ, mo wul kaapaat baavǝl.
ACT 19:8 Pool wur ɗel nɗǝǝn lu Naan, mbǝ tar mo kun, ɓǝ wur leshap nǝ, baa ashak kǝ kǝǝrmuut kas, kǝzak wur cìn ɓeetshik kǝ mo, ɗang wur ɗaar mbǝkǝ nwur kám ɗe mmo agaak nkaa mulki mǝ Naan.
ACT 19:9 Ɗangɓǝ pak mo cǝǝr ɓal mputuup, kǝ mmo cii shinzeen, ɓǝ mo leshap ɗebuu nkaa pwoo mǝ Naan ntoom gurum mo jir. Aasǝ ɓǝ, Pool yit mo ɗe, ɓǝ wur pǝrep nen shinzeen nǝ mo shin jì ashak. Ɓǝ koo a puus ɗeɗangyii, ɓǝ wur yakshii kǝ pwoo mo nɗǝǝn lu kam-kam ɗe mǝ Tairanus.
ACT 19:10 Moo naa ncìn a kǝsǝ dǝm wul mbǝ ɓit vǝl. Aasǝ ɓǝ, nen ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn yil Eshiya, nen Yahudi mo, kǝ nnen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, mo jir mo kǝlǝng pwoo kǝ Naan.
ACT 19:11 Naan le kǝ Pool cìn mbii lukshik mo ɗes, ɗe baa mo kǝ cam naa mo kas.
ACT 19:12 Nǝ le har mmo lap lee ɗewur kǝ pwes wun ɗishik, kǝ nlǝr ɗewur kǝ lep mo, kǝ mo dǝm tung nengok mo ɗishik, ɓǝ mo kat bar nɗǝǝn shwal mo mo shini-shini, kǝzak riin ɗebish mo pwat mɓut ngurum mo ɗes zak.
ACT 19:13 Ɗangɓǝ mee des mo ɗi mɓut nnen Yahudi mo, ɗe moo mwaan dǝm shiyil-shiyil, kǝn mmo kǝ ceen riin ɗebish mo ɗi. Mo ɗoom leshap nnen ɗe mo kǝ riin ɗebish mo nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu, ɓǝ mo sat nǝnee, <<Nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Jesu ɗe Pool kǝ leshap nkaa wur sǝ, ɓǝ an nsat ngha, a put aku.>>
ACT 19:14 Mee ɗyemnǝǝnshak mo ɗi pwoovǝl, ɗe mo a jep mee pris ɗeɗes mǝ nnen Yahudi mo, ɗi sǝm wur a Skiiva. A mo a nnen cìn mǝnǝ.
ACT 19:15 Riin ɗebish nǝ lap mmo nǝnee, <<Wen man Jesu, kǝ wen mman Pool zak, ɗang wun a wii mo yii?>>
ACT 19:16 Ɓǝ gwar ɗewur kǝ riin ɗebish nǝ, wur yool met nkaa mo, ɓǝ wur met mmo mɓal jir mo. Wur nas mo, ɗang wur le láa mmo, ɓǝ wur yilang nlǝr mmo, ɓǝ mo yool shwe pwat nɗǝǝn lu nǝ ngúm, ɓǝ toom kǝ sham mmo.
ACT 19:17 Kaaɗe mbii ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗemǝman pǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nnen Heleni mo ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn yil Afisus, ɓǝ kǝǝrmuut yaa mo jir, ɓǝ gurum mo le ɗeɗes nsǝm kǝ Daa Jesu.
ACT 19:18 Gurum mo ɗes mɓut nnen ɗe mo shinzeen, mo jì woo shikbish mo mo, kǝ ɗak mo ɗebish mo agaak zak.
ACT 19:19 Pak gurum mo ɗes mɓut nnen ɗe moo cìn yen ɗebish mǝ gwampee mo, mo kok ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ yen mo nǝ mo, kǝn mmo jì fwoo mo nwus ntoom gurum nǝ mo jir. Kaaɗe mo tang shool mǝ ɓǝǝt-haal ɗe mo fwo nwus nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo kat shool azurfa mo wul ngal laarpaat.
ACT 19:20 Aasǝ ɓǝ, pwoo mǝ Daa nǝ mwaan shipee-shipee jir, nǝ le nǝ ɓal hakyeng.
ACT 19:21 Aɓwoon ɗe mbii ɗesǝ mo kǝ cìn, ɓǝ Pool naa nǝ ret nǝ, kǝ nɗyin dǝm nJerusalem, ɓǝ ɗyin mbǝ yaa ar nǝ dǝm put a mMasidoniya kǝ Akaya. Ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Aɓwoon ɗe an ndǝm wul nJerusalem, ɓǝ nǝ atǝng an mbǝ ndǝm nyil nRom zak.>>
ACT 19:22 Pool lep Timoti kǝ Erastus ɗe mo a nenɓam wur mo, kǝ mmo dǝm mMasidoniya akyeen wur, ɗang wur shikáa fin, wur mpan yém ɗi lee nɗǝǝn yil Eshiya nǝ.
ACT 19:23 Nciit kǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ gurum mo yool kǝ pwoo ɗebish ɗe nǝ daampee zam nkaa pwoo Naan nǝ.
ACT 19:24 Mee ngukǝlem, ɗewur kǝ ɗak mbii mo shi azurfa, ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Demetriyus. Wur naa nkǝlem pak jep kùm mo, shi azurfa ɗe mo lapshak kǝ war kùm Atemis ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓǝ ɗak ɗesǝ nii jì kǝ shool nnenkǝlem nǝ mo zam.
ACT 19:25 Demetriyus pǝrep nenkǝlem nǝ mo jì ashak jir, kǝ nen ɗe ɗak mo nǝ mo, a koo mǝ nenkǝlem nǝ mo sǝ zak. Yaksǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Daa mo! Wu man nǝ, mmun muu kat shool ɗes a nɗǝǝn ɗak fun ɗesǝ.
ACT 19:26 Yaksǝ wun shikáa fuu, ɓǝ wu naa, kǝ wuu kǝlǝng mbii ɗe gwar ɗe moo pet wur a Pool sǝ wur kǝ cìn. Wur sat nǝ, naan ɗe gurum mo kǝ ɗak mo a shi sar, ɓǝ baa mo a naan kas koo lee lee, ɗang wur ciir kǝ pǝtuup gurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn pee nkaam Afisus, kǝ yil ɗe mo ngaar Eshiya jir. Nǝ, taji mo seet kùm nǝ mo kas.
ACT 19:27 Wu naa zak, yaksǝ baa ɗak fun nǝ kutɗi kǝ mee sǝm ɗeret kas. Baa a ɗak fun nǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, kǝ Atemis ɗeɗes, war mbǝ ɗee a mbii shwar ngurum mo, kǝ naan nǝ war shikáa fer zak. Gurum ɗe mo ngaar yil Eshiya, kǝ yil sǝ jir, mo kǝ seyil a nwar.>>
ACT 19:28 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nǝ láa mmo mɓut zam, mo le or pwoo mǝndong, mo sat nǝnee, <<Atemis mǝ Afisus war a ɗeɗes!>>
ACT 19:29 Gurum ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ, mo jir mo lap or nǝ zak. Gurum nǝ mo dǝm yaa Gayus kǝ Aristakus ɗe mo a nen Masidoniya mo, kǝ ɗe mo a shaar mwaan mǝ Pool, ɓǝ mo dǝm kǝ mo kǝkǝlak a peekuur.
ACT 19:30 Pool reɓet dǝm ɗar akyeen gurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo cíi nwur.
ACT 19:31 Pak nen ɗenan-nan ɗe nyil Eshiya mo, ɗe mo a shaar Pool. Mo lep shindǝm nwur nǝ, taji wur dǝm ɗi a peekuur nǝ kas.
ACT 19:32 Gurum nǝ mo le or a peekuur nǝ jir, mon nkaa sat mbii mo shini-shini, mbǝɗe ɗes mǝ gurum nǝ mo, baa mo man mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝ mo kuur ashak kas.
ACT 19:33 Nen Yahudi mo le kǝn Alekzanda dǝm ɗar akyeen mǝ gurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur ɗiyeep sar, mbǝkǝ ngurum nǝ mo ɗok ɗi tǝtǝk, mbǝɗe wur kǝ reɓet leshap ngurum nǝ mo nǝ, baa ɗyin kǝ nen fin mo, ɗuu cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas. Mbǝɗǝ kaaɗe gurum nǝ mo naa Alekzanda kǝ ɗar akyeen, ɓǝ mo pan nǝ, a wur kǝ mbii nǝ.
ACT 19:34 Kǝzak kaaɗe mo naa nǝ, wur a ngu Yahudi, ɓǝ mo sǝǝt le or pwoo mǝndong jir, mbǝ awa vǝl. Mo nkaa sat nǝnee, <<Atemis, kǝ nǝ Afisus mo, war a ɗeɗes!>>
ACT 19:35 Kaaɗe nguran mǝ pee nkaam nǝ wur le kǝ ngurum mo ɗok tǝtǝk, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wun nen Afisus mo! A wii nook man nǝ, a wun a nnen ɗe wun pǝ tap kǝ lu kùm mǝ Atemis ɗeɗes nɗǝǝn Afisus kas yii? Kǝzak nghǝk ɗe gyet nǝ tong aɗeng sham taa mpee ɗesǝ kas yii?
ACT 19:36 Baa mee gurum mak cíipwoo mǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo kas. Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ nǝ ret kǝ nwun tong coot, taji wu cìn mee mbii kǝkǝlak kǝsǝ kas.
ACT 19:37 Wun wu jì kǝ nen ɗesǝ mo mpee ɗesǝ, ɓǝ baa mo kǝ cìn mee wat nɗǝǝn lu kùm fuu nǝ mo kas, kǝ baa mo sat mee pwoo ɗebish nkaa naan fuu ɗeɗes war kas zak.
ACT 19:38 Katɗang Demetriyus ashak kǝ nniyee fin mo, mo kǝ mee pwoo nkaa mee gurum, ɓǝ mo dǝm kǝ pwoo nǝ nluɗyeel mpee ɗe nenɗyeel mo ɗi, mbǝkǝ mmo ɓeetpwoo nǝ ɗi.
ACT 19:39 Ɗangɓǝ kat wun pǝ tang a mee mbii ɗecì, ɓǝ wu ɓeetpwoo mǝnǝ a peekuur kǝ nenyil nǝ mo.
ACT 19:40 Azeen-zeen mun mbǝ teer ɗiɓut katɗang mo dǝm kǝ mun nluɗyeel mbǝ or ɗǝ cicinsǝ, mbǝɗe baa mun manshii mǝ mbii ɗe wun pǝ ɗyeep or nkaa nǝ kas, kǝzak, baa kuur fuu nǝ kǝ mee koop nǝ kas.>>
ACT 19:41 Aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ leshap mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur sat ngurum nǝ mo dǝm ntul mo.
ACT 20:1 Aɓwoon ɗe or nǝ kyes, ɓǝ Pool pǝrep nenseet nɗang Jesu mo, ɓǝ wur leshap kǝ mo, mbǝ shínɓal mmo mputuup, ɓǝ wur sat ɗang mukaat mmo, ɓǝ wur yool dǝm mMasidoniya.
ACT 20:2 Wur mwaan dǝm ngaar nyil mǝnǝ mo jir, wur nkaa caa pǝtuup ngurum nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur jì wul nyil nGris.
ACT 20:3 A mpee ɗewur cìn tar kun ɗi. Nen Yahudi mo ɓalpwoo mo ashak nkaa wur, ɓǝ kaaɗe wur mbǝ ɗel nɗǝǝn tii mbǝ dǝm nyil nSiriya, ɓǝ wur waa yaa ar nǝ a mMasidoniya.
ACT 20:4 Ɓǝ Sopata làa Pires ngu Beriya, dǝm nɗang Pool kǝ Aristakus kǝ Sekundus, ɗe mo a nnen Tasoloni mo, kǝ Gayus ngu Debi, kǝ Timoti, kǝ Tikikus, kǝ Trofimus ɗe mo a nen Eshiya mo.
ACT 20:5 Nen ɗesǝ mo shee dǝm wul nTrowas mmun akyeen, kǝn mmo ɗar naa jì fun a mpee nkaam mǝnǝ.
ACT 20:6 Mun mu ɗel nɗǝǝn tii nFilipi, aɓwoon retnyit mǝ se gǝǝl aas ɗe baa nǝ kǝ yist kas. Ɓǝ nɗǝǝn teer mo paat, ɓǝ mu dǝm mu wul pǝ mo ɗe nTrowas nǝ. Mun cìn teer pwoovǝl ɗi mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 20:7 Parpuus ɗenshee mɓut nteer ɗepwoovǝl, ɓǝ mu kuur ashak mbǝ se Tong Ashak. Pool kǝ ɗak shin, mbǝkǝ daar wur yool mwaan ɗi, ɓǝ wur leshap ngurum mo. Wur naa a nleshap nǝ ɗak, dǝm wul nnaar mpar.
ACT 20:8 Mo lewus naapee mo ɗi ɗes nɗǝǝn luɗeng ɗe muu kuur ɗe nǝ.
ACT 20:9 Mee zǝlang ɗe mo kǝ pet sǝm wur a Yutikus kǝ tong mpwoo fung mǝ luɗeng nǝ, ɓǝ kaaɗe Pool naa an satpwoo Naan nǝ ɗak, ɓǝ saam ɗoom yaa Yutikus, ɓǝ saam nǝ jì met nwur mɓal, ɓǝ wur yool mpwoo fung mǝ luɗeng ɗekun nǝ, sham taa nyil, kaaɗe mo sham mang wur, ɓǝ mo kat wur kǝ muut.
ACT 20:10 Yaksǝ Pool sham zan shik fin nkaa kúm mǝ zǝlang nǝ, ɓǝ wur kup kúm nǝ, ɓǝ wur sat ngurum nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Taji nǝ daampee nwun kas, mbǝɗe wur ɗe kǝ seen.>>
ACT 20:11 Ɓǝ Pool baakàa ɗi nluɗeng nǝ, wur tep gǝǝl aas se. Aɓwoon ɗewur kǝ leshap kǝ mo har ɓit mang, ɓǝ wur yool seet.
ACT 20:12 Mo dǝm kǝ ɗyem zǝlang nǝn ntul kǝ seen, ɓǝ mo kat retnyit ɗes hakyeng.
ACT 20:13 Pool sat mmun nǝ, ɗyin pǝ reɓet dǝm Asos a nshii, mbǝmǝnǝ ɓǝ mun mu dǝm mu ɗel nɗǝǝn tii dǝm mu wul Asos nwur akyeen, a pee ɗe mu mang wur ɗi.
ACT 20:14 Kaaɗe wur jì kat mun Asos, ɓǝ mu mang wur nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, kǝ mu dǝm mMitilini.
ACT 20:15 Mu yool mMitilini nǝ, ɓǝ ɗaar nǝ mu dǝm mu wul kus kǝ yil nKiyos. Daar nǝ zak, ɓǝ mu jì mu wul ngaar Samos, kǝ daar nǝ zak, ɓǝ mu jì mMiletus.
ACT 20:16 Pool leɗyeen mbǝ ɗel dǝm Afisus nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, mbǝkǝ taji wur waa taa ɗee nɗǝǝn yil Eshiya kas, mbǝɗe wur reɓet wurung, mbǝkǝ kat nǝ mak cìn, ɓǝ wur wul ɗi nJerusalem parpuus Pentikos.
ACT 20:17 Kaaɗe Pool wul mMiletus, ɓǝ wur lep shindǝm nen ɗenan-nan mǝ Eklesiya ɗe Afisus mo, nǝ mo jì kat nɗyin ɗi.
ACT 20:18 Ɓǝ kaaɗe mo jì wul pǝ wur ɗi, ɓǝ wur leshap mmo nǝnee, <<Wun shikáa fuu, wu man tong fen nnaar fuu peedǝ ɗi an nshee jì ɗi ngaar nyil Eshiya.
ACT 20:19 Gyet ncìn ɗak mǝ Daa nǝ, baa a shi mee ɗiyeepkáa kas, kǝzak an kǝ shwaajeel ɗes mbǝ cìn ɗak nǝ shiɓit shiɓit, kǝ mbǝ gwak ɗe dǝ nen Yahudi mo ɓwet mbǝ an.
ACT 20:20 Wun shikáa fuu wu man zak nǝ, baa gyet nsak shii mbǝ sat mee mbii ɗe nǝ kǝkoop nwun pǝ wun ɗi kas. An mbǝ kámpwoo nkaa Jesu nwun jir agaak, kǝ an kǝ dǝm nkámpwoo nǝ nwun shilu-shilu zak.
ACT 20:21 Gyet wen kǝn sat zeen nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, ɓalɓal nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ mmo tuwap jir, kǝ mo jì pǝ Naan ɗi, kǝ mmon shinzeen ɗe nDaa fun Jesu Kristi zak.
ACT 20:22 Yaksǝ, wu naa an mbǝ dǝm nJerusalem, mbǝɗe a Riin Ɗeɓang lep an shindǝm, ɗang baa wen man mbii ɗe nǝn ndǝm kat an ɗi mpee mǝnǝ kas.
ACT 20:23 Ɗangɓǝ Riin Ɗeɓang kǝ kám nghan nǝ jir nɗǝǝn pee nkaam ɗeɗangyii, kǝ jeel pǝ ɗarnaa an, ɓǝ gurum mon yaa an shoot zak.
ACT 20:24 Baa wen lesen fen nǝ kǝ mee koop nǝ pǝ an ɗi kas, ɗang an kǝn reɓet kǝ nghan kyes a ɗak ɗe Daa Jesu kǝ shin nghan mbǝ cìn nǝ. Ɗak ɗewur shin nǝ nghan nɗesǝ, kǝ nghan leshap ɗeret ɗi ngurum mo nkaa zuum mǝ Naan.
ACT 20:25 <<Yaksǝ wen man nǝ, baa memee nɗǝǝn wun, ɗe gyet an kǝn mwaan nnaar fuu, mbǝ leshap nwun nkaa yil mishkoom mǝ Naan nǝ, wun baa wu naa an ɗi kas.
ACT 20:26 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, wen kǝn sat nwun cicinsǝ nǝ, katɗang ɓǝ memee fuu muut mɓut shikbish, ɓǝ sar fen mo paat.
ACT 20:27 Mbǝɗǝ baa gyet wen nsak shii mbǝ sat pan mǝ Naan mo jir nwun kas.
ACT 20:28 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, wun nen ɗe Riin mǝ Naan kǝ le a nennaa kuur mǝ tǝm nǝ mo jir, wu tap kǝ káa fuu mo rǝret, kǝn nwun kyeer Eklesiya mǝ Naan ɗewur kǝ seet nshin shi toom mǝ káa fin.
ACT 20:29 Wen man nǝ, aɓwoon ɗe wen kǝn seet, ɓǝ ncuwe ɗeɓyaal mo, mon njì ɗel nnaar fuu, ɓǝ baa mon nyit tǝm nǝ mo ɗe kas.
ACT 20:30 Pee nǝ pǝ jì, ɓǝ pak gurum mon nyool nnaar fuu, mo mbǝ sat pwoo ɗe mo a ɗung nkaa zeen nǝ, mbǝkǝ mmo dul nenseet nɗang Jesu mo dǝm ɗi nɗang mo.
ACT 20:31 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wu tong shi gongpee, taji wu munsuk kas nǝ, gyet mbǝ ɓit mo kun, ɓǝ baa wen nook leshap nǝ nwun mpar kǝ puus ɓalɓal, kǝ yitmwaa kas.
ACT 20:32 <<Yaksǝ, ɓǝ wen le wun nsar Naan, kǝ pwoo ɗeret wur ɗe nǝ kǝ ɓal mbǝ ɗyik wun, mbǝkǝ nǝ shin ɗeret mǝ Naan, ɗi wur kǝ nǝ mbǝ nnen wur mo jir nwun zak.
ACT 20:33 Baa wen kǝn coor mee azurfa, koo zinariya, koo nlǝr mǝ mee gurum kas.
ACT 20:34 Wun shikáa fuu wu man nǝ, a shi sar fen ɗesǝ mo, ɓǝ an kǝn cìn ɗak shi mo, mbǝ mbii ɗe an kǝn reɓet mo, kǝ mbǝ mbii ɗe nnen ɗe mo ashak kǝ an mo kǝ reɓet zak.
ACT 20:35 An kǝn nkám nwun nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir, nǝ, a shi ɗak mǝ káa fuu mo, ɗang wun ɓam nen ɗe baa mo katɓal kas, kaaɗe muu panpwoo ɗe Daa Jesu kǝ sat shikáa fin sǝ nǝnee, <Kat gurum shin mbii, ɓǝ wur nkat ɗeret met ngwe ɗewur lap nǝ.> >>
ACT 20:36 Aɓwoon ɗe Pool sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur kurum nkaa furum ashak kǝ mo jir, kǝn nwur ɗangnaan ɗi
ACT 20:37 Kaaɗe mo ɗoom sat ɗang mukaat mPool, ɓǝ mon nkaa wal, ɗang mo kǝ jì lesar nwur ntook, kǝ mo kǝ tung wur shi mishpwoo zak.
ACT 20:38 Mbii ɗe nǝ sǝǝt wàt pǝtuup mmo met jir, nǝ aapwoo ɗe Pool sat mmo nǝ, baa mon nkutɗi mbǝ naa yit fin kas. Mo dǝm ɓwet wur mpwoo tii.
ACT 21:1 Aɓwoon ɗe muu sat ɗang mukaat mmo, ɓǝ mu ɗel nɗǝǝn tii ɓǝ mu yaa ar wur-wur mu dǝm nyil nKos. Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mu dǝm mu wul nRodes. Mu yool mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu dǝm mPatara.
ACT 21:2 Kaaɗe mu kat mee tii ɗe nǝ mbǝ canɗel mFonisha, ɓǝ mu ɗel nɗǝǝn nǝ, ɓǝ mu yool.
ACT 21:3 Kaaɗe mu naa yil nSaiprus kǝ ɗee, ɓǝ mu yit nǝ nsarkul, mu ɗel mǝ dǝm akyeen nyil nSiriya. Mu dǝm mu sham mpee nkaam nTaya, mbǝɗe tii nǝn nsham kǝ lee mo a mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 21:4 Kaaɗe mu katpee ɗe pak nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗe, ɓǝ mo sat mPool nǝ, taji wur dǝm nJerusalem kas.
ACT 21:5 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe puus seet fun nǝ jì wul, ɓǝ mu yool mǝ sekyeen kǝ mwaan fun. Ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo ashak kǝ shurep fur mo, kǝ jep fur mo, mo dǝm nɗang mun mɓwoon pee nkaam nǝ, a pee ɗe mǝ kurum nkaa furum mbǝ ɗangnaan ɗi ashak kǝ mo mpwoo am kuur nǝ.
ACT 21:6 Aɓwoon ɗe mu sat ɗang mukaat nshak, ɓǝ mmun mu ɗel nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, ɓǝ mo baa ntul.
ACT 21:7 Yaksǝ mmun mu sekyeen kǝ mwaan fun. Mu yool nTaya, ɓǝ mu jì mǝ wul mPolemayas. Ɓǝ mu dǝm mu tok kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu tong ashak kǝ mo, mu teer mǝndong.
ACT 21:8 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mu yool, mu dǝm mu wul nSizariya, ɓǝ mu tong ntul Filip ngusat pwoo Naan ɗewur a memee mɓut nnen ɗepwoovǝl sǝ mo, ɗe gyet mo bǝlǝp mo nJerusalem.
ACT 21:9 Filip kǝ jiraap mo feer, ɗe baa mo kǝ yool ɗyik kas. Jiraap ɗesǝ nǝ mo kǝ leshap nkaa mbii ɗe nǝ mbǝ jì.
ACT 21:10 Kaaɗe mu pan mu yém ɗe, mbǝ meeteer mo ruk, ɓǝ mee ngusatpwoo mǝ Naan ɗi sǝm wur a Agabus, wur kǝ tong nJudiya jì ɗi.
ACT 21:11 Kaaɗe wur jì pǝ mun ɗi, ɓǝ wur mang zaal ɗe Pool kǝ ɗyiin mɓwoon, ɓǝ wur ɓwoot sar kǝ shii fin mo ɗishik. Ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Riin Ɗeɓang sat nǝ, nnen Yahudi ɗe mon nJerusalem, mon ndǝm ɓwoot ngu zaal ɗesǝ nǝ a kǝsǝ zak, kǝn mmo shin wur nsar mǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas.>>
ACT 21:12 Kaaɗe mu kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mmun kǝ koor nǝ mo, mu ɗang pǝ Pool mbǝkǝ taji wur dǝm nJerusalem kas.
ACT 21:13 Ɗangɓǝ Pool lap nǝnee, <<A mii le ɗang wun pǝ wal, kǝn nwun wàt pǝtuup fen ɗi yii? Yaksǝ wen kǝn ɗak sen, baa a mbǝkǝ mmo ɓuɓwoot an ɗi ɓejee ɗak kas, koo a mbǝkǝ nghan muut ɗi nɗǝǝn yil nJerusalem zak, mbǝ sǝm mǝ Daa Jesu.>>
ACT 21:14 Kaaɗe baa mu mak daam wur kas, ɓǝ mu nook, ɗang mu sat nǝnee, <<Ɗee a mbii ɗe Daa Naan naa kǝ gha ɗak.>>
ACT 21:15 Aɓwoon rep meeteer mo, ɓǝ mu ɓwoot lee fun mo, kǝ mmun kàa ɗi nJerusalem.
ACT 21:16 Pak nen Jesu ɗe mon nSizariya mo jì nɗang mun, ɗe mo jì wul kǝ mun ntul Mason, a mpee ɗe mǝ tong ɗi. Wur a ngu Saiprus, ɗang wur a memee mɓut nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗenshee mo.
ACT 21:17 Kaaɗe mu jì mu wul nJerusalem, ɓǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo kaat mun shi retnyit.
ACT 21:18 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ Pool dǝm kǝ mun pǝ Jemis ɗi, a pee ɗe nennan mǝ Eklesiya mo ɗe ashak jir.
ACT 21:19 Aɓwoon ɗe Pool kǝ tok kǝ mo, ɓǝ wur yaa yakshii nǝ mmo ɓang-ɓang, mbii ɗe Naan le kǝn nwur cìn mo nɗǝǝn nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas.
ACT 21:20 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mbii mǝnǝ mo, ɓǝ mo kwoop Naan hakyeng. Ɓǝ mo sat mPool nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnǝǝn fun, a naa nnen Yahudi mo ɗes hakyeng mo kǝ ɗee a nen shinzeen mo, ɗang mo fes le pǝtuup fur mo nkaa Wàar mǝ Mosis.
ACT 21:21 Mo kǝ kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa gha nǝnee, <Waa a kám nnen Yahudi mo jir, ɗe mo kǝ tong mɓut nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, nǝ, mo yit Wàar Mosis mo, ɗang nǝ taji mo can jep fur mo kas, kǝzak nǝ taji mo tap kǝ mbii ɗe puun fun mo kǝ loot kǝ cìn mo kas.>
ACT 21:22 Ɓǝ, yaksǝ, ɓǝ gha arang yaksǝ yii? A lekom kǝn nghan kǝlǝng mbii ɗe mun nsat, ɗe nǝ ret kǝ nghan cìn. Mbǝɗǝ tǝng mon nkǝlǝng nǝ, aa jì.
ACT 21:23 A mbii ɗe muu reɓet kǝ nghan cìn nɗesǝ. Mun kǝ gurum mo feer, ɗe mo kǝ cweerpwoo nDaa Naan nkaa káa fur.
ACT 21:24 A dǝm ashak kǝ mo, kǝn nwun cìn mbii ɗe wun nlesuk ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang nyit mǝ Naan. A gha nkwat shool mbǝ mbii ɗe mon ncìn jir. Ɓǝ mon mmak sak shweepkáa fur mo zak. A nɗǝǝn ar ɗesǝ, ɓǝ jir mo mman nǝ, baa mee zeen mɓut pwoo ɗe mo kǝ sat nkaa gha nǝ kas, mbǝɗe gha shikáa fwaa aa tap kǝ Wàar mǝ Mosis nǝ mo.
ACT 21:25 Mbǝ nnen ɗe mo shinzeen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas, ɓǝ mu ten mulep a rǝran mmo, nkaa pwoo ɗe gyet mu yool mu ɗar nkaa nǝ, nǝ, taji mo se mee mbiise ɗe mo kǝ ten shin nkùm kas, kǝ taji mo se toom kas, kǝzak taji mo se long ɗe mo miyoor took nnǝ kas, kǝ taji mo cin ngaa kas.>>
ACT 21:26 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ Pool seet ashak kǝ des ɗefeer nǝ mo, kǝ mmo cìn mbii ɗe mon nlesut ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang nyit mǝ Naan. Yaksǝ wur ɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan Ɗeɗes nǝ, mbǝkǝ nwur sat ɗi ngurum mo, puus ɗe mon nlesut ɗee a ɗeɓang nǝn nkyes ɗi, parpuus ɗe koo a wii, ɓǝ wur nshin mbiizuum mbǝ shik.
ACT 21:27 Kaaɗe teer ɗepwoovǝl nǝ mo kus kǝgam, ɓǝ pak nnen Yahudi ɗe mo kǝ tong Eshiya mo jì naa Pool nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes, ɓǝ mo kar, kǝzak mo lepshii nkuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo jir, ɓǝ mo yaa Pool.
ACT 21:28 Moo le or, ɓǝ mon nkaa sat nǝnee, <<Wun nnen Isreil mo, wu ɓam mun! Wu naa gwar ɗe dǝ wur dǝm shipee-shipee nɗǝǝn yil nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ nwur kám ngurum mo, kǝn mmo ɓák mun nnen Isreil mo ɗe, kǝ Wàar mǝ Mosis mo, kǝ Lu Naan ɗeɗes sǝ zak. Baa a mǝnǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, wur kǝ ɗel kǝ pak nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes zak. Wur kǝ le Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu.>>
ACT 21:29 Mo leshap ɗesǝ, a mbǝɗe mo kǝ naa Trofimus ngu Afisus ashak kǝ wur nɗǝǝn pee nkaam, ɓǝ mo pan nǝ, ntong a Pool kǝ jì kǝ wur nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ.
ACT 21:30 Ɓǝ nen pee nkaam nǝ mo yool jir, gurum nǝ mo shwe jì kuur ashak abet, koo a nkoop pee ɗeɗangyii, mo yaa Pool, ɓǝ mo fee wur put mɓwoon Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓǝ mo shoot pwoolu nǝ mo abet-abet.
ACT 21:31 Kaaɗe mo nkaa tangpee tu Pool, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon mǝ nnen Rom mo, kǝlǝng nǝ, Jerusalem nǝ gam kǝ or ɗes zam.
ACT 21:32 Abet-abet ɓǝ wur pǝrep shiitoon mo, kǝ pak ɗǝnan-nan mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo, ɓǝ mo shwe dǝm pǝ nen ɗe mo yaa Pool ɗi. Kaaɗe mo naa ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ kǝ shiitoon mo, ɓǝ mo nook nǝrem Pool.
ACT 21:33 Yaksǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ jì kus kǝ Pool, ɓǝ wur yaa Pool, wur le kǝ mmo ɓwoot Pool shi shoolbǝring mo vǝl. Wur tal nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur a wii? Kǝzak wur cìn a mii?>>
ACT 21:34 Yaksǝ kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo le or. Pak mo nkaa sat mee mbii, ɗang pak mo nkaa sat mee mbii ɗecì mo zak. Kaaɗe baa ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ wur mak manshii mǝ mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝn ngurum nǝ mo kǝ ɗyeep ɗoo ɗes kas, ɓǝ wur le kǝ mmo dǝm kǝ wur mpeetong mǝ shiitoon mo.
ACT 21:35 Kaaɗe mo jì wul a pee kǝkàa mpwoo lu nǝ, ɓǝ shiitoon mo mang wur ɗiyeep aɗeng mbǝɗe kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo ɗee a koo nentar mo sǝ.
ACT 21:36 Mo nkaa ɗiyeep ɗoo ɓǝ, mo nkaa sat nǝnee, <<Wu tu wur, wu tu wur!>>
ACT 21:37 Kaaɗe mo nkaa ɗel kǝ Pool nɗǝǝn peetong mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur sat ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Kyet a mmak yit nghan nsat mee mbii ɗi nghan wo?>> Ngu taakyeen nǝ tal pǝ wur nǝnee, <<A man pwoo mǝ nnen Heleni mo ee?
ACT 21:38 Tan! Baa a gha a ngu Ijip ɗe gyet nɗǝǝn meeteer ɗeɗel sǝ mo, ɓǝ wur ɓwetɓeer nkaa gwomnati, ɗewur dul gurum mo ngal feer, dǝm nɗang shin a naaryil, mbǝ twe gurum mo sǝ kas ee?>>
ACT 21:39 Pool lap nwur nǝnee, <<An a ngu Yahudi. Mo làa an a nTarsus nɗǝǝn yil nSilisiya. An a laayil mǝnǝ, ɗe nǝ a mǝ man nkòo a wii. An pǝ ɗang pǝ gha, a shínpee nghan nleshap ɗi kǝ kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo.>>
ACT 21:40 Ngu taakyeen nǝ wur shínpee nwur. Yaksǝ Pool ɗar nkaa pee kǝkàa nǝ, wur ɗiyeep sar nkuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mmo ɗok ɗe tǝtǝk. Kaaɗe mo ɗok tǝtǝk, ɓǝ wur leshap ngurum nǝ mo shi liispwoo Hiburu. Wur sat mmo nǝnee,
ACT 22:1 <<Ɗyemnaa mo, kǝ puun fen mo, wu lekom kǝn nwun kǝlǝng an ɗi, kǝn nghan leshap ɗe nwun agaak, ɗe nenkám nǝ, baa wen kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas.>>
ACT 22:2 Kaaɗe mo kǝlǝng wur leshap mmo a shi liispwoo Hiburu, ɓǝ mo sǝǝt ɗok tǝtǝk. Yaksǝ Pool sat nǝnee,
ACT 22:3 <<An a ngu Yahudi, ɗe mo làa an a nTarsus mǝ yil nSilisiya. Ɗangɓǝ nwurang a nɗǝǝn pee nkaam ɗesǝ. An nkam tang ran a nsar mǝ Gamaliyel. Mo kǝ tap kám nghan rǝret hakyeng nɗǝǝn Wàar ɗe mo a mǝ puun fun mo, ɗe an kǝ zuur ɗes zam mbǝ cìn ɗak Naan, koo wun sǝ.
ACT 22:4 Nǝ le gyet wen kǝn shinjeel ɗes, nnen ɗe mo kǝ seet nɗang Jesu Kristi, kǝzak, wen kǝn twe pak mo, ɗang kǝn mɓwoot shurep mo kǝ daas mo, ɗe nle mo nlushoot.
ACT 22:5 Koo a pris ɗeɗes sǝ, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan ɗesǝ mo, ɓǝ mon mmak ɗar langtǝng fen, nǝ pwoo ɗe an pǝ sat nǝ azeen. Mbǝɗǝ gyet wen kǝn lap ɓǝǝt-haal a pǝ mo, mbǝkǝ nghan ndǝm kǝ nǝ nɗyemnǝǝn fun nnen Yahudi mo, ɗe mo kǝ tong nɗǝǝn Damaskus, kǝ nghan nyak nenseet nɗang Jesu, ɗe mo kǝ tong pee nkaam mǝnǝ. Mbǝkǝ nghan jì ɗi kǝ mo nJerusalem a ɓuɓwoot, kǝn mmo shinjeel ɗi mmo.>>
ACT 22:6 <<Kaaɗe an a ar yoo mwaan nǝ, ɓǝ jì nwul kus kǝ Damaskus, koo puus a naar sǝ. Nnen mman, ɓǝ mee peeɓang ɗeɗes, tong aɗeng sham ɓangpee ɗe an ɗi cǝǝrkaat.
ACT 22:7 Yaksǝ ntaa nyil, ɓǝ kǝlǝng mee ɗoo nǝ pǝ sat nghan nǝnee, <Sool, Sool, a mii le ɗang aa shin jeel nghan yii?>
ACT 22:8 Ɓǝ ntal nǝnee, <A gha wii Daa?> ɓe wu sat nghan nǝnee, <A an Jesu ngu Nazaret ɗe gha nkaa shinjeel nghan.>
ACT 22:9 Nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ an, mo naa peeɓang nǝ, ɗang baa mo kǝlǝng ɗoo mǝ ngwe ɗewur leshap kǝ an nǝ kas.
ACT 22:10 Ɓǝ ntal nǝnee, <Daa, waa a reɓet kǝn nghan cìn a mii?> Yaksǝ Daa sat nghan nǝnee, <A yool a dǝm nDamaskus, a mpeemǝnǝ ɓǝ mon nsat mbii mo nghan jir, ɗe an kǝn nle mo mbǝkǝ gha cìn ɗi.>
ACT 22:11 Wen ncǝǝr nɗee a vum, mbǝ ɓal mǝ peeɓang nǝ. Ɓǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ an, mo yaa sar nghan, ɓǝ mo dǝm kǝ an nDamaskus.
ACT 22:12 <<Mee gwar ɗi ɗe mo kǝ petsǝm wur a Ananiyas, wur a mee nguseet ndang Naan, ɗewur kǝ cìn mbii ɗe Wàar Mosis moo sat rǝret. Nnen Yahudi ɗe mo kǝ tong nDamaskus jir, moo shin ɗeɗes nwur.
ACT 22:13 Wur jì ɗar kus kǝ an, ɓǝ wur sat nghan nǝnee, <Ɗyemnǝǝn fen Sool, a naapee> Abet-abet ɓǝ nnaapee, ɗe nǝ le nghan nnaa wur.
ACT 22:14 Ɓǝ wur sat nghan zak nǝnee, <Naan mǝ puun fun mo, kǝ bǝlǝp gha, mbǝkǝ nghan man mbii ɗe Naan kǝ reɓet kǝn gha cìn ɗi, kǝ mbǝkǝ nghan naa Ngwe ɗe ndǝre sǝ, kǝ nghan kǝlǝng ɗoopwoo wur ɗi zak.
ACT 22:15 Mbǝɗǝ gha mbǝ ɗee a langtǝng wur, mbǝkǝ nghan leshap ɗi ngurum mo nkaa mbii ɗe aa naa, kǝ mbii ɗe aa kǝlǝng zak.
ACT 22:16 Yaksǝ, ɓǝ aa yap a mii? A yool kǝn mmo cìn baptisma ɗe ngha, Mbǝkǝ nghan ɗang ɗi nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Daa, kǝn nwur vwang shikbish fwaa mo ɗi.> >>
ACT 22:17 <<Kaaɗe waa baa nji nJerusalem, ɓǝ an nkaa ɗangnaan nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes, ɓǝ nsuun suun.
ACT 22:18 An naa Daa, ɓǝ wur sat nghan nǝnee, <A yool nkyen, a put aku nɗǝǝn Jerusalem nǝ, mbǝɗe baa mon lap langtǝng ɗe gha mbǝ sat nǝ nkaa an kas.>
ACT 22:19 Ɓǝ nlap nǝ, daa, mo shikáa mo, mo man nǝ, gyet an kǝn ɗel nkòo a lu Naan ɗeɗangyii, mbǝkǝ nghan twe nen ɗe mo shinzeen ngha, kǝ gyet an kǝn nǝrem mo zak.
ACT 22:20 Kǝzak, kaaɗe gyet mo tu Stivin ngusatpwoo fwaa, ɓǝ gyet an kǝn ɗar ɗi zak, ɗang gyet an aɓwoon mǝ mbii ɗe mo cìn nǝ jir, ɗe gyet a an nyaa leelep mǝ nen ɗe mo tu Stivin nǝ zak.
ACT 22:21 Ɓǝ Daa sat nghan nǝnee, <A yool a dǝm, mpeeɗe an mbǝ lep gha dǝm jong-jong, pǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas.> >>
ACT 22:22 Kuur mǝ gurum nǝ mo lekom pǝ kǝlǝng Pool ɓǝ jì wul mpwoo ɗewur sat nǝ, ɗangɓǝ mo waa baa ɗyeep ɗoo ɗi zak, mo sat nǝnee, <<Wu tu wur! Wu tu wur! Wu baa kǝ gwar ɗe mǝnǝ aku nɗǝǝn yil nǝ. Baa nǝ ret kǝ mmo yit gwar ɗe mǝnǝ ɗi mmeen kas!>>
ACT 22:23 Kaaɗe mo nkaa ɗyeep ɗoo nǝ, kǝ mo nkaa taat leelep fur mo shin kaa aɗeng, ɗang mo nkaa woo ǝrong kaa kǝ nǝ aɗeng zak.
ACT 22:24 Yaksǝ ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon mo, le kǝn mmo ɗel kǝ Pool nɗǝǝn lu ɗe a peetong mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo. Wur le kǝ mo cam Pool shi mbwat, mbǝkǝ nwur mak manshii mǝ mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝ nkuur gurum nǝ mo kǝ ɗyeep ɗoo ɗi nkaa wur.
ACT 22:25 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe mo ɓwoot wur shi teng shim, mbǝkǝ mmo shin mbwat ɗi nwur, ɓǝ Pool sat mmee ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo, ɗewur ɗar kus kǝ wur nǝnee, <<Tan, kyet nǝ a ndǝre kǝn nwun shin mbwat ngwe ɗewur a ngu Rom, ɓǝ baa mo kǝ tok mee ɗyeel ɗe nǝ yaa wur kas aa?>>
ACT 22:26 Kaaɗe shiitoon ɗeɗes kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm sat ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Aa reɓet cìn a mii ngwar ɗesǝ yii? Gwar ɗesǝ nǝ wur a ngu Rom.>>
ACT 22:27 Ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ wur jì sat mPool nǝnee, <<A sat an azeen-zeen, gha a ngu Rom ee?>> Yaksǝ wur lap nǝnee, <<Kǝzak an a ngu Rom!>>
ACT 22:28 Ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ sat nwur nǝnee, <<Gyet wen nkwat a shool ɗes, akuɗang ɓǝ wen ɗee a nguyil nRom nǝ.>> Pool sat nǝnee, <<Ɗang mo làa wen a ngu Rom.>>
ACT 22:29 Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ reɓet cìn tal pǝ wur ɗe, mo yool abet ɓǝ mo yit wur mbǝshin. Kaaɗe ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ man nǝ, Pool a ngu Rom, ɓǝ kǝǝrmuut yaa wur hakyeng, mbǝɗe wur kǝ ten ɓwoot wur.
ACT 22:30 Ɗangɓǝ daar nǝ, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ reɓet man zeen mǝ mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝ nnen Yahudi mo reɓet yaa wur nǝ. Yaksǝ wur fwen Pool, wur le kǝn mmo pǝrep pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nenɗyeel mo, mo kuur ashak jir, ɗang wur dǝm le Pool ɗar ntoom nenɗyeel nǝ mo.
ACT 23:1 Pool ban yit nkaa nenɗyeel nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, an kǝn ncìn ɗak mǝ Naan a shi pan kǝ pǝtuup fen ɗe nǝ a nɗe ndǝre ntoom mǝ Naan jiwul nCicinsǝ.>>
ACT 23:2 Kaaɗe Ananiyas, pris ɗeɗes kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur sat nnen ɗe moo ɗar kus kǝ Pool, kǝ mmo shweer wur mpwoo.
ACT 23:3 Ɓǝ Pool sat nwur nǝnee, <<Naan nshweer gha zak, gha a koo shiɓutlu ɗe mo pwes shi tweep piyaa piyaa sǝ. Waa aa tong mbǝkǝ nghan tokɗyeel ɗi nghan shi wàar nǝ mo, ɗang a gha waa ciir a tep wàar nǝ zak. Mbǝɗǝ a gha sat nǝ mo shweer an.>>
ACT 23:4 Nen ɗe moo ɗar ɗi a pee nǝ, mo sat mPool nǝnee, <<Waa aa fǝlǝp a pris ɗeɗes mǝ Naan mmǝnǝ.
ACT 23:5 Pool sat nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, baa wen mman nǝ, wur a pris ɗeɗes mǝ Naan kas, mbǝɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Naan nǝnee, <Taji a sat mee pwoo ɗebish nkaa ngwe ɗeɗes ɗewur nkaa nen fwaa mo kas.> >>
ACT 23:6 Kaaɗe Pool man nǝ, pak mo nɗǝǝn nenɗyeel nǝ mo a nnen Sadusi mo, kǝ pak mo a nnen Farisi mo, ɓǝ wur ɗiyeep ɗoo nɗǝǝn luɗyeel nǝ. Wur sat nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, an a ngu Farisi, ɗang a ngu Farisi làa an zak. A mbǝɗe wen shinzeen nǝ, gurum mon nyool a peemúut, a nǝ le ɗang mo mbǝ tokɗyeel nghan nɗesǝ.>>
ACT 23:7 Kaaɗe Pool sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ ɓǝlep yool nnaar nnen Farisi mo, kǝ nnen Sadusi mo, ɓǝ kuur kǝ gurum nǝ mo ɓak sut vǝl.
ACT 23:8 Nen Sadusi moo sat nǝ baa gurum mon nyool a peemúut kas, kǝ baa mee nenlep mǝ Naan mo ɗi kas, kǝ baa mee mǝ riin mo ɗe kas zak, ɗang nnen Farisi mo shinzeen nǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗe jir.
ACT 23:9 Ɓǝ or ɗeɗes yool ɗi nɗǝǝn luɗyeel nǝ. Pak nenkám Wàar mǝ Mosis ɗe mo a nnen Farisi mo, mo yool ɗar atǝng, mo yaa ɓeetshik ɗes hakyeng. Mo sat nǝnee, <<Baa mu naa mee mbii ɗebish nɗǝǝn gwar ɗesǝ kas, ngul a mee riin, koo a mee ngulep mǝ Naan leshap kǝ wur.>>
ACT 23:10 Kaaɗe ɓeetshik nǝ naat zam, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes kǝǝr nǝ, mon nyool tu Pool, ɓǝ wur lep shiitoon mo dǝm dul wur ɓalɓal shin put nɗǝǝn luɗyeel nǝ, kǝ mmo dǝm kǝ wur a mpeetong mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo.
ACT 23:11 Parmǝnǝ mpar, ɓǝ Daa jì woo shin mPool, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa gha kas, kaaɗe aa leshap ngurum mo nkaa an nɗǝǝn Jerusalem kǝ kaaɗe a ɗee a langtǝng nkaa an sǝ, ɓǝ tǝng gha mbǝ dǝm a leshap ngurum mo nkaa an nɗǝǝn Rom a kǝsǝ zak.>>
ACT 23:12 Daar mɓít, ɓǝ pak nnen Yahudi mo ɓalpwoo mo shi ɓal ashak, kǝ mmo ɓǝlemcuk shi toom nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Naan nǝ, baa ɗun nse mee mbii, koo shwaa mee am kas, tǝng ɗun tu Pool akuɗang.
ACT 23:13 Nen ɗe mo ɓalpwoo ashak mbǝ tu Pool nǝ, mo met nlaarfeer.
ACT 23:14 Yaksǝ mo jì pǝ pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mo, mo sat nǝnee, <<Mun muu ɓalpwoo fun ɓalɓal ashak, kǝ mmun tuweer nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Naan nǝ, baa mun cam mee mbiise kas, tǝng mun tu Pool akuɗang.
ACT 23:15 <<Mbǝ mǝnǝ yaksǝ, wun kǝ nenɗyeel mo jir, wu sat ngwe ɗeɗes, kǝn nwur jì kǝ Pool pǝ wun ɗi, koo wuu tang a naa pwoo wur nǝ ɗi rǝret sǝ. Mun mun ten mu ɗak sun, mbǝkǝ mun taa mu tu wur ɗi a ar, akuɗang wur jì wul pǝ wun ɗi.>>
ACT 23:16 Ɗangɓǝ kǝn Pool, kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe mo sat nkaa loom ndǝm mo pǝkom ar nǝ, ɓǝ wur dǝm ɗel nɗǝǝn Peetong shiitoon nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur woo pwoo mǝnǝ mPool.
ACT 23:17 Yaksǝ Pool pet memee mɓut ɗenan mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<A dǝm kǝ làa zǝlang ɗesǝ pǝ ngwe ɗeɗes ɗi, mbǝɗe wur kǝ mee pwoo ɗewur kǝ reɓet sat nǝ ngwe ɗeɗes.>>
ACT 23:18 Mee ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon nǝ mo, wur mang làa zǝlang nǝ, wur dǝm kǝ wur pǝ ngwe ɗeɗes ɗi, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<A Pool ɗewur a ɓuɓwoot sǝ, a wur pet an, kǝn nwur ɗang pǝ an, kǝn nghan njì kǝ làa zǝlang ɗesǝ pǝ gha ɗi. Nǝ, làa nǝ wur kǝ mee pwoo ɗewur kǝ reɓet sat nǝ ngha.>>
ACT 23:19 Ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ yaa sar làa zǝlang nǝ, wur dǝm kǝ làa zǝlang nǝ mmee koop mbǝshin. Yaksǝ wur tal pǝ làa zǝlang nǝ coot nǝnee, <<Waa aa mee pwoo ɗǝɗang ɗe aa reɓet sat nǝ nghan yii?>>
ACT 23:20 Làa zǝlang nǝ sat nǝnee, <<A nnen Yahudi mo kǝ ɓalpwoo mo ashak nǝ, mo mbǝ jì ɗang pǝ gha, mbǝkǝ daar a dǝm ɗi kǝ Pool a pee ɓeetpwoo. Mo mbǝ cìn koo mo a mbǝ baa naa pwoo nǝ ɗi rǝret sǝ.
ACT 23:21 Taji a reɓet mmo kas, mbǝɗe gurum mo met nlaarfeer mɓut mmo, mo kǝ lǝǝm a ar, mo mbǝ yap Pool dǝm. Mo kǝ ɓǝlemcuk shi toom nɗǝǝn sǝm mǝ Naan nǝ, baa ɗun nse, koo shwaa mee mbii kas, tǝng ɗun ntu Pool akuɗang. Yaksǝ mo kǝ ɗak sut, moo ɗar naa a ɗe gha mbǝ lep Pool shindǝm ɓejee.>>
ACT 23:22 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ wur ɓwet làa zǝlang nǝ shinseet, ɓǝ wur sat làa zǝlang nǝ nǝnee, <<Taji a woo mmee gurum nǝ aa leshap ɗesǝ nǝ nghan kas.>>
ACT 23:23 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nǝ pet mee ɗǝnan-nan mǝ shiitoon mo vǝl, ɗe mo kǝ tap shiitoon mo kambil kambil. Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Wu le shiitoon mo kambil vǝl, kǝ shiitoon mǝ lang bǝring mo laarpwoovǝl, kǝ shiitoon mǝ lek lek shi kop mo kambil vǝl zak. Mbǝkǝ mmo dǝm nSizariya, koo naapuus pwoofeer ɗe mǝ par cicinsǝ.>>
ACT 23:24 Wur sat kǝn mmo le mee bǝring ɗe nǝn mang Pool, mbǝkǝ mo seet kǝ wur ryang pǝ gofna Feliks ɗi.
ACT 23:25 Ngu taakyeen nǝ ran mee lep a rǝran shindǝm ngofna Feliks, ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee,
ACT 23:26 <<Tokshik nsar ngwe ɗeɗes Klodiyus Lisiyas, dǝm pǝ ngwe ɗeɗes gofna Feliks ɗi.
ACT 23:27 Nnen Yahudi mo kǝ yaa gwar ɗesǝ, ɗang dǝ mo yappee ɗe mon ntu wur ɗi, a kǝsǝ ɓǝ a, an ndǝm kǝ shiitoon mo, ɓǝ a an mɓam wur, mbǝɗe nkǝlǝng nǝ, wur a ngu Rom.
ACT 23:28 Kaaɗe an pǝ reɓet manshii mǝ mbii ɗe nǝ le ɗang mo yaa wur, ɓǝ ndǝm kǝ wur nɗǝǝn luɗyeel mo.
ACT 23:29 Yaksǝ nkat mo yaa wur a mbǝ pak mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Wàar mo mo, ɗang pwoo ɗe mo sat nkaa wur nǝ, ɓǝ baa nǝ mak muut nwur, koo nǝ le kǝ mo shoot wur kas.
ACT 23:30 Ɓǝ kaaɗe nkǝlǝng nǝ pak nnen Yahudi nǝ mo kǝ ɓalpwoo mo mbǝ tu gwar nǝ, ɓǝ nlep wur shindǝm pǝ gha ɗi abet. An kǝn nsat nnen ɗe mo kǝ pwoo nkaa wur nǝ, kǝn mmo dǝm leshap ɗe mo kǝ nǝ nkaa wur ɗi ntoom fwaa.>>
ACT 23:31 Aasǝ ɓǝ shiitoon nǝ mo mang Pool, kaaɗe mo kǝ sat mmo sǝ, mo dǝm kǝ wur Antipatris mpar.
ACT 23:32 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mo yit kǝn nnenbǝring mo dǝm kǝ wur, kǝn nnenshii mo waa baa ɗi a peetong shiitoon nǝ mo.
ACT 23:33 Kaaɗe nenbǝring ɗesǝ nǝ mo dǝm wul nSizariya, ɓǝ mo shin Pool kǝ lep ɗi a rǝran nǝ ngofna.
ACT 23:34 Kaaɗe gofna tang lep ɗi a rǝran nǝ, ɓǝ wur tal pǝ Pool nǝnee, <<Waa a put a nkoop yil ɗeɗangyii>> Ɓǝ kaaɗe wur kǝlǝng nǝ Pool put a nkoop nSilisiya,
ACT 23:35 Yaksǝ gofna nǝ sat nǝnee, <<An mbǝ kǝlǝng pwoo fwaa nǝ, katɗang nen ɗe mo pungwool fwaa nǝ mo jì wul.>> Wur le kǝn mmo shoot Pool nkoop tul mǝ mishkoom Herot.
ACT 24:1 Aɓwoon meeteer mo paat, ɓǝ Ananiyas pris ɗeɗes, jì ashak kǝ pak pris ɗenan mo, kǝ mee Nguɓerepdyeel ɗe sǝm wur a Tartulus, mo dǝm kǝ ɗyeel nkaa Pool pǝ gofna ɗi.
ACT 24:2 Kaaɗe mo pet Pool, ɓǝ Tartulus ɗoom leshap nkaa Pool nǝnee, <<Waa Feliks ngwe ɗeret met jir. A mbǝ gha, ɗang muu tongriyang, hakyeng, kǝ a mbǝ ɗak ɗeret fwaa mo zak, ɗang yil fun ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗe ɗak, koo a mpee ɗeɗangyii.
ACT 24:3 Mbii ɗe a cìn nǝ mo, ɓǝ mu plang ɗes zam, koo a nii, ɓǝ gurum moo plang gha.
ACT 24:4 Ɗangɓǝ mbǝkǝ taji nle kǝn nghan yool a yaa pwoo a tong mpee ɗesǝ kas, ɓǝ an pǝ ɗang pǝ gha mbǝ ɗeret fwaa, a lekom kǝn nghan kǝlǝng mun ɗi mbǝ reppee lee.
ACT 24:5 Mu kat gwar ɗesǝ wur a ngu tǝkook kǝ pee, ɗǝ wur le ɓǝlep ɗebish yool nnaar kǝ nnen Yahudi mo. Koo mpee ɗeɗangyii nɗǝǝn yil nǝ. Kǝzak wur a ngu taakyeen mǝ soon mǝ nnen Nazarin mo zak.
ACT 24:6 Nǝ le gyet wur reɓet le Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ ɗee a mbii ɗebuu, ɗang mu yaa wur. Muu reɓet tokɗyeel nwur a shi wàar fun mo.
ACT 24:7 Ɗangɓǝ gyet ngwe ɗeɗes Lisiyas jì dul wur put kǝnǝ shiɓal nsar fun.
ACT 24:8 Yaksǝ Lisiyas sat nnen ɗe mo kǝ pwoo nkaa wur nǝ, kǝn mo jì pǝ gha ɗi. Katɗang a tal pwoo mo nkaa mbii ɗe muu sat sǝ mo shikáa fwaa pǝ wur, ɓǝ a mman zeen mǝ pwoo ɗesǝ mo jir, ɗe muu jì kǝ mo nkaa wur.>>
ACT 24:9 Nen Yahudi mon mɓwoon pwoo ɗe Ngu ɓǝrep ɗyeel nǝ sat, dǝm mo tong a langtǝng nǝ, pwoo ɗe Ngu ɓǝrep ɗyeel sat nǝ mo azeen jir.
ACT 24:10 Ɓǝ gofna kam sar mPool, mbǝkǝ nwur leshap ɗi. Yaksǝ Pool sat nǝnee, <<Wen man nǝ, waa aa cìn ɓit mo ɗes, ɓǝ gha nkaa tokɗyeel nnen ɗesǝ mo. Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ an pǝ leshap ɗesǝ nǝ a shi retnyit, mbǝ put kǝ káa fen.
ACT 24:11 Waa shikáa fwaa a mak bǝlǝp shii mǝnǝ, ɓǝ a mman nǝ, mɓut teer ɗe mo ɗel kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo, ɓǝ gyet wen nkàa nJerusalem mbǝ seyil nNaan.
ACT 24:12 Baa nnen Yahudi mo kǝ cam kat an mpwoo kǝ mee gurum nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes kas, kǝ baa mo cam kat wen nle mee gurum ɓwetɓeer kas, koo a nɗǝǝn Lu Naan mo, kǝ koo a nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nǝ kas zak.
ACT 24:13 Kǝzak, baa mon mmak kám nghan agaak azeen-zeen nkaa mbii ɗe mo ji kǝ dyeel fen pǝ gha yaksǝ nǝ kas.
ACT 24:14 Ɗangɓǝ nǝ azeen-zeen, an kǝn seyil nNaan mǝ puun fun mo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗe mǝ mo kǝ pet a ɗung. An kǝn seyil nNaan mǝ puun fun mo, ɗang nshinzeen mbii ɗe mo ran mo nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ Mosis mo jir. Kǝ mbii ɗe mo ran mo nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt-haal mǝ nen satpwoo mǝ Naan mo zak.
ACT 24:15 An kǝn canciin nɗǝǝn Naan, kaaɗe mǝ mo kǝ canciin nɗǝǝn Naan sǝ zak nǝ, mon nyool kǝ gurum mo a peemúut jir, nnen ɗe ndǝre mo, kǝ nen ɗebish mo zak.
ACT 24:16 A mbǝ canciin mǝnǝ, ɗang an pǝ mbǝ gung, mbǝkǝ nghan tong ɗe shi mǝse ɗeret ntoom kǝ Naan, kǝ ntoom kǝ gurum mo shidaar-shidaar.
ACT 24:17 <<Aɓwoon mǝ ɓit mo ruk, ɓǝ wen njì kǝ shool mbǝ ɓam nen fen mo, kǝ mbii mo mbǝ wus mbiizuum nNaan zak.
ACT 24:18 Kaaɗe an nkaa cìn mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo jì kat an nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓǝ kǝn lesen a ɗeɓang. Ɓǝ baa mo kat an ashak kǝ mee kuur gurum mo, ɗe mun nkaa ɗyeep ɗoo koo wat mee mbii mo kas. Gyet pak nnen Yahudi ɗe mo pwat Eshiya mo ɗi.
ACT 24:19 Katɗang yoo mo kǝ mee pwoo nkaa an, ɓǝ yoo nǝ nret kǝn nnen Yahudi ɗe mo pwat Eshiya sǝ, mo ɗe ntoom fwaa, mbǝ jì kǝ ɗyeel nkaa an nǝ.
ACT 24:20 An mbǝ reɓet kǝ nnen ɗe mon mpee ɗesǝ shikáa fur kǝn mmo sat mbii ɗebish ɗe mo kat nɗǝǝn an, kaaɗe ɗe nɗar ntoom nenɗyeel mo sǝ ɗi.
ACT 24:21 Ɗee a mbii mǝndong, ɗe ɗiyeep ɗoo fen nnaar mo, ɓǝ a an sat mmo nǝnee, <A mbǝ pwoo nkaa yool a peemúut, ɗang wun bǝ tokɗyeel nghan ntoom fuu cicinsǝ, ɓejee ɗak.> >>
ACT 24:22 Ɗangɓǝ mbǝɗe Feliks pan man pwoo nkaa ar nǝ rǝret, ɓǝ wur ɗar kǝ ɗyeel nǝ. Wur sat nǝnee, <<Katɗang parpuus ɗe Lisiyas ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon mo jì wul, ɓǝ an nsǝǝt nnaa pwoo fuu nǝ.>>
ACT 24:23 Wur sat ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon mo, kǝ nwur tap kǝ Pool, ɗang wur shínpee mPool, taji mo daampee nshaar mǝ Pool mo mbǝ jì cìn ɓam nwur kas.
ACT 24:24 Aɓwoon pak meeteer mo, ɓǝ Feliks jì ashak kǝ mat fin Drusila, ɗe war a reep Yahudi. Yaksǝ wur lep mmo dǝm jì kǝ Pool. Feliks lekom kǝn nwur kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe Pool nkaa sat nǝ, ɗe nǝ a mǝ shinzeen nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi.
ACT 24:25 Pool leshap nkaa tong ɗe ndǝre-ndǝre, kǝ ngurum yaashin, kǝ pwoo nkaa tokɗyeel ɗe nǝn mbǝ jì. Ɓǝ kǝǝrmuut yaa Feliks, nǝ le nwur sat mPool nǝnee, <<A mak seet yaksǝ aku, katɗang parpuus ɗe nkatpee, ɓǝ an mbǝ pet gha zak.>>
ACT 24:26 Feliks leɗyeen nǝ, tong Pool mbǝ shin a shool nɗyin, a nǝ le ɗang wur naa mpet Pool shidaar-shidaar, mbǝkǝ nwur leshap ɗe kǝ nwur.
ACT 24:27 Aɓwoon ɓit mo vǝl, ɓǝ Poncus Festus wur kaa a gofna a koppee Feliks. Gyet a mbǝɗe Feliks reɓet kǝn nnen Yahudi mo ɗee a shaar fin mo, a nǝ le ɗang gyet wur yit Pool nɗǝǝn lushoot.
ACT 25:1 Aɓwoon meeteer mo kun, ɗe Festus kǝ jì nɗǝǝn yil mǝ mulki mishkoom fin, ɓǝ wur yool nSizariya kàa nJerusalem.
ACT 25:2 Yaksǝ pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nennan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo jì kǝ ɗyeel mǝ mbii ɗebish mo, ɗe nǝ, Pool kǝ cìn mo pǝ Festus ɗi, mo ɗang pǝ wur,
ACT 25:3 mbǝkǝ nwur ɓam mo ɗi. Moo reɓet kǝn Festus lep mmo jì kǝ Pool nJerusalem, mbǝɗe mo kǝ tap ɗaksut, mbǝkǝ mmo táa tu Pool ɗi a ar.
ACT 25:4 Ɗangɓǝ Festus lap mmo nǝnee, <<Pool wur a ɓuɓwoot nSizariya. An shikáa fen, wen nreɓet yool sham nSizariya nǝ nɗǝǝn meeteer ɗesǝ mo.
ACT 25:5 Wur sat zak nǝnee, wu yit kǝn mpak nen ɗenan-nan mo mɓut nwun, mo sham ashak kǝ an, mbǝkǝ mmo sat mbii ɗebish ɗe gwar nǝ wur cìn mo ɗi.>>
ACT 25:6 Aɓwoon ɗe Festus tong ashak kǝ mo mbǝ teer mo pwookun koo kaapaat, ɓǝ wur yool sham nSizariya. Yaksǝ wur tong nkaa mbii tong mǝ tokɗyeel, ɓǝ wur sat mmo dǝm jì kǝ Pool.
