ACT 25:7 Kaaɗe mo jì wul kǝ Pool, ɓǝ nnen Yahudi mo jì, ɗe mo tong nyil Jerusalem kǝ pwoo ɗebish mo ɗes nkaa wur, ɗe baa mǝ mo shikáa mo mo mak kám agaak zeen mǝ pwoo nǝ mo kas.
ACT 25:8 Pool ɗar ɓalɓal mbǝ shang káa fin, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Baa an kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas, koo a nkaa Wàar mǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ koo a nkaa Lu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ, kǝ koo a nkaa Wàar mǝ mishkoom Siza kas koo lee lee.>>
ACT 25:9 Ɗangɓǝ mbǝɗe Festus reɓet kǝ nnen Yahudi mo ɗee a shaar fin, ɓǝ wur tal pǝ Pool nǝnee, <<Kyet aa reɓet kàa nJerusalem, kǝn nghan tokɗyeel ɗi nghan mpeemǝnǝ nkaa mbii ɗesǝ mo aa?>>
ACT 25:10 Ɓǝ Pool sat nǝnee, <<An mbǝ ɗar a ntoom mbii tong mǝ tokɗyeel mǝ Siza, a pee ɗe nǝ ret kǝ mmo tokɗyeel ɗi nghan mmǝnǝ. Baa an kǝn cìn mee shikbish nnen Yahudi mo kas. Waa shikáa fwaa a man azeen-zeen nǝ, baa an kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas.
ACT 25:11 Katɗang yoo an kǝn tep Wàar nǝ, koo cìn mee mbii ɗebish ɗe nǝ mak kǝn mmo tu an, ɓǝ ɗi baa an kǝǝrmuut nǝ kas. Ɗangɓǝ katɗang ɓǝ baa mee zeen ɗi nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe nnen ɗesǝ moo ɗyeel fen mbǝ nǝ kas, ɓǝ baa mee gurum mak shin an nsar mo kas. An kǝn reɓet kǝ a Siza tokɗyeel nǝ nghan.>>
ACT 25:12 Ɓǝ aɓwoon ɗe Festus ɓeetpwoo nǝ ashak kǝ nnen ɗe moo ɓam wur nɗyéel, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Waa a ɗang mbǝ dǝm pǝ Siza ɗi! Ɓǝ gha mbǝ dǝm a pǝ Siza ɗi.>>
ACT 25:13 Aɓwoon teer mo ruk, ɓǝ mishkoom Agripa kǝ Benis mo jì wul nSizariya, mbǝkǝ mmo sat mwaanlee ɗi nFestus.
ACT 25:14 Mbǝɗǝ mo kǝ cìn teer mo ɗes ɗi nSizariya nǝ, ɓǝ Festus yakshii mǝ pwoo nkaa Pool mishkoom Agripa, wur sat nǝnee, <<Mee gwar ɗi, ɗe gyet Feliks yit wur a ɓuɓwoot nlushoot.
ACT 25:15 Kaaɗe dǝ nkàa nJerusalem, ɓǝ pris ɗenan mo, kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo jì kǝ ɗyeel nkaa gwar nǝ pǝ an ɗi. Mo ɗang pǝ an, mbǝkǝ nghan canɗyeel muut ɗi ngwar nǝ.
ACT 25:16 Ɗangɓǝ nlap mmo nǝ, baa nǝ a mǝse mǝ nnen Rom mo, kǝn mmo canɗyeel mmee gurum, ɗe mo kǝ jì kǝ ɗyeel nkaa wur nen pee mmo kǝn shínpee nwur, kǝn nwur leshap mǝ shang káa fin ɗi nluɗyeel ashak kǝ nen ɗe mmo ji kǝ ɗyeel nǝ mo kas. Ɗangɓǝ tǝng mo nshee shínpee nwur, kǝn nwur leshap mǝ shang káa fin ɗi akuɗang mon ncanɗyeel ngwar nǝ.
ACT 25:17 Kaaɗe mo jì mpee ɗesǝ ashak kǝ an, ɓǝ baa wen nɗar ɗi kǝ pwoo nǝ kas, ɓǝ daar nǝ, ɓǝ wen tong nkaa mbii tong mǝ tokɗyeel, ɓǝ wen nle kǝ mmo dǝm jì kǝ gwar nǝ.
ACT 25:18 Kaaɗe nen ɗe mo jì kǝ ɗyeel nkaa gwar nǝ, mo yool ɗar leshap, ɓǝ baa mo sat mee pwoo ɗebish mo nkaa gwar nǝ, kaaɗe an kǝn pan sǝ kas.
ACT 25:19 Ɗangɓǝ pwoo ɗe mo sat nkaa wur nǝ, a pwoo nkaa pak mbii ɗe mo a mǝ mǝse mǝ seyil nNaan mo, kǝ pwoo nkaa mee ngwe ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Jesu zak. Ɗe nǝ, wur muut. Ɓǝ nǝ, Pool leshap ngurum mo ɓalɓal nǝ, Jesu ɗe mmeen.
ACT 25:20 Kaaɗe baa wen mman mbii ɗe an mbǝ cìn nkaa pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ mo kas, ɓǝ wen ntal pǝ Pool nǝ, kyet aa reɓet kàa nJerusalem, kǝ mmo tokɗyeel ɗe nghan nkaa mbii ɗesǝ mo mpeemǝnǝ aa?
ACT 25:21 Ɗangɓe kaaɗe Pool ɗang nǝ, tǝng a Siza tokɗyeel nǝ nɗyin, ɓǝ wen nle kǝ mmo tap kǝ wur rǝret, dǝm wul parpuus ɗe an mbǝ lep wur shindǝm pǝ Siza ɗi.>>
ACT 25:22 Ɓǝ Agripa sat nFestus nǝnee, <<An kǝn nreɓet kǝlǝng pwoo mǝ gwar mǝnǝ shikáa fen.>> Festus sat nǝnee, <<Dǝɗaar ɓǝ gha mbǝ nkǝlǝng wur.>>
ACT 25:23 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ Agripa kǝ Benis mo jì nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes mo hakyeng, ɓǝ mo ɗel nɗǝǝn luɗyeel nǝ ashak kǝ pak shiitoon ɗǝnan-nan mo, kǝ nnen ɗǝnan-nan mǝ pee nkaam nǝ mo. Yaksǝ Festus lep mmo dǝm jì kǝ Pool.
ACT 25:24 Ɓǝ Festus sat nǝnee, <<Mishkoom Agripa, kǝ wun nen ɗe wun ashak kǝ mun jir mpee ɗesǝ. Wu naa gwar ɗesǝ, dǝ nnen Yahudi mo jir, mo kǝ jì kǝ ɗyeel nkaa wur pǝ an ɗi nJerusalem, kǝ mpee ɗesǝ zak. Dǝ mon nkaa ɗyeep ɗoo ɗang moo sat nǝ baa nǝ ret kǝ mmo yit gwar ɗesǝ ɗi mmeen kas.
ACT 25:25 Ɗangɓǝ baa wen kat wur kǝ cìn mee mbii ɗebish ɗe nǝn mmak kǝ mmo tu wur kas. Pool shikáa fin, ɗang kǝ mmo dǝm kǝ ɗyeel fin nǝ pǝ Siza ɗi. Yaksǝ ɓǝ wen kǝn leɗyeen mbǝ lep Pool shindǝm pǝ Siza ɗi.
ACT 25:26 Ɗangɓǝ baa wen mman zeen kǝ mǝ mbii ɗewur cìn nǝ, ɗe wen nran Agustus nkaa nǝ kas. Mbǝ mǝnǝ wen njì kǝ wur ntoom fuu, met jir, ɓǝ a ntoom fwaa mishkoom Agripa, mbǝkǝ aɓwoon ɗe mo bǝlǝp pwoo wur nǝ, ɓǝ an nkat mee mbii ɗe an nran shindǝm ɗi Agustus.
ACT 25:27 Mbǝɗǝ wen naa nǝ ɗee a koo ɗak mwen sǝ, kǝn mmo lep mee gurum shindǝm a ɓuɓwoot, baa ashak kǝ satpwoo nkaa mbii ɗebish ɗe ngwe nǝ cìn kas.>>
ACT 26:1 Mishkoom Agripa sat mPool nǝnee, <<Mo shínpee ngha, mbǝkǝ nghan leshap ɗi shikáa fwaa.>> Aasǝ ɓǝ Pool ɗiyeep sar fin, ɓǝ wur leshap mǝ shang káa fin. Wur sat nǝnee,
ACT 26:2 <<Azeen-zeen, mishkoom Agripa, yaksǝ ɓǝ nǝ fes shang nghan zam, mbǝɗe wen nkatpee leshap mǝ shang nkáa fen ntoom fwaa cicinsǝ, nkaa mbii ɗe nnen Yahudi moo sat cin nkaa an mo jir.
ACT 26:3 Mbǝɗǝ gha kǝ man ɗes zam, nkaa mǝse mǝ mbii ɗe mo a mǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ pwoo nkaa mbii ɗe moo ɓǝlep nkaa nǝ zak. Wen nɗang pǝ gha, a gung kǝn nghan kǝlǝng mbii ɗe an mbǝ nsat mo shi pǝtuup mǝ gung.
ACT 26:4 Nnen Yahudi mo jir, mo man tong fen, peegyet nkutɗi a nzǝlang. Mɓut nnen fen mo, kǝ nɗǝǝn Jerusalem zak, jì wul cicinsǝ.
ACT 26:5 Mo man an peegyet ɗi nshee. Kǝzak katɗang ɓǝ ɗe moo reɓet langtǝng nǝ, yoo mon nsat nǝ, azeen an a ngu Farisi, ɗe nǝ a mee soon ɗe mo fes ɗar ɓal-ɓal nkaa seyil nNaan fun nǝ.
ACT 26:6 Mbǝmǝnǝ kǝn ɗar mpee ɗesǝ, mbǝkǝ mmo tokɗyeel ɗi nghan, a mbǝɗe an pǝ canciin nkaa gampwoo ɗe gyet Naan kǝ cweer nǝn mpuun fun mo.
ACT 26:7 A pwoo ɗe gyet Naan kǝ cweer nsoon fun ɗe kaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo, ɗe moo canciin mbǝ lap nǝ, ɗang mo kǝ gung mbǝ seyil nNaan mpar kǝ puus, mbǝ canciin ɗesǝ. Ɓǝ nnen Yahudi mo dǝm kǝ ɗyeel fen, ntoom fwaa mishkoom!
ACT 26:8 A mii le ɗang baa nnen Yahudi mon mmak shinzeen nǝ, Naan mbǝ nyool kǝ nnen ɗe mo kǝ murep a peemúut kas yii?
ACT 26:9 Gyet wen mpan shikáa fen nǝ, an mbǝ cìn mbii ɗe mmak jir, mbǝkǝ nghan tekook kǝ sǝm Jesu ngu Nazaret ɗi.
ACT 26:10 Gyet a mbii ɗe ncìn nJerusalem mmǝnǝ, ɗe kǝn nlap ɓal pǝ pris ɗenan mo. Gyet kǝn shoot nenseet nɗang Jesu mo ɗes nɗǝǝn lushoot, kǝzak gyet an mɓwoon nnen ɗe mo twe nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo zak.
ACT 26:11 Yit ɗes, ɓǝ nshinjeel nnenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo nɗǝǝn lu Naan mo zak. Gyet kǝn reɓet le kǝn mmo cíipwoo nǝ, baa Jesu a Kristi kas. Mbǝɗǝ gyet njar naa mo nyit bǝbish zam. Mbǝ mǝnǝ ɓǝ gyet mmwaan ndǝm mpee nkaam ɗe baa mo a mǝ nnen Yahudi mo kas, mbǝkǝ nghan nshinjeel ɗi nnenseet nɗang Jesu mo.>>
ACT 26:12 <<Par sǝ mpuus ɓǝ an a ar dǝm nDamaskus mbǝ yak nenseet nɗang Jesu nǝ mo, shi ɓal ɗe kǝn nlap pǝ pris ɗenan mo, ɗǝ a mo lep an zak.
ACT 26:13 Ɓǝ kaaɗe puus a naar, mishkoom! Yaksǝ nnaa mee peeɓang ɗe nǝ tong aɗeng sham ɓangpee, ɗe nǝ met mɓangpee mǝ puus. Nǝ ɓangpee neer an cǝǝrkaat ashak kǝ nen ɗe mo ashak kǝ an.
ACT 26:14 Ɓǝ mun jir mu ɗong nyil, ɓǝ nkǝlǝng mee ɗoo nǝ sat nghan shi liispwoo Hiburu nǝnee, <Sool, Sool, a mii le ɗang waa aa shinjeel nghan yii? Nǝn nshwal ngha, kǝn nghan cut sak shi deelkam ɗe peet peet.>
ACT 26:15 Ɓǝ ntal nǝnee, <A gha wii Daa?> Yaksǝ Daa sat nghan nǝnee, <A an Jesu ɗe aa shinjeel nghan sǝ.
ACT 26:16 Yaksǝ a yool a ɗar atǝng, mbǝɗe an mbǝ woo sen fen ngha, a mbǝkǝ nghan ɗee ɗe a nguɗak fen, kǝ nguɗar langtǝng ngurum mo nkaa mbii ɗe aa naa, kǝ mbii ɗe an mbǝ kám mo nghan zak.>
ACT 26:17 An mbǝ ɓam gha nsar nnen Isreil mo, kǝ nsar nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas. An mbǝ lep gha shindǝm pǝ nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas zak.
ACT 26:18 Mbǝkǝ nghan wang yit mo mo ɗi. Kǝn mmo yit peenkwoo, kǝ mmo ɗel ɗi nɗǝǝn peeɓang. Kǝzak mbǝkǝ mmo put ɗi mɓut mɓal mǝ ngujwaan. Kǝn mmo jì ɗi pǝ Naan zak. Mbǝkǝ katɗang mo shinzeen, ɓǝ mon nkat fwoo mǝ shikbish fur mo, kǝn mon nkat peetong ɗe ashak kǝ nen ɗe Naan kǝ ten bǝlǝp mo zak.>>
ACT 26:19 <<Mishkoom Agripa, baa gyet ncii cìn mbii ɗe suun ɗe nǝ tong aɗeng sham sat nghan kas.
ACT 26:20 Gyet nshee satpwoo Naan nǝ a nnen Damaskus mo, ɗang ndǝm kǝn nghan sat ɗe nnen Jerusalem mo, kǝ yil ɗe mo neer Judiya jir. Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ nsat nnen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas zak. An pǝ sat mmo tuwap, kǝn mmo ciir pǝ Naan ɗi, kǝn mmo cìn ɗak ɗe nǝ kám tuwap mo nǝ ɗi zak.
ACT 26:21 A mpeemǝnǝ, ɗang nnen Yahudi mo yaa an nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes, kǝ gyet mo kǝ tang ar mbǝ tu an.
ACT 26:22 Ɗangɓǝ mbǝɗe nkat ɓam pǝ Naan ɗi, a nǝ le ɗang kǝn nɗar ɗi ntoom fwaa mbǝ cicinsǝ. An nkaa satpwoo Naan nǝ nennan mo, kǝ jep ɗeɗyeen mo jir. Baa nsat a mmee pwoo ɗecì kas, tǝng a pwoo ɗe nensatpwoo Naan mo, kǝ Mosis mo kǝ ten sat nǝ, nǝn nyool cìn a kǝsǝ.
ACT 26:23 Nǝ, tǝng Kristi mbǝ shwaajeel, kǝ a wur a ngwe ɗenshee mǝ yool a peemúut zak. A wur mbǝ shee leshap nkaa peeɓang nǝ nnen Yahudi mo, kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nnen Yahudi mo kas zak.>>
ACT 26:24 Kaaɗe Pool nkaa leshap mbǝ shang káa nǝ, ɓǝ Festus sat shii ɗoo ɗeɗes nǝnee, <<Pool aa tǝttar aa? Man fwaa nii le gha ɗee a ngutar.>>
ACT 26:25 Ɓǝ Pool lap nǝnee, <<Baa an a ngutar kas Festus, ngwe ɗeret met jir. An kǝn sat a pwoo ɗe mo azeen-zeen kǝ ɗe mo a ndǝre zak.
ACT 26:26 Mishkoom man mbii ɗe kǝn nsat sǝ mo agaak. Mbǝɗǝ mman azeen-zeen nǝ, baa mee mbii loom gha mɓut mbii ɗesǝ mo jir kas. Mbǝɗǝ baa gyet mo cìn mbii mǝnǝ mo a sǝsok kas.
ACT 26:27 Mishkoom Agripa, a shinzeen nnensat pwoo mǝ Naan mo ee? Mman nǝ, a shinzeen.>>
ACT 26:28 Mishkoom Agripa sat mPool nǝnee, <<Nɗǝǝn reppee ɗi lee sǝ, ɓǝ aa reɓet ciir kǝ an, kǝn nghan nɗee ɗi a nguseet nɗang Jesu ee?>>
ACT 26:29 Pool lap nǝnee, <<koo a nɗǝǝn reppee lee. Koo a nɗǝǝn pee ɗe nǝ ɗes, ɓǝ an nkaa ɗangnaan mbǝ gha, kǝ nnen ɗe mo nkaa kǝlǝng an cicinsǝ jir, mbǝkǝ mmo tuwap kǝn mmo ɗee ɗi a nenseet nɗang Jesu koo an sǝ. Ɗangɓe taji a shi shoolbǝring kaaɗe an kǝ nǝ sǝ kas.>>
ACT 26:30 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mishkoom yool, kǝ gofna, kǝ Benis, kǝ nnen ɗe mo kǝ tong ashak kǝ mo.
ACT 26:31 Ɓǝ mo dǝm mmee koop mbǝsut, ɓǝ mo ɓeet kǝ shak nǝnee, <<Baa gwar ɗesǝ kǝ cìn mee mbii ɗebish ɗe nǝ mak muut, koo mo nle wur nɗǝǝn lushoot kas.>>
ACT 26:32 Agripa sat nFestus nǝnee, <<Katɗang yoo baa gwar ɗesǝ wur kǝ ɗang mbǝ dǝm kǝ ɗyeel nǝ pǝ Siza ɗi kas, ɓǝ yoo mon ɓwet wur.>>
ACT 27:1 Kaaɗe mo ɓeet nǝ, mun nɗel ntii kǝn mmo dǝm ɗi nyil Itali, ɓǝ mo le Pool kǝ pak nen ɗe mo a ɓuɓwoot, nsar mǝ mee ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon mo, ɗe moo pet sǝm wur a Juliyus, ɗe nǝ a soon mǝ nentap mǝ mishkoom Agustus.
ACT 27:2 Mu ɗel nɗǝǝn mee tii ɗe nǝ tong a nyil Adramitiyum jì, ɗang nǝn mbǝ yool mbǝ dǝm ngaar yil ɗe mo nkoop yil Eshiya mo. Yaksǝ mu yool mwaan nǝ nɗǝǝn tii nǝ. Aristakus mee ngu Masidoniya mǝ yil nTasoloni, wur ɗi ashak kǝ mun zak.
ACT 27:3 Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mǝ wul nSidon. Juliyus cìn ɗeret mPool, wur shínpee mPool kǝ nwur dǝm pǝ shaar fin mo, mbǝkǝ mmo ɓam wur ɗi.
ACT 27:4 Kaaɗe mǝ yool mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu dǝm shigǝng mǝ yil nSaiprus nǝ, mbǝɗe kut nǝ daampee mmun zam.
ACT 27:5 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu dǝm mu wul nkor kuur ɗe nǝn ngaar Silisiya kǝ Pamfiliya. Yaksǝ mu dǝm mu wul mMira ɗe nǝn nyil nLisiya.
ACT 27:6 A mMira nǝ, ɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon mo, kat mee tii ɗe nǝ tong Alekzandriya jì, ɗe nǝn mbǝ dǝm Itali, ɓǝ wur le mun nɗǝǝn nǝ.
ACT 27:7 Mu cìn teer mo ɗes-ɗes mun mmwaan lee-lee, nkaa am kuur nǝ, a purut-purut ɗang mǝ jì mǝ wul kus kǝ Nidus. Kaaɗe baa kut nǝ yit mmun dǝm ɗe a kyeen kas, ɓǝ mǝ waa mǝ yaa ar nǝ shigǝng mǝ yil nKrit, kus kǝ Salmone.
ACT 27:8 A purut-purut ɗang mu jì mu wul ɗi a pǝkom ɗǝǝr nǝ, ɓǝ mu jì mǝ wul mmee mpee ɗe mo kǝ pet a peekaat ɗeret, ɗe nǝ kus kǝ pee nkaam nLasiya.
ACT 27:9 Mbǝɗǝ mun mbǝ yém ɗi mpeemǝnǝ mbǝ teer mo ɗes, ɓǝ kaaɗe mǝ yaa mwaan, ɓǝ nǝ jì kǝ jeel ɗes, mbǝɗe tar mwaan nkaa am nǝ kǝ ten ɗel, ɗang nǝ aɓwoon tartong kǝ neen, ɓǝ Pool leshap nnen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn tii nǝ.
ACT 27:10 Wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Daa mo, wen nnaa mwaan fun ɗesǝ nǝn nɗen kǝ jeel, kǝ lée ɗe mun kǝ mo nɗǝǝn tii nǝ mon ntǝkook, ɗang tii mǝnǝn ntǝkook, dǝm wul kǝ seen fun mo zak.>>
ACT 27:11 Jir aasǝ baa ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon nǝ mo, leɗyeen mpwoo ɗe Pool sat kas, tǝng wur nkǝlǝng a pwoo mǝ ngutung tii nǝ ɗak, kǝ mǝ ngu tii nǝ met mbii ɗe Pool sat nwur.
ACT 27:12 Baa peeɗar mǝ tii ɗesǝ nii ret ntarkut kas, a kǝsǝ ɓǝ ɗes mǝ gurum nǝ mo ɓeet nǝ, ngyel mǝ yool aku mpeemǝnǝ, kǝ koo ɗe arang yii ɓǝ mu nwul ɗi nFoniks, ɗe nǝ a mee pee am kuur ɗeret nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nKrit, nii naa gaar ngyeen, nsar puusru, kǝ ngaar ndeng nsar puusru zak, mu hos ntarkut a mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 27:13 Kaaɗe kut nǝ ɗoom cut pee lee-lee ngaar ngyeen, ɓǝ mo pan nǝ, nǝn njì wuɗun nciit kǝ pan fur mo, ɓǝ mo dul ɓwootsǝǝp nǝ, kǝ mmo tung tii nǝ shindǝm kus kǝ pǝkom ɗǝǝr mǝ yil nKrit.
ACT 27:14 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe mo lang ɗi lee, ɓǝ mee kut ɗeɗes ɗe moo pet a Yurakium dǝ nǝ put nnar kwang ɗeng kǝ sar puus kaa nǝ cutpee jì ɗi nkaa pee nkaam nǝ.
ACT 27:15 Kaaɗe kut ɗeɗes nǝ cut tii nǝ, ɓǝ baa tii nǝ mak dǝm ngaar pee ɗe kut nǝ kǝ jì ɗe kas. Ɓǝ mu yit nkut nǝ tǝp mun shindǝm ɗi mmee ngaar ɗyik.
ACT 27:16 Mu ɗel shigǝng mǝrep mee yil ɗe am neer ciirkaat ɗe moo pet a Kauda. A purut-purut ɗang mu mak ɓwoot làa tii nǝ nkaa ɗeɗes nǝ.
ACT 27:17 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ ɗiyeep làa tii nǝ le nɗǝǝn tii ɗeɗes nǝ, ɓǝ mo ɓwoot teng shin ciir nkaa tii ɗeɗes nǝ. Mo sham kǝ nlǝr mǝ tii nǝ mo. Mbǝɗǝ mo kǝǝr nǝ, taji kut nǝ tǝp tii nǝ dǝm shweer shi pǝkom ɗyees nSirtis kas. Mo dul ɓwootsǝǝp mǝ tii nǝ kàa nɗǝǝn am nǝ kǝn mmo yit, kǝn nkut nǝ tǝp tii nǝ shindǝm ɗi.
ACT 27:18 Mbǝɗǝ kut nǝ ɗes zam, ɗang nǝ fes yoon mun ɗes zam. Daar nǝ, ɓǝ mo ɗoom kok pak lee ɗe mo nɗǝǝn tii nǝ car mɓut am.
ACT 27:19 Parpuus ɗekun nǝ zak, ɓǝ mo shikáa fur, mo kok lee tii nǝ mo car mɓut am zak.
ACT 27:20 Mu cìn teer mo ɗes, baa mu mak naa puus koo zar mo kas. Ɗee a kut ɗeɗes, kǝ tungzung mo kàa paa mun ɗak, ɗe nǝ le kǝn mmun put kǝ pǝtuup nǝ baa mun mbar kas.
ACT 27:21 Mbǝɗǝ gurum nǝ mo kǝ cìn teer mo ɗes nnen se mbiise, ɓǝ Pool yool nnaar mo, ɓǝ wur sat nǝnee, <<Daa mo, katɗang dǝ wu kǝlǝng pwoo fen, ɓǝ baa dǝ wun nyool nɗǝǝn yil nKrit, kǝn nwun shwaajeel ɗesǝ, kǝn nwun bǝlang nlée fuu mo kǝrong kas.
ACT 27:22 Mbǝmǝnǝ an pǝ sat nwun, wu yaa pǝtuup fuu mo, mbǝɗe baa mee gurum nɗǝǝn wun, mbǝ mmuut kas, a tii nǝn mpyan kash-kash ɗak.
ACT 27:23 Mbǝɗǝ dǝdoon mpar, ɓǝ mee ngulep mǝ Naan ɗe an a mǝwur, kǝ ɗe an kǝn nseyil nwur zak, wur jì woo shin nghan.
ACT 27:24 <<Ɓǝ wur sat nghan nǝnee, <Taji kǝǝrmuut yaa gha kas Pool. Nǝ a tǝng gha mbǝ ɗar ntoom kǝ Siza. A naa Naan kǝ cìn ɗeret ngha, ashak kǝ nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn tii nǝ jir. Baa mee gurum nɗǝǝn tii nǝn mmuut kas.>
ACT 27:25 Mbǝ mǝnǝ, daa mo, wu cìn retnyit. Mbǝɗǝ wen nshinzeen nNaan nǝ, mbii ɗe mo woo nghan, ɓǝ nǝn ncìn a kǝsǝ.
ACT 27:26 Ɗang jir kǝsǝ ɓǝ kut nǝn tǝp tii nǝ shweer nkaa mee yil ɗe am neer nǝ ciirkaat.>>
ACT 27:27 Nɗǝǝn teer ɗe kaapaat baafeer nǝ, ɓǝ kut nǝ tǝp mun kàa kǝ sham nɗǝǝn am kuur mǝ Adriya. Yaksǝ nnaar par, ɓǝ nen tii nǝ mo pan nǝ, muu wul kus kǝ mee yil.
ACT 27:28 Ɓǝ mo kam lu mǝ am nǝ, ɓǝ mo kat nǝ a shii mo kambil mǝndong kǝ laarvǝl (120). Kaaɗe mu gyes mu dǝm ɗi lee, ɓǝ mo cin shin kam lu mǝ am nǝ ɗe zak, ɓǝ mo kat nǝ wul a shii laarpwoofeer (90).
ACT 27:29 Mbǝ kǝǝrmuut ɗe nǝ, meesǝ, kut nǝn ndǝm shweer tii nǝ nkaa ngǝk, ɓǝ mo fwen ɓwootsǝǝp nǝ mo sham feer mɓwoon mǝ tii nǝ, mbǝkǝ ntii nǝ ɗar ɗi coot, mbǝɗe mo le pan nkaa ɓit ɗe nǝn mbǝ mang.
ACT 27:30 Nentung tii nǝ mo nkaa yap ar ɗe mon nshwe yit tii nǝ ɗi, ɓǝ mo kǝ ten shang làa tii nǝ shinsham mɓut am kuur nǝ. Mo cìn kǝsǝ a mbǝ gwam gurum mo, kǝn mmo naa ɗi nǝ, wuɗun a mbǝ fwo ɓwootsǝǝp nǝ ɗe mon mpǝkyeen mǝ tii nǝ, ɗe moo ɓwet shinsham sǝ.
ACT 27:31 Ɗangɓe Pool sat ngwe ɗeɗes mǝ shiitoon nǝ mo nǝnee, <<Katɗang ɓǝ baa nentung tii nǝ mo tong ɗi nɗǝǝn tii nǝ kas, ɓǝ wu mmurep jir.>>
ACT 27:32 Ɓǝ shiitoon mo can teng mǝ làa tii nǝ, mo yit nǝ sham taa nɗǝǝn am nǝ, yaksǝ kut mang nǝ seet kǝ nǝ.
ACT 27:33 Kaaɗe ɓit kus kǝ mang, ɓǝ Pool sat ngurum nǝ mo jir kǝ mmo se mbiise, wur sat nǝnee, <<A teer mo kaapaat baafeer nɗesǝ, ɓǝ wun pǝ tong gongpee, kǝ baa wu se mee mbiise kas.
ACT 27:34 Mbǝmǝnǝ kǝn ɗang pǝ wun, mbǝkǝ nwun se mbiise, mbǝɗe mǝnǝn nshínɓal nwun nɗǝǝn shik fuu mo. Baa mee shweepkáa mǝ mee gurum mǝndong nɗǝǝn wun nǝn nloom kas.>>
ACT 27:35 Kaaɗe Pool sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wur mang gǝǝl aas, ɓǝ wur ɗangnaan ɗe mǝ plang Naan a yit gurum nǝ mo jir, ɓǝ wur tep gǝǝl aas nǝ, ɓǝ wur yaa se nǝ.
ACT 27:36 Yaksǝ gurum nǝ mo jir mo kat retnyit, ɓǝ mo shikáa fur mo se gǝǝl aas nǝ zak.
ACT 27:37 Mun gurum ɗe mun nɗǝǝn tii nǝ jir, mu wul kambil vǝl kǝ laarpwoovǝl kǝ peemee (276).
ACT 27:38 Kaaɗe gurum mo se mbiise mo ǝɓǝl, ɓǝ mo kok aàs ɗǝɓen ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn tii nǝ, mo car shinsham mɓut am kuur nǝ, kǝn ntii nǝ pan fiyeel ɗi.
ACT 27:39 Kaaɗe ɓitmang, ɓǝ baa nentung tii nǝ mo man yil ɗe mo ɗi nǝ kas, ɓǝ mo naa mee pǝkom ɗǝǝr ɗe nǝ kǝ ɗyees, ɓǝ mo ɓeet nǝ, katɗang nǝ mak cìn, ɓǝ mo dǝm kǝ tii ɗi pǝkom nǝ.
ACT 27:40 Ɓǝ mo saa teng ɗe mo yaa ɓwootsǝǝp nǝ mo, kǝn mmo yit ɓwootsǝǝp nǝ mo mɓut am kuur nǝ, kǝn mmo fween teng ɗe moo yaa mbii ciir kǝ tii nǝ. Yaksǝ mo ɗiyeep nlǝr ɗe nǝn mpǝkyeen mǝ tii nǝ nkor ɗe kut kǝ jì ɗi, ɓǝ mo yaa ar dǝm pǝkom ɗǝǝr.
ACT 27:41 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe mu wul mmee mpee ɗe kut kǝ cut am nǝ jì kaat ɗi, ɓǝ tii nǝ ɗel shamru mɓut ɗiyees, ɗe baa nǝ kutɗi kǝ tungpee kas, ɓǝ koor mɓwoon mǝ tii nǝ ɗoom pyan, mbǝ ɓal mǝ kut ɗe nii cut nǝ.
ACT 27:42 Yaksǝ shiitoon nǝ mo ɓeetpwoo, mbǝ twe nen ɗe mo a ɓuɓwoot jir, mbǝkǝ taji mo cut lung, kǝ mo dǝm loom ɗi kas.
ACT 27:43 Ɗangɓǝ ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa shiitoon nǝ mo, kǝ reɓet ɓam Pool, ɓǝ wur cíi mmo. Wur le kǝ nnen ɗe mo man lung jir, mo mǝrep sham mɓut am nǝ, kǝn mmo taa lung dǝm wul ɗe a pwoo ɗǝǝr.
ACT 27:44 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ koor gurum nǝ mo mǝrep sham taa nkaa shiyeep mo, kǝ pak mo nkaa yoom mǝ tii ɗe nǝ pyan nǝ zak.
ACT 28:1 Aɓwoon ɗe mu wul nɗǝǝn yil nǝ nkoom jir, ɓǝ mu kǝlǝng nǝ, moo pet sǝm yil ɗe am neer nǝ cǝǝrkaat a Malta.
ACT 28:2 Nenyil nǝ mo kaat mun jir, kǝzak mo ɓam mun zam, ɓǝ mo ɓil wus mmun, mbǝɗe fwan nkaa jì, kǝ pee zuum zak.
ACT 28:3 Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe Pool kok yoom le nwus, ɓǝ mbǝ tal mǝ wus nǝ, ɓǝ mee nwòo ɗe sǝm nǝ a pang, nǝ pus sar mPool, ɗang nǝ ɗyiin nkaa sar wur.
ACT 28:4 Kaaɗe nenyil nǝ mo naa nwòo ɗesǝ nii ɗyiin mPool nkaa sar, ɓǝ mo sat nshak nǝnee, <<Azeen-zeen gwar ɗesǝ wur a ngutukáa, koo ɗewur kǝ put mɓut njeel mǝ am kuur nǝ, ɓǝ baa kwat mǝ shikbish nǝ mak yit wur ɗe mmeen kas.>>
ACT 28:5 Ɓǝ Pool vwet nwòo nǝ sham taa nwus. Mbǝɗǝ nwòo ɗe nǝ pus wur nǝ, ɓǝ baa nǝ cìn mee mbii nwur kas.
ACT 28:6 Nenyil nǝ mo pan nǝ, yak mon nnaa Pool wup, koo mo nnaa wur taa nyil muut. Ɗangɓǝ kaaɗe mo tong naapee, ɓǝ baa mo naa mee mbii cìn Pool kas, ɓǝ mo waa sheepwoo ɗe, mo sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗesǝ wur a mee naan.>>
ACT 28:7 Kus kǝ peemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mee maar mǝ Pubiliyus ngwe ɗeɗes nkaa yil ɗe am neer cǝǝrkaat nǝ, wur kaat mun le nlu fin mbǝ teer mo kun, ɗang wur tap kǝ mun, wur cìn ɗeret mmun zam.
ACT 28:8 Puun mǝ Pubiliyus, baa wur nkoom kas, wur a peesaam kǝ shikshwal, kǝ ɗyestoom zak. Pool ɗel pǝ ngunan nǝ ɗi, ɓǝ wur ɗangnaan ɓǝ wur lesar fin nkaa ngunan nǝ, ɓǝ ngunan nǝ bar.
ACT 28:9 Kaaɗe Pool cìn mǝnǝ, ɓǝ koor nengok ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil ɗe am neer cǝǝrkaat nǝ, mo jì jir, mbǝkǝ mPool bar mo ɗi.
ACT 28:10 Nenyil nǝ mo shin zuum mo mmun ɗes, ɗang kaaɗe mun mbǝ ɗel nɗǝǝn tii nǝ mbǝ seet, ɓǝ mo shin mbii ɗe mon mɓam mun a ar mwaan nǝ jir zak.
ACT 28:11 Aɓwoon tar mo kun, ɓǝ mǝ yool nɗǝǝn mee tii ɗe nǝ tong a Alekzandriya jì, ɗe nii hos ntarkut nɗǝǝn yil ɗe am neer cǝǝrkaat sǝ. tii ɗesǝ nǝ kǝ sǝmpwoo (alaama) mǝ káa Jan ɗemish mo nkaa nǝ, ɗe mo a Kasto, kǝ Pollukus, mee naan mǝ mo, nǝ mo.
ACT 28:12 Mu jì mǝ wul nSirakus, ɓǝ mu cìn teer mo kun ɗi, mpee mǝnǝ.
ACT 28:13 Kaaɗe mu yool mpee mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mu jì mu wul nRegiyum. Mu teer mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mee kut yool nkor ngyeen, ɓǝ ɗaar nǝ, ɓǝ mu dǝm mu wul mPutiyoli.
ACT 28:14 Mu kat nenseet nɗang Jesu mo mpeemǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo ɗang mun kǝn mmun cìn teer mo pwoovǝl ɗi ashak kǝ mo. A mwaan fun nǝ mmǝnǝ, ɗee mu dǝm mu wul nRom.
ACT 28:15 Kaaɗe nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗe mon mpee nkaam nRom, mo kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mun, ɓǝ mo pwat jì mbǝ kaat mun, ɓǝ mo jì wul mpeepring Apiyus, kǝ pee ɗe lumǝzep mo ɗekun. Kaaɗe Pool naa mo, ɓǝ wur plang Naan, ɗang pǝtuup wur nǝ sǝǝt katɓal.
ACT 28:16 Kaaɗe mu jì mu wul nɗǝǝn pee nkaam nRom, ɓǝ mo shínpee mPool tong ɗi mbǝshin mpee ɗewur rǝɓet, ashak kǝ shiitoon ɗewur kǝ tap Pool.
ACT 28:17 Aɓwoon teer mo kun, ɓǝ Pool pǝrep nen ɗenan-nan mǝ nnen Yahudi mo. Kaaɗe mo kuur ashak, ɓǝ wur sat mmo nǝnee, <<Ɗyemnaa mo, baa kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish nnen fun mo kas. Koo a nkaa mǝse mǝ wàar puun fun mo, ɓǝ baa kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas, jir kǝsǝ, ɓǝ mo yaa an shin nnen Rom mo a ɓuɓwoot nɗǝǝn yil nJerusalem.
ACT 28:18 Kaaɗe nnen Rom mo tokɗyeel nghan, ɓǝ mo rǝɓet ɓwet an, mbǝɗe baa kǝn cìn mee mbii ɗebish ɗe nǝ mak kǝ mmo tu an kas.
ACT 28:19 Ɗangɓǝ baa nnen Yahudi mo rǝɓet kǝ mmo ɓwet an kas, ɓǝ nǝ ɗee nghan a tǝng kǝn nghan ɗang nǝ, mo jì kǝ ɗyeel fen nǝ pǝ Siza ɗi. Baa nǝ, kǝn rǝɓet yap a nen fun mo kǝ ɗyeel kas.
ACT 28:20 A mbǝ pwoo ɗesǝ, ɓǝ wen nyappee ɗe an nnaa wun ɗi, mbǝkǝ wen leshap ɗi kǝ wun, mbǝɗe a mbǝ canciin ɗe nnen Isreil mo kǝ nǝ, ɗang an ɗi a ɓuɓwoot shi shoolbǝring ɗesǝ.>>
ACT 28:21 Mo sat nwur nǝnee, <<Baa mmun muu kat mee lep a rǝran nyil Judiya nkaa gha kas. Kǝzak baa mee ɗyemnǝǝn fun mo jì mpee ɗesǝ, kǝn mmo satpwoo ɗi mmun nkaa gha, koo mo sat mee pwoo mmun nkaa mbii ɗebish ɗe a cìn mo kas zak.
ACT 28:22 Ɗangɓǝ mu rǝɓet kǝlǝng nǝ mpwoo fwaa mbii ɗe gha naa nǝ ret, mbǝɗe katɗang a pwoo nkaa Ar ɗesǝ nǝ, ɓǝ mu man nǝ, koo a nii, ɓǝ mo nkaa leshap ɗebish nkaa nǝ.>>
ACT 28:23 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓǝ mo lepuus. Ɓǝ kaaɗe puus nǝ wul, ɓǝ gurum mo ɗes mo jì pǝ Pool ɗi a pee ɗewur kǝ tong ɗi. Yool mbít, dǝm wul nkansǝǝn, ɓǝ Pool kámshii mǝ mulki mǝ Naan nǝ ngurum mo, ɗang wur tong a langtǝng nkaa nǝ zak. Wur rǝɓet dul mo jì pǝ Jesu ɗi, shi kám mǝ Wàar mǝ Mosis, kǝ shi kám mǝ nensatpwoo mǝ Naan mo zak.
ACT 28:24 Pak gurum nǝ mo shinzeen mpwoo ɗewur sat nǝ, ɗang baa pak mo shinzeen kas.
ACT 28:25 Kaaɗe baa mo kǝlǝngkar nǝ ashak jir kas, ɓǝ akuɗang moo rangkáa, ɓǝ Pool sat mee pwoo mmo mǝndong, nǝnee, <<Azeen-zeen pwoo ɗe gyet Riin Ɗeɓang wur kǝ sat mpuun fuu mo nsar kǝ ngusat pwoo Naan Aizaya nǝnee,
ACT 28:26 <A dǝm pǝ nnen ɗesǝ mo ɗi, kǝn nghan sat mmo nǝnee, wun nsat a kǝlǝngpee, ɗang baa wun mmanshii mǝ mbii ɗe wun kǝlǝng nǝ kas koo dǝɓen. Wun nsat a nnaapee ɗak, ɗang baa wun mmanshii mǝ mbii ɗe wuu naa nǝ kas koo dǝɓen.
ACT 28:27 Mbǝɗǝ pǝtuup mǝ nnen ɗesǝ nǝ mo fii ɗee kakras. Mo kǝ duur kom fur mo, ɗang mo kǝ kup ar fur mo zak. Mbǝkǝ taji mo naapee shi yit fur mo, kǝ taji mo kǝlǝngpee shi kom fur mo zak, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ taji mo manshii nǝ nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo. Kǝn mmo ciir pǝ an ɗi, ɓǝ yool an ɓam mo.>
ACT 28:28 <<Mbǝ mǝnǝ, ɓǝ wen nrǝɓǝt kǝ nwun man nǝ, mo kǝ lep pwoo nkaa ɓam mǝ Naan nǝ shindǝm nnen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Yaksǝ mon nlekom mbǝ pwoo nǝ, ɓǝ mon nkǝlǝng.>>
ACT 28:29 Kaaɗe Pool leshap ɗesǝ mmo, ɓǝ nnen Yahudi mo rangkáa, kǝ mon nkaa ɓeetpwoo nǝ kǝ shak.
ACT 28:30 Pool tong nɗǝǝn lu ɗe a wur kwat shikáa fin, mbǝ ɓit mo vǝl. Wur kǝ kaat nen ɗe mo jì pǝ wur ɗi jir.
ACT 28:31 Wur leshap ngurum mo nkaa mulki mǝ Naan nǝ, baa ashak kǝ mee kǝǝrmuut kas, kǝ baa mee ngwe cíi nwur kas, kǝzak, wur kámpwoo ngurum mo nkaa Daa Jesu Kristi.
1CO 1:1 Lepran ɗǝsǝ nǝ put a nsar kǝ Pool, ɗe shi ɗem Naan, ɓe Naan pet wur kǝ wur ɗee a laalep mǝ Kristi Jesu, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun Sosfenes.
1CO 1:2 Wen kǝn lep pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ dǝm pee Ekǝlisya mǝ Naan ɗe nǝ nyil nKoronti. Nen ɗe Naan kǝ ten bǝlǝp mo le, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗi a nen fir mo ndǝǝn Jesu Kristi, kǝ mpee nen ɗi koo a nneye, ɗe moo pet sǝm kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi ɗewur a Daa fur kǝ Daa fun zak.
1CO 1:3 Ɗeret kǝ tongryang ɗe nǝ put a pee Naan puun kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi nǝ tong ashak kǝ wun.
1CO 1:4 Wen pǝlang Naan shidaar-shidaar mɓe wun, mɓeɗǝ Naan wur cin ɗeret wun ndǝǝn Kristi Jesu.
1CO 1:5 nƊǝǝn Jesu Kristi, ɓe Naan wu kǝ shin man mbii mo wun, kǝ man leshap rǝret ɗes hakyeng.
1CO 1:6 Mbǝɗe langtǝng fun nkaa Kristi nǝ ɗee azeen-nzeen ndǝǝn wun.
1CO 1:7 Mɓemǝnǝ, ɓe baa wu nook kat mee zuum ɗe nǝ a mǝ Riin Naan kas, kaaɗe wuu choor mɓe kum parpuus ɗi Daa fun Jesu Kristi wun njì put agaak.
1CO 1:8 Wur nwaa shin ɓal nwun har peekyes nǝ, mbǝkǝ wu ɗee ɗi a ɗe ndǝre-ndǝre parpuus mǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi.
1CO 1:9 Naan ɗewur kǝ ten pǝrep wun, kǝ wu ɗee ɗi a nentong ashak kǝ Làa fir Jesu Kristi, Daa fun, wur a nguzeen.
1CO 1:10 Ɗyemnaa mo, wen ɗang pee wun, ndǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi, nee, nǝ ret kǝ pwoo fuu mo dǝm ndangshak, mbǝkǝ taji mee ɓàkshak yool nnaar fuu kas. Ɗangɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu ɗee a ɗemǝndong ndǝǝn pan fuu mo kǝ ndǝǝn mbii ɗe wu rǝɓet cìn mo.
1CO 1:11 Ɗyemnaa mo, nentul kǝ Klo mo jì sat wen nǝ, ɓǝlep kǝ yool nnaar fuu.
1CO 1:12 Mbii ɗe mo sat nǝ a nǝ, koo a weye ndǝǝn wun, ɓe wur sat mbii mo shini-shini, pak moo sat nǝnee, <<Wen a mǝ Pool,>> Koo <<wen a mǝ Apolos,>> Koo, <<wen a mǝ Kefas,>> Koo, <<wen a mǝ Kristi.>>
1CO 1:13 Kristi wur ɗee a ɗeɓǝɓak ee? Gyet mo pwas a Pool nkaa shiyeepyoom mbǝ wun aa? Aa koo gyet mo cìn baptisma nwun a ndǝǝn sǝm kǝ Pool yii?
1CO 1:14 Wen pǝlang Naan, mɓeɗǝ baa gyet wen cìn baptisma memee fuu kas, tǝng a Krispus kǝ Gayus ɓejee ɗak.
1CO 1:15 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe baa mee fuu mmak sat nǝ, gyet mo cìn baptisma wuɗin a ndǝǝn sǝm fen kas.
1CO 1:16 (Ɗangɓe gyet wen cìn baptisma nentul Stifenas mo. Katɗang baa a mo kas, ɓe baa wen pan nǝ, gyet Wen cìn baptisma mmee gwe kas.)
1CO 1:17 Baa gyet Kristi wur lep wen a mbǝkǝ wen cìn baptisma ɗi kas, amma gyet wur lep an, a mbǝkǝ wen satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗi, baa a shi mee seen kǝ man satpwoo kas. Mbeekǝ taji mo leɓal mǝ shiyeepmúut kǝ Kristi nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu kas.
1CO 1:18 Pee nenyil ɗi mo nkaa loom, ɓe pwoo nkaa shiyeep nǝ a pwoo ɗebuu pee mo ɗi. Ɗangɓe pee mun, nen ɗe muu kat seen, ɓe shiyeep nǝ a iiko Naan.
1CO 1:19 Mbǝɗe mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Wen nshirip seen nenseen mo, kǝ nghan mmang man kǝ nenman mo nle mmee kwang akuɗang.>>
1CO 1:20 Katɗang nǝ a kǝsǝ, ɓe nguseen nǝ a nneyii? Ɓe nguman mbii a nneyii? Ɓe nguɓeetshik mɓut mɓít ɗǝsǝ a nneyii? Naan wu kǝ ten shin ciir kǝ nenseen mǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a mwen mo.
1CO 1:21 Mɓǝɗǝ ndǝǝn seen kǝ Naan, ɓe yil nǝ shi seen kǝ nǝ, baa nǝ man Naan kas. Ɗangɓe nǝ ret Naan nyit mɓe pwoo ɗeret ɗi mǝ sat nǝ, ɗe pak nenkǝlengpwoo mo, ɓe moo sat nǝ, nǝ a pwoo mwen mo. Ɗangɓe nǝ a ɓam mpee nen ɗe mo shinzeen.
1CO 1:22 Nen Yahudi moo tang mbii aapwoo mo, kǝ nen Heleni moo tang a seen.
1CO 1:23 Ɗangɓe mun, muu sat a pwoo nkaa Kristi ɗe mo pwas wur nkaa shiyeepyoom. Ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a mbii canshii nen Yahudi mo, kǝ nǝ ɗee a pwoo mwen pee nen ɗi baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas.
1CO 1:24 Ɗangɓe pee nen ɗe Naan kǝ ten pǝrep mo, koo a nen Yahudi mo, koo a nen Heleni mo, ɓe Kristi wur a iiko mǝ Naan kǝ seen fir zak.
1CO 1:25 Mbǝɗe mwen Naan nǝ met nseen gurum mo, kǝ ɓwàar kǝ Naan nǝ kǝ ɓal met ɓal mǝ gurum mo.
1CO 1:26 Ɗyemnaa mo, wu pan kaaɗe Naan wur pǝrep wun sǝ. Baa gyet wur pǝrep a nen ɗe moo seen mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ ɗes kas, kǝ baa gyet a nen ɗe mo kǝ iiko ɗes kas. Baa a nen ɗe gyet mo làa mo mɓut nɗang mǝ nenlong mo ɗes kas.
1CO 1:27 Ɗangɓe Naan wur bǝlǝp a mbii ɗemwen mǝ yil nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ wur cin yitlwaan ɗi nenseen mǝ yil nǝ mo. Naan wur bǝlǝp mbii ɗe baa mo kǝ ɓal ndǝǝn yil nǝ kas, mbǝkǝ mo shweep mbii ɗe moo ɓal mo ɗi.
1CO 1:28 Naan wur bǝlǝp a mbii ɗe yil nǝ ɓees, kǝ yil nii naa mo a kaa mbii ɗebuu mo sǝ, har kaa mbii ɗi baa mo ɗi kas sǝ, mbǝkǝ nǝ twe mbii ɗe yil nii naa mo, a kaa mbii ɗe moo koop nǝ sǝ ɗe.
1CO 1:29 Mbeekǝ taji mee gwe canjoom nyit Naan kas.
1CO 1:30 Ɗangɓe Naan wur jì kǝ wun ndǝǝn Kristi Jesu, kǝ wur le Jesu Kristi a seen fun, kǝ ɗeret fun, kǝ a mɓee wur ɗangɓe wu mak ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit Naan, kǝ a wurang mun mɓut shikbish fun mo zak.
1CO 1:31 Nǝ a kaa ɗe mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Koo a weyii ɗe wur canjoom, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur canjoom nǝ ndǝǝn ɓe ɗe Daa Naan Cin.>>
1CO 2:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, kaaɗe gyet wen jì pee wun ɗe, ɓe baa gyet wen satpwoo nwun nkaa mbii ɗesǝsok mǝ Naan nǝ mo a shi liispwoo ɗeshang kǝleng, kǝ man satpwoo mǝ seen kas.
1CO 2:2 Mɓǝɗǝ, kaaɗe gyet wen ashak kǝ wun, ɓe gyet wen kǝ ten lesen a kaa gwe ɗi baa wur man mǝ ɓe kas, a Jesu Kristi ɓejee, ɗe mo kǝ pwas wur nkaa shiyeepyoom sǝ.
1CO 2:3 Gyet wen ashak kǝ wun, ɓe wen a ndǝǝn cíinɓal, kǝ ndǝǝn kǝǝrmuut kǝ ɗaar zak.
1CO 2:4 Kǝ gyet pwoo ɗe wen kǝn sat nǝ, kǝ kám fen nǝ mo, baa gyet wen kǝn sat mo a shi pwoo ɗeshang kǝlǝng kǝ seen mǝ man satpwoo kas, amma gyet nǝ a ndǝǝn kám mǝ iiko kǝ Riin.
1CO 2:5 Mbeekǝ taji wu le shinzeen fuu mo tong a ndǝǝn seen mǝ gurum mo kas, amma wu le shinzeen fuu mo a ndǝǝn iiko kǝ Naan.
1CO 2:6 Ɗangɓe muu sat a pwoo ɗi mǝ man, pee nen ɗe mo kǝ wurang ndǝǝn mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Riin Naan. Baa man ɗǝsǝ nǝ a mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ kas, kǝ baa nǝ put a pee nen mulki mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ mo, ɗe mo mbǝ ɗel dǝm sǝ kas.
1CO 2:7 Ɗangɓe mun muu sat a pwoo nkaa man Naan ɗe nǝ a sǝsok ngurum mo, man ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten le mbe ɗeɗes fun akuɗang wur leyil nǝ.
1CO 2:8 Baa mee ngu mulki mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ mmak man mǝnǝ kas. Katɗang ɗe gyet moo man mǝni, ɓe baa gyet mon mpwas Daa ɗe hai nkaa shiyeepyoom kas.
1CO 2:9 Kaaɗǝ mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal sǝ nǝnee, <<Mbii ɗi baa gurum kǝ cham naa kǝ yit kas, <<ɗe baa gurum kǝ cham kǝlǝng nǝ shi kom kas, <<ɗe baa pǝtuup gurum kǝ cham pan <<mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ tap ɗak nǝ le, <<nen ɗe mo wal nwur mo kas.>>
1CO 2:10 Ɗangɓe Naan wur kámshii mǝnǝ mmun a shi Riin fir, mɓeɗǝ Riin wur bǝlǝp mbii mo jir, har koo ɗi a jurum kǝ mbii aapwoo mǝ Naan mo.
1CO 2:11 A gurum ɗeɗang mmak man pan kǝ mee gwe yii? Katɗang baa a riin kǝ gwe nǝ kas yii? Nǝ aasǝ zak, baa mee ngwar cham man pan Naan kas, naa tǝng a Riin Naan ɓejee ɗak.
1CO 2:12 Baa mun mu kat a riin mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ kas, amma mǝ lap a Riin Naan, mbǝkǝ mu manshii kǝ mbii ɗe Naan wur ten shìn mmun ɗe.
1CO 2:13 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, pwoo ɗe muu sat nwun, baa nǝ put a mɓut mman mǝ gurum kas, amma a Riin wur woo nǝ mmun. Riin nǝ wur woo zeen, mbe nen ɗe mo kǝ Riin Naan ndǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo.
1CO 2:14 Ngwar ɗi baa wu kǝ Riin kǝ Naan ndǝǝn pǝtuup fin kas, ɓe baa wur mak lap zuum ɗe mo a mǝ Riin Naan kas. Mɓǝɗǝ mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Riin Naan, mo a pwoo ɗebuu pee gwe mǝnǝ ɗi, kǝzak, baa pan kǝ gwe mǝnǝ mak manshii mo nǝ kas, mɓeɗǝ a Riin Naan kǝ mak le gurum man mbii ɗǝsǝ nǝ mo.
1CO 2:15 Ngwe ɗewur kǝ Riin Naan ndǝǝn pǝtuup fir, ɓe wur mak manshii mbii ɗǝsǝ nǝ mo, amma baa mee gurum mak tokɗyeel nwur kas.
1CO 2:16 Kaaɗǝ mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<A wii kǝ man pan Daa yii? Mbeekǝ gwe mǝnǝ ɓeetpwoo ɗe kǝ wur yii?>> amma mun kǝ pǝtuup mǝ Kristi.
1CO 3:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, baa wen mak leshap kǝ wun kaa nen ɗe mo kǝ Riin Naan sǝ kas, ɗangɓe Wen katpwoo kǝ wun a kaa nen ɗi mǝ yil nǝ mo sǝ, mɓeɗǝ gyet wun a laa njuu mo ndǝǝn mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Kristi.
1CO 3:2 Gyet wen kǝn shin a wur nwun. Baa gyet a mbiise ɗeɓal kas, mɓeɗǝ baa gyet wu mak se mbiise ɗeɓal kas, har yaksǝ ɓe baa wuu ɗaksuk mɓe se mbiise ɗeɓal nǝ kas.
1CO 3:3 Tong fuu, nǝ ɗe a mǝ yil ɗǝsǝ, mɓeɗǝ wun kǝ cìn zuur, kǝ wuu jǝǝr kǝ shak. Kiyeet kǝ tong ɗesǝ kám nǝ, wun ɗe a mǝ yil nǝ, kǝ wuu mwaan a ndǝǝn shiimwaan mǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ.
1CO 3:4 Katɗang memee fuu sat nǝ, wuɗin a mǝ Pool, kǝ memee sat nǝ, wuɗin a mǝ Apolos, ɗang ntan azeen-nzeen ɓe wuu sat mbii mǝnǝ mo a ndǝǝn pan mǝ gurum kas aa?
1CO 3:5 A wii a Apolos yii? A wii a Pool yii? Mun a kǝrem Naan, ɗe Naan wur shìn ɗak mun kǝ har wu shinzeen. Koo ɗang a weyi ndǝǝn mun, ɓe gyet muu cìn a mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten le nsar fun.
1CO 3:6 A an kop, ɗangɓe Apolos wur le am ɗike, amma a Naan wur le nǝ wurang.
1CO 3:7 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe gwe ɗewur kop mbii, kǝ gwe ɗewur le am ɗike, ɓe baa mo a mee mbii kas, amma a Naan bǝshin wur kǝ le mbii nǝ mo wurang.
1CO 3:8 Ngwe ɗe wur kop, kǝ gwe ɗewur le am ɗikǝ, ɓe mo a nchiit-nchiit. Koo a weyi ɓe wur nlap kwat fir a nchiit-nchiit kǝ ɗak ɗe gwe nǝ cìn.
1CO 3:9 Mun jir a shaar ɗak kǝ Naan. Wun a bong kǝ Naan, kǝ wun a lu kǝ Naan.
1CO 3:10 Shi ɗeret ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten shin nǝ wen, ɓe wen kǝn ɓwet kuklu nǝ, a kaa nguman ɗyiklu sǝ, kǝ mee gwe ɗyiklu nkaa kuk nǝ. Ɗangɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ koo a weyi, ɓe wur tap kǝ ɗyikpee ɗe wur ɗyik nǝ nkaa kuk nǝ.
1CO 3:11 Baa mee kuk ɗi, ɗe mee gurum nwaa baa ɓwet ɗi, waa met kuk ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten ɓwet nǝ, shi Jesu Kristi kas.
1CO 3:12 Yaksǝ, katɗang mee gwe kǝ ɗyikpee nkaa kuk nǝ a shi zinariya, koo shi azurfa, koo shi ghǝk ɗekǝrǝm mo, koo shi yoom, koo shi shit, koo shi yangkas,
1CO 3:13 ɓe nǝ ret kǝ ngwar mǝnǝ man nǝ, ret kǝ ɗak fir nǝn nɗee agaak parpuus ɗe Daa Jesu wur mbaajì ndǝǝn yil ɗesǝ. Parpuus mǝnǝ ɓe mon nwoo ɗak kǝ koo a ngwar ɗeɗangyii, har a wus ncham ret mǝ ɗak kǝ koo weyii.
1CO 3:14 Katɗang baa wus se mbii ɗe gurum kǝ ten ɗyik nkaa kuk nǝ kas, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ nlap kwat.
1CO 3:15 Ɗangɓe katɗang wus se mbii ɗe gurum kǝ ten cìn nǝ, ɓe nǝn nɗee a ɗak ɗebuu, amma gwar mǝnǝ shikáa fir, ɓe wur nkat ɓam wur, amma nǝ ɗee kaa wu ɗel put wus nǝ a shi tambut sǝ.
1CO 3:16 Baa wu man nǝ, wun shikáa fuu wun a lu ɗǝǝɗes kǝ Daa Naan kas aa? Kǝ Riin kǝ Naan kǝ tong ndǝǝn wun kas aa?
1CO 3:17 Katɗang mee ngwar tǝkook lu kǝ Naan nǝ, ɓe Naan wun tǝkook gwar mǝnǝ zak. Mɓeɗǝ lu kǝ Naan nǝ a ɗeɓang kǝ a wuwun a lu kǝ Naan nǝ.
1CO 3:18 Taji mee gurum numkáa fir kas, katɗang mee gurum ndǝǝn wun ɗi wu kǝ lekáa fir a kaa ngwar ɗi kǝ seen nyìcinsǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ gwar mǝnǝ lekáa fir kaa mwen sǝ, mbǝkǝ wur kat seen ɗi.
1CO 3:19 Mɓeɗi seen mǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ a mwen nyit Naan ɓejee, kaaɗe mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Naan wur yak nenseen mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo, nɗǝǝn seen fur ɗebish.>>
1CO 3:20 Kǝzak, <<Daa wur man nǝnee, <<pan kǝ nenseen mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo nǝ a mbii ɗebuu.>>
1CO 3:21 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe taji mee gurum canjoom nkaa gurum mo kas. Mɓeɗi mbii mo jir a muu.
1CO 3:22 Koo ɗang ɗe a Pool, koo a Apolos, koo a Kefas, koo ɗe a yil ɗesǝ, koo ɗe a seen, koo ɗe a muut, koo ɗe a yaksǝ, koo ɗe a mbii ɗe mo akyeen, ɓe mo jir a muu.
1CO 3:23 Kǝzak, wun a mǝ Kristi, kǝ Kristi wur a mǝ Naan.
1CO 4:1 Nǝ ret kǝ gurum mo man mun a kaa jeplep kǝ Kristi mo sǝ, kǝ kaa nenɗak mo, ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten le zeen mbii fir ɗesǝsok mo ndǝǝn sar fun sǝ.
1CO 4:2 Nǝ a tǝng nen ɗe mo kǝ ten le zeen nǝ nsar fur, ɓe mo ɗee a nenyil ɗe mon ncínzeen mmo.
1CO 4:3 Baa nǝ daampee wen kas koo dǝɓen, katɗang wu cham an, koo ɗe cham nǝ a nluɗyeel mǝ gurum mo, baa wen kǝn tokɗyeel nsen kas.
1CO 4:4 Wen man nǝ, baa an ɗel ɗike kas, amma jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa nǝ kám nǝ wen a nen nshikbish kas. A Daa wur a gwe ɗe wur tokɗyeel wen.
1CO 4:5 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe, taji wu canɗyeel nkaa mee gurum kas, atǝng pee nǝ wul akuɗang. Wu gong waaji nDaa. Daa wur njì le mbii ɗe mo a sǝsok mo ɗee agaak, kǝ wur nwang pan ɗe mo ndǝǝn pǝtuup kǝ gurum mo ɗee agaak zak. A nchiit kǝ mǝnǝ ɓe koo a weyii, ɓe Naan wun nkwoop wur nchiit-nchiit kǝ kwoop ɗe nǝ ret kǝ wu kat.
1CO 4:6 Yaksǝ ɗyemnaa mo, wen kǝn sat sǝmpwoo ɗǝsǝ mo nkaa Apolos kǝ sen fen, mbǝkǝ mu ɗee ɗi a mbiikám pee wun ɗi, <<Taji wu cìn mbii mo met mbii ɗi mo kǝ ten ran nǝ kas,>> Kǝ taji memee fuu cìn roop nkaa mee gurum, kǝ wur ɓees mee gurum ɗi kas zak.
1CO 4:7 A wii le waa met niyee mo yii? Baa dǝ a Naan shin mbii ɗe waa kǝ mo jir kas aa? Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe a me le ɗang gha kǝ ɗyeepkáa ye, kaa baají waa lǝlap a nzuum sǝ kas sǝ aa?
1CO 4:8 Wuu ten wu kat mbii ɗe wuu Rǝɓet mo jir. Wuu ten wu ɗee a nenlong mo. Wuu ɗee a mishkoom mo, baa ashak kǝ mun kas. Ɗyen wen kǝ ɗe wuu ten wu ɗee a mishkoom mo, kǝ mun ɗee ɗi a mishkoom ashak kǝ wun.
1CO 4:9 Nnaa mǝnǝ, ɓe Naan wu kǝ le mun a jeplep Jesu mo. Muu ɗee a nen ɗe mo tong sham sǝǝt nǝ, kaa nen ɗe mo kǝ ten canɗyeel muut mmo sǝ, mbǝkǝ mo twe mun ɗi nyit gurum mo ɗes. Mu ɗee a mbiishwar nyil nǝ jir, nyit mǝ Nenlep Naan mo, kǝ nyit gurum mo zak.
1CO 4:10 Mu ɗee a mwen mo mɓe sǝm kǝ Kristi, amma wun a nenseen mo ndǝǝn Kristi. Baa mun kǝ ɓal kas, amma wun kǝ ɓal. Gurum mo shìn ɗeɗes nwun, amma mo ɓees mun.
1CO 4:11 Har yaksǝ ɓe neen kǝ láa mmun, kǝ neen am kǝ tu mun. Muu jwal a goklee mo, kǝ gurum moo nas mun. Baa mun kǝ mee tul kas.
1CO 4:12 Muu cìn ɗak ɓalɓal shi sar fun mo. Katɗang gurum mo ɓees mun, ɓe muu le ɗeret nkaa mo. Katɗang mo lejeel mmun, ɓe muu gung.
1CO 4:13 Katɗang mo satpwoo ɗebish nkaa mun, ɓe muu lap mmo shi pwoo ɗeret. Yaksǝ, ɓe mo ɗee a kaa zungtung ɗi gurum moo ɓeerpee ɗe sǝ. Muu ɗee a mbii ɗebish ɗe koo weyii kǝ cii mun ndǝǝn yil nǝ.
1CO 4:14 Wen kǝn ran ɗesǝ nwun, baa a mbǝkǝ an cin yitluwaan ɗi nwun kas, amma a mbǝkǝ nghan kámshii nǝ ɗi nwun, kaa jep fen ɗi nghan wal mmo sǝ.
1CO 4:15 Koo ɗang ɗi wun kǝ nenkám mo ngal kaapaat ndǝǝn Kristi, amma ɓe wun kǝ puun a mǝndong. Mɓǝɗǝ ndǝǝn Jesu Kristi, ɓe wen kǝn ɗee a puun fuu ndǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ.
1CO 4:16 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɓe Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ wun, kǝ wu mwaan ndǝǝn shiimwaan fen zak.
1CO 4:17 A mbii ɗe nǝ le mmǝnǝ, ɗangɓe Wen kǝn lep Timoti, ɗyem fen, ɗe wen wal nwur, ɗe wur kǝ ɗar ɓalɓal ndǝǝn Daa, dǝm pee wun ɗǝ. Wur yee nwun nkaa mwaan fen ndǝǝn Kristi Jesu. Mwaan fen nǝ nchiit-nchiit kǝ mbii ɗi Wen kǝn kám ngurum mo, koo a nneye ndǝǝn Ekǝlisya mo.
1CO 4:18 Pak mo ndǝǝn wun, moo roop kaa baa wen nkuɗi kǝn mbaadǝm pee wun ɗi kas sǝ.
1CO 4:19 Katɗang Daa wur rǝɓet, kǝ wen dǝm pee wun ɗi kǝlak-kǝlak, ɓe wen nnaa mbii ɗe nenroop nǝ moo sat, kǝ wen nnaa iiko ɗe mo kǝ nǝ zak.
1CO 4:20 Baa mulki Naan nǝ a sat shi pwoo kas, amma nǝ a iiko.
1CO 4:21 Wu rǝɓet a ɗeɗangyii? Kyet wen njì pee wun ɗi a shi mbwat wo? Koo ɗang a shi wal mǝ riin ɗe nǝ a pǝɗok yii?
1CO 5:1 Azeen gurum moo sat nwen nǝ nencìn ngaa mo ɗi nnaar fuu, kaan ngaa ɗe koo a nenkum mo, ɓe baa moo cìn mǝnǝ kas. Mɓeɗi wen kǝlǝng nǝ, laa kǝ saam kǝ mat kǝ puun fin.
1CO 5:2 Har nnǝ, wuu cìn roop kǝ mǝnǝ. Baa ɗi nǝ ret kǝ wu gam aa wat pǝtuup, kǝ ɗi nǝ ret kǝ wu ceen kaan nen ɗe moo cìn mbii ɗebish mǝnǝ mo ndǝǝn tong ashak fuu kas aa?
1CO 5:3 Koo ɗang ɗi baa nghan ashak kǝ wun mɓut nan kas, amma wen ɗi ashak kǝ wun ndǝǝn Riin, kǝ wen kǝn ten canɗyeel ɗebish gwe ɗi wu cìn mbii ɗebish mǝnǝ nɗeen sǝm kǝ Jesu Kristi, kaa nghan ɗi ashak kǝ wun sǝ.
1CO 5:4 Katɗang wu kuur ashak ndǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa Jesu, ɓe wen ɗi ashak kǝ wun ndǝǝn riin, kǝ iiko mǝ Daa fun Jesu nǝ ɗi ashak kǝ mun.
1CO 5:5 Wu shin ngucìn ngaa nǝ nsar Shetan, mbǝkǝ shin fin ɗi nǝ a mǝ cìn shikbish nǝ muut ɗi, amma riin fir nǝ ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓǝɓam parpuus mǝ Daa Jesu.
1CO 5:6 Baa roop fuu nǝ ret kas, koo dǝɓen. Baa wu man nǝ a rep yist nlee ɓe nii fuk gǝǝl aas kas aa?
1CO 5:7 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe wu pwat kǝ yist ɗesǝǝr mǝ shikbish nǝ ndǝǝn tong fuu mo aku mbǝkǝ wu ɗee ɗi a nenyil ɗeɓang mo. Gyet Jesu Kristi wu muut a mbǝ shikbish fun mo, a wu a Laatǝm mǝ Retnyit kǝ Canɗel fun, ɗe mo kǝ ten shin wur a mbiizuum sǝ.
1CO 5:8 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe wu yit kǝ mu sekyeen kǝ cìn Retnyit mǝ Canɗel fun, baa a shi gǝǝl aas ɗe nii yist ɗesǝǝr mǝ shikbish kǝ ɓutbish kas. Ɗangɓe mǝ cìn Retnyit mǝ Canɗel nǝ shi gǝǝl aas ɗi baa nii yist kas, gǝǝl aas ɗe nǝ a mǝ pǝtuup mǝndong kǝ zeen.
1CO 5:9 Gyet wen kǝn ran nwun ndǝǝn lepran fen nnǝ taji wu ɓalkaa fuu ashak kǝ nencìn ngaa mo kas.
1CO 5:10 Baa gyet wen kǝn satpwoo a nkaa nencìn ngaa ɗi mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo, kǝ nenrǝɓet mbii mo, koo wat mo, koo nenyil ɗi moo seyil nkùm mo kas. Katɗang wu rǝɓet kǝ taji mee mbii ɓàl wun kǝ nenyil ɗesǝ mo kas, ɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ wun mpwat aku ndǝǝn yil ɗesǝ kǝnding-nding mǝnǝ.
1CO 5:11 Amma wen kǝn ran nwun, nǝ, taji wu ɓalkaa fuu kǝ ngwar ɗe wu kǝ pet shin a ngudǝm nɗang Jesu, ɗangɓe wur kǝ cìn ngaa, koo rǝɓet mbii, koo seyil nkùm, koo satpwoo ɗebish nkaa gurum mo, koo shwaamwes, koo ngucìn wat kas. Baa nǝ ret kǝ wu se mbiise ashak kǝ gwar mǝnǝ kas.
1CO 5:12 Baa nǝ a ɗak fen mbǝkǝ an tokɗyeel nenyil ɗi baa mo a nen dǝm nɗang Jesu mo kas. A wun tokɗyeel nenyil ɗe mo ndǝǝn Ekǝlisya mo ɓejee.
1CO 5:13 A Naan nwur ntokɗyeel nenyil ɗi baa mo a nendǝm nɗang Jesu kas. Wen sat nǝnee, <<Wu ceen ngwar ɗebish put aku mbut nwun.>>
1CO 6:1 Katɗang memee ndǝǝn wun kǝ mee pwoo nkaa ɗyemnǝǝn fin, ɓe wu naa nǝ ret kǝ wu mang pwoo nǝ, dǝm kǝ nǝ ntoom kǝ nguɗyeel ɗi baa wu a ngucínzeen kas aa? Baa nǝ ret kǝ a nen Naan mo ɓeetpwoo mǝnǝ kas aa?
1CO 6:2 Baa wu man nǝ, a nen Jesu mon ntokɗyeel nyil nǝ kas aa? Katɗang a wun nyool wu tokɗyeel nyil nǝ, ɓe baa, wu mak ɓeet rep jep pwoo ɗelee-lee mo kas aa?
1CO 6:3 Baa wu man nǝ, parmeeci ɓe a mun ntokɗyeel Nenlep kǝ Naan mo kas aa? Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe a me le ɗang baa mǝ mak ɓeet ɗyeel ɗi mǝ yil ɗesǝ kas ye?
1CO 6:4 Katɗang wun kǝ ɗyeel mo, ɓe a me le ɗang wuu dǝm kǝ ɗyeel nǝ a ntoom kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a mee mbii pee Ekǝlisya mo ɗe kas ye?
1CO 6:5 Wen sat ɗesǝ nǝ a mbǝkǝ nǝ shweep wun ɗi. A nǝ le ɗang kǝn sat nwun nǝ, baa wun kǝ mee gurum ɗeseen ndǝǝn wun, ɗewur mmak ɓeet ɗyeel mǝnǝ mo nwun nendǝm nɗang Jesu mo kas aa?
1CO 6:6 Kyet nǝ ret kǝ ngudǝm nɗang Jesu mang ɗyemnǝǝn fir ngudǝm nɗang Jesu zak, dǝm kǝ wur nluɗyeel, mbǝkǝ wu ɗar ɗi ntoom nguɗyeel ɗe baa wu a ngucínzeen kas wo?
1CO 6:7 Katɗang wuu mangshak wu dǝm kǝ nǝ nluɗyeel, ɓe nǝ kám nǝ, wuu taa wu ɗee kǝnding-nding mmǝnǝ. Gyel ɗesǝ ɓe wu yit kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fuu mo wàt pǝtuup wun met aku ɗi wun dǝm kǝ shak nluɗyeel. Gyel ɗee a sǝ ɓe wu yit kǝ mo seen kaa wun kas aa?
1CO 6:8 Ɗangɓe wun shikáa fuu, wuu wàt pǝtuup nshak, kǝ wuu seen kaa shak zak. Jir ɗi wun a ɗyemnǝǝn ɗemǝndong ndǝǝn Kristi.
1CO 6:9 Baa wu man kas aa? Nǝ, baa nen ɗǝbish mon nɗel mmulki Daa Naan kas. Taji wu numkáa fuu kas. Baa nencìn mbii ɗebish mo, koo nenseyil nkùm mo, koo nencìn ngaa mo, koo mish ɗe moo teer kǝ shak, koo mat ɗi moo teer nshak, koo wat mo, koo nenrǝɓet mbii mo, koo nenshwaa mwos mo, koo nensatpwoo ɗebish nkaa gurum mo. Koo ɗang nenseen akǝ gurum mo.
1CO 6:10 Baa mon mmak ɗel ndǝǝn mulki Naan kas.
1CO 6:11 Gyet yam ɓe pak fuu mo kǝ cìn mbii ɗiisi mo, amma mo kǝ vwang wun mɓut shikbish. Yaksǝ mo kǝ le kǝ wu ɗee a nen Naan. Yaksǝ ɓe Daa Jesu Kristi, kǝ Riin Naan fun, wu kǝ le kǝ wu ɗee a nen ɗin ɗǝre mo nyit Naan.
1CO 6:12 Meeɓe mee gurum sat nǝ, <<Baa mee mbii ɗe nǝ cíi cìn ɗi kas.>> Ii, azeen, amma baa a mbii mo jir ɗi mo kǝ kwoop nǝ kas, <<Pee wen ɗi, ɓe nǝ azeen-nzeen nǝ, baa mee mbii ɗe nǝ cíi cìn ɗi wen kas.>> Ɗangɓe baa Wen rǝɓet ɗee a kǝrem kǝ mee mbii kas.
1CO 6:13 Mee gwe tal nǝnee, <<Mbiise nǝ a mbǝ ɓut, kǝ ɓut a mbǝ mbiise.>> Nǝ azeen, amma Naan wu nshirip mo weet. Baa mo leshin kǝ gurum, a mbǝ cìn mbii ɗebish mo kaa ngaa sǝ kas. Ɗangɓe mo leshin kǝ gurum a mbǝkǝ nǝ cìn ɗak ɗi Daa, kǝ a Daa wur tap kǝ shin kǝ gurum nǝ zak.
1CO 6:14 Naan wu yool kǝ Daa a peemúut, ɓe wu nyool kǝ mun a peemúut shi iiko fin aasǝ zak.
1CO 6:15 Baa wu man nǝ, fwoshik fuu nǝ mo, a ɓeep kǝ Kristi kas aa? Chinarang ɗangɓe wen mmang mee ɓeep kǝ Kristi, kǝ nghan ɓal nǝ ashak kǝ ɓeep mǝ mat ngaa yii? Baa mǝnǝ mmak cìn kas koo dǝɓen!
1CO 6:16 Baa wu man nǝ, ngwar ɗi wu ɓàlshin fin kǝ mat ngaa, ɓe wu ɗee a nan ɗemǝndong kǝ mat ngaa nǝ kas aa? Mɓǝɗǝ mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Mo vǝl, mon nɗee a nan ɗemǝndong.>>
1CO 6:17 Ɗangɓe ngwar ɗe wu ɓal shin kǝ Daa, ɓe mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong ndǝǝn Riin.
1CO 6:18 Wu swa wu baa aku pee mbii ɗebish mo, kaa ngaa sǝ. Koo a shikbish ɗeɗangyii, ɗe gurum kǝ cìn nǝ, ɓe wur kǝ cìn nǝ a kǝɓwoon kǝ fwoshik fin. Ɗangɓe gwar ɗi wu kǝ cìn ngaa, ɓe wu kǝ cìn shikbish a nkaa fwoshik fin.
1CO 6:19 Baa wu man nǝ, fwoshik fuu nǝ a lu kǝ Riin kǝ Naan ɗewur tong ndǝǝn wun kas aa? A Naan wu shin Riin mǝnǝ wun kǝ baa wun a mukáa fuu kas.
1CO 6:20 Jesu kǝ seet kǝ wun shi mbii ɗekǝrǝm, mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ a tǝng, kǝ wu shìn ɗeɗes nNaan shi fwoshik fuu mo.
1CO 7:1 Yaksǝ, ɓe wen kǝn rǝɓet satpwoo nwun nkaa mbii ɗe ɗí wu ran mo. Nǝ ret kǝ gurum tong kǝsǝ nen nlapmat.
1CO 7:2 Ɗangɓe mɓe jwaan mǝ cìn ngaa, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ koo a mish ɗeɗangyi, ɓe wur kǝ mat fin, kǝ koo a mat ɗeɗangyi, ɓe war kǝ mish fer.
1CO 7:3 Nǝ ret kǝ mish nǝ wu cìn mbii ɗe nǝ ret kǝ wur cìn mmat fin, kǝ nǝ ret kǝ mat nǝ waa cìn mbii ɗi nǝ ret kǝ war cìn mmish fer zak.
1CO 7:4 Baa mat war kǝ iiko nkaa fwopshik fer kas, amma mish war wur kǝ nǝ. Nǝ aasǝ zak, baa mish wur kǝ mee iiko nkaa fwoshik fin kas, amma a mat wur war kǝ nǝ.
1CO 7:5 Taji wu cíi nshak akǝ fwoshik fuu mo kas, see katɗang wuu ten wu lap ii kǝ shak nǝ, wun nnookɗi mɓe rep mee pee mo nlee ɗak, mbǝkǝ wu lekáa fuu ɗi mɓe cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan). Ɗangɓe aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe wu baa wu kaat ɗi nshak, mbǝkǝ taji ngujwan gwam wun mɓe cíin yaasuk kas.
1CO 7:6 Wen kǝn satpwoo ɗesǝ mo nwun a kaa chiin sǝ, baa wen kǝn sat a mee Wàar nwun kas.
1CO 7:7 Azeen, wen rǝɓet kǝ, ɗe wun ntong kaa an sǝ, amma koo weyi, ɓe wu kǝ lap zuum pee Naan ɗi ɗyík kǝ mǝ gǝnǝǝn. Naan wu shin zuum mo mmun a shini-shini.
1CO 7:8 Yaksǝ, wen kǝn sat nen ɗi baa mo kǝ cìnɗyik kas, kǝ matkaa mo nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ mo tong kǝ sǝ, kaa an sǝ.
1CO 7:9 Ɗangɓe katɗang ɓe baa mo mak yaasut kas, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mo cìnɗyik, mbǝɗe ngyel gurum cìnɗyik, met aku ɗi coor se seen ngurum.
1CO 7:10 Mpee nen ɗe mo kǝ cìnɗyík, ɓe wen kǝ mee Wàar ɗi, (baa a an kas, amma a Daa wu kǝ shin nwen) mbǝkǝ an sat ɗi mo nǝ. Taji mat waa ɓàkshak kǝ mish fer kas.
1CO 7:11 Katɗang war ɓàkshak kǝ mish war, ɓe taji war baa cìn mee ɗyik ɗi zak kas, kasɓe, war waaji pee mish waa ɗi, kǝ mo ɗak ɗyik fur ɗi. Taji mee mish wur tuɗyík kǝ mat fin kas.
1CO 7:12 Mpee koor nǝ mo, ɓe wen sat nǝ, (baa a Daa wu sat mǝnǝ kas, a an), katɗang mee ngudǝm nɗang Jesu, wur kǝ mat ɗi baa war kǝ cinzeen kas, ɗangɓe war rǝɓet tong ashak kǝ mish fer, ɓe taji wur ɓàkshak kǝ war kas.
1CO 7:13 Katɗang mee mat dǝm nɗang Jesu war kǝ mish ɗi baa wur kǝ shinzeen kas, ɗangɓe wur rǝɓet tong ashak kǝ war, ɓe taji war ɓàkshak kǝ wur kas.
1CO 7:14 Mbǝɗe mish ɗi baa wur kǝ shinzeen kas, ɓe wur ɗee a ɗelǝlap nyit Naan, mɓe mat fin ɗi war kǝ shinzeen. Kǝzak, mat ɗi baa war kǝ cinzeen kas, ɓe war ɗee a ɗelǝlap nyit kǝ Naan, mɓe mish war ɗewur shinzeen. Kat kǝsǝ kas, ɓe jep fuu mon nɗee a kaa jep kǝ nenkum mo sǝ, amma yaksǝ ɓe mo a ɗelǝlap nyit Naan.
1CO 7:15 Ɗangɓe katɗang mish koo mat, ɗe baa mo kǝ shinzeen kas, moo rǝɓet ɓàkshak, ɓe wur yit kǝ mo ɓàkshak ɗi. Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe ngushínzeen nǝ, kyet a mish aa, koo a mat nǝ ye, ɓe gwe nǝ kǝ pee, mɓe cìn mbii ɗi wur naa nǝ ret. Mɓǝɗǝ Naan wur pǝrep mun a mbǝkǝ mu tong ɗe ryang kǝ shak.
1CO 7:16 Wii mat dǝm nɗang Jesu, cirang yi mman ɗi ye? Ngul yi nyool yi ɓam wur mish yii? Waa mish ngudǝm nɗang Jesu, cirang gha mman ɗi yii? Ngul waa nyool a ɓam mat fwaa yii?
1CO 7:17 Koo weyi, ɓe wur tong nchiit kǝ peeɗe Daa wur le gwe nǝ ɗi, Naan wur kǝ pet gwe nǝ mɓe nǝ. A ɗǝsǝ nǝ a Wàar fen pee koo a Ekǝlisya ɗeɗangyi.
1CO 7:18 Ngwe ɗi gyet mo kǝ ten can wur akuɗang Naan kǝ pet wur, ɓe taji wur yappee ɗewur nɗee ɗi nsuluk kas. Kǝ gwar ɗe baa gyet mo kǝ ten can wur kas, ɗangɓe Naan pet wu, ɓe taji wur waa tang ar ɗi mon ncan wur ɗi kas.
1CO 7:19 Mɓǝɗǝ koo ɗi mo can gwe nǝ, kǝ koo ɗi baa mo can ngwar nǝ kas, ɓe baa mǝnǝ mo kǝkoop nǝ kas. Ɗangɓe mbii ɗe nǝ kǝkoop nǝ, a ɗi gurum ntap kǝ Wàar kǝ Naan mo ɓejee ɗak.
1CO 7:20 Koo weyi, ɓe wur tong ɗi ndǝǝn peeɗi gyet wur kǝnǝ, akuɗang Naan kǝ pet wur sǝ.
1CO 7:21 Katɗang gyet waa a kǝrem, akuɗang Naan kǝ pet gha, ɓe taji mǝnǝ daampee nwaa kas. Ɗangɓe katɗang waa mak katpee, mbǝkǝ a ɗee ɗi a mukáa fwaa, ɓe a gung kǝ a kat nǝ ɗi.
1CO 7:22 Ngwe ɗi gyet Naan pet wur ɓe wur kuɗi a kǝrem, ɗangɓe yaksǝ, ɓe wur ɗee a mukáa fin ndǝǝn Daa. Nǝ aasǝ zak, gwe ɗe gyet wur a laa lu kaa ɗe Naan pet wur, amma yaksǝ gwe mǝnǝ ɗee a kǝrem mǝ Kristi.
1CO 7:23 Jesu Kristi sǝrep wun a shi toom ɗekǝrǝm, Mɓemǝnǝ ɓe taji wu ɗee a kǝrem mǝ gurum mo kas.
1CO 7:24 Nǝ aasǝ, ɗyemnaa mo, koo ɗi gyet mo pǝrep wun a ndǝǝn tong ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mu tong ɗi a ndǝǝn tong mǝnǝ ashak kǝ Naan.
1CO 7:25 Pwoo nkaa nen ɗe baa mo kǝ cìnɗyik kas, ɓe baa wen kǝ mee Wàar pee Daa ɗi, mbe mo kas. Ɗangɓe wen kǝn sat a pan fen, kaa gwe ɗi ndǝǝn kambok kǝ Naan, ɓe gurum mo mak shinzeen wen sǝ, ɓe wen kǝn pan nǝ,
1CO 7:26 Mpee mbii daampee ɗi mo ɗi yaksǝ, ɓe wen naa nnǝ nǝ ret kǝ taji gurum cìnɗyik kas.
1CO 7:27 Ɗangɓe katɗang waa kǝ mat, ɓe taji a tang ar mɓe tuɗyik nǝ kas. Katɗang baa waa kǝ mat kas, ɓe taji a tang ar mbǝkǝ a lapmat ɗi kas.
1CO 7:28 Ɗangɓe katɗang waa cìnɗyik, ɓe baa waa cìn a shikbish kas, kǝ katɗang mee reep cìnɗyik, ɓe baa war cìn shikbish kas. Ɗangɓe jir kǝsǝ, nen ɗi mo cìnɗyik, ɓe mon nkat jeel mǝ yil nǝ. Mɓǝmǝnǝ, nnaa fen ɓe taji gurum cìnɗyik kas, mbǝkǝ taji wur shwaajeel.
1CO 7:29 Mbii ɗe wen kǝn rǝɓet sat nǝ nɗesǝ ɗyemnaa mo, peeɗi Naan wur kǝ ten bǝlǝp nǝ le, nǝ kǝ wul kus. Yool nyaksǝ, ɓe nen ɗe mo kǝ mat mo, ɓe mo tong kaa baa mo kǝ cham cìnɗyik kas sǝ.
1CO 7:30 Nen ɗi mon mmaap, ɓe mo tong kaa nen ɗi baa mon mmaap kas sǝ. Nen ɗi mon nretnyit, ɓe mo tong kaa baa mo a nretnyit kas sǝ. Nen ɗi mo nkaa nweer mo, ɓe mo tong kaa nen ɗi baa mo kǝ mee mbii kas sǝ.
1CO 7:31 Nen ɗi moo cìn ɗak kǝ mbii mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo, ɓe mo tong kaa baa mo kǝ cham cìn mee mbii kǝ mbii mǝ yil nǝ mo kas sǝ. Mɓǝɗǝ mbii ɗe mǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ mo nkaa ɗel seet.
1CO 7:32 Ɗyeen nwen, kǝ taji wu daampee nsuk kas. Ngwe ɗi baa wu kǝ cìnɗyik kas, ɓe wur le pǝtuup fin a nkaa mbii ɗi mo a mǝ Daa. Wur pan a ar ɗi wur ncìn ɗak ɗi mo ret ɗi nDaa nyit.
1CO 7:33 Ɗangɓe ngwar ɗi wu kǝ cìnɗyik, ɓe wur kǝ le pǝtuup fin a nkaa mbii mǝ yil nǝ mo, wur kǝ pan a ar ɗi wur ncìn mbii ɗe mo ret ɗi mmat fin nyit.
1CO 7:34 Ɗesǝ nǝ le kǝ pan fin mo ɓak vǝl mmǝnǝ. Mat ɗi baa war kǝ cìnɗyik kas, koo reep, ɓe war le pǝtuup war a nkaa ar ɗi war ncìn mbii ɗe mo ret ɗi nDaa nyit, kǝ ar ɗi war nɗee a ɗeɓang ndǝǝn nan, kǝ ndǝǝn Riin. Ɗangɓe mat ɗi war kǝ cìnɗyik, ɓe waa le pǝtuup fer a nkaa mbii mǝ yil nǝ mo, ɗi war ncìn, mbǝkǝ nǝ ret ɗi mmish fer nyit.
1CO 7:35 Wen kǝn sat ɗesǝ a mbǝkǝ nǝ ɓam wu wun ɗi, baa wen cíi a cìnɗyik nwun kas, ɗangɓe wen sat pwoo sǝ mo a mbǝkǝ mbii mo dǝm ɗi nwun ndǝre-ndǝre, kǝ mbǝkǝ wu cìn ɗak mǝ Daa ɗi shi pǝtuup mǝndong.
1CO 7:36 Katɗang nǝ dampee mǝ gwar, kaa baa wur pee cin ɓe ɗe nɗere nmat kwam fin kas ɗang katɗang coor mat kǝ jar dampee nwur, ɗang wur nan nǝ ret kǝ mo cin dyik ɗi, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur cin ɓe ɗe nǝ nbut pan wur, baa wur pee cin a shikbish kas.
1CO 7:37 Ɗangɓe katɗang ɓe wur naa nǝ, baa nǝ a tǝng kǝ wur cìnɗyik nreep fin kas, kǝ wur ɗar kǝ pan fin nkaa mbii ɗi wur naa nǝ ret nwur, kǝ wur fes le pǝtuup fin ɓalɓal nǝ, wur mmak tap kǝ waar, ɓe wur cìn a mbii ɗe nǝ ret.
1CO 7:38 Ngwe ɗe wur cìnɗyik, ɓe wur cìn a mbii ɗi nǝ ret, ɗangbe gwe ɗi baa wur cìnɗyik kas, ɓe wur cìn a mbii ɗe nǝ waa ret met.
1CO 7:39 Mat war a nder mish fer, har parpuus ɗi wur mmuut. Katɗang mish nǝ muut, ɓe waa kǝ pee mɓe cìnɗyik koo a weyi ɗi war kǝ rǝɓet, ɗangɓe tǝng a gwe ɗi wur ndǝǝn Daa.
1CO 7:40 Amma katɗang a nnaa mǝnǝ, ɓe war ntong shi retnyit met, katɗang war nook cìnɗyik. Pan fen, ɓe wen kǝ Riin Naan zak.
1CO 8:1 Yaksǝ, pwoo nkaa mbiise ɗi mo kǝ ten shìn nkùm mo, mǝ man nǝnee, <<mun jir mun kǝ man >> Man nii le kǝ gurum ɗyeepkáa, ɗangbe wal nii tap ɗyik gurum kàa rǝret.
1CO 8:2 Katɗang mee gurum kǝ pan nǝ, wuɗi man mee mbii, ɓe baa wu kǝ man mee mbii kaaɗe nǝ ret kǝ wur man sǝ kas.
1CO 8:3 Ɗangɓe gwe ɗe kǝ wur wal nNaan, ɓe Naan man gwe mǝnǝ.
1CO 8:4 Yaksǝ, pwoo nkaa se mbiise ɗe mo kǝ ten shin nǝ nkùm mo, mǝ man azeen nǝ, baa kùm mo kǝ mee seen kas. Kǝzak, mǝ man nǝ, Naan wur a ɓishin ɓejee ɗak.
1CO 8:5 Koo ɗi pak mbii mo ɗi, ɗe moo pet mo a naan mo, ɗi mo ndǝǝn ɗengnaan, koo ɗe mo ndǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, mbǝɗe naan mo ɗi ɗes, kǝ daa mo ɗi ɗes zak.
1CO 8:6 Ɗangɓe jir kǝsǝ, ɓe pee mumun ɗi, ɓe Naan wur a mǝndong ɓejee, ɗewur a puun fun, a wur le mbii mo jir, kǝ a mbǝ wur ɗangɓe mun kǝ seen. Daa fun wur a mǝndong ɓejee zak, wur Jesu Kristi, ɗi a ndǝǝn wur ɓe Naan le mbii mo jir, kǝ a ndǝǝn wur ɓe mun kǝ seen.
1CO 8:7 Ɗangɓe baa a gurum mo jir mo kǝ man zeen ɗesǝ nǝ kas. Pak mo kǝ fes loot kǝ kùm mo hakyeng, har mbǝ cicinsi, ɓe katɗang mo se mbiise, ɓe moo pan nǝ mbiise nǝ a mǝ kùm. Baa pan ɗe mputuup fur nǝ ɓal kas, kǝ mo pan nǝ, wuɗun kǝ ɗee, a ɗewuwat mbǝ mbiise.
1CO 8:8 Baa mbiise mak jì kǝ mun kus kǝ Naan kas. Koo ɗi mu se mbiise, ɓe baa mun nshee ɗi kas, kǝ koo ɗi baa mu se mbiise kas, ɓe baa mun ntaa mǝ kat kas.
1CO 8:9 Ɗangɓe wu tap taji katpee fuu mɓe cìn mbii ɗi wuu rǝɓet nǝ ɗee a mbii canshii nen ɗi baa shinzeen fur nǝ ɓal kas.
1CO 8:10 Mɓǝɗǝ katɗang mee gwar ɗe baa shinzeen fin nǝ ɓal ndǝǝn mbii ɗesǝ mo kas, wur naa gha gwar ɗi waa kǝ man, aa se mbii nlukùm, ɓe baa nǝn nshìn ɓal nwur ndǝǝn pǝtuup wur ɓe kǝ wur se mbiise ɗi mo kǝ ten shin nǝ nkùm kas aa?
1CO 8:11 Nǝ aasǝ, ɓe shi man fwaa, gha le kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fwaa ɗi Kristi kǝ muut mɓe wu, wu ɗee a ɗelǝloom.
1CO 8:12 Katɗang gha cìn mbii mǝnǝ, ɓe gha cìn shikbish nkaa gǝnang, mbǝɗe gha kǝ le kǝ pǝtuup fin ɗi baa nǝ kǝ ɗar ɓalɓal kas nǝ pal, kǝzak, gha cìn shikbish a nkaa Kristi shikáa fin.
1CO 8:13 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, katɗang mbii ɗe wen nse, nǝn nɗee a mbii le canshii nɗyemnǝǝn fen, ɓe baa wen nkuɗi kǝn se mbiise mǝnǝ zak kas, mbǝkǝ taji wen le kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fen canshii kas.
1CO 9:1 Baa wen mak cìn mbii ɗi wen kǝn rǝɓet kas aa? Baa wen a laalep Kristi kas aa? Baa wen kǝn ten naa Daa fun Jesu Kristi kas aa? Baa gyet a Wen satpwoo Naan nǝ nwun, ɗangɓe wu ɗee a nen dǝm nɗang Daa kas aa?
1CO 9:2 Koo ɗi baa pak gurum mo lap an kaa laalep Kristi sǝ kas, ɓe nǝ a tǝng wen a laalep Kristi pee wun ɗi. Mɓǝɗǝ wun a langtǝng mǝ ɗak fen kaa laalep Kristi sǝ pee Daa ɗi.
1CO 9:3 A ɗesǝ nǝ a mbii ɗi wen kǝn sat, nen ɗi moo chakpwoo nɗang wen.
1CO 9:4 Baa wen kǝ pee mbǝkǝ wen se mbiise kǝ shwaa mbii shwaa ɓe ɗak fen kas aa?
1CO 9:5 Baa wen kǝ pee, mɓe lapmat ɗi war a ngudǝm nɗang Jesu, kǝ wen pan war nɗang sen kas aa? Kaaɗǝ koor jeplep kǝ Kristi mo, kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn mǝ Daa mo, kǝ Pita moo cìn sǝ kas aa?
1CO 9:6 Aa koo a wen kǝ Barnabas ɓejee ɗe tǝng see mǝ cìn ɗak aku mu kat mbiise ɗe mun nse ɗi aa?
1CO 9:7 A mee shiitoon ɗeɗang wur kǝ cham kwat shool ɗak ɗi wur cìn nshin ye? A wii kǝ cham kop anab mbong, ɓe baa wur nyool se làa anab nǝ kas yi? A wii kǝ cham kyeer long mo, ɓe baa wur nshwaa wur mo nǝ kas yi?
1CO 9:8 Kyet wen kǝn sat ɗesǝ nǝ a shi pan mǝ gurum wo? Baa Wàar Mosis nǝ sat aasǝ zak kas aa?
1CO 9:9 Mo kǝ ten ran nǝ ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Wàar Mosis nǝnee, <<Taji a lep shang nkus randong mpwoo, <<kaaɗǝ nǝ nkaa tǝreng ɗeɓen mbong <<mbǝkǝ aas nǝ put ɗi kas.>> Naan wur kǝ pan aa randong mo aa?
1CO 9:10 Ɗangɓe gyet wur le kǝ mo ran Wàar mǝnǝ mo a mɓe mun gurum. Mbǝkǝ gwe ɗi wur kop kǝ gwe ɗi wur ɗiip, ɓe mo cìn ɗak fur ɗi shi canciin mɓe se ɗǝɓen nǝ.
1CO 9:11 Katɗang mun, muu ten mu kop a mbii ɗi nǝ a mǝ Riin mɓut nwun, ɓe baa nǝ ret, kǝ wuwun wu ɓam mun kǝ mbii ɗi mǝ yil nǝ mo kas aa?
1CO 9:12 Katɗang pak gurum moo kat mbii ɗesǝ mo pee wun ɗi, ɓe baa nǝ ret kǝ mun, mu kat mbii mo ɗes met mumo nǝ pee wun ɗi kas aa? Baa mun muu le tǝng nwun, mbǝkǝ wu shin mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗi mmun kas, ɗangbe muu gung mbii mo jir, a mbǝkǝ taji mu daam sekyeen mpwoo ɗeret mǝ Kristi kas.
1CO 9:13 Baa wu man nǝ, nen ɗi moo cìn ɗak ndǝǝn Lu Naan ɗǝɗes, ɓe moo kat mbiise fur a nLu Naan ɗeɗes nǝ kas aa? Kǝ baa wu man nǝ nen ɗi moo wus mbiizuum a peewus mbiizuum mo, ɓe moo se a pak mbiizuum nǝ kas aa?
1CO 9:14 Nǝ aasǝ zak, ɓe Daa wu satpwoo nǝ. Nen ɗi moo satpwoo ɗeret ngurum mo, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mo kat mbiise fur a ɗeɓut zak.
1CO 9:15 Ɗangɓe, baa wen kǝn cham cìn ɗak kǝ iiko fen ɗesǝ kas, kǝ baa Wen ran lepran ɗesǝ nwun, a mbǝkǝ wu shin mbii mo ɗi nwen kas. Ngyal ɗesǝ ɓe wen muut, met a kuɗi mee gwe le mbii ɗi wen kǝn canjoom nkaa nǝ ɗee a mbii ɗebuu.
1CO 9:16 Mɓǝɗǝ koo ɗi wen kǝn satpwoo ɗeret nǝ, ɓe baa wen kǝ pee mɓe canjoom kas. Ɗangɓe kǝn satpwoo ɗeret nǝ a mɓeɗǝ, a Naan wur kǝ letǝng an, mbǝkǝ an satpwoo nǝ ɗi. Jeel ɗi mɓe wen, katɗang baa wen satpwoo ɗeret nǝn ngurum mo kas.
1CO 9:17 Katɗang ɗi wen kǝn satpwoo nǝ a shi ɗyen fen, ɓe ɗi wen nkat kwat. Ɗangɓe wen kǝn satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ngurum mo, baa a shi ɗyen fen kas, mɓeɗǝ a ɗak ɗi Naan wur kǝ le nǝ nsar fen mmǝnǝ.
1CO 9:18 Kwat fen nǝ a meyii? A kwat fen nǝn nɗesǝ, a peeɗi Naan wur kǝ shínpee nwen, mbǝkǝ wen satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ngurum mo shi zuum, baa wen kǝn cìn ɗak kǝ iiko fen mɓe tang kwat pee wun ɗi kas.
1CO 9:19 Koo ɗi baa wen a kǝrem kǝ mee gurum kas, ɗangbe wen kǝn ten nle sen a kǝrem kǝ gurum mo jir, mbǝkǝ wen jì ɗi kǝ gurum mo ɗes nDaa.
1CO 9:20 Mbǝ nen Yahudi mo, ɓe wen ɗee a kaa mo sǝ, mbǝkǝ wen jì kǝ mo ɗi nDaa. Kǝzak, nen Yahudi mo, a ndǝr Wàar Mosis, ɓe wen ɗee a kaa mo sǝ, koo ɗi baa wen shikáa fen an a nder Wàar Mosis kas. Ɗangɓe wen kǝn ɗee a kaa nen ɗi mon ndǝr Wàar Mosis nǝ sǝ, mbǝkǝ wen jì kǝ mo ɗi nDaa.
1CO 9:21 Mpee nen ɗi baa mo kǝ Wàar kǝ Mosis kas, ɓe wen ɗee a kaa mo sǝ, mbǝkǝ wen jì kǝ mo ɗi nDaa. Ɗangɓe wen kǝn tap kǝ Wàar Naan. Azeen wen a ndǝr kǝ Wàar mǝ Kristi.
1CO 9:22 Mpee nen ɗi baa mo kǝ ɓal ndǝǝn shinzeen kas, ɓe wen fwang mo, mbǝkǝ wen jì kǝ mo nDaa. Wen kǝn ten ɗee a mbii mo jir, pee gurum mo ɗi jir, mbǝkǝ koo ɗi a ndǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi, ɓe wen ɓam pak mo ɗi.
1CO 9:23 Wen kǝn lesen ndǝǝn mbii mo jir, a mɓe pwoo ɗeret nǝ, kǝ mbǝkǝ wen kat pak ɗeret mǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗi zak.
1CO 9:24 Baa wu man nǝ, ndǝǝn kwoon mǝ sushii, ɓe gurum mo ɗes moo shwe, ɗangbe a ngumǝndong kǝ lap zuum nǝ ɓejee ɗak kas aa? Nǝ aasǝ zak, nǝ ret kǝ wu shwe, mbǝkǝ wu kat zuum nǝ ɗi.
1CO 9:25 Koo weyi, ɗi wur a ngusushii, ɓe wu naa nkar shin fin ndǝǝn mbii mo jir. Wur kar shin fin, mbǝkǝ wur lap zuum ɗi nii kǝlak kǝ wat ɗi, amma mumun, muu lap a zum ɗi baa nǝn cham wat kas.
1CO 9:26 Baa wen kǝn su a buu-buu kas, kǝ cutpee ɗi wen kǝn cìn nǝ, baa wen kǝn cut a buu kas.
1CO 9:27 Ɗangɓe wen kǝn cìn kǝ sen fen, mbǝkǝ sen fen nǝ ɓal ɗi, kǝ nǝ ɗee ɗi ndǝr fen kaa kǝrem sǝ, mbǝkǝ taji aɓwoon ɗi wen kǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ngurum mo, ɗangɓe mo yool baa kǝ wen shikáa fen mɓwoon kas.
1CO 10:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, wen rǝɓet kǝ wu man, gyet puun fun mo jir, mo a nder nluu, kǝ gyet mo jir mo can am Bahar Ɗenaat mo ɗel ryang nɗang Mosis zak.
1CO 10:2 Gyet mo cìn baptisma mmo jir a ndǝǝn nluu, kǝ ndǝǝn am bahar kaaɗe gyet mo dǝm nɗang Mosis sǝ.
1CO 10:3 Gyet mo jir, mo se mbiise ɗi gyet Naan shin mmo ɗi nǝ a mǝ Riin.
1CO 10:4 Gyet mo jir mo shwaa am ɗi Naan shin mmo. Mɓeɗi gyet mo shwaa am ɗi gyet nǝ jì put mɓut jwak. Gyet jwak ɗesǝ nǝ mwaan nɗang mo. Gyet jwak ɗesǝ a Kristi shikáa fir.
1CO 10:5 Jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa gyet Naan wur kat retnyit kǝ pak mo kas. Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɓe mo murep ɗes a naaryil.
1CO 10:6 Yaksǝ, ɓe mbii ɗesǝ mo jir, mo ɗee a mbiikám mumun. Mo gwak mun, mbǝkǝ taji mu coor mbii ɗebish mo, kaaɗe gyet mo cìn sǝ kas.
1CO 10:7 Taji wu ɗee a nenkum mo, kaaɗe gyet pak mo ndǝǝn mo, mo cìn sǝ kas, kaaɗe mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal mǝ Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Gurum nǝ mo tong nyil, <<mbǝkǝ mo se gwom kùm, <<kǝ shwaa mwes, <<kǝ mo yool a tǝng mɓe cìn kook.>>
1CO 10:8 Taji mu cìn ngaa kas, kaaɗe gyet pak mo ndǝǝn mo, mo cìn sǝ, har gurum mo ngal laarvǝl baakun, mo murǝp parpuus mǝndong.
1CO 10:9 Taji mu kam Daa kas, kaaɗe gyet pak mo ndǝǝn mo, mo cìn sǝ, ɓe har gyet nwòo mo, twe mo.
1CO 10:10 Taji mǝ chakpwoo nɗoom-nɗoom kas, kaaɗe gyet pak mo ndǝǝn mo, mo cìn sǝ, har mo murǝp nsar kǝ ngulep mǝ muut.
1CO 10:11 Mbii ɗi gyet nǝ kat mo, nǝ ɗee a mbiikám pee mun ɗi. Mo kǝ ten ran mo, a mbǝkǝ mo gwak mun ɗi, mun ɗe peekyes kǝ ɓit nǝ mo kǝ jì a nkaa mun.
1CO 10:12 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɓe koo a weyi, ɗi wur kǝ pan nnǝ wuɗin kǝ ɗar ɓalɓal, ɓe wur tap, taji wur pal kas.
1CO 10:13 Baa mee jwaan ɗe nǝn nkat wun ɗi kas, see a ɗi nǝn nkat koor gurum mo jir zak. Naan wur a nguzeen, baa wur nyit kǝ mee jwaan kat wun, ɗe nǝn mmet mɓal fuu kas. Ɗangɓe a shi jwaan nǝ, ɓe nwun nle ar put nǝ ɗi zak, mbǝkǝ wu mak gung jwaan nǝ ɗi.
1CO 10:14 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo, taji wu seyil nkùm mo kas.
1CO 10:15 Wen kǝn katpwoo wun, a kaa nen ɗe mo kǝ ɗyen sǝ, Naan wur kǝ ten kám ar nǝ wun sǝ. Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu ɓeet kǝ suk, nkaa mbii ɗi wen kǝn sat nǝ.
1CO 10:16 Katɗang mu mang laaɗaa mǝ Se Tong Ashak ɗi muu pǝlang Naan mɓe nǝ, ɓe baa wu man nǝ, muu ɓàl a káa fun mo ashak kǝ Kristi ndǝǝn toom fir kas aa? Gill aas ɗe muu yilang sǝ, ɓe baa wu man nǝ, muu ɓàl a káa fun ndǝǝn fwoshik Kristi kas aa?
1CO 10:17 Mɓǝɗǝ gill aas nǝ a mǝndong, ɗi muu yilang nǝ mǝ mu se ashak. Nǝ aasǝ zak, mun ɗi ɗes, ɗangbe mun a nan ɗemǝndong, mbǝɗe muu se a gill aas ɗemǝndong.
1CO 10:18 Wu pan nkaa nen Iisreal mo ndǝǝn nan, nen ɗi moo se ndǝǝn mbiizuum ɗi mo wus nǝ, ɓe moo ɓal a káa fur kǝ Naan ɗi moo shìn nǝ nwur.
1CO 10:19 Wen kǝn rǝɓet sat a meyii? Kyet mbiise ɗi moo shìn nkùm, mǝnǝ a mee mbii ee? Koo a kùm nǝ a mee mbii ye?
1CO 10:20 Hai yo, wen kǝn sat a nǝ, mbii ɗi nenkum moo gap mpee cìn zuum, ɓe moo shìn nǝ a riin ɗebish mo, baa moo shin zuum nǝ a nNaan kas. Baa wen rǝɓet kǝ wu ɓalkaa fuu mo ashak kǝ riin ɗebish mo kas.
1CO 10:21 Baa wun mmak shwaa mɓut laaɗaa mǝ Daa, kǝ wu waa wu shwaa mɓut laaɗaa mǝ riin ɗebish mo zak kas.
1CO 10:22 Taji mu cìn mee mbii ɗi nǝn nle kǝ Naan cìn tuup kas. Kyet mun, mu ɓal met wur wo?
1CO 10:23 Gurum mo sat nǝ, <<Mu mak cìn koo meye, ɗi mu rǝɓet.>> Nǝ azeen, ɗangbe baa a mbii mo jir ɗi mo mak ɗik wun koo moo koop nǝ mbǝ gurum kas.
1CO 10:24 Taji mee gurum tang mbii ɗe mo ret mukáa fin kas. Amma nǝ ret kǝ wur tang a mbii ɗi mo ret mbǝ niyee mo.
1CO 10:25 Wu se mbii ɗi moo sǝrep mo ndǝǝn lutuk mǝ luwaa mo. Taji wu talpwoo kas, mbǝ pan ɗi nǝ ndǝǝn pǝtuup.
1CO 10:26 Mɓǝɗǝ mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Yil nǝ kǝ mbii ɗe mo ndǝǝn nǝ jir, mo a mǝ Daa.>>
1CO 10:27 Katɗang mee gwar ɗi baa wur kǝ shinzeen nDaa Jesu kas, wur pet wun mbǝ sese ashak kǝ wur. Katɗang wuu lap ii, nnǝ wun ndem, ɓe wu se mbii ɗi wu nle a kyeen fuu. Taji wu tal kas, mbǝ pan ɗi nǝ ndǝǝn pǝtuup fuu.
1CO 10:28 Amma katɗang mee gwe kǝ ten sat nwun nǝnee, <<Mo kǝ ten shin luwaa ɗesǝ nǝ nkùm.>> Ɓe taji wu se luwaa nǝ kas, mbǝ gwar ɗe wu sat pwoo mǝnǝ nwun, kǝ mɓe pan ɗe nǝ ndǝǝn pǝtuup.
1CO 10:29 Baa a mɓe pan muu mo kas, amma a mɓe pan kǝ gwar nǝ. Mbǝme ɗang pan kǝ mee gurum nǝn ncíi nwen, mbǝ katpee ɗe wen kǝ nǝ, mɓe cìn mbii ɗi wen kǝn rǝɓet yi?
1CO 10:30 Katɗang wen pǝlang Naan mɓe mbiise fen. Ɓe cirang ɗangɓe gurum moo leshap ɗebuu nkaa wen, mbǝ mbiise ɗi wen kǝn ten pǝlang Naan nkaa nǝ yi?
1CO 10:31 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe koo a mbii ɗeɗangyi ɗe wuu cìn, koo a se mbiise, koo a shwaa mbiishwaa, ɓe wu cìn mbii mo jir mbǝ shin ɗehai Naan.
1CO 10:32 Taji wu le kǝ mee gurum canshii kas. Koo ɗang ɗi gwe nǝ a ngu Yahudi koo baa a ngu Yahudi kas, koo ɗi a Ekǝlisya mǝ Naan.
1CO 10:33 Kaaɗǝ wen kǝn gung mbǝkǝ wen cìn mbii ɗi mo shang ɗi ngurum mo jir. Baa wen kǝn tang a ɗeret mukáa fen kas, ɗangɓe wen kǝn tang a ɗeret mǝ gurum mo ɗes, mbǝkǝ mo kat ɓam wur ɗi.
1CO 11:1 Wu mwaan ndǝǝn shiimwaan fen, kaaɗi wen kǝn mwaan ndǝǝn shiimwaan mǝ Kristi sǝ.
1CO 11:2 Wen kwoop wun, mɓeɗǝ wuu pan an ndǝǝn mbii mo jir, kǝ wuu mwaan ndǝǝn kám dǝ wen kám mo nwun zak.
1CO 11:3 Amma wen rǝɓet kǝ wun man nǝ, a Kristi wu a káa kǝ koo a mish ɗeɗangyi, kǝ a mish wu a káa kǝ mat fin, kǝ Naan wu a káa kǝ Kristi.
1CO 11:4 Mɓǝmǝnǝ koo mish ɗeɗangyi ɗi wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), kǝ satpwoo Naan ndǝǝn ɗuu kǝ gurum mo kǝ káa fin a pǝpaa, ɓe wur jì kǝ yitluwaan nkaa Kristi ɗi a wu a káa fin mmǝnǝ.
1CO 11:5 Koo mat ɗeɗangyi ɗi war cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), kǝ satpwoo kǝ Naan ɗi baa war Paakáa war kas, ɓe war jì kǝ yitluwaan nkaa mish war. Ɗewur a káa fin, kǝzak, ɓe war ɗee a kaa mat ɗi mo sak káa nwar ngau sǝ mmǝnǝ.
1CO 11:6 Katɗang baa mat Paakáa fin kas, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ war saa shweepkáa fer. Amma katɗang saa shweepkáa koo sak shweepkáa nǝn njì kǝ yitluwaan mmat, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ war Paakáa fer.
1CO 11:7 Baa nǝ ret kǝ ngumish Paakáa fin kas, mɓeɗǝ Naan ɗak mish a kaa shin sǝ, kǝ wur kám a ɗeɗes kǝ Naan. Amma mat war kǝ kám a ɗeɗes mǝ mish.
1CO 11:8 Baa gyet Naan ɗak mish a shi fwoshik mǝ mat kas, ɗangbe gyet wur ɗak mat a fwoshik mǝ mish.
1CO 11:9 Kǝzak, baa gyet Naan wu le mish a mɓe mat kas, amma gyet wur le mat a mɓe mish.
1CO 11:10 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mat Paakáa war, kǝ nǝ kám ɗi nǝ, war nder kǝ mish fer, kǝ mɓe nenlep kǝ Naan mo zak.
1CO 11:11 Jir kǝsǝ, ɓe seen fun ɗi mun kǝ nǝ ndǝǝn Daa, ɓe baa mat war ɗyik kǝ mish fer kas, kǝ baa mish wur ɗik kǝ mat fin kas zak.
1CO 11:12 Mɓeɗi gyet Naan wu ɗak mat a shi mee ɗyes kǝ mish, kǝ nǝ aasǝ zak, yaksǝ ɓe a mat war kǝ làa mish. Mbii moo pwat a pee Naan ɗi jir.
1CO 11:13 Wun shikáa fuu, wu ɓeetpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ, kyet nǝn ndere mbǝkǝ mat war cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nNaan ndǝǝn kuur kǝ gurum mo, ɗe baa war Paakáa war kas wo?
1CO 11:14 Koo a shi ɗyen, ɓe nǝ kám nwun kas aa? Nǝ a mbii yitluwaan kǝ mish wur ɗyel shweepkáa shwal-shwal.
1CO 11:15 Amma katɗang ɓe mat war ɗyel sheepkáa ɗeshwal-shwal, ɓe mǝnǝ a mbii jwat nwar kas aa? Mɓǝɗǝ mo shin sheepkáa ɗeshwal-shwal nǝ nwar, a mbǝkǝ waa Paakáa war ɗi.
1CO 11:16 Amma katɗang mee ngwar kǝ rǝɓet ɓeetshik nkaa pwoo ɗesǝ, ɓe baa mumun, koo Ekǝlisya mǝ Naan mo, baa mu loot kǝ mee ar ɗi nǝ a mǝ seyil nNaan ɗi nǝ ɗik kǝ mǝnǝ kas.
1CO 11:17 nƊǝǝn wàar ɗǝsǝ, ɓe baa wen kwoop wun kas, mɓeɗǝ kuur fuu nǝ baa nii kwoop nǝ kas. Mɓeɗi katɗang wu jì wu kaat ndǝǝn kuur fuu, ɓe mbii ɗi wuu cìn nǝ mo, ɓe baa mo ret kas. Nii waa wuwat gurum mo met aku ɗi nǝn mɓam mo.
1CO 11:18 To, ɗinshee nǝ, katɗang wu kuur, kaa Ekǝlisya sǝ, mɓe seyil nNaan, ɓe baa pwoo fuu moo dǝm ndangshak kas, har kaaɗe ɗe wen kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe wen ɗoom shinzeen nǝ.
1CO 11:19 Baa nǝ kǝ mee kyetwoo kas, nǝ a tǝng, kǝ mo kat ɓàkshak ɗi ndǝǝn wun, mbǝkǝ mo man nen dǝm ndang Naan ɗe ɗǝre nǝ mo ɗi azeen-nzeen.
1CO 11:20 Katɗang wu jì wu kaat ashak, ɓe baa wuu se a Tong Ashak mǝ Daa nǝ kas.
1CO 11:21 Mɓǝɗǝ katɗang wu ɗoom se nǝ, ɓe koo weye wur yaa se mbiise ɗi wur jì kǝni, har wuu le kǝ neenláa mpak mo, kǝ pak moo shwaa ɓe yiirkaa ɗi.
1CO 11:22 Kai! Baa wun kǝ tul ɗi wun nse kǝ shwaa ɗi kas aa? A me le ɗang wuu toklong shi nkuur mǝ Ekǝlisya kǝ Daa ye? Kǝ a me le ɗang wuu shin yitluwaan nen ɗi baa mo kǝ mee mbii kas yi? Wen nsat a me nwun mbǝ mbii kaa ɗesǝ sǝ yi? Wen nkwoop wun aa? Hai yo, baa wen nkwoop wun kas koo dǝɓen.
1CO 11:23 Wen lap kám ɗǝsǝ nǝ a pee Daa ɗǝ, ɗe wen kǝn shin nwun sǝ zak. Nǝ, mpar ɗi gyet mo seet Daa Jesu ɗi, ɓe Daa Jesu wur mang gill aas.
1CO 11:24 Aɓwoon ɗi wur kǝ cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan nkaa gill aas nǝ, ɓe wur yilang nǝ, wur sat nǝnee, <<Ɗesǝ nǝ a fwoshik fen, <<ɗi wen kǝn shin nǝ mɓe wun, <<Wu naa nshìn aasǝ, <<mbǝkǝ taji wu muunshik nwen kas.>>
1CO 11:25 Nǝ aasǝ zak, ɓe aɓwoon ɗi mo se mbiise, ɓe wur mang laaɗaa, ɓe wu sat nǝnee, <<Laaɗaa ɗǝsǝ nǝ a ɓǝlemcuk shi toom kǝ Naan ɗepwoo, ɗi nǝ ndǝǝn toom fen. Katɗang koo a pǝrangye ɗi wun nshwaa am anab ndǝǝn laaɗaa nǝ, ɓe wuu shwaa nǝ a mbǝkǝ taji wu muunshik wen kas.>>
1CO 11:26 Shii kǝ ɗǝsǝ nǝ a nǝ, koo a pǝrangye ɗi wuu se gill aas nǝ, kǝ wu shwaa am anab ndǝǝn laaɗaa nǝ, ɓe wuu cìn a langtǝng nkaa muut kǝ Daa Jesu, har parɗi wur mbaa jì.
1CO 11:27 Katɗang mee gwe kǝ se gill aas nǝ kǝ shwaa am anab ndǝǝn laaɗaa mǝ Daa nǝ, baa a ndǝǝn ar ɗin ɗǝre kas, ɓe gwe mǝnǝ kǝ cìn a shikbish nkaa fwoshik mǝ Jesu kǝ toom fir mmǝnǝ.
1CO 11:28 Nǝ ret kǝ gurum shee kyamshin fin akuɗang wur se gill aas, kǝ shwaa am anab ɗi nǝn ndǝǝn laaɗaa mǝ Daa nǝ.
1CO 11:29 Mɓǝɗǝ katɗang baa gurum manshii kǝ shin mǝ Daa Jesu kǝ toom fin nǝ kas, ɗangɓe wu kǝ se gill aas kǝ shwaa am anab ɗi nǝ ndǝǝn laaɗaa mǝ Daa ni, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ kǝ jì aa ɗyeel nkaa fwoshik fin mmǝnǝ.
1CO 11:30 A nii le, ɗangɓe pak fuu mo a gok, kǝ baa pak mo kǝ ɓal kas, har pak fuu mo ɗes, mo kǝ murǝp.
1CO 11:31 Amma katɗang mǝ kyamsun fun mo azeen-nzeen, kǝ mǝ cìn mbii mon ndǝre-ndǝre ɓe baa Naan tokɗyeel mmun kas.
1CO 11:32 Amma Naan wur tokɗyeel mmun, kǝ wur kar mun, a mbǝkǝ taji wu ncanɗyeel ɗebish mmun ashak kǝ gurum ɗebish, ɗi mo ndǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, parkyes kǝ yil nǝ kas.
1CO 11:33 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɗyemnaa mo, katɗang wu kuur ashak mɓe Se Tong Ashak mǝ Daa, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu ɗarnaa shak.
1CO 11:34 Katɗang neenláa mmemee fuu, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ gwar mǝnǝ sese ntul fir akuɗang wur jì kuur nǝ. Mbeekǝ taji Naan wur canɗyeel ɗebish nkaa wun jir, a peekuur fuu nǝ. Pwoo nkaa koor mbii ɗi mo ɗee ɗi, ɓe see parɗǝ wen wul pee wun ɗi, ɗangɓe wen nsatpwoo nwun nkaa mo jir.
1CO 12:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, pwoo nkaa zuum ɗi Riin Naan wur shin ngurum. Baa wen rǝɓet kǝ wu nook manshii nǝ kas.
1CO 12:2 Wu man nǝ, kaaɗe gyet wu kuɗi a nenseyil nkùm mo, ɓe wuu seyil nkùm ɗe baa mo kǝ seen kas, shi ar mo shinǝ-shinǝ.
1CO 12:3 Wen rǝɓet kǝ wu man nǝ, baa mee gwe, ɗi wur katpwoo shi Riin Naan, wur mmak sat nǝnee <<Jesu canɗoor!>> kas, kǝ baa mee gurum mak cìn langtǝng nǝnee, <<Jesu wur a Daa.>> Katɗang baa wur mwaan a ndǝǝn Riin Naan kas.
1CO 12:4 Zuum ɗi Riin kǝ Naan wur shin ngurum mo, mo ɗi shinǝ-shinǝ, amma a Riin ɗemǝndong wur cin mo ngurum mo.
1CO 12:5 Ɗak mo ɗi shinǝ-shinǝ, amma Daa a mǝndong.
1CO 12:6 Man ɗi gurum moo cìn ɗak ɗishik mo shinǝ-shinǝ, ɗangbe a Naan ɗemǝndong wur cìn man nǝ ngurum mo, mbǝkǝ mo cìn ɗak nǝ ɗi.
1CO 12:7 Riin Naan wur kám shin ngurum mo ndǝǝn ar mo shinǝ-shinǝ, mbǝkǝ mo cìn ɗak ɗe nǝ mɓam niyee mo ɗi jir.
1CO 12:8 Mee gurum, ɓe Riin Naan nǝ shin a zuum mǝ man satpwoo nwur shi seen, kǝ mee gurum ɓe Riin nǝ shìn a zuum mǝ man mbii nwur.
1CO 12:9 Mee gurum, ɓe Riin nǝ shin a zuum mǝ cinzeen nwur, kǝ mee gurum ɓe Riin nǝ shin a iiko nwur mɓe bar nenchǝǝnkoom mo.
1CO 12:10 Mee gurum ɓe Riin Naan nǝ shin a zuum mǝ cìn mbii aapwoo nwur, kǝ mee gurum ɓe Riin Naan nǝ shin a iiko mu satpwoo Naan gwe nǝ. Mee gurum ɓe Riin wur shin a man mǝ ɓàkyit nzuum ɗe mo put a pee Riin Naan ɗi, kǝ riin ɗi baa mo put a pee Naan ɗi kas zak. Mee gurum ɓe Riin wu shin a zuum mǝ katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ ngwar mǝnǝ. Kǝ Mee gurum zak, ɓe wur shin a zuum ɗe mǝ manshii kǝ pǝring lǝpwoo mǝ gurum mo shinǝ-shinǝ gwe nǝ.
1CO 12:11 A Riin Naan ɗesǝ wur mǝndong, ɗi wur shin zuum ɗǝsǝ mo ngurum mo shinǝ-shinǝ zak, kaaɗe wur naa nǝ ret nwur nyit sǝ.
1CO 12:12 Kristi wur a kaa fwoshik kǝ gurum sǝ. Kaaɗǝ wu man nǝ, shin kǝ gurum nǝ kǝ ɓeep mo ɗes, amma jir kǝsǝ ɓe fwoshik kǝ gurum nǝ a mǝndong ɓejee ɗak, koo ɗi nǝ kǝ ɓeep mo shinǝ-shinǝ.
1CO 12:13 Mo cìn baptisma mmun jir a ndǝǝn Riin ɗemǝndong, aasǝ ɓe mu ɗee a ɗemǝndong, koo ɗi mun a nen Yahudi mo, koo ɗi baa mun a nen Yahudi mo kas, koo ɗi mun a kǝrem mo, kǝ koo ɗi mun a jeplu mo zak. Mun jir, ɓe muu ten mǝ shwaa a bwut Riin Naan ɗemǝndong.
1CO 12:14 Baa fwoshik kǝ gurum nǝ kǝ ɓeep a mǝndong ɓejee kas, amma nǝ kǝ ɓeep mo a ɗes.
1CO 12:15 Katɗang shii sat nǝnee, <<mbǝɗe baa wen a sar kas, ɓe baa wen a memee mɓut fwoshik kǝ gurum kas.>> Koo ɗe shii sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe baa nǝn nnook ɗee a memee mɓut ɓeep mǝ fwoshik kǝ gurum kas.
1CO 12:16 Kǝzak, katɗang ɓe kom sat nǝnee, <<mbǝɗe baa wen a yit kas, ɓe baa wen a memee mɓut fwoshik kǝ gurum kas.>> Koo ɗe kom sat pwoo mǝnǝ, ɓe baa kom nǝn nnook ɗee a memee mɓut shin kǝ gurum kas.
1CO 12:17 Katɗang ɗi fwoshik kǝ gurum nǝ a yit jir, ɓe ɗe gurum kǝ kǝlǝngpee a shi meyii? Katɗang ɗi fwoshik kǝ gurum a kom jir ɓejee, ɓe ɗe cirang gurum nkǝlǝng ɗu kǝ mbii mo ɗi yi?
1CO 12:18 Amma Naan wur leɓeep mo shinǝ-shinǝ ndǝǝn fwoshik kǝ gurum, kaaɗe wur naa nǝ ret nwur nyit sǝ.
1CO 12:19 Katɗang ɓe ɗi ɓeep nǝ a mǝndong ɓejee ɗak, ɓe ɗi fwoshik kǝ gurum nǝ a nneyi?
1CO 12:20 Kaaɗǝ ɓeep kǝ gurum mo ɗi ɗes, amma ɓe fwoshik kǝ gurum nǝ a mǝndong ɓejee ɗak,
1CO 12:21 mpeemǝnǝ, ɓe baa yit mmak sat nsar nǝ, <<Baa wen kǝn rǝɓet wii kas.>> Kǝzak, baa káa mmak sat nshii nǝnee, <<Baa wen kǝn rǝɓet wii kas.>>
1CO 12:22 Azeen, baa nǝ aasǝ kas, mɓeɗǝ rep ɓeep ɗi muu naa mo kaa baa mo kǝ ɓal kas sǝ, ɓe mo kǝkoop nǝ ɗes mɓe fwoshik kǝ gurum.
1CO 12:23 Kǝ muu tap kǝ ɓeep ɗi muu ɓák mo ɗes zam. Ɓeep ɗe mo mɓut nsun funu mo, ɗi baa mo ret naa kas, ɓe muu tap kǝ mo rǝret.
1CO 12:24 Ɗangɓe baa muu shin ɗeɗes mǝnǝ mɓeep fun ɗeret naa nǝ mo kas. A Naan wur tap le fwoshik kǝ gurum aasǝ, mbǝkǝ ɓeep ɗi baa mo kǝ ɓal kas, ɓe mu tap ɗi kǝ mo rǝret zak.
1CO 12:25 Mbǝkǝ taji mee ɓàkshak yool ndǝǝn fwoshik kǝ gurum kas. Amma koo a ɓeep ɗeɗangyi ɓe nii tap kǝ gǝnǝǝn.
1CO 12:26 Katɗang jeel taa nkaa mee ɓeep nǝ, ɓe koor ɓeep nǝ mo jir mon nshwaajeel nǝ. Amma katɗang mo kwoop mee ɓeep nǝ, ɓe koor ɓeep nǝ mo jir, mon ncìn retnyit ashak kǝ ɓeep mǝnǝ.
1CO 12:27 Wun jir wun a fwoshik kǝ Kristi, koo a weye ndǝǝn wun, ɓe wur a memee mɓut mɓeep fin.
1CO 12:28 nƊǝǝn Ekǝlisya, ɓe Naan wu kǝ bǝlǝp gurum mo le shinǝ-shinǝ. Ɗin nshee, ɓe wu kǝ bǝlǝp jeplep kǝ Jesu mo, ɗevǝl, ɓe wu bǝlǝp nensatpwoo Naan mo, ɗekun, ɓe wur kǝ bǝlǝp nenkám mo. Kǝ wur bǝlǝp nen cìn ɗak mǝ mbii aapwoo mo. Ɗangɓe wur kǝ bǝlǝp nen bar gurum mo, kǝ nenɓam gurum mo, nennaa gurum mo, mbǝkǝ mo cìn ɗak ɗi ndǝre-ndǝre, kǝ nnen katpwoo mo shi liispwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ zak.
1CO 12:29 Baa a gurum mo jir a jeplep kǝ Jesu kas. Baa a gurum mo jir mo a nensatpwoo Naan kas. Baa a gurum mo jir mo a nen kamkam kas. Baa a gurum mo jir mo cin dak ɗi mǝ aapwoo kas.
1CO 12:30 Baa a gurum jir moo mak barr gurum mo kas. Baa a gurum jir mo kǝ mak katpwoo shi liispwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ kas. Baa a gurum mo jir, ɗi moo mak yakshii mbii ɗi moo sat shi liispwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ kas.
1CO 12:31 Ɗangɓe nǝ ret kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo ɗee a nkaa zuum ɗi mo kǝkoop nǝ met ndǝǝn zuum ɗesǝ nǝ mo. Yaksǝ, ɓe wen nkám wun mee mbii ɗe nǝ ret kǝ wu cìn met koor mbii mo jir.
1CO 13:1 Katɗang wen mak katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mǝ gurum mo, kǝ mǝ nenlep Naan mo, ɗangɓe katɗang baa an kǝ wal ndǝǝn pǝtuup fen kas, ɓe wen ɗee a kaa wal tuul ɗe nǝn nfii sǝ, koo kaa wal kungguleng sǝ.
1CO 13:2 Katɗang ɓe Wen kǝ zuum mǝ satpwoo Naan nkaa mbii ɗe mo pǝ jì, kǝ wen manshii mbii ɗesǝsok mo, har kǝ koor seen mo jir, kǝ koo ɗi wen kǝ shinzeen ɗi nǝ le kǝ wen sat njwak mo yool aku, a peeɗe mo ɗi, ɓe katɗang baa wen kǝ wal ndǝǝn pǝtuup fen kas, ɓe baa wen a mee mbii kas, koo dǝɓen.
1CO 13:3 Koo ɗe wen shin long fen mo jir ngurum mo shi zuum, kǝ koo ɗe wen shin sen fen mbǝkǝ mo wus nǝ ɗi, ɓe katɗang baa wen kǝ wal kas, ɓe baa nii mee koop pee wen ɗi kas, koo dǝɓen.
1CO 13:4 Wal nǝ a gung mbii mo, kǝ naajeel gurum mo zak. Baa wal nǝ kǝ cìn zuur koo canjoom kas koo wup nsat kas.
1CO 13:5 Baa wal nǝ kǝ roop, koo toklong ngurum mo kas. Baa wal nǝ kǝ ɗar a nkaa mbii ɗe mo ret nǝ nyit ɓejee ɗak kas. Baa wal nǝ kǝ langtuup, koo nǝ wet nyaa shikbish ɗe gurum kǝ nǝ mputuup kas.
1CO 13:6 Baa wal nǝ kǝ kat retnyit kǝ mbii ɗebish mo kas, amma wal nii kat retnyit a ndǝǝn mbii ɗi mo azeen.
1CO 13:7 Wal nǝ kǝ gung ndǝǝn mbii mo jir, kǝ nii shinzeen ndǝǝn mbii mo jir zak. Wal nii canciin ndǝǝn mbii mo jir, kǝ nii yaa sat ndǝǝn mbii mo jir.
1CO 13:8 Baa wal nii kyes kas, har ngaa-ngaa. Amma satpwoo Naan nkaa mbii ɗe mo pǝ jì mon nɗel dǝm, kǝ zuum mǝ iiko mǝ katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, mon nɗel dǝm. Manshii mbii mo, ɓe mǝnǝ nɗel seet zak.
1CO 13:9 Azeen baa man fun nǝ a ɗe kǝgam kas, kǝzak, satpwoo Naan nkaa mbii ɗe mo pǝ jì, baa nǝ a ɗegǝgam kas.
1CO 13:10 Amma katɗang parɗi gwe ɗi wu a ɗegǝgam wu njì, ɓe mbii ɗi baa mo a ɗegǝgam kas, mon nɗel dǝm sǝ.
1CO 13:11 Kaaɗǝ gyet wen kuɗi a làa, ɓe wen kǝn katpwoo a kaa làa sǝ. Wen kǝn cìn a pan njep mo ndǝǝn pǝtuup fen, kǝzak, wen kǝn cìn mbii mo a kaa làa sǝ. Amma, yaksǝ kaaɗe wen a ngunan, ɓe wen yit ɗak ɗi mo a mǝ jep mo jir.
1CO 13:12 Mbii ɗi muu naa mo yaksǝ, ɓe muu naa mo a shir-shir kaaɗe muu naa muriin ndǝǝn mbii naayit ɗi baa nǝ naapee rǝret kas sǝ. Amma parmeeci ɓe mun nnaa mbii mo rǝret shi yit kǝ yit. Yaksǝ ɓe mbii ɗe wen man mo akáa-akáa ɓejee ɗak, amma parpuus mǝnǝ ɓe wen mman mbii mo ndǝre-ndǝre jir, kaaɗe Naan wur kǝ ten man wen sǝ.
1CO 13:13 Mbii mo ɗe kun, ɗe baa mon cham ɗel kas, mo a shinzeen, kǝ le pǝtuup, kǝ wal, amma wal nǝ ɗes met mmo jir.
1CO 14:1 Nǝ ret kǝ wu naa tong ndǝǝn wal, kǝzak, wu le pǝtuup fuu mo nkaa zuum ɗi Riin wur shin mo, met jir, ɓe a zuum mǝ satpwoo Naan nkaa mbii ɗi mon ncìn.
1CO 14:2 Koo a weyi ɗi wu kǝ katpwoo a shi mee lǝpwoo ɗecǝ, ɓe wur katpwoo aa Naan, baa wur katpwoo aa gurum mo kas. Mɓǝɗǝ baa mee gurum man mbii ɗi wu sat nǝ kas, wur sat a mbii ɗi mo a sǝsok ndǝǝn ɓal kǝ Riin.
1CO 14:3 Ɗangɓe koo a weyi, ɗewur sat a mbii ɗe Naan kǝcin nwur, mbǝkǝ wur sat ɗi ngurum mo, ɓe wur leshap aa gurum mo jir mmǝnǝ. Mbǝku wur ɓal kwak ɗi ngurum mo, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wur gang kwak mo ɗi, kǝ mbǝkǝ wur caa mo ɗi.
1CO 14:4 Ngwe ɗewur katpwoo a shi mee lǝpwoo ɗecǝ, wur ɓam a káa fin ɓejee. Amma gwe ɗi wur sat a pwoo ɗi Naan kǝ shin nwur, mbǝkǝ wur sat ɗi ngurum mo, ɓe wur ɓam a Ekǝlisya nǝ jir.
1CO 14:5 Wen rǝɓet kǝ wun jir, wu katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, amma ɗyen nwen nǝ, ɗi wun jir, wun nsat a pwoo ɗe Naan kǝ shin nwun, mbǝkǝ wu sat ɗe ngurum mo. Ngwe ɗi wur sat a pwoo ɗe Naan kǝ shin nwur mbǝkǝ wu sat ɗi ngurum mo, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ met gwar ɗi wur kǝ katpwoo shi mee lǝpwoo ɗecǝ, see koo katɗang ɓe mee gurum ɗi, ɗi wur mmak pǝring kǝ pwoo nǝ akuɗang, mbǝkǝ nǝ ɓam Ekǝlisya nǝ ɗi.
1CO 14:6 Yaksǝ ɗyemnaa mo, katɗang wen dǝm pee wun ɗi, ɗangɓe wen katpwoo kǝ wun a shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, ɓe kyet nghan kǝ mee koop nǝ pee wun ɗi wa? Katɗang baa nghan dǝm aa mee lep ɗepwoo nwun pee Naan ɗi, koo mee man, koo mee pwoo ɗi Naan wu kǝ shin nwen, mbǝkǝ nghan kám ɗi nwun kas, ɓe baa nǝ kǝ mee koop nǝ pee wun kas.
1CO 14:7 Koo ɗang a mbii cìn kook ɗi baa mo kǝ mee seen kas, kaa koor kǝ ndeng-ndeng sǝ, katɗang baa ngutaa nǝ, taa ɗoo nǝ rǝret kas, ɓe cirang ɗang gurum mmanshii kǝ kook ɗi gwar nii taa ɗi yi?
1CO 14:8 Kǝzak, katɗang baa ngutaa feer wu taa ɗoo nǝ rǝret kas, ɓe cirang ɗang gurum mon ɗak sut mɓe lek yi?
1CO 14:9 Nǝ aasǝ zak kǝ wun, katɗang wu sat mbii mo a shi lǝpwoo ɗecǝ ɗi baa gurum mo manshii nǝ rǝret kas, ɓe cirang ɗang gurum mon mmanshii kǝ mbii ɗi wuu sat nǝ ɗi yi? Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe pwoo ɗi wuu sat nǝ, ɓe kut kǝ mang nǝ ɗel dǝm kǝ nǝ sǝ zhaap.
1CO 14:10 Azeen lǝpwoo mo ɗi shinǝ-shinǝ ndǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, kǝ koo a ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ kǝ manshii nǝ.
1CO 14:11 Ɗangɓe katɗang baa wen manshii lǝpwoo ɗi mee gurum kǝ sat kas, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ a mǝzep pee wen ɗi, kǝ wen ɗee a mǝzep pee gwar mǝnǝ ɗi zak.
1CO 14:12 Nǝ aasǝ zak kǝ wuwun. Kaaɗǝ wun wuu fes wu coor zuum mo ɗi Riin kǝ Naan wur kǝ Shin mo, ɓe wu gung kǝ wu cìn ɗak ɗi, a shi zuum ɗe mon ncìn mɓam mɓe ɗyik Ekǝlisya nǝ.
1CO 14:13 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ngwar ɗe wur katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, ɓe wu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), mbǝkǝ Naan wu shin zum mǝ man pǝring shii kǝ mbii ɗi wur nsat nǝ mo ɗi zak.
1CO 14:14 Mbǝɗe katɗang wen ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nNaan shi mee lǝpwoo ɗiiɗik, ɓe riin fen nii ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nǝ zak, ɗangbe baa pan fen nii koop nǝ kas.
1CO 14:15 Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe wen ncìn a meye? Wen nɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) shi riin fen, kǝ wen ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) shi pan fen zak. Wen ncìn kook ndǝǝn riin fen, kǝ wen ncìn kook nǝ shi pan fen zak.
1CO 14:16 Katɗang waa ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang Naan ndǝǝn kuur a shi riin fwaa ɓejee, ɗi baa gurum mo kǝlǝng mbii ɗi gha sat nǝ kas, ɓe cirang mon nsat nǝnee <<nǝ akǝse>> mɓe ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mǝ pǝlang ɗi gha sat nǝ ye? Mɓeɗǝ baa gurum nǝ mo man mbii ɗi gha sat nǝ kas.
1CO 14:17 Koo ɗang ɗi ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) fwaa mǝ pǝlang Naan nǝ ret nNaan nyit, ɓe baa nǝ ɓam gǝnang kas.
1CO 14:18 Wen pǝlang Naan, mɓeɗǝ wen kǝn leshap mo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ met nwun jir.
1CO 14:19 Ɗang be ndǝǝn kuur mǝ Ekǝlisya, ɓe ngyel wen satpwoo mo a paat ɓejee, ɗi gurum mon nkǝleng, kǝ nǝ kám mbii mo zak, met ɗi wen nsatpwoo mo ngal kaapaat shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ ɗe baa gurum mo manshii nǝ kas.
1CO 14:20 Ɗyemnaa mo, taji wu cìn pan kaa jep mo sǝ kas, wu ɗee kaa jep mo sǝ ndǝǝn mbii ɗebish mo, ɗangbe wu ɗee kaa nennan mo sǝ ndǝǝn pan fuu mo.
1CO 14:21 Mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<A shi gurum ɗi moo leshap ɗecǝ mo, <<kǝ a shi lǝpwoo kǝ mǝzep mo, <<ɓe wen nkatpwoo nen ɗesǝ mo, <<a ɗishik ɗangbe jir kǝsǝ, <<ɓe baa mon nkǝlǝng wen kas, Daa wur sat aasǝ.>>
1CO 14:22 Katpwoo shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, nǝ ɗee a ɓee naa man mɓe nen ɗi baa mo shinzeen kas. Satpwoo ɗi Naan kǝ shin mmee gurum, mbǝkǝ wu sat mbii ɗi ngurum mo, mǝnǝ a mɓe nen ɗi mo kǝ ten shinzeen mo, baa mǝnǝ a mɓe nen ɗi baa mo kǝ shinzeen kas.
1CO 14:23 Mɓǝmǝnǝ katɗang nenyil Ekǝlisya mo kaat ashak, ɗangɓe koo weyi wu ɗoom leshap shi lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ, ɓe katɗang nen ɗi baa mo man mee mbii kas, koo nen ɗi baa mo kǝ shinzeen kas, mo jì ɗel ndǝǝn kuur fuu nǝ, ɓe wu pan nnǝ, mon nsat nǝ wun a nentar mo kas aa?
1CO 14:24 Ɗangɓe katɗang ɓe koo weyi wur sat a pwoo kǝ Naan, ɓe katɗang mee gurum ɗi baa wur kǝ shinzeen kas, koo gwar ɗi baa wur man mee mbii kas, wur jì ɗel ndǝǝn kuur fuu nǝ. Ɓe pwoo Naan ɗi wuu sat nǝ, nǝn nle kǝ gwar mǝnǝ man nǝnee azeen-nzeen ɗi a ngushikbish, ɓe pwoo ɗewur kǝlǝng nǝ, nǝn mɓiyang pǝtuup fin.
1CO 14:25 Mbii ɗi gwar mǝnǝ kǝ pan mo a sǝsok ndǝǝn pǝtuup fin, ɓe mon nkàa put agaak, kǝ har wu ntaa nyil, kǝ wu seyil ɗi nNaan, kǝ wur nsat ɗi nǝ, azeen-nzeen Naan wu ɗi nnaar fuu.
1CO 14:26 A mbii ɗe wen kǝn rǝɓet sat nǝ nɗesǝ, ɗyemnaa mo. Katɗang wu kuur ashak mɓe seyil nNaan, ɓe memee fuu kǝ kook mǝ kwoop Naan, kǝ memee kǝ mbiikám, kǝ memee kǝ pwoo ɗi Naan kǝ woo nwur, kǝ memee kǝ satpwoo ndǝǝn lǝpwoo ɗecǝ mo, kǝzak, memee kǝ pǝring mbii ɗi moo sat shi lǝpwoo ɗecǝ nǝ mo. Wu yit kǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo jir, mo ɗee a mbii ɗe mon cìn ɓal Ekǝlisya nǝ.
1CO 14:27 Katɗang mee gurum mo man katpwoo shi lǝpwoo ɗecǝ mo, ɓe gurum mo kaa vǝl koo kun sǝ, mo katpwoo nǝ ndangshak-ndangshak, ɓe nǝ a tǝng mee gurum pǝring shii mbii ɗe mo sat nǝ ngurum mo jir.
