1CO 14:28 Ɗangɓe katɗang baa mee gurum ɗi, ɗewur mmak yakshii mbii ɗe ngusatpwoo shi lǝpwoo ɗecǝ nǝ wu sat kas, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ ɗok tǝtǝk ndǝǝn kuur Ekǝlisya nǝ, ɓe see wu leshap mǝnǝ a ndǝǝn pǝtuup fin kǝ Naan ɓejee ɗak.
1CO 14:29 Gurum mo kaa vǝl koo kun sǝ, mo leshap ɗe Naan wur kǝ shin mo, mbǝkǝ mo sat nǝ ɗi ngurum mo. Nǝ ret kǝ kwoor nǝ mo ɓeetshii kǝ mbii ɗi mo sat nǝ.
1CO 14:30 Ɗangɓe katɗang Naan wu shin mee pwoo mee gurum ɗewur ɗi ndǝǝn kuur nǝ, mbǝkǝ wur sat ɗi ngurum nǝ mo, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ gwar ɗewur nkaa leshap nshee sǝ wur ɗok tǝtǝk.
1CO 14:31 Wu mak satpwoo kǝ Naan nǝ ngurum mo ndangshak-ndangshak, mbǝkǝ koo weyi ɓe wu kám mee mbii ɗi kǝ nǝ ɓam pǝtuup nwur ɗi zak.
1CO 14:32 Zuum mǝ satpwoo Naan, nǝ a nder kǝ ngusatpwoo Naan nǝ.
1CO 14:33 Baa Naan wur a Naan ɗewur cìn mbii mo a ɓurish kas, amma wur a Naan ɗewur tap cìn mbii mo ndangshak-ndangshak ndǝǝn ryang. ndǝǝn Ekǝlisya mǝ nen ɗeɓang mo jir,
1CO 14:34 nǝ ret kǝ, mat mo ɗok tǝtǝk ndǝǝn kuur mǝ Ekǝlisya mo. Baa mu rǝɓet mmo, kǝ mo leshap ɗi kas. Amma nǝ ret kǝ, mo sham kǝ káa fur mo, kaaɗi Wàar kǝ nen Yahudi mo sat sǝ.
1CO 14:35 Katɗang mo rǝɓet man mee mbii, ɓe mo tal pǝ mish fur mo ntul. Mɓeɗi nǝ a mbii shweeppee, mbǝkǝ mat katpwoo ndǝǝn kuur kǝ Ekǝlisya mo.
1CO 14:36 Ɗe mo shee pwoo kǝ Naan nǝ a shi wun aa? Koo a wun a nen ɗi pwoo Naan nǝ wul pee wun ɗi ɓejee ɗak yi?
1CO 14:37 Katɗang mee gurum kǝ pan nǝ, wuɗin a ngusatpwoo Naan, koo wuɗi kǝ zuum ɗi nǝ a mǝ Riin, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ gwar mǝnǝ man nǝ, mbii ɗe wen kǝn ran nwun nǝ a Wàar Naan.
1CO 14:38 Katɗang gwar mǝnǝ chii kǝlǝng pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ mo, ɓe taji wu kǝlǝng wu kas.
1CO 14:39 Mɓǝmǝnǝ, ɗyemnaa mo, wu le pǝtuup fuu mo a nkaa satpwoo kǝ Naan, kǝ taji wu cíi katpwoo ndǝǝn lǝpwoo mo shinǝ-shinǝ kas.
1CO 14:40 Amma wu cìn koo a meyii ndǝǝn ɗyen, kǝ ndangshak-ndangshak zak.
1CO 15:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, yaksǝ ɓe wen rǝɓet baa lepan ɗi nwun, nkaa pwoo ɗeret, ɗe gyet wen kǝn sat nǝ nwun, ɗe gyet wuu lap nǝ, kǝ ɗe wu shinzeen, ɗi wuu ɗar a nkaa nǝ zak.
1CO 15:2 A shi pwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ nǝ, ɓe wuu kat ɓam wur katɗang ɓe wu yaa pwoo ɗi nghan kǝn sat nǝ nwun ɓalɓal. Katɗang aasǝ kas, ɓe shinzeen fuu nǝ a ɗebuu.
1CO 15:3 Mbii ɗi gyet nghan kǝn lap nǝ, ɓe wen kǝ shin a nǝ nwun, ɗi nǝ kǝ kwoop nǝ hakyeng nǝ Kristi wu muut mɓe shikbish fun mo, kaaɗi mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ.
1CO 15:4 Mo wum wur, ɓe wur yool a peemúut par shii ɗekun, nchiit kǝ mbii ɗi mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan sǝ.
1CO 15:5 Wur shee kámshin fin mPita, ɗangɓe wu kámshin fin njeplep fin ɗekaapaat baavǝl sǝ mo.
1CO 15:6 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe wur kámshin fin nenshínzeen mo, ɗi mo met kambǝlpàat a nook mǝndong. Pak nenyil ɗe jì mo naa wu, mo ɗi ɗes ɗe mo kuɗin kǝ seen, amma pak mo kǝ ten murep.
1CO 15:7 Wur kámshin fin nJemis zak, kǝ jeplep fin nǝ mo jir.
1CO 15:8 Ɗangɓe a peekyes nǝ, ɓe wur kámshin fin nwen zak, wen ɗe an a kaa làa ɗe mo taa làa, ɓe baa tar làa nǝ kǝ wul kas sǝ.
1CO 15:9 Mɓeɗi nghan a ɗelee mɓut jeplep kǝ Jesu nǝ mo. Baa ɗi nǝ ret kǝ mo pet wen a memee mɓut jeplep Jesu mo kas, mbǝɗe gyet wen kǝn shin jeel Ekǝlisya Naan.
1CO 15:10 Amma mɓe ɗeret Naan, ɓe wen ɗe, a agwe ɗe wen a nǝ yaksǝ sǝ. Ɗǝret ɗesǝ ɗe Naan wu shin nwen, nǝ kǝ cìn ɗak ɗes ndǝǝn wen. Har wen kǝn cìn ɗak shiɓal met jeplep fin nǝ mo jir. Ɗangɓe jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa a wen cìn ɗak mǝnǝ mo kas, ɗangɓe a ɗeret Naan ɗe nǝ cìn ɗak ndǝǝn pǝtuup fen.
1CO 15:11 Nǝ aasǝ, koo ɗi gyet, a Wen satpwoo nǝ, koo ɗi gyet a mo satpwoo nǝ, ɓe muu sat a mbii ɗemǝndong, kǝ wun wuu shinzeen a pwoo mǝnǝ.
1CO 15:12 Katɗang moo satpwoo nǝ, Kristi wur kǝ yool a peemúut, ɓe a me le ɗang pak fuu moo sat nnǝ, baa mee yool a peemúut ɗi mɓe nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mo kas yi?
1CO 15:13 Katɗang baa mee yool a peemúut ɗi, mɓe nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp kas, ɓe nǝ kám nǝ, baa Kristi wur kǝ yool a peemúut kas mmǝnǝ.
1CO 15:14 Katɗang ɓe baa ɗi Kristi wur kǝ yool a peemúut kas, ɓe pwoo ɗeret, ɗi muu sat nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu, kǝ ɓe ɗe shinzeen fuu nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu zak.
1CO 15:15 Ɓe ɗi mǝ ɗee a nen cìn langtǝng mǝ ɗung mo nkaa Naan, mɓeɗǝ muu cìn langtǝng nkaa Naan nǝ, a Naan wur yool kǝ Kristi a peemúut. Amma katɗang ɗi nǝ azeen-nzeen nnǝ, baa nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mon nyool a peemúut kas, ɓe baa Naan wu kǝ yool kǝ Kristi a peemúut kas mǝnǝ zak.
1CO 15:16 Katɗang baa nen ɗi mo kǝ murǝp mon nyool kas, ɓe baa Kristi wur kǝ yool kas zak.
1CO 15:17 Katɗang ɗi baa Kristi wur kǝ yool a peemúut kas, ɓe shinzeen fuu nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu, ɓe ɗe har yaksǝ, wuu tong ɗi a mɓut shikbish fuu mo vit.
1CO 15:18 Ɓe ɗi nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mɓut Kristi, mo kǝ ɗee a ɗiilǝloom mo mmǝnǝ zak.
1CO 15:19 Katɗang ɗi canciin fun ndǝǝn Kristi nǝ a mɓe seen ɗi mǝ yil ɗiisi ɗak, ɓe ɗi mǝ ɗee a mbii naajeel, met koor gurum mo jir.
1CO 15:20 Yaksǝ Naan wur kǝ yool kǝ Kristi a peemúut azeen-nzeen. A wur a ɗinshee, mǝ yool a peemúut, mǝ nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mo jir.
1CO 15:21 Kaaɗǝ gyet, muut nǝ ɗel ndǝǝn yil ɗǝsǝ, a mɓe ngumǝndong, nǝ aasǝ zak, ɓe a mɓe ngumǝndong, ɓe Naan wur nyool kǝ gurum ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mo a peemúut zak.
1CO 15:22 Mɓeɗǝ a mɓe Adam ɓe gurum mo jir mo murǝp, nǝ aasǝ zak, a ndǝǝn Kristi ɓe gurum mo jir mon nyool a peemúut kǝ seen.
1CO 15:23 Ɗangɓe koo meye ɓe mo a ndangshak-ndangshak. A Kristi wur a ɗinshee mǝ yool a peemúut akuɗang. Katɗang wur mbaajì, ɗangɓe nen wur mon nyool a peemúut zak.
1CO 15:24 Ɗangɓe peekyes kǝ yil nǝn njì wul, ɓe Kristi wur nshin mulki nǝ nNaan puun, aɓwoon ɗi wur kǝ ten twe koo a mulki, kǝ iiko, kǝ koo a ɓal ɗeɗang ye.
1CO 15:25 Mɓǝɗǝ tǝng Kristi wur ncìn mulki nǝ har parpuus ɗe Naan wur nle shaarlek kǝ Jesu mo ɗee nder shii fen.
1CO 15:26 Shaarlek ɗe wur ntu nǝ a peekyes nǝ, a muut.
1CO 15:27 Mɓǝɗǝ Naan wur kǝ ten le mbii mo jir nder shii fen. Kaaɗǝ mo kǝ sat sǝ nǝnee, <<mo kǝ le mbii mo jir nder shii fen.>> Ɓe nǝ ɗee agaak nnǝ, baa a Naan ɗee nder fir kas, amma Naan wur kǝ le mbii mo jir nder kǝ Kristi.
1CO 15:28 Dangbe, aɓwoon ɗi mo kǝ le mbii mo jir, nder mulki mǝ Naan, ɓe Làa nǝ wur shikáa fen, wur nleshin fen nder kǝ Naan. Naan ɗi wur le mbii mo jir nder Kristi, mbǝkǝ Naan wur se mulki ɗi nkaa mbii mo jir.
1CO 15:29 Yaksǝ, katɗang ɓe ɗe baa mee yool a peemúut ɗi kas, ɓe ɗi nen ɗe moo cìn baptisma mmo a koppee kǝ nen ɗi mo kǝ murǝp, ɓe mon nkat a meye? Katɗang ɗi baa mee yool a peemúut ɗi kas, ɓe a me le ɗangɓe gurum moo cìn baptisma a koppee kǝ nenmuut mo ye?
1CO 15:30 Kǝzak, ɓe ɗi a me le ɗangɓe muu lappee, kǝ muu shwaajeel ɗi kǝsǝ shidaar-shidaar yi?
1CO 15:31 Ɗyemnaa mo, wen kǝn naa muut, koo a puus ɗeɗang yi. A roop ɗi wen kǝnǝ ndǝǝn wun, ɗi nǝ a seen fun ndǝǝn Kristi Jesu, Daa fun, a nǝ le ɗang wen sat pwoo mǝnǝ.
1CO 15:32 Katɗang ɗi gyet wen cìn lek ashak kǝ luwayil mo nyil Afisus a mbe pan mǝ gurum ɗak, ɓe lǝɓet ɗi wen nkat nǝ a me yi? Katɗang ɓe baa mo yool kǝ nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp a peemúut kas, <<Ɓe wu yit kǝ mu se, mu shwaa, mbǝkǝ dǝɗaar ɓe mǝ murǝp ɗi.>>
1CO 15:33 Taji wu yit kǝ mee gurum ngwam wun kas. Katɗang gurum kǝ mwaan ashak kǝ nenɗebish mo, ɓe mǝse fin nǝn nɗee a ɗebish zak.
1CO 15:34 Wu baa wu jì ndǝǝn pan fuu mo kaaɗi nǝ ret kǝ wu cìn sǝ, kǝ wu nook cìn shikbish. Wen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, baa pak fuu mo man Naan kas. Wen kǝn sat ɗiisi a mbǝkǝ nǝ shweep wun ɗi.
1CO 15:35 Meeɓe, mee gurum ntal nǝnee, <<Chinarang ɗangɓe nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp, mon mbaa yool ɗi a peemúut kǝ seen yi? Mon nyool a shi nkan fwoshik ɗeɗang yi?>>
1CO 15:36 Waa mwen! A man nǝ, katɗang a kop cirem ndǝǝn yil, ɓe see cirem nǝn nwam, ɗangɓe àas mbii ɗi a kop nǝ kàa put.
1CO 15:37 Katɗang a kop mee cirem nyil, ɓe baa waa kǝ iiko nkaa nǝ kas, amma waa kǝkop a àas nǝ ɓejee ɗak. Bishmee ɓe, nǝ a àas shwaa, kas meeɓe mee cirem ɗeɗik.
1CO 15:38 Ɗangɓe Naan wur nshin mee fwooshin ɗi nnǝ, kaaɗe wur kǝ ten le nǝ sǝ. Koo àas cirem ɗeɗangyi, ɓe Naan wur ntap shin fwooshin kǝ nǝ ɗík.
1CO 15:39 Baa nan mo a nchiit-nchiit jir kas. Gurum mo kǝ nan muru ɗyik, kǝ luwa mo kǝ nan muru ɗyik, kǝ nyer mo kǝ nan muru ɗyik, kǝ pupwap mo kǝ nan muru ɗyik zak.
1CO 15:40 Mun ɗi kǝ fwoshik ɗi mo a mǝ ɗengnaan, kǝ mun ɗi kǝ fwoshik ɗi mo a mǝ yil ɗesǝ zak. Amma fwoshik fun ɗi mo a mǝ ɗengnaan, ret kǝ ɗeɗes kǝ mo ɗík zak kǝ fwoshik fun ɗe mo a mǝ yil ɗesǝ.
1CO 15:41 Ret ɗeɗes mǝ puus nǝ ɗík, ret kǝ ɗeɗes mǝ tar nǝ ɗík, kǝ mǝ zar mo ɗík zak, jir kǝsǝ, ɓe pak ret kǝ ɗǝɗes, mǝ zar nǝ moo met nshak zak. Mo ɗe kǝ ɗeɗes fur mo shinǝ-shinǝ.
1CO 15:42 Nin nɗee aasǝ zak, parpuus ɗi nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murep, mon nyool a peemúut. Kaaɗǝ mo wum gurum, ɓe fwoshik fin nǝ wam, amma kaaɗe Naan wu nyool kǝ gurum a peemúut, ɓe baa fwoshik fin nǝn nwam ɗi zak kas.
1CO 15:43 Kaaɗǝ mo wum gurum, ɓe nii bish naa, kǝ baa nǝ kǝ ɓal kas, amma parpuus ɗe Naan wur nyool kǝ nǝ a peemúut, ɓe nǝn yool a ndǝǝn ɗǝɗes, nǝn nret naa zak.
1CO 15:44 Kúm gurum ɗi moo wum nǝ aa fwoshik mǝ nan ɓejee ɗak, ɗangɓe parpuus ɗi Naan wur nyool kǝ gurum a peemúut, ɓe nǝ ɗen a fwoshik mǝ riin. Kaaɗǝ fwoshik ɗi nǝ a mǝ nan nǝ ɗi sǝ, ɓe azeen-nzeen fwoshik ɗe nǝ a mǝ riin nǝ ɗi zak.
1CO 15:45 Mo kǝ ten ran ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Naan wur shee le Adam wur a gurum ɗeseen.>> Amma Adam ɗe mǝ kyes nǝ, wur a Riin, kǝ wur shin seen ngurum mo.
1CO 15:46 Baa gyet a gwe mǝ riin wur shee jì kas, amma gyet a gwe mǝ nan shee jì ɗangɓe gwe mǝ Riin kǝ waaji.
1CO 15:47 Gwar ɗe gyet Naan shee le wur, ɓe gyet Naan ɗak wur a shi yil, ɗangɓe gwar ɗevǝl nǝ wur tong aɗeng sham ɗi.
1CO 15:48 Nen ɗi mo a mǝ yil nǝ, ɓe mo a kaa gwar ɗi gyet Naan shee ɗak wur shi yil nǝ sǝ. Ɗangɓe nen ɗi mo a mǝ ɗeng, ɓe mo a kaa gwar ɗi gyet wur tong aɗeng sham ɗi sǝ.
1CO 15:49 Kaaɗǝ muu lep a fwoshik ɗi nǝ a kaa mǝ gwar ɗe gyet Naan ɗak wur a shi yil sǝ, ɓe mun nyool mǝ lep a fwoshik ɗe nǝ a kaa mǝ gwar ɗewur tong aɗeng sham ɗi sǝ zak.
1CO 15:50 Ɗyemnaa mo, wen kǝn sat nwun agaak nǝ, baa gurum ndǝǝn mǝse mǝ nan kǝ toom, mak sekoop mǝ mulki Naan kas. Kǝ baa mbii ɗewam, nǝn mmak sekop a koppee kǝ mbii ɗi baa nii cam wam kas, zak.
1CO 15:51 Wu lekom, kǝ wen sat mee mbii ɗe nǝ a sǝsok ɗi nwun. Baa mun jir mun mmurep kas, amma Naan wur nchǝǝr kǝ fwoshik fun nǝ mo jir.
1CO 15:52 Kǝlak kaa ɗyaapyit (kup yit chǝǝr wang) sǝ, parpuus ɗi mon ntàa feer ɗi mǝ kyes nǝ, ɓe nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murep, mon nyool kǝ seen. Baa mon mbaa wam ɗi zak kas. Ɗangɓe mon nchǝǝr kǝ fwoshik fun nǝ mo jir.
1CO 15:53 Mɓǝɗǝ nǝ a tǝng parpuus mǝnǝ, ɓe fwoshik fun ɗi mo a mǝ wam, mon nlep sun ɗi baa mǝnǝ mon cham wam kas zak, kǝ sun fun ɗi mo a mǝ muut, ɓe baa mon cham murǝp kas zak.
1CO 15:54 Aɓwoon ɗi fwoshik fun ɗi mo a mǝ wam, mo lep fwoshik ɗi baa mon cham wam kas, kǝ fwoshik fun ɗi mo a mǝ muut, mo lep fwoshik ɗi baa mon cham murǝp kas zak. Ɗangɓe sǝmpwoo ɗi mo kǝ ten ran nǝ ndǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan nǝn ngam ɗi, ɗe nǝ sat nǝnee, <<Mo kǝ see koorong kǝ muut hakyeng kǝnding-nding.
1CO 15:55 Muut, koorong fii nǝ a nneyi? Muut, ɓal fii ɗi wii twe gurum mo ɗishik sǝ nǝ a nneyi?>>
1CO 15:56 Ɓal mǝ twapee kǝ muut nǝ a shikbish, kǝ a mbǝ Wàar ɗangɓe shikbish nǝ kat iiko.
1CO 15:57 Ɗangɓe yaksǝ, mǝ pǝlang Naan, ɗewur shin se koorong mmun ndǝǝn Daa funu Jesu Kristi.
1CO 15:58 Mɓǝmǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo, wu ɗar ɓalɓal. Taji wu le kǝ mee mbii tǝr wun kas. Ɗangɓe wu sat a ncìn ɗak mǝ Daa shidaar-shidaar, mbǝɗe wu man nǝ, koo a ɗak ɗeɗangyi ɗe wuu cìn nǝ mɓe Daa, ɓe baa nǝn cham ɗee a mbii ɗebuu kas, koo dǝɓen
1CO 16:1 Yaksǝ, ɓe pwoo nkaa kok shool ɗi wun ntul nǝ mɓe ɓam nen Naan ɗe mo nyil nJudiya, nǝ ret kǝ wu cìn kaaɗe gyet wen kǝn sat Ekǝlisya ɗi mo ndǝǝn yil nGalati mo cìn sǝ.
1CO 16:2 Koo a puus Láadi ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ koo weye wu le mee shool mɓe shin zuum nciit-nciit kǝ ɓal fin, mbǝkǝ katɗang parpuus ɗe wen ndem pee wun ɗi, ɓe taji wu ɗee ncak mee shool kas.
1CO 16:3 Katɗang wen ndem wul pee wun ɗi, ɓe wen nshin lepran Nen ɗe wuu ten wu bǝlǝp mo, mbǝkǝ mo dǝm ɗi kǝ shool nǝ yilkaam nJerusalem.
1CO 16:4 Katɗang wen naa nǝ ret, kǝ wen dǝm nJerusalem, ɓe mon ndem ashak kǝ wen zak.
1CO 16:5 Wen njì pee wun ɗi, aɓwoon ɗe wen kǝn dǝm nyil mMasidoniya, mɓeɗǝ wen kǝn Rǝɓet yaa ar nǝ ɗel dǝm a nyil mMasidoniya nǝ.
1CO 16:6 Meeɓe wen mpan nyém pee wun ɗi mɓe rep pee mo nlǝr ɗak, kǝ meeɓe wen ntong pee wun ɗi mɓe tar kut, mbǝkǝ wu ɓam wen ɗi, a ar mwaan fen, koo pee ɗeɗang ye ɗi wen ndem ɗi.
1CO 16:7 Ɗyeen nwen nnaa wun zam, baa a ɗe wen nnaa wun, ɓe wen a ar ɗel dǝm kǝlak-kǝlak kas. Katɗang Daa wur rǝɓet, ɓe wen ncanciin mɓe dǝm tong pee wun ɗi pan pong.
1CO 16:8 Amma wen ntong mpeesǝ nyil Afisus, har see parpuus mǝ serǝɓet mǝ Pentikos.
1CO 16:9 Mɓǝɗǝ, pee ɗe nwen ɗes mpee ɗesǝ, mbǝkǝ wen katpee cìn ɗak ɗeret, kǝ ɗi nii koop nǝ ndǝǝn nyil Afisus nǝ zak. Koo ɗe gurum mo ɗes moo cii ɗak fen nǝ.
1CO 16:10 Katɗang Timoti wur dǝm wul pee wun ɗi, ɓe wu kaat wur rǝret nnaar fuu. Taji wu le mee kǝǝrmuut yaa wur kas, mɓeɗǝ wur kǝ cìn a ɗak kǝ Daa, kaaɗe wen kǝn cìn sǝ zak.
1CO 16:11 Taji mee gurum ɓák wur kas, amma nǝ ret kǝ wu ɓam wur ndǝǝn mwaan fin, mbǝkǝ wur sekyeen ɗi kǝ mwaan fin nǝ ndǝǝn ryang, kǝ mbǝkǝ wur waaji ɗi pee wen ɗi zak, mɓeɗǝ wen kǝn leyit mɓe naa waaji fin ashak kǝ pak ɗyemnaa mo zak.
1CO 16:12 Yaksǝ, pwoo nkaa ɗyemnǝǝn fun, Apolos, ɗí wen kǝn satpwoo nwur shiɓal nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ wur dǝm naa wun ashak kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn mo. Baa gyet ɗyeen nwur ndǝm pee wun ɗi nciit kǝ mǝnǝ kas, ɗangɓe katɗang wur nkatpee, ɓe wur ndǝm pee wun ɗi.
1CO 16:13 Wu tong shi gongpee, kǝ wu ɗar ɓalɓal ndǝǝn shinzeen fuu. Wu ɗee a nengung mo ndǝǝn pǝtuup, kǝ nenɗeɓal mo.
1CO 16:14 Wu cìn ɗak fuu mo jir ndǝǝn wal.
1CO 16:15 Wu man nǝ, gyet a nentul kǝ Stifenas mo a nen ɗi gyet mo shee shinzeen ndǝǝn nyil Akaya, kǝ mo shin sut fur mo mɓe cìn ɗak ɗi mo ɓam nen Naan mo ɗi zak. Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ wun ɗyemnaa fen mo,
1CO 16:16 kǝ wu mwaan nɗang mǝse kǝ gurum mo kaa mǝnǝ mo sǝ, kǝ wu mwaan nɗang koo weyi ɗe wu shin káa fin, mɓe cìn ɗak mǝ ɓam wur, ashak kǝ mo.
1CO 16:17 Nǝ fes ret nwen nyit zam, mɓe jì kǝ Stifenas kǝ Fortunatus, kǝ Akaikus, mɓeɗǝ mo jì kǝ mbii mo nwen a koppee fuu, mbii ɗe baa ɗí wen kǝ mo kas.
1CO 16:18 Kǝzak, mo caa wen, kaaɗe ɗi moo caa wuwun sǝ. Gurum mo kaa mo sǝ, nǝ ret kǝ wu shin ɗeɗes mmo.
1CO 16:19 Ekǝlisya ɗe mon nkwang yil mǝ Eshiya moo lep tokshik fur mo dǝm pee wun ɗi. Akwila kǝ Priskila, kǝ Ekǝlisya ɗi moo kaat ashak ndǝǝn tul fur, mo lep tokshik mǝ nen dǝm nɗang Jesu mo dǝm nwun ndǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa.
1CO 16:20 Ɗyemnǝǝn fun, ɗi mo mpeesǝ, moo lep tokshik fur mo dǝm pee wun ɗi jir. Wu tok kǝ shak ndǝǝn wal kaa mǝ nen dǝm ndang Naan mo sǝ.
1CO 16:21 A wen Pool, kǝn ran tokshik ɗesǝ nwun, shi sar fen.
1CO 16:22 Koo ngwar ɗeɗangyi ɗe baa wur wal nDaa kas, ɓe wu yit kǝ gwar mǝnǝ ɗee a mbii caan Naan. Daa fun wur mbǝ waaji.
1CO 16:23 Ɗǝret kǝ Daa fun Jesu nǝ tong ashak kǝ wun jir.
1CO 16:24 Wal fen nǝ tong ashak kǝ wun jir ndǝǝn sǝm kǝ Kristi Jesu. Nǝ aa sǝ.
2CO 1:1 Lepran desǝ nǝ put a nsar Pool laalǝp mǝ Kristi Jesu, shi reɓet Naan, kǝ nsar kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun nǝ Timoti. Wen kǝn lep lepran desǝ nǝ dǝm pee Ekǝlisya joon Naan ɗi moo nKoronti, kǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu ɗi mo nɗǝǝn yil Akaya jir.
2CO 1:2 Ɗeret, kǝ ryang mǝ Naan puun fun, kǝ mǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi mo tong ashak kǝ wun.
2CO 1:3 wen kǝn pǝlang Naan puun Daa fun Jesu Kristi. Puun ɗi wur gam kǝ kussuk mǝ naajeel. Naan ɗi wur a nguɓam mun jir.
2CO 1:4 A wur ɓam mun mɓut njeel fun mo jir, mbǝkǝ mǝ katpee ɓam nen ɗi moo shwaajeel mu shinǝ-shinǝ shi ɓam ɗi mu mǝ kat nǝ pee Naan ɗi sǝ zak.
2CO 1:5 Kaaɗe mu shwaajeel ɗes, nɗǝǝn jeel ɗe Kristi wur kǝ shwaajeel sǝ, bǝ Naan wur mɓam mun ɗes nɗǝǝn Kristi aasǝ zak.
2CO 1:6 Katɗang mu shwaajeel, bǝ nǝ a mbǝ gang pǝtuup fuu mo, kǝ nǝ a mbǝ ɓam fuu zak. Katɗang Naan wur ɓam mun, bǝ nǝ a mbǝ ɓam wun zak, ɗi nǝn nle kǝ wu gung caan jeel ɗi wuu shwaa nǝ mo, kaa mun sǝ zak.
2CO 1:7 Mbǝmǝnǝ bǝ canciin fun ɗi nǝ nɗǝǝn wun, baa nǝ mak yoon kas, koo lee. Pe gyet di mu man nǝ, kaaɗi wuu shwaajeel ashak kǝ mun sǝ, bǝ wun nkat ɓam ashak kǝ mun aasǝ zak.
2CO 1:8 Ɗyemnaa mo, muu reɓet kǝ mǝ le nwun npan, nkaa jeel ɗi mǝ shwaa nǝ nɗǝǝn yil Eshiya. Gyet jeel nǝ fes ten mun toon-toon hakyeng, har gyet nǝ met mmun mɓal, kǝ har gyet mu put kǝ pǝtuup fun mo nǝ, baa mun mbar kas.
2CO 1:9 Kǝ gyet mǝ naa kaa mo can a ɗyeel tukáa mmun sǝ, ɗang nǝ cìn aasǝ, a mbǝkǝ taji mu gángkáa fun a nkaa sun fun mo kas, amma mu gángkáa fun nǝ mo a nkaa Naan ɓejee ɗak. Naan ɗi wur yool kǝ gurum mo a peemúut.
2CO 1:10 Naan wur ten put kǝ mun nɗǝǝn muut nǝ, kǝ wur mbǝ put kǝ mun nɗǝǝn muut nǝ zak. Mun mǝ shinzeen nǝ, wur waa put kǝ mun nɗǝǝn muut nǝ ryang zak.
2CO 1:11 Wu ɓam mun shi ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) fuu mo, mbǝkǝ gurum mo ɗes mo pǝlang Naan ɗi mbǝ mun, mbǝ ɓam ɗi Naan wur cam cìn nǝ mmun. Pe ɗi Naan wur lap ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) ɗi gurum mo ɗes moo cìn nǝ mbǝ mun.
2CO 1:12 A mbii ɗe mu canjoom ɗikǝ nɗesǝ, apan ɗi nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo kǝ cìn langtǝng nǝ, tong fun nɗǝǝn yil desǝ nǝ a shi pǝtuup mǝndong, pǝ Naan, kǝ pee wun ɗi zak. Baa a shi mee seen ɗi nǝ a mu gurum mo kas, amma a shi ɗeret mǝ Naan.
2CO 1:13 Baa mu ran a mee pwoo ɗeluk nwun nɗǝǝn ran nǝ kas, ɗang a pwoo nkaa mbii ɗe wun mmak tang nǝ, bǝ wun mmanshii nǝ zak. Wen canciin nǝ, wun mmanshii nǝ rǝret.
2CO 1:14 Kaaɗe wuu ten wu manshii nǝ lee sǝ nǝ, wun mmak canjoom shi mun, kaaɗe mumun ncanjoom shi wun sǝ zak, parɗe Daa fun Jesu wur njì nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ zak.
2CO 1:15 A mbǝɗe gyet wen naa nǝ ret aasǝ, a nǝ le ɗang gyet wen kǝ reɓet dǝm pee wun ɗi nshee, mbǝkǝ wu kat ɗeret ɗi kaa yit vǝl sǝ.
2CO 1:16 Wen kǝn reɓet taa pee wun ɗi, a ar dǝm mMasidoniya, kǝ katɗang wen dǝm mMasidoniya nǝ, bǝ wen njì taa pee wun ɗi zak, mbǝkǝ wu ɓam wen ɗi a ar dǝm nyil nJudiya.
2CO 1:17 Ashee! Kaaɗe di wen reɓet cìn kǝsǝ, bǝ wen cìn a mbii ɗe nkan mmǝnǝ aa? Aa koo, wu yee nǝ wen kǝn cìn mbii a buubuu, kaaɗi gurum mǝ yil nǝ moo cìn sǝ yi? Ɗe wen nsat nǝnee, <<Ii, Ii>> ɗangɓe nbwoon, bǝ wen waa sat nǝnee, <<haiyoo, haiyoo>> Zak aa?
2CO 1:18 Kaaɗe Naan wur a nguzeen sǝ, bǝ pwoo ɗe muu sat nwun, baa nǝ a <<Ii>> Kǝ <<haiyoo>> Kas.
2CO 1:19 Pwoo ɗi gyet Silas kǝ Timoti kǝ wen, mu sat nwun nkaa Jesu Kristi làa Naan, bǝ baa pwoo mǝnǝ a Ii, koo haiyoo kas. Amma nɗǝǝn Naan, bǝ koo a pǝrangye, bǝ pwoo mǝnǝ a <<Ii>>
2CO 1:20 Pe gyet ɗi pwoo ɗe Naan wur tuweerpwoo mo jir, bǝ mo gampwoo mǝnǝ mo a nɗǝǝn Jesu, kǝ a mbǝ Jesu ɗangɓe muu sat nǝnee, <<Nǝ aasǝ>> Zak mbǝkǝ mo le Naan ɗi a ɗeɗes.
2CO 1:21 A Naan ɗi wur bǝlǝp mun le ɗyik, a wur le mun ashak kǝ wun nɗǝǝn Kristi.
2CO 1:22 Wur bii naa man wur nkaa mun, nǝ mun a mu wur mo. Wur shin Riin wur ɗeɓang mmun nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo, mbǝkǝ Riin nǝ kám ɗi mmun mbii ɗe wur le nǝ mmun a kyeen.
2CO 1:23 Amma wen pet Naan a langtǝng fen nǝ, mbii ɗe di nǝ le kǝ wen nook dǝm nKoronti nǝ, a mbǝkǝ taji wen lejeel nwun kas.
2CO 1:24 Baa muu gung a mbǝkǝ mu le tǝng ɗi nwun nkaa mbii ɗi wu shinzeen nnǝ kas koo lee, mbǝɗe wuu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen nǝ. Amma muu cìn ɗak ashak kǝ wun, mbǝkǝ wu kat retnyit ɗi.
2CO 2:1 Wen lepan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fen nǝ, baa wen mbaa dǝm pee wun ɗi kas, mbǝkǝ taji wen wàt pǝtuup nwun.
2CO 2:2 Katɗang bǝ wen wàt pǝtuup nwun, bǝ a wii nɗee ɗi a ɗe wur nle retnyit nwen yi? A wun nen ɗi wen wàt pǝtuup nwun, bǝ a wun ncaa wen.
2CO 2:3 A mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ wen ran-ran nǝ nwun, mbǝkǝ katɗang wen jì pee wun ɗi, bǝ taji wen kat mee mbii wàt pǝtuup mɓut nwun, nen ɗi wu le retnyit nwen kas. Wen shinzeen nwun jir nǝ, retnyit fen nǝ a muu jir zak.
2CO 2:4 Wen ran-ran nǝ nwun a shi pǝtuup ɗeewuwat hakyeng, kǝ shi yitmwaa, kǝ jeel ɗes zak. Wen ran-ran desǝ, baa a mbǝkǝ wen wàt pǝtuup ɗi nwun kas, amma a mbǝkǝ wu man ɗi nǝ, wen wal nwun zam.
2CO 2:5 Katɗang mee ngwe wàt pǝtuup mmee gurum, bǝ baa ngwe mǝnǝ tǝkook a pǝtuup mǝnǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, amma wur tǝkook aa pǝtuup muu, koo a pǝtuup mǝ pak fuu mo. Baa ɗyen nwen nsatpwoo shiɓal nkaa ngwe mǝnǝ kas.
2CO 2:6 Mpee nkaan ngwe mǝnǝ, bǝ kar ɗe wuu ten shin nwur, nǝ mak.
2CO 2:7 Amma yaksǝ, bǝ ngyel wu fwo ɗi ngwar mǝnǝ, mbǝkǝ wu ɓam wur ɗi, mbǝkǝ taji pǝtuup ɗe wat wur nǝ waa sǝǝt daampee nwur hakyeng.
2CO 2:8 Mbǝmǝnǝ wen ɗang pee wun, wu sǝǝt wu kám wal fuu moo nwur.
2CO 2:9 Gyet wen ran-ran nǝ nwun, a mbǝkǝ wen cam wun ɗi, kǝ wen man ɗi nǝ, kyet wun a nen cìn mbii mo, nɗǝǝn ɗyen jir wo?
2CO 2:10 Koo ngwe ɗeɗangyi ɗi wu fwo nwur, mbǝ mee ɗebish ɗe wur cìn, bǝ wen nfwo ngwe nǝ aasǝ zak. Katɗang bǝ mee mbii mǝ fwo nǝ ɗi, bǝ wen nfwo ngwe mǝnǝ a mbǝ wun, mbǝ ɗeret Kristi.
2CO 2:11 Mbǝkǝ taji Gujwan kat mee lǝɓet nɗǝǝn mun kas, mbǝɗe baa seen wur ɗebish mo a ɗesǝsok mmun kas.
2CO 2:12 Kaaɗe wen baaji nTrowas mbǝ satpwoo nkaa Kristi ngurum mo, bǝ wen kat Daa wur kǝ wang ar mbǝ wen.
2CO 2:13 Jir kǝsǝ, bǝ baa pǝtuup fen nǝ kat retnyit kas, mbǝɗe baa wen kat ɗyemnǝǝn fen Titus ɗi mpǝmǝnǝ kas. Mbǝmǝnǝ bǝ gyet wen sat ɗang-mukaat mmo, bǝ wen ɗel dǝm nyil Masidoniya.
2CO 2:14 wen pǝlang Naan, ɗe a wur kǝ ɓwet mun shidaar-shidaar, kǝ mu ɗee ɗi a koorong mo, mbǝ ɗeret Kristi. A shi mun, bǝ wur pwǝǝr man Kristi ɗe nǝ a kaa mbii ɗe nǝ kǝ toos shangshang sǝ, koo a mpee ɗeɗangyi.
2CO 2:15 Pe gyet ɗi pee Naan ɗi, bǝ mun a kaa toos deshang mo, mǝ Kristi, pǝ nen ɗe mo kat ɓam, kǝ nen ɗe mo a ar loom.
2CO 2:16 A mǝ peekyes nǝ nɗesǝ, ɗu ɗevǝl nǝ a ɗu ɗe mǝ wam, mǝ muut ɗi nǝ dǝm a peeloom. Amma a mu ɗinshee nǝ nɗesǝ, nǝ a fwaap deshang mǝ seen ɗi nǝ dǝm a peeseen. A wii mmak mang toon mbii ɗesǝ mo yii?
2CO 2:17 Mɓeɗe baa mun a kaa pak gurum ɗe moo satpwoo Naan nǝ a mbǝ kat lǝɓet mǝ shool kas. Pwoo munu nǝ a mǝndong, mbii ɗi Naan wur sat mmun, bǝ mu sat a pwoo mǝnǝ dǝǝn zeen ntoom Naan aasǝ, kaa kǝrem Kristi mo sǝ.
2CO 3:1 Yaksǝ, bǝ mun nwaa mǝ ɗoom kwoop a káa fun zak aa? Kyet mu reɓet mee ran nkaa mu mǝ langtǝng dǝm pǝ wun ɗi, koo ran mǝ langtǝng nkaa wun ji pǝ mun ɗi, kaaɗǝ pak gurum moo kǝ cìn sǝ wo?
2CO 3:2 Wun shikáa fuu, a wun a ran fun, ɗi mon cin langtǝng ɗishik nǝ. Mo joon ran nǝ nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, mbǝkǝ koo wii wur man nǝ ɗi, kǝ wur tang ɗi zak.
2CO 3:3 Nǝ kám agaak nǝ, a Kristi shikáa wur ran-ran desǝ nǝ mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, ɗangɓe wur lep nǝ nsar fun. Baa mo ran-ran desǝ nǝ a shi ink kas, kǝ baa mo ran nǝ a nkaa sulet mǝ ngǝk kas. Amma mo ran nǝ a nɗǝǝn pǝtuup gurum mo, shi Riin Naan ɗi wur mmeen har ngaa-ngaa.
2CO 3:4 Muu sat pwoo mǝnǝ, a mbǝɗe mu gàngkàa nkaa Naan nɗǝǝn Kristi.
2CO 3:5 Baa mee mbii nɗǝǝn mun, ɗi nǝ mak le kǝ mu sat nǝ, mǝ cìn mbii desǝ mo a shikáa fun nǝ kas. Ɗak desǝ nǝ a ɓal ɗi mu mak cìn pak mbii mo, put a pee Naan ɗi.
2CO 3:6 Mbǝɗe a wur le kǝ mǝ ɗee a nen cìn ɗak mǝ ɓǝlemcuk shi toom Naan ɗepwoo, baa a shi Wàar ɗerǝran mo kas, amma a shi Riin. Wàar ɗerǝran nǝ jì kǝ muut, amma Riin mǝ Naan wur shin seen.
2CO 3:7 Gyet mo ran Wàar Mosis nǝ mo a nkaa sulet mǝ ngǝk mo, kǝ Kaaɗe gyet Naan shin Wàar nǝ mo mMosis, bǝ ɗeɗes mǝ Naan jì put agaak. Koo ɗi gyet mǝlep mǝ yit Mosis nǝ kyes, bǝ baa gyet nen Yahudi mo mak tǝǝr yit fur mo nkaa yit Mosis kas, mbǝ peeɓang ɗi nǝ ɗes nǝ. Katɗang bǝ gyet Wàar mǝ Mosis ɗi nǝ jì kǝ muut nǝ jì aa ɗeɗes aasǝ,
2CO 3:8 ɓe nǝ a tǝng ɗak mǝ Riin mǝ Naan nǝn nɗes met mǝ Wàar nǝ.
2CO 3:9 Katɗang bǝ mo le ɗak mǝ Wàar ɗi nǝ jì kǝ loom a ɗeɗes, bǝ azeen-nzeen ɗak mǝ Riin ɗi nǝn njì kǝ ɗeret mǝ Naan, nǝ a ɗeɗes met ɗak mǝ Wàar nǝ hakyeng.
2CO 3:10 Nɗǝǝn desǝ, bǝ wu naa nǝ, mbii ɗi gyet nǝ a ɗeɗes, bǝ mbii ɗi nǝn ntong ɗi har ngaa-ngaa nǝ fes met ɗi gyet yam nǝ.
2CO 3:11 Katɗang bǝ mo kám nǝ, mbii ɗi ndung ɗel dǝm a ɗeɗes, bǝ mbii ɗi nǝ ntong ɗi har ngaa-ngaa nǝn nɗen kǝ ɗeɗes met ɗi nǝ ndung ɗel dǝm nǝ, ɗes hakyeng.
2CO 3:12 Mbǝɗe mun kǝ canciin nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ aasǝ, bǝ muu satpwoo fun shiɓal agaak hakyeng.
2CO 3:13 Baa mun a kaa Mosis sǝ kas, ɗi gyet wur paa yit wur shi fwaat, mbǝkǝ taji nen Yahudi mo naa kyes ɗeɗes, mǝ mǝlep mǝ yit wur ɗi nǝn nɗel dǝm sǝ kas.
2CO 3:14 Mbǝɗe gyet pan fur nǝ mo a ɗeduduur har mbǝ cicinsǝ. Katɗang mo ɗoom tang pwoo Naan ɗesǝǝr, bǝ fwaat paapee desǝ nǝ paa nǝ, kǝ nǝ kutdi, a ɗepǝpaa pee mo ɗi. See katɗang gurum shinzeen nKristi ɓejee, ɗangɓe moo mmak mang fwaat nǝ waa kǝ nǝ.
2CO 3:15 Azeen-nzeen har cicinsǝ, katɗang mo ɗoom tang Wàar mǝ Mosis nǝ mo, bǝ fwaat desǝ, nǝ kǝ paa pǝtuup fur mo ɗi vit.
2CO 3:16 Amma katɗang mee gurum cǝǝr pee Daa ɗi, bǝ abet, mon mmang fwaat nǝ baa kǝ nǝ aku pee ngu nǝ ɗi.
2CO 3:17 Daa wur a Riin, kǝ peeɗe Riin Daa nǝ ɗi, bǝ gurum mo ɗee a mukáa fur.
2CO 3:18 Yaksǝ, mun nenseet nɗang Jesu mo jir, bǝ mo mang fwaat ɗi nǝ paa yit fun mo ba kǝ nǝ aku. Yaksǝ bǝ gurum moo naa a ɗeɗes kǝ Daa nɗǝǝn tong fun nǝ mo, kǝ wur cǝǝr kǝ mun, kǝ mǝ ɗee ɗi kaa wur sǝ, nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes wur ɗi nǝ nkaa wurang. Ɗesǝ nǝ put a pee Riin mǝ Naan ɗewur a Daa.
2CO 4:1 A Naan Wur cin ɗak mǝ Satpwoo wur ɗeret wo mun nɗǝǝn ɗeret mǝ kussuk wur. Mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ taji nǝ waam kwak mun kas.
2CO 4:2 Mu cii cìn ɗak ɗebish mo, kǝ mbii naashweep ɗe a sǝsok, kǝ mbii ɗe mo le naashweep ngurum mo jir. Baa mun ncìn ɗung ngurum mo, koo sat ɗung nkaa pwoo kǝ Naan kas. Ɗang mu sat zeen nǝ agaak, mbǝkǝ koo a wii, bǝ wur naa zeen fun nǝ di, nɗǝǝn ɗyen wur, nyit Naan.
2CO 4:3 Katɗang bǝ pwoo Naan ɗe muu sat nǝ a ɗepǝpaa, bǝ nǝ a pǝpaa a mɓee nen ɗe mo a ar loom ɓejee ɗak.
2CO 4:4 Baa mo shinzeen kas, a mbǝɗe mishkoom ɗebish mǝ yil desǝ wur kǝ paa yit fur mo, Mɓǝkǝ taji mo naa peeɓang mǝ pwoo ɗeret mǝ Kristi kas, ɗewur a ɗemǝndong kǝ Naan.
2CO 4:5 Mbǝɗe baa muu satpwoo nǝ ngurum mo nkaa fwoshik fun kas, amma a pwoo nkaa Jesu Kristi, ɗi wur a Daa, kǝ mun shikáa fun bǝ mu ɗee a kǝrem fuu mo mbǝ sǝm kǝ Jesu.
2CO 4:6 Naan wur kǝ ten sat nǝ, peeɓang nǝ put a nɗǝǝn peenkwoo, kǝ nǝ ɓangpee ɗi. A wur le kǝ nǝ ɓang pǝtuup fun mo, mbǝkǝ nǝ shin peeɓang ɗi mmun, kǝ mbǝkǝ mu man ɗeɗes Naan ɗi, nɗǝǝn yit Jesu Kristi.
2CO 4:7 Mun kǝ long ɗe mǝ Riin kǝ Naan nǝ, a nɗǝǝn Tuulwan. Shii kǝ mǝnǝ, a fwoshik fun mo, mbǝkǝ mo kám ɓal ɗeɗes desǝ nǝ ɗi, agaak nǝ, nǝ a mǝ Naan, kǝ baa nǝ a munu kas.
2CO 4:8 Moo tǝreng mun koo a nkwoop ɗeɗangyi, jir kǝsǝ, bǝ baa mo mpyan mun kas. Moo wuk mun, jir kǝsǝ bǝ baa kǝǝrmuut yaa mun kas.
2CO 4:9 Gurum mo lejeel mmun, jir kǝsǝ, bǝ pak gurum moo wal mmun. Moo hǝr mun car nyil, jir kǝsǝ, bǝ baa Mu murep kas.
2CO 4:10 Koo a pǝrangyi, bǝ mun a nɗǝǝn jeel mǝ muut, kaa caan kǝ muut ɗe gyet Jesu cìn sǝ, mbǝkǝ gurum mo naa mǝse kǝ Jesu nǝ ɗi nɗǝǝn fwoshik fun mo.
2CO 4:11 Kaaɗe mun ɗe mmeen sǝ, bǝ muu tong a tong mǝ muut mbǝ Jesu, mbǝkǝ mo kám mǝse kǝ Jesu nǝ ɗi, nɗǝǝn fwoshik fun, ɗe mo a mǝ muut sǝ.
2CO 4:12 Ɗesǝ nǝ kám nǝ, muut nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mun, amma seen nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn wun.
2CO 4:13 Mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan nǝnee, <<wen shinzeen, a nǝ le ɗangɓe wuu satpwoo.>> A mbǝɗe mun mǝ shinzeen nNaan aakǝsǝ, a nǝ le ɗang mu satpwoo zak.
2CO 4:14 Mu man nǝ, ngwe dǝ wur yool kǝ Daa Jesu a peemúut, nwur nyool kǝ mun ashak kǝ Jesu aasǝ zak, kǝ wur njì kǝ mun ashak kǝ wun ntoom wur zak.
2CO 4:15 Mbii ɗesǝ mo jir a mbǝ wun, mbǝkǝ ɗeret kǝ Naan nǝ wul ɗi mɓut ngurum mo ɗes, kǝ mbǝkǝ gurum mo ɗes mo pǝlang Naan ɗi mbǝ ɗeɗes wur.
2CO 4:16 Mɓemǝnǝ, bǝ baa nǝ waam mmun kas. Koo dǝ mun kǝ fwoshik ɗi nǝ a mu gurum, ɗe nǝ wam, amma jir kǝsǝ, bǝ koo puus ɗeɗangyi, bǝ moo le riin fun nǝ mo ɗee a ɗepwoo.
2CO 4:17 Mbǝɗe rep jeel ɗe mu shwaa nǝ a mbǝ rep pee lee ɗak, nǝn nkǝlak kǝ ɗel dǝm, kǝ nǝn njì kǝ ɗeɗes ɗe nǝ dǝm ngaa-ngaa, ɗe nǝ met mu sat, nǝ met jir.
2CO 4:18 Baa mu leyit fun nǝ mo nkaa mbii ɗe gurum moo naa nǝ yaksǝ kas, amma muu leyit fun nǝ mo a nkaa mbii dǝ baa mu mak naa nǝ yaksǝ sǝ kas. Mbǝɗe mbii ɗe gurum mo mak naa mo shi yit yaksǝ, ɓe a mo a mbii ɗe mo nkǝlak kǝ ɗel dǝm. Amma mbii ɗe baa gurum mo mak naa mo yaksǝ shi yit kas, a mo a mbii ɗe moo tong ɗi har ngaa-ngaa.
2CO 5:1 Yaksǝ bǝ mu man nǝ, katɗang bǝ fwoshik fun ɗe mun kǝ mo nɗǝǝn yil desǝ, mo wam, bǝ Naan wur kǝ ɗak mee fwoshik fun ɗe mon ntong ɗe har ngaa-ngaa nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan. A Naan wur ɗak fwoshik mǝnǝ mo shikáa wur.
2CO 5:2 Nɗǝǝn fwoshik fun, bǝ muu gwaar gwan, kǝ mu coor, mbǝkǝ Naan shin fwoshik fun ɗe mo a mǝ ɗengnaan sǝ ɗe mmun.
2CO 5:3 Mbǝɗe katɗang Naan cin fwoshik fun mǝnǝ mo mmun, bǝ baa mo mmak kat mun ngum kas.
2CO 5:4 Kaaɗe mu kutdi mu tong nɗǝǝn fwoshik fun ɗe nǝ. A mǝ yil nǝ, bǝ muu gwaar gwan mbǝ jeel ɗe mu shwaa. Baa a mbǝɗe nǝ, muu reɓet a ɓàkshak kǝ fwoshik fun ɗe mo a mǝ yil desǝ kas. Amma muu reɓet kǝ Naan shin fwoshik fun ɗe mo a mǝ ɗengnaan sǝ mmun. Ɓe fwoshik fun ɗe mo kǝ seen sǝ, mo nɗee ɗe a koppee kǝ fwoshik fun ɗe mo a mǝ muut yaksǝ.
2CO 5:5 A Naan wur ɗak mun, mbǝ cǝǝr ɗesǝ mo, kǝ wur kǝ ten shin Riin wur mmun, ɗe nǝ ɗee a ɓe naa man mǝ mbii ɗewur kǝ ɗak mo le mbǝ mun.
2CO 5:6 Mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ koo a pǝrangyi, bǝ mun kǝ shinzeen nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun, kǝ mu man zak nǝ, kaaɗe mu kutdi nɗǝǝn fwoshik fun ɗe mǝ yil desǝ, bǝ baa mun ashak kǝ Daa kas. Mu jong kǝ wur.
2CO 5:7 Muu tong nɗǝǝn yil desǝ nǝ a shi shinzeen, baa a shi mbii ɗe mu naa mo shi yit kas.
2CO 5:8 Azeen-nzeen mun kǝ shinzeen nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun, kǝ ɗyeen mmun mɓàkshak kǝ fwoshik desǝ nǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mu tong ɗe ashak kǝ Daa ntul.
2CO 5:9 Mbǝmǝnǝ bǝ koo ɗe mun ɗi nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, kǝ koo a nɗǝǝn yil ɗe nǝn ndung jì, bǝ ɗyen mmun kǝ mu cin a mbii ɗe mo ret nNaan nyit.
2CO 5:10 Mbǝɗe tǝng, mun jir, mun nɗar ntoom kǝ mbii tong mǝ tokɗyeel kǝ Kristi, mbǝkǝ koo a weyi ɓe wur nlap kwat mǝ ɗak ɗe wur kǝcin mo, bǝ wur kutdi nɗǝǝn shin mǝ yil desǝ. Kyet kwat nǝ a ɗeret aa? Aa koo a ɗebish yi?
2CO 5:11 A mbǝɗe mu manshii mǝ kǝǝr Daa, a nǝ le ɗang mu gung mbǝ dul gurum mo jì pee Kristi ɗi. Nɗǝǝn tong fun, bǝ Naan wur man rǝret hakyeng, kǝ mu canciin nǝ, wun wu man mun akǝsǝ zak, nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
2CO 5:12 Baa muu gung a mbǝkǝ mu waa mu baa mu sat mee langtǝng ɗe nkaa sun fun mo pee wun ɗi kas. Amma mu kám a ar nwun, mbǝkǝ wu cìn retnyit ɗe shi mun, kǝ mbǝkǝ wu katpee lappwoo ɗe nen ɗi moo canjoom a shi ɗeɗes fur mo. Baa a shi mǝse fur mo kas sǝ.
2CO 5:13 Mbǝɗe koo ɗe baa mun ɗe mɓut mǝse fun nǝ mo kas, bǝ mǝnǝ a mbǝ Naan, kǝ katɗang mun ɗi nɗǝǝn mǝse fun mo, bǝ mǝnǝ a mbǝ wun.
2CO 5:14 Yaksǝ, bǝ wal kǝ Kristi nǝ se mulki nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo mbǝ wun, kǝ mu man azeen nǝ, mee ngwe mǝndong wur kǝ muut mbǝ gurum mo jir. Mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ gurum mo jir mo cam muut zak.
2CO 5:15 Wur muut a mbǝ gurum mo jir, mbǝkǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ lap seen wur, bǝ taji mo waa baa tong ɗi a mukáa fur. Zak kas. Amma mo tong a mǝ ngwe ɗewur kǝ muut mbǝ mo, kǝ mo waa yool kǝ wu a peemúut mbǝ mo zak.
2CO 5:16 Mbǝmǝnǝ, yaksǝ, bǝ baa mu kutdi mu naa tong kǝ gurum a shi yit ɗe mǝ yil desǝ kas. Ɗe mu naa Kristi a shi shin ɗe mǝ yil ɗesǝ, amma yaksǝ, bǝ baa mu kutdi mu naa wur a shi fwoshik ɗe mǝ yil sǝ kas.
2CO 5:17 Koo ngwe ɗeɗangyi ɗe wur tong nɗǝǝn Kristi, ɓe ngwe mǝnǝ kǝ ɗee a ɗepwoo. Mbǝɗe mǝse wur ɗesǝǝr mo kǝ ɗel dǝm jee, kǝ koo mii nǝ kǝ ɗee a ɗepwoo zak.
2CO 5:18 Mbii desǝ mo jir, a cìn Naan, ɗe wur cǝǝr kǝ mun shaarlek wur mo, mbǝkǝ mu ɗee ɗi a shaar wur mo shi Kristi. Wur cin ɗak ɗesǝ mmun, mbǝkǝ mu cǝǝr kǝ gurum mo, ɗi mo a shaarlek wur mo, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗi a shaar wur mo zak.
2CO 5:19 A pwoo ɗe mun nkaa sat nǝ desǝ nǝ, Naan wur nkaa le gurum ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ, kǝ mo ɗee a shaar wur. Baa Naan wur tang shikbish kǝ gurum nǝ mo nkaa mo kas, kǝ wur kǝ lepwoo mu cǝǝr kǝ gurum ɗe mo a shaarlek wur mo, kǝ mo ɗee a shaar wur mo nsar fun zak.
2CO 5:20 Mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ yaksǝ mun a jeplep mǝ Kristi mo, ɗe Naan wur pǝrep gurum mo a shi mun. Mu ɗang pǝ wun a koppee kǝ Kristi, wu yit kǝ Naan wur cǝǝr kǝ wun, kǝ wu ɗee ɗi a shaar wur mo.
2CO 5:21 Wur ɗe baa wur man cìn mee shikbish kas, bǝ Naan le wur mang shikbish fun mo, mbǝkǝ nɗǝǝn wur bǝ mu ɗee ɗi a nen ɗin ndǝre mo, nyit Naan.
2CO 6:1 Kaaɗe mun mu cìn ɗak ashak kǝ Naan zak, bǝ mu ɗang pee wun, mbǝkǝ taji wu lap ɗeret kǝ Naan wu le nǝ a mbii ɗebuu kas.
2CO 6:2 Wu kǝlǝng mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ sat nǝnee, <<Kaaɗe pee mǝ cìn ɗeret nǝ wul, ɓǝ wen cìn ɗeret nwaa. Kaaɗe puus ɓam nǝ jì wul, ɓǝ wen ɓam waa zak.>> Azeen-nzeen wen sat nwun nǝ, cicinsǝ nǝ a pee mǝ lap ɗeret mǝ Naan! Kǝzak, cicinsǝ nǝ a puus mǝ kat ɓam pee Naan ɗi.
2CO 6:3 Baa mu le mee mbii canshii mmee gurum kas, mbǝkǝ taji mo ɓees ɗak fun nǝ ɗi kas.
2CO 6:4 Amma koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi, bǝ muu kám ngurum mo azeen-nzeen nǝ, Mun a kǝrem mǝ Naan mo, kǝ muu kám nǝ, mun a kǝrem kǝ Naan mo shi gung kǝ shwaajeel ɗes, kǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn mbii lejeel mo.
2CO 6:5 Muu shwaanas, kǝ mo naa mɓwoot mun, kǝ muu tong mɓut nenyool kǝ ɓǝlep mo, kǝ ɗak mo ɗes, kǝ tong shi gongpee, kǝ tong kǝ neen, kǝ ciin saam zak.
2CO 6:6 Muu kám zeen fun shi mǝse ɗeret kǝ man, kǝ gung shi mǝse ɗe mǝ naajeel nɗǝǝn Riin Ɗeɓang, kǝ shi wal mu azeen-zeen zak,
2CO 6:7 kǝ shi pwoo ɗe mo azeen-nzeen, kǝ shiɓal kǝ Naan. Mun kǝ zeen nǝ, kaa leelek ɗin ndǝre mo sǝ, nsarse kǝ nsarkul fun mo.
2CO 6:8 Gurum mo le mun a ɗeɗes, amma pak moo waa lejeel mmun zak. Pak gurum moo kwoop mun, ɗang pak moo waa ɓees mun zak. Moo le mun a kaa nenɗung mo sǝ, ɗang mun a nensat zeen mo.
2CO 6:9 Gurum mo le mun a kaa baa mo man mun kas sǝ, ɗang mun a ɗe mǝ man pee mo. Mu ɗee kaa muu mumurep sǝ, ɗang mun ɗi kǝ seen. Mo nǝrem mun, jir kǝsǝ, bǝ baa mo twe mun kas.
2CO 6:10 Mu ɗee kaa mun aa pǝtuup ɗeewat sǝ, ɗangɓe mun a mɓut nretnyit shidaar-shidaar. Mu ɗee kaa nenjeel mo sǝ, ɗang jir kǝsǝ, bǝ mu le kǝ gurum mo ɗes mo kat long. Mu ɗee kaa baa mun kǝ mee mbii kas sǝ, ɗang jir kǝsǝ, bǝ koo mbii ɗeɗangyi bǝ nǝ a munu.
2CO 6:11 Wun nen Koronti mo, wu man nǝ, baa mu sok mee mbii nwun kas. Gyet muu satpwoo nwun agaak mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun jir.
2CO 6:12 Baa gyet mu nook sat nwun mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun kas. Gyet a wun wu nook sat mmun mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
2CO 6:13 Wen ɗang pee wun kaa jep fen mo sǝ, mbǝkǝ wu woo mbii dǝ mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo mmun.
2CO 6:14 Taji wu ɓàlsuk ashak kǝ nen ɗe baa mo shinzeen nNaan kas. Mbǝɗe a mii ɓal ɗak ɗeret kǝ ɗak ɗebish yii? Kǝ a mii ɓal peeɓang kǝ peenkwoo yii?
2CO 6:15 Baa mee shaar ashak ɗe nnaar Kristi kǝ Gujwan kas. A mii ɓal ngushinzeen, kǝ ngwe ɗe baa wur shinzeen kas yi?
2CO 6:16 A mii ɓal Lu Naan ɗeɗes kǝ lu kùm yii? Pǝtuup fun mo a peeɗe Naan wur tong ɗi, Kaaɗe wur kǝ ten sat sǝ nǝnee, <<wen ntong ashak kǝ mo, kǝ wen mmwaan nnaar fu zak. Wen nɗee a Naan fu, kǝ mon nɗee a nen fen mo zak.>>
2CO 6:17 Mbǝmǝnǝ bǝ wu put aku, <<mɓut nen ɗe baa mo shinzeen kas, kǝ wu ɓàkshak kǝ mo zak, Daa Naan wur sat akǝsǝ. Taji wu tung mee mbii ɗe nǝ a ɗerap kas, ɗangɓe wen nlap wun.
2CO 6:18 Wen nɗee a puun fuu, kǝ wun nɗee a jep fen ɗemish mo, kǝ ɗe mat mo. A Daa ɗeɓal met jir, wur sat pwoo mǝnǝ.>>
2CO 7:1 Shaar fen mo ɗe wen wal nwun, kaaɗe Naan wur kǝ ten tuweerpwoo mbii ɗesǝ mo mmun akǝsǝ, bǝ nǝ ret kǝ mu lesun fun mo ɗee a ɗeɓang, nɗǝǝn koo a mbii ɗebish ɗeɗangyi, ɗe nǝ tǝkook kǝ nan fun mo, kǝ riin fun mo zak. Nǝ ret kǝ mu ɗee a nen ɗeɓang mo rǝret nɗǝǝn shiimwaan fun mo, mbǝ shin ɗeɗes nNaan.
2CO 7:2 Wu wang pǝtuup fuu mo mmun, mbǝɗe baa di mu cìn mee mbii ɗebish mmee gurum kas, kǝ baa mu tikook kǝ mee gurum kas zak. Baa di mu seen nkaa mee gurum kas.
2CO 7:3 Baa wen sat desǝ nǝ a mbǝkǝ wen le wun ɗi a nenshikbish mo kas, ɗang wen satpwoo ɗesǝ nǝ a mbǝɗe di wen kǝ ten sat nwun nǝ, mu wal nwun zam. Kǝ koo ɗe a nɗǝǝn muut, kǝ koo ɗe mun ɗi kǝ seen, bǝ mun ɗi ashak vit nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo.
2CO 7:4 Wen shinzeen nwun azeen-nzeen, kǝ wen kǝ cìn roop ɗes a shi wun zak. Har wu fes wu caa pǝtuup fen nǝ rǝret hakyeng. Jir kǝ jeel ɗe muu shwaa nǝ, bǝ wen nkaa cìn retnyit ɗes zam.
2CO 7:5 Kaaɗe gyet mu dǝm mu wul nyil mMasidoniya sǝ, ɓe baa gyet mu kat mee pee ɓwet sun kas. Gurum mo shin jeel mmun ɗes, koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi. Gurum mo ɓǝlep kǝ mun, kǝ gyet nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo, bǝ kǝǝrmuut nǝ ɗi zak.
2CO 7:6 Ɗangnaan wur shin ɓal kǝ wur caa pǝtuup mu nen ɗe baa mo ɓal mputuup kas. Gyet wur shin ɓal pǝtuup fun mo shi jì kǝ Titus.
2CO 7:7 Baa a jì kǝ Titus nǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, ɗang ashak kǝ ɗi gyet wu cìn caa pǝtuup wur, har wur sat mmun nǝ, wu coor mbǝ naa wen, kǝ wuu naajeel fen, kǝ nǝ, wun mɓwoon fen zak. Pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ mo sǝǝt le retnyit nwen ɗes hakyeng.
2CO 7:8 Koo ɗe gyet wen wàt pǝtuup nwun shi ran ɗe wen ran nwun sǝ, ɓe baa gyet nǝ daampee nwen, mbǝɗe wen ran-ran nǝ nwun kas. Gyet yam ɓe nǝ wàt pǝtuup nwen, mbǝɗe gyet wen naa nǝ, ran nǝn wàt pǝtuup fuu mo zam. Koo ɗi gyet nǝ wàt pǝtuup nwen a mbǝ rep pee mo lee ɗak.
2CO 7:9 Ɗang yaksǝ wen kat retnyit. Baa nǝnee mbǝɗe a ran nǝ le pǝtuup fuu mo tikook kas, ɗang a mbǝkǝ wu tuwap ɗi, mbǝ mbii ɗe mo le kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo tikook. Daa Naan wur reɓet a kyeet kǝ tikook kǝ pǝtuup mǝnǝ, mbǝɗe nǝ nle kǝ wu tuwap. Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe baa mu cìn a mee mbii ɗebish nwun kas.
2CO 7:10 Mbǝɗe kyeet kǝ pǝtuup ɗewat ɗi a Naan le, nǝ kǝ jì kǝ tuwap, kǝ nǝ jì kǝ kat ɓam zak. Baa nǝ le kǝ gurum mak sat nǝnee, <<katɗang ɗi wen oo!>> Kas. Ɗang pǝtuup ɗewat mǝ yil ɗesǝ, mǝnǝ kǝ jì aa muut.
2CO 7:11 Wu naa, mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ cìn kǝ pǝtuup ɗewat nǝ, nǝ le kǝ wu ɗak mǝse fuu mo azeen-nzeen. Kǝ nǝ le kǝ wuu reɓet kám agaak nǝ, baa gyet wu man mee mbii ɗebish kas, har nǝ kǝ le kǝ wu kat canciin. Nǝ le kǝ wu katɓal, kǝ nǝ le kǝ wu kat gung nɗǝǝn kar fuu zak. Mɓut mbii ɗesǝ mo, bǝ koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ kám azeen-nzeen nǝnee, << wuu mwaan a nɗǝǝn ɗeret.
2CO 7:12 Koo ɗe gyet wen kǝ ran-ran nwun, bǝ baa nǝ a mbǝ mee ngwe ɗe wur kǝ cìn shikbish kas. Kǝ baa nǝ a nkaa mee ngwe dǝ mo cìn ɗebish nwur kas. Ɗang wen ran-ran nǝ, a mbǝkǝ nǝ kám ɗi nwun agaak ntoom kǝ Naan, canciin fuu mbǝ mun.
2CO 7:13 A mbǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo, ɗangɓe gyet pǝtuup fun mo katɓal. Baa gyet nǝ gang a kwak fun mo ɓejee ɗak kas, ɗang mu kat retnyit ɗi kǝ ɗes, mbǝ retnyit kǝ Titus, mbǝɗe gyet wun jir wuu kaat wur shi retnyit.
2CO 7:14 Gyet wen kǝ ten canjoom fuu nwur, ɓe baa gyet mee naashweep yaa wen mbǝmǝnǝ kas. Mbii ɗe mu sat mo nwun sǝ, mo azeen-nzeen. Canjoom fun ɗe mu sat nTitus nkaa wun, nǝ azeen a kǝ sǝ zak.
2CO 7:15 Wur le pǝtuup wur nkaa wun jir met ɗeyam hakyeng. Kaaɗe wur yee nǝ, wun jir, wun a nen gyet ɗe wu lappwoo ɗewur sat mo nwun. Kǝ wu kaat wur shi retnyit, kǝ gyet wu cìn mbii ɗeret wur zak.
2CO 7:16 Wen kat retnyit mbǝɗe wen mak kǝk kaa nkaa wun rǝret hakyeng.
2CO 8:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, muu reɓet kǝ wu man pwoo nkaa ɗeret ɗe Naan wur shin nǝ Ekǝlisya ɗe mo nyil mMasidoniya.
2CO 8:2 Koo ɗe ɗi mo kǝ cam mo shi jeel ɗenaat, kǝ mo nkaa shwaajeel mǝ mbii mo zak, bǝ jir kǝsǝ, retnyit fur nǝ ɗes. Ɓǝ nǝ le kǝ mo cìn mbii ɗeret mbǝɗe mo shin mbii fur mo shi zuum, koo ɗe baa mo kǝ mee mbii ɗes kas.
2CO 8:3 Wen man azeen nǝ, mbii ɗe mo cin nǝ a nciit kǝ ɓal fur, har nǝ met ɓal fur, mbǝɗe mo shin nǝ a shi reɓet kǝ pǝtuup fur mo.
2CO 8:4 Moo ɗang pǝ mun ɗes hakyeng nǝ, mu shin pee nɗun kǝ mo leɗun mɓut nen ɗe mon ncìn ɓam mbǝ nen Jesu mo sǝ.
2CO 8:5 Har mo shin mbii mo ɗes met mbii ɗe mu lepan. Ɗang mo shee shin a pǝtuup fur mo nDaa, kǝ mun zak, nciit kǝ mbii ɗe Naan kǝ rǝɓet kǝ mo cìn.
2CO 8:6 Kaaɗe mu naa nǝ ret, bǝ mu lep Titus dǝm pee wun ɗi, mbǝɗe ɗi a wur shee cìn ɗak ɗeret desǝ nǝ nɗǝǝn wun, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ a wur nsǝǝt sekyeen kǝ ɗak nǝ.
2CO 8:7 Wun kǝ sekyeen nɗǝǝn koo a mbii ɗeɗangyii, har nɗǝǝn shinzeen, kǝ satpwoo, kǝ man, kǝ gung mbii mo ɗes, kǝ wal ɗi wun kǝ nǝ mbǝ mun. Nǝ ret kǝ wu sekyeen kǝ cìn ɗak ɗeret mǝ shin zuum shi pǝtuup mǝndong.
2CO 8:8 Baa wen kǝ le a mee wàar pee wun ɗi kas, ɗang nǝ a mbǝ kám gung ɗe nwun, mbǝkǝ wen man ɗi azeen nǝ, wal ɗe wun kǝ nǝ, mbǝ ɓam niyee mo, nǝ azeen.
2CO 8:9 Mbǝɗe wun kǝ man ɗeret mu Daa fun Jesu Kristi, koo ɗe gyet wur a ngulong, jir kǝsǝ, bǝ wur lekáa wur ɗee kaa ngujeel sǝ mbǝ wun. Mbǝkǝ nɗǝǝn jeel wur nǝ, ɓe wu ɗee ɗi a nenlong mo.
2CO 8:10 A pan mǝnǝ nkaa mbii nǝ nɗesǝ, nǝn nret kǝ yaksǝ bǝ wu sǝǝt koor mbii ɗe gyet wuu yaa cìn nǝ doontoom sǝ. Gyet a wun shee shin mbii, kǝ wun kǝ pǝtuup mu shin mbii hakyeng.
2CO 8:11 Nǝ ret kǝ wu kyes koor ɗak nǝ shi reɓet kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo, nciit kǝ ɓal fuu, kaaɗe gyet wu shee cin nǝ sǝ.
2CO 8:12 Katɗang ɓe mee gurum kǝ pǝtuup ɗe mǝ shin mbiizuum, ɓe Naan nlap mbiizuum kǝ ngwe nǝ nciit kǝ mbii ɗe ngwe nǝ shin nNaan. Baa Naan wur ntang a mbii ɗi ngwe nǝ nnǝ kas.
2CO 8:13 Baa wen sat pwoo mǝnǝ a mbǝkǝ pak gurum mo nook shin mbiizuum, mbǝkǝ nǝ toon ɗi wuwun kas.
2CO 8:14 Ɗang a mbǝkǝ mo le mbii mo ɗee ɗin ndǝre, bǝ wu ɓam mo yaksǝ, shi mbii kǝkat fuu mo, mbǝɗe baa mo kǝ mee mbii kas. Mbǝkǝ katɗang parpuus ɗe wu táa njeel, ɓe mo ɓam wun ɗi zak. Ɗesinǝ nǝ a mbǝkǝ mo shwap mbii mo ɗi nciit-nciit.
2CO 8:15 Kaaɗe mo kǝ ten ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Ngwe ɗewur chak ɗes, ɓe baa nǝn njar ɗes kaa wur kas, kǝ ngwe ɗewur chak lee, ɓe baa nǝn njar kat kaa wur kas.>>
2CO 8:16 wen pǝlang Naan, ɗe wur lepan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup kǝ Titus, mbǝkǝ wur ɓam wun ɗi, kaaɗe wen kǝn cìn wun sǝ.
2CO 8:17 Baa wur lap ii a mbǝ ɗang fun ɓejee ɗak kas, amma wur kǝ fes lepan wur, mbǝkǝ wur dǝm pee wun shi pan mukáa wur.
2CO 8:18 Muu lep wur dǝm pee wun ɗi ashak kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗi gurum moo fes shin ɗeɗes nwur, mbǝ satpwoo kǝ Naan nɗǝǝn Ekǝlisya mo jir.
2CO 8:19 Baa a mǝnǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, amma Ekǝlisya mo bǝlep wur, mbǝkǝ wur dǝm ɗi ashak kǝ mun, mbǝ dǝm kǝ mbiizuum ɗe muu shin nǝ, mbǝ le Daa a ɗeɗes, kǝ kám agaak nǝ, mun kǝ pǝtuup ɗe nǝ a mǝ ɓam zak.
2CO 8:20 Baa muu reɓet kǝ mee gurum fǝlǝp mun nkaa mbiizuum ɗesǝ, ɗe gurum moo shin nǝ shi pǝtuup mǝndong, ɗe mun nkaa shin nǝ sǝ kas.
2CO 8:21 Mbii ɗe muu reɓet nɗesǝ, kǝ wu cìn mbii mo ɗi ndǝre-ndǝre, baa a ntoom kǝ Daa ɓejee ɗak kas, har kǝ ntoom kǝ gurum mo jir zak.
2CO 8:22 Muu lep ɗyemnǝǝn fun ashak kǝ mo zak. Mun kǝ cam ɗyemnǝǝn fun wur yit mo ɗes, ɓe mǝ kat wur a nguɗak zam nɗǝǝn ar mo shinǝ-shinǝ. Yaksǝ bǝ wur cìn ɗak nǝ waa met ɗeyam zak. Wur kǝ cìn ɗak ɗeret nǝ ɗes mbǝ ɓam wun.
2CO 8:23 Titus wur a shaarmwaan fen, ɗewur cìn ɗak ashak kǝ wen mbǝ ɓam wun zak. Mpee ɗyemnǝǝn fun desǝ mo, ɓe mo a nen ɗe Ekǝlisya mo lep mo, mbǝkǝ mo le sǝm kǝ Kristi ɗi a ɗeɗes.
2CO 8:24 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu kám wal fuu mmo, mbǝkǝ Ekǝlisya nǝ mo man ɗi azeen-nzeen nǝ, joom ɗe mu can nǝ mbǝ wun, nǝ a ndǝre azeen-nzeen.
2CO 9:1 Pwoo nkaa cin ɓam mbǝ nenseet nɗang Jesu mo, ɓe baa nǝ a tǝng kǝ wen ran mee pwoo nwun nkaa nǝ kas.
2CO 9:2 Mbǝɗe wen man sekyeen fuu, har wen kǝ canjoom shi wun ntoom kǝ nen Masidoniya mo. Wen sat mmo nǝ, gyet doontoom ɓe Ekǝlisya ɗin Akaya war kǝ ten ɗak set mbǝ cin ɓam. Rǝɓet fuu mbǝ shin mbiizuum ɗe wu shin nǝ ɓalkwak ngurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn mo zam.
2CO 9:3 Amma wen lep ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗesǝ mo dǝm pee wun ɗi, mbǝkǝ taji canjoom ɗe mu sat shi wun, nkaa mbii ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a mbii ɗebuu kas, ɗang mbǝkǝ wu tong ɗi shi ɗak suk, kǝ mbiizuum nǝ, kaaɗe gyet wen kǝn sat nwun nǝ, wu tong shi ɗak suk sǝ.
2CO 9:4 Mbǝɗe katɗang pak nen Masidoniya nǝ mo yool jì ashak kǝ wen, ɗangɓe mo jì kat baa wuu ɗak suk kas, bǝ naashweep nyaa mun, kǝ nǝn nsǝǝt yaa wun met nwen zak, mbǝɗe muu shinzeen nwun.
2CO 9:5 Nǝ akǝsǝ ɓe wen naa nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ wen ɗang ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗesǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mo shee dǝm pee wun ɗi nwen atǝleng, mbǝkǝ mo cak mbiizuum ɗe gyet wuu tuweer nǝ, wun nshin nǝ ɗi. Katbaa wen kǝn dǝm wul pee wun ɗi, ɓe mo kǝ ten chak mbiizuum nǝ mo. Ɓe nǝ kám nǝ, wu shin mbiizuum nǝ a shi reɓet kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo, baa a mee gurum le tǝng nwun kas.
2CO 9:6 Taji wu munsuk kas nǝ, ngwe ɗewur kop cirem lee nɗǝǝn maar wur, ɓe wur nɗiip ɗeɓen nǝ a lee ɗak. Ngwe ɗewur kop cirem ɗes, bǝ wur nɗiip ɗeɓen nǝ ɗes akǝsǝ zak.
2CO 9:7 Koo weyi ɓe wur cin mbii ɗewur kǝ pan mputuup mbǝ shin nǝ, baa a shi pǝtuup vǝl-vǝl kas, kǝ baa a gurum mo le tǝng nwur kas. Mbǝɗe Naan wur kǝ reɓet a ngwe ɗewur shin mbiizuum, a shi retnyit nɗǝǝn pǝtuup wur.
2CO 9:8 Naan wur kǝ ɓal ɗe wur nshin mbii mo nwun ɗes met mbii ɗe wuu reɓet mo. Mbǝkǝ koo a pǝrangyi, ɓe wu kat mbii ɗe wuu reɓet mo ɗi mbǝ suk fuu mo, kǝ mbǝkǝ wu katpee shin mbiizuum ɗi shi pǝtuup mǝndong mbǝ ɗak ɗeret mo jir.
2CO 9:9 Kaaɗe mo kǝ ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Wur shin mbii nenjeel mo shi zuum ɗes, kǝ shi pǝtuup mǝndong, Ɗeret wur nǝn ntong ɗe har ngaa-ngaa.>>
2CO 9:10 A Naan kǝ shin cirem ngumaar, kǝ a wur shin mbiise mu se zak. A wur nshin cirem nwun wu kop, kǝ a wur nle kǝ nǝ kàa wurang. Wur nle ɗeret nkaa ɗak fuu ɗin ndǝre, kǝ nǝ ɗes ɗi hakyeng.
2CO 9:11 Wur nle kǝ wu ɗee a nenlong mo koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi, mɓekǝ wu naa nshin mbiizuum ɗi shi pǝtuup mǝndong. Mbiizuum ɗe wun nshin nǝ, nǝ nɗee ngurum mo a mbii pǝlang pee Naan.
2CO 9:12 Mbǝɗe ɗak fuu ɗeret ɗesǝ nǝ, baa nǝ ɓam a nen Naan mo ɓejee ɗak kas, ɗang nǝ waa sǝǝt le kǝ gurum mo pǝlang Naan ɗes zam.
2CO 9:13 Ɗak fuu ɗeret desǝ nǝ kám nǝ, shinzeen fuu nǝ ɗar ɓalɓal hakyeng. Nǝn nle kǝ gurum mo le Naan a ɗeɗes, mbǝ mbiizuum ɗe wu shin mo ashak kǝ koor gurum nǝ mo shi pǝtuup mǝndong. Ɓe nǝ kám agaak nǝ, wuu lappwoo ɗeret mu Kristi nǝ azeen-nzeen.
2CO 9:14 A mbǝ wal ɗe gurum mo kǝ nǝ mbǝ wun, ɓe mo ncìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mbǝ wun, Mbǝɗe mo man nǝ, Naan wur kǝcin ɗeret nwun ɗes zam.
2CO 9:15 Wu yit kǝ mu pǝlang Naan mbǝ zuum ɗe wur shin mmun. Zuum ɗi nǝ met mɓal mu sat.
2CO 10:1 Wen Pool shikáa fen, wen ɗang pee wun, mbǝ mǝse mu pǝɗok kǝ ɗeret mǝ Kristi. Wen ɗe moo sat nǝ, wen a nguɗokpwoo tǝktǝk, katɗang wen ashak kǝ wun, ɗang Nnee wen kǝn sat mbii mo nwun agaak, katɗang baa wen ashak kǝ wun kas.
2CO 10:2 Wen ɗang pee wun, mbǝkǝ taji wu le tǝng nwen satpwoo nwun shiɓal kas, katɗang wen jì pee wun ɗi. Mbǝɗe wen man azeen nǝ, wen mak satpwoo shiɓal nen ɗe moo sat nnǝ, mbii ɗe muu cìn sǝ ɓe nǝ a ɗak mǝ yil ɗesǝ.
2CO 10:3 Koo ɗe muu tong a nɗǝǝn yil nǝ, ɓe mbii ɗe mun nkaa cìn lek mbǝ nǝ, baa nǝ a mǝ yil ɗesǝ kas.
2CO 10:4 Leelek ɗe muu cìn lek ɗishik, baa nǝ a mǝ yil desǝ kas. Ɗang leelek fun nǝ a ɓal mǝ Naan, ɗe nǝn mmak shirip kok ɗeɓal mo.
2CO 10:5 Muu shirip pwoo kǝ nen ɗe moo jì kǝ mbii langkáa nkaa man Naan, kǝzak, muu shirip koo a kok mǝ roop ɗeɗangyi ɗe nǝ daam man Naan ngurum mo. Kǝ muu le kǝ koo a pan kǝ weyi, ɓe nǝ cìn ɗyen kǝ Kristi ɗi zak.
2CO 10:6 Aɓwoon ɗe wun nkám agaak azeen-nzeen nǝ, wuu kǝlǝng pwoo fun, bǝ mun ɗak sun fun rǝret mbǝ kar nencii kǝlǝngpee mo.
2CO 10:7 A mii le ɗang wuu leyit fuu mo nkaa mbii dǝ mo aɓwoon yi? Katɗang mee gurum kǝ leshin nnǝ, wuɗin a mǝ Kristi, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur pan rǝret, kǝ wur man nnǝ mun a mǝ Kristi zak.
2CO 10:8 Mbǝɗe koo dǝ wen canjoom ɗes shi ɓal ɗe Daa wur shin mmun, ɓe nǝ a mbǝkǝ mu ɗak wun ɗi, baa a mbǝkǝ mu shirip wun ɗi kas. Baa mee naashweep yaa wen kas.
2CO 10:9 Taji wu pan nǝ, wen kǝn gung a mbǝkǝ wen lekǝǝrmuut ɗi nwun shi ran fen nǝ mo kas.
2CO 10:10 Mbǝɗe pak gurum moo sat nǝ, mbii ɗe wur ran nɗǝǝn ran wur nǝ mo toon, kǝ mo ɓal zam, amma katɗang gurum naa wur nyit, bǝ baa shin wur nǝ kǝ mee ɓal kas. Pwoo ɗe wur sat nǝ, ɓe baa nǝ ke koop nǝ kas.
2CO 10:11 Nǝ ret kǝ nen sat pwoo mǝnǝ mo man nǝ, mbii ɗe muu sat nɗǝǝn ran, bǝ baa nǝ ɗyik kǝ mbii ɗe muu sat nwun nyit kǝ yit kas, katɗang mukaat ashak kǝ wun.
2CO 10:12 Baa mu mak lekáa fun, koo mu kámkáa fun mo nciit kǝ nen ɗe moo canjoom a shi sut fur mo kas. Mbǝɗe moo kám sut fur mo kǝ shak, kǝ moo camsut fur kǝ shak zak. Nen mǝnǝ mo a mwen mo.
2CO 10:13 Baa mun ncanjoom ɗel peeɗe nǝ ret kǝ mu ɗar ɗi kas. Amma mu ɗar a nkaa pee ɗak ɗe Naan wur kǝ can nǝ mmun, desǝ nǝ ɓal kǝ ɗak fun nnaar fu.
2CO 10:14 Wun a nɗǝǝn pee ɗak dǝ Naan wur kǝ can mun, akǝsǝ bǝ baa di mu canjoom mbǝ ɗak fun ɗik kas, kaaɗe gyet mu dǝm kǝ pwoo mǝ Kristi nǝ nwun sǝ.
2CO 10:15 Baa canjoom fun nǝ ɗel met mbii dǝ nǝ ret kas, kǝ baa nǝ tung ɗak ke mee gurum mo kas. Amma mu canciin nǝ, a shinzeen fuu nǝ ɓul hakyeng, ɓe ɗak fun nɗǝǝn wun, nǝn mɓul ɗes hakyeng zak.
2CO 10:16 Mbǝkǝ mu katpee satpwoo kǝ Naan ɗi nɗǝǝn yil ɗe mo a kyeen fuu. Baa mu canjoom a shi peeɗe mee gurum kǝ cam cìn ɗak ɗi kas.
2CO 10:17 Amma kaaɗe moo kǝ ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal kǝ Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Jir ngwe ɗe wur canjoom, bǝ nǝ ret kǝ wur canjoom nǝ a shi mbii ɗe Daa wur kǝ cìn.>>
2CO 10:18 Mbǝɗe baa Naan wur kǝ reɓet ngwe ɗe wur ke kwoop a shin kas, amma a ngwe ɗe Daa wur kǝ kwoop ɓejee.
2CO 11:1 Wen canciin nǝ, wu ngung kǝ wen mbǝ rep mwen fen sǝ. Kussuk wu gung kǝ wen!
2CO 11:2 Wen kǝn cìn zuur nkaa wun mbǝ Naan. Wun a kaa reep nuk ɗe baa war kǝ man mish kas. Wen kǝn tuweerpwoo mbǝ shin wun nɗyik, kaa matpoo sǝ pee mish war ɗe, a Kristi wur a mish fuu nǝ.
2CO 11:3 Amma wen kǝn kǝǝr, taji nǝ yool ɗee a kaa gyet nwoo gwam Iif shi seen wur ɗe mu ɗung sǝ kas. Taji mo yool gwam wun, kǝ mo mer kǝ pan fuu mo nkaa wal ɗeret, ɗe wun kǝ nǝ mbǝ Kristi kas.
2CO 11:4 A mii le ɗang katɗang mee gurum jì satpwoo nkaa mee Jesu ɗe ɗyík kǝ pwoo ɗe mun mu sat nǝ nwun bǝ wuu kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ yi? Wu pan nǝ riin mǝnǝ ɗyík kǝ Riin Naan ɗe wuu kat nǝ yi? Kǝ wu pan nǝ, mee pwoo Naan nǝ ɗe ɗyik waa met pwoo Naan ɗe wuu lap nǝ yi?
2CO 11:5 Wen man azeen nǝ, baa wen a ɗekat met jir nɗǝǝn jeplep nǝ mo kas.
2CO 11:6 Meeɓe, baa wen man satpwoo rǝret kas, amma wen man satpwoo ɗeret nǝ. Muu kám man nǝ nwun agaak koo a pǝrangyi mɓut mbii mo jir.
2CO 11:7 Tan, gyet wen cìn a mbii ɗebish, mbǝɗe gyet wen sham kǝ káa fen, mbǝkǝ Naan wur ɗiyeep wun ɗi kaaɗe wen satpwoo kǝ Naan nǝ nwun shi zuum sǝ wa?
2CO 11:8 Wen lap ɓam pǝ pak Ekǝlisya mo, mbǝkǝ wen cìn ɗak ɗi nnaar fuu. Wen mak sat nǝ, gyet wen ghǝr a long fur mo, mbǝkǝ wen ɓam wun ɗi.
2CO 11:9 Kaaɗe gyet wen ɗe ashak kǝ wun, bǝ baa gyet wen kǝ mee mbii kas, kǝzak, baa gyet wen lejeel mmee gurum kas. Mbǝɗe ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗe mo tong mMasidoniya jì ɗi, a mo jì shin wen mbii ɗe wen kǝn reɓet mo. A mbǝmǝnǝ, ɗangɓe koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi, ɓe baa wen le mee jeel wun kas. Kaaɗe baa gyet wen lejeel wun kas sǝ.
2CO 11:10 Mbǝɗe wen man nǝ, pwoo ɗe wen kǝn sat nǝ a pwoo mǝ Kristi azeen, ɓe baa mee ngwe mak cíi canjoom nwen nɗǝǝn yil Akaya kas.
2CO 11:11 A mii le ɗang wen sat kǝsǝ yi? A mbǝɗe baa wen wal nwun kas aa? Naan wur man nǝ, wen wal nwun zam.
2CO 11:12 Ɗak ɗe wen nkaa cìn nǝ, ɓe wen sat a ncìn a nǝ, mbǝkǝ wen shootpwoo mu canjoom ɗi jeplep ɗe moo sat nǝ, ɗak fur nǝ a nciit kǝ munu.
2CO 11:13 Kaan kǝ nen mǝnǝ mo a jeplep mu ɗung mo. Moo cìn a ɗak ɗe mu numpee mo. Moo lekáa fur kaa mo a jeplep mu Kristi mo sǝ, ɗang baa mo a jeplep Kristi kas.
2CO 11:14 Baa nǝ ɗee a mbii aapwoo kas, mbǝɗe koo a Gujwan shikáa wur, bǝ wur leshin kaa wur a ngulep mu peeɓang sǝ.
2CO 11:15 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe baa nǝ ɗee a mbii aapwoo kas, katɗang bǝ kǝrem mu Gujwan mo lesut fur, kaa mo a nen cìn ɗak ɗeret mo sǝ zak. A peekyes nǝ, ɓe mon nlap kwat fur mo nciit kǝ ɗak fur mo zak.
2CO 11:16 Wen kǝn baa sat ɗi zak nǝ, taji mee gurum pan nǝ, wen a mwen kas. Amma katɗang wu pan nǝ, wen a mwen, ɓe wu lap wen ɗesǝ kaa mwen nǝ sǝ, mbǝkǝ wen kat pee can rep joom ɗi lee.
2CO 11:17 Pwoo ɗe wen sat sǝ, ɓe baa wen sat a mee pwoo ɗe Daa wur lep wen kas, amma wen kǝn satpwoo nǝ a kaa mwen sǝ, wen kǝn sat pwoo mǝnǝ a tyap.
2CO 11:18 Kaaɗe gurum mo ɗes moo can a joom ɗe mu yil ɗesǝ ɓejee ɗak sǝ, ɓe wen ncanjoom nǝ akǝsǝ zak.
2CO 11:19 Wun nen ɗe wu seen ɓe wu gung kǝ nenmwen mo shi retnyit.
2CO 11:20 Mbǝɗe katɗang, ɓe mee gurum le wun kaa kǝrem mo sǝ, koo wur ghǝǝr wun, koo wur se lǝɓet nkaa wun, kǝ koo wur kám a ɓal mu tuur nwun, kǝ koo wur nǝnas wun, jir kǝsǝ ɓe wuu gung kǝ ngwe mǝnǝ.
2CO 11:21 Nǝ shweep wen mbǝ lap ii, nǝ gyet mun kǝ ɓal mbǝ cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo kas, amma katɗang mee gurum kǝ canjoom nkaa mee mbii, ɓe wen kǝn satpwoo nǝ a kaa mwen sǝ. Wen ncanjoom akǝsǝ zak.
2CO 11:22 Katɗang ɓǝ, mo a nen Hiburu mo, bǝ wen a ngu Hiburu zak. Katɗang ɓe, mo a nen Izrel mo, ɓe wen a ngu Izrel zak. Katɗang ɓe mo a ɗang kǝ Abraham, ɓe wen a ɗang kǝ Abraham zak.
2CO 11:23 Katɗang ɓe mo a kǝrem mu Kristi mo, ɓe wen a kǝrem mu Kristi zak. Wen satpwoo nǝ a kaa ngutar sǝ! Mbǝɗe wen cìn ɗak ɗe nǝ ɗes met mumo nǝ. Mo kǝ ɓwoot wen le nlushoot, kǝ wen shwaanas met mǝ sat zak. Wen kǝn shwaajeel mo shinǝ-shinǝ har kus kǝ muut zak.
2CO 11:24 Gyet yit paat, ɓe nen Yahudi mo fwo ngwoor nwen laarkun baapwoofeer.
2CO 11:25 Nennan-nan mu Rom mo sǝrem wen shi gwoor yitkun. Nen Yahudi mo car wen shi nding yit mǝndong, mbǝkǝ mo tu wen ɗi. Yitkun ɓe tii am, nǝ taa pyan kǝ mun. Wen kǝn cam teer kǝ wet nkaa am bahar.
2CO 11:26 Shidaar-shidaar bǝ wen a ar mwaan mo ɗes, kǝ nwen kǝn naa muut shi yit fen mɓut ndung mo. Wen kǝn naa muut nsar kǝ nenwat mo, kǝ nwen naa muut nsar kǝ ɗang fun nǝ Yahudi mo zak. Wen kǝ naa muut nsar kǝ nenkum mo. Wen kǝn naa muut nɗǝǝn yilkaam mo, kǝzak, wen kǝn naa muut a naaryil mo. Wen kǝ naa muut nkaa am bahar mo. Wen kǝn naa muut nsar kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn ɗe mu ɗung mo.
2CO 11:27 Wen kǝn shwaaɗak mo, kǝ wen kǝn shwaajeel mo, kǝn nnaa nteer mmeen, kǝ wen kǝ shwaaneen zak, kǝ neen am tu wen zak. Yit mo ɗes baa wen kat mee mbiise kas. Wen kǝn shwaakut, mbǝ ciin mbiisǝp,
2CO 11:28 kǝ pak mbii mo ɗes ɗe kǝzak. Mbii ɗe mo daampee nwen, koo puus ɗeɗangyi, nǝ a mbǝɗe wen kǝ toon mǝ tap kǝ Ekǝlisya mo jir zak.
2CO 11:29 Katɗang baa mee ngwe katɓal kas, ɓe nǝ le kǝ baa wen katɓal kas zak. Katɗang mee ngwe taa pal nɗǝǝn shikbish, ɓe nǝ shwal nwen zam.
2CO 11:30 Katɗang bǝ nǝ a tǝng kǝ wen canjoom, ɓe wen canjoom nǝ a nkaa mbii ɗe nǝn nkám agaak nǝ baa wen kǝ ɓal kas,
2CO 11:31 Naan puun kǝ Daa Jesu ɗe sǝm wur nǝ kat ɗeret har ngaa-ngaa. Wur man azeen-nzeen nǝ, baa wen kǝn sat a ɗung kas.
2CO 11:32 Nɗǝǝn yil nDamaskus, ɓe gofna ɗewur ndir kǝ mishkoom Aritas wur shootpwoo sheep pǝbong ɗin nDamaskus mo, mbǝkǝ mo yaa wen ɗi.
2CO 11:33 Mo le wen sham nɗǝǝn kǝci ɗeɗes mmee fung mu fwang mu yilkaam nǝ, har wen put nkoom nsar wur.
2CO 12:1 Wen ncanjoom a tǝng, koo ɗe baa wen kat mee lǝɓet nɗǝǝn nǝ kas. Amma yaksǝ ɓe wen nsekyeen kǝ satpwoo nkaa suun mo, kǝ mbii ɗe Daa wur woo mo nwen.
2CO 12:2 Wen man mee gurum nɗǝǝn Kristi ɗe gyet Naan mang wur kàa kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan ɗekun. Nǝ wul a ɓit mo kaapaat baafeer yaksǝ. Kyet, gyet Naan kàa kǝ wur a nɗǝǝn nan mu yil ɗesǝ aa? Ɓe baa wen man kas, amma Naan man.
2CO 12:3 Wen man nǝ, mo mang gwar nǝ kàa kǝ wur a mparadayis. (Shii kǝ mǝnǝ a peeɗe Naan ɗi). Kyet a shi nan mu yil ɗesǝ aa? Koo baa a shi fwoshik mu yil ɗesǝ kas aa? Ɓe baa wen man kas, amma Naan wur man.
2CO 12:4 Wur kǝlǝng mbii mo, ɗe baa mon mmak sat mo shi pwoo kas, kǝ mbii ɗe baa gurum mo mak sat shi lǝpwoo kas zak.
2CO 12:5 Wen kǝn canjoom a shi gwar ɗesǝ. Baa wen kǝn canjoom a shikáa fen kas. Amma wen kǝn kám a ciin ɓal fen agaak.
2CO 12:6 Koo ɗe wen reɓet canjoom nǝ, ɓe baa wen ɗee a mwen kas, mbǝɗe wen kǝn sat azeen. Amma baa wen canjoom kas, mbǝkǝ taji mee gurum lepan nkaa wen, waa met mbii ɗewur naa wen kǝn cìn mo, kǝ mbii ɗewur kǝlǝng kǝ pwoo fen kas.
2CO 12:7 Mbǝkǝ taji wen ɗiyeep káa fen mbǝ suun ɗeɗes ɗesǝ ɗi Naan kǝ kám mo nwen kas. Amma mo le mee ghǝr nɗǝǝn fwoshik fen, ɗe nǝ ɗee a mee shwal pee wen ɗi, ngulep kǝ Gujwan wur daampee nwen, mbǝkǝ taji wen canjoom kǝ fwoshik fen kas.
2CO 12:8 Wen kǝn ɗang pee Daa yit kun, mbǝkǝ wur shang mbii ɗesǝ nǝ baa kǝ nǝ aku.
2CO 12:9 Amma Daa wur sat nwen nǝnee, <<Ɗeret fen nǝ mak waa. Mbǝɗe a nɗǝǝn ciin ɓal mu gurum, ɗangɓe mon naa gam kǝ ɓal fen.>> Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe wen sǝǝt canjoom nɗǝǝn ciin ɓal fen nǝ. Mbǝkǝ ɓal mu Kristi nǝ tong ɗi nɗǝǝn wen.
2CO 12:10 Aasǝ ɓe wen kǝn kat retnyit nɗǝǝn sǝm mu Kristi, mbǝ ciin ɓal fen nǝ, kǝ fǝlǝp ɗe moo cìn nwen, kǝ mbii daampee mo, kǝ jeel mo, kǝ luk mo shinǝ-shinǝ, mbǝ Kristi. Mbǝɗe katɗang baa wen kǝ ɓal kas, ɓe wur shínɓal nwen.
2CO 12:11 Wen kǝn lesen ɗee a kaa mwen sǝ, amma a wun wu le kǝ wen ɗee a mwen nǝ. Gyet nǝ ret kǝ a wun, wun nkwoop wen, mbǝɗe baa wen a ɗekat met jir nɗǝǝn jeplep nǝ mo kas, koo ɗe baa wen a mee mbii kas.
2CO 12:12 Naan cìn mbii lukshik kǝ mbii aapwoo mo, kǝ ɗak ɗenan-nan mo shi wen, kaaɗe wen gung mbǝ cìn ɗak fen mo shidaar-shidaar. Ɗak mu mbii aapwoo ɗe mo kám agaak nǝ, wen a ngulep azeen-nzeen.
2CO 12:13 Wen kǝn cìn a mii, koor Ekǝlisya nǝ mo yii? Ɗi baa wen kǝn cìn mǝnǝ nwun kas yi? Aa koo a mbǝɗe baa gyet wen le mee toon nwun kas aa? Ɓe wu fwo ɗi nwen.
2CO 12:14 Yaksǝ ɓe wen kǝn ɗak sen mbǝ dǝm pee wun ɗi, ɓe a dǝm ɗekun pee wun ɗi mmǝnǝ. Baa wen le kǝ wu kwat wen kas, mbǝɗe baa wen kǝn tang a mee mbii pee wun ɗi kas, amma wen kǝn tang a wuwun. Mbǝɗe baa a jep mon ntang mbii le mbǝ puun fur mo kas. Amma puun nǝ mon ntang mbii le mbǝ jep fur mo.
2CO 12:15 Nǝ nret nwen nyit zam, mbǝkǝ wen cin mbii ɗe wen kǝ nǝ jir, kǝ sen fen zak, mbǝ ɓam wun. Wen wal nwun ɗes, ɗangɓe wun wu wal nwen a lee ɗak aa?
2CO 12:16 Wu man azeen nǝ, baa gyet wen lejeel wun kas. Amma mee gurum sat nǝ gyet wen sǝseen nkaa wun, kǝ wen le cip mu gwampee wun zak.
2CO 12:17 Kyet wen kǝn cam seen a wun shi gwampee mɓut nen dǝ wen lep mo dǝm pee wun ɗi wa?
2CO 12:18 Gyet wen ɗang Titus, kǝ wur dǝm pee wun ɗi, ashak kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗesǝ. Kyet, gyet Titus wur lap mee mbii pee wun ɗi wa? Baa a Riin Naan ɗe mǝnɗong wur ɓwet mun weet kas aa? Baa mun weet muu cìn ɗak nǝ a ar ɗe mǝnɗong kas aa?
2CO 12:19 Tan, peeɗi ɗi ɓe wuu pan nǝ, mu jì aa mee mbii langkáa mbǝ sun fun pee wun ɗi wa? Hai. Muu sat a pwoo mu Kristi ntoom Naan. Shaar fen mo, mbii ɗe muu cìn mo jir, ɓe muu cìn mo a mbǝ ɓam wun.
2CO 12:20 Mbǝɗe wen kǝǝr nǝ, meeɓe, katɗang wen dǝm pee wun ɗi, ɓe wen nkat mǝse fuu nǝ ɗyik kǝ mǝse dǝ ɗyeen nwen nkat wun kǝ nǝ. Kǝzak, wun nnaa mǝse mǝnǝ nǝ ɗyík, kǝ mǝse dǝ ɗyeen wun naa wen kǝ nǝ. Meeɓe wen kat ɓǝlep, kǝ zuur, kǝ tuup, kǝ walnkáa, kǝ ɗung kǝ pwoo nɗom ndom, kǝ ɗyeepkáa, kǝ ciin tongryang nnaar fuu.
2CO 12:21 Wen kǝǝr nǝ, katɗang wen waa ndǝm pee wun ɗi, ɓe baa Naan fen wur nsham kǝ wen ntoom fuu kas. Katɗang Naan sham kǝ wen ntoom fuu, bǝ wen nkat pǝtuup ɗewat, kǝ gurum mo ɗes nɗǝǝn wun. Nen dǝ gyet mo kǝ cìn shikbish yam, ɗangɓe baa mo kǝ tuwap kas mbǝ mǝse ɗebish, kaa cìn ngaa, kǝ koor mu cìn mbii ɗebish mo zak.
2CO 13:1 Wen kǝn dǝm pee wun ɗi, a ɗekun nɗesǝ, <<Mbǝkǝ mo man zeen kǝ meepwoo azeen-nzeen, bǝ nǝ a tǝng kǝ mo kat langtǝng mo vǝl koo kun>> kaaɗe mo ran nɗeen bǝǝt haal.
2CO 13:2 Wen kǝn gwak a nen dǝ gyet mo cìn shikbish yam, kǝ koor nǝ mo jir zak. Gyet wen kǝn gwak mo, ɓe baa wen ɗi ashak kǝ mo kas. Wen gwak wun kaaɗe gyet wen gwak wun nji fen ɗevǝl pee wun ɗi sǝ, nǝ, katɗang wen mbaajì, ɓe wen nshin kar nen ɗe ɗi mo cìn shikbish sǝ, kǝ koor nǝ mo.
2CO 13:3 Katɗang ɓe ɗyeen nwun kǝ wu man azeen-nzeen nǝ, wen kǝn satpwoo ɗesǝ mo a shi ɓal mu Kristi, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu man nǝ Kristi wur kǝ ɓal ɗes. A wur nkar wun, kǝ a wur kám ɓal wur nɗǝǝn wun.
2CO 13:4 Mbǝɗe koo ɗe gyet mo pwas wur nkaa shyeep, ɓe gyet a wur shin shin nǝ mo pwas nkaa shyeep nǝ, ɓe jir kǝsǝ, ɓe wur ɗi kǝ seen shi iiko mu Naan. Mun a nen ɗe baa mun kǝ ɓal kas, ɗang nɗǝǝn iiko mu Naan shi Kristi, ɓe mun ɗi kǝ seen, mbǝkǝ mu ɓam wun ɗi.
2CO 13:5 Wu camkáa fuu mo, kǝ wu man ɗi rǝret nǝ, kyet wuu mwaan a nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu nǝ mo wa? Wu camkáa fuu mo rǝret. Baa wu man nǝ, Jesu Kristi wur kǝ tong a nɗǝǝn wun kas aa? See koo katɗang wuu taa wu pal kǝnding-nding.
2CO 13:6 Muu reɓet kǝ wu man nǝ, baa mun mu taa mu kat kas.
2CO 13:7 Muu ɗang pǝ Naan kǝ taji wu cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas. Muu ɗang pǝ Naan, baa a mbǝkǝ nǝ cám ɗi agaak nǝ, mun kǝ se koorong nkaa cam nǝ kas, amma see a mbǝkǝ wun wu cìn mbii ɗeret mo ɗi, koo dǝ wu naa kaa mun muu taa mu kǝkat sǝ.
2CO 13:8 Mbǝɗe baa nǝ mmak cìn kǝ mu cìn mee mbii nkaa zeen nǝ kas, amma see muu sat azeen nǝ.
2CO 13:9 Muu kat retnyit, katɗang baa mun kǝ ɓal kas, kǝ wun ɗi kǝ ɓal. Ɗangnaan ɗe muu cìn nǝ a mbǝkǝ wu ɗee ɗi a ɗegǝgam.
2CO 13:10 Mbǝmǝnǝ, bǝ wen ran-ran ɗesǝ dǝm wun bǝ baa wen ɗi ashak kǝ wun kas, a shiɓal dǝ Naan wur shin nǝ nwen mbǝ ɗyik wun, baa nǝ a mbǝ shirip wun kas.
2CO 13:11 Peekyes kǝ nǝ, ɗyemnaa mo, ɗang mukaat. Wu ɗak mǝse fuu mo. Wu kǝlǝng pwoo fen mo. Wu lappwoo kǝ shak, kǝ wu tongryang kǝ shak zak. Naan dǝ wur a wal, kǝ ryang, wur ntong ashak kǝ wun.
2CO 13:12 Wu tok kǝ shak shi wal rǝret.
2CO 13:13 Nen Naan mo jir, moo tok kǝ wun.
2CO 13:14 Ɗeret kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi, kǝ wal Naan, kǝ shaar ashak kǝ Riin Ɗeɓang, mo tong ashak kǝ wun jir. Nǝ a kǝ sǝ.
GAL 1:1 Wen Pool, laalep Jesu Kristi, ɗe baa a gurum mo pet an koo a me gwar pet an, ɗang nǝ le kǝ nghan ɗee a laalep wur kas, ɗangɓe a shi rǝɓet Jesu Kristi, kǝ Naan puun, ɗewur yool kǝ Jesu a peemúut.
GAL 1:2 Ɗyemnaa ɗe mo ashak kǝ wen, moo lep tokshik fur mo shindǝm pǝ nendǝm ndang Naan (Ekǝlisya) ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nGalati.
GAL 1:3 Naan puun kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi mo naa wun shi yit mǝ naajeel, kǝ mo shin tongryang nwun zak.
GAL 1:4 Jesu Kristi wur shín shin mbǝ shikbish fun mo, mbǝkǝ wur ɓam mun ɗe nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗebish ɗesǝ mo, nciit-nciit kǝ rǝɓet kǝ Naan puun fun.
GAL 1:5 Ɗeɗes ɗee pǝ wur mbe ngaa-ngaa kǝ ngaa-ngaa. Nǝ aasǝ.
GAL 1:6 Nǝ aapwoo nwen zam, mbǝɗe wu ciir wu cii ngwe ɗewur pet wun shi yit naajeel mǝ Kristi kǝlak-kǝlak aasǝ, mbǝkǝ wu shindǝm ɗe nɗang mee pwoo Naan ɗecì.
GAL 1:7 Azeen-nzeen baa mee pwoo ɗeret waa ɗee ɗe, ɗe nǝ waa met ɗe wuu kǝlǝng pǝ ghan ɗe kas. Ɗang pak gurum moo daampee nwun, kǝ mo rǝɓet ciir kǝ pwoo ɗeret mǝ Kristi nǝ.
GAL 1:8 Ɗangɓe koo ɗe a mun, jir ɗe a mee ngulep Naan tong a ɗengnaan sham, ɗangɓe wur sat mee pwoo ɗeret ɗe nwun, ɗyik kǝ mbii ɗe mu ten mu sat nwun, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ ɗee a mbii ɗebuu-buu mbǝ vit.
GAL 1:9 Kaaɗe mu ten mu sat sǝ, an kǝn baa nsat ɗe nǝnee. Katɗang mee ngusatpwoo ɗeret ɗe nwun ɗyik kǝ ɗe mu ten mu sat nwun, ɓe wu yit kǝ ngwar mǝnǝ ɗee ndǝr tuup Naan mbǝ vit.
GAL 1:10 Wu pan nee, an kǝn tang a ɗeɗes pǝ gurum mo ɗe aa? Aa koo a pǝ Naan ɗi yi? ɗang wu pan nee, an tang a tong ɗyen ngurum mo ghe? Katɗang ɗe an kǝn tang a tong ɗyen ngurum mo, ɓe ɗe baa an a kǝrem Kristi kas.
GAL 1:11 Ɗyemnaa mo, ɗyen wen kǝ wun man nee, pwoo ɗeret ɗe gyet wen kǝn sat nwun, baa nǝ put a pǝ mee gurum ɗi kas.
GAL 1:12 Mbǝɗe, baa gyet wen nla nǝ a nsar mee gurum kas. Kǝzak, baa a mee gurum kám nǝ nwen kas, a Jesu Kristi shikáa wur, wur woo nǝ nwen.
GAL 1:13 Wu kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa shiimwaan fen, ɗe gyet nyam, nɗǝǝn seyil nNaan mǝ nen Yahudi mo, mɓít mǝnǝ, ɓe wen shínjeel Ekǝlisya Naan mo hakyeng, mbe gyet wen kǝn gung mbǝkǝ nghan tu nǝ ɗi.
GAL 1:14 Gyet nɗǝǝn gang fen mo, ɓe wen met mmo jir, mbǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn rat nen Yahudi mo. Gyet wen cìn zuur mbǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn wàar puun fen ɗe moo ten murep mo.
GAL 1:15 Ɗangɓe Naan ɗewur ten bǝlǝp an yam-yam, akuɗang moo làa an, ɓe nɗǝǝn ɗeret wur, ɓe wur pet ghan mbǝkǝ wen ɗee ɗi a mǝ wur.
GAL 1:16 Ɓe nǝ ret nNaan wur nyit ɓe wur kám Làa wur nwen, mbǝkǝ nghan sat pwoo ɗeret ɗe nkaa wur, nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Baa gyet wen ɓeet mǝnǝ kǝ mee gurum kas.
GAL 1:17 Kǝzak, baa gyet wen kàa nJerusalem, pǝ jeplep Jesu Kristi mo ɗe kas, ɗe gyet wur shee pǝrep mo baaɗang wur pet an. Ɗangɓe wen dǝm nyil Arabiya, aɓwoon mǝnǝ ɓe wen waa mbaa dǝm nDamaskus.
GAL 1:18 Aɓwoon ɓit mo kun, ɓe wen kàa nJerusalem, mbǝkǝ nghan naa Kefas ɗi. Wen tong ashak kǝ wur mbee teer mo kaapaat baapaat.
GAL 1:19 Baa gyet wen waa nkaat kǝ memee nɗǝǝn jeplep Jesu mo kas. Gyet wen kaat aa Jemis ɗyemnǝǝn Daa, ɓejee ɗak.
GAL 1:20 Ntoom Naan, ɓe mbii ɗe wen ran nwun, baa mo a ɗung kas.
GAL 1:21 Aɓwoon mǝnǝ, ɓe wen ndǝm nkwang yil nSiriya kǝ Silisiya.
GAL 1:22 Baa gyet nendǝm nɗang Kristi ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Judiya nǝ mo man wen kas.
GAL 1:23 Moo kǝlǝng a gurum mo nkaa sat nǝnee, <<Gwar ɗe dǝ wur shínjeel mmun sǝ, yaksǝ ɓe wur nkaa satpwoo ngurum mo nkaa shinzeen ɗe gyet wur gung mbǝ tu nǝ.>>
GAL 1:24 Mo kwoop Naan mbǝ an.
GAL 2:1 Aɓwoon ɓit mo kaapaat baafeer, ɓe wen mbaa nkàa nJerusalem, ashak kǝ Barnabas. Gyet wen mang Titus mpan ɗi.
GAL 2:2 Wen kàa nJerusalem nǝ, a mbǝɗe Naan woo nwen nǝ, nkàa ɗi. Gyet nciit kǝ mǝnǝ, ɓe nkaat kǝ nen ɗenan-nan nǝ mo a sǝsok, mbǝkǝ wen sat ɗi mmo, nkaa pwoo ɗeret ɗe wen nkaa sat nǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Mbǝkǝ taji, ɗak ɗe gyet wen cìn nǝ kǝ ɗe wen nkaa cin yool ɗee a buu kas.
GAL 2:3 Ɗangɓe Titus, ɗewur ashak kǝ wen, jir ɗewur a ngu Heleni, ɓe baa gyet mo letǝng nwur, kǝ mo can nwur ɗi kas.
GAL 2:4 Ɗang pak nendǝm nɗang Kristi ɗe mǝ ɗung sǝ mo, mo tap jì ɗel nɗǝǝn mun, kaa nengwol mo sǝ, mbǝkǝ mo tap gwol mun, kǝ mo katpee ɗe mɓut mun, ɗe mun nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu, mbǝkǝ mo le mu ɗee ɗi a kǝrem fur mo.
GAL 2:5 Baa gyet mu shínpee mmo kas koo dǝɓen, mbǝkǝ mu tap ɗe kǝ zeen mǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗe mbǝ wun.
GAL 2:6 Ɗangɓe mbǝ nen ɗe mo lekáa fur mo a kaa mee mbii sǝ, koo ɗe mo a wii mo yi, ɓe baa nǝ daampee nwen kas. Baa Naan wur shwatyit mmee gurum kas. Nen ɗe kǝn sat mmo, koo ɗe gyet mo a nen ɗenan-nan mo, ɗangɓe ɓe jir kǝsǝ, ɓe baa gyet mo le mee mbii ɗyik nkaa pwoo fen nǝ kas.
GAL 2:7 Akoppee mǝnǝ bǝ mo naa nǝ, Naan wur cin ɗak mǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas nsar fen, kaaɗe wur cin ɗak mǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ mPita mbǝ nen Yahudi mo sǝ.
GAL 2:8 Ɓe mo naa nǝnee, << Naan ɗewur shinɓal mPita, mbǝkǝ wur ɗee ɗe a ngusatpwoo ɗeret nǝ nen Yahudi mo, a wur shinɓal nwen zak, mbǝkǝ wen ɗee ɗi a ngusatpwoo ɗeret nǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas.
GAL 2:9 Kaaɗe mo naa ɗeret ɗe Naan wur cin nwen, Jemis kǝ Pita, kǝ Joon, ɗe gyet mo a nen nan mǝ nendǝm ndang Naan nǝ mo, (Ekǝlisya) nǝ, mo shin sarse fur ɗe mǝ shaarshak nwen, kǝ Barnabas. Mo sat nǝ, mmun mu dǝm mu satpwoo Naan nǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ nwuɗun, ɗu dǝm ɗe pee nen Yahudi mo.
GAL 2:10 Mo sat mmun nee, taji mu mundǝr nenjeel ɗe mo nɗǝǝn mo kas, a mbii ɗe gyet kǝn fes le pǝtuup fen mbee cìn nǝ mǝnǝ.
GAL 2:11 Ɗang kaaɗi Pita gyet kàa nAntiyok, ɓe wen shin sar wur nyit, mbǝ mbii ɗe gyet wur cìn nǝ baa nǝ nkaa ar kas.
GAL 2:12 Akuɗang pak gurum mo tong pǝ Jemis jì ɗe, ɓe wur kǝ sese ashak kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, ɗangɓe kaaɗe des ɗesǝ nǝ mo jì wul, ɓe wur cii sese ashak kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, mbǝɗe wur kǝǝr nen Yahudi mo.
GAL 2:13 Ashak kǝ wur, ɓe koor nen Yahudi ɗe mo a nendǝm nɗang Jesu mo, baa mo ɗar nkaa zeen kas, kaa wur sǝ, ɗang kǝ Barnabas zak, wur mɓwoon mo nɗǝǝn mwaan mo kǝ pǝtuup ɗe vǝl-vǝl nǝ.
GAL 2:14 Ɗang kaaɗe wen naa mǝnǝ, baa mo ɗar ndǝre-ndǝre nkaa zeen mǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ kas, ɓe nsat mPita, nnaar mo nǝnee, <<Katɗang waa ɗe waa a ngu Yahudi aa tong a kaa ngwe ɗe baa wur a ngu Yahudi kas, ɓe cirang ɗangɓe gha nle tǝng nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ mo tong kaa nen Yahudi mo sǝ yi?>>
GAL 2:15 Mun shikáa fun, mo làa mun a nen Yahudi mo, baa a nen shikbish kaa koor gurum mo sǝ kas.
GAL 2:16 Ɗang mu man nee, baa gurum kǝ ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit Naan, a shi ɗak ɗewur cìn nɗǝǝn Wàar mo kas, ɗangɓe gurum kǝ ɗee a ɗeɓang, a mbǝ shinzeen nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi. Har mun, mu shinzeen nɗǝǝn Kristi, mbǝkǝ mmun ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang shi shinzeen nKristi, baa a shi mee ɗak ɗe mu cìn nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ kas. Mbǝɗe, shi ɗak ɗe gurum cìn nǝ nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ, ɓe baa gurum ncam ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit Naan kas.
GAL 2:17 Ɗangɓe muu gung kǝ mun ɗee ɗe a ɗeɓang nɗǝǝn Kristi. Katɗang mo waa kat a mun a nenshikbish mo, ɓe nǝ kám nǝ, Kristi wur a mee ngulep mǝ shikbish aa? Hai baa aasǝ kas koo dǝɓen!
GAL 2:18 Ɗangɓe katɗang wen kǝn ɗyik, a nkaa mbii ɗe wen kǝn ten nshirip mo, ɓe kǝn kám káa fen agaak nǝ, an a ngushikbish.
GAL 2:19 Wen kǝn ɗee a ɗemumuut nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ, mbǝkǝ wen tong ɗe kǝ seen pǝ Naan ɗe.
GAL 2:20 Mo pwas an ashak kǝ Kristi. Baa a an kǝn tong nɗǝǝn seen ɗesǝ kas, ɗangɓe a Kristi wur kǝ tong nɗǝǝn an. Kǝ seen ɗe wen kǝ nǝ yaksǝ nɗǝǝn an ɗesǝ, an kǝn tong a shi shinzeen nɗǝǝn Làa Naan, ɗewur wal nwen, ɗang wur shìn kaashin mbǝ an.
GAL 2:21 Baa wen cii ɗeret Naan kas, mbǝɗe katɗang gurum kǝ ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit Naan, a shi Wàar mo, ɓe muut ɗe Kristi wur muut nǝ, nǝ nɗee a buu mǝnǝ ɓe baa nǝ kǝ mee koop nǝ kas.
GAL 3:1 Hai! Wun nen Galati mo, wu mwen zam. A soot ɗeɗang kǝ se ɓut nwun yi? A yit fuu mo, ɓe mo sat nwun agaak kaaɗe mo pwas Kristi.
GAL 3:2 Wu ɗar kǝ wen cìn mee tal ɗe pǝ wun. Gyet wu lap Riin nǝ a mbǝ ɗak ɗe wu cìn nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ aa koo a mbǝɗe gyet wu shinzeen yi?
GAL 3:3 Wun wu mwen aasǝ wo? Gyet wu shee wu yaa a nɗǝǝn Riin, ɗangɓe yaksǝ, ɓe wuu rǝɓet kyes nǝ a nɗǝǝn nan fuu mo aa?
GAL 3:4 Tan wu shwaajeel kǝ mbii mo shini-shinǝ a buu mǝnǝ aa? Taji wu yit kǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗebuu kas.
GAL 3:5 Wur ɗewur shin Riin wur nwun, kǝ wur cìn mbii aapwoo mo nɗǝǝn wun, ɓe wu pan nee, a mbǝɗe wuu tap kǝ Wàar nǝ mo aa koo a mbǝɗe wu kǝlǝng, ɗang wu shinzeen pwoo ɗeret nǝ yi?
GAL 3:6 Wu cìn pan nkaa Abraham, kaaɗe pwoo Naan nǝ sat sǝ nǝnee, <<Wur shinzeen nNaan mbǝ mo tang mǝnǝ wur a kaa ngwe ɗe ndǝre sǝ.>>
GAL 3:7 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe yaksǝ, wu naa a nenshínzeen mo a jep Abraham nǝ mo.
GAL 3:8 nƊǝǝn pwoo Naan, ɓe mu ten mu naa nǝ, Naan wur le nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, kǝ mo ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit wur a mbee shinzeen. Mo satpwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ nǝ mɓít mǝ Abraham nǝnee, <<A nɗǝǝn waa ɓe gurum mo jir, nɗǝǝn nyil nǝ mon nkat ɗeret.>>
GAL 3:9 Nǝ aasǝ ɓe, nen ɗe mo shinzeen, mon nkat ɗeret ashak kǝ Abraham, mbǝɗe gyet wur kǝ shinzeen.
GAL 3:10 Nen ɗe moo le pǝtuup fur mo, a nkaa ɗak Wàar nǝ, ɓe mo a ndǝr tuup Naan. Mo ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Koo a wii ɗe baa wur gam Wàar ɗe mo ran mo nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal mǝ Wàar nǝ kas, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ a ndǝr tuup Naan.>>
GAL 3:11 Yaksǝ, nǝ ɗee agaak nǝ, baa mee gurum mak ɗee a ɗeɓang nyit Naan shi Wàar mo kas. Mbǝɗe koo a wii, ɗewur ɗee a ɗe ndǝre a mbǝ shinzeen wur, ɓe a wur nkat seen.
GAL 3:12 Ɗangɓe baa Wàar nǝ ɗar a nkaa shinzeen kas, <<Koo a wii ɗewur ngam Wàar nǝ mo, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ wur nkat seen a shi mo.>>
GAL 3:13 Mun jir, mon ntokɗyeel ɗebish mun, mbǝɗe baa mu gam Wàar nǝ mo jir kas, ɗangɓe Kristi, wur can mun nɗǝǝn ɗyeel ɗebish nǝ. A mbǝ mun, ɓe wur shwaajeel fun mo, ɗang wur mang ɗyeel ɗebish nǝ le nkaa shin. Nǝ a rǝran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee, <<Koo a wii, ɗe mo pwas wur nkaa tǝng, ɓe wur a ndǝr tuup Naan.>>
GAL 3:14 Mbǝkǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu, ɓe ɗeret mǝ Abraham nǝ ɗee nkaa nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Kǝzak, mbǝkǝ mun mu lap Riin ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ nnǝ, wuɗin ncin mmun mbǝ shinzeen fun mo.
GAL 3:15 Ɗyemnaa mo, an ncìn kám kǝ mbii ɗe mu ten mu loot kǝ mo nɗǝǝn tong fun mo shidaar-shidaar. Katɗang gurum mo vǝl moo ten ɓwootpwoo ashak nkaa me mbii, ɓe nǝ nluk kǝ mee gurum ɗyik teppwoo ɗe mo kǝ ten ɓwoot nǝ, kǝzak, baa mee gurum mak le mee mbii ɗe nkaa nǝ kas, mbǝɗe mo kǝ ten ɓwoot nǝ.
GAL 3:16 Nǝ aasǝ, Naan wur kǝ ten cweerpwoo mo Abraham yam-yam kǝ ɗang wur. Baa mo ran a nee kǝ ɗang wur mo kas. Katɗang ɗe mo sat nee, a ɗang wur mo, ɓe ɗe nǝ kám nǝ, ɗang nǝ mo a ɗes, ɗangɓe mo ran a nkaa ɗang wur mǝndong ɓejee. Dang wur ɗemǝndong ɗesǝ nǝ a Kristi.
GAL 3:17 Mbii ɗe an nkaa sat nǝ a nee, gyet yam-yam, ɓe Naan wur kǝ ten ɓǝlemcuk shi toom. Ɗangɓe aɓwoon ɓit mo kambil feer kǝ laarkun, aku ɗang Naan wur shin Wàar nǝ nen Yahudi mo. Wàar ɗe Naan wur shin ɗesǝ nǝ, baa nǝ mak teppwoo ɗe gyet wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ kas, kǝzak, baa Wàar nǝ mo mak tupwoo ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweer mo kas.
GAL 3:18 Katɗang ɗe Naan wur shin zuum wur ngurum mo a mbǝɗe moo tap Wàar nǝ, ɓe ɗe baa gurum mo nkat zuum wur nǝ a mbǝ pwoo ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ kas. Ɗang mu man nee, a mbǝɗe gyet Naan kǝ ten cweer nǝ, ɗangɓe wur shin zuum nǝ Abraham.
GAL 3:19 Ɗang, a mii a koop Wàar nǝ yi? Naan wur shin Wàar nǝ mo, a mbǝkǝ mmun man mbii ɗebish mo ɗi. Gyet Naan wur shin Wàar nǝ mo mmun, a mbǝkǝ mo tap mun ɗi, mbǝ reppee lee, ɓe parɗe pee nǝ wul, mbǝkǝ ɗang Abraham nǝ jì ɗi. Mbǝɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweerpwoo mǝnǝ a nwur. Naan wur shin Wàar nǝ a nnenlep wur mo, mbǝkǝ mo sham shin ɗi nsar mee gurum ɗe gyet wur a ngu ar nnaar Naan kǝ gurum mo.
GAL 3:20 Katɗang ngu ar ɗe mɓut mee mbii, bǝ nǝ kám mmun nǝ wur ɗar a naar gurum mo vǝl. Ɗang nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗe gyet Naan cweer Abraham nǝ, ɓe gyet a Naan wur mbǝshin ɓejee, ɗe gyet wur cweerpwoo mǝnǝ.
GAL 3:21 Kyet ɗesǝ nǝ kám mmun nǝ, Wàar nǝ a nkaa koon kǝ pwoo ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ wo? Baa nǝ aasǝ kas koo dǝɓen. Katɗang gyet mee Wàar nǝ ɗe, ɗe gyet nǝ mmak shìn seen ngurum mo, ɓe gyet nǝ mmak le gurum mo ɗee a ɗe ndǝre nyit Naan. Ɗang baa mee kaan Wàar mǝnǝ ɗi kas.
GAL 3:22 Ɗang kaaɗe mo ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ nee, mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil nǝ jir, mo a ndǝr shikbish. A nen ɗe mo shinzeen nJesu Kristi, mo lap mbii ɗi Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝnee, wuɗin shìn nen ɗe mo shinzeen Kristi ɓejee.
GAL 3:23 Gyet akuɗang shinzeen nǝ jì, ɓe mun a ɗe shishoot nɗǝǝn Wàar nǝ, aku ɗang Naan wur wang ar mmun, kǝ mu shinzeen ɗi nJesu Kristi.
GAL 3:24 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe gyet Wàar nǝ a ngukám fun, akuɗang Jesu Kristi wur jì. Kaaɗi wur jì ɓe mu ɗee a ɗi ndǝre nyit Naan, mbǝɗe mu shinzeen wur.
GAL 3:25 Ɗang nyaksǝ, kaaɗi Naan kǝ wang ar nǝ mun, mbǝkǝ mu shinzeen ɗe Jesu Kristi, ɓe baa mu kuɗi a ndǝr ngupan mun kas.
GAL 3:26 Mbǝɗe yaksǝ bǝ shinzeen, nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi, ɓe wun a jep Naan mo jir.
GAL 3:27 Wun ɗe moo cìn baptisma nwun jir nɗǝǝn Kristi, ɓe wuu ɗee a ɗebǝɓal kǝ Kristi mǝnǝ. Mbǝmǝnǝ mu mwaan nɗǝǝn ɗyen mǝ Kristi.
GAL 3:28 Yaksǝ, baa mee shwatyit kuɗi nnaar nen Yahudi mo kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, koo naar kǝrem kǝ jeplu mo kas, koo nnaar mish mo kǝ mat mo kas, mbǝɗe wun a ɗemǝndong jir nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu.
GAL 3:29 Katɗang wun a mǝ Kristi, ɓe wun a jep Abraham mo. Wuu lap mbii mo jir, ɗe gyet Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ.
GAL 4:1 Mbii ɗe an nkaa sat nǝ a nee, làa ɗewur nsekop, baa wur met kǝrem kas, naar ɗewur kuɗi a làa, jir kǝ ɗe long nǝ mo a mǝ wur.
GAL 4:2 Kaaɗi wur kuɗi a làa, ɓe a gurum moo tap wur zak. A gurum moo naa mbii wur mo, har parpuus ɗe puun wur le nǝ wul.
GAL 4:3 Nǝ kǝ mun aasǝ zak. Gyet nyam, naar ɗe gyet baa mu manshii zeen kǝ mbii mo kas, ɓe gyet mun a kǝrem mon ndǝr Wàar kǝ mbii ɗe gurum mo loot kǝ cìn mo, ɗe mo nyil ɗesǝ mo.
GAL 4:4 Ɗang kaaɗi pee nǝ wul tyap, ɓe Naan wur lep Làa wur sham nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ. Mo làa wur a kaaɗi mo kǝ làa gurum mo sǝ, ndǝr Wàar.
GAL 4:5 Mbǝkǝ wurang nen ɗe mon ndǝr Wàar nǝ ɗi, mbǝkǝ wur le mun ɗee ɗe a jep Naan mo.
GAL 4:6 Mbǝɗe wun a jep wur mo yaksǝ, ɓe Naan wur lep Riin kǝ Làa wur sham nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo. Riin nǝ wur petpee shiɓal nee, Daa puun!
GAL 4:7 Yaksǝ, ɓe nɗǝǝn Naan, baa wu kuɗi a kǝrem mo kas, ɗangɓe wun a jeplu mo. Katɗang wu ɗee a jeplu mo, ɓe wun nsekop kǝ mbii ɗe Naan wur ncìn nǝ jep wur mo.
GAL 4:8 Gyet nyam, ɓe baa wu man Naan kas, ɓe gyet wun a kǝrem mo ndǝr riin ɗe baa mo a naan kas.
GAL 4:9 Ɗangɓe yaksǝ kaaɗi wu man Naan sǝ, koo kaaɗi Naan kǝ man wun sǝ, ɓe cirang ɗang wun ciir kǝɓwoon nNaan, kǝ wun waa wu baa wu dǝm ɗe nɗang Wàar kǝ mbii ɗe gurum mo loot kǝ cìn yi mǝ riin ɗe mo nyil ɗesǝ baa moo mee ɓal kas yi? Ɗyen nwun kǝ wu baa wu ɗee ɗe a kǝrem mo zak aa?
GAL 4:10 Wuu tap kǝ teer mo, kǝ puus serǝɓet mo, kǝ tar mo, kǝ pak teer mo nɗǝǝn ɓit nǝ.
GAL 4:11 Ɗangɓe wu shin kǝǝrmuut taji ɗak ɗe gyet wen cìn pee wun, nǝ yool ɗee a ɗebuu.
GAL 4:12 Ɗyemnaa mo, an kǝn ɗang pee wun, kǝ wu ɗee kaa ghan sǝ. Kaaɗi ghan kǝn ɗee kaa wun sǝ. Baa wuu cìn mee mbii ɗebish nwen kas.
GAL 4:13 Wu man nee, gyet a wen shee jì kǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ nwun. Mbii ɗe gyet nǝ le ɗang wen tong pee wun ɗe, a mbǝɗi baa gyet wen nkoom kas.
GAL 4:14 Koo ɗe gyet shwal nǝ daampee nwun, bǝ baa wu cii an kas, kǝzak, baa wu ɓak an kas. Ɗangɓe wu lap ghan shi pǝtuup mǝndong kaa wuu lap a mee ngulep Naan sǝ. Gyet wu lap ghan a kaa Kristi Jesu shikáa wur sǝ.
GAL 4:15 A nee, retnyit ɗe gyet wu cìn ashak kǝ wen sǝ, nǝ a nii? Mbǝɗe wen sat nwun azeen, katɗang ɗe a mbii ɗe nǝ mmak cìn, ɓe ɗi gyet wun shwatyit fuu mo wu shìn nghan.
GAL 4:16 Cirang ɗangɓe wen mbǝ ciir nɗee a shaarlek fuu yi? Mbǝɗe wen sat zeen nǝ nwun aa?
GAL 4:17 Nen ɗe mo nkaa cìn ɗung nwun sǝ mo, moo gung a mbǝkǝ mo kat ɗeret ɗe nyit fuu, ɗangɓe mbii ɗe nǝ le ɗang mo rǝɓet cìn kǝsǝ nǝ, baa nǝ ret kas. Mo rǝɓet a kǝ wun ɓàkshak ɗe kǝ wen, mbǝkǝ wu kǝlǝng a mo ɗi ɓejee.
GAL 4:18 Katɗang gurum mo tap shak a mbee mbii ɗeret, ɓe nǝ ret zam. Ɗesǝ nǝ azeen-nzeen, koo a pǝrangyi. Koo ɗe ghan ashak kǝ wun, koo ɗe baa ghan ashak kǝ wun kas, ɓe wen kǝn pan wun.
GAL 4:19 Jep fen ɗe kǝn wal nwun sǝ mo, ghan a kaa mat ɗe war nkaa shwaajeel mbee làa-làa sǝ. Wen nsat a nshwaajeel nǝ ɗak, har parɗi mǝse fuu ɗee nciit-nciit kǝ mǝ Kristi.
GAL 4:20 Ɗyeen ghan ndǝǝm pee wun ɗe zam, mbǝkǝ nghan man ar ɗe an nsat mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗe nwun. Yaksǝ, baa wen man mbii ɗe an nsat nwun kas. Mbii nǝ daampee nwen nkaa wun zam.
GAL 4:21 Wun nen ɗe wu sat nee, wun a ndǝr Wàar nǝ mo. Wu sat nwen yaksǝ, wu kǝlǝng mbii ɗe Wàar ɗesǝ nǝ mo nkaa sat nǝ aa?
GAL 4:22 Mo ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝnee <<Gyet Abraham kǝ jep ɗemish mo vǝl. Gyet nǝǝn memee war a kǝrem, kǝ nǝǝn ɗevǝl nǝ, baa war a kǝrem kas.>>
GAL 4:23 Ɗangɓe mo làa-làa kǝ mat ɗe gyet war a kǝrem sǝ, nɗǝǝn nan, ɗangɓe làa mat ɗe gyet baa war a kǝrem kas sǝ, mo làa wur a nciit-nciit kǝ pwoo ɗe gyet Naan wur ten cweer nǝ Abraham.
GAL 4:24 Pwoo ɗesǝ nǝ mee mbiikám ɗejurum ɗe ɓut. Mat ɗevǝl ɗesǝ nǝ mo, mo ɗee a kaa cweerpwoo shi toom mo vǝl sǝ, ɗe gyet Naan wur sat nǝ mo. Hagar a mat ɗe war a kǝrem sǝ, war ɗee a sǝmpwoo ɗe Naan wur cweer nǝ mMosis nkaa jwak Sinai. A war ɗe war làa-làa mo ɓe mo ɗee a kǝrem mo.
GAL 4:25 Hagar war ɗee a sǝmpwoo kǝ jwak Sinai ɗe nǝ nyil Arabiya. War ɗee a kaa Jerusalem sǝ, ɗe war kǝ jep war mo, mo ɗee nkaa cìn ɗak kǝrem mbǝ cicinsǝ.
GAL 4:26 Ɗang Jerusalem ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, baa war a kǝrem kas, war a nǝǝn fun.
GAL 4:27 Ɓǝǝt haal Naan sat nǝnee, <<Wii jeer, yi cìn retnyit. Wii ɗe baa yii cam shwaajeel mǝ làa-làa kas, mbǝɗe mat ɗemish ceen war, war kat jep mo ɗes met mat ɗe war tong ashak kǝ mish war.>>
GAL 4:28 Yaksǝ, ɗyemnaa, mo mmun a jep ɗe mo kǝ tuwap nkaa ɗe wun a kaa Aizik sǝ.
GAL 4:29 Gyet nyam nǝ, ɓe làa ɗe gyet mo làa wur a nɗǝǝn nan sǝ, wur shínjeel laa ɗe gyet mo làa wur a nɗǝǝn Riin. Nǝ aasǝ yaksǝ.
GAL 4:30 Ɗang, mbii ɗe mo ran nǝ nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan nǝ sat a mbǝmi? Nǝ sat nǝnee, <<A ceen kǝrem nǝ war kǝ làa war nǝ, mbǝɗe baa làa kǝrem nǝ mmak sekop ashak kǝ laalu nǝ kas.>>
GAL 4:31 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo, baa mun a kǝrem mo kas, ɗangɓe mun a jeplu mo.
GAL 5:1 Mbii ɗe nǝ le, ɗangɓe Kristi wur pwat kǝ mun ndǝr Wàar kǝ nen Yahudi nǝ mo, a mbǝkǝ mun ɗee ɗi a nankáa sun azeen-nzeen. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wen kǝn sat nwun nee, wu ɗar ɓalɓal kaa nen ɗe mo a nankáa sut sǝ. Taji wu baa wu shìn káa fuu, mbǝkǝ wu baa wu ɗee ɗi a kǝrem kas.
GAL 5:2 Wen Pool, an nkaa sat nǝ wun nee, katɗang wu yit mmee gurum can wun, ɓe nǝ ɗee agaak nǝnee, << mbii ɗe Kristi kǝ cìn mbǝ wun, ɓe nǝ ɗee a buu mǝnǝ.
GAL 5:3 Wen kǝn rǝɓet kǝ koo a weyi man azeen-nzeen nǝ, katɗang mee gurum waa rǝɓet kǝ mo can wur, ɓe nǝ ɗee a tǝng kǝ wur gam koor wàar nǝ mo ɗi jir.
GAL 5:4 Wun nen ɗe wu pan nee, wuu ɗee a ɗe ndǝre nyit Naan, mbǝɗe wuu tap kǝ wàar nǝ mo, ɓe wu pwat kǝ káa fuu mo aku nɗǝǝn Kristi. Wuu ɗee a ɗepǝpal nɗǝǝn ɗeret ɗe Kristi kǝ ten cìn mo mbǝ wun.
GAL 5:5 Ɗangɓe mun nen ɗe baa mu leyit a nkaa can kas, ɓe nɗǝǝn Riin shi shinzeen ɓe, muu tong a shi gongpee shi canciin mǝ ɗe ndǝre mǝ Naan.
GAL 5:6 Katɗang mu ɗee a ɗemǝndong kǝ Kristi Jesu, ɓe baa nǝ kuɗi mee koop nǝ kas, koo ɗe mo can gurum, kǝ koo ɗe baa mo can gurum kas, ɗangɓe mbii ɗe nǝ kǝkoop nǝ a shinzeen ɗe nǝ kám sat nɗǝǝn wal.
GAL 5:7 Dǝ nyam, ɓe wun nkaa sekyeen nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ hakyeng, ɗangɓe yaksǝ, ɓe a me le ɗang baa wu kuɗi wuu mwaan nɗǝǝn zeen nǝ kas yi?
GAL 5:8 Baa a Naan ɗewur pǝrep wun, a wur cíi sekyeen nwun kas.
GAL 5:9 <<A rep yist lee nǝ le kǝ bred wup ɗi.>>
GAL 5:10 Ɗang mbǝɗe mun a ɗemǝndong nɗǝǝn Daa fun, ɓe an shinzeen nee, baa pan fuu mo waa ɗen ɗyik kǝ mǝnǝ kas. Wen shinzeen nee, ngwe ɗewur nǝk wun sǝ, koo ɗewur a wii, ɓe Naan nshín kar wur.
GAL 5:11 Ɗang ɗyemnaa mo, katɗang an kǝn sat an satpwoo nǝ, can nǝ a tǝng, ɓe a me le ɗang ghan kǝn sat a nshwaajeel ɗak yi? Katɗang nǝ aasǝ, ɓe moo shang mbii ɗe nǝ le canshii ngurum mo nɗǝǝn shiyeepyoom Kristi.
GAL 5:12 Nen ɗe mo daampee nookɗi nwun sǝ, wen fes nrǝɓet kǝ mo dǝm pun sut kǝ mo ɗee ɗi a meermuut mo.
GAL 5:13 Ɗyemnaa mo, Naan wur pǝrep wun, mbǝkǝ taji wu ɗee a kǝrem mo ndǝr wàar mǝ nen Yahudi mo kas, ɗangɓe, taji wu le kǝ katpee fuu nǝ, nǝ ɗee a ar ɗe wun ncìn mbii ɗebish mǝ nan ɗi kas. Ɗangɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu walnshak kǝ ɓamshak zak.
GAL 5:14 Mo gam wàar nǝ mo jir a nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗesǝ nǝnee, <<A wal ngǝnang fwaa kaa sak sǝ.>>
GAL 5:15 Katɗang wun nɗee a kaa luwaayil ɗe moo seshak sǝ, ɓe wu tap taji wu tu shak kyes kǝdǝng-ndǝng.
GAL 5:16 Wen kǝn sat nwun nee, wu mwaan nɗǝǝn Riin, mbǝkǝ taji wu gam ɗyen mǝ nan nǝ kas.
GAL 5:17 Mbǝɗe mbii ɗenan nǝ kǝ rǝɓet, ɓe baa mo a nciit kǝ mbii ɗe Riin nǝ rǝɓet kas. Kǝzak, mbii ɗe Riin nǝ rǝɓet ɓe baa mo a nciit kǝ mbii ɗenan nǝ rǝɓet kas. Mbii ɗevǝl sǝ mo baa moo rǝɓet shak kas. Ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee nee baa wu mak cìn mbii ɗe wuu rǝɓet kas.
GAL 5:18 Ɗang katɗang wuu mwaan a nɗǝǝn Riin Naan, ɓe baa wu kuɗi a ndǝr Wàar nǝ kas.
GAL 5:19 Ɗak ɗe gurum moo cìn nɗǝǝn mǝse kǝ gurum, nǝ agaak. Kyeet kǝ ɗak mǝnǝ mo, a kaa cin ngaa, ɗak ɗebish mo, cìn mbii ɗebish nen yitlwaan.
GAL 5:20 Seyil nkùm, ɗak soot, ciishak, jǝǝr, zuur, tuup, rǝɓetkáa, ɓákshak, mǝse ɗe nǝ a mǝ yilangpee.
GAL 5:21 Zuur ɗebish, shwaayuur, kuur ashak ɗebish mo, kǝ mbii ɗebish mo ɗe shini-shinǝ. Wen kǝn satpwoo nwun shiɓal, kaaɗe gyet ghan kǝn sat nwun sǝ nǝ, nen ɗe moo cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo jir, ɓe baa mon ncam ɗel nɗǝǝn mulki Naan kas, koo dǝɓen.
GAL 5:22 Ɗang ɗak ɗe gurum moo cìn nɗǝǝn Riin Naan mo a, walnshak, kǝ retnyit, tongryang, gung mbii mo, naajeel nshak, cìn mbii ɗeret mo, shinzeen,
GAL 5:23 sham kǝ káa, yaasuk. Mbii ɗesǝ mo jir, baa mee Wàar ɗe nkaa mo kas.
GAL 5:24 Nen ɗe mo a mǝ Kristi Jesu, mo kǝ ten pwas nan fur mo nkaa shiyeep ashak kǝ koor nǝ.
GAL 5:25 Katɗang mu tong a nɗǝǝn Riin, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mu mwaan nɗǝǝn Riin nǝ zak.
GAL 5:26 Taji mu ɗiyeepkáa kas, kǝ taji mu le tuup nshak kas. Taji mu cìn zuur kǝ shak kas zak.
