GAL 6:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, katɗang mee gurum taa pal, ɓe wun ɗe wun a ɗe ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn Riin Naan wu ɓam wur, mbǝkǝ wur tuwap ɗe. Wu sham kǝ káa fuu mo, kaaɗe wun nkaa ɓam wur. Wu tap kǝ káa fuu, mbǝkǝ taji wun wu waa wu ɗel nɗǝǝn jwaan nǝ kas.
GAL 6:2 Wu ɓamshak, katɗang wu cìn aasǝ ɓe wu gam Wàar Kristi mǝnǝ.
GAL 6:3 Katɗang memee fuu lekáa wur a mee mbii, ɗangɓe nɗǝǝn zeen nǝ, ɓe baa wur a mee mbii kas, ɓe gwar mǝnǝ nǝk a kaa shin ɓejee ɗak.
GAL 6:4 Ɗang nǝ ret kǝ, koo a wii ɓe wur cam ɗak wur, ɗangɓe wur nleshap shikáa shin, baa ashak kǝ ɗewur kám shin kǝ mee gurum kas.
GAL 6:5 Koo a weyi nɗǝǝn wun ɓe wur mang toon kǝ mbii ɗewur cìn mo shikáa wur.
GAL 6:6 Koo weyi ɗewur nkaa lap kámpwoo Naan, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur ɓàk mbii ɗeret mo jir, ashak kǝ ngukám nǝ.
GAL 6:7 Taji mee gurum gwamkáa shin kas, mbǝɗe baa mee ngwe cam zaal nNaan kas. Mbii ɗe gurum kop ɓe wur nɗyiip a nǝ.
GAL 6:8 Ngwe ɗewur kop a nɗǝǝn nan nwur, ɓe wur nɗyiip a mbii ɗewam nɗǝǝn nan nǝ. Ɗang ngwe ɗewur kop nɗǝǝn Riin Naan, ɓe nɗǝǝn Riin ɓe wur nɗyiip a seen ɗe ngaa-ngaa.
GAL 6:9 Taji kwak fun mo waam mbǝ cìn mbii ɗeret mo kas, mbǝɗe katɗang pee nǝ wul, ɓe mun nɗyiip ɗeret mǝ ɗak fun mo, ka baa mu taa mu muutleet kas.
GAL 6:10 Aasǝ, nǝ ret kǝ mu cìn mbii ɗeret mo, kaaɗe mu katpee nǝ sǝ. Mu cìn mbii ɗeret ngurum mo jir, met jir, a ɗyemnǝǝn fun mo, ɗe mo a nendǝm nɗang Kristi mo.
GAL 6:11 Ran ɗenan-nan ɗe wu naa sǝ mo, a an ran mo shi sar fen shindǝm nwun.
GAL 6:12 A nen ɗe mo rǝɓet leshap nɗǝǝn nan ɗesǝ, a moo rǝɓet letǝng nwun, mbǝkǝ wu can-can ɗe, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ taji mo shwaajeel, mbǝ shiyeepyoom Kristi kas.
GAL 6:13 Nen ɗe moo ten can mo, mo shikáa fur, baa mo kyeer wàar nǝ kas. Ɗangɓe nǝ a rǝɓet kǝ mo, kǝ mo can wun, mbǝkǝ mo katpee ɗe mbǝ canpwoo nkaa wun nɗǝǝn nan.
GAL 6:14 Ɗangɓe pee wen ɗe ɓe a shi shiyeepyoom Daa fun Jesu Kristi, a nǝ a mbii mǝndong ɗe nǝ mmak le kǝ nghan canpwoo ɓejee ɗak. A mbǝ shiyeepmúut wur, ɓe mbii ɗe mǝ nyil ɗesǝ mo, baa mo kuɗi mee koop nǝ pee ghan ɗe kas. Nǝ ɗee a kaa moo ten pwas mo nkaa shiyeepmúut Kristi, kǝzak, an a kaa ngwe ɗe kǝ ten muut sǝ, har wen kǝn yit mbii mǝ nyil ɗesǝ mo mɓwoon.
GAL 6:15 Koo ɗe mo can gurum, kǝ koo ɗe baa mo can gurum kas, ɓe baa nǝ kǝ mee koop nǝ kas. Mbii ɗe nǝ kǝkoop nǝ hakyeng nǝ nɗesǝ, Naan wur shin seen ɗepwoo mun.
GAL 6:16 Mbǝ ɗe mo kǝ mwaan nɗǝǝn seen ɗepwoo ɗesǝ nǝ, ɓe mo a nen Naan mo azeen. Moo tongryang kǝ Naan kǝ wur naa mo shi yit naajeel zak.
GAL 6:17 Yool yaksǝ, ɓe baa ɗyen nwen kǝ mee gurum daampee nwen zak kas, mbǝɗe nǝmer ɗe mo nkaa an mo kám nǝ, an a kǝrem mǝ Jesu.
GAL 6:18 Ɗyemnaa mo, ɗeret mǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi nǝ tong ashak kǝ riin fuu mo jir. Nǝ a kǝsǝ.
EPH 1:1 Pool laalep Kristi shi rǝɓet Naan, shindǝm pee nen Naan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil Afisus, ɗe mo shinzeen nJesu Kristi azeen-nzeen.
EPH 1:2 Ɗeret kǝ ryang mǝ Naan puun fun kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi mo tong ashak kǝ wun.
EPH 1:3 Mu pǝlang Naan puun, kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi, ɗewur le ɗeret wur nkaa mun, shi koo a ɗeret ɗeɗangyi ɗe nǝ a mǝ Riin nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan mo, shi Kristi.
EPH 1:4 Akuɗang Naan wur leyil nǝ, ɓe wur kǝ ten bǝlǝp mun, mbǝkǝ mu ɗee a mǝ wur nɗǝǝn Kristi, mbǝkǝ mu ɗee ɗe a ɗeɓang nɗǝǝn wal mbǝɗe baa mee shikbish ɗi ntoom nwur kas.
EPH 1:5 Naan kǝ ten sat nee, nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi, ɓe ɗyin nle kǝ mun ɗee a jep wur mo. Ɗesǝ nǝ put a nɗǝǝn pan mǝ retnyit wur.
EPH 1:6 Wu yit kǝ mun kwoop wur mbǝ ɗeɗes mǝ yit naajeel nwur, ɗewur shìn mmun nzuum nɗǝǝn Làa wur ɗewur wal wur.
EPH 1:7 Mbǝɗe a shi muut Kristi ɗangɓe mo fween mun, shii mǝnǝ a nee, mo fwo shikbish fun mo mmun. Yit naajeel nNaan nǝ ɗes zam,
EPH 1:8 ɗewur ɗoo nǝ nkaa mun ɗes, kǝ seen kǝ manshii mbii mo jir.
EPH 1:9 Yaksǝ Naan wur le kǝ mun man mbii ɗe mo a sǝsok mǝ pan wur mo, nciit-nciit kǝ pan wur ɗewur kǝ ten le nǝ, kǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗegǝgam nɗǝǝn Kristi.
EPH 1:10 Mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten sat nee, wuɗyin ncìn mo katɗang pee nǝ wul. Ɓe Naan wur njì kǝ mbii ɗewur kǝ ten le mo nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ ashak, kǝ ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan kǝ ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ jir, ɓe Kristi wur nɗee a káa mmo jir.
EPH 1:11 Mon cìn mbii mo jir a nciit-nciit kǝ mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten sat nǝ wuɗin cìn mo. Naan wur ten bǝlǝp mun, kǝ mun ɗee a nen wur mo nɗǝǝn Kristi nciit-nciit kǝ pan wur. Mbii mo ɗes aasǝ, nciit-nciit kǝ mbii ɗewur kǝ ten sat nǝ wuɗin cìn mo pǝgyet ɗi nshee.
EPH 1:12 Mun ɗe mu shee canciin nkaa Kristi, wu yit kǝ mun kwoop Naan mbǝ ɗeɗes wur.
EPH 1:13 A wun zak, wu ɗee a nen Naan mo kaaɗi wu kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe azeen nǝ. Pwoo ɗeret ɗe nǝ jì ɓam wun, kaaɗe wu shinzeen nKristi sǝ, ɓe Naan wur kǝ le sar wur nkaa wun, kǝ nwun ɗee ɗe a mǝ wur. Kaaɗe wur shin Riin Ɗeɓang nǝ nwun nciit-nciit kǝ mbii ɗewur kǝ ten sat sǝ.
EPH 1:14 Riin Ɗeɓang ɗe Naan wur shin nǝ mun, wur ɗee a mbii ɗenshee ɗe nǝ kám mun nǝ, mu lap mbii ɗe Naan ten sat nǝ wuɗyin shìn nen wur mo. Ɗesǝ nǝ kám mun nǝ, Naan wur shínpee nen ɗe mo a mǝwur mo, yit kǝ mu kwoop Ɗehai wur ɗi.
EPH 1:15 Mbǝ mbii ɗesǝ, ɓe yool mparpuus ɗe wen kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa shinzeen fuu nǝ nɗǝǝn Daa Jesu, kǝ wal fuu nǝ mbǝ nen Naan mo jir,
EPH 1:16 ɓe baa wen kǝn nook pǝlang Naan mbǝ wun kas. Wen kǝn pan wun nɗǝǝn ɗangnaan fen mo.
EPH 1:17 Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ Naan kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi, puun ɗehai shidaar-shidaar nee, ɗewur nshin Riin nwun, kǝ wur le nwun ɗee a nenseen mo, kǝ woo man mǝ Naan nwun rǝret hakyeng.
EPH 1:18 Yit kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo wang ɗi, kǝ wu naan pee ɓang wur ɗi, mbǝkǝ wu man mbii ɗe wuu canciin ɗe ke ɗewur kǝ ten pǝrep wun mbǝ nǝ, kǝ kop ɗewur nshin nen wur mo.
EPH 1:19 Baa mee ngwe mmak kám ɗeɗes wur, ɗe nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mun kas, mun nen ɗe mu shinzeen wur. Iiko ɗe nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mun, nǝ nciit-nciit kǝ ɗeɗes mǝ ɓal wur,
EPH 1:20 ɗe gyet wur cìn ɗak kǝ nǝ, mbǝkǝ wur yool ɗe kǝ Kristi a peemúut, kǝ nNaan wur le kǝ Kristi kàa tong nsarse wur nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan.
EPH 1:21 Kristi wur met mɓal mishkoom mo jir, kǝ iiko, kǝ ɓal, kǝ ɗes mǝ se mishkoom mo jir. Sǝm wur nǝ met koor sǝm mo jir. Baa a nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗeyaksǝ ɓejee ɗak kas, ɗangɓe kǝ nɗǝǝn ɓit ɗe mo ndung jì akyeen.
EPH 1:22 Naan wur kǝ ten le mbii mo jir ndershii wur, kǝzak wur le wur ɗee a káa mbii mo jir mbǝ Ekǝlisya nǝ.
EPH 1:23 Kuur nendǝm nɗang wur mo, a shin wur, ɗe mo gam kǝ wur shikáa wur, ɗewur gam mbii mo jir, koo a nɗǝǝn ar ɗeɗangyi
EPH 2:1 Gyet nyam ɓe, wun a ɗemǝmurep nɗǝǝn tep waar kǝ shikbish fuu mo.
EPH 2:2 Gyet nciit kǝ mǝnǝ, ɓe wuu mwaan a nɗǝǝn coor ɗebish mǝ yil ɗesǝ, kǝ nwun kǝlǝng a ɗoo mǝ mishkoom ɓal kǝ riin ɗe mo nɗǝǝn kut mo, riin ɗe nǝ pǝ cin dak nkaa nen ɗe mo cii cìn ɗyen Naan.
EPH 2:3 Gyet mu tong a kaa mo sǝ, nɗǝǝn coor mǝ nan fun mo. Kǝ gyet mu cìn mbii ɗe mu naa mo shang nnan fun mo, kǝ pan mǝ pǝtuup fun mo zak. ɗang nɗǝǝn tong fun, kaa koor gurum mo sǝ, ɓe dǝ mu ten mu ɗee a ɗe mun nshwaajeel mbǝ tuup Naan.
EPH 2:4 Ɗang mbǝɗe kussuk Naan kǝ wal wur nǝ ɗes zam,
EPH 2:5 ɓe jir ɗe gyet mun a ɗemǝmurep nɗǝǝn shikbish fun mo, ɓe wur le kǝ mu kat seen ashak kǝ Kristi. Nǝ a mbǝ yit naajeel Naan, ɗangɓe mu kat ɓam.
EPH 2:6 Naan wur nle kǝ mun yool ashak kǝ Kristi, kǝ wur le kǝ mun tong ashak kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan mbǝ sǝm kǝ Kristi Jesu.
EPH 2:7 nƊǝǝn ɓit ɗe mo pǝ jì, ɓe wur nkám mmun ɗes shi ɗeɗes wur ɗe baa mee gurum mak kám nǝ kas. Ɗesǝ nǝ a yit naajeel wur ɗeɗes mbǝ mun nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu.
EPH 2:8 A mbǝ yit naajeel Naan, ɗangɓe wu kat ɓam, mbǝɗe wu shinzeen. Baa wu kat ɓam ɗesǝ nǝ a mbǝ mee ɗak ɗeret ɗe wu cìn kas, nǝ a zuum mǝ Naan.
EPH 2:9 Baa nǝ a mbǝ mǝnǝ ɗak kas. Mpeemǝnǝ, ɓe taji mee gurum ɗiyeepkáa wur kas.
EPH 2:10 A Naan wur le mun shi sar wur, kaaɗe mun ɗe sǝ, ɗangɓe yaksǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi, ɓe wur le mun a mbǝ cìn ɗak ɗeret mo, ɗewur kǝ ten ɗak nǝ le mbǝ mun, mbǝkǝ mun cìn mo ɗi.
EPH 2:11 Taji wu mundǝr kas, nǝ, gyet nyam ɓe wun a nen ɗe baa mo làa wun a nen Yahudi mo kas. Ɓe gyet nen Yahudi ɗe dǝ mo lesut a nen ɗe mo can mo nɗǝǝn nan shi sar gurum mo, moo pet wun a nen ɗe nsuluk mo.
EPH 2:12 Taji wu mundǝr kas nǝ, gyet mɓít mǝnǝ mo, ɓe baa wu kus kǝ Kristi kas, kǝ baa gyet wu man Naan kas. Gyet mo shwat wun nɗǝǝn jep mǝ nen Yahudi mo, kǝ gyet wun a mǝzep mo. Mbǝɗe Naan kǝ ten ɓǝlemcuk shi toom, kǝ baa gyet wun kǝ mee mbii canciin nɗǝǝn yil nǝ kas.
EPH 2:13 Amma, yaksǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu, ɓe wun ɗe gyet wu jong, mo kǝ jì kǝ wun kus, shi toom Kristi.
EPH 2:14 A Kristi jì kǝ tongryang mmun, ɓe wur le kǝ nen Yahudi mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong kǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Wur shirip kok ɗe gyet nǝ ɓàk mun, mbǝkǝ mun ɗee ɗi a shaarshak.
EPH 2:15 Wur mang Wàar nen Yahudi mo baa kǝnǝ aku, mbǝkǝ wur waa le gurum ɗepwoo mo ɗe nɗǝǝn ɗang ɗevǝl sǝ mo. Ɗe a nɗǝǝn ar ɗesǝ, ɓe wur jì kǝ tongryang.
EPH 2:16 A shi muut wur nkaa shiyeepyoom, ɓe wur tu mbii ɗe nǝ jì kǝ ciishak ngurum mo. A shi shiyeepmúut wur, ɓe wur ɓàl ɗang mo shini-shini, kǝ mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong nɗǝǝn Naan.
EPH 2:17 Jesu wur jì satpwoo, mǝ ryang nwun. Wun nen ɗe gyet wu jong kǝ Naan, kǝzak, wur jì kǝ pwoo nǝ nen ɗe gyet mo kus kǝ Naan zak.
EPH 2:18 A nɗǝǝn Kristi ɓe mun gurum jir, mu mak jì nɗǝǝn Riin ɗemǝndong pǝ puun fun ɗi.
EPH 2:19 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe yaksǝ, wun nen ɗe baa wun a nen Yahudi mo kas, baa wu kuɗi a mǝzep koo pǝkor mo kas. Yaksǝ wun a ɗemǝndong kǝ jepyil mǝ nen Naan mo, kǝ nwun ɗee a jeplu mǝ Naan mo zak.
EPH 2:20 Mo ɗyik wun a nkaa kuk ɗe jeplep kǝ Jesu mo, kǝ nensatpwoo Naan mo kǝ ten ɗyik nǝ. Jesu Kristi wur shikáa wur, a nghǝk ɗeɗes mǝ kwang lu nǝ.
EPH 2:21 A nɗǝǝn wur, ɓe jir koor lu nǝ kǝkàa nkaa wur, kǝ a wur le kǝ lu nǝ wurang, kǝ nǝ ɗee a lu ɗeɓang mǝ Daa.
EPH 2:22 A nɗǝǝn wur, ɓe mo ɗyik wun, kǝ nwun ɗee a pee ɗi Naan wur tong ɗi, shi riin wur.
EPH 3:1 A mbǝ ɗesǝ, ɓe wen Pool, an a shishoot mbǝ Kristi Jesu, mbǝ wun nen ɗe baa wun a nen Yahudi mo kas.
EPH 3:2 Azeen-nzeen wu man nee, nɗǝǝn ɗeret Naan, ɓe wur shin ɗak ɗesǝ nǝ nwen, mbǝkǝ nghan cìn ɗi mbǝ wun.
EPH 3:3 Naan wur woo mbii ɗesǝsok mo nwen ɗewur kǝ ten sat nǝ wuɗin ncìn nwen. Wen kǝn ran pwoo nwun lee nkaa nǝ.
EPH 3:4 Katɗang wu tang mbii ɗe ghan kǝn ran nǝ, ɓe wun mmanshii mman fen, nkaa mbii ɗesǝsok mǝ Kristi.
EPH 3:5 Gyet nyam, ɓe baa mo woo mbii ɗesǝsok nǝ mo ngurum mo kas, amma yaksǝ ɓe Naan wur kǝ woo nǝ agaak pee jeplep Jesu Kristi mo, kǝ nensatpwoo Naan ɗeɓang mo, shi Riin wur ɗeɓang.
EPH 3:6 Mbii ɗesǝsok nǝ a nee, nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, yaksǝ nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ, ɓe mo kat ɗeret mǝ Naan ashak kǝ nen Yahudi nǝ mo. Kǝzak yaksǝ, ɓe nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, mo ɗee a mbii ɗemǝndong. Mo mak sekop nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten cweer nǝ, nwur gam nǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi.
EPH 3:7 A mbee pwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ, ɓe Naan wur nle kǝ ghan ɗee a ngucìn ɗak wur, nciit kǝ zuum ɗeret mǝ yit naajeel wur ɗewur kǝcin nwen, ɗe nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn ɓal wur.
EPH 3:8 Koo ɗe ghan a ɗetaakat met jir nɗǝǝn nen Naan mo, amma Naan wur cin ɗak ɗesǝ nǝ nwen, ɗe nǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ mbǝ nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas. Pwoo nkaa long Kristi ɗe baa nǝ kǝ peekyes kas.
EPH 3:9 Kǝzak, mbǝkǝ nghan le kǝ gurum mo manshii mbii ɗesǝsok mǝ Naan mo ɗi, ɗe Naan ɗewur le mbii mo nɗǝǝn nyil nǝ jir, ɓe wur kǝ ten sok mbii ɗesǝ nǝ mbee ɓit mo ɗes.
EPH 3:10 Pan wur ɗesǝ nǝ, yaksǝ nɗǝǝn nendǝm nɗang wur mo, ɓe ɗeɗes mǝ seen wur nǝ ɗee agaak nɗǝǝn ar mo shini-shini, pǝ nenlep Naan mo kǝ iiko ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan
EPH 3:11 Nciit-nciit kǝ mbii ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten sat nee, wuɗin ncìn nǝ shindǝm ngaa-ngaa, ɗewur gam nǝ nɗǝǝn ɓalkaa fun ashak kǝ Kristi Jesu Daa fun.
EPH 3:12 Kǝ shinzeen fun nɗǝǝn wur, ɓe mu katɓal mpǝtuup, kǝ mu dǝm ɗe ntoom Naan, baa a shi kǝǝrmuut kas.
EPH 3:13 Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ wun, taji kwak fuu mo murep kas, mbǝɗe jir shawaajeel ɗe an nkaa shwaa nǝ a mbǝ wun. Shwaajeel fen nǝ kǝkoop nǝ pee wun ɗi.
EPH 3:14 A mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe an kǝn kurum ntoom puun,
EPH 3:15 a mbǝ wur, ɓe koo a weyi ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan kǝ ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ moo kat sǝm wur.
EPH 3:16 Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ Naan nɗǝǝn long wur ɗeɗes, mbǝkǝ wur shin iiko ɗe nwun nɗǝǝn Riin wur. Mbǝkǝ nwun katɓal ɗe nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
EPH 3:17 Mɓe kǝ Kristi wur tong nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, mbǝɗe wu shinzeen wur. Wu shamseen, kǝ nwun ɗar nkaa kuk ɗe nǝ a wal.
EPH 3:18 Mbǝkǝ nwun, ashak kǝ nen Naan mo, ɓe wu man kaam, kǝ shwal, kǝ wurang, kǝ jurum mǝ wal mǝ Kristi ɗi.
EPH 3:19 Kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wu man wal mǝ Kristi ɗe nǝ met nkoor man mo jir, mbǝkǝ wu gam ɗi kǝ man Naan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
EPH 3:20 Yaksǝ, pee wur, ɗewur kǝ iiko ɗe nǝ cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mun, met mbii ɗe mu mak ɗang mo, koo pan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun.
EPH 3:21 Ɗeɗes nǝ ɗee a mǝ Naan nɗǝǝn nendǝm ndang wur mo, kǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu mbǝ pǝ mo jir, yool yaksǝ kǝ, har ngaa-ngaa. Nǝ a kǝsǝ.
EPH 4:1 Wen ɗe an a shishoot mbǝ sǝm Daa. Wen kǝn ɗang pǝ wun, mbǝkǝ wu mwaan-mwaan ɗe mo lapshak kǝ petpee ɗe Naan wur kǝ pǝrep wun mbǝ nǝ.
EPH 4:2 Wu sham kǝ káa fuu mo koo pǝranyi. Wu cìn mbii mo nɗǝǝn ɗyen, kǝ wun gung zak. Wu kám wal fuu mo agaak, kǝ nwun fwangshak zak.
EPH 4:3 Wu gung, kǝ nwun tap ɗe kǝ ɓalkaa ɗe Riin wur shin nwun, shi tongryang ɗe nǝ ɓàl wun ashak.
EPH 4:4 Shin nǝ a mǝndong, kǝ Riin nǝ mǝndong ɓejee. Kaaɗi mo kǝ pǝrep wun, nɗǝǝn canciin mǝndong nkaa mbii ɗe mo kǝ pet wun mbǝ nǝ.
EPH 4:5 Daa a mǝndong, shinzeen nǝ a mǝndong, baptisma nǝ a mǝndong,
EPH 4:6 Naan a mǝndong, ɗewur a puun fun jir. Wur met mbii mo jir, kǝ a wur cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn mun jir, kǝ a wur nɗǝǝn mun jir zak.
EPH 4:7 Ɗang koo a weyi nɗǝǝn mun, ɓe wur kǝ lap ɗeret nciit-nciit kǝ zuum kǝ Kristi.
EPH 4:8 Kaaɗe mo kǝ ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal Naan sǝ nǝnee, <<Kaaɗe Kristi wur kaa aɗeng, ɓe wur pan kǝrem ɗeyiyak mo ɗes ashak kǝ wur, kǝ wur shin zuum ngurum mo zak.>>
EPH 4:9 Yaksǝ, ɓe nǝnee, <<wur kaa aɗeng >> ɓe shii mǝnǝ a mii? Shii mǝnǝ nee, nshee ɓe wur sham nɗǝǝn jurum kǝ peekyes kǝ yil ɗesǝ.
EPH 4:10 Mbǝmǝnǝ, gwar ɗe gyet wur sham, a wur a gwar ɗewur kaa aɗeng-ɗeng a kǝkyeen ɗengnaan mo, mbǝkǝ wur gam ɗeng kǝ yil jir.
EPH 4:11 A wur shìn zuum ngurum mbǝkǝ npak mo ɗee ɗi, a jeplep mo, kǝ npak mo ɗee a nensatpwoo Naan mo, kǝ npak mo ɗee ɗi a nenkop pwoo Naan mo, kǝ npak mo ɗee ɗi a Pasto mo, kǝ npak mo ɗee ɗi a nenkám kam mo zak.
EPH 4:12 Wur shin zuum ɗesǝ mo, a mbǝkǝ nǝ ɗak nen Naan mo ɗe, mbǝ ɓamshak, kǝ mbǝkǝ mo ɗyik fwoshik kǝ Kristi ɗi.
EPH 4:13 Nǝ aasǝ, ɓe mun jir, mun nyool mu ɗee a ɗemǝndong nɗǝǝn shinzeen fun, kǝ man fun ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn Làa Naan. Mun nyool mu ɗee a nen ɗe kǝ man mo, Mbǝkǝ mun wul mbǝ gam ɗeɗes mǝ Kristi.
EPH 4:14 Ɓe baa mu kuɗi a jep ɗeɗyeen mo kas mǝnǝ, ɗe mo nnum mun shindǝm sǝ, Mbǝkǝ mo mang mun pán, shi koo a kyaan kám ɗeɗangyi kas. Mo a nenseen mo ɗe mo a korong mbǝ ɓǝrǝm ɗung.
EPH 4:15 Akoppee mǝnǝ nǝ ret kǝ mun sat zeen nǝ nɗǝǝn nwal. Nǝ ret kǝ mun wurang nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir, nɗǝǝn Kristi ɗewur a káa fun.
EPH 4:16 A mbǝ wur, ɗangɓe koo a ɓeep ɗeɗangyi, mo shini-shini, mo tap ɓàl ashak, kǝ koo a peeɓal ɗeɗangyi, nǝ katɓal a nɗǝǝn wur. Katɗang koo a ɓeep ɗeɗangyi nǝ kǝ cìn ɗak war rǝret, ɓe fwoshik nǝ nwurang, kǝ nǝ ɗyik set ɗi nɗǝǝn nwal zak.
EPH 4:17 nƊǝǝn sǝm Daa, ɓe nkǝn satpwoo wun shiɓal nǝ, taji wu sat a ntong kaa nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas sǝ, ɗe pan mo a ɗebuu.
EPH 4:18 Pan ɗe nɗǝǝn pǝtuup mo, nǝ a mǝ peenkwoo, baa mo kǝ mee lǝɓet nɗǝǝn seen ɗe Naan shin kas, mbǝɗe baa mo kǝ mee man kas, kǝ mo ɗee a nencinshik mo.
EPH 4:19 Baa mo kuɗi kǝ naashweep kǝ mee mbii kas. Mo fes shínkáa fur mo mbǝ cìn mbii ɗebish mo, kǝ moo coor mbǝ cìn koo a mbii ɗebish ɗeɗangyi. Baa moo kǝ mee yaasut kas.
EPH 4:20 Amma baa a mbii ɗe wun wu kám pee Kristi ɗe mǝnǝ kas!
EPH 4:21 Mo sat nnǝ, wuu ten wu kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa wur, kǝ mmoo kám nwun zeen ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn Jesu.
EPH 4:22 Wu shwat suk ɗesǝǝr nǝ mo wu baa kǝ mo aku, ɗe dǝ moo nnum wun nɗǝǝn coor mǝ nan sǝ.
EPH 4:23 Nǝ a tǝng kǝ npǝtuup fuu mo kǝ pan fuu mo ɗee a ɗepwoo,
EPH 4:24 Kǝzak, nǝ a tǝng kǝ wu jwal fwoshik ɗepwoo nǝ mo, ɗe Naan wur ɗak mǝnǝ shikaa fin sǝ, kǝ nǝ woo káa nnǝ agaak nɗǝǝn seen ɗe nǝ azeen-nzeen ɗe nǝ a ɗeret kǝ ɗeɓang.
EPH 4:25 Mbǝmǝnǝ, wu baa kǝ ɗung nɗǝǝn wun, kǝ koo a weyi ɓe wur sat azeen ngǝnǝǝn wur ɓejee ɗak. Mbǝɗe mun a ɗemǝndong kǝ shak nɗǝǝn Kristi.
EPH 4:26 Katɗang wu langtuup, ɓe taji wu cìn shikbish kas. Taji puus shamru, ɓe wun ɗe nkaa langtuup kas.
EPH 4:27 Taji wu shínpee ngujwaan kas.
EPH 4:28 Ngwe ɗe wur cìn wat, ɓe taji wur baa cìn ɗe kas, ɗangɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur cìn ɗak ɗeret shi sar wur, mbǝkǝ wur mak cin mee mbii ɗe nen ɗe mo mɓut njeel
EPH 4:29 Taji pwoo ɗebish mo put nɗǝǝn pwoo fuu mo kas, ɗangɓe ɗang a mbii ɗeret mo, ɗe mon nɗyik wun, kaaɗi nǝ tap ret kǝ pee nǝ sǝ. Mbǝkǝ nǝ jì ɗe kǝ ɗeret nen ɗe moo kǝlǝng nǝ.
EPH 4:30 Taji wu wàt pǝtuup nRiin Ɗeɓang mǝ Naan kas, wur ɗe a wur ɗee a langtǝng nǝ, wuu ɗee a ɗe fufwang mbǝ parpuus ɗe mon mɓam wun.
EPH 4:31 Wu pwat kǝ pwoo ɗeɗeet mo, kǝ ciishak, kǝ tuup, kǝ ɓutbish, kǝ fǝlǝppee ashak kǝ cìn nyang mo jir.
EPH 4:32 Ɗang nǝ ret kǝ nwun naajeel shak, kǝ nwun ɓam shak, kǝ nwun fwo ɗi nshak, kaaɗi Naan wur fwo ɗi nwun nɗǝǝn Kristi sǝ.
EPH 5:1 Kaaɗe wun a jep Naan mo ɗewur wal wun sǝ, ɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ nwun kám shiimwaan Naan.
EPH 5:2 Kǝzak, wu mwaan nɗǝǝn wal, kaaɗe Kristi wur wal mmun sǝ, ɓe wur shìn kaashin mbǝ mun kaa zuum kǝ mbiizuum ɗe nǝ kǝ toos shang shang pǝ Naan ɗi.
EPH 5:3 Taji pwoo nkaa ngaa, kǝ mbii ɗebish mo, kǝ rǝɓet mbii mo pwat nɗǝǝn pwoo fuu mo kas. Mbǝɗe pwoo nkaa kaan kǝ mǝnǝ mo, baa nǝ ret kǝ mo pwat mpwoo nen Naan mo kas.
EPH 5:4 Kǝsǝ zak, taji mee pwoo ɗebish mǝ le naashweep kǝ pwoo mǝ mwen mo, kǝ pwoo ɗebuu mo, mo pwat nɗǝǝn pwoo fuu mo kas, amma wu yit kǝn plang put pwoo fuu mo.
EPH 5:5 Taji wu mundǝr nee, nen ɗe moo cìn ngaa, kǝ nen ɗe pan mo a ɗebish, kǝ ngutǝlǝk mo, ɓe baa mee kaan nen mǝnǝ moo mee lǝɓet mǝ sekop nɗǝǝn mulki Kristi kǝ mǝ Naan kas.
EPH 5:6 Taji wu yit kǝ mee gurum nnum wun shi pwoo ɗebuu mo kas, mbǝɗe a mbǝ mbii mo kaa ɗesǝ mo ɓe tuup Naan nǝ taa nkaa nencii kǝlǝngpee mo.
EPH 5:7 Mbǝmǝnǝ, taji wu ɓalkaa fuu ashak kǝ nen mǝnǝ mo kas.
EPH 5:8 Gyet nyam, wun a nɗǝǝn peenkwoo, ɗangɓe yaksǝ wun a nɗǝǝn peeɓang, nɗǝǝn Daa. Nǝ ret kǝ wu mwaan kaa nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn peeɓang nǝ sǝ.
EPH 5:9 Ɗak nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn peeɓang, nǝ a nɗǝǝn mbii ɗeret mo, kǝ ɗe ndǝre mo, kǝ zeen zak.
EPH 5:10 Wu gung, kǝ nwun kám mbii ɗe mon nret nNaan nyit.
EPH 5:11 Taji wu lesar fuu mo nɗǝǝn ɗak ɗe mo a mǝ peenkwoo, ɗe baa mo kǝkoop nǝ kas, ɗangɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu woo ɗak mǝnǝ mo agaak.
EPH 5:12 Nǝ a mbii naashweep mbee satpwoo nkaa mbii ɗe moo cìn mo a sǝsok.
EPH 5:13 Ɗang katɗang jir mbii ɗe nǝ agaak, a pee ɗe ɓang ɗi, ɓe nǝ nɗee a ɗe gurum mo mak naa nǝ. Mbǝɗe jir mbii ɗe gurum mo mak naa nǝ, ɓe nǝ a nɗǝǝn peeɓang.
EPH 5:14 Nǝ a kaaɗi mo kǝ ran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal nNaan sǝ nǝnee, <<Ngusaam, a mii, a yool a peemúut Mbǝkǝ Kristi wur shin peeɓang ɗe ngha>>
EPH 5:15 Wu tap kǝ shiimwaan fuu mo. Taji wu mwaan kaa mwen mo sǝ kas, ɗangɓe wu mwaan kaa nen ɗe kǝ seen mo sǝ.
EPH 5:16 Wu cìn ɗak koo a pee ɗeɗangyi, mbǝɗe teer ɗe yaksǝ nǝ mo gam kǝ mbii ɗebish mo.
EPH 5:17 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe taji wu ɗee a mwen mo kas, amma wu manshii kǝ mbii ɗe Daa wur rǝɓet kǝ nwun cìn.
EPH 5:18 Taji wu shwaa am anab kǝ nǝ yuur wun kas, mbǝɗe mǝnǝ mak jwaan wun, amma wu ɗee a ɗegǝgam shi Riin Ɗeɓang.
EPH 5:19 Wu sat mee pwoo kǝ shak shi kook ɗe mǝ kwoop mo, kǝ kook ɗe mo a mǝ Riin. Wu cìn kook ɗeret mo nNaan, kǝ pǝlang nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
EPH 5:20 Koo pǝranyi ɓe wu plang Naan puun mbǝ mbii mo jir nɗǝǝn sǝm nDaa fun Jesu Kristi.
EPH 5:21 Wu shin ɗeɗes ndǝr shak, mbǝkǝ wu shin ɗeɗes ɗi nKristi.
EPH 5:22 Mat mo, wu shin ɗe ɗeɗes mmish fuu mo, kaaɗi wuu cìn nDaa sǝ.
EPH 5:23 Mbǝɗe mish wur a káa mat, kaaɗi Kristi wur a káa Ekǝlisya sǝ, shii kǝ mǝnǝ a fwooshin fin kǝ wur shikáa fin a Nguɓam war zak.
EPH 5:24 Kaaɗe Ekǝlisya war ndǝr Kristi, nǝ aasǝ zak, wun mat mo, wu shin ɗeɗes mmish fuu mo nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir.
EPH 5:25 Mish mo, wu wal mmat fuu mo, kaaɗi Kristi wur wal Ekǝlisya nǝ sǝ, har wur shinkaa shin mbǝ war.
EPH 5:26 Mbǝkǝ wur le war ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang shi vwang war kǝ am, kǝ pwoo Naan.
EPH 5:27 Mbǝkǝ wur ɗak Ekǝlisya nǝ le ɗe nshin, nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes, kǝ ɗemen, baa ashak kǝ mee rap, kǝ mee pee taakat mɓut mo kas. Mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗe a ɗeɓang baa kǝ mee rap kas.
EPH 5:28 Ni ret kǝ mish mo wal mmat fur mo kaa sut sǝ. Ngwe ɗewur wal mmat wur, ɓe wur wal a nshin mǝnǝ.
EPH 5:29 Baa mee gurum kǝ cam cii shin kas, ɗangɓe wur tap shin mbiise nnǝ, kǝ wur tap kǝ nǝ rǝret, kaaɗi Kristi wur cìn Ekǝlisya sǝ
EPH 5:30 Mbǝɗe mun a ɓeep mǝ foshik nwur.
EPH 5:31 A mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe gurum wur nyit puun wur kǝ nǝǝn wur, kǝ wur ɓalkaa ɗe ashak kǝ mat wur, kǝ mo vǝl mo ɗee ɗi a ɗemǝndong.
EPH 5:32 Ɗesǝ nǝ a mee mbii ɗeɗes ɗesǝsok. Mbii ɗe wen kǝn sat nǝ, a nkaa Kristi kǝ Ekǝlisya.
EPH 5:33 Jir arang ɓe wu yit koo weyi wur wal mmat wur, kaa kaashin sǝ, kǝ mat war shin ɗeɗes mmish war zak.
EPH 6:1 Jep mo, wu kǝlǝng pwoo mpuun fuu mo nɗǝǝn Daa, mbǝɗe mǝnǝ a mbii ɗe ndǝre.
EPH 6:2 <<A shin ɗeɗes mpuun fwa kǝ nǝǝn fwaa mo,>> ɗesǝ nǝ a Wàar ɗenshee ɗe mo kǝ ten le,
EPH 6:3 <<mbǝkǝ a tong ɗi ryang, kǝ mbǝkǝ a kat teer mo ɗi ɗes nɗǝǝn nyil nǝ.>>
EPH 6:4 Puun mo, taji wu le kǝ pǝtuup jep fuu mo wat, kǝ nǝ le kǝ mo cìn tuup kas, amma wu kyeer mo, kǝ wu kar mo nɗǝǝn kám ɗe mo a mǝ Daa Naan.
EPH 6:5 Kǝrem mo, wu kǝlengpwoo nen ɗe moo ɗyel wun nsar fur mo. Kǝn sat a puun fuu ɗe mo a mǝ yil ɗesǝ nǝ. Wu kǝlengpwoo mo nɗǝǝn kǝǝr kǝ ɗaar shi pǝtuup mǝndong, kaaɗi wuu cìn nKristi sǝ.
EPH 6:6 Taji wu cìn ɗak a yit gurum mo ɓejee, kǝ mo plang wun ɗe kas, amma wu cìn ɗak kaa kǝrem mǝ Kristi sǝ. Wu cìn ɗyen nNaan nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
EPH 6:7 Wu cìn ɗak shi pǝtuup ɗeret, mbǝɗe wu cìn a nDaa Naan, baa a mmee gurum kas.
EPH 6:8 Taji wu mundǝr kas nǝ, ɗak ɗeret ɗe gurum kǝ cìn mo, ɓe wur nwaa lap kwat nǝ pee Daa ɗi, koo ɗewur a kǝrem, kǝ ɗewur a laalu.
EPH 6:9 Wun nen ɗe wun kǝ kǝrem mo wu cìn mbii ɗeret mmo zak. Taji wu wuk mo kas, mbǝɗe wu man nǝ, Daa fu kǝ moo, wur a nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, baa wur kǝ nshwatyit kas.
EPH 6:10 Peekyes nǝ, wu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn Daa nɗǝǝn iiko mǝ ɗeɗes wur.
EPH 6:11 Wu jwal leelek ɗe Naan wur shin mo wun jir, mbǝkǝ nwun mak ɗar ɗi ɓalɓal nkaa Ngujwaan kǝ gwampee wur.
EPH 6:12 Mbǝɗe baa mu cìn lek nǝ a nkaa gurum mo, ɗe moo nan kǝ toom kas, ɗangɓe nǝ a nkaa se mishkoom, nen iiko ɗe mo a mǝ Ngujwaan mo, nkaa se mishkoom kǝ nen peeknwoo ɗe nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan mo.
EPH 6:13 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu jwal leelek ɗe Naan wur nshin nwun, mbǝkǝ nwun ɗar ɗi ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn teer ɗebish mo. Mbǝkǝ taji Ngujwaan wur se koorong nkaa wun kas.
EPH 6:14 Wu ɗar ɓalɓal shi ɗak suk, kǝ ɓwoot ɓwoon fuu mo shi zeen, kǝ cìn mbii ɗe ndǝre kaa kawung ɗe nǝ tap tuur ngurum sǝ.
EPH 6:15 Wu jwal kwoopshii nshii fuu mo, mbǝ satpwoo ɗeret, ɗe nǝn jì kǝ tongryang.
EPH 6:16 Koo pǝrangyi, ɓe wu mang gwat ɗe nǝ a shinzeen ashak kǝ wun, mbǝ tap pas mǝ wus ɗe gwar ɗebish nǝ wur mpwas shinji nkaa wun.
EPH 6:17 Wu mang ɓam ɗe Naan wur cìn nwun, kaa mbiikáa shool ɗe nenlek moo lep mbǝkǝ nǝ tap káa ɗi mmo sǝ. Kǝ wu ɗyel pwoo Naan nǝ, kaa kwai ɗe Riin Ɗeɓang wur shin nwun sǝ.
EPH 6:18 Wu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), mbǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo shidaar-shidaar nɗǝǝn Riin. Wu tong shi gongpee, kǝzak, wu gung nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir. Wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mbǝ nen Naan mo jir.
EPH 6:19 Wu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mbǝ ghan zak, mbǝkǝ Naan wur cìn mbii ɗe wen nsat mo ɗi, kǝ mbǝkǝ ghan sat mbii ɗesǝsok mǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ mo, ɗe shiɓal baa a shi kǝǝrmuut kas.
EPH 6:20 A mbǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ, ɗang mo lep an mbǝkǝ wen sat nǝ ɗi. Ɓe wen a shishoot shi tǝsek mǝ shool yaksǝ. Jir kǝ ɗe an a shishoot, ɓe wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan), mbǝkǝ wur shinɓal ɗi nwen, kǝn satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗe shiɓal, kaaɗi nǝ ret kǝ wen cìn sǝ.
EPH 6:21 Tikikus ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗe mu wal wur, ɗewur a kǝrem Daa azeen-nzeen, wur nsat mbii mo nwun jir, nkaa an, kǝ nkaa ɗak ɗe ghan nkaa cìn nǝ.
EPH 6:22 Wen kǝn ten nlep wur shindǝm pee wun ɗe, a mbǝkǝ wur satpwoo ɗi nwun nkaa mun, mbǝkǝ nwun man tong fun ɗe, kǝ nǝ ɓam pǝtuup fuu mo ɗi zak.
EPH 6:23 Naan puun, kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi shin tongryang, kǝ wal, kǝ shinzeen nɗyemnǝǝn fun mo jir.
EPH 6:24 Ɗeret Naan nǝ ɗee ashak kǝ nen ɗe mo wal nDaa fun Jesu Kristi, shi wal ɗe baa nii peekyes kas har ngaa-ngaa.
PHI 1:1 Lepran ɗesǝ nǝ put a nsar Pool kǝ Timoti kǝrem Daa Jesu Kristi mo, shindǝm pee nen Naan, ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil nFilipi ɗe mo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak kǝ Kristi, jir kǝ nen ɗenan-nan mǝ Ekǝlisya mo, kǝ nenɓam mo, kǝ Bishop mo, kǝ Dikon mo.
PHI 1:2 Naan puun fun kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi, mo shin ɗeret kǝ tongryang nwun.
PHI 1:3 Wen kǝn plang Naan koo a pǝrangyi, katɗang wen yee wun,
PHI 1:4 nɗǝǝn ɗangnaan ɗe kǝn cìn mbǝ wun jir shidaar-shidaar, ɓe kǝn cìn nǝ a shi retnyit
PHI 1:5 mbǝɗe wu fes wu ɓalkaa fuu kǝ an nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ, yool mpuus ɗe gyet wu shee kǝlǝng nǝ jiwul cicinsǝ.
PHI 1:6 Wen man azeen-nzeen nee, Naan ɗewur yaa cìn ɗak ɗeret ɗesǝ nɗǝǝn wun, wur nsat a ncìn nǝ har parpuus ɗe Kristi Jesu wur mbaaji.
PHI 1:7 Wen kǝn yee wun nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fen shidaar-shidaar, mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wen kat pan mǝnǝ nkaa wun. Mbǝɗe wu ɓalkaa fuu mo kǝ an nɗǝǝn ɗeret ɗe Naan wur cin nwen. Kaaɗi yaksǝ, ɓe wen nɗǝǝn lushoot, kǝ kaaɗi gyet wen katpee mbǝkǝ wen kám ɗi ngurum mo nee, pwoo ɗeret nǝ azeen-nzeen.
PHI 1:8 Naan wur a langtǝng fen, pan ɗe ghan kǝ nǝ mbǝ wun nǝ a kaa wal ɗe Jesu Kristi shikáa wur kǝ nǝ mbǝ mun sǝ.
PHI 1:9 Wen kǝn ɗangnaan, mbǝkǝ nwal fuu nǝ naa nwurang ɗe, kǝ mbǝkǝ wu kat man kǝ seen ɗi wun mman ɓeet mbii mo ɗe ndǝre-ndǝre.
PHI 1:10 Mbǝkǝ nwun bǝlǝp mbii ɗe nǝ rǝret met ɗi, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wu ɗee ɗe a ɗeɓang, ɗe baa wun kǝ mee rap kas parpuus Kristi wur mbaaji.
PHI 1:11 Seen fuu mo gam kǝ mbii ɗeret mo azeen-nzeen, ɗe a Jesu Kristi wur mak shìn nǝ ɓejee, mbǝ le Naan a ɗeɗes kǝ kwoop wur.
PHI 1:12 Ɗyemnaa mo, kǝn rǝɓet kǝ nwun man nee, jeel ɗe mo kat wen, ɓe nǝ le kǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ sekyeen.
PHI 1:13 har shiitoon ɗe moo tap lu mishkoom nRom, kǝ pak gurum mo, mo man nǝ, wen a shishoot a mbǝ sǝm Jesu Kristi.
PHI 1:14 Pak ɗyemnǝǝn fun mo ɗes ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Daa mo waa katɓal nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo, mbǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ shi pǝtuup mǝndong, baa a shi kǝǝrmuut kas, mbǝɗe wen a shishoot a mbǝ sǝm Jesu.
PHI 1:15 Ii, azeen-nzeen, pak moo satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Kristi a mbǝ zuur, kǝ ɓǝlep, ɗangɓe pak moo sat a shi pǝtuup mǝndong.
PHI 1:16 Nen ɗe moo satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Kristi shi pǝtuup mǝndong sǝ, moo sat mǝnǝ a nɗǝǝn nwal, kǝzak, mo man nǝ, wen a shishoot a mbǝɗe an kǝ ɗar ɓalɓal bǝ tap pwoo ɗeret nǝ.
PHI 1:17 Ɗangɓe nen ɗe moo satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Kristi a mbǝ zuur sǝ, moo rǝɓet wat a pǝtuup fen, kǝ mo pan nǝ, wuɗun jì aa jeel nkaa wen nɗǝǝn lushoot nǝ.
PHI 1:18 Baa nǝ daampee nghan kas, katɗang mo satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Kristi, koo a mbǝ mbii ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ ret nwen nyit. Koo ɗe moo sat a nɗǝǝn pan ɗebish, koo ɗe moo sat a nɗǝǝn pan ɗeret, ɓe ghan nsat a nkat retnyit ɗak, mbǝɗe gurum moo kǝlǝng pwoo ɗeret nkaa Kristi jir neyi.
PHI 1:19 Mbǝɗe wen man nǝ, shi ɗangnaan fuu mbǝ ghan, kǝ ɓam ɗe nǝ put pǝ Riin Jesu Kristi ɗi, ɓe mon nbwoot wen.
PHI 1:20 A ɗyen fen kǝ canciin fen ɗesǝ nǝ, baa wen cìn mee mbii ɗe nǝ njì kǝ naashweep nkaa ghan kas. Ɗangɓe rǝɓet fen, kǝ nghan satpwoo ɗeret nǝ shiɓal baa shi kǝǝrmuut kas mbǝkǝ koo a ɗeɗangyi, kǝ koo a pǝrangyi, ɓe wen shin ɗeɗes ɗe nKristi shiɓal kǝ foshik fen jir. Koo ɗe wen ɗe kǝ seen, kǝ koo ɗi wen mmuut.
PHI 1:21 Pee wen ɗi, ɓe seen fen nǝ a Kristi, kǝ muut fen nǝ a lǝɓet zak.
PHI 1:22 Ɗang katɗang wen sat a ntong nɗǝǝn nan ɗesǝ ɗak, ɓe ghan ncìn ɗak ɗe nǝ mɓam gurum mo. Yaksǝ baa nghan mman ar ɗe ghan mbǝlǝp kas.
PHI 1:23 Wen ɗee a kaa kamlang a naar kǝ am sǝ. Pan ɗevǝl ɗesǝ nǝ mo dul ghan shindǝm nɗǝǝn ar mo vǝl. Wen kǝn rǝɓet kǝ ghan muut ɗe yaksǝ, mbǝkǝ ghan dǝm ntong ɗe ashak kǝ Kristi, mǝnǝ ret nwen met.
PHI 1:24 Ɗang nǝ kǝkoop nǝ zam, mbǝkǝ nghan tong ɗi kǝ seen nɗǝǝn fwoshik ɗesǝ, mbǝ ɓam wun.
PHI 1:25 Mbǝɗe nghan man zeen nǝ aasǝ. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wen man nee, baa nghan mmuut yaksǝ kas, nghan ntong ɗi, mbǝkǝ wen ɓam wun ɗe kǝ wu sekyeen ɗe shi retnyit nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu.
PHI 1:26 Mbǝkǝ katɗang wen mbaajì pee wun ɗi zak, ɓe wu kat mbii ɗe wun canpwoo ɗi kaa an, mbǝ seen ɗe wun kǝ nǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu, mbǝ tong ɗe wen ntong ashak kǝ wun nǝ.
PHI 1:27 Nǝ a tǝng kǝ nwun mwaan a nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe pwoo ɗeret Kristi nǝ sat nnǝ wu cìn mo. Mbǝkǝ koo ɗe nghan njì naa wun, koo ɗe baa nghan nkatpee baaji naa wun kas, ɓe nghan kǝlǝng nǝ, wuu ɗar a ɗe ɓalɓal, kǝ pwoo fuu mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong, kǝ pan fuu mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong zak. Mbǝkǝ wu cìn lek ɗi ashak, mbǝ pwoo ɗeret, ɗe wuu shinzeen nǝ.
PHI 1:28 Taji wu kǝǝr shaarlek fuu mo kas, koo dǝɓen. Ɗesǝ nǝ nkám mmo nǝ, Naan wur kǝ ten ɓam wun, ɗangɓe wur ntwe mo mbǝ shikbish fur mo. Mbǝkǝ nwun man ɗe zak nǝ, Naan shikáa wur, wur nshin korong nǝ nwun aasǝ.
PHI 1:29 Naan wur shínpee nwun, baa a mbǝkǝ wu shinzeen ɗi nKristi ɓejee kas, ɗangɓe a mbǝkǝ wu shwaajeel ɗe mbǝ wur zak.
PHI 1:30 Yaksǝ nwun mak cìn lek nǝ ashak kǝ an. Lek ɗesǝ nǝ a lek ɗemǝndong kǝ ɗe gyet wu naa an nkaa cìn nǝ, kǝ kaaɗe wu kǝlǝng nǝ, an ɗe a nkaa cìn lek mǝnǝ jiwul cicinsǝ.
PHI 2:1 Katɗang seen fuu ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi mo ɗee a ɗeɓal. Katɗang wal wur nǝ jwan wun, katɗang wuu shaar ashak kǝ Riin wur, katɗang wuu naajeel shak kǝcin ɗeret shak,
PHI 2:2 ɓe wu le kǝ retnyit fen nǝ gam, kǝ pan fuu mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong kǝ wal fuu nǝ ɗee a ɗemǝndong kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo ɗee a ɗemǝndong nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir.
PHI 2:3 Taji wu cìn mee mbii mbǝ rǝɓetkáa kǝ ɗiyeepkáa kas, ɗangɓe wu sham kǝ káa fuu mo. Wu shin ɗeɗes nshak met nkáa fuu mo.
PHI 2:4 Taji memee fuu ɗee ntap a mbii ɗe mo a mǝkáa fin ɓejee ɗak kas, ɗangɓe wun ntap kǝ mbii mǝ nyee fuu mo zak.
PHI 2:5 Wu yit kǝ mǝse fuu mo ɗee a kaa mǝse Jesu Kristi wur kǝ nǝ.
PHI 2:6 Jesu ɗewur a ɗemǝndong kǝ Naan, ɗangɓe baa wur lekáa fin nciit-nciit kǝ Naan kas. Ɗang baa a mbii ɗewur nyaa nǝ rip shiɓal kǝ wur ɗee ɗi kaa Naan sǝ kas.
PHI 2:7 Ɗangɓe Jesu wur sham kǝ káa fin, har wur leshin a káa kǝrem sǝ. Mo làa wur nɗǝǝn nan kaa koor gurum mo sǝ.
PHI 2:8 Ɗangɓe kaaɗi gyet wur ɗe nɗǝǝn nan kaa gurum sǝ, ɓe wur sham kǝ káa fin, ɗang wur shín shin mbǝ muut nkaa shiyeepyoom.
PHI 2:9 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe Naan ɗiyeep wur a ɗeɗes hakyeng, kǝ wur shìn sǝm wur a nJesu, ɗe nǝ met koor sǝm mo jir.
PHI 2:10 Mbǝkǝ nɗǝǝn sǝm Jesu, ɓe gurum mo jir nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, kǝ nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ, kǝ ndǝr nyil ɗesǝ, ɓe mon njì kurum ntoom Jesu.
PHI 2:11 Kǝzak, koo a pwoo ɗeɗangyi, ɓe nǝ nsat nǝ, Jesu Kristi wur a Daa, mbǝ ram Naan puun.
PHI 2:12 Mbǝmǝnǝ, wun ɗe wen wal nwun sǝ kaaɗi shidaar-shidaar ɓe wuu naa ncìn mbii ɗe dǝ wen nsat nee, wu cìn mo, ɓe an ashak kǝ wun sǝ. Ɓe wu sat a sekyeen kǝ cìn mbii ɗe gyet wen sat mo nwun ɗak. Jir kǝ ɗe baa an kuɗi ashak kǝ wun kas, ɓe wu shin ɗeɗes nNaan, kǝ wu kǝǝr wur nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo zak. Wu cìn ɗak shiɓal fuu mo, mbǝkǝ ɓam fuu nǝ ɗee ɗi a ɗegǝgam.
PHI 2:13 Mbǝɗe a Naan ɗewur kǝ cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo shidaar-shidaar. A wur kǝ le kǝ nwun cìn mbii ɗe mo ret wur nyit. Wur nshín ɓal nwun mbǝkǝ nwun cìn mbii ɗeret nǝ mo ɗi.
PHI 2:14 Wu cìn mbii mo jir, baa a shi pwoo nɗoom-nɗoom kǝ ɓeetshik kas,
PHI 2:15 mbǝkǝ taji gurum mo naa bish fuu kas. Mbǝkǝ nwun ɗee ɗe a ɗeɓang kaa jep Naan ɗegǝgam mo sǝ, ɗe moo tong nɗǝǝn nyil ɗebish sǝ, kǝ nɗǝǝn gurum ɗe mo gam kǝ shikbish sǝ. Wu ɗee a peeɓang mɓut mmo nɗǝǝn nyil ɗesǝ nǝ, kaa peeɓang mǝ zar ɗe mo aɗeng sǝ.
PHI 2:16 Kaaɗi wuu satpwoo ɗeret mǝ seen nǝ mo sǝ. Katɗang wu cìn aasǝ, ɓe ghan nkatpee mbǝ leshap shi wun parpuus mǝ Kristi. Mbǝɗi parpuus mǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ nɗee agaak nee, ɗaar kǝ ɗak ɗe dǝ ghan kǝn cìn nǝ, baa nǝ a buu kas.
PHI 2:17 Koo ɗe mon nfet ghan, kǝ mo ɗoo toom fen kaa mbiizuum ɗe shang sǝ mbǝ shinzeen fuu nɗǝǝn Naan, ɓe nǝ ret nwen nyit, kǝ nǝ shang nwen ashak kǝ wun jir.
PHI 2:18 Nǝ aasǝ zak, nǝ ret kǝ wun, wu cìn retnyit ashak kǝ an zak.
PHI 2:19 Katɗang Daa Jesu Kristi wur rǝɓet, ɓe wen kǝn lepan nǝ, an nlep Timoti shindǝm pee wun ɗe kǝkǝlak. Mbǝkǝ katɗang wur baaji, ɓe wen kǝlǝng pwoo ɗe nkaa tong fuu, kǝ nǝ caa an ɗi.
PHI 2:20 Baa nghan kǝ mee ngwe kaa wur sǝ kas, ɗewur kǝ shìn shin azeen-nzeen mbǝ sekyeen fuu.
PHI 2:21 Koor gurum nǝ mo ɗee a ncìn mbii ɗe mǝkáa fur mo ɓejee ɗak, baa mo kak sekyeen mǝ pwoo Jesu Kristi kas.
PHI 2:22 Wun shikáa fuu wuu man tong Timoti, mbǝɗe an kǝ wur, mun a kaa puun kǝ ɗyem nwur sǝ, ɗe muu cìn ɗak ashak mbǝ satpwoo ɗeret nǝ.
PHI 2:23 Mbǝmǝnǝ kǝn lepan, mbǝkǝ wen lep wur shindǝm pee wun ɗi kǝlak-kǝlak. kaɗang mman mbii ɗe nǝ kat an ɗi.
PHI 2:24 Wen shinzeen nɗǝǝn Daa nee, Baa nǝ ntong ɗes kas, ɓe wur nle kǝ nghan shikáa fen wen dǝm pee wun ɗi.
PHI 2:25 Wen kǝn pan nee, nǝ ret kǝ nghan lep Epafradaitus ɗyemnǝǝn fun, wur a shaarɗak fen, ɗewur kǝ cìn lek nǝ ashak kǝ an, shindǝm pee wun ɗi. Gyet a wun lep wur jì pee an ɗi, mbǝkǝ wur ɓam an ɗe nɗǝǝn ɗak mo.
PHI 2:26 Gyet wur kǝ fes lepan mbǝkǝ wur naa wun ɗe jir, ɗangɓe wur kǝ pǝtuup ɗewat mbǝɗe baa gyet wur nkoom kas kaaɗi gyet wu kǝlǝng sǝ.
PHI 2:27 Azeen-nzeen baa gyet wur nkoom kas, mbǝ gyet wur kus kǝ muut, ɗangɓe Naan wur naajeel wur. Baa Naan naa a jeel wur ɓejee kas, ɗangɓe kǝ wen jir, mbǝkǝ taji nkat pǝtuup ɗewat nkaa pǝtuup ɗewat kas.
PHI 2:28 Mbǝmǝnǝ, wen kǝn fes nlepan, mbǝkǝ nghan lep wur shindǝm pee wun ɗi. Mbǝkǝ nwun kat retnyit ɗe mbǝ baa naa wur shi yit fuu mo, mbǝkǝ pǝtuup mǝnǝ pan saam ɗe zak.
PHI 2:29 Mbǝmǝnǝ, wul a wur nɗǝǝn sǝm nDaa shi retnyit hakyeng. Wu shin ɗeɗes nkaan nen mǝnǝ mo.
PHI 2:30 Gyet ɗee ɗi a lee kǝ wur muut mbǝ ɗak Kristi. Gyet wur shin seen wur, mbǝkǝ wur ɓam an ɗe, nɗǝǝn ɗak ɗe baa wun shikáa fuu wu mak cìn nǝ kas.
PHI 3:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, mpee kyes nǝ, ɓe wu cìn retnyit nɗǝǝn Daa. Baa nǝ daampee nwen mbǝ baa ran pwoo ɗe gyet wen kǝn ten ran mo nwun kas, ɗangɓe nǝ a mbǝkǝ nǝ ɓam wun ɗe, kǝ wun tong ɗe ryang.
PHI 3:2 Wu tap kǝ nen ɗe moo cìn mbii ɗebish, kaa as mo sǝ. Nen ɗe mo sat nee, nǝ a tǝng kǝ gurum mo can-can.
PHI 3:3 A mun a ɗe mo kǝ can mun, baa a mo kas. Mbǝɗe muu seyil nNaan a nɗǝǝn Riin wur, kǝ muu cìn retnyit nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi, mbǝɗe seen fun mo a nɗǝǝn wur. Baa muu gángkáa fun a nkaa mbii ɗe gurum moo cìn, ɗe mo a mǝ nan kas.
PHI 3:4 Katɗang ɓe ɗe kǝn rǝɓet, ɓe ɗe an mmak gángkáa fen, nkaa mbii ɗe gurum moo cìn mǝ nan nǝ. Mbǝmǝnǝ, katɗang mee gurum kǝ pan nǝ, wur kǝ mbii gángkáa nɗǝǝn nan nǝ, ɓe an met ngwar mǝnǝ hakyeng nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe mo a mǝ nan nǝ mo.
PHI 3:5 Kaaɗi gyet mo làa an, ɓe aɓwoon ɗe kǝn wul teer pwookun, ɓe mo can ghan. Wen a ngu Yahudi, nɗǝǝn soon mǝ Benjamin. Wen a ngu Hiburu, làa nen Hiburu tyap. Katɗang a nɗǝǝn ar mǝ tap Wàar mǝ nen Yahudi mo, ɓe ghan kǝn tap Wàar nǝ a kaa nen Farisi mo sǝ.
PHI 3:6 Gyet kǝn shin jeel nendǝm nɗang Jesu mo. Nkwang mǝ tap Wàar nnen Yahudi mo, ɓe kǝn tap Wàar nǝ mon ndǝre-ndǝre jir.
PHI 3:7 Ɗangɓe nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe gyet wen kǝn kat mo, kaa lǝɓet sǝ, ɓe yaksǝ kǝn le mo ɗee a ɗebuu mbǝ sǝm nKristi.
PHI 3:8 Ii, azeen-nzeen, kǝn le mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗee a ɗebuu, mbǝɗe yaksǝ, wen kǝn man ɗeɗes mǝ wal Kristi Jesu Daa fen, ɗe nǝ met mbii mo jir. Mbǝ sǝm wur, ɓe ghan kǝn fwo mbii mǝnǝ mo jir. Yaksǝ, ɓe kǝn nnaa moo ɗee a kaa pee ɗe mo ɓeer a zungtung sǝ, mbǝɗe wen cii mo jir. kǝ nghan ɗee ɗi a mǝ Kristi,
PHI 3:9 kǝ nghan tong ɗe nɗǝǝn wur. Baa a mbǝ ɗeret fen kas, ɗe an mak kat nǝ mbǝ tap Wàar nǝ mo kas. Ɗang a mbǝ ɗeret ɗe mu kat nǝ mbǝ shinzeen ɗe mun kǝ nǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi. A ɗeret ɗe nǝ put a pǝ Naan ɗi, ɗe nǝ ɗar a nkaa shinzeen.
PHI 3:10 A mbii ɗe nkǝn fes nrǝɓet nɗesǝ, kǝ nghan man Kristi ɗi kǝ Iiko nyool a peemúut nwur. Kǝ nghan shwaa pak jeel wur nǝ ɗe zak, mbǝkǝ nghan ɗee ɗe kaa wur sǝ nɗǝǝn muut wur.
PHI 3:11 Mbǝkǝ koo ɗe a me cìn yii, ɓe wen kat yool a peemúut nǝ ɗi zak.
PHI 3:12 Baa kǝn ten kat mbii ɗe kǝn leyit nkaa mo kas. Koo ɗe baa kǝn ɗee a ɗe ndǝre-ndǝre kas, ɗangɓe kǝn gung mbǝkǝ mbii mǝnǝ mo ɗee ɗe a mǝnǝ, mbǝɗe Kristi Jesu wur le kǝ wen ɗee a mǝ wur.
PHI 3:13 Ɗyemnaa mo, baa an kǝn lesen nǝ, kǝn ten nkat mbii ɗesǝ nǝ mo kas, ɗangɓe mbii mǝndong ɗe kǝn cìn, wen kǝn mundǝr mbii ɗe mo kǝ ten ɗel. Yaksǝ, wen kǝn leyit fen ndǝre-ndǝre a nkaa mbii ɗe mo a tǝleng fen ɓejee ɗak.
PHI 3:14 Wen kǝn gung mbǝ dǝm wul a peekyes nɗak fen, mbǝkǝ nghan lap kwat ɗe mǝ kaa aɗeng ɗe ashak kǝ Jesu Kristi, nɗǝǝn petpee ɗe Naan wur pet an nǝ ɗi.
PHI 3:15 Wu yit kǝ pan ɗesǝ, nǝ ɗee nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fun mo. Mun nen ɗe mun kǝ seen, katɗang mee mbii ɗi, ɗe baa wu manshii nǝ kas, ɓe Naan wur nkámshii nǝ nwun.
PHI 3:16 Nǝ ret kǝ mun cin mbii mo nciit-ciit ɗe muu ten mu man nɗǝǝn Kristi.
PHI 3:17 Ɗyemnaa mo, wun jir wu mwaan nɗǝǝn shiimwaan fen, kǝzak, wu naa nen ɗe mwaan mo mo a ɗeret nɗǝǝn ar nǝ, kaaɗi mun muu ɗee a mbiikám pee wun ɗe sǝ.
PHI 3:18 Wen kǝn ten sat mbii ɗesǝ mo nwun, yit ɗes. Yaksǝ, ɓe nghan baa sat a nǝ ɗe nwun, jir shi yitmwaa. Gurum mo ɗǝɗes nɗǝǝn wun, ɗe mo a shaarlek mǝ shiyeepmúut mǝ Kristi.
PHI 3:19 Peekyes mǝ nen ɗesǝ nǝ mo, a muut mǝ aawus ɗe baa nii peekyes kas, mbǝɗe naan mmo nǝ a ɓut mo. Baa mo kǝ mee naashweep kas. Moo ɗiyeepkáa fur mo. Mo fes le pǝtuup fur mo a nkaa mbii ɗe mǝ nyil ɗesǝ mo.
PHI 3:20 Ɗang mun, ɓe tul fun nǝ a nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan. A pee ɗe muu naa Nguɓam fun Daa Jesu Kristi ɗewur ntong aɗeng sham ɗe.
PHI 3:21 Wur mbǝ ciir kǝ mǝse fun ɗebish sǝ mo, mbǝkǝ mo ɗee ɗe kaa mǝ ram wur sǝ. Shi iiko wur ɗesǝ, ɓe wur njì kǝ mbii mo jir, kǝ mo ɗee ɗe ntoom wur.
PHI 4:1 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo, ɗe wen wal nwun. Wen fes nrǝɓet wun, ɗe kǝn kat retnyit a shi wun, kǝ ghan kǝn cìn roop a shi wun zak. Wu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn Daa.
PHI 4:2 Wen kǝn satpwoo Yudiya, mo kǝ Sintiki nǝ. Nǝ ret kǝ mo tongryang kǝ shak, mbǝɗe mo jir vǝl mo a nɗǝǝn Kristi.
PHI 4:3 Wen ɗang pee waa ɗyemnǝǝn fen, ɗe muu cìn ɗak ashak, kussuk a ɓam mat ɗesǝ mo. Mbǝɗi mat ɗesǝ nǝ moo cìn ɗak ashak kǝ an nɗǝǝn satpwoo ɗeret nǝ, ashak kǝ Kelemen kǝ koor des ɗe muu cìn ɗak ashak kǝ mo jir. Nen ɗe sǝm mo a ɗerǝran nɗǝǝn ɓǝǝt haal mǝ seen.
PHI 4:4 Wu cìn retnyit nɗǝǝn Daa shidaar-shidaar. Wen baa nsat a nǝ ɗe nwun zak nǝ, wu cìn retnyit.
PHI 4:5 Wu yit kǝ gurum mo jir, mo naa gung fuu. Mbǝɗǝ baaji Daa nǝ wul kus.
PHI 4:6 Taji wu yit kǝ mee mbii daampee nwun kas, ɗangɓe nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir, ɓe wu sat mbii, ɗe wuu rǝɓet mon nNaan, nɗǝǝn ɗangnaan kǝ plang.
PHI 4:7 Tongriyang nNaan ɗe nǝ met man mo jir, nǝ tap kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo kǝ pan fuu mo, nɗǝǝn Kristi Jesu.
PHI 4:8 Ɗyemnaa mo, peekyes nǝ, ɓe jir mbii ɗe nǝ azeen, ɗe nǝ mak shin ɗeɗes, ɗe nǝ a ɗe ndǝre, ɗe nǝ a ɗeɓang, jir a ɗe nǝ a nwal, kǝ jir mbee ɗe nǝ rit naa, jir katɗang nii mee mbii ɗeret met jir ɗe, jir ɗe nǝ mee mbii ɗe nǝ ret plang ɗe, ɓe wu cìn pan nkaa mbii ɗesǝ mo jir.
PHI 4:9 Wu cin ɗak kǝ mbii ɗe gyet wuu ten wu kám mo, kǝ mbii ɗe gyet wuu ten wu lap mo, kǝ mbii ɗe gyet wuu ten wu naa mo, kǝ mbii ɗe gyet wuu ten wu kǝlǝng mo pee an ɗi. Naan ɗewur shin tongryang mmun, wur ntong ashak kǝ wun.
PHI 4:10 Wen kat retnyit nɗǝǝn Daa hakyeng, mbǝɗe gyet wuu ɗoom mundǝr nwen, ɗangɓe yaksǝ wuu pan ghan. Azeen-nzeen, gyet wuu pan an, ɗangɓe baa gyet wu kat a pee mbǝ ɓam an kas.
PHI 4:11 Baa nǝ, a mee mbii jee nwen kas, mbǝɗe gyet wen kǝn ten kám ar mǝ gung nɗǝǝn jir mbii ɗe ghan kǝ nǝ. Jir ɗe nǝ ɗes, kǝ jir ɗe nǝ a lee, ɓe wen kǝn tong a shi retnyit.
PHI 4:12 Wen man mbii ɗe an cin, katɗang baa ghan kǝ mee mbii kas, kǝzak, mman mbii ɗe ghan ncìn katɗang ghan kǝ mbii mo ɗes. nƊǝǝn mbii mo jir, ɓe ghan kǝn kám mbii ɗesǝsok ɗesǝ, mbǝkǝ nghan katpee ɗar ɗe ɓalɓal, jir a nɗǝǝn ghǝɓǝl kǝ an nɗǝǝn neen.
PHI 4:13 Wen mak cìn mbii mo jir, a nɗǝǝn ɓal ɗe Kristi wur shìn nwen shidaar-shidaar.
PHI 4:14 Wen plang wun, mbǝɗe dǝ wu ɓam an nɗǝǝn jeel fen.
PHI 4:15 Wun nen Filipi mo, wu man shikáa fuu nǝ, gyet nshee mǝ pwoo ɗeret nǝ, kaaɗi gyet an yool yit yil mMasidoniya, ɓe baa mee Ekǝlisya ɗe nǝ shínkáa war ashak kǝ an mbǝ shin zuum mo, kǝ lap zuum mo kas, ɗang a wun ɓejee ɗak.
PHI 4:16 ɗang kaaɗi gyet nghan nɗǝǝn nyil nTasoloni, ɓe wuu lep ɓam shindǝm nwen nkaashak-nkaashak, baa a yit mǝndong kǝ vǝl ɓejee kas.
PHI 4:17 Baa nǝ, a mbǝɗe an kǝn tang a mee zuum pee wun ɗi kas, ɗangɓe kǝn rǝɓet kǝ nwun wu kat lǝɓet ɗe nkaa kwat fuu mo.
PHI 4:18 Wuu ten wu kwat ghan kǝndǝng, mbǝɗe kǝn kat mbii ɗe kǝn rǝɓet nǝ, ɗang nǝ ɗes met mbii ɗe dǝ ghan kǝn rǝɓet nǝ. Mbǝɗe nghan kǝn la zuum ɗe wu lep shinji nwen nsar nEpafradaitus. Mbiizuum fuu ɗesǝ nǝ mo, moo toos shang shang a kaa zuum ɗe gurum moo shin nNaan sǝ. Mbiizuum ɗe Naan lap ɗe mo shang nyit nNaan hakyeng.
PHI 4:19 Kǝzak Naan fen wur shin jir mbii ɗe nǝ ret kǝ nwun kat ɗi nciit-nciit kǝ ɗeɗes mǝ long wur nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi.
PHI 4:20 Ɗeɗes nǝ ɗee a mǝ Naan puun fun mbǝ ngaa-ngaa, Nǝ aasǝ.
PHI 4:21 Wu tok kǝ nen Naan ɗe mo a mǝ Kristi Jesu jir. Ɗyemnaa ɗe mo ashak kǝ an, moo tok kǝ wun.
PHI 4:22 Nen Naan mo jir moo tok kǝ wun. Met jir, a nen Naan ɗe mon ntul mishkoom ɗeɗes Siza.
PHI 4:23 Ɗeret kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi nǝ tong ashak kǝ riin fuu mo jir. Nee aasǝ.
COL 1:1 Lepran ɗesǝ nǝ put a nsar mǝnǝ Pool ɗe Naan wu kǝ ten bǝlǝp nghan mbǝkǝ nghan tong ɗe a laalep nJesu Kristi, kǝ Timoti ɗyemnǝǝn fun nɗǝǝn Kristi.
COL 1:2 Dǝm pee nen Naan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nKolosi, pee ɗyemnǝǝn fun mo ɗe mo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak kǝ Jesu Kristi. Ɗeret kǝ Naan puun fun kǝ tongryang fin ɗee ashak kǝ wun jir.
COL 1:3 Muu chìn ɗangnaan nNaan mɓe wun shidaar-shidaar. Kǝzak, muu naa pǝlang Naan ɗe wu a puun kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi.
COL 1:4 Mbǝɗe mu kǝlǝng nǝ, shinzeen fuu nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi nii sekyeen, kǝzak nnǝ, wuu wal nen kǝ Naan mo jir.
COL 1:5 Mbǝɗe wuu le pǝtuup nkaa mbii ɗe Naan wu kǝ ten ɗak nǝ le nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, Wu kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mbii ɗesǝ mo a nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret ɗe nǝ azeen ɗe di wuu ten wu kǝlǝng nǝ.
COL 1:6 Pwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ nǝ, nǝn nkaa mwan dǝm shipee-shipee nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ. Nii shin ciir kǝ pǝtuup gurum mo, ɗangɓe nii le kǝ mo chìn ɗak ɗeret mo. Yaksǝ, gurum mo ɗes, mo nkaa shinzeen ɗikǝ-ɗikǝ. Nǝ aasǝ, ɓe nǝ kǝ dǝm wul mpee fuu, ɗangɓe nǝ nkaa ciir kǝ pǝtuup fuu mo, mbǝkǝ wun chìn ɗak ɗeret mo ɗe. Yaa mparpuus ɗe di wu shee kǝlǝng nǝ, ɓe yaksǝ wu manshii kǝ nǝ azeen-nzeen, kaaɗi Naan wur le ɗeret nkaa wun sǝ.
COL 1:7 Wu shee kǝlǝng pwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ, a mpwoo kǝ Abafaras, ɗe muu wal nwur, ɗang wur a shaarɗak fun. Wur cìn ɗak kǝ Jesu Kristi shi pǝtuup mǝndong nnaar fuu a koppee fun.
COL 1:8 A wur sat mmun pwoo nkaa nwal fuu nɗǝǝn Riin Ɗeɓang.
COL 1:9 Nǝ aasǝ, ɓe yool mparpuus ɗe di mu kǝlǝng pwoo mǝnǝ nkaa wun, ɓe muu ɗangnaan(leshap kǝ Naan) (leshap kǝ Naan) mbǝ wun shidaar-shidaar. Muu ɗang pǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ wur gam wun ɗe seen mǝ man ɗyen fen, man ɗe nǝ put a pee Riin wur jì ɗi.
COL 1:10 Man mǝnǝ le, kǝ mwaan fuu mo lapshak kǝ mǝ nen ɗe mo dǝm nɗang Jesu. Mwaan ɗe nǝ tong ɗyen nJesu. Katɗang wu mwaan a nɗǝǝn ɗyen Jesu, ɓe mǝse fuu nǝn nle kǝ wu chìn ɗak ɗeret mo, kǝ wu sat a nwurang nɗǝǝn man pwoo nkaa Naan ɗak.
COL 1:11 Muu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nǝ, Naan ɗewur ɓal met jir, wur nshínɓal nwun, mbǝkǝ wu ɗar ɗe ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir. Kǝzak, koo ɗe a me cìn yi, ɓe nwun sat a ngung ɗe ɗak, kǝ nwun kat retnyit ɗi zak.
COL 1:12 Wu pǝlang puun fun ɗewur aɗeng, wur ɗewur wang ar nǝ mmun, mbǝkǝ mu sekop fen ɗe ashak kǝ nen fin mo nɗǝǝn pee ɗeɓang.
COL 1:13 Wur put kǝ mun nɗǝǝn iiko mu peenkoo, ɗangɓe wu waa mang mun ɗel kǝ mun nɗǝǝn mulki kǝ Làa fin.
COL 1:14 A Làa fin, wu ang mun, ɗe nǝ kam nǝ a wur fwo shikbish fun mo mmun.
COL 1:15 Baa mee gwar kǝ cam naa Naan kas, amma gurum mo kǝ naa Jesu ɗe wu lapshak kǝ Naan. A wur kám tong kǝ Naan mmun agaak. Jesu wur a Làa Naan ɗenshee, ɗewur met mbii ɗe Naan wur le mo jir.
COL 1:16 A nɗǝǝn Jesu, ɓe Naan wur le mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ jir. Mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan kǝ ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ. Mbii ɗe gurum moo mak naa mo, kǝ mbii ɗe baa gurum moo mak naa mo kas. A nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes wur, ɓe Naan wur le mbii ɗe mo kǝ iiko nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan. Mbii ɗenan mo kǝ ɗeɗyeen mo nciit-nciit kǝ ɓal fur mo. A nɗǝǝn Jesu, ɓe Naan wur le mbii mo jir, kǝ mbii mo jir, a Jesu wu kǝ mo nsar, ɓe mo a mu wur jir zak.
COL 1:17 Pǝgyet ɗe yam-yam, ɓe Jesu wur ɗe, akuɗang Naan wur le mbii mo nɗǝǝn yil nǝ. Naan ɓàl mbii mo jir ashak a nɗǝǝn Jesu.
COL 1:18 nƊǝǝn nen Naan mo, ɓe Jesu a káa mo. Koor gurum nǝ mo a foshik wur. A Jesu a káa mǝ nen dǝm ndang Naan mo. A wur a ɗenshee, zak, a wur shee yool a peemúut. Mpee mbii ɗesǝ mo, ɓe a wur a ɗenshee nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir.
COL 1:19 Nǝ ret nNaan nyit, ɓe wur le kǝ ɗyen fen nǝ gam, kǝ nǝ tong nɗǝǝn Jesu.
COL 1:20 Nǝ ret Naan nyit zak, mbǝkǝ wur waaji kǝ mbii mo jir pǝ shin ɗi nɗǝǝn Jesu. A nɗǝǝn toom ɗe Làa kǝ Naan wur ɓeer nkaa shiyeepyoom, ɗangɓe Naan wur rǝɓet waa baaji kǝ mbii mo jir, pǝ shin ɗi. Mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, kǝ ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan.
COL 1:21 Di mmee nnaar, ɓe wuu tong a jong-jong kǝ Naan, kǝ di wun a shaarlek Naan, mbǝ mbii ɗebish, ɗe di wuu cìn mo, kǝ pan fuu ɗebish mo.
COL 1:22 Amma yaksǝ, mbǝ muut Làa Naan, ɗe mo làa wur nɗǝǝn nan, ɓe Naan le kǝ wu ɗee a shaar fin mo, mbǝkǝ pǝtuup fuu mo ɗee ɗi a ɗeɓang, kǝ mbǝkǝ wur jì kǝ wun ɗe ntoom Naan, ɗewur a ɗeɓang.
COL 1:23 A mbii ɗe Jesu cìn nwun mmǝnǝ, katɗang wu sekyeen kǝ shinzeen nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ. Kǝzak, katɗang wu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn mbii ɗesǝ mo. Wu sat a nlepǝtunp, nkaa mbii ɗe wu kǝlǝng pwoo nkaa mo nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗeret nǝ. A pwoo nkaa pwoo ɗeret, ɗe moo ten sat nǝ nkòo a weyi, nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ. Wen Pool, ɗak fen nǝ a mbǝkǝ nghan sat ɗe ngurum mo, pwoo nkaa pwoo ɗeret ɗesǝ nǝ.
COL 1:24 Kaaɗe wen nkaa shwaajeel mbǝ sǝm fuu, ɓe nghan kǝ retnyit mputuup. Kaaɗe gyet Daa Jesu shwaajeel sǝ, ɓe wen zak, kǝn shwaajeel nɗǝǝn nan mbǝ sǝm kǝ nen fin mo ɗe mo a fwooshin fin. Wen shwaajeel nǝ a mbǝkǝ wen sǝǝt nkyes koor ɗak wur nǝ ɗi.
COL 1:25 A Naan wur bǝlǝp nghan, mbǝkǝ nghan ɗee ɗi a kǝrem mǝ nen kǝ Jesu mo, ɓe wu le ɗak ɗesǝ nǝ nsar fen mbǝ sǝm fuu. Ɗak ɗe wu le nsar fen nǝ, a mbǝkǝ nghan satpwoo fen ɗeret ɗe ngurum mo kǝdǝng.
COL 1:26 Pwoo ɗe wen kǝn sat ngurum mo, ɓe gyet yam, ɓe nǝ a ɗe sǝsok. Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe baa gyet gurum mo manshii nǝ kas, amma yaksǝ Naan woo mmun agaak nen fin mo.
COL 1:27 Nǝ ret nNaan nyit, ɓe wu le, kǝ nen fin mo manpwoo ɗejurum ɗesǝ, ɗe nǝ a mbii aapwoo zam. Nii koop nǝ hakyeng, mbǝ gurum mo jir, koo a nɗǝǝn yil ɗeɗangyi. Pwoo ɗewur woo nǝ mmun, a nǝ, Jesu Kristi wur tong nɗǝǝn wun. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu lepǝtuup, mbǝ parpuus ɗe wun ntong ashak kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ram fen.
COL 1:28 A mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe muu satpwoo ngurum mo jir nkaa Jesu Kristi. Muu satpwoo nkòo a weyi, kǝ wur tap, kǝzak, muu kám seen ngurum mo nkaa mbii ɗesǝ nǝ mo, a mbǝkǝ koo a weyi, ɓe wur ɗee ɗe kǝ seen nɗǝǝn Kristi.
COL 1:29 A mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wen kǝn cìn ɗak shiɓal ɗe Jesu wu shin nghan, ɗang wen kǝn gung mbǝkǝ nghan kyes ɗak ɗesǝ nǝ ɗi.
COL 2:1 Ɗyen nghan, kǝ wun man ɗak ɗe nghan kǝn gung mɓe cìn nǝ mbǝ sǝm fuu, kǝ mɓe nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil Lodisiya, kǝ jir nen ɗe baa mo kǝ cam naa an kas.
COL 2:2 Wen nkaa cìn ɗak ɗesǝ nǝ, a mbǝkǝ mo katɓal ɗe mputuup fur mo, mbǝkǝ mo wal ɗe nshak, mɓekǝ mo ɗee ɗe a ɗemǝndong. Ɗyeen nghan kǝ mo man jurum kǝ man nkaa Jesu hakyeng nǝ kyeet, mbǝkǝ mo manshii kǝ mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗe jir. Ɗesǝ nǝ njì kǝ ɗeret nkaa mo hakyeng. Mbii ɗejurum nǝ, a Kristi shikáa fen.
COL 2:3 Mo sok long mǝ seen kǝ man mo jir, a nɗǝǝn Jesu.
COL 2:4 Wen kǝn sat mbii ɗesǝ mo nwun, a mbǝkǝ taji mee gurum ngwom wun shi liispwoo ɗe nǝ shangkǝlǝng kas.
COL 2:5 Koo ɗang ɗe baa wen ashak kǝ wun nɗǝǝn nan kas, ɓe nghan ɗe ashak kǝ wun nɗǝǝn riin. Nǝ shang nghan zam, kaaɗe wen nnǝ kǝlǝng nǝ, wuu cìn mbii mo a nciit-nciit nɗǝǝn ar ɗeret, kǝzak, wuu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn Kristi.
COL 2:6 Kaaɗe, wu mang Jesu Kristi kaa Daa fuu sǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu mwaan-mwaan ɗe nǝ ret kǝ nen ɗe mo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak kǝ Jesu, moo cìn. Wu tong nɗǝǝn wur.
COL 2:7 Wu sham seen fu mo nɗer-nɗer nɗǝǝn nwur, wu ɗyik seen fu mo kaa wur, kǝ wun ɗeng kǝ ɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen nwur, kaaɗe mǝ kám nwun sǝ. Kǝzak, wu pǝlang wu shidaar-shidaar mbǝ mbii mo jir.
COL 2:8 Wu tap, taji mee gurum ngwom wun shiman mǝ yil ɗesǝ, mbǝkǝ wu taa wu mer ɗe a ar ɗeret nǝ kas. Kyaan kǝ man ɗe nǝ put a nɗǝǝn wàar mǝ gurum mo, kǝ nɗǝǝn riin ɗebish mǝ yil ɗesǝ, baa nii put a pee Kristi ɗi kas.
COL 2:9 A nɗǝǝn Jesu, ɓe muu naa gam kǝ ɗyeen Naan, kǝ tong nɗǝǝn nan nǝ zak.
COL 2:10 Mo shin seen nwun, a mbǝɗi wuu ɓalkaa ashak kǝ Jesu. A wur a káa kǝ mulki kǝ mɓal mo jir.
COL 2:11 A nɗǝǝn wur, ɓe mo can wun, baa a can ɗe moo cìn shi sar nɗǝǝn nan kas, ɗangɓe a can ɗe Jesu Kristi wur cìn nwun ɗe nǝ put kǝ wun nɗǝǝn shikbish.
COL 2:12 Kaaɗe gyet mo cìn baptisma nwun, mɓe mo wum wun ashak kǝ Kristi, ɗangɓe mo waa yool kǝ wun ashak kǝ wur a peemúut.
COL 2:13 Gyet yam ɓe wun a ɗemumuut mɓe shikbish fuu mo, kǝ baa gyet wun a nen Naan mo kas ɗe baa moo mee waar kas. Ɗangɓe Naan shin seen nwun ashak kǝ Kristi, kǝzak, Naan kǝ fwo shikbish fun mo jir.
COL 2:14 Gyet yam ɓe mun a ɗemumurep mo nder wàar mǝ Naan, mbǝɗi baa gyet muu cìn mbii ɗe wàar kǝ Naan nǝ sat kas. Dangɓe yaksǝ, Naan wur mang shikbish mǝnǝ mo baa kǝnǝ aku nkaa káa fun mo, kǝ wu fwo ɗe mmun jir zak. Mbǝɗe gyet mo pwas Jesu Kristi nkaa shiyeepyoom, a mɓe shikbish fun ɗesǝ nǝ mo.
COL 2:15 Kaaɗe gyet Jesu Kristi muut nkaa shiyeepyoom, ɓe wur se koorong nkaa riin ɗebish mo kǝ iiko mo, wur kám ngurum mo a agaak nǝ, wur ɓal met mmo jir.
COL 2:16 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe taji wu yit kǝ mee gurum lewàar nwun nkaa mbii ɗe wuu se, kǝ shwaa kas, koo nkaa puus ɗeɓang mo, koo nkaa mbii ɗe wuu cìn mo, mɓe tar ɗepwoo, koo nkaa puus Nookɗi.
COL 2:17 Mbii ɗesǝ mo ɗee a mǝ riin, ɗe gyet moo kám ngurum mo mbii ɗe mo pǝ jì akyeen. Mbii ɗe gyet moo ɗee a mǝ riin ɗesǝ nǝ, moo gam, a Kristi shikáa fin.
COL 2:18 Mbǝmǝnǝ, taji wu yit kǝ nen ɗe mo lesut a kaa nenɗenan mo sǝ, mo tokɗyeel ɗebish nwun kas. Nen ɗe mo sat nǝ, Naan kǝ woo mbii mo nwuɗun zuum. Mo sat nǝ, wu sham kǝ káa fuu mo mǝ ɗung, kǝzak, nnǝ wu seyil nenlep Naan mo. Nen mǝnǝ, moo roop, koo ɗe baa mo a mee mbii kas. Pan fur mo a mǝ yil ɗesǝ.
COL 2:19 Baa moo rǝɓet ɓalkaa fur ashak kǝ Kristi ɗe wu a káa mǝ nen mwaan ndang Naan nǝ mo kas. Ɗe a wur shínɓal mmo, ɗang a wur shin mbiise mmo zak. Jir nen ɗe moo ɓalkaa fur mo ashak kǝ Jesu, ɓe wur kǝ shínɓal mmo, mbǝkǝ mo jì ɗe ashak zak. Kǝ mbǝkǝ, mo wurang ɗe a nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Kristi, kaaɗi Naan wur rǝɓet sǝ. Ɓeep mǝ fwoshik fun moo kaat shishak, mbǝɗe mo kǝ peeɓal mo, kǝ paar mo. Nǝ a kaaɗi Kristi wu ɓàl nen mwaan nɗang wur mo, ɗe mo a shin fin sǝ.
COL 2:20 Kaaɗe wu murap ashak kǝ Kristi, ɓe baa riin ɗe mǝ yil ɗesǝ mon nkat ɓal nkaa wun kas. Dangɓe a me le ɗang wuu sekyeen kǝ mwaan kaa kor gurum ɗe mǝ yil ɗesǝ mo yi? A me le ɗangɓe wu cínkáa fuu nder kǝ wàar ɗe gurum sat nee, wu cìn yi
COL 2:21 Kaaɗe moo sat nwun nǝ, taji wu tung mbii ɗesǝ shi sar kas. Taji wu se mbii ɗesǝ kas, kǝzak, taji wu tung mbii ɗesǝ shi sar kas.
COL 2:22 Kyaan kǝ wàar ɗesǝ mo, mo a kám mǝ gurum. Ɗe katɗang mo gung cìn ɗak kǝ mo, ɓe mo ɗee a ɗebuu.
COL 2:23 Wàar kaa ɗesǝ mo sǝ, mo kǝ lapshak kaa mo aa mee koop mǝ seen sǝ. Mɓeɗi wàar nǝ mo letǝng ngurum mo, kǝ mo seyil ɗe nɗǝǝn ar ɗeret, kǝ mo sham kǝ káa fur mo, mǝ ɗung zak, kǝ moo shínjeel ɗe nsut fur mo, ɗangɓe azeen-nzeen, baa moo mee koop nǝ kas, mbǝɗe baa moo mee ɓal ɗe mon mɓam gurum, mbǝkǝ wu tap ɗe nǝ coor mǝ nan nǝ kas.
COL 3:1 Mbǝɗe mo kǝ yool kǝ wun nɗǝǝn seen ashak kǝ Kristi, mpeemǝnǝ, ɓe wu le pǝtuup fuu mo nkaa mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, a peeɗi Kristi wur tong ɗe, nsarse kǝ Naan.
COL 3:2 Wu lepan fuu mo a nkaa mbii ɗe mo aɗeng. Taji wu lepan fuu mo nkaa mbii ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ kas.
COL 3:3 Mɓeɗi wuu murep, ɗang ɓe seen fuu ɗepwoo nǝ mo a sǝsok pee Kristi ɗe nɗǝǝn Naan.
COL 3:4 Katɗang Kristi ɗewur a seen fuu, wur jì put, ɓe wuwun zak, wun mput ashak kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ɗehai fin.
COL 3:5 Wu twe mbii ɗe mo a mǝ yil ɗesǝ, ɗe moo cin ɗak nɗǝǝn seen fuu mo jir. Mbii kaa cìn ngaa mo sǝ, kǝ mwaan ɗebish mo, kǝ coor mbii mǝ nan mo, kǝ rǝɓet mbii ɗebish mo kǝ tǝlǝk, ɗe nǝ a see nyil mee naan ɗeci.
COL 3:6 A mbǝ mbii ɗebish kaa ɗesǝ mo sǝ, ɓe Naan wur woo tuup fin nkaa nenyil ɗe mo cii kǝlǝng ɗoo fin.
COL 3:7 Gyet wun, shikáa fuu, wuu cìn mbii ɗesǝ mo, har gyet wuu mwaan a nɗǝǝn mo.
COL 3:8 Ɗangɓe yaksǝ, kaaɗi wun kǝ seen ɗepwoo sǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu shwat sar fuu mo aku, nɗǝǝn mbii ɗebish ɗesǝ nǝ mo jir. Mbii mo kaa langtuup, pan ɗebish nkaa shak, pwoo ɗebuu nkaa shak, kǝ jir pwoo ɗe baa mo kǝ mee koop nǝ kas. Taji wu baa wu cìn mo ɗe zak kas koo dǝɓen.
COL 3:9 Taji wu cìn ɗung nshak kas, mbǝɗe wuu ten wu yit shiimwaan fuu ɗe gyet yam nǝ mo ɗi.
COL 3:10 Mbǝmǝnǝ wu shee shiimwaan ɗepwoo ɗe Naan wu le nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, ɗe nǝ nɗak shiimwaan fuu mo, kǝ wu ɗee ɗe kaa wu sǝ, mbǝkǝ wu man wu ɗikǝ.
COL 3:11 Yaksǝ, baa mee shwatnyit ɗe nnaar kǝ ngu Heleni kǝ ngu Yahudi kas, koo nnaar kǝ gwar ɗe moo can wu kǝ gwar ɗe nsuluk kas. Nnaar kǝ nenseen mo, kǝ nenyil ɗe baa moo seen kas, nnaar kǝ mǝzep mo, kǝ nenyil mo, nnaar kǝ kǝrem mo, kǝ jeplu mo. Yaksǝ ɓe gurum mo ɗee a nciit-nciit, nɗǝǝn Kristi, mbǝɗe wu met mbii mo jir.
COL 3:12 Taji wu muunshik nǝ, Naan wal nwun zam, har wur bǝlǝp wun, mbǝkǝ wu ɗee ɗe a nenyil fin mo. Nǝ a tǝng kǝ shiimwaan fuu mo ret, kaa jep Naan mo sǝ. Wu naajeel mǝ shak. Wu cìn mbii ɗeret nshak. Wu sham kǝ kaa fuu mo. Wu cìn mbii mo nɗǝǝn ɗyeen, kǝzak, wu gung nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir.
COL 3:13 Taji wu kǝlak kǝ langtuup kǝ shak kas. Kat mee gurum cìn shikbish ngǝnǝǝn, ɓe gwar ɗe mo cìn shikbish nǝ nwur, wu fwo ɗe ngucìn shikbish nǝ. Daa Naan kǝ fwo shikbish fuu mo, mpeemǝnǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wuwun, wu fwo ɗi nshak zak.
COL 3:14 Mbii ɗe nii koop nǝ met jir, wu wal, mbǝɗe nwal nǝ kǝ ɓàl gurum mo ashak nɗǝǝn tong ɗe mbii mo a ɗekǝgam jir.
COL 3:15 Wu yit kǝ tongryang mǝ Kristi, nǝ se mishkoom nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo. A mpeemǝnǝ ɓe Naan wu pǝrep wun, mbǝkǝ wu tong nɗǝǝn tongryang mǝnǝ. Wu pǝlang Naan shidaar-shidaar.
COL 3:16 Wu yit kǝ pwoo kǝ Kristi nǝ tong nɗǝǝn wun hakyeng, kaaɗi wu cìn kám, kǝ ɓamshak nɗǝǝn seen ɗe Naan wu cìn nwun sǝ. Wu kwoop Naan shi kook mo, kǝ kook ɗe mo a mǝ Riin, ɗe mo put nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu, ɗe Riin kǝ Naan wu cìn wun. Kaaɗe wuu koop Naan shi kook mo sǝ, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wu pǝlang wu nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo.
COL 3:17 nƊǝǝn mbii ɗe wuu cìn mo jir, koo ɗe a nɗǝǝn ɗak, ɓe wu cìn mo jir a nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa fun Jesu. Wu pǝlang Naan puun nɗǝǝn sǝm fin.
COL 3:18 Wun mat mo, wu shin ɗeɗes mish fuu mo, kaaɗe nǝ ret kǝ nendǝm ɗangnaan mo cìn sǝ.
COL 3:19 Wun mish mo, wu nwal mmat fuu mo. Taji wu tong kǝ mo a shi lek kas.
COL 3:20 Wun jep mo, wu kǝlǝng pwoo puun fuu mo, mbǝɗe mǝnǝ ret nNaan nyit zam.
COL 3:21 Wun puun mo, taji wu le kǝ jep mo langtuup kas, mbǝɗe kat wu le kǝ mo langtuup, ɓe nǝ nroop kwak mmo.
COL 3:22 Wun kǝrem mo, wu cìn mbii ɗe nenlu fuu mo sat nnǝ wu cìn. Taji wu cìn mbii mo a mbǝɗe moo naa wun kas, mbǝkǝ wu kat ɗeret ɗe pee mo ɓejee kas, ɗangɓe wu cìn mbii mo a shi pǝtuup ɗemǝndong, kǝ shin ɗeɗes nNaan.
COL 3:23 Koo ɗang ɗe ɗak fuu nǝ a meyii, ɓe wu cìn nǝ shi pǝtuup mǝndong, kaaɗe wuu cìn a nNaan sǝ, baa a mɓe gurum mo kas.
COL 3:24 A Daa Jesu Kristi wu a Daa fuu. Wun nlap kwat fuu mo a pǝ wu ɗe. Kwat ɗe wu nshin nwun nǝ, a sekop ɗe wu ɗak nǝ le mɓe nenyil fin mo nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, mbǝɗe ɗak ɗe wuu cìn nǝ, ɓe wuu seyil nDaa Jesu Kristi.
COL 3:25 Ngwar ɗe wu cìn mbii ɗebish, ɓe Daa wu nkwat gwar mǝnǝ a shi mbii ɗebish, nciit-nciit kǝ mbii ɗebish ɗe gwar mǝnǝ cìn. Baa mee shwatyit ɗe kas koo dǝɓen.
COL 4:1 Wun nen ɗe wun kǝ kǝrem mo, wu fwang mo nɗǝǝn ar ɗeret, nɗǝǝn zeen zak, mbǝɗe wu man nǝ, wun ɗe kǝ mee gwar ɗeɗes zak, nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, ɗewur kǝ fwang wun.
COL 4:2 Wu ɗangnaan(leshap kǝ Naan) shidaar-shidaar. Wu tong shi gongpee, kǝzak, wu pǝlang Naan mɓe mbii mo jir.
COL 4:3 Wu ɗangnaan(leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe mun zak, mbǝkǝ Naan wang ar ɗǝ mmun, kǝ mu satpwoo fin ɗe ngurum mo. Kǝ mbǝkǝ mu yakshii nǝ ɗe ngurum mo mbii ɗe jurum, ɗe Naan wu woo mmun nkaa Jesu Kristi. A mɓe pwoo ɗeret nǝ, ɗangɓe nghan a shishoot nɗǝǝn lushoot.
COL 4:4 Wu ɗang pǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ nghan satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗe ngurum mo agaak, kǝ mo manshii nǝ ɗi, kaaɗe nǝ ret kǝn ghan sat sǝ.
COL 4:5 Wu mwaan shi seen, pǝ nenyil ɗe baa mo a nendǝm ndang Naan mo kas. Wu cìn ɗak kǝ koo a pee ɗeɗangyi ɗe Naan shin wun!
COL 4:6 Wu yit kǝ liispwoo fuu mo shang kǝlǝng ngurum mo, kaa mbii ɗǝ mo tap le kǝǝn ɗike sǝ, mbǝkǝ wu man mbii ɗe wun nlap ɗe ngurum mo katɗang mo tal mee mbii pǝ wun.
COL 4:7 Tikikus satpwoo nwun, nkaa mbii ɗǝ an kǝn cìn mo jir. Wur a ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗe muu wal wur nɗǝǝn Kristi. Wur kǝ cìn ɗak kǝ nendǝm ndang Naan mo, a shi pǝtuup mǝndong. Wen kǝ wu, mun a kǝrem kǝ Daa Jesu nɗǝǝn ɗak fin.
COL 4:8 Wen kǝn lep wur dǝm pee wun ɗi, a mbǝkǝ wur sat ɗe nwun mbii ɗe muu cìn mo jir, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wu caa wun ɗi.
COL 4:9 Unisimus ɗewur a nguyil fuu, wur ndǝm ashak kǝ Tikikus. Mon nsat nwun mbii mo jir, nkaa an. Unisimus wu a ɗyemnǝǝn fun, ɗe muu wal nwur. Wur cìn ɗak kǝ nen dǝm ndang Naan mo a shi pǝtuup mǝndong.
COL 4:10 Aristaakus ɗewur a shishoot ashak kǝ an, wur kǝ tok kǝ wun jir. Maak kǝn kǝ Barnabas, wur kǝ tok kǝ wun zak. Wen kǝn ten ran pwoo nwun nkaa wur zak. Katɗang wur dǝm pǝ wun ɗe, ɓe wu lap wu shi pǝtuup mǝndong rǝret.
COL 4:11 Joshuwa ɗe moo pet wur a Jastus, wur tok kǝ wun. Das ɗekun sǝ mo, moo ɓam nghan zam. A mo a nen Yahudi ɗe moo cìn ɗak ashak kǝ nghan mpeesǝ. Muu sat ngurum mo nǝ, Naan wu a mishkoom.
COL 4:12 Abafaras ɗewur a nɗǝǝn wun, wur tok kǝ wun. Abafaras wu a kǝrem kǝ Jesu Kristi. Wur ɗangnaan(leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe wun shidaar-shidaar. Wur ɗang pǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ wu ɗar ɗe ɓalɓal, nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Naan, mbǝkǝ wu man mbii ɗe moo ret ɗe nNaan nyit. Kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wu kǝlǝng ɗoo fin ɗe, nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir.
COL 4:13 Wen shikáa fen, nghan kǝn naa, kaaɗe wur cìn ɗak ɓalɓal mɓe sǝm fuu wun ɗe wun nɗǝǝn Kolosi, kǝ ɓe nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Lodisiya kǝ Hirapolis.
COL 4:14 Luka ɗewur a nguyen, ɗe muu wal nwur zam, kǝ Dimas moo tok kǝ wun.
COL 4:15 Wu tok kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Lodisiya, kǝ Nimfas, kǝ nendǝm ndang Naan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn tul nwur.
COL 4:16 Aɓwoon ɗe mo kǝ tang lepran ɗesǝ nwun, ɓe wu le kǝ mee gurum tang nǝ nɗǝǝn nendǝm ndang Naan ɗe mon nLodisiya zak. Wu tang lepran, ɗe nendǝm ndang Naan ɗǝ mon nyil nLodisiya mon nlep shiin ji nwun zak.
COL 4:17 Wu sat Arkipus nǝnee, <<Wur kyes ɗak ɗe di Daa Jesu Kristi Shìn nwur, mbǝkǝ wur cìn ɗe sǝ.>>
COL 4:18 A an Pool ran lepran ɗesǝ nwun shi sar fen. Taji wu muunshik nǝ, an a shishoot nɗǝǝn lushoot kas. Ɗeret Naan tong ashak kǝ wun jir. nǝ aasǝ.
1TH 1:1 Lepran ɗesǝ nǝ put a nsar Pool kǝ Silas kǝ Timoti shin dǝm pǝ nenɗǝm ndang Naan ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nTasoloni, ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn Naan puun kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi. Naan cin ɗeret nwun kǝ tongryang zak.
1TH 1:2 Koo pǝrangyi, ɓe muu pǝlang Naan mɓe wun jir, kǝzak, muu yee wun jir nɗǝǝn leshap kǝ Naan fun mo shidaar-shidaar.
1TH 1:3 Muu yee wun mɓe Naan fun, ɗewur aɗeng, kaaɗe wu kám cinzeen fuu nǝ nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe wuu cìn mo. Kǝ kaaɗe wal fuu nii le kǝ wu cìn ɗak shiɓal, kǝ kaaɗe canciin fuu nkaa Jesu Kristi nǝ ɗar ɓalɓal sǝ.
1TH 1:4 Ɗyemnaa mo, mu man nee, Naan wur wal nwun, ɗang wur kǝ ten bǝlǝp wun, kǝ wu ɗee a nen fin mo zak.
1TH 1:5 Mbǝɗe baa gyet mu satpwoo ɗeret nǝ nwun a shi lepwoo fun ɓejee kas, amma a nɗǝǝn iiko mǝ Riin Ɗeɓang. Kǝ mun mu cinzeen nee, mbii ɗǝ mǝ sat nǝ azeen. Wu man tong fun, kaaɗe gyet mun ɗe ashak kǝ wun. Muu cìn mbii mo jir a mɓe fuu.
1TH 1:6 Gyet wun, wuu yaa mwaan nɗǝǝn shiimwaan fun, kǝ nɗǝǝn shiimwaan kǝ Daa fun, koo ɗe wuu shwaajeel, amma nǝ a mbǝɗe wun kǝ lappwoo ɗeret nǝ shi retnyit ɗe Riin Ɗeɓang shin nwun.
1TH 1:7 Nǝ aasǝ ɓe, wu ɗee a mbii kám nkoor nenshínzeen nJesu Kristi ɗe mo nɗǝǝn nyil mMasidoniya kǝ Akaya.
1TH 1:8 A mbǝ wun ɗangɓe nenyil ɗe mo kus, kǝ ɗejong mo, mo kǝlǝng pwoo Daa. Baa a mMasidoniya kǝ Akaya ɓejee kas, amma shinzeen fuu nɗǝǝn Naan nǝ dǝm wul koo pee ɗeɗangyi. Mbǝmǝnǝ, baa mun kǝ mee mbii mbǝ sat kas.
1TH 1:9 Gurum mo, koo a nnǝyi, ɓe moo sat a wun, kaaɗe gyet wu lap mun shi pǝtuup mǝndong sǝ, kǝ kaaɗe gyet wu yit kùm fuu mo, mbǝkǝ wu seyil ɗi nNaan ɗewur kǝ seen kǝ wur azeen,
1TH 1:10 kǝ wuu tong shi gongpee mbǝ waaji kǝ Làa fin nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan, shii kǝ mǝnǝ a Làa nwur Jesu Kristi ɗe Naan wu yool kǝ wur a peemúut, kǝ wur ɓam mun nɗǝǝn tuup Naan ɗe nǝn a ar jì zak.
1TH 2:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, wun wu man shikáa fuu nee, jì fun pee wun ɗe baa nǝ a buu kas.
1TH 2:2 Wu man kaaɗe mun mu ten mu shwaajee kǝ fǝlǝp nɗǝǝn yil nFilipi, akuɗang muu jì pee wun ɗe nTasolonǝ. Koo ɗe gyet gurum mo ɗes mmo cii mun, ɗangɓe Naan fun wur shínɓal mmun mputuup, mbǝkǝ mǝ satpwoo wur ɗeret nǝ ɗe nwun.
1TH 2:3 Pwoo ɗe mu sat nwun nǝ, baa nǝ a ɗung koo pan ɗebish kas. Baa gyet mǝ sat nǝ, a mbǝkǝ mǝ gwam mee gurum ɗe kas.
1TH 2:4 Amma mbǝɗe Naan wur kǝ ten bǝlǝp mun, kǝ wur kǝ ten le pwoo nwur nǝ nɗǝǝn sar wur. Muu cìn kǝ mǝ tong ɗyeen ɗǝ a nNaan, ɗewur man pǝtuup fun mo jir. Baa muu cìn mbǝkǝ mutong ɗyeen ɗe a ngurum kas.
1TH 2:5 Wu man nǝ, baa muu kam jì kǝ mee pwoo ɗeshang mmee gurum shi lǝpwoo fun mo kas, mbǝkǝ mǝ gwam wun, kǝ mǝ kat shool ɗe pee wun kas. Naan wu man nǝ aasǝ.
1TH 2:6 Baa muu cam tang a ɗeɗes pee gurum mo ɗe kas, koo pǝ wun, koo pee nenɗeci mo. Koo ɗi mun kǝ pee mɓe cìn ɗak kǝ iiko fun kaa nenlep Kristi mo sǝ.
1TH 2:7 Dangɓe jir kǝsǝ, ɓe gyet muu fwang wun, a kaaɗe nǝǝn kyee war fwang jep war mo sǝ.
1TH 2:8 Mbǝɗe mǝ wal nwun zam, har gyet mu rǝɓet mbǝkǝ mǝ shin seen fun mo mɓe wun, baa a mɓe pwoo ɗeret Naan ɗe gyet mǝ sat nwun ɓejee kas.
1TH 2:9 Ɗyemnaa mo, wu yee nɗak ɗe gyet mun mu cìn shiɓal pee wun ɗi. Gyet mun mu cìn ɗak mpar kǝ puus, mbǝkǝ taji mu lejeel nwun kas, nnaar ɗe gyet mun nkaa satpwoo ɗeret mǝ Naan nǝ nwun.
1TH 2:10 Wun a langtǝng fun, kǝ Naan zak, Gyet shiimwaan fun mo mbǝ wun ɗi, wun ɗe wu shinzeen nǝ a ɗeɓang, ɗeret ɗang nii mee luk kas.
1TH 2:11 Wu man nee, mu tap wun a kaaɗe puun kǝ tap jep nwur mo sǝ.
1TH 2:12 Muu caa wun, muu ɓam wun zak, kǝzak, mun kǝ sat nǝ yit ɗes nǝ, nǝ ret kǝ wun mwaan a mwaan ɗe nǝ ret nNaan nyit. Naan ɗewur pǝrep wun, mbǝkǝ wu ɗel ɗe nɗǝǝn mulki nwur, kǝ mǝ tong ɗe ashak kǝ wur nɗǝǝn ram fin.
1TH 2:13 Mee mbii ɗe nii le, kǝ mu pǝlang Naan shidaar-shidaar zak, gyet mǝ shee satpwoo Naan nǝ nwun, ɓe kaaɗe wu kǝleng, ɓe wu lap nǝ, baa a kaa pwoo gurum sǝ kas, amma wu lap nǝ a kaa pwoo Naan sǝ ɗang nǝ a pwoo nǝ azeen, ɗe nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, wun nen ɗe wu cinzeen.
1TH 2:14 Ɗyemnaa fun mo, wu mwaan nɗǝǝn shiimwaan nenɗǝm ndang Naan ɗe mo a mǝ Kristi Jesu, ɗe mo nɗǝǝn yil nJudiya. Wuu nshwaajeel nsar nenyil fuu mo, kaaɗe gyet mu shwaajeel nsar nen Yahudi mo sǝ.
1TH 2:15 Gyet a nen Yahudi nǝ mo tu Daa Jesu, kǝ mo twe nensatpwoo Naan mo. Mo ceen mun zak. Baa mbii ɗe mo cìn nǝ ret nNaan nyit kas koo lee. Kǝzak, mo a shaarlek gurum mo jir.
1TH 2:16 Mbǝɗe moo yaappee, mbǝkǝ mo cíi satpwoo ɗeret nǝ ɗe mmun, mɓe nen ɗe baa mo a nen Yahudi mo kas, mbǝkǝ taji mo kat seen ɗe zak. A nɗǝǝn ar ɗesi ɓe, mo gam shi ɓutbish fur ɗe moo naa ncìn nǝ, amma yaksǝ tuup Naan nii taa nkaa mo jir.
1TH 2:17 Ɗyemnaa mo, kaaɗe gyet mu ɓàkshak kǝ wun, mɓe rep pee lee, yaksǝ nǝ daampee mmun, koo ɗe a yit fun mo ɓàkshak ɗak, ɓe pǝtuup fun moo pan wun ɗe shidaar-shidaar.
1TH 2:18 Ɗyeen mmun naa yit fuu mo zam. Muu fes mǝ rǝɓet dǝm pee wun ɗe zam. An Pool, kǝ lepan fen mbǝ dǝm pee wun ɗi met nyitvǝl, amma nGujwaan ɗar a ar nǝ.
1TH 2:19 A me a mbii canciin fun, kǝ retnyit fun, ɗe nǝ kám nnǝ, muu se koorong nyit Daa fun Jesu, parpuus ɗewur mbaajì yii? Baa a wun kas aa?
1TH 2:20 A wun a nen ɗe wu le kǝ mu kat retyit kǝ nǝ nshang mmun parpuus ɗe mun nnaa Jesu Kristi.
1TH 3:1 Mbǝmǝnǝ, kaaɗe baa mu mak gung kǝ kas. Nǝ aasǝ, ɓe rǝɓet fun nǝ, mun koor nǝ mo, mun ntong Afens mbusun,
1TH 3:2 kǝ mǝ lep Timoti shinɗǝm pee wun ɗe. Timoti wur a ɗyemnǝǝn fun nɗǝǝn ɗak Naan, mu satpwoo ɗeret nkaa Jesu Kristi. Mu lep wur shinɗǝm pee wun ɗi, mbǝkǝ wur caa pǝtuup fuu mo ɗe, kǝ wur kám ɗǝ nwun, kǝ wu ɗar ɗi ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu.
1TH 3:3 Mbǝkǝ taji jeel ɗe wun nkaa shwaa nǝ lee, kǝ memee fuu baa mɓwoon kas. Wun wu man nnǝ, Naan wu kǝ ten lee nnǝ, mun nen fin mo mun nshwaajeel.
1TH 3:4 Kaaɗe gyet mun ɗe ashak kǝ wun, ɓe muu sat nwun nnǝ, nǝ a tǝng mun jir mun nshwaajeel. Yaksǝ wun nkaa naajeel nǝ, kaaɗe gyet muu ten mu sat nwun sǝ.
1TH 3:5 Gyet wen man nnǝ, wun nkaa shwaajeel, a nǝ le ɗangɓe nghan lep Timoti dǝm pee wun, mbǝkǝ ghan man ɗe. Kyet wuu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu nǝ wo? Baa di wen kuɗi kǝn mak gung kas mbǝɗe kǝǝrmuut ɗoom yaa an. Wen yee nee, meeɓe ngujwaan wur kǝ cǝǝr kǝ wun, mbǝkǝ ɗak ɗe gyet mu cìn nnaar fuu, ɓe nǝ a ɗee buu.
1TH 3:6 Yaksǝ Timoti wur kǝ jì pee mun ɗi. Wur satpwoo ɗe nǝ ret mmun nyit, kaaɗe wuu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu nɗǝǝn Jesu Kristi, kǝ wal fuu nǝ ɓal zak. Wur sat mmun nee, wuu yee mun shidaar-shidaar shi retnyit, kǝ nnǝ ɗyeen nwun nnaa mun kaaɗe ɗyeen mmu nnaa wun sǝ zak.
1TH 3:7 Ɗyemnaa mo, kaaɗe mu kǝlǝng nee, shinzeen fuu nii sekyeen, ɓe koo ɗe mun nkaa shwaajeel, kǝ mbii mo ɗes moo daampee mmun, ɓe ɗesǝ nǝ, fes ɓam pǝtuup mmun zam. A shinzeen fuu nǝ ɓam pǝtuup fun mo.
1TH 3:8 Yaksǝ mun nkat gangkwak, katɗang wu ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn Daa Jesu.
1TH 3:9 Mu pǝlang Naan ɗeɗes hakyeng mɓe wun, kǝ mu kat retnyit a kyeen nwur mɓe wun. Mu pǝlang wur mɓe retnyit ɗe mu kat ntoom Naan fun, mɓe wun.
1TH 3:10 Muu naa ncìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) shidaar-shidaar, par kǝ puus, mbǝkǝ, katɗang mǝ katpee, ɓe mun njì pee wun ɗe, kǝ mǝ naa wun ɗe shi yit fun. Kǝ mǝ ɓam wun ɗe, nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe moo luk wun nɗǝǝn shinzeen fuu nǝ.
1TH 3:11 Muu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nee, Naan puun fun shikáa nwur, kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi wur nwang ar nǝ mmun, kǝ mu dǝm pee wun ɗi.
1TH 3:12 Daa wur le kǝ wu sekyeen kǝ wal kǝ koor gurum mo jir, kaaɗe muu wal nwun sǝ.
1TH 3:13 Mbǝkǝ wur gangkwak ɗe nwun nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fuu mo, mbǝkǝ shiimwaan fuu nǝ ɗee ɗe a ɗeret, kǝ ɗeɓang nyit Naan ɗewur a puun fun jir, parɗe Daa fun Jesu Kristi wur njì nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ ashak kǝ nen nwur ɗeɓang mo jir.
1TH 4:1 Ɗyemnaa mo peekyes nǝ, muu ɗang pǝ wun nɗǝǝn sǝm nDaa Jesu. Wu kám shi mun, caan kǝ mwaan ɗe mun muu cìn, mbǝkǝ nǝ gam ɗyeen Naan ɗe. Azeen, wuu ten wu yaa kyeet kǝ mwaan mǝnǝ, naa tǝng wun sekyeen nɗǝǝn mwaan mǝnǝ ɗikǝ ɗikǝ.
1TH 4:2 Wu man kám ɗe gyet mu cìn nwun nɗǝǝn ɓal Daa Jesu Kristi.
1TH 4:3 Naan wur rǝɓet kǝ wu ɗee a ɗeɓang. Taji wu ɗel nɗǝǝn shikbish ɗe nǝ a mǝ ngaa kas.
1TH 4:4 Koo weyi nɗǝǝn wun, ɓe nǝ ret kǝ wur man kaaɗe wur yaa kaa fin ɗi nɗǝǝn ar ɗǝɓang, ɗe nǝ ret.
1TH 4:5 Baa a shi coor mǝ nan kas, kaaɗe nenkum ɗe baa mo man Naan kas, moo cìn sǝ.
1TH 4:6 Taji mee gwe cìn mbǝɗe bish nkaa ɗyemnǝǝn nwur kas, mbǝɗe Daa wur cii nen ɗe moo cìn kaan mbii mǝnǝ mo jir. Muu ten mu satpwoo nwun shiɓal nkaa nǝ.
1TH 4:7 Baa Naan wur pet mun a mbǝkǝ mu ɗee ɗi a nɗǝǝn shikbish kas, amma kǝ mǝ ɗee ɗi a ɗǝɓang.
1TH 4:8 Mbǝmǝnǝ kat mee gurum cii kám ɗesǝ mo, ɓe baa gwar mǝnǝ cii a gurum kas, amma wur cii a Naan, ɗewur shìn Riin nwur Ɗeɓang nwun.
1TH 4:9 Baa nii mee kwoop nǝ kǝ nghan ran mee mbii nwun, nkaa wal nɗyemnǝǝn fuu mo kas, mbǝɗe Daa Naan shikáa nwur, wur kǝ ten kám nwun kaaɗe wun nwal nshak zak.
1TH 4:10 Azeen, wu wal nenɗǝm nɗang Jesu Kristi ɗe mo nɗǝǝn Masidoniya jir, amma muu ɗang pǝ wun ɗyemnaa mo, mbǝkǝ wu sekyeen ɗe kǝ wal ɗikǝ ɗikǝ, mɓe mo jir.
1TH 4:11 Wu gung kǝ wu mwaan ɗi shi mǝse mǝ pǝɗok, wu tap kǝ mbii ɗe wun pǝ cin mo, ɗang wu cìn ɗak shi sar fuu mo, kaaɗe gyet mu sat nwun sǝ.
1TH 4:12 Katɗang wu cìn mbii ɗe mǝ sat nwun sǝ mo, ɓe nen ɗe baa mo shinzeen nDaa Jesu kas, mon nshin ɗeɗes nwun, kǝ baa wun ntaa wu kat mɓut mme mbii kas.
1TH 4:13 Ɗyemnaa mo, mǝ rǝɓet kǝ wu man mee mbii hakyeng, nkaa nen ɗi mo kǝ ten murǝp mo, mbǝkǝ taji pǝtuup fuu mo wat, kaa nen ɗi baa mo shinzeen nyool a peemúut nǝ sǝ kas.
1TH 4:14 Mun mu shinzeen nee, Jesu kǝ muut, kǝ wur kǝ baa yool a peemúut. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe mu man nee, katɗang Jesu wur njì, ɓe Naan wur nle kǝ nen ɗe mo kǝ murǝp nɗǝǝn Jesu, ɓe mon njì ashak kǝ Jesu.
1TH 4:15 Pwoo ɗe muu sat nwun sǝ, nǝ put a pee Daa ɗe shikáa nwur. Katɗang Daa Jesu wur njì nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, ɓe mun nen ɗe mǝ kuɗi mmeen, baa a mun ntaa tǝleng, nen ɗe mo kǝ ten murǝp mo kas.
1TH 4:16 Parpuus mǝnǝ, ɓe Daa wur nɗyeep ɗoo shiɓal, kǝ ngulep Naan ɗeɗes, wur ntàa feer. Ɗangɓe Daa Jesu wur nyool yit ɗengnaan kǝ wur sham ɗe nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ. Nen ɗe mo kǝ ten murǝp nɗǝǝn Kristi, a mon nshee yool a peemúut nǝ.
1TH 4:17 Mun nen ɗǝ mu kuɗi mmeen nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ, ɓe Naan wur nlap mun kàa kǝ mun nɗǝǝn nluu, mbǝkǝ mukaat ɗikǝ Jesu nnaar kǝ ɗengnaan. Yool mmǝnǝ ɓe mun ntong ashak kǝ Daa har ngaa-ngaa.
1TH 4:18 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe wu caa pǝtuup nshak shi pwoo ɗesǝ mo.
1TH 5:1 Ɗyemnaa mo, baa nii mee kwoop nǝ, kǝ mu ran mee mbii nwun nkaa parpuus kǝ peeɗi Daa Jesu wur njì kas.
1TH 5:2 Wuu ten wu man pwoo nkaa nǝ. Wun shikáa fuu, wuu ten wu man nee, parpuus mǝnǝ ɓe Daa wur njì a kaa wat ɗe kǝ jì mpar sǝ.
1TH 5:3 Nciit kǝ mǝnǝ, ɓe gurum mon mɓwet sut, ɗang mon nsat nǝnee, << <<Koo meyii, ɓe nǝ ɗe ryang, kǝ mbii mo ɗi rǝre.>> Ɗangɓe, ndi mman, mee jeel kǝ shwal ntaa nkaa mo, kaa shwal ɗe mat moo kǝlǝng nǝ, kaaɗe mo pǝ làa-làa sǝ. Parmǝnǝ ɓe baa mee gwar mbar kas koo mǝndong.
1TH 5:4 Amma wun ɗyemnaa fen mo, baa wun a nɗǝǝn peenkoo kas. Mbǝmǝnǝ taji parpuus mǝnǝ ɗee nwun a mbii aapwoo, kaaɗe jì kǝ wat aapwoo ngurum mo sǝ kas.
1TH 5:5 Wun jir, wun a nen ɗe mo nɗǝǝn peeɓang, ɗe wuu mwaan mpuus, baa wun a nen ɗe nɗǝǝn peenkwoo mo kas, ɗe muu tong nɗǝǝn peenkwoo sǝ kas.
1TH 5:6 Mbǝmǝnǝ, taji wu saam kaaɗe koor gurum moo cìn sǝ kas, amma mu yaasun, kǝ mǝ tong ɗi shi gongpee.
1TH 5:7 Gurum moo saam a mpar, kǝ gurum moo yuur a mpar,
1TH 5:8 amma mun, muu mwaan a mpuus. Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe mǝ yaasun fun mo. Mu sat a nsekyeen nɗǝǝn shinzeen, kǝ wal nɗǝǝn Daa Jesu. Mbǝɗe ɗesǝ mo a kaa nlǝr shool, ɗe shiitoon moo lep mɓe gong tuur mmo, mbǝkǝ taji mee mbii tung mo kas sǝ. Kǝzak, wu yit kǝ mu sat a nleyit nkaa Daa Jesu ɗǝ wur ɓam mun. Mbǝɗe leyit ɗesǝ nǝ ɗee a kaa mbiikáa shool ɗe kǝ fwang káa ngurum nɗǝǝn lek sǝ.
1TH 5:9 Mu man nǝ, Naan wu bǝlǝp mun, baa a mbǝkǝ mǝ ɗel ɗe nɗǝǝn jeel kǝ tuup nwur kas, ɗangɓe wur bǝlǝp mun a mbǝkǝ mu kat ɓam ɗe nɗǝǝn Daa Jesu Kristi.
1TH 5:10 Wur ɗewur muut, mbǝkǝ katɗang wur mbaajì, ɓe koo ɗe mu kuɗi mmeen nɗǝǝn yil nǝ, kǝ koo ɗe muu ten mu murǝp, ɓe mun ntong ashak kǝ nwur.
1TH 5:11 Mbǝmǝnǝ wu gangkwak nshak, kǝ wu ɓamshak kaaɗe wuu pǝ ncìn nǝ sǝ.
1TH 5:12 Ɗyemnaa mo, mu ɗang pǝ wun kǝ wu shìn ɗeɗes nen ɗe moo cìn ɗak pee wun ɗi. Muu sat a nen ɗe moo fwang wun kǝ kam wun nɗǝǝn kǝǝr nDaa.
1TH 5:13 Wu shìn ɗeɗes mmo hakyeng, kǝ wu wal mmo zak, mbǝ ɗak ɗe moo cìn nǝ. Wu tongryang kǝ shak jir.
1TH 5:14 Ɗyemnaa mo, muu ɗang pǝ wun, mbǝkǝ wu gwak nenseer mo, ɗe sar fur mon nfii. Wuu gang pǝtuup nen ɗe moo kǝǝrmuut mo, kǝ wu ɓam nen ɗe baa moo ɓal kas, kǝ wu gung kǝ shak jir zak.
1TH 5:15 Wu tap, mbǝkǝ taji mee gwar kwat ɗebish shi ɗebish kas, amma wu gung kǝ wu cìn ɗeret ɗe nshak kǝ gurum mo jir, koo pǝrangyi.
1TH 5:16 Wu cìn retnyit koo pǝrangyi.
1TH 5:17 Wu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) shidaar-shidaar.
1TH 5:18 nƊǝǝn mbii mo jir, ɓe wu pǝlang Naan, mbǝɗe nii ret nNaan mbǝ wun nen ɗe mo kǝ ɓal wun kǝ Jesu Kristi, kǝ wun cìn zak.
1TH 5:19 Taji wu cíi cìn ɗak nRiin Naan ɗe wu nɗǝǝn wun kas.
1TH 5:20 Taji wu ɓákpwoo ɗe mo put a pǝ Naan ɗi kas.
1TH 5:21 Wu kam mbii mo jir, mbǝkǝ wu man ɗi nǝ azeen ɗe. Wu yaa mbii ɗe mo a ɗeret.
1TH 5:22 Taji wu cìn mee mbii ɗebish kas koo le.
1TH 5:23 Wen cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) nǝ, Naan shikáa fin, wur ɗewur cìn tongryang nwun, wu nle kǝ wu ɗee a ɗeɓang nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir. nƊǝǝn riin fuu mo, kǝ seen fuu mo, kǝ suk fuu mo, mbǝkǝ wu ɗak suk fuu mo ɗe, mɓe puus jì Daa Jesu Kristi, ɓe baa wun nɗen kǝ mee yitluwaan (naasheep) kas.
1TH 5:24 Naan ɗewur pǝrep wun agu cinzeen baa wur mmak ɓam wun kas.
1TH 5:25 Ɗyemnaa mo, wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe mun.
1TH 5:26 Wu tok kǝ nen cínzeen nǝ mo jir shi tokshik ɗǝɓang, wu yaa sar nshak nɗǝǝn wal ɗe nǝ a mǝ Naan.
1TH 5:27 nƊǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa, ɓe an kǝn satpwoo nwun shiɓal nee, nǝ a tǝng wu tang lepran ɗesǝ nǝ nkom nen cínzeen nǝ mo jir.
1TH 5:28 Ɗeret Daa fun Jesu Kristi nǝ tong ashak kǝ wun. Nǝ aasǝ.
2TH 1:1 Lepran ɗesǝ nǝ put a nsar Pool kǝ Silas, kǝ Timoti. Muu tok kǝ nenɗǝm ndang Naan ɗe mon nTasoloni, ɗe mo a mǝ Naan puun fun kǝ Jesu Kristi.
2TH 1:2 Naan puun fun kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi mo shín ɗeret nwun kǝ tongryang zak.
2TH 1:3 Ɗyemnaa mo, nǝ a tǝng kǝ mu pǝlang Naan mɓe wun shidaar-shidaar. Nǝ ret kǝ mun, mu pǝlang wun aasǝ zak, mbǝɗe cinzeen fuu nǝ nkaa wurang hakyeng, kǝzak, wal fuu mbǝ niyee fuu mo nii seet ɓuɓul ɗak.
2TH 1:4 A nǝ le ɗang mun shikáa fun muu canpwoo shi wun nenɗǝm ndang Naan mo, mbǝ gung fuu, kǝ shinzeen fuu, kaaɗe wuu ɗar ɗi ɓalɓal jir kǝ ɗe wuu gung kǝ shinjeel kǝ shwaajeel ɗe wuu shwaa mo shini-shini.
2TH 1:5 Mbǝ mbii ɗe wuu shwaajeel nǝ mo yaksǝ, parmee puus ɓe mon nkat wun kǝ kwoop nǝ mbǝ mulki Naan. Ɗesǝ mo ɗee a langtǝng mɓe kám nwun nee,
2TH 1:6 Naan a ngucanɗyeel ɗen ndǝre ndǝre. Mbǝmǝnǝ, wur nshìnjeel nen ɗe mo shínjeel nwun.
2TH 1:7 Wur nshìn nookɗi nwun kǝ mun jir nɗǝǝn jeel ɗe muu shwaa mo yaksǝ. Mbii ɗesǝ mon nɗen aasǝ parɗe Daa fun Jesu wur ntong nɗǝǝn ɗengnaan sham. Wur nkámkáa fin ashak kǝ nenlep nwur ɗeɓal mo.
2TH 1:8 Wur njì shi wus ɗe nii bǝlempee, mbǝkǝ wur kwat nen ɗe mo cii Naan ɗe, kǝ nen ɗe mo ciipwoo ɗeret nkaa Daa fun Jesu Kristi.
2TH 1:9 Kwat mo nǝn nɗee a muut ɗel dǝm kǝ mo ngaa-ngaa. Baa mon mmak naa yit Naan koo ɗeɗes mǝ iiko nwur kas, koo le.
2TH 1:10 Katɗang wur njì, parpuus ɗeɗes mǝnǝ, ɓe nen nwur mo jir, mon nshin ɗeɗes nwur. Jir nen ɗe mo shinzeen nwur, ɓe mon nkwoop wur, kǝ wun zak wun nɗee nɗǝǝn nen ɗe mon nkwoop wur, mbǝɗe wuu ten wu shinzeen mpwoo wur ɗe mun kǝ sat nǝ nwun.
2TH 1:11 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe muu ɗangnaan (Leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe wun shidaar-shidaar, mbǝkǝ Naan wur le kǝ wu ɗee ɗekoop nǝ, mɓe zeen ɗe Naan wur pǝrep wun mbǝmǝnǝ. Naan wur le kǝ wu mak cìn koo a mbii ɗeret ɗeɗangyi ɗe wuu pan cìn nǝ mɓe shinzeen fuu shiɓal nwur.
2TH 1:12 A nɗǝǝn kaan kǝ ar ɗesǝ, ɓe gurum mon nle ram nsǝm Daa Jesu nɗǝǝn wun, kǝ wun ɗe nɗǝǝn wur zak, shi ɗeret Daa Naan fun kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi.
2TH 2:1 Pwoo nkaa ji nDaa fun Jesu Kristi, kǝ kuur fun pee wur ɗe. Ɗyemnaa mo, mu ɗang pǝ wun,
2TH 2:2 taji pan fuu mo ɗee a ɗecicǝǝr koo nǝ daampee nwun kas. Mbǝɗe pak gurum moo sat nee, puus Daa nii ten ji. Koo ɗe gurum mo sat pwoo mǝnǝ a nɗǝǝn Riin, nnǝ puus nii ten ɗel, koo a shi liispwoo nǝ, mo aasǝ. Koo kaaɗe pak mo nkaa sat nǝ, nǝ di mu ran pwoo nwun, nkaa nǝ aasǝ nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗe di mu ran nwun sǝ.
2TH 2:3 Taji wu le kǝ mee gurum ngwam wun kas, koo le. Baa puus nǝ kǝ waaji kas, atǝng nnaar ɗe gurum mon ncíi tuwap kǝ mo cii Naan, nǝn nshee dì akuɗang, kǝ gwar ɗebish, ɗewur ɗee a ɗelǝloom, ɗe mon nvwet wur nɗǝǝn wus, wu njì put agaak akuɗang zak.
2TH 2:4 Wun ncìn lek nkaa mbii ɗe gurum mo kǝ seyil mmo jir, kǝ wur nlekáa fin a kaa Naan sǝ. A wur nsat nee, wuɗi met mmo jir, kǝzak wur nɗel nɗǝǝn Lu Naan ɗeɗes, kǝ wur ntong a peetong, ɗangɓe wur leshin a Naan.
2TH 2:5 Baa wu pan kas aa? kaaɗe gyet mun ashak kǝ wun sǝ, ɓe wen kǝn ten nsat nwun nee, mbii ɗesǝ mo jir mon nɗen aasǝ.
2TH 2:6 Yaksǝ ɓe, a mee mbii kǝ yaa wur baa kǝnǝ. Wun shikáa fuu, wu man mbii mǝnǝ. Katpee nǝ wul, ɓe gwar ɗebish wur njì put agaak.
2TH 2:7 Jurum kǝ ɓal kǝ ngwar ɗebish nǝ nkaa cìn ɗak yaksǝ nɗǝǝn yil ɗesǝ nǝ. Ɗangɓe mee ngwar kǝ yaa wu baa kǝ nǝ mɓe reppee ɗeɓen ɗak. Katɗang mo mang ngwar ɗe nii yaa wur baa kǝnǝ,
2TH 2:8 ɓe ngwar ɗebish nǝ wur njì put. Dangɓe Daa Jesu wur ntu ngwar ɗebish nǝ shi nook kǝ pwoo fin. Katɗang Daa Jesu wur mbaajì nɗǝǝn ɗeɗes fin.
2TH 2:9 Katɗang ngwar ɗebish wur njì put, ɓe wur njì a nɗǝǝn ɓal mǝ ngunjwaan. Wun ngwam gurum mo shi mbii aapwoo mo ɗes ɗewur ncìn mo.
2TH 2:10 Wur ncìn ɗak kǝ koo mbii ɗebish ɗeɗangyi, mbǝkǝ wu ngwam nenyil ɗe mon nloom ɗe. Nen ɗesǝ mo ɗee a ɗelǝloom mbǝɗe di mo cii shinzeen, kǝ mo cii wal nzeen. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe baa mo kat ɓam kas.
2TH 2:11 Aasǝ ɓe, Naan cǝǝr kǝ pan fur mo, mbǝkǝ mo shinzeen ɗe a mbii ɗǝ nǝ a ɗung ɓejee ɗak.
2TH 2:12 Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe mon nɗee a ɗelǝloom, mbǝɗe mo cii shinzeen atǝng mo kǝlǝng shang mǝ cìn shikbish ɗak.
2TH 2:13 Ɗyemnaa fun mo, Daa wu wal nwun. Mbǝmǝnǝ ɓe nǝ ret kǝ mu pǝlang Naan mɓe wun. Naan wur ten bǝlǝp wun, pǝgyet ɗi nshee, mbǝkǝ wur kat ɓam wur ɗe nɗǝǝn ɓal Riin fin ɗeɓang, ɗewur le wu ɗee a nen fin ɗeɓang mo shi shinzeen nɗǝǝn mbii ɗe nǝ azeen-nzeen.
2TH 2:14 Naan wu pǝrep wun, mbǝkǝ wu tong ɗe ashak kǝ Daa Jesu nɗǝǝn ram fin, mɓe pwoo ɗeret ɗe mun kǝ sat nǝ nwun.
2TH 2:15 Mbǝmǝnǝ ɗyemnaa mo, wu ɗar ɓalɓal, kǝ wu yaa mbii ɗe gyet mu kám mo ɗe, koo ɗe gyet mǝ sat a shipwoo, kǝ koo ɗe gyet mu sat a shi lepran ɗe gyet mǝ ran mo nwun zak.
2TH 2:16 Daa fun Jesu Kristi shikáa nwur, kǝ Naan puun fun moo ɓam pǝtuup fuu mo.
2TH 2:17 Kǝ wur shínɓal nwun, mbǝkǝ wur cìn koo a ɗak ɗeɗangyi, kǝ pwoo ɗeret ɗe wuu sat zak.
2TH 3:1 Ɗyemnaa fun mo, pwoo ɗe muu rǝɓet sat mǝ kyes nǝ a nee, muu ɗang pǝ wun, mbǝkǝ wu ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) ɗe mbǝ mun. Mbǝkǝ pwoo Naan nǝ kaatpee mo ɗe, kǝ mbǝkǝ gurum mo lap nǝ ɗi kǝkoop, kaaɗe gyet wun wu lap nǝ sǝ.
2TH 3:2 Kǝzak, wu cìn ɗangnaan (leshap kǝ Naan) mɓe mun, mbǝkǝ Naan wur ɓam mun ɗe nɗǝǝn sar kǝ nen bish mo, ɗe pǝtuup fur mo a ɗe ɗeet. Baa a gurum mo jir, mo shinzeen mpwoo nǝ kas.
2TH 3:3 Dangɓe Daa wur kǝ ɗar nkaa zeen. Wur nshin ɓal nwun kǝ wur tap fwang wun aku nsar ngujwaan.
2TH 3:4 Mu shinzeen nDaa ɓe wun, nǝ, wu cìn mbii ɗe mu sat mo ɗe, kǝ wuu sekyeen kǝ cìn mo zak.
2TH 3:5 Daa wur nle kǝ wu man wal Naan ɗeɗes mɓe wun, kǝ gung kaaɗe Daa Jesu gung sǝ zak.
2TH 3:6 Ɗyemnaa mo, nɗǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi, muu sat nwun shiɓal nee, taji wu ɓalkaa kǝ ɗyemnǝǝn fun ɗe mo a seer mo kas. Shii kǝ mǝnǝ, a nen ɗe baa moo mwaan nkaa kám ɗe gyet mu kám nwun kas.
2TH 3:7 Wun shikáa fuu, wu man nee, nǝ ret kǝ wu mwaan nɗǝǝn shiimwaan fun, mbǝɗe gyet mun ashak kǝ wun, ɓe baa gyet muu tong kǝ sar fun mo nfii kas,
2TH 3:8 kǝ baa muu se mbiise nsar mee ngwar zuum kas, amma muu cìn ɗak shiɓal kǝ sar fun mo mpar kǝ puus, mbǝkǝ taji mu lejeel mmee ngwar nɗǝǝn wun kas.
2TH 3:9 Gyet mun kǝ iiko mbǝkǝ mǝ sat nwun nnǝ wu shin mbiise mmun, ɗangɓe baa gyet mu tal pǝ wun kas, mɓeɗi gyet mu rǝɓet kám nwun ar ɗe wun ncìn ɗak shi sar fuu mo.
2TH 3:10 Kaaɗe gyet mun ɗe ashak kǝ wun, ɓe muu naa nsatpwoo nwun shiɓal nǝ, katɗang baa mee gurum cìn ɗak kas, ɓe taji wu shín mee mbii nwur se kas.
2TH 3:11 Mu kǝlǝng nee, pak mo nɗǝǝn wun, moo ɗee a seer mo. Nnǝ baa moo cìn mee ɗak kas, amma nnǝ, moo ɗee mwaan buu, mbǝkǝ mo lep pwoo ɗe nɗǝǝn ɗak kǝ gurum mo.
2TH 3:12 nƊǝǝn sǝm kǝ Daa Jesu Kristi, muu satpwoo shiɓal nee, nǝ ret kǝ nen mǝnǝ mo nook mwaan mǝnǝ, mbǝkǝ mo cìn ɗak, ɗe mon nkat mbiise mukáa fur mo ɗi, mbǝ pwoo fur mo.
2TH 3:13 Ɗyemnaa mo, taji kwak fuu mo murǝp mbǝ cìn ɗak ɗeret kas.
2TH 3:14 Katɗang mee ngwar cii cìn mbii ɗe mu sat nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗesǝ, ɓe wu naa gwar mǝnǝ rǝret. Taji wu cìn mee mbii ashak kǝ wun kas, mbǝkǝ naashweep yaa gwar mǝnǝ ɗi.
2TH 3:15 Ɗangɓe taji wu naa wur a kaa shaarlek sǝ kas, ɗangɓe wu fwang wur kaa ɗyemnǝǝn sǝ.
2TH 3:16 Daa Jesu shikáa fin, ɗe ryang kǝ put a pee wur ɗi, wur shìn tongryang nwun nɗǝǝn mbii mo jir. Daa Jesu tong ashak kǝ wun jir.
2TH 3:17 Ɗesǝ a sar ran mǝnǝ Pool, ɗe an kǝn le nǝ nɗǝǝn pwoo ɗe moo put pee ghan ɗi. Wen kǝn ran aasǝ.
2TH 3:18 Ɗeret kǝ Daa fun Jesu Kristi nǝ tong ashak kǝ wun jir. Nǝ aasǝ.
TIT 1:1 A ghan Pool kǝrem nDaa Naan, kǝ laalep mǝ Daa Jesu Kristi, ran wasika ɗesǝ nǝ. A Jesu wur bilip ghan, mbǝkǝ nghan ɓam nen ɗe Naan wur kǝ ten bilip mo, mbǝkǝ shinzeen mo wurang ɗe nɗǝǝn Naan, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ mo man zeen nǝ ɗe jir nkaa ar kǝ Naan.
TIT 1:2 Kǝ mo leyit fur mo ɗe nkaa seen ɗe nǝ azeen, ɗe ngha-ngha. Naan ɗe baa wur cìn ɗung kas, wur kǝ ten sat nǝ, wur shin seen mǝnǝ ngurum mo.
TIT 1:3 Nciit-nciit kǝgam pee nǝ, ɓe wur nwoo seen ɗesǝ nǝ agaak shi pwoo wur, ɗewur kǝ ten le nǝ nsar fen. A Naan ɗewur ɓam mun, a wur a ngwe ɗewur ten lep nghan, mbǝkǝ ghan satpwoo wur ɗe ngurum mo.
TIT 1:4 Wen nkaa ran wasika ɗesǝ nghan Titus, làa fen ɗe azeen-nzeen nɗǝǝn shinzeen, ɗe mun kǝ nǝ vǝl. Ɗeret, kǝ ryang pee Naan puun nJesu Kristi Nguɓam fun, mo tong ashak kǝ waa.
TIT 1:5 Mbii ɗe nǝ le kǝ nghan yit waa nyil nKrit, a mbǝkǝ gha sǝǝt a ɗak mbii mo ɗe ndǝre-ndǝre, kǝ gha bilip nennan mo ɗe mbee jir lu nNaan ɗeɗang ghi, ɗe nǝ nɗǝǝn nyil nKrit. Taji a mundǝr mbii ɗe dǝ nsat nghan kas.
TIT 1:6 Jir we ɗe a bilip kaa ngunan sǝ, ɓe nǝ a tǝng kǝ gwar mǝnǝ kǝ mǝse ɗeret, ngwe ɗewur kǝ mat a mǝndong ɓejee ɗak. Kǝ jep wur mo zak, nǝ a tǝng kǝ mo ɗen a nen ɗe mo shinzeen. Ngwe ɗe mǝse wur nǝ mak le kǝ gurum mo naa nǝ, baa wur a ngucìn mbii ɗebish kas, kǝzak, baa a ngukáaɓál kas.
TIT 1:7 Jir a wii ɗewur a ɗeɗes nɗǝǝn nendǝm ndang Naan mo, ɓe wur naa a mbii ɗe mo a mǝ Naan. Mbǝmǝnǝ, ɓe mǝse wur nǝ a tǝng kǝ nǝ ɗee a ɗeret. Baa wur nɗee a nguroop, jir a ngwe ɗe mbii kǝkǝlak làa wur mɓut kas. Baa wur nshwaa am anab (filip) kǝ nǝ yuur wur ɗe kas, baa wur a nguɓwanbish kas. Baa wur a ngurǝɓet mbii mbee kat lǝɓet ɗebuu kas.
TIT 1:8 Ni ret kǝ wur ɗee a ngula gurum mo nɗǝǝn tulu wur. Nǝ a tǝng kǝ wur wal mbii ɗeret mo. Nǝ ret kǝ wur ɗee a ngwe ɗe mwaan wur nǝ a ndǝre-ndǝre, kǝ mǝse wur nǝ ɗee a ɗe nǝ shang nNaan zak. Nguyaashin.
TIT 1:9 A ngwe ɗewur ɗar ɓalɓal nɗǝǝn shinzeen ɗe mu kám nǝ, mbǝkǝ wur mak kám ɗe ngurum mo zak. Mɓe kǝ mo katɓal ɗe nɗǝǝn pǝtuup fur mo, kǝzak, mbǝkǝ wur man mbii ɗewur nkám ɗe nen ɗe moo satpwoo ɗebuu mo, kǝ wur kám ɗe mmo, pee ɗe mo taa ɗel ɗe.
